NV_1.1.1^1	pramāṇa ādi padārtha tattva jñānāt niḥśreyasa adhigamaḥ iti etat śāstrasya ādi sūtram tasya abhisambandha vākyam pramāṇataḥ artha pratipattau iti evam ādi tasya anusandhāna vākyam śāstrasya puruṣa śreyaḥ abhidhāyaka tvāt śāstram punar pramāṇa ādi vācaka pada samūhaḥ vyūha viśiṣṭaḥ padam punar varṇa samūhaḥ pada samūhaḥ śūtram sūtra samūhaḥ prakaraṇam prakaraṇa samūhaḥ āhnikam āhnika samūhaḥ adhyāyaḥ pañca adhyāyī śāstram tad padārthāḥ pramāṇa ādayaḥ tasya śāstrasya padānām arthāḥ pramāṇa ādayaḥ ṣoḍaśa ātmānaḥ tat śāstram puruṣa śreyaḥ abhidhatte 
NV_1.1.1^2	 pratyakṣa anumāna adhigata vastu tattva anvā ākhyānam śāstra dharmaḥ tasya viṣayaḥ pratyakṣa anumāna an adhigata vastu tattvaḥ ādhyātmika śakti sampad i uktaḥ aantevāsī puruṣaḥ punar caturdhā bhidyate pratipannaḥ apratipannaḥ sandigdhaḥ viparyastaḥ ca iti tatra pratipannaḥ pratipādayitā itare sa apekṣāḥ santaḥ pratipādyāḥ te yadā indriya artha sannikarśam apekṣante tadā pratyakṣena yadā liṅga darśana smṛti ādi apekṣante tadā anumānena yadā punar upadeśam apekṣante tadā śāstram pravartate śreyaḥ punar sukham ahita nivṛttiḥ ca tat śreyaḥ bhidyamānam dvedhā vyavatiṣṭate dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa bhedena 
NV_1.1.1^3	 dṛṣṭam sukham adṛṣṭam ahita nivṛttiḥ ahita nivṛttiḥ api ātyantikī ca anātyantikī ca anātyantikī kaṇṭaka ādeḥ duḥkha sādhanasya parihāreṇa ātyantikī punar ekaviṃśati prabheda bhinna duḥkha hānyāḥ ekaviṃśati prabheda bhinnam punar duḥkham śarīram ṣaṣ indriyāṇi ṣaṣ viṣayāḥ ṣaṣ buddhayaḥ sukham duḥkham ca iti śarīram duḥkha āyatana tvāt duḥkham indriyāṇi viṣayāḥ buddhayaḥ ca tad sādhana bhāvāt sukham duḥkha anuṣaṅgāt duḥkham svarūpataḥ iti tasya hāniḥ dharma adharma sādhana parityāgena anutpannayoḥ dharma adharmayoḥ anutpādena utpannayoḥ ca upabhogāt prakṣayena iti 
NV_1.1.1^4	 puruṣāḥ rāga ādi mantaḥ vīta rāgāḥ ca tatra rāgaḥ viṣaya abhiṣvaṅga lakṣaṇaḥ sa yeṣām asti te rāga ādimantaḥ vairāgyam punar bhoga anabhiṣvaṅga lakṣaṇam tat yeṣām asti te vīta rāgāḥ pravṛtteḥ dvaividhyam puruṣa bheda anuvidhānena teṣām puruṣāṇām yāḥ pravṛttayaḥ tāḥ puruṣa bhedam anuvidhīyamānāḥ ubhaya rūpāḥ bhavanti vīta rāga pravṛttiḥ ekadhā tatra yā vīta rāgāṇām pravṛttiḥ sā khalu eka rūpāḥ aniṣṭa pratiṣedha arthāḥ aniṣṭam hāsyāmaḥ iti evam eva pravartante na punar eṣām kvacid abhiṣvaṅgaḥ asti iti rāga ādimad pravṛttiḥ tu dvi rūpāḥ 
NV_1.1.1^5	 ye tu rāga ādimantar teṣām yāḥ pravṛttayaḥ tāḥ dvividhāḥ bhavanti iṣṭāniṣṭa viṣaya adhigama pratiṣedha arthāḥ iṣṭam āpsyāmi iti rāgāt pravartate aniṣṭam hāsyāmi iti dveṣāt nivartate pravṛtteḥ api dvaividhyam bhavati samartha asamartha bhedāt yā khalu rāga ādimad pravṛttiḥ sā samarthā ca asamarthā ca bhavati iṣṭam āpsyāmi iti pravartamānaḥ yadā prāpnoti tadā samartha aniṣṭam hāsyāmi iti pravartamānaḥ yadā jahāti tadā api samarthāḥ yadā viparyayaḥ tadā asamartha iti tat punar pravṛtteḥ dvaividhyam pramāṇasya arthavat anarthaka tvāt pramāṇam tāvat artha paricchedakam pramāṇa sāmānyāt pramāṇa pratirūpakam api pramāṇam iti upacaryate 
NV_1.1.1^6	 kim punar pramāṇa sāmānyam pramāṇa ābhāsasya sāmānya paricchedaka tvam pramāṇena api sāmānyam paricchidyate pramāṇa ābhāsena api saḥ ayam pramātā yadā pramāṇena artham avadhārya pravartate tadā asya pravṛttiḥ samarthā bhavati yadā punar pramāṇa ābhāsena avadhārya pravartate tadā asamarthāḥ tasyāḥ punar arthavat tvam pramāṇataḥ artha pratipattau iti ādi bhāṣyam paraspara apekṣi tvāt ubhaya asiddhiḥ iti ced nānā ādi tvāt yadi pramāṇataḥ artha pratipattau pravṛtti sāmarthyam yadi vā pravṛtti sāmarthyāt pramāṇataḥ artha pratipattiḥ kim pūrvam kim vā paścāt iti vācyam 
NV_1.1.1^7	 yadi tāvat pramāṇataḥ pūrvam artha pratipattiḥ pravṛtti sāmarthyam antareṇa kim iti pratipadyate atha pūrvam pravṛtti sāmarthyam anavadhārya arthe kim iti pravartate tasmāt pravṛtteḥ pramāṇataḥ artha pratipatteḥ vā pūrva apara bhāvaḥ na kalpate iti tat ca na evam kasmāt anādi tvāt anādiḥ ayam saṃsāraḥ iti pūrva abhyasta sūtre pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ ādimati ca saṃsāraḥ eṣa doṣaḥ kim pūrvam pramāṇataḥ artha pratipattiḥ uta aho pūrvam pravṛtti sāmarthyam iti pramāṇa pravṛttyoḥ vā bala abala jijñāsāyām ubhaya sāmarthya pradarśana artham vākyam lokaḥ khalu pravartamānaḥ pramāṇena artham avadhārya pravartate 
NV_1.1.1^8	 sa ca tathā pravartamānaḥ phalam upalabhate tatra idam cintyate kim pramāṇataḥ artha pratipattiḥ samarthota aho pravṛttiḥ iti ubhayam samartham tat na antarīyaka tvāt phalasya asya ca arthasya upadarśana artham vākyam iti loka vṛtta anuvādaḥ vā sarvaḥ pramātā pramāṇena artham avadhārya pravartamānaḥ phalam upalabhate iti loka vṛttam tad vākyena anūdyate iti heya hāna upāya adhigantavya bhedāt catvāri artha padāni heyam duḥkham tat hetuḥ ca duḥkham uktam duḥkha hetuḥ avidyā tṛṣṇe dharma adharmau iti 
NV_1.1.1^9	 hānam tattva jñānam tat punar yathā avasthita padārtha adhigatiḥ tat ca pramāṇam upāyaḥ śāstram tat api uktam adhigantavyaḥ apavargaḥ sa punar ātyantikaḥ duḥkha abhāvaḥ etasmin ca caturvarge pramāṇasya prādhānya pradarśana artham ca iti katham punar anena vākyena pramāṇa ādi caturvargaḥ pradarśyate iti pramāṇa prameya adhigatayaḥ śruti gamyāḥ pramātā tat na antarīyaka tvāt na hi pramātāram antareṇa pramāṇam sambhavati tat idam vākyam avayavaśas upanyasya varṇyate tatra pramāṇataḥ iti tasiḥ vacanam vacana vibhakti vyāpti jñāpana artham 
NV_1.1.1^10	 pramāṇataḥ iti iyam nimitta pañcamī asya abhidhānam vacana vyāpti artham vibhakti vyāpti artham ca katham punar pañcamī vyatirekeṇa tasiḥ labhyate labhyate iti āha ādi a ādau upasaṃkhyānāt iti tat kim siddham bhavati vacana vyāptyā saṃplavaḥ vyavasthā ca pramāṇena pramāṇābhyām pramāṇaiḥ pratipattiḥ iti saṃplavaḥ gamyate pramāṇena eva iti vyavasthā vibhakti vyāptyā hetu karaṇa bhāvaḥ pramāṇāt artha adhigatiḥ bhavati iti hetu tvam pramāṇena artham sādhayati iti sādhakatama tvāt karaṇa arthaḥ saṃplava anupapattiḥ viśiṣṭa viṣaya tvāt iti ced na anabhyupagamāt 
NV_1.1.1^11	 syāt matiḥ eṣā viśiṣṭa viṣayāṇi pramāṇāni viśeṣa viṣayam pratyakṣam sāmānya viṣayam anumānam iti etāvat ca adhigantavyam yat uta sāmānyam viśeṣaḥ ca na ca sāmānya viṣayam pratyakṣam na jātu anumānam viśeṣa viṣayam iti etat ca na anabhyupagamāt na tāvat pramāṇa dvayam pratipadyāmahe na viṣaya dvayam na api asaṃkaram kim kāraṇam pramāṇāni tāvat catvāri viṣayaḥ ca sāmānya viśeṣa tadvat bhedāt tredhā saṃkaraḥ api ekasya sarvaiḥ pramāṇaiḥ adhigateḥ indriya vat iti indriyam khalu artha prakāśaka tvāt pramāṇam tasya vyavasthā saṃkaraḥ ca vyavasthā gandha ādiṣu 
NV_1.1.1^12	 saṃkaraḥ pṛthivī ādiṣu dvi indriya grāhya tvāt sattāyām guṇa tve ca sārva indriyam jñānam iti adhigata tvāt vaiyarthyam iti ced na anyathā tad adhigateḥ syāt matam yadi saṃkīryeran pramāṇāni nanu ekena pramāṇena adhigate arthe dvitīyam pramāṇam vyartham āpadyeta adhigatam ca artham adhigamayatā pramāṇena piṣṭapeṣaṇam syāt na anyathā tad adhigateḥ na brūmaḥ yathā pratyakṣena arthaḥ adhigamyate tathā anumāna ādibhiḥ api iti anyathā pratyakṣena indriya sambaddhaḥ indriya asambaddaḥ anumānena saṃjñā saṃjñi saṃbandha pratipattiḥ upamānena śabda ullekhena āgamena iti 
NV_1.1.1^13	 viṣaya antare vyavasthā darśanāt ca na ca sarvasmin arthe saṃplavaḥ asti iti atas na vaiyarthyam iti tasmāt vyavasthitam etat tasiḥ vacanam vacana vibhakti vyāpti jñāpana artham iti pramāṇa svarūpa avadhāraṇam kartavyam kim punar pramāṇasya pramāṇa tvam kim ca uktam bhavati pramāṇam iti upalabdhi hetuḥ pramāṇam upalabdhi hetu tvam pramāṇa tvam yat upalabdhi nimittam tat pramāṇam iti samāna tvāt alakṣaṇam iti ced yadi upalabdhi hetuḥ pramāṇam nanu pramātṛ prameyayoḥ api upalabdhi hetu tvāt pramāṇa tvam prasajyeta viśeṣaḥ vā vaktavyaḥ iti 
NV_1.1.1^14	 ayam viśeṣaḥ pramāṇe pramātṛ prameyayoḥ caritārtha tvāt pramāṇe pramātā prameyam ca caritārtham acarita artham tu pramāṇam atas tat eva upalabdhi sādhanam iti akaraṇā pramāṇa utpattiḥ iti ced na indriya artha sannikarṣasya karaṇa bhāvāt yadi pramātṛ prameyābhyām pramāṇam janyate akaraṇā tarhi pramāṇa utpattiḥ prāpnoti na indriya artha sannikarṣasya karaṇa bhāvāt na akaraṇā pramāṇa utpattiḥ pramāṇa utpattau indriya artha sannikarṣam apekṣamāṇābhyām pramātṛ prameyābhyām pramāṇam janyate iti na akaraṇa pramāṇa utpatti prasaṅgaḥ 
NV_1.1.1^15	 yadi tarhi pramāṇa utpattau indriya artha sannikarṣam apekṣete pramātṛ prameye atha tarhi indriya artha sannikarṣa utpattau kim apekṣeta iti tasmin api indriyam iti anādiḥ kartṛ karaṇa bhāvaḥ yat yat paścāt bhavati tat tat pūrva bhāvinam apekṣate iti anādiḥ kartṛ karaṇa bhāvaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ iti yadi pramātṛ prameyābhyām sadbhyām pramāṇam janyate tatas pramāṇam antareṇa pramātṛ prameya bhāvasya asiddha tvāt pramātṛ tvam prameya tvam ca anupapannam iti katham pramāṇam iti yathā kāraka śabdaḥ ayam tathā prameyam pramātā iti ca na ca kāraka śabdāḥ kriyā sambandham antareṇa ātmānam labhante iti 
NV_1.1.1^16	 na ca dravya mātram kārakam na ca kriyā mātram iti kāraka śabdaḥ hi pravartamānaḥ kriyā sādhane kriyā viśeṣa yukte pravartate pramātṛ prameya śabdau ca kāraka śabdau tau antareṇa kriyām na pravarteyātām iti na pācaka ādi śabda vat tri kāla viṣaya tvāt na brūmaḥ kriyā sambandhena eva kāraka śabdāḥ pravartante iti api tu tri kāla viṣayāḥ ete yadi kriyā sambandha nimittāḥ eva syuḥ na kriyām antareṇa pravarteran kriyā sambandham antareṇa tu pravartante kim punar nimittam sāmarthyam tat ca triṣu api kāleṣu asti iti tasmāt upapannam pramātṛ prameyābhyām pramāṇam janyate tad upalabdhi sādhanam iti 
NV_1.1.1^17	 sādhakatama tvāt vā na prasaṅgaḥ na ca ayam prasaṅgaḥ asti pramātā ca prameyam ca upalabdhi nimitta tvāt pramāṇam prasajyate iti kasmāt sādhakatama tvāt sādhakatamam pramāṇam na tu pramātṛ prameye kaḥ khalu sādhakatama arthaḥ sādhakatamam pramāṇam iti kevalam vākyam abhidhīyate na arthaḥ iti bhāva abhāvayoḥ tadvat tā na pramātari prameye vā asati pramā bhavati sati tu bhavati na punar sati bhavati eva pramāṇe tu sati bhavantī bhavati eva sa ca ayam atiśayaḥ sādhakatama tvam ucyate yadvān vā pramimīte saḥ atiśayaḥ kiṃvān pramimīte pramāṇavān 
NV_1.1.1^18	 ayam pramāṇe sati pramimīte na asati iti satoḥ vā akartṛ tvam yat abhāvāt yasya ca abhāvāt pramātṛ prameye na pramām kurutaḥ saḥ atiśayaḥ saṃyoga vat carama bhāvitāḥ vā yathā vā saṃyogaḥ paścāt bhāvī dravya śaktiḥ bhavati tathā pramāṇam caram a bhāvi pramātṛ prameyayoḥ pramā śaktiḥ bhavati paścāt bhāvaḥ atiśayaḥ pratipatteḥ ānantaryam vā yat vā pramāṇa anantaram pratipatteḥ janma sa ca ayam atiśayaḥ iti asādhāraṇa karaṇa tā vā pramātā tāvat sādhāraṇam kāraṇam pratyakṣa ādi jñānānām sarva pratipattīnām prameyam api aśeṣa puruṣa sādhāraṇa tvāt tathābhūtam 
NV_1.1.1^19	 pramāṇam tu asādhāraṇa kāraṇa tvāt pradhānam prādhānyāt ca sādhakatama tvena abhidhīyate iti pramā kāraṇa saṃyoga viśeṣaka tvam vā yaḥ vā pramā kāraṇam saṃyogaḥ tasya pramāṇam anugrahe vartamānam atiśaya śabda vācyam artha grahaṇam pramāṇa viṣaya pratipatti pratiṣedha artham yatas na pramāṇa viṣayā pratipattiḥ puruṣam itikartavya tāyām prayojayati kim tu arthasya tathā abhāva viṣayā yadā ayam arthasya tathā abhāvam pratipadyate atha pravartate iti upekṣaṇīya vastu pratiṣedha artham vā na hi upekṣaṇīya vastu viṣayā pratipattiḥ puruṣam itikartavya tāyām prayojayati kim tu arthasya sukha duḥkha hetu bhāva viṣayā 
NV_1.1.1^20	 yadā ayam arthasya sukha duḥkha hetu bhāvam pratipadyate atha pravartate iti pramāṇa grahaṇam gamyamāna tvāt iti ced na pramāṇa viśeṣa jñāpana artha tvāt artha pratipattau pravṛtti sāmarthyāt iti abhidhīyamāne gamyate eva etat pramāṇataḥ iti na hi kācid artha pratipattiḥ pramāṇam antareṇa sambhavati iti tat ca na evam pramāṇa viśeṣa jñāpana artha tvāt asti ayam pramāṇa śabdaḥ pramāṇe vartamānaḥ asti ca pramāṇa sāmānyāt pramāṇa ābhāse api iti tat yā iha pramāṇena pratipattiḥ sā pravṛtti sāmarthyam pratipādayati pramāṇam na itarat iti 
NV_1.1.1^21	 na ca pramāṇa grahaṇam antareṇa nimitta pañcamī abhidhānam labhyate tena ca prayojanam atas ca pramāṇa grahaṇam kṛtam iti artha grahaṇam sukha duḥkha tad hetu tvena sarva saṃgrahaḥ arthyamāṇa tvāt ca sarvaḥ pramāṇa ādiḥ arthaḥ sukha duḥkha hetuḥ sarvaḥ ca arthyate arthyamāṇa tvāt arthaḥ iti na vyāghātāt avivakṣita tvāt ca sarvaḥ pramāṇa ādiḥ arthaḥ sukha duḥkha hetuḥ iti bruvataḥ heya ādi bhedāt catvāri artha padāni iti vyāhanyeta na ca pramāṇa ādi hānam śakyam kartum na ca pramāṇa ādi hanam vivakṣitam tasmāt apavyākhyānam etat 
NV_1.1.1^22	 kim tu sukha duḥkha tvena tad hetu tvena ca yāvatām saṃgrahaḥ te abhidhīyante adhikārāt na saṃvidaḥ grahaṇam anadhikārāt akarma tvāt ca na saṃvid dheya asukha duḥkha tvāt atad hetu tvāt ca na api arthyate aphala tvāt saḥ ayam pramāṇa arthaḥ aparisaṃkhyeyaḥ iyān ayam pramāṇa viṣayaḥ iti na parisaṃkhyātum śakyam ānantyāt na ubhayasya api parisaṃkhyāta tvāt etāvān ayam pramāṇa arthaḥ yat uta sukha duḥkhe tad hetuḥ ca iti tat ca ubhayam parisaṃkhyātam atas na yuktam ānantyāt na parisaṃkhyātate iti prāṇabhṛt bhedasya ca aparisaṃkhyeya tvāt aparisaṃkhyeyaḥ pramāṇa arthaḥ iti asambaddham uktam iti 
NV_1.1.1^23	 na artha śabdasya prayojana vāci tvāt pramāṇa arthaḥ aparisaṃkhyeyaḥ iti pramāṇa prayojanam aparisaṃkhyeyam iti ayam vākya arthaḥ katham saḥ eva arthaḥ keṣāñcid sukha hetuḥ bhavati keṣāñcid duḥkha hetuḥ iti arthavati ca samarthe pramāṇe arthavanti bhavanti samarthāni iti anyatamatva arthaḥ sādhakatama tva arthaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ prakaraṇāt prakaraṇam hi caturvarge pramāṇam pradhānam iti vartate yadi punar yathāśruti vākyam arthavat syāt kim pramāṇa sāmarthyam varṇitam syāt tasmāt yathoktam nyāyyam iti pramātā svatantraḥ kim punar svātantryam 
NV_1.1.1^24	 kāraka phala upabhoktṛ tvam yasmāt kārakāṇām phalena ayam abhisambadhyate tad samavāyaḥ vā yat vā aśeṣa kāraka niṣpādyāyāḥ kriyāyāḥ puruṣaḥ āśrayaḥ bhavati tat prayoktṛ tvam itara aprayojya tā vā yat vā paridṛṣṭa sāmarthyāni kāraka cakrāṇi prayuṅkte taiḥ ca na prayujyate iti tattva parisamāptiḥ viniyoga yogyata upekṣyatā vā yāsau= avisaṃvāditā sa avadhāritasya arthasya viniyoga yogya tā sukha sādhanam vā duḥkha sādhanam vā ayam arthaḥ iti jñātvā viniyogaḥ sā samāptiḥ tad prāptiḥ tad pratiṣedhaḥ ca yat vā na sukha sādhanam na duḥkha sādhanam vā iti upekṣā iti 
NV_1.1.1^25	 kim punar tat sat asatī tat tasya bhāvaḥ tattvam iti atra tat vācyam yasya bhāvaḥ iti sadasatī tat pramāṇa viṣaya tvena adhikārāt sat asatī pramāṇasya viṣayau iti adhikṛtam tasmāt sat asatī tat iti tad bhāvaḥ sat asat tvam sat asatoḥ pramāṇa viṣaya tā tad pratiṣedhaḥ ca tayoḥ khalu sat asatoḥ bhāvaḥ dvi rūpaḥ vidhīyamānaḥ pratiṣidhyamānaḥ ca yat ekatra vidhīyate tat anyatra pratiṣidhyate tat yathā gandhavatī pṛthivī agandhā āpaḥ iti pramāṇa viṣaya tvāt sat asatayoḥ viśeṣa prasaṅgaḥ iti ced nānā ekāntāt 
NV_1.1.1^26	 tatra bhavet eṣā buddhiḥ yadi pramāṇena sat asatī gamyete tatas pramāṇa viṣaya tvāt ubhayoḥ aviśeṣaḥ prāptaḥ iti tat ca nānā ekāntāt sarvam idam go ghaṭa ādi dravya jātam pramāṇa gamyam bheda vat ca tasmāt anekāntaḥ ayam iti svatantra paratantra upalabdhi anupalabdhi kāraṇa bhāvāt ca viśeṣaḥ sat khalu pramāṇasya ālambanam svatantram bhavati asat tu paratantram pratiṣedha mukhena pratipadyate pradīpa vat iti tat yathā pradīpaḥ khalu apavaraka ādi sthitam ghaṭa ādikam artham pratipādayati tadvat asat api pratipādayati na hi asat pratipattau upāya antaram āsthīyate 
NV_1.1.1^27	 dṛśyamāne hi ghaṭa ādike arthe na anena samāna jātīyam dṛśya antaram asti yadi abhaviṣyat idam iva adrakṣyata na ca dṛśyate tasmāt darśana abhāvāt na asti iti gamyate evam pramāṇena api sati pramīyamāṇe na anena samāna jātīyam prameya antaram asti yadi abhaviṣyat idam iva amāsyata na tu mīyate tasmāt māna abhāvāt na asti iti tat evam sataḥ prakāśakam pramāṇam asat api prakāśayati iti tatra asat bhedāḥ svātantryeṇa na prakāśante iti na ucyante caturvarga anantarbhāvāt vā bhāva prapañca vat abhāva prapañcaḥ api uddiṣṭaḥ veditavyaḥ iti bhāva upadeśāt eva abhāvaḥ upadiṣṭaḥ bhavati iti 
NV_1.1.1^28	 atas ca na ucyantaḥ iti tatra sat ca khalu ṣoḍaśadhā vyūḍham upadekṣyate iti vyūhaḥ saṃkṣepaḥ te ete sat bhedāḥ iti sūtram pramāṇa prameya saṃśaya prayojana dṛṣṭānta siddhānta avayava tarka nirṇaya vāda jalpa vitaṇḍā hetvābhāsa= chala ja ati nigraha sthānānām tattva jñānāt niḥśreyasa adhigamaḥ sarva padārtha pradhānaḥ samāsaḥ dvandvaḥ kim uktam bhavati sarve ete pramāṇa ādayaḥ vijñeyāḥ iti anyathā hi samāsa antara parigrahāt viśeṣaṇa tvena upayuktānām pramāṇa ādīnām avijñeya tā syāt yathāvacanam vigrahaḥ iti yat eva nirdeśe vacana bheda upādāne prayojanam tat iha api draṣṭavyam iti 
NV_1.1.1^29	 pramāṇa ādīnām tattvam iti śaiṣikī ṣaṣṭhī kaḥ punar śeṣaḥ kārakāṇām avivakṣā śeṣaḥ iti yatra na kārakam kāraka arthaḥ vā vivakṣyate sa śeṣaḥ tat yathā brāhmaṇasya kamaṇḍaluḥ iti tattvasya pramāṇa ādibhyaḥ anyān anya tve doṣaḥ yadi tāvat pramāṇa ādi vyatiriktam tattvam na pramāṇa ādi jñānāt niḥśreyasa adhigamaḥ iti prāptam kim kāraṇam tattva viśeṣaṇa tvena upādānāt rāja puruṣa ānayana kriyā vat iti atha abhedaḥ tattva grahaṇa ānarthakyam yadi pramāṇa ādi vyatiriktam tattvam na pratipadyasaḥ evam tarhi tattva grahaṇam anarthakam sampadyate iti 
NV_1.1.1^30	 na ubhayathā api adoṣāt iti eke yadi tāvat pramāṇa ādi vyatiriktam tattvam syāt tasya asvatantra tvāt pramāṇa ādayaḥ api gamyante id kuṇḍe badara vṛtti vat iti yathā ukte kuṇḍe badarāṇām vṛttiḥ iti bhāve deśite bhāvasya asvatantra tvāt kuṇḍe badarāṇi vartante iti uktam bhavati tathā iha api tattva jñānāt niḥśreyasa adhigamaḥ iti pramāṇa ādīnām grahaṇam bhāvasya asvatantra tvāt iti abhede api iṣu sthiti vat tad bhāva pratiṣedhaḥ na artha antaram iti na pramāṇa ādi mātram ucyate api tu artha antaram pratiṣidhyate yathā iṣoḥ sthitiḥ iti na iṣu mātram sthitiḥ api tu gatimat artha antaram na bhavati iti 
NV_1.1.1^31	 tat na anartha antara tva asiddheḥ tattva jñānāt niḥśreyasa adhigamaḥ iti tattvam jñāyamānam karma sampadyate niḥśreyasam ca adhigamyamānam karma bhavati iti kim punar tattvam kim vā niḥśreyasam iti tattvam padārthānām yathā vyavasthita ātma pratyaya utpatti nimitta tvam yaḥ yathā vyavasthitaḥ padārthaḥ sa tathābhūtasya pratyayasya utpatti nimittam bhavati iti etat tattvam niḥśreyasam punar dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa bhedāt dvedhā bhavati tatra pramāṇa ādi padārtha tattva jñānāt dṛṣṭam niḥśreyasam na hi kaścid padārthaḥ jñāyamānaḥ hāna upādāna upekṣā buddhi nimittam na bhavati iti 
NV_1.1.1^32	 evam ca kṛtvā sarve api padārthāḥ jñeyatayā upakṣipyante iti param tu niḥśreyasam ātma ādeḥ tattva jñānāt bhavati iti dṛṣṭam pramāṇa ādi parijñānāt adṛṣṭam punar ātma ādeḥ prameyasya tattva parijñānāt iti na pramāṇam asti na na asti arthasya tathā abhāvāt arthaḥ eva ayam tathābhūtaḥ yat ātma ādeḥ prameyasya tattva jñānāt niḥśreyasam adhigamyate yadā hi ayam ātma ādi prameyam viparyayeṇa adhyavasitaḥ bhavati atha saṃsāram na ativartate iti enam ca artham dvitīya sūtre pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ yadi punar pramāṇa ādi padārtha tattva jñānāt niḥśreyasam syāt na mokṣamāṇā mokṣāya ghaṭeran 
NV_1.1.1^33	 na hi kasyacid kvacid ca tattva jñānam na asti iti tasmāt ātma ādi eva prameyam mumukṣuṇā jñeyam iti pṛthak upadeśāt ca yadi ca pramāṇa ādi eva prameyam syāt tasya ca parijñānāt niḥśreyasam bhavet na ātma ādi prameyam pṛthak upadṛṣṭam syāt prameya avadhāraṇa arthāyām ca uttara sūtra prakriyāyām prameyasya vihita tvāt ādyena sūtreṇa akuśalaḥ sūtrakāraḥ syāt tat ca etat uttara sūtreṇa anūdyate iti bhāṣyam heya hāna upāya adhigantavya bhedāt catvāri artha padāni samyak buddhvā niḥśreyasam adhigacchati iti heyam iti heyam duḥkham tasya nirvartakam avidyā tṛṣṇe dharma adharmau iti 
NV_1.1.1^34	 hānam tattva jñānam upāyaḥ śāstram adhigantavyaḥ mokṣaḥ etāni catvāri artha padāni sarvāsu adhyātma vidyāsu sarva ācāryaiḥ varṇyante iti saṃśaya ādi agrahaṇam pṛthak prameya antarbhāvāt iti ced na vidyā prasthāna prabheda jñāpana artha tvāt iti saṃśaya ādayaḥ prameye antarbhavanti iti pṛthak te na vācyāḥ na vidyā prasthāna prabheda jñāpana artha tvāt catasraḥ imāḥ vidyāḥ bhavanti iti tāḥ ca pṛthak prasthānāḥ agni hotra havana ādi prasthānā trayī hala śakaṭa ādi prasthānāḥ vārtā svāmi amātya bheda anuvidhāyinī daṇḍanītiḥ saṃśaya ādi bheda anuvidhāyini ānvīkṣikī 
NV_1.1.1^35	 tasyāḥ saṃśaya ādi prasthānam antareṇa adhyātma vidyā mātram iyam syāt tatas kim syāt adhyātma vidyā mātra tvāt upaniṣad vidyāvat trayyām eva antarbhāvaḥ iti catuṣṭvam nivartate tasmāt pṛthak ucyante iti tatra saṃśayaḥ tāvat vastu svarūpa anavadhāraṇa ātmakaḥ pratyayaḥ anavadhāraṇa ātmakaḥ ca pratyayaḥ ca iti vyāhanyate na vyāghātaḥ svarūpa avadhāraṇāt sva rūpam asya avadhāryate asti me saṃśaya jñānam iti vastu svarūpam tu na anena paricchidyate tat ubhayam anavadhāraṇa ātmakaḥ ca pratyayaḥ ca iti sa katham nyāyasya aṅgam bhavati iti yasmāt na anupalabdhe na nirṇīte arthe nyāyaḥ pravartate 
NV_1.1.1^36	 upalabdhaḥ anirṇītaḥ ca iti vyāghātaḥ yadi upalabdhaḥ na anirṇītaḥ atha anirṇītaḥ na upalabdhaḥ upalabdhaḥ anirṇītaḥ ca iti vyāhatam na asti vyāghātaḥ sāmānyena upalabdhaḥ viśeṣataḥ anirṇītaḥ iti evam api yathā upalabdhaḥ tathā anirṇītaḥ iti vyāghāta anivṛttiḥ na anivṛttiḥ yathā tathā iti vyapadeśāt sarvathā nirṇīte yathā nirṇītaḥ tathā upalabdhaḥ iti anarthakam syāt tasmāt sāmānyatas upalabdhaḥ viśeṣataḥ anirṇītaḥ iti sa ca ayam saṃśayaḥ evambhūtaḥ prameye antarbhavan evam artham pṛthak ucyate atha prayojanam kim punar prayojanam iti 
NV_1.1.1^37	 yena prayuktaḥ pravartate tat prayojanam iti laukikaḥ ayam arthaḥ kena punar prayujyate dharma artha kāma mokṣaie iti kecid vayam tu paśyāmaḥ sukha duḥkha āpti hānibhyām prayujyate iti sukha duḥkha sādhana bhāvāt tu sarve arthāḥ cetanam prayojayanti tat idam prayojanam nyāyasya āśrayaḥ kaḥ āśraya arthaḥ ādhāra arthaḥ tāvat na bhavati upakāraka tvam āśraya arthaḥ tad mūla tvāt parīkṣā vidheḥ prayojane sati parīkṣyate iti prayojanam parīkṣām pravartayati iti kā punar iyam parīkṣā nyāyaḥ kaḥ punar ayam nyāyaḥ pramāṇaiḥ artha parīkṣaṇam nyāyaḥ kim uktam bhavati 
NV_1.1.1^38	 samasta pramāṇa vyāpārāt artha adhigatiḥ nyāyaḥ iti na ekaikam pramāṇam artha pariccheda hetu bhāvena vyavatiṣṭhamānam nyāyaḥ iti ucyate kiṃtu samastāni saḥ ayam vipratipanna puruṣa pratipādaka tvāt paramaḥ nyāyaḥ iti vakṣyāmaḥ pratyakṣa āgama āśritam ca anumānam iti pratyakṣa āgama āśritam iti pratyakṣa āgama avirodhi yadi hi anumāna adhigataḥ arthaḥ pratyakṣa āgamābhyām anusandhīyeta atha sphuṭataraḥ pratyayaḥ bhavati yatra punar etāni pramāṇāni itara itara apratisaṃhitāni vyāvṛttāni prayujyante nyāya viplavaḥ asau lābha pūjā khyāti kāmaiḥ tīrtha pratirūpakaḥ pravādaḥ varṇyate 
NV_1.1.1^39	 yat punar anumānam pratyakṣa āgama viruddham nyāya ābhāsaḥ saḥ iti pratyakṣa viruddham tāvat anuṣṇaḥ agniḥ kṛtaka tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat iti kaḥ punar asya anumānasya virodhaḥ anumāna aviṣaye prayogaḥ na ayam anumānasya viṣaye prayogaḥ na ayam anumānasya viṣayaḥ yasmin viṣaye etat prayujyate sa pratyakṣena apahṛtaḥ iti apare punar aśrāvaṇaḥ śabdaḥ iti pratyakṣa virodham varṇayanti taiḥ tu na pratyakṣasya viṣayaḥ jñātaḥ na anumānasya viṣayaḥ iti kim kāraṇam indriya vṛttīnām atīndriya tvāt śrāvaṇa tvam ca indriya vṛttiḥ sā katham pratyakṣā bhavati 
NV_1.1.1^40	 āgama viruddham śuci nara śiraḥ kapālam prāṇi aṅga tvāt śaṅkha śukti vat iti katham idam āgama viruddham śuci nara śiraḥ kapālam iti bruvatā śuci arthaḥ vācyaḥ kim uktam bhavati śuci iti yadi spraṣṭuḥ pratyavāya abhāvaḥ sa kasya iti vācyam yadi ātmanaḥ iti brūyāt tad āgama anuṣṭhāna tātparyena avasthānāt evam etat atha trayī vidām iti brūyāt trayī abhyupagamāt virodhaḥ iti vācyam śuci nara śiraḥ kapālam iti kaḥ arthaḥ viśeṣa vidhānam etat viśeṣa vidhānam ca śeṣam pratiṣedhati yadi śuci nara śiraḥ kapālam iti kim aśuci iti vācyam 
NV_1.1.1^41	 atha sarvam eva śuci dṛṣṭāntaḥ na asti sarvasya pakṣīkṛta tvāt atha anumāna viruddham kasmāt anumānam na bhavati ekasmin anumāna dvaya samāveśa asambhavān na virodhaḥ na hi anvaya vyatireka sampanne anumāne ekasmin vastuni samāviśataḥ tasmāt na anumāna viruddham pratyakṣa virodhi api tarhi na prāpnoti na na prāpnoti anvaya vyatireka sampannasya pratyakṣena bādhita tvāt atha upamāna viruddham kasmāt na bhavati na upamāna viruddham pūrva pramāṇa virodha anuvidhānāt upamāna virodhaḥ pūrva pramāṇa virodha anuvidhāyini āgama ahita saṃskāra smṛti apekṣam ca sārūpya jñānam upamānam iti vakṣyāmaḥ 
NV_1.1.1^42	 pratyakṣa āgamayoḥ virodhāt uktam tat iti tatra vāda jalpau sa prayojanau iti bhāṣyam tasya kutas utthānam tena anena prayojanena sarve prāṇinaḥ sarvāṇi karmāṇi sarvāḥ ca vidyā vyāptāḥ iti tatra vāda jalpau kiṃprayojanau iti yuktaḥ vicāraḥ iti atas āha tatra vāda jalpau sa prayojanau iti tasmin nyāya ābhāsaḥ iti vitaṇḍā tu parīkṣyate sa prayojanā niṣprayojanā vā iti eke tāvat bruvate niṣprayojanā dūṣaṇa mātra tvāt iti tat ca na evam na dūṣaṇa mātram vitaṇḍā kim tarhi abhyupetya pakṣam yaḥ na sthāpayati sa vaitaṇḍikaḥ iti ucyate 
NV_1.1.1^43	 atha pakṣam api na pratipadyate unmatta vat upekṣaṇīyaḥ bhavati atha para pakṣa pratiṣedha jñāpanam prayojanam iti tādṛś eva etat etasmin api caturvargam ced pratipadyate saḥ asya pakṣaḥ caturvargaḥ bhāṣyaḥ uktaḥ atha na pratipadyate pūrvavat upekṣyaḥ pratipakṣa sthāpanā hīnam ca vākyam vitaṇḍa iti ucyate tasya abhidheyam yadi artham pratipadyate saḥ asya pakṣaḥ atha na pratipadyate pūrvavat doṣaḥ iti uktam prayojanam pratyakṣa viṣayaḥ arthaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ kim uktam bhavati laukika parīkṣakāṇām darśana avighāta hetuḥ iti evam ca ātma ādi vypāptiḥ iti 
NV_1.1.1^44	 darśana avighāta hetutvena dṛṣṭānte varṇyamānaḥ ātma ādi vyāptam bhavati pratyakṣa ādi viṣaya tāyām ca ātmā ādi tyaktam bhavati tatas ca udāharaṇa sūtram vyāhanyeta saḥ ayam dṛṣṭāntaḥ prameyam upalabdhi viṣaya tvāt tasya pṛthak upadeśaḥ nyāyasya tad mūla tvāt sati tasmin anumāna āgamau syātām asati ca na syātām iti pūrva pratyakṣam artham anumimīte pūrva jñātam ca artham parasmāy ācaṣṭe iti nāstikasya ca vyāghātaḥ abhyupagame anabhyupagame vā tat uktam bhāṣyaḥ iti abhyupagama vyavasthā siddhāntaḥ abhyupagamaḥ idam ittham bhūtam ca iti 
NV_1.1.1^45	 idam iti sāmānyatas ittham bhūtam iti viśeṣataḥ tasya vyavasthā idam sāṃkhyeṣu eva idam yogeṣu eva iti sarva tantra siddhāntaḥ tarhi na siddhāntaḥ avyavasthānāt na hi ayam kva cit vyavatiṣṭhate iti tat ca na yaḥ ayam sarvaiḥ abhyupagamaḥ iyam eva vyavasthā tasya prameye antar bhrūtasya pṛthak vacanam vāda ādi viṣaya tvāt siddhānta bhede sati vāda jalpa vitaṇḍāḥ pravartante iti atha avayavāḥ avayavāḥ vākya eka deśāḥ kim punar vākyam pūrva pada smṛti apekṣaḥ antya pada pratyayaḥ smṛti anugrahena pratisandhīyamānaḥ viśeṣa pratipatti hetuḥ vākyam tasya bhāgāḥ eka deśāḥ iti 
NV_1.1.1^46	 te kiyantaḥ yāvadbhiḥ siddhiḥ parisamāpyate iti kā punar iyam siddhiḥ padārthasya tathā tā kā parisamāptiḥ viśeṣa pratyayaḥ te samākhyā śabdaiḥ abhidhīyante pratijña ādayaḥ iti tatra āgamaḥ pratijñā iti na yuktam āgamasya tattva vyavacchedaka tvāt pratijñā arthasya ca pratipādya tvāt āgama adhigatasya pratipādya tvāt āgamaḥ pratijñā iti na doṣaḥ yaḥ eva arthaḥ āgamena adhigataḥ tam eva parasmāy ācaṣṭe iti āgamaḥ pratijñā iti ucyate evam liṅga darśana mātre hetu upacārāt dhetuḥ anumānam iti yat tu dvitīyam liṅga darśanam tad sambandha smṛti vyakti hetu bhāvāt dhetuḥ iti ucyate 
NV_1.1.1^47	 smṛti viṣayasya pratyakṣatas punar upadarśanāt udāharaṇam pratyakṣam yasmāt pūrva anubhūtam artham smarati tam ca smṛti viṣayam udāharaṇa tvena upādatte iti tena pūrva anubhava prasiddham anuvidhīyamānam pratyakṣam iva pratyakṣam iti kaḥ punar upamāna arthaḥ avipratipattiḥ yathā pratyakṣe na vipratipadyate evam udāharaṇe api iti yathā tathā iti upamāna eka deśaḥ upamāna upacārāt upamānam upanayaḥ iti upamānam khalu yathā tathā iti upadeśa upayoge sati pratyakṣa āgama smṛti pūrvakam sārūpya jñānam upamānam iti tatra upamāna eka deśe upamānam iti upacaranti 
NV_1.1.1^48	 sarveṣām eka artha samavāye sāmarthya pradarśanam nigamanam iti kaḥ punar eka artha samavāyaḥ eka vākya adhyāropaḥ kim punar sāmarthyam itaretara sampratyāyita artha apekṣi tvam etat ca vakṣyāmaḥ iti nigamyante anena pratijña ādaye eka arthe sambadhyante iti saḥ ayam paramaḥ nyāyaḥ iti kaḥ punar parama arthaḥ vipratipanna puruṣa pratipādaka tvam ekaika śah pramāṇāni varttamānāni apratipannam puruṣam pratipādayanti vākya bhāva āpannāni punar vipratipannam atas ayam paramaḥ iti kim punar avayavāḥ pramāṇa antaram uta teṣu eva antarbhavanti 
NV_1.1.1^49	 kim ca atas yadi pramāṇa antaram parisaṃkhyānam ayuktam atha teṣu eva antarbhavanti pṛthak abhidhāna ānarthakyam avayavānām iti na pramāṇa antaram iti brūmaḥ saṃhatānām eteṣām vākya paratantrāṇām vipratipanna puruṣa pratipādaka tvena pṛthak upādānam iti te ete avayavāh pramāṇebhyaḥ pṛthak bhavantaḥ vāda jalpa vitaṇḍānām pravṛtti hetavaḥ bhavanti tattva vyavasthāyāḥ ca āśrayāḥ bhavanti iti kaḥ āśraya arthaḥ viśeṣa pratipādaka tvam iti tarkaḥ na pramāṇa saṃgṛhītaḥ na pramāṇa antaram aparicchedaka tvāt pramāṇam paricchedakam na tarkaḥ tasmāt na pramāṇam na pramāṇa antaram api atas eva 
NV_1.1.1^50	 pramāṇa viṣaya vibhāgāt tu pramāṇānām anugrāhakaḥ yaḥ pramāṇānām viṣayaḥ tam vibhajate kaḥ punar vibhāgaḥ yukta ayukta vicāraḥ idam yuktam idam ayuktam iti yat tatra yuktam bhavati tat anujānāti na tu avadhārayati anavadhāraṇāt na pramāṇam bhavati tasya udāharaṇam bhāṣye karma nimittam janma iti katham punar karma nimitta tā janmanaḥ bhedavat tvāt kaḥ punar bhedaḥ sugatiḥ durgatiḥ ca iti sugatau devaḥ manuṣyaḥ iti manuṣya tve pumān itaraḥ iti puṃstve brāhmaṇaḥ anyaḥ iti brāhmaṇa tve paṭu indriyaḥ mṛdu indriyaḥ iti paṭu indriya tāyām ucca abhijanaḥ nīca abhijanaḥ iti 
NV_1.1.1^51	 ucca abhijana tāyām sakalaḥ niṣkalaḥ iti sākalye vidvān mūrkhaḥ iti vidvattāyām samāśvāsinī paritrastaḥ iti samāśvāse vaśī parāyatte iti durgatau api tiryak nārakaḥ iti nāraka tve api kuṭaśālmalyām ayaḥ kumbhyām iti tiryaktāyām gauḥ itaraḥ iti saḥ ayam bhedaḥ anekam avasthitam anityam eka dravyam pratyātma niyatam nimittam antareṇa na yuktaḥ kim kāraṇam pṛthivī ādīnām sarva puruṣa sādhāraṇa tvāt pṛthivī ādi gatasya ca niyama hetoḥ abhāvāt sarvam sarva ātmakam prasajyeta dṛṣṭaḥ ca niyama bhedaḥ tasmāt karma niyāmakam iti 
NV_1.1.1^52	 saḥ ayam itthaṃbhūtaḥ tarkaḥ upalabdhi viṣaya tvāt prameyam nirṇayaḥ tattva jñānam pramāṇānām phalam kadā punar nirṇayaḥ pramāṇānām phalam bhavati yadā vastu antara pariccheda hetu bhāvena na upādīyate tadā phalam yadā tena paricchinatti tadā pramāṇam iti na vyavatiṣṭhate pramāṇa phala bhāvaḥ etat ca vakṣyāmaḥ prameyā ca tulā prāmāṇya vat iti etasmin sūtre nimitta dvaya samāveśāt ekam vastu dvi śabda vācyam iti tau etau tarka nirṇayau lokayātrām vahate iti buddhvā buddhvā lokaḥ pravartamānaḥ tarka nirṇayābhyām heyam jahāti upādeyam ca upādatte 
NV_1.1.1^53	 asya antarbhāvaḥ pramāṇeṣu prameyeṣu vā yadā phalam tadā prameyam yadā anena paricchidyate tadā pramāṇam vādaḥ nānā pravaktṛkaḥ iti siddhānta bheda anuvidhānāt nānā pravaktṛkaḥ iti pratyadhikaraṇa sādhanaḥ anyatara adhikaraṇa nirṇaya avasānaḥ iti adhikaraṇam adhikaraṇam prati pratyadhikaraṇam asya sādhanam kim uktam bhavati ubhābhyām sādhanam vaktavyam iti anyatarasmin adhikaraṇe nirṇayaḥ etat ca vakṣyāmaḥ saḥ ayam kiṃrūpaḥ vādaḥ vākya samūhaḥ iti āha nanu ca pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambhaḥ iti śrūyate 
NV_1.1.1^54	 pramāṇāni ca jñāna ātmakāni indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam jñānam iti evam ādinā prakrameṇa pramāṇāni jñāna ātmakāni iti uktam tarkaḥ ca ūhaḥ sa ca uhaḥ jñāna ātmakaḥ eva tasmāt vākya samūhaḥ vādaḥ iti na yuktam na pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambha śabdasya anyathā vyākhyānāt tat ca sūtram varṇayiṣyantaḥ vakṣyāmaḥ tad viśeṣau jalpa vitaṇḍe iti kaḥ punar viśeṣaḥ aṅga ādhikyam aṅga hāniḥ ca iti chala ja ati nigraha sthāna prayogāt adhikaḥ jalpaḥ sa pratipakṣa sthāpanā hīnaḥ tu vitaṇḍā etāvatā ca viśeṣeṇa kathā mārga bhedaḥ iti viṣaya bhedāt ca bhedaḥ śiṣya ādi viṣayaḥ vādaḥ śiṣyamāṇa viṣaye jalpa vitaṇḍe iti 
NV_1.1.1^55	 anyatama liṅga dharma anuvidhānena pravartamānāḥ ahetavaḥ santaḥ hetu vat ābhāsantaḥ iti hetvābhāsāḥ te ca nigraha sthānam nigraha sthāna prāptānām punar eṣām pṛthak upadeśaḥ vāde codanīya tvāt iti bhāṣyam yasmāt kila ete vāde codyanta atas pṛthak upadiśyante iti na ubhayathā api asambandhān na vāde codanīya tvam pṛthak upadeśa avinābhāvi pṛthak upadeśaḥ vā vāde codanīya tva āvinā abhāvi iti yadi tāvat yaḥ pṛthak upadiśyate sa vāde ca udyate iti sarve padārthāḥ vāde codanīyāḥ prasajyante iti kim kāraṇam sarve pṛthak ukadiṣṭāḥ iti atha vāde codyante ye te pṛthak upadiśyante iti 
NV_1.1.1^56	 tat api na anekāntāt na tāvat nigraha sthānebhyaḥ nyūna adhikayoḥ pṛthak upadeśaḥ atha ca codyete vādaḥ iti tasmāt vāde codanīya tvāt pṛthak upadeśaḥ iti yat kiṃcid etat etat eva tu nyāyyam pṛthak upadeśa prayojanam vidyā prasthāna bheda jñāpana artha tvāt iti atha kasmāt nigraha sthāna bhāva āpannānām hetvābhāsānām pṛthak upadeśaḥ iti pramāṇa sāmānyāt pṛthak upadeśaḥ iti atha kasmāt vāde deśyante pramāṇa sāmānyāt pramāṇāni vāde abhidhīyante pramāṇa sāmānyam ca hetvābhāseṣu asti atas pramāṇa sāmānyāt vāde abhidhīyante iti 
NV_1.1.1^57	 atha vāde nigraha sthānāni kānicid santi kānicid na iti kim ayam padārthānām niyogaḥ atha tathābhūtānām anvākhyānam iti kim ca atas yadi tāvat niyogaḥ evam bhavatā evam mā bhūta iti padārthān niyuñjānaḥ bhavān upekṣaṇīyaḥ atha svarūpataḥ eva avasthitāḥ padārthāḥ tān anujānāti bhavān iti kasmān nigraha sthānāni kānicid vāde bhavanti kānicid na iti vaktavyam na lakṣaṇa paratantra tvāt artha tathā bhāvasya iti brūmaḥ na padārthāḥ vaktuḥ niyogam anuvidhīyante yathā tu bhavanti tathābhūtāḥ eva arthāḥ anvākhyāyante 
NV_1.1.1^58	 saḥ ayam lakṣaṇa paratantram tattvam anvācakṣāṇaḥ nābhi ākhyeyaḥ padārthāḥ bhavatā niyujyante iti vādasya śiṣya ādi viṣaya tvāt na ca śiṣya ādibhiḥ saha vādam kurvāṇena api apratibhā ādi codanā kāryā tāvat asya abhidheyam yāvat asau bodhitaḥ bhavati iti pramāṇa pratirūpaka tvāt tu hetvābhāsānām avarodhaḥ iti kim kāraṇam bhrānteḥ puruṣa dharma tvāt puruṣa dhramaḥ eva ayam bhrāntiḥ iti saḥ ayam bhrāntyā pramāṇam bruvan pramāṇa ābhāsam api brūte atas asya nigrahaḥ iti kaḥ punar śiṣya ācāryayoḥ nigrahaḥ iti vivakṣita artha apratipādaka tvam nyūna adhika apasiddhāntānām vāde katham avatāraḥ pramāṇa sāmānyāt eva 
NV_1.1.1^59	 nyūnasya api pramāṇa sāmānyam adhikasya api pramāṇa sāmānyam asti avayava hīna tā ca avayava adhika tā ca vākyasya bhrāntyā bhavataḥ iti asti avatāraḥ jalpa vitaṇḍayoḥ tu nigraha sthānāni iti vijigīṣuḥ jalpa vitaṇḍābhyām pratyavastheyaḥ tasya yathāsambhavam nigraha sthānāni vaktavyāni iti na upekṣaṇīyaḥ chala ja ati nigraha sthānānām sva vākye parivarjanam para vākye paryanuyogaḥ parijñāna artham eva kevalam chala ja ati nigraha sthānāni svayam na prayojyāni iti jāteḥ tu svayam ca sukaraḥ prayogaḥ iti na vyāghātāt sva vākye parivarjanam sukaraḥ ca prayogaḥ iti vyāhatam 
NV_1.1.1^60	 yadi sukaraḥ prayogaḥ na sva vākye parivarjanam atha sva vākye parivarjanam na sukaraḥ prayogaḥ iti vyāghātaḥ na vyāghātaḥ praśna apākaraṇa artha tvāt svayam ca sukaraḥ prayogaḥ iti kim uktam bhavati pareṇa jātau prayuktāyām praśnikān bravīti jātiḥ anena prayuktā iti te enam pratyanuyuñjīran katham jātiḥ katamā jātiḥ iti ataas jāti abhijñaḥ sukham śaknoti vaktum evam jātiḥ iyam ca jātiḥ iti evam ca sukaraḥ prayogaḥ iti tasmāt ete saṃśaya ādayaḥ padārthāḥ pramāṇe prameye ca antarbhavantaḥ vidyā prasthāna bheda jñāpana artham pṛthak upadiṣṭāḥ iti 
NV_1.1.1^61	 sā iyam ānvīkṣikī nyāya vidyā pramāṇa ādibhiḥ padārthaiḥ vibhajyamānā pradīpaḥ sarva vidyānām bhavati prakāśaka tvāt pradīpaḥ pramāṇa ādi pratipāditam artham itarāḥ vidyāḥ pratipadyante iti kim itarāsu vidyāsu pramāṇa ādīni na santi na santi iti āha katham na santi anadhikārāt na tāḥ vidyāḥ pramāṇa ādi parijñānena adhikriyante iti pramāṇa ādi prakāśite tu arthe tāḥ pravartante iti upāyaḥ sarva karmaṇām iti pramāṇa prakāśitānām karaṇāt upāyaḥ yasmāt pramāṇa prakāśitam artham itarāḥ vidyāḥ kurvanti āśrayaḥ sarva dharmāṇām iti sarva vidyā upakāraka tvāt āśrayaḥ 
NV_1.1.1^62	 sarvāsām vidyānām iyam upakaroti upakāri tvāt āśrayaḥ rāja bhṛtya vat iti tat idam tattva jñānam niḥśreyasa adhigamaḥ ca yathāvidyam veditavyam sarvāsu vidyāsu tattva jñānam asti niḥśreyasa adhigamaḥ ca iti trayyām tāvat kim tattva jñānam kaḥ ca niḥśreyasa adhigamaḥ iti tattva jñānam tāvat agnihotra ādi sādhanānām svāgata ādi parijñānam anupahata ādi parijñānam ca niḥśreyasa adhigamaḥ api svarga prāptiḥ tathā hi atra svargaḥ phalam śrūyate iti atha vārtāyām kim tattva jñānam kaḥ vā niḥśreyasa adhigamaḥ iti bhūmi ādi parijñānam tattva jñānam 
NV_1.1.1^63	 bhūmiḥ kaṇṭaka ādi anupahata iti etat tattva jñānam niḥśreyasam sasya adhigamaḥ tat phalam daṇḍanītyām kim tattva jñānam kaḥ vā niḥśreyasa adhigamaḥ iti sāma dāna daṇḍānām yathākālam yathādeśam yathāśakti viniyogaḥ tattva jñānam niḥśreyasam api pṛthivī jayaḥ iti iha tu adhyātma vidyāyām ātma ādi jñānam tattva jñānam niḥśreyasa adhigamaḥ apavarga prāptiḥ iti yat punar pramāṇa ādi tattva jñānāt niḥśreyasam na tat vivakṣitam mada māna ādi nimitta tvāt vāda ādi parijñānasya nābhi sambandhaḥ niḥśreyasena iti kecid na ca anabhisambaddham pratipādayati iti ayuktam uktam pramāṇa ādi tattva jñānāt niḥśreyasam iti 
NV_1.1.1^64	 na sūtra artha aparijñānāt sūtra artham naḥ na vyajñāsīḥ yatas evam pratyapatthāḥ kaḥ evam sūtra artham varṇayanti pramāṇa ādi padārtha tattva jñānāt niḥśreyasam iti api tu yat parijñānāt niḥśreyasam tat anantara sūtre vakṣyāmaḥ uktam ca ātma ādeḥ khalu prameyasya tattva jñānāt niḥśreyasa adhigamaḥ iti yat ca idam ucyate mada māna ādi nimitta bhūtāḥ vāda ādayaḥ iti etat ca na asati bhāvāt sati ca abhāvāt asati vāda ādi jñāne rāga ādayaḥ sanaka ādīnām bhavanti sati ca tattva vidām na bhavanti tasmāt na nimittam vāda ādi parijñānam rāga ādīnām iti 
NV_1.1.2^1	 na tattva parijñānāt apavargaḥ ubhayathā doṣāt yadi tāvat tattva jñāna anantaram eva apavargaḥ syāt tadvatām avasthānam na syāt tadvatām ca avasthānam dṛṣṭam kutas śāstra sampradāya avicchedāt sampradāyaḥ nāma śiṣya ācārya sambandhasya avicchedena śāstra prāptiḥ yadi tattva jñānāt anantaram apavargaḥ syāt śāstra sampradāyaḥ vicchidyeta yasya yadā tattva jñānam utpannam sa tadā eva apavṛktaḥ iti atha utpanna tattva jñānaḥ avatiṣṭhate na tattva jñānam kāraṇam sati api abhāvāt sati api tattva jñāne yasya abhāvāt na apavṛjyate saḥ anyaḥ arthaḥ iti kāraṇam hi nāma tat bhavati yasmin sati yat bhavati yasmin ca asati yat na bhavati anadhigata artha pūrvaka tvam vā śāstrasya syāt atha tattva jñāna anantaram apavarge vāta putrīyam śāstram prāpnoti na tattva dṛś pūrvakam iti na niḥśreyasasya para apara bhedāt 
NV_1.1.2^2	 yat tāvat aparam niḥśreyasam tat tattva jñāna anantaram eva bhavati tathā ca uktam jīvan eva hi vidvān saṃharṣa āyāsābhyām vipramucyate iti ayam śāstra arthaḥ iti param tu niḥśreyasam tattva jñānāt kramena bhavati krama pratipādana artham ca idam sūtram duḥkha janma pravṛtti doṣa mithyā jñānānām iti evam ādi etat sambandhena eva arthavat padārthaḥ tu vaktavyaḥ tatra ātma ādi apavarga paryantam prameyam jñeyam tasmin mithyājñānam aneka prakārakam vartate kaḥ vṛtti arthaḥ viṣaya arthaḥ tatra ayam bhedaḥ tatra ātmani tāvat na asti iti ātmā tāvat astitvena pramāṇa sāmarthyāt samadhigataḥ astitvena samadhigate na asti iti vijñānam mithyā pratyayaḥ tasya anupapattiḥ sat asatoḥ sārūpya abhāvāt iti ced na pramāṇa gamyatā upapatteḥ na hi satasatī sarūpe yatas asat sāmyāt asat dharma adhyāropeṇa ātmani mithyā pratyayaḥ syāt 
NV_1.1.2^3	 tat ca na evam pramāṇa gamyatā upapatteḥ sat asatoḥ pramāṇa gamya tvam sārūpyam kriyā guṇa vyapadeśaḥ tat rahita tā ca viśeṣaḥ saḥ ayam asat dharmān sati ātmani samāropya viparyeti na asti ātmā iti evam anātmani śarīre ātmā iti kim punar anātmanaḥ śarīra ādeḥ ātmanā sādharmyam yatas etat bhavati anātmani ātmā iti ahaṅkāra viṣaya tvam sāmānyam icchā ādi ādhāra tān ādhāra tā iti viśeṣaḥ yathā eva ātma ahaṅkārasya viṣayaḥ tathā śarīra ādayaḥ api katham punar śarīre ahaṅkāraḥ śarīra vācaka śabda sāmānādhikaraṇyāt śarīre ahaṅkāraḥ gauraḥ aham iti evam ādiḥ icchā ādi ādhāraḥ ātmā na śarīra ādayaḥ iti viśeṣaḥ etat ca upariṣṭāt pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ saḥ ayam ātma dharmān icchā ādīn śarīra ādiṣu adhyāropya viparyeti aham ete iti evam sāmānya viśeṣa dharma parijñāne sati tad viparīta dharma adhyāropena viparyayaḥ sarvatra bhavati iti 
NV_1.1.2^4	 kaḥ punar ayam viparyayaḥ atasmin tat iti pratyayaḥ śeṣam bhāṣye te ime duḥkha ādayaḥ mithyājñāna paryavasānāḥ avicchedena pravartamānāḥ saṃsāraḥ iti kaḥ punar ayam saṃsāraḥ duḥkha ādīnām kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ sa ca anādiḥ pūrva apara kāla bhāvasya aniyamāt na ca śakyam vaktum pūrvam duḥkha ādayaḥ paścāt mithyājñānam pūrvam vā mithyājñānam paścāt duḥkha ādayaḥ iti yadā tu tattva jñānāt mithyājñānam apaiti iti katham apāyaḥ samāne viṣaye tayoḥ virodhāt yasmāt mithyājñānam tattva jñānam ca ekasmin viṣaye virudhyete vastunaḥ dvairūpya asambhavāt na hi ekam vastu dvi rūpam bhavati tasmāt mithyājñānam tattva jñānena nivartyate iti katham punar pūrva utpannam mithyājñānam paścāt bhāvinā tattva jñānena nivartyate mithyājñānasya asahāya tvāt mithyājñānam asahāyam atas nivartate iti 
NV_1.1.2^5	 samyak jñānasya punar viṣayaḥ sahāyībhavati kasmāt tathā tvena avasthānāt tathābhūtaḥ asau viṣayaḥ yathā tatra tattva jñānam iti pramāṇa antara anugrahāt ca āgama anumāna ādi ca pramāṇam tattva jñānasya saha ahībhavati yadā hi ayam āgama anumānyoḥ pratisaṃhitayoḥ viṣayam bhāvayati samāhitaḥ ananya manāḥ cintayati tatas asya vipacyamāne dhyāne viviktāyām dhyāna bhāvanāyām tasmin arthe tattva pratibodhi jñānam pratyakṣam utpadyate iti saḥ ayam āgama anumāna pratyakṣāṇām viṣayam pratipadyamānaḥ tattvam etat iti pratipadyate tattva pratipatteḥ asya mithyājñānam nivartate iti nivṛtte ca mithyājñāne na punar tad viṣayam mithyājñānam utpadyate virodhāt iti uktam kaḥ punar virodhaḥ saha asambhavaḥ mithyājñāna abhāve rāga ādayaḥ apayanti iti kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt eva kāraṇam mithyājñānam kāryā rāga ādayaḥ 
NV_1.1.2^6	 na hi kāraṇe asati kāryam utpattum arhati iti ye tāvat anutpannā rāga ādayaḥ te kāraṇa abhāvāt mā bhūvan ye tu utpannāḥ te katham teṣām api vairāgyāt nivṛttiḥ kim punar vairāgyam bhoga anabhiṣvaṅga lakṣaṇam iti uktam asaktiḥ ca saktim bādhate tat punar vairāgyam katham bhavati tattva jñānāt viṣaya doṣa darśanāt iti doṣa abhāve pravṛtti abhāvaḥ yadā asya samyak jñānavataḥ doṣāḥ apayanti atha doṣa abhāve pravṛttiḥ nivartate kā punar iyam pravṛttiḥ dharma adharmau janma sādhana tvāt na asmin sūtre kriyā pravṛtti śabdena ucyate api tu dharma adharmau tad sādhana bhāvāt janma sādhanam dharma adharmau na pravṛttiḥ kṣaṇika tvāt dharma adharmayoḥ tu pravṛtti śabdaḥ pravṛtti sādhana tvāt iti yau tāvat anāgatau dharma adharmau tayoḥ doṣa abhāvāt abhāvaḥ yuktaḥ yau vartamānau tayoḥ na yuktaḥ 
NV_1.1.2^7	 kim kāraṇam nirdoṣasya api bhāvāt nirdoṣaḥ api ayam avatiṣṭhate dharma adharmayoḥ ca phalam upabhuṅktaḥ iti nānāgatayoḥ sādhana abhāvena iṣṭa tvāt na brūmaḥ yau vartamānau dharma adharmau tau doṣa abhāvāt na bhavataḥ iti api tu yau anāgatau tau kāraṇa abhāvāt na utpadyeta iti vartamānayoḥ punar kārya avasāyāt prakṣayaḥ yau tu vartamānau dharma adharmau tayoḥ yat āvasānikam kāryam tena vyāvṛttiḥ pravṛtti abhāve janma abhāvaḥ atra api dharma adharmayoḥ vyāvṛttayoḥ yat anyat śarīram tat na bhavati na punar vartamānam na bhavati iti atha vartamānasya katham nivṛttiḥ saṃskāra kṣayāt yāvat asya sthiti hetuḥ saṃskāraḥ dharma adharma samākhyātaḥ avatiṣṭhate tāvat tiṣṭhati iti janma abhāve duḥkha abhāvaḥ iti nirāyatanasya anutpatteḥ na hi nirāyatanam duḥkham utpattum arhati iti 
NV_1.1.2^8	 etat ca tat āhuḥ yāvat ātmani dharma adharmau tāvat āyuḥ śarīram indriyāṇi viṣayāḥ ca iti saḥ ayam mithyājñāna ādinā kalāpena sarvatas viyuktaḥ vimuktaḥ iti ucyate tattva jñānam tu khalu mithyājñāna viparyayeṇa vyākhyātam svarūpataḥ tu yathāvyavasthita padārtha adhigatiḥ iti uktam kasmāt punar ayam hātā sukha duḥkhe jahāti na punar sukham ādāya duḥkham jahāti iti viveka hānasya aśakya tvāt viveka hānam aśakyam kartum atas sukham upabhoktu kāmena duḥkham api bhoktavyam duḥkham vā jihāsatā sukham api hātavyam sa viṣa anna vat iti sukham duḥkha anuṣaktam anādeyam iti anuṣaṅgaḥ avinābhāvaḥ yatra ekam tatra itarat iti samāna nimitta tā vā anuṣaṅgaḥ yāni vā sukha sādhanāni tāni eva duḥkha sādhanāni iti samāna ādhāra tā vā anuṣaṅgaḥ yatra sukham tatra duḥkham iti samāna upalabhyatā vā anuṣaṅgaḥ yena sukham upalabhyate tena duḥkham api iti 
NV_1.1.3^1	 trividhā ca asya śāstrasya pravṛttiḥ iti bhāṣyam pravṛtteḥ traividhyam kutas arthasya tathā abhāvāt nāmī padārthāḥ vaktṛā tredhā vyavasthā apyante evam bhavatā iti kim tu arthaḥ eva ayam tathābhūtaḥ yena tredhā bhavati iti nāmadheyena padārtha mātra abhidhānam uddeśaḥ iti ayuktam ghrāṇa ādi sūtra vyāghātāt ghrāṇa rasana cakṣuḥ tvac śrotrāṇi indriyāṇi iti lakṣaṇam uktam na ca idam nāmadheyena uddeśa mātrāt bhidhyate mātra grahaṇa sāmarthyāt aprasaṅgaḥ padārtha abhidhāna mātram iti uktam na ca ghrāṇa ādīnām padārtha abhidhāna mātra tvam kāraka śabda tvāt kāraka śabdāḥ ete ghrāṇa ādinī iti tasmāt na uddeśa prasaṅgaḥ uddiṣṭasya vibhāgaḥ dvedhā bhavati lakṣitasya alakṣitasya ca lakṣitasya chala ādeḥ 
NV_1.1.3^2	 alakṣitasya pramāṇa ādeḥ iti atha uddiṣṭa vibhāga dvāreṇa sūtram pratyakṣa anumāna upamāna śabdāḥ pramāṇāni iti sūtra arthaḥ nigadena eva vyākhyātaḥ uddiṣṭasya vibhāga ānarthakyam vyāghātāt trividhā ca asya śāstrasya pravṛttiḥ iti uktam uddiṣṭa vibhāgaḥ ca na trividhāyām śāstra pravṛttau antarbhavati tasmāt uddiṣṭa vibhāgaḥ na yuktaḥ na uddiṣṭa vibhāgasya uddeśaḥ eva antar bhāvāt uddiṣṭa vibhāgaḥ uddeśaḥ eva antar bhavati kasmāt lakṣaṇa sāmānyāt samānam lakṣaṇam nāmadheyena padārtha abhidhāna mātram uddeśaḥ iti kim punar vibhāgena prayojanam niyamaḥ yadi pratyakṣa anumāna upamāna śabdāḥ pramāṇāni iti vibhāgaḥ na kriyeta niyamaḥ na gamyeta catvāri eva pramāṇāni iti 
NV_1.1.3^3	 lakṣaṇataḥ catuṣṭvā adhigatiḥ iti ced na lakṣaṇasya itaretara vyavaccheda hetu tvāt syāt eṣā buddhiḥ lakṣaṇataḥ pramāṇa catuṣṭvam gamyate iti yasmāt caturṇām lakṣaṇam uktam iti na lakṣaṇasya itaretara vyavaccheda hetu tvāt lakṣaṇam khalu lakṣyam padārtham samāna asamāna jātīyebhyaḥ vyavacchinatti niyamam tu na śaknoti kartum anya artha tvāt anyāsambhavasya tatas anadhigateḥ na hi lakṣaṇataḥ anyāsambhavaḥ adhigamyate tatas caturṇām anabhidhāne caturṇām lakṣaṇa upadeśe syāt saṃśayaḥ kim vidyamānāni na lakṣitāni uta aho avidyamānāni iti tasmāt saṃśaya nivṛtti artham yuktaḥ vibhāga uddeśaḥ iti akṣasya akṣasya prativiṣayam vṛttiḥ pratyakṣam iti 
NV_1.1.3^4	 ayam ca sūtra vivakāyām avyayībhāvaḥ samāsaḥ anyathā tu vastunirdeśaḥ na samāsaḥ samāse hi akṣasya iti ṣaṣṭhī na śrūyeta kaḥ punar atra samāsaḥ prādi samāsaḥ ayam draṣṭavyaḥ pratigatam akṣam pratyakṣam iti yathā upagataḥ gobhiḥ upaguḥ iti evam anumāna ādiṣu draṣṭavyam mitena liṅgena liṅginaḥ arthasya paścāt mānam anumānam iti na yuktam phala abhāvāt etasmin vyākhyāne aphalam anumānam prāpnoti kim kāraṇam arthasya mita tvāt na eṣa doṣaḥ mitena liṅgena arthasya paścāt mānam yatas bhavati iti brūmaḥ bhavatu vā ayam arthaḥ laiṅgikī pratipattiḥ anumānam iti nanu ca phala abhāvaḥ doṣaḥ uktaḥ 
NV_1.1.3^5	 na doṣaḥ hāna upādāna upekṣā buddhīnām phala tvāt sarvam ca pramāṇam sva viṣayam prati bhāva sādhanam pramitiḥ pramāṇam iti viṣaya antaram prati karaṇa sādhanam pramīyate anena iti pramāṇam yadi bhāva sādhanaḥ pramāṇa śabdaḥ kim phalam viṣayasya adhigata tvāt uktam phalam hāna ādi buddhayaḥ iti jñāte tad bhāvāt jñāte khalu arthe trividhā buddhiḥ bhavati heyaḥ vā upādeyaḥ vā upekṣaṇīyaḥ vā iti kecid tu sannikarṣam eva pratyakṣam varṇayanti na tat nyāyam pramāṇa abhāvāt sannikarṣaḥ eva pramāṇam iti na pramāṇam asti ubhayam tu yuktam paricchedaka tvāt ubhayam paricchedakam sannikarṣaḥ jñānam ca ekānta vādinaḥ tu doṣaḥ iti sāmīpyamānam upamānam iti na yuktam upamānasya anyathā vyākhyānāt 
NV_1.1.3^6	 samākhyā sambandha pratipattiḥ upamāna arthaḥ iti uktam idānīm tu ucyate sāmīpyamānam upamānam iti nanu vyāghātaḥ na asti vyāghātaḥ sāmīpyamānena samākhyā sambandha pratipatteḥ iṣṭa tvāt yasmāt ayam upayukta upamānaḥ godarśī āgama pratyaya ahita smṛti pūrvakam gavā sādṛśyam pratyakṣena pratipadya asya gavaya śabdaḥ saṃjñā iti saṃjñā saṃjñi sambandham pratipadyate tasmāt avyāghātaḥ iti śabda viṣayā pratipattiḥ śābdam pramāṇam phalam tat eva kecid tu krame prayojanam varṇayanti ādau pratyakṣa grahaṇam prādhānyāt tad anantaram anumānam tad pūrvaka tvāt tad anantaram upamānam tat sādharmyāt tad anantaram śabdaḥ mahā viṣaya tvāt iti 
NV_1.1.3^7	 tat ca ayuktam iti apare manyante krama abhidhānasya nyāya prāpta tvāt nyāya prāptam krama abhidhānam krama varṇa vṛtti tvāt vācaḥ iti mahā viṣaya tāyām ca śabdasya ādau abhidhāna prasaṅgaḥ iti etat ca ayuktam krama varṇa vṛtti tvāt vācaḥ ayugapad abhidhānam yuktam pūrva apara abhidhāne tu na sādhanam etat tasmāt anyaḥ nyāyaḥ vaktavyaḥ sa ca ayam nyāyaḥ pratyakṣam pūrvam prādhānyāt mahā viṣaya tvāt ādau śabda upadeśaḥ iti na ubhayam mahā viṣayam śabdaḥ pratyakṣam ca katham iti pratyakṣena api sāmānya viśeṣa tadvatām grahaṇam śabdena api iti tatra kim śabdasya ādau upadeśaḥ bhavatu āhosvit pratyakṣasya iti pratyakṣasya iti yuktam kim kāraṇam sarva pramāṇānām pratyakṣa pūrvaka tvāt iti 
NV_1.1.3^8	 kim punar etāni pramāṇāni saṃplavante atha pratiprameyam vyavatiṣṭhante iti ubhayathā darśanam tat ca pramāṇataḥ iti atra eva darśitam sā iyam pramitiḥ pratyakṣa parāḥ iti pratyakṣena adhigate arthe ākāṅkṣā bhāvāt tad parā yathā ayam laukikaḥ amutra agniḥ iti āpta upadeśāt agnim pratyāhita pratyayaḥ tam deśam gacchati pratyāsīdan punar dhūma viśeṣaṇam dhūma aṅga tvena vyavasthitam hutabhujam pratipadyate āsannataraḥ tu adānīm indriya artha sannikarṣa vaśāt agnau agni pratyayam karoti tadā nirākāṅkṣaḥ bhavati tasmāt pradhānam pratyakṣam iti yatra saṃplavaḥ tatra evam yatra punar vyavasthā tatra pradhāna guṇa bhāvaḥ na cintyate iti 
NV_1.1.4^1	 atha idānīm vibhaktānām lakṣaṇa vacanam iti lakṣaṇam ucyate tatra indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam iti evam ādi sūtram sūtra arthaḥ tu samāna asamāna jātīya viśeṣaka tvam atha padānām arthaḥ katham indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam iti indriyeṇa arthasya sannikarṣāt yat utpadyate jñānam tat pratyakṣam iti indriyāṇi punar vakṣyamāṇakāṇi arthāḥ ca sannikarṣaḥ punar ṣoḍhā bhidyate saṃyogaḥ saṃyukta samavāyaḥ saṃyukta samaveta samavāyaḥ samavāyaḥ samaveta samavāyaḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ ca iti tatra cakṣuḥ indriyam rūpavān ghaṭa ādiḥ arthaḥ tena sannikarṣaḥ saṃyogaḥ tayoḥ dravya svabhāva tvāt adravyeṇa tu tad gata rūpa ādinā saṃyukta samavāyaḥ yasmāt cakṣuṣā saṃyukte dravye rūpa ādi vartate iti 
NV_1.1.4^2	 vṛttiḥ ca samavāyaḥ evam rūpa ādi vṛttinā sāmānyena saṃyukta samaveta samavāyaḥ sannikarṣaḥ evam ghrāṇa ādiṣu gandha vat ādi dravyena saṃyogaḥ tad samaveteṣu gandha ādiṣu saṃyukta samavāyaḥ tad vṛttiṣu ca sāmānyeṣu saṃyukta samaveta samavāyaḥ śabde ca samavāyaḥ ayam khalu śabdaḥ saṃyoga vibhāga yoniḥ ādyaḥ tatra katamaḥ śabdaḥ saṃyoga yoniḥ katamaḥ ca vibhāga yoniḥ iti ākāśa guṇa tvāt śabdasya ākāśa vṛttiḥ saṃyogaḥ kāraṇam guṇa karmasu ārabdhavyeṣu sa apekṣaḥ iti sa apekṣaḥ na nirapekṣaḥ iti kim apekṣate bherī ākāśa saṃyogaḥ tāvat śabdasya asamavāyi kāraṇam tasya anugrāhe bherī daṇḍa saṃyogaḥ daṇḍa gata vega apekṣaḥ iti 
NV_1.1.4^3	 yadi punar bherī daṇḍa saṃyogaḥ eva śabdasya kāraṇam syāt vyadhikaraṇaḥ saṃyogaḥ śabda kāraṇam iti sarvatra śabdasya utpatti prasaṅgaḥ vibhāga ja vibhāgāt ca śabdaḥ vaṃśa dala vibhāga anugṛhītāt vaṃśa dala ākāśa vibhāgāt śabdaḥ iti saḥ utpannaḥ śabdaḥ sarva dikkāni śabda antarāṇi karoti tāni api pratyekam śabda antarāṇi tāvat yāvat karṇa śaṣkulī māna ākāśa deśaḥ iti yaḥ karṇa śaṣkulīm ati ākāśa deśe samavaiti sa samavāyāt upalabhyate tad gateṣu ca sāmānyeṣu samaveta samavāyāt iti samavāye ca abhāve ca viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvāt iti saḥ ayam sannikarṣa śabdaḥ saṃyoga samavāya viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva vyāpaka tvāt upāttaḥ iti saḥ ayam sannikarṣaḥ pratyakṣasya kāraṇam bhavati iti lakṣaṇa tvena ucyate 
NV_1.1.4^4	 yadi indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ pratyakṣasya kāraṇa tvāt upadiśyate ati alpam idam ucyate anyāni api pratyakṣasya kāraṇāni bahūni santi tāni api vaktavyāni tat yathā ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ indriya manaḥ saṃyogaḥ viṣaya prakāśa saṃyoga viṣaya stham rūpam viṣaya saṃyogi stham ca mahat tvam aneka dravyavat tvam upalabdhiphalaḥ saṃskāraḥ iti kasmāt tad bhāve bhāvāt tad abhāve ca abhāvāt iti tat yadi kāraṇa bhāvāt indriya artha sannikarṣa grahaṇam etāni api kāraṇa antarāṇi vaktavyāni na vaktavyāni na idam kāraṇa avadhāraṇa artham sūtram api tu samāna asamāna jātīya viśeṣaṇa artham yat pratyakṣasya asādhāraṇam kāraṇam tat abhidhīyate na punar sādhāraṇam kāraṇam nivartyate iti 
NV_1.1.4^5	 indriya manaḥ saṃyogaḥ tarhi asādhāraṇa tvāt upasaṃkhyeyaḥ na hi ayam anumāna ādi jñānānām kāraṇa tvena sambhavati na anena eva tasya ukta tvāt indriya artha sannikarṣa grahaṇena indriya manaḥ saṃyogaḥ uktaḥ veditavyaḥ kim kāraṇam ubhayoḥ asādhāraṇa tvāt na ca yāvat asādhāraṇam kāraṇam sarvam tat vaktavyam iti sūtra arthaḥ api tu anyatareṇa api bhidyate iti anyatara upādānam indriya artha sannikarṣa grahaṇam vā viśeṣaka tvāt yat indriya artha sannikarṣāt upajāyate vijñānam tasya anyatarat viśeṣakam bhavati indriyam arthaḥ vā tad viśeṣakam tena vyapadeśāt yasmāt idam jñānam indriyeṇa vā vyapadiśyate arthena vā rūpa vijñānam iti vā cakṣuḥ vijñānam iti vā 
NV_1.1.4^6	 na punar indriya manaḥ saṃyogena vyapadiśyate na hi bhavati rūpa ālambane vijñāne manaḥ jñānam iti yadā tu ātma manaḥ saṃyogāt mānasyaḥ buddhayaḥ sampravartante tad ātmanā vyapadiśyante manasā ca yat ca asādhāraṇam kāraṇam tat vyapadeśa bhāj bhavati tat yatha rtva ādi kāraṇa sannidhānāt prādurbhavan aṅkuraḥ na ṛtva ādibhiḥ vyapadiśyate api tu asādhāraṇena bījena vyapadiśyate yava aṅkuraḥ iti tathā iha api iti adoṣaḥ indriya manasoḥ saṃyogasya vā agrahaṇam bhede abhedāt yasmāt pratyakṣa jñāna bhedaḥ indriya manaḥ saṃyogaḥ na bhidyate iti yadi abhedāt agrahaṇam indriya artha sannikarṣasya api tarhi agrahaṇam eka indriya grāhyeṣu abhedāt iti prāptam yathā śuklaḥ gauḥ gacchati iti na ukta uttara tvāt 
NV_1.1.4^7	 ukta uttaram etat na idam kāraṇa avadhāraṇa artham sūtram iti anabhyupagamāt ca indriya manaḥ saṃyogasya ca agrahaṇam samāna tvāt kena samāna tvāt iti vācyam ātma manaḥ saṃyogena samāna tvāt kim punar tat vyapadeśa abhāvaḥ iti uktam atīndriya ādhāra tā vā sāmānyam yathā vā ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ atīndriya ādhāraḥ evam indriya manaḥ saṃyogaḥ api iti viṣaya āvṛtti tvam vā yathā vā ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ viṣaya āvṛttiḥ tathā indriya manaḥ saṃyogaḥ api iti manaḥ vṛtti tvam vā yathā vā ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ manaḥ vṛttiḥ evam indriya manaḥ saṃyogaḥ api iti tasmāt indriya manaḥ saṃyogasya ātma manaḥ saṃyoga sāmānyāt anyatara abhidhānena vā caritārtha tvāt anabhidhānam iti indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam iti ayuktam indriyasya aprāpyakāri tvāt 
NV_1.1.4^8	 aprāpya kāriṇī cakṣuḥ śrotre iti eke tatra ca nyāyam bruvate aprāpya kāri cakṣuḥ sa antara grahaṇāt pṛthutara grahaṇāt ca iti sa antarasya arthasya viprakṛṣṭa deśa avasthitasya grahaṇam dṛṣṭam na tu cakṣuṣaḥ tena arthena prāptiḥ asti bhūta viśeṣasya indriya bhāvāt yaḥ eva ayam kṛṣṇasāra lakṣaṇaḥ bhūta viśeṣaḥ sa bāhya bhūta viśeṣa prasāda anugṛhītaḥ tad tṛṣṇā pūrvaka karma apekṣaḥ cakṣuḥ iti ucyate tathā ca uktam rūpa upalabdhi saṃvartakena karmaṇā tat tṛṣṇā pūrvakeṇa cakṣuḥ abhinirvṛttam atas rūpa upalabdheḥ kāraṇam bhavati iti evam śeṣeṣu na ca bhūta viśeṣa anugṛhītasya golakasya prāptiḥ viṣayena asti tasmāt sa antara grahaṇāt aprāpyakārī iti apare tu sāntaraḥ iti grahaṇam hetum varṇayanti 
NV_1.1.4^9	 na hi prāpya kāriṣu ghrāṇa ādiṣu sāntaraḥ iti grahaṇam dṛṣṭam dṛṣṭam tu cakṣuṣi pṛthutara grahaṇāt ca rāṣṭra vanādi rūpam ca mahat upalabhyate na ca akṣṇoḥ tathā pṛthu avabhāsaḥ iti diś deśa vyapadeśāt ca yadi prāpya kāri cakṣuḥ bhavet diś deśa vyapadeśaḥ na syāt na hi prāpya kāriṣu ghrāṇa ādiṣu etat asti iti sannikṛṣṭa viprakṛṣṭayoḥ tulya kāla grahaṇāt ca yat khalu gatimat bhavati tat tām gatim abhindat sannikṛṣṭam āśu prāpnoti viprakṛṣṭam cireṇa śākhā candramasoḥ tulya kāla grahaṇam dṛṣṭam tasmāt aprāpya kārī iti yat tāvat sāntara grahaṇāt iti tat ayuktam vikalpa anupapatteḥ sa antara grahaṇam iti kaḥ arthaḥ 
NV_1.1.4^10	 kim tāvat sāntarasi grahaṇam aprāptasya grahaṇam iti ayam arthaḥ āhosvit saha antareṇa grahaṇam sa antara grahaṇam iti astu tāvat pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ aprāptasya grahaṇam sa antara grahaṇam iti nanu ayam pratijñā arthaḥ eva tatas ca hetu abhāvaḥ kim kāraṇam hetu arthasya pratijñā arthena ākṣipta tvāt etat uktam bhavati aprāpya kāri cakṣuḥ aprāpyagrahaṇāt iti na pratijñā arthāt bhidyate atha brūṣe saha antareṇa grahaṇam iti kim tad antaram nāma yat cakṣuṣā viṣayeṇa saha upalabhyate iti kim ākāśam abhāvaḥ dravya antaram vā yadi ākāśam tat na cakṣuṣaḥ viṣayaḥ na hi ākāśam cakṣu grāhyam arūpa tvāt iti atha rūpavat dravya antara śabda vācyam tasya vyavadhāyaka tvāt tena saha grahaṇam na yuktam atha abhāvaḥ antara śabda vācyaḥ 
NV_1.1.4^11	 sa svatantraḥ cakṣuḥ viṣayaḥ na bhavati iti tena saha upalabdhau anaikāntikam na ca anyā gatiḥ asti tasmāt śūnyam abhidhānam sa antara grahaṇāt iti yaiḥ api vidvasyamānaiḥ sa antara grahaṇāt iti asya sāntaraḥ iti grahaṇam iti etat vyākhyānam kriyate tat api ayuktam sāntaraḥ iti grahaṇasya anya nimitta tvāt anyathā eva sāntaraḥ iti grahaṇam bhavati śarīra avadhi nimitta tvāt śarīram avadhim kṛtvā sāntara nirantare bhavataḥ na punar indriya prāpti aprāpti apekṣe yatra śarīram indriyam ca ubhayam arthena sambadhyate tatra nirantaram iti grahaṇam bhavati yatra punar indriya mātre sambandhaḥ tatra sāntaraḥ iti tasmāt sāntaraḥ iti grahaṇasya anya nimitta tvāt na sa antara grahaṇāt aprāpyakāri tvam sidhyati iti 
NV_1.1.4^12	 yat api pṛthutara grahaṇāt iti tat api ayuktam sambandha mātreṇa mahat aṇvoḥ grahaṇāt sambandha mātrena eva mahati vāṇau vā viṣaya bheda anuvidhāyī pratyayaḥ upajāyate tasmāt acodyam etat api iti yat punar etat uktam diś deśa vyapadeśāt iti tat api śarīra avadhi nimitta tvena pratyuktam yatra indriyam śarīram ca arthena sambadhyate tatra diś deśa vyapadeśaḥ na bhavati dūra antika anuvidhānam vā yatra punar indriyam eva kevalam sambadhyate tatra śarīram avadhim kṛtvā saṃyukta saṃyoga alpīyaḥ tvam tat bhūyaḥ tvam vā apekṣamāṇasya diś deśa pratyayāḥ sannikṛṣṭa viprakṛṣṭa pratyayāḥ ca bhavanti iti yat punar etat śākhā candramasoḥ tulya kāla grahaṇāt iti tat api na anabhyupagamāt 
NV_1.1.4^13	 kaḥ hi svastha ātmā śākhā candramasoḥ tulya kāla grahaṇam pratipadyate kāla bhedasya agrahaṇāt mithyā pratyayaḥ eṣaḥ utpala dala śata vyatibheda vat iti katham punar avagamyate kāla bheda agrahaṇa nimittaḥ eṣa yugapad pratyayaḥ na punar eka kāla grahaṇa nimittaḥ eva iti idam anumānam āvaraṇa anupapatteḥ iti yadi aprāpya kāri cakṣuḥ bhavati na kuḍya kaṭādeḥ āvaraṇasya sāmarthyam asti iti āvaraṇa anupapattiḥ syāt na ca vyavahita artha upalabdhiḥ asti tasmāt na aprāpya kāri iti dūra antika anuvidhānam ca anupalabdhi upalabdhyoḥ na syāt aprāpya cakṣuḥ artham gṛhṇāti iti yat idam arthasya dūre agrahaṇam antike ca grahaṇam ubhayam etat na syāt dṛṣṭam tu tasmāt na aprāpya kāri 
NV_1.1.4^14	 viṣayībhāvāt iti ced tat ca na evam sambandha vyatirekeṇa tu viṣayībhāva anabhyupagamāt atha api idam syāt yaḥ cakṣuṣoḥ viṣayībhavati arthaḥ saḥ upalabhyate yaḥ tu na bhavati na asau upalabhyate iti na ca vyavahitānām dūra avasthitānām vā arthānām cakṣuṣaḥ viṣayībhāvaḥ asti tasmāt na te gṛhyante iti tat ca na evam sambandha vyatirekeṇa viṣayībhāva anabhyupagamāt kaḥ punar sambandha vyatirekeṇa viṣayībhāvaḥ kevalam bhavatām saṃjñā mātram bhidyate na arthaḥ iti mayā ucyate sambandhaḥ iti bhavatā abhidhīyate viṣayībhāvaḥ iti na kaḥ cit viśeṣaḥ iti atha prāpya kāri tve cakṣuṣaḥ kim pramāṇam indriya tvam eva prāpya kāri cakṣuḥ indriya tvāt ghrāṇa ādi vat ghrāṇa ādi indriyam prāpya kāri dṛṣṭam 
NV_1.1.4^15	 tathā ca cakṣuḥ tasmāt prāpya kārī iti atha punar na kim cit api indriyam prāpya kāri pratipadyate tadā sarvāṇi pakṣīkṛtya karaṇa tvāt iti vācyam karaṇam vā asya ādi prāpya kāri dṛṣṭam tathā ca indriyāṇi tasmāt prāpya kārīṇi iti atha punar vaiyātyāt sarvān eva arthān aprāpya kāriṇaḥ pratipadyate tadā katham saḥ api dṛṣṭa sāmarthyānām kāraṇānām sarvatra kārya anutpattyā pratyavastheyaḥ yadi khalu etāni kāraṇāni paraspara prāpti anapekṣāṇi svayam anupajāta śaktikāni kāryam ārabhante iti kasmāt kāryam sarvatra na bhavati iti vaktavyam atas na kāraṇam aprāpya kārī asti iti aneka daṇḍa cakra ādi udāharaṇam lokaḥ iti tasmāt vyavasthitam indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam iti 
NV_1.1.4^16	 atha jñāna grahaṇam kim artham sukha ādi vyudāsa artham indriya artha sannikarṣāt sukha duḥkhe api bhavataḥ tat vyudāsa artham āha jñānam iti tat ca indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam jñānam viṣaya nāmadheyena abhidhīyate iti bhāṣyam tad pratiṣedha artham āha avi apadeśyam iti yat idam anupayukta śabda artha sambandhasya viṣaya bheda anuvidhāyi jñānam tat pratyakṣam kṛta śabda artha sambandhasya api tad utpatti kāle tādṛś eva apare tu avyapadeśyam iti anena anumānam nirākurvanti tat ca na evam kasmāt indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam iti vacanāt na hi anumeyasya indriyeṇa sannikarṣāt anumānam bhavati atas na prasaṅgaḥ anumānaḥ iti grīṣme marīcayaḥ iti bhāṣyam 
NV_1.1.4^17	 tad pratiṣedha artham idam ucyate avyabhicāri iti kim idam vyabhicāri yat atasmin tat iti bhavati kim punar atra vyabhicāri kim arthaḥ āho jñānam iti eke tāvat varṇayanti arthasya vyabhicāraḥ arthaḥ tu tathā na bhavati iti tad vyabhicārāt tad viṣayam jñānam api vyabhicāri iti ucyate iti tat ca na evam kasmāt arthasya tathā abhāvāt yat tat udaka ādi jñānam upajāyate marīciṣu spandamāneṣu na tatra arthaḥ vyabhicarati iti na hi te na marīcayaḥ na vā spandante kim tu jñānam vyabhicarati atasmin tat iti bhāvāt iti na hi tatra udakam asti tān tu marīcīn indriya upaghāta doṣāt indriyeṇa ālocya viparyeti iti jñānasya vyabhicāraḥ na arthasya iti 
NV_1.1.4^18	 dūrāt cakṣuṣā hi artham paśyan na avadhārayati iti bhāṣyam tad vyudāsa artham āha vyavasāya ātmakam iti na saṃśayasya anindriya artha sannikarṣa ja tvāt na hi indriyārtha sannikarṣāt saṃśaya jñānam bhavati api tu mānasaḥ pratyayaḥ saṃśītiḥ saṃśayaḥ iti tat ca na evam saṃśayasya ubhaya nimitta tvāt ubhayam tu saṃśayasya nimittam ātma antaḥkaraṇa saṃyogaḥ indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ ca iti tatra yat indriya artha sannikarṣa anavadhāraṇa pūrvakam manasā anavadhāraṇam tat iha sambadhyate tasya hi indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ kāraṇam iti pūrvam tu na sambadhyate yat ātma antaḥkaraṇa saṃyogāt bhavati iti tasmāt asti viṣayaḥ viśeṣaṇasya iti yuktam uktam vyavasāya ātmakam iti 
NV_1.1.4^19	 indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam iti evam ādi lakṣaṇam ātma ādiṣu sukha ādiṣu ca na asti manasaḥ anindriya tvāt atas avyāpakam etat pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam iti katham punar indriyam manaḥ na bhavati indriya sūtre apaṭhita tvāt paripaṭhitāni ghrāṇa ādīni indriyāṇi na ca teṣu manaḥ paripaṭhitam tasmāt manaḥ na indriyam pṛthak ca vidhānāt na asti manasaḥ indriya tve pramāṇam tatas ca na indriyam manaḥ iti na ca evam pratyakṣāḥ sukha ādayaḥ bhaviṣyanti iti pratyakṣāḥ ca ete na anumānikā liṅga abhāvāt na hi liṅgam antareṇa anumeyaḥ arthaḥ gamyate na api anyat pramāṇam pratipādakam sukha ādīnām na ca teṣām aprameya tvam na ca anyā gatiḥ asti tasmāt kartavyam sukha ādīnām pratyakṣeṇa grahaṇa upasaṃkhyānam iti 
NV_1.1.4^20	 kaḥ ca evam āha na pratyakṣā sukha ādayaḥ iti indriya artha sannikarṣa janya pratyakṣa vādi āha na eṣa doṣaḥ manasaḥ indriya tvāt indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam sukha ādi jñānam iti yat tu sūtre anabhidhānam tat vaidharmyāt vaidharmyam sarva viṣaya tva asarva viṣaya tve sarva viṣayam manaḥ asarva viṣayāṇi indriyāṇi sarva viṣayam tu manasaḥ smṛti kāraṇa saṃyoga ādhāra tvāt ātma vat sukha grāhaka saṃyoga ādhāra tvāt samasta indriya adhiṣṭhātṛ tvāt ca ātma vat bhautika abhautika tvam tu na virodhāt na hi bhautikam manaḥ na api abhautikam iti kārya dharmau etau bhautika tvam abhautika tvam ca na ca kāryam manaḥ tasmāt na bhautikam na api abhautikam iti śrotre ca asambhavaḥ 
NV_1.1.4^21	 yadi bhautikā bhautika tva lakṣaṇāt vaidharmyāt aparipāṭhaḥ sūtre manasaḥ śrotram api tarhi na paṭhitavyam na hi śrotram bhautikam na ca api abhautikam iti sva arthe pratyaya ādhānam iti ced na pratyaya vaiyarthyāt syāt eṣā buddhiḥ svārthikaḥ eṣa pratyayaḥ bhūtam eva bhautikam iti tat ca na pratyaya vaiyarthyāt na hi bhautikam iti anena ākāśe kaḥ cit tad hita arthaḥ janyate tasmāt vyāhatam etat sva arthe pratyaya vidhānam iti yat punar etat pṛthak abhidhānam na asti iti na na asti ayugapad jñāna upapatteḥ iti yugapad jñāna anutpattiḥ manasaḥ liṅgam iti uktam tena ca pratipāditam etat manasaḥ karaṇa tvam iti sa guṇānām indriya bhāvaḥ vaidharmyam iti etat api na yuktam śrotra an abhidhāna prasaṅgāt eva 
NV_1.1.4^22	 tasmāt sarva asarva viṣaya tvam vaidharmyam iti etat eva ca jyāyaḥ tantra antara samācārāt ca manaḥ indriyam iti tantra antareṣu manaḥ indriyam iti paṭhyate tat ca iha na pratiṣiddham apratiṣedhāt upāttam tat iti na śeṣa abhidhāna vaiyarthya adoṣāt śeṣāṇi api indriyāṇi taiḥ paripaṭhitāni tasmāt tāni api na vaktavyāni yadi apratiṣedhāt upādānam bhavati iti na tantra yukti anavabodhāt na bhavatā tantra yuktiḥ parijñāyate para matam apratiṣiddham anumatam iti hi tantra yuktiḥ na ca yasya sva pakṣa parigrahaḥ na asti tasya sva matam para matam vā vidyate bhavatā ca para mata anurodhena sarvam sva matam nivāryate iti tad nivāraṇāt sva matam para matam iti etat eva na syāt 
NV_1.1.4^23	 tasmāt asti manaḥ indriyam ca iti tat upapannam indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam sukha ādiṣu jñānam iti vyāpakam lakṣaṇam samastam asamastam ca iti sandehaḥ kim idam pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam samastam āho asamastam iti sandehaḥ kutas ubhayathā darśanāt samastam lakṣaṇam bhavati vyastam ca icchā dveṣa prayatna sukha duḥkha jñānāni ātmanaḥ liṅgam iti vyasta lakṣaṇam ekaśas pratipādaka tvāt tathā samāna aneka dharma upapatteḥ iti evam ādi ca vyastam samastam punar vacana vighātaḥ artha vikalpa upapattyā chalam samastena anena chalam lakṣyate prasiddha sādharmyāt sādhya sādhanam upamānam iti ca lakṣaṇam ca idam atas sandehaḥ kim samastam uta asamastam iti samastam iti āha 
NV_1.1.4^24	 yasmāt ekaśas anumāna sukha śabda viparyaya saṃśaya jñānāni nivartante iti yadi indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam iti ādi ekaśas padam abhidhīyate yaḥ yaḥ ekaikena padena arthaḥ saṅgṛhītaḥ sa sa pratyakṣaḥ syāt iti tena pūrva uktānām anumāna ādīnām pratyakṣa tva prasaṅgaḥ syāt iti evam dvayoḥ padayoḥ upādāne pada dvayena upāttasya pratyakṣa tva prasaṅgaḥ evam trayāṇām padānām upādāne taiḥ upāttasya pratyakṣa tva prasaṅgaḥ evam caturṇām padānām upādāne taiḥ upāttasya pratyakṣa tva prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt eka dvi tri catuṣpada paryudāsāt pañca pada parigraheṇa triṃśat koṭīḥ vyudasya samastam lakṣaṇam iti ucyate tatra eka pada parigraheṇa tāvat pañca koṭayaḥ dvipada parigraheṇa daśa 
NV_1.1.4^25	 tripada parigraheṇa api daśa eva catuṣpada parigraheṇa pañca ekatriṃśattamī punar samasta parigraheṇa upāttā iti kasmāt viśeṣa vidhi pratiṣedhayoḥ śeṣa pratiṣedha vidhi abhyanujñā viṣaya tvāt ayam khalu viśeṣa vidhiḥ pravartamānaḥ śeṣam pratiṣedhayati yathā dakṣiṇena akṣṇā paśyati iti viśeṣa pratiṣedhaḥ ca śeṣa abhyanujñā viṣayaḥ bhavati yathā vāmena akṣṇā na paśyāmi iti tathā iha api eka deśa abhyupagame śeṣa pratiṣedhaḥ śeṣa vidhānam vā gamyate iti vyavasthitam pratyakṣam iti apare punar varṇayanti tatas arthāt vijñānam pratyakṣam iti tat na tatas arthāt iti yasya arthasya yat vijñānam vyapadiśyate yadi tatas eva tat bhavati na artha antarāt tat pratyakṣam etena anumāna ādi jñānam apakṣiptam bhavati 
NV_1.1.4^26	 na hi tatas eva tat bhavati kim tarhi tatas ca anyatas ca tat bhavati atra tāvat artha grahaṇam na kartavyam tatas vijñānam iti ucyamāne gamyate eva tad arthāt iti avadhāraṇa arthaḥ artha śabdaḥ iti ced syāt matiḥ eṣā avadhāraṇa arthaḥ artha śabdaḥ bhaviṣyati iti yat uktam bhavati tatas eva iti tat uktam bhavati tatas arthāt iti tat na yuktam eka padasya api avadhāraṇa arthasya dṛṣṭa tvāt abbhakṣaḥ iti yathā etena eva anumāna ādi vyudāsaḥ api pratyuktaḥ yat punar etat saṃvṛti jñānam anena apakṣiptam iti tat etat na budhyāmahe katham tat apakṣiptam iti yadi brūṣe rūpa ādibhyaḥ utpannam jñānam ghaṭasya vyapadiśyate iti atas na tatas bhaviṣyati iti apakṣiptam tat na yuktam 
NV_1.1.4^27	 na hi rūpa ādibhyaḥ utpannam vijñānam ghaṭasya vyapadiśyate rūpa ādibhyaḥ utpannam rūpa ādīnām ghaṭāt vijñānam ghaṭasya iti na prasaṅgaḥ atha api ayam manorathaḥ na rūpa ādi vyatiriktāḥ ghaṭa ādayaḥ iti manaḥ modaka upayoga mātram etat yathā tu tad vyatiriktā ghaṭa ādayaḥ tathā vakṣyāmaḥ sarvam ca sva viṣayāt vijñānam bhavati iti tatas grahaṇam anarthakam iti nanu ca mithyājñānam atasmāt api bhavati na hi atasmāt tat bhavati iti kim tarhi atasmin tat bhavati iti na bhavatā mithyājñānam api vyajñāyi tatas grahaṇam artha grahaṇam ca antareṇa vijñāna mātram avaśiṣyate tathā ca na lakṣaṇam uktam syāt sarvam ca jñānam pratyakṣam syāt 
NV_1.1.4^28	 yadi api etat sūtram yathāśruti bhavati tathā api grāhya grāhaka jñānayoḥ ayugapad bhāvāt jñānam apratyakṣam syāt nāśa utpādau samam iti ced tat ca na udāharaṇa abhāvāt na hi samam nāśa utpāde kim cit udāharaṇam asti vinaṣṭaḥ ca arthaḥ pratyakṣaḥ iti syāt tulyam iti ced syāt matiḥ bhavatām yugapad ava sthāne kim udāharaṇam iti tat ca na evam ukta uttara tvāt ukta uttaram etat sphāṭika ādi sūtraḥ iti apare tu manyante pratyakṣam kalpanā apoḍham iti atha kā iyam kalpanā nāma jāti ādi yojanā yat kila na nāmnā abhidhīyate na ca jāti ādibhiḥ vyapadiśyate viṣaya svarūpa bheda anuvidhāyi paricchedakam ātma saṃvedyam tat pratyakṣam iti te idam praṣṭavyāḥ atha pratyakṣa śabdena kaḥ arthaḥ abhidhīyate iti 
NV_1.1.4^29	 yadi pratyakṣam katham avācyam atha na pratyakṣam avācakaḥ tarhi pratyakṣa śabdaḥ atha pratyakṣa śabdena sāmānyam ucyate iti etat api sāmānyam kim pratyakṣa vyatirekī āhosvit avyatirekī iti yadi pratyakṣa vyatireki na pratyakṣam uktam atha avyatireki katham na uktam kalpanā apoḍha śabdena api yadi pratyakṣam ucyate tada vyāghātaḥ atha na ucyate tathā api kalpanā poḍha śabda uccāraṇam vyartham pratyakṣam kalpanā apoḍham iti ca vākyam atha asya vākyasya kaḥ arthaḥ yadi pratyakṣam vyāghātaḥ katham pratyakṣam kalpanā apoḍham iti ca anena vākyena abhidhīyate na ca abhidheyam iti kaḥ anyaḥ bhadantāt vaktum arhati 
NV_1.1.4^30	 atha na pratyakṣam asya arthaḥ varṇa uccāraṇa mātram tarhi etat vākyam pratyakṣam kalpanā apoḍham iti anitya ādi śabda viṣaya tvāt ca na sarvathā avācyam anityam pratyakṣam duḥkham śūnyam anātmakam ca pratyakṣam eṣām ced śabdānām viṣaya tām upayāti katham avācyam atha na upaiti na sarvam saṃskṛtam anityam iti etat tathāgatena ākhyātavyam atha svarūpataḥ na vyapadeśyam iti ayam kalpanā apoḍha śabda arthaḥ sarve arthāḥ tarhi pratyakṣāḥ prāpnuvanti kim kāraṇam na hi kaḥ cit su śikṣitaḥ api padārthānām svarūpam nirdeṣṭum śaknoti asāmayika tvāt sarvasya ca vastunaḥ dvau ākārau sāmānya ākāraḥ viśeṣa ākāraḥ ca tatra vastu sāmānyena eva ākāreṇa abhidhīyate na viśeṣa ākāreṇa na ca tathā anabhidhānāt na uktam bhavati 
NV_1.1.4^31	 na hi manuṣya śabdasya brāhmaṇaḥ na vācyaḥ ye tu tasya asādhāraṇa dharmāḥ puruṣa antara vyāvṛtta pratyaya hetavaḥ na taiḥ saha abhidhīyate na ca taiḥ saha anabhidhānāt na uktaḥ bhavati evam pratyakṣam api sāmānya viśeṣa ākāra vat tasya viśeṣa ākāreṇa na abhidhānam sāmānya ākāreṇa tu abhidhānam eva yadi ca viśeṣa ākāreṇa anabhidhānam yat tat lakṣaṇam pratyakṣasya na kevalam pratyakṣasya trailokyasya etat lakṣaṇam iti evam ca pratyakṣasya lakṣaṇam na uktam syāt atha kalpanā apoḍha śabdena pratyakṣasya svarūpam abhidhīyate evam api anivṛttaḥ vyāghātaḥ svarūpam ca anabhidheyam anena ca śabdena ucyate iti atha anena śabdena na eva kim cit abhidhīyate kim asya śabdasya uccāraṇa sāmarthyam pratyakṣam kalpanā apoḍham iti 
NV_1.1.4^32	 apratipādaka tvāt mūka svapna sadṛśam etat evam yathā yathā idam lakṣaṇam vicāryate tathā tathā nyāyam na sahate iti sat samprayoge puruṣasya indriyāṇām buddhi janma tat pratyakṣam iti etat api saṃśaya ādi utpatti nimitta tvāt alakṣaṇam iti tathā ca uktam pratyakṣa sūtram varṇayadbhiḥ iti etena pratyakṣam indriya artha sannikarṣa manaḥ prakāśa viśeṣeṣu satsu iti pratyuktam tathā śrotra ādi vṛttiḥ iti kim kāraṇam pañca pada parigraheṇa pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam uktam yatra anyatama pada parigrahaḥ na asti tat pratyakṣa ābhāsam iti evam anena nyāyena yāni api anuktāni lakṣaṇāni tāni etasmāt lakṣaṇāt na bhidyamānāni na lakṣaṇāni iti vyākhyātam pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam iti 
NV_1.1.5^1	 atha tad pūrvakam trividham anumānam iti atha iti ānantarye anumāna viśeṣaṇa artham sūtram tad pūrvakam anumānam iti anena samāna asamāna jātīyebhyaḥ anumānam vyavacchidyate iti tāni te tat pūrvam yasya tat idam tat pūrvakam yadā tāni iti vigrahaḥ tadā samasta pramāṇa abhisambandhāt sarva pramāṇa pūrvaka tvam anumānasya varṇitam bhavati pāramparyeṇa punar tat pratyakṣam eva vyavatiṣṭhate iti pratyakṣa pūrvaka tvam uktam bhavati yadā api vigrahaḥ te dve pūrve yasya iti te dve pratyakṣe pūrve yasya pratyakṣasya tat idam tat pūrvakam pratyakṣam iti katare dve pratyakṣe liṅga liṅgi sambandha darśanam ādyam pratyakṣam liṅga darśanam ca dvitīyam bubhutsau atas dvitīyāt liṅga darśanāt saṃskāra abhivyakti anantara kālam smṛtiḥ smṛti anantaram ca punar liṅga darśana mayam dhūmaḥ iti 
NV_1.1.5^2	 tat idam antimam pratyakṣam pūrvābhyām pratyakṣābhyām smṛtyā ca anugṛhyamāṇam liṅga parāmarśa rūpam anumānam bhavati kaḥ punar anumāna arthaḥ anumīyate anena iti karaṇa arthaḥ kim punar asya phalam agni viṣayā pratipattiḥ iti katham punar anya viṣayam karaṇam anya viṣayām kriyām karoti na hi śāli ādi viṣayasya musala ādeḥ karaṇasya śyāmākeṣu abhihatiḥ bhavati na aniyamāt iti eke yat viṣayam karaṇam tat viṣayā kriyā iti na niyamaḥ asti dṛṣṭā hi vṛkṣa ādi viṣayasya chedanasya avayaveṣu kriyā vṛkṣaḥ chidyate avayaveṣu cchidā bhavati kva cit punar yat viṣayam karaṇam tat viṣayā eva kriyā yathā taṇḍulāḥ pacyante pākaḥ teṣu eva kva cit punar ātmā eva bhavati kartā karaṇam ca 
NV_1.1.5^3	 kriyā ca tasya eva tat yathā vṛkṣaḥ tiṣṭhati iti kim uktam bhavati vṛkṣaḥ sva ātmanā tiṣṭhati iti kim uktam bhavati ātmanā iti yasmāt ayam sva sthitau kāraka antaraṇ na prayuṅkte iti evam anya viṣayasya karaṇasya anya viṣayā kriyā iti kva cit punar yat viṣayam pramāṇam tat viṣayā eva kriyā yadā saḥ eva arthaḥ pramīyate iti kim punar tasya pramīyate pramita tvāt pramīyate heya tvena upādeya tvena upekṣaṇīya tvena vā avagamyate iti tat na pramāṇa phalayoḥ viṣaya bheda anabhyupagamāt yadā punar tat pūrvam yasya tat idam tat pūrvakam iti tadā bhedasya avivakṣita tvāt liṅga liṅgi sambandha darśana anantaram liṅga darśana sambandha smṛtibhiḥ liṅga parāmarśaḥ viśiṣyate tasya tad pūrvaka tvāt kim punar taiḥ anumīyate śeṣaḥ arthaḥ iti 
NV_1.1.5^4	 anumānam iti atra kim kārakam bhāvaḥ karaṇam vā yadā bhāvaḥ tadā hāna ādi buddhayaḥ phalam yadā karaṇam tadā śeṣa vastu paricchedaḥ phalam iti liṅga liṅgi sambandha smṛtiḥ liṅga darśanam vā iti sandehaḥ eke tāvat varṇayanti liṅga liṅgi sambandha smṛtiḥ anumānam itaraiḥ liṅga liṅgi sambandha darśana ādibhiḥ anugṛhyamāṇāḥ apare punar manyante liṅga parāmarśaḥ anumānam itaraiḥ anugṛhyamāṇaḥ iti vayam tu paśyāmaḥ sarvam anumānam anumiteḥ tat na antarīyaka tvāt pradhāna upasarjana bhāva vivakṣāyām tu liṅgaparāmarśaḥ iti nyāyam kaḥ punar atra nyāyaḥ ānantarya pratipattiḥ yasmāt liṅga parāmarśāt anantaram śeṣa artha pratipattiḥ iti tasmāt liṅga parāmarśaḥ nyāyaḥ iti smṛtiḥ na pradhānam kim kāraṇam smṛti anantaram apratipatteḥ 
NV_1.1.5^5	 na hi bhavati yatra dhūmam adrākṣam tatra agnim adrākṣam iti etasyāḥ ca smṛteḥ anantaram tasmāt agniḥ iti śeṣa artha grahaḥ iti yuktam vaktum tasmāt smṛti anugṛhyamāṇaḥ liṅga parāmarśaḥ abhīṣṭa artha pratipādakaḥ bhavati iti evam ca upanayasya arthavat tā yadi ca ayam smṛti anugṛhītaḥ liṅga parāmarśaḥ anumānam bhavati evam sati upanayaḥ arthavān iti evam ca sati vākya aṅga tvam upanayasya uktam bhavati tasmāt vyavasthitam etat tad pūrvakam anumānam iti yadi pratyakṣa pūrvakam anumānam saṃskāre nirṇaye ca prasaṅgaḥ iti pratyakṣa pūrvakaḥ bhāvanā ākhyaḥ smṛti hetuḥ saṃskāraḥ nirṇayaḥ ca pratyakṣa phala tvāt anumānam prasajyate iti na eṣa doṣaḥ vijñānasya adhikṛta tvāt indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam jñānam iti jñāna adhikāraḥ vartate iti tena na saṃskāre ati prasaṅgaḥ 
NV_1.1.5^6	 nirṇayaḥ tu ubhayathā kadā cit pramāṇam kadā cit phalam sva viṣaya paricchedaka tvāt phalam śeṣa paricchedaka tvāt pramāṇam iti trividham iti anvayavyatirekī anvaī vyatirekī ca iti tatra anvyavyatirekī vivakṣita tad jātīya upapattau vipakṣa āvṛttiḥ yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ sāmānya viśeṣavat tve sati asmad ādi bāhya karaṇa pratyakṣa tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat iti anvayī vivakṣita tad jātīya vṛtti tve sati vipakṣa hīnaḥ yathā sarva anitya tva vādinām anityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tvāt iti asya hi vipakṣaḥ na asti vyatirekī vivakṣita vyāpi tve sati sa pakṣa abhāve sati vipakṣa āvṛttiḥ yathā na idam jīvat śarīram nirātmakam aprāṇa ādimattva prasaṅgāt iti atha vā trividham iti pūrvavat śeṣavat sāmānyatodṛṣṭam ca iti pūrvam sādhyam tat vyāptyā yasya asti iti tat pūrvavat 
NV_1.1.5^7	 sādhyasa jātīyaḥ śeṣaḥ sa yasya asti tat śeṣavat pūrvavat nāma sādhya vyāpakam śeṣavat iti tad samāne asti sāmānyatas ca adṛṣṭam caśabdāt pratyakṣa āgama aviruddham ca iti evam catur lakṣaṇam pañca lakṣaṇam anumānam iti atha vā trividham iti pūrvavat śeṣavat sāmānyatodṛṣṭam ca iti tatra pūrvavat nāma yatra kāraṇena kāryam anumīyate iti bhāṣyam kim punar idam uktam bhavati kāraṇena kāryam anumīyate iti yadi tāvat ayam arthaḥ kāraṇa darśanāt kārya astitvam pratipadyate iti tat na asti na hi kāraṇam gṛhītvā kaḥ cit svastha ātmā kāryam pratipadyate iti tathā ca vyāhatam bhavati iti atha punar evam anumīyate yatra kāraṇam tatra kāryam iti etat api na asti kārya kāraṇayoḥ bhinna deśa tvāt 
NV_1.1.5^8	 tantavaḥ sva avayaveṣu aṃśuṣu paṭaḥ tantuṣu iti kāraṇa darśanāt ca kāryam anumīyate iti bruvāṇaḥ anumāna mudrām bhinatti kā punar iyam anumāna mudrā na anupalabdhe na nirṇīte nyāyaḥ pravartate iti yadi kāraṇa darśanāt kāryam anumīyate anupalabdhe arthe nyāyaḥ pravartate iti syāt tathā ca vyāhatam syāt na anabhyupagamāt kaḥ evam āha kāraṇa darśanāt kārya astitvam pratipadyate iti kaḥ vā bravīti yatra kāraṇam tatra kāryam iti kāryam tu kāraṇa viśeṣaṇa tvena upayuktam guṇa bhūtam anumīyate iti sūtra arthaḥ tathā ca na mudrā bhedaḥ iti evam śeṣavata ādiṣu api vyākhyeyam atra api kāraṇam kāryasya aṅga bhūtam anumīyate iti katham punar śeṣa śabdena kāryam ucyate dvayoḥ anumāna bhāvena upakṣiptayoḥ kāraṇasya upayogāt anupayuktam kāryam iti 
NV_1.1.5^9	 kāryam śeṣa śabda vācyam udāharaṇam megha unnatyā bhaviṣyati vṛṣṭiḥ iti kāraṇena kārya anumānam katham punar asya prayogaḥ vṛṣṭimantaḥ ete meghāḥ gambhīra dhvānavat tve sati bahula balākāvat tve saty acira prabhāva tve ca sati unnatattvāt tat anya vṛṣṭimat megha vat iti nadyāḥ pūrṇa tvam śeṣavat udāharaṇam katham punar nadī pūraḥ nadyām vartamānaḥ uparivṛṣṭimantam deśam anumāpayati vyadhikaraṇa tvāt na upari vṛṣṭimat deśa anumānam nadī pūraḥ kim tarhi nadyā eva upari vṛṣṭimat deśa sambandhi tvam anumīyate nadī dharmeṇa eva uparivṛṣṭimat deśa sambandhinī nadī śīghratara srotaḥ tve sati phala kāṣṭha ādi vahanavat tve ca sati pūrṇa tvāt tad anya vṛṣṭimat pūrva nadī vat iti bhaviṣyati bhūtā vā iti kālasya avivakṣita tvāt yaḥ kaḥ cit kāle upādeyaḥ iti 
NV_1.1.5^10	 sāmānyatodṛṣṭam nāma akārya kāraṇa bhūtena yatra avinābhāvinā viśeṣaṇena viśeṣyamāṇaḥ dharmī gamyate tat sāmānyatodṛṣṭam yathā balākayā salila anumānam katham punar balākayā salila anumānam yāvanasya deśaḥ balākayā ajahat vṛtti tvena prasiddhaḥ bhavati tāvantam antarbhāvya vṛkṣa ādikam artham pakṣīkṛtya balākāvat tvena sādhayati apare punar manyante sāmānyatodṛṣṭam ādityasya gati anumānam iti tat tu na buddhyāmahe katham anumīyate iti yadi tāvat gatimān ādityaḥ iti anumīyate tat kena pratipadyate na hi āditya gateḥ kim cit sambaddham liṅgam asti na ca asambaddhaḥ arthaḥ anumātum śakyate tathā ca sarvam sarveṇa anumīyeta atha api deśa antara prāptiḥ liṅgam iti tat na adṛṣṭa tvāt na hi savituḥ kaḥ cit deśa antara prāptim paśyati 
NV_1.1.5^11	 deśa antaram khalu ākāśa deśaḥ vā diś deśaḥ vā bhavet ubhayam ca apratyakṣam na ca anyā gatiḥ asti tasmat deśa antara prāpti darśanam ayuktam sarvatra khalu ayam ādityasya maṇḍalam eva kevalam upalabhate na ca vastu mātra darśanāt anumānam yuktam api ca kena cit prakārena ādityasya gatiḥ śakyāḥ draṣṭum upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tvāt na punar deśa antara prāptiḥ nityam atīndriya tvāt na hi kadā cit api pratyakṣa apratyakṣa vṛttiḥ saṃyogaḥ bhavati pratyakṣaḥ atha devadattasya deśa antara prāpti darśanena ādityasya gati anumānam sāmānyatodṛṣṭam iti manyase na kevalam ādityasya sarva arthānām gati anumānam etat tarhi bhavān api gacchati iti evam kasmāt na anumimīṣe na eva idam āditya gati anumānam sākṣāt kim tarhi
