NV_1.1.41^6	 yadā tu ekaḥ avatiṣṭhate ekaḥ nivartate tadā nirṇayaḥ iti atas saṃhatya ubhau pakṣa pratipakṣau nirṇaya hetuḥ iti etasmin viṣaye kadā nirṇayaḥ bhavati kim prathamaḥ uta dvitīyaḥ uta tṛtīyaḥ iti sarvatra bhavati arthasya tathā abhāvāt atha vā tṛtīyaḥ iti yuktam katham iti ekaḥ tāvat sādhanena pakṣam avasthāpayati dvitīyaḥ sādhanam buddhvā nivartate sādhana ābhāsam vā buddhvā sādhana doṣa udvibhāvayiṣayā pravartate tam nivartya sādhanam bravīti prathamaḥ idānīm niścitam sādhanam iti yadi buddhyate na pravartate 
NV_1.1.41^7	 atha dūṣaṇa ābhāsam iti buddhyate tattva udbhāvanā artham pravartate tad nivṛttyā ca dvitīya pakṣa sādhanam api nivartate kim kāraṇam prathama pakṣa sādhanasya nirdoṣa tvāt nirdoṣe ca prathama pakṣa sādhane na dvitīyasya avakāśaḥ iti nivartate dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ iti yaḥ atra avatiṣṭhate tasmin nirṇayaḥ sa ca nirṇayaḥ sambhava asambhavābhyām pakṣa pratipakṣayoḥ saṃhatya kriyate iti nirṇayaḥ anumānam iti ke cit ke cit varṇayanti nirṇayaḥ anumānam eva na padārtha antaram iti na liṅga liṅgi sambandha smṛti apekṣa tvāt anumānasya nirṇaye ca tad abhāvaḥ pramāṇa phala tvāt 
NV_1.1.41^8	 pramāṇam anumānam pramāṇa phalam tu nirṇayaḥ nirṇayaḥ sva viṣayaḥ eva anumānam tu sva viṣaye anyatra ca yathā dhūma darśanam dhūma paricchede na anumānam api tu nirṇayaḥ yadā ca paricchinatti dhūmena tadā anumīyate anena iti anumānam agni paricchedaḥ phalam yadā tu karaṇa sādhanam āśritya ucyata anumānam nirṇayaḥ iti tadā abhyanujñayā vartitavyam yadā tu karaṇa sādhanam āśritya ucyata anumānam nirṇayaḥ iti tadā pratiṣedhaḥ vacanīyaḥ kārya kāraṇayoḥ bhedāt kāraṇam anumānam kāryaḥ nirṇayaḥ tasmāt na anumānam nirṇayaḥ iti 
NV_1.2.1^1	 tisraḥ kathāḥ bhavanti vādaḥ jalpaḥ vitaṇḍa iti na ayam kathā niyamaḥ kim tu vicāra vastu niyamaḥ yat vastu vicāryate tat tredhā vicāryate tatra vicāraḥ vādaḥ jalpaḥ vitaṇḍā ca tatra guru ādibhiḥ saha vādaḥ vijigīṣuṇā saha jalpa vitaṇḍe tatra yathoddeśam lakṣaṇa apadeśaḥ iti vādasya lakṣaṇam ucyate tatra pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambhaḥ iti sūtram tatra vādaḥ pakṣa pratipakṣa parigrahaḥ kau punar etau pakṣa pratipakṣau vastu dharmau eka adhikaraṇau viruddhau eka kālau anavasitau vastu dharmau iti vastu viśeṣau vastunaḥ sāmānyena adhigata tvāt viśeṣataḥ anadhigata tvāt ca viśeṣa avagama nimittaḥ vicāraḥ tasmāt vastu dharmau tad viśeṣau eka adhikaraṇau iti nānā adhikaraṇau tu vicāram na prayojayataḥ ubhayoḥ pramāṇena upapatteḥ tat yathā anityā buddhiḥ nityaḥ ātmā iti 
NV_1.2.1^2	 aviruddhau api evam eva yau viruddhau tau vicāram prayojayataḥ na aviruddhau iti tat yathā kriyāvat dravyam guṇavat ca iti eka kālau iti bhinna kālayoḥ na vicāra prayojaka tvam pramāṇena upapatteḥ yathā kriyāvat dravyam niṣkriyam ca iti kāla bhedena iti anavasitau iti aniścitau vicāram prayojayataḥ na avasitau iti nirṇaya uttara kālam vicāra abhāvāt tau etau viruddhau evaṃviśeṣaṇau dharmau pakṣa pratipakṣau tayoḥ parigrahaḥ itthambhāva niyamaḥ evaṃdharma ayam dharmī na evam dharmā iti saḥ ayam pakṣa pratipakṣa parigrahaḥ vādaḥ asya ca kathā mārga traye api samāna tvāt viśeṣaṇa artham pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambhaḥ iti pramāṇaiḥ tarkeṇa ca sādhanam upālambhaḥ ca asmin kriyate iti asmin bhavati iti asmin iti saptamī nirdeśaḥ viṣaya jñāpana arthaḥ asmin vicāre 
NV_1.2.1^3	 katham punar tarkeṇa sādhanam upālambhaḥ ca apramāṇa ātmaka tvāt pramāṇa anugrāhaka tvāt na pramāṇa saṃgṛhītaḥ tarkaḥ na pramāṇa antaram iti uktam saḥ ayam apramāṇa ātmakaḥ san katham siddhi upālabdhyoḥ kāraṇam bhaviṣyati na brūmaḥ tarkaḥ siddhi upālabdhyoḥ kāraṇam api tu pramā viṣaya vivecanāt tarkaḥ pramāṇāni anugṛhṇāti tarka viviktam viṣayam pramāṇāni pravartamānāni paricchindanti saḥ ayam pramāṇānām anugrāhaka tvāt pramāṇa sahitaḥ vāde apadiṣṭaḥ iti sādhanam upālambhaḥ ca asmin bhavati iti kim tāvat siddhiḥ sādhanam upālambhanam upālambhaḥ atha sādhyate anena iti sādhanam upālabhyate anena iti upālambhaḥ yadi tāvat bhāva sādhanau sādhana upālambha śabdau tadā pramāṇaiḥ tarkeṇa ca na yuktau pramāṇānām tarkasya ca para apratipādaka tvāt pramāṇāni ātma pratipatti sādhanāni para pratipādana arthaḥ ca ayam vicāraḥ 
NV_1.2.1^4	 tasmāt na pramānaiḥ tarkeṇa ca siddhi upālabdhī bhavataḥ atha karaṇa sādhanau tathā api pañca avayava upapannaḥ iti pṛthak na paṭhitavyam kim kāraṇam pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambhaḥ iti karaṇa sādhanena padena avayava arthasya ukta tvāt na anyārtha tvāt pañca avayava upapannaḥ iti asya anyaḥ arthaḥ tathā ca vakṣyāmaḥ atha etau sādhana upālambha śabdau bhāva sādhanau kim viṣayau pramāṇaiḥ tarkeṇa ca kriyete nanu uktam pakṣa pratipakṣa viṣayau iti pakṣa viṣayam sādhanam pratipakṣa viṣayaḥ upālambhaḥ iti satyam uktam na punar yuktam kā punar yukti hāniḥ atra upālambhasya pratipakṣā viṣaya tvāt pramāṇa tarka sādhanā siddhiḥ pakṣasya bhavatu na punar upālambhasya pratipakṣaḥ viṣayaḥ na brūmaḥ pratipakṣa viṣayaḥ upālambhaḥ iti kim tu sādhana viṣayaḥ 
NV_1.2.1^5	 pratipakṣasya yat sādhanam tat viṣayaḥ upālambhaḥ iti katham punar pratipakṣa sannidhau apadiśyamānaḥ upālambha śabdaḥ pratipakṣa vyatirekeṇa sādhanena sambadhyate sāmarthyāt asāmarthyāt ca yat upālambha yogyam tat upālabhyate na ca pratipakṣaḥ upālambha yogyaḥ katham iti upālabhyamānasya anupālabhyamānasya ca vastunaḥ tathā abhavāt yathābhūtam ca vastu upālabhyamānam tathābhūtam eva anupālabhyamānam sādhane api tarhi tulyam sādhanam api karaṇam tat api svarūpam na kadā cit jahāti tasmāt sādhanasya api upālambhaḥ na yuktaḥ iti evam etat na upālambhaḥ karaṇe na karmaṇi ca karma karaṇayoḥ sva viṣaye sāmarthyāt sarvam karma sva viṣaye samartham karaṇam api evam tasya tu viṣaya antare na sāmarthyam asti yat ca viṣaya antare asamartham na tena karmaṇaḥ karaṇasya vā vaiguṇyam 
NV_1.2.1^6	 kasya tarhi ayam upālambhaḥ yaḥ ayam nigṛhyate kaḥ ca nigṛhyate puruṣaḥ apratipatti vipratipattī puruṣasya na karmaṇaḥ na karaṇasya saḥ ayam pratipādayitā samarthayoḥ karma karaṇayoḥ upādānāt nigṛhyate pratipattā api yathā abhihita padārtha apratipattyā vipratipattyā ca iti saḥ ayam puruṣa dharmaḥ vacana dvāreṇa udbhāvi ate iti vacanaḥ upacarya puruṣa dharmam vacanam upālabhyate iti katham punar ayam arthaḥ sūtra padeṣu labhyate labhyate iti āha katham pramāṇa tarka sādhanaḥ pakṣaḥ pramāṇaiḥ tarkeṇa ca sādhanasya upālambhaḥ pramāṇa tarka sādhanaḥ ca pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambhaḥ ca pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambhaḥ ekasya sādhana śabdasya gamyamāna artha tvāt lopaḥ yathā uṣṭra mukhī kanyā iti atha pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambhaḥ iti anena padena jalpa vitaṇḍābhyām katham vādaḥ viśiṣyate 
NV_1.2.1^7	 nanu idam pakṣa pratipakṣa parigraha vat trayāṇām api samānam bhavati na samānam vāde pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambhasya niyata tvāt pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambha eva vādaḥ chala ja ati nigraha sthāna sādhana upālambhe jalpa vitaṇḍe yathā viṣāṇi tvam gavi gavaye ca samānam api saṃvṛta kaṇṭha tayā sāsnādi mattayā ca viśiṣyamāṇam ubhau go gavayau viśinaṣṭi tathā pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambhaḥ iti chala ja ati nigraha sthāna sādhana upālambhaḥ jalpaḥ iti abhidhānāt vāde nigraha sthāna pratiṣedhaḥ viśeṣa vidhānāt tatas ca na upālambhaḥ vādaḥ iti pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambhaḥ iti abhidhānāt vāde api nigraha sthānāni iti adoṣaḥ upālambha śravaṇāt samasta nigraha sthāna prasakteḥ saṃjñā bheda mātram yadi upālambha grahaṇāt vāde api nigraha sthānāni vidyante iti manyase nanu 
NV_1.2.1^8	 saṃjñā bheda mātram jalpāt vādasya na viśeṣaḥ tatra api nigraha sthānāni iha api iti na uttarayoḥ padayoḥ niyama artha tvāt yasmāt eva upālambha śabdena samastāni nigraha sthānāni labhyate atas eva niyama arthe uttare pade ārabhyete siddhānta aviruddhaḥ pañca avayava upapannaḥ ca iti siddhānta aviruddhaḥ iti anena kila padena viruddhaḥ hetvābhāsaḥ labhyate tat na anyatas adhigateḥ anyaḥ eva ayam labhyate pañca avayava upapannaḥ iti pañca grahaṇāt nyūna adhike labhyete avayava grahaṇāt tad ābhāsā labhyante iti labhyamānasya arthasya punar abhidhānena sūtrakāreṇa piṣṭam piṣṭam syāt tasmāt na ayam arthaḥ atha kim idam padam siddhānta aviruddhaḥ iti anarthakam eva na anarthakam apasiddhānta avarodha artha tvāt siddhāntam abhyupetya aniyamāt kathā prasaṅgaḥ apasiddhāntaḥ iti 
NV_1.2.1^9	 saḥ anena avarudhyate tasmāt na anarthakam kasmāt punar ayam niyamaḥ vāde avayava ābhāsa apasiddhāntaḥ ca nigraha sthānam iti guru ādibhiḥ saha vāda upadeśāt niyamaḥ yasmāt ayam tattva bubhūtsuḥ guru ādibhiḥ saha trividham phalam ākāṅkṣan vādam karoti tatas asya tattva bubhūt sau atas tāvat sādhanam vaktavyam yāvat anena jñātavyam iti apratidvan dvi tvāt pratidvandvinā ca saha na vādaḥ kim tu jalpaḥ tatra samasta nigraha shtāna prayogaḥ iti yuktam pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambhaḥ iti abhidhānāt ubhayoḥ siddhi asiddhi prasaṅgaḥ yadi pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambhaḥ vādaḥ ubhayoḥ vādi prativādinoḥ pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambha abhidhāne adhikāraḥ iti ubhaya mata siddhi asiddhi prasaṅgaḥ na eṣa doṣaḥ aparti jñānāt na idam pratijñāyate ubhayoḥ vādinoḥ pramāṇāni santi iti api tu tābhyām sādhanam vaktavyam iti etat niyamyate 
NV_1.2.1^10	 na punar sādhanam eva etat bhavati iti dūṣaṇam api evam apare tu sva para pakṣayoḥ siddhi asiddhi artham vacanam vādaḥ iti vāda lakṣaṇam varṇaynti atra ca pakṣa viśeṣaṇa artham upāttayoḥ sva para śabdayoḥ anupapattiḥ vikalpa anupapatteḥ samāsāsambhavāt ca etau khalu sva para śabdau parigraha varjana arthau vā syātām sādhanīya dūṣaṇīya arthau vā pūrva uttara pakṣa artha vyavasthāpakau vā pakṣa pratipakṣa avadyotakau vā prathama dvitīya pakṣa abhidhāyakau vā ekasya vā aneka viśeṣaṇa abhisambandhinaḥ aneka śabda abhidhānam iti tatra parigraha parivarjana artha tā tāvat anupapannā kimaḥ artha asambhavāt na hi parigraha artha tāyām kimaḥ arthaḥ sambhavati kasya ayam svaḥ bhaviṣyati kaḥ ca sva arthaḥ iti svīkaraṇam parigraha arthaḥ yaḥ svīkaroti tasya svaḥ iti 
NV_1.2.1^11	 etat eva cintyate kim tat svīkaraṇam iti mama iti pratyaya utpatti kāraṇa bhāva abhāvau sva para śabda arthaḥ nirdiṣṭaḥ sva arthaḥ na punar asya svam na hi śāstra kārasya svar paraḥ vā sambhavati yat artham idam syāt yat ca yasya svam bhavati tat tasya siddhi artham kim cit upakāram karoti na punar svāminaḥ pakṣeṇa kaḥ cit upakāraḥ kriyate tasmāt parigraha varjana arthau tāvat sva para śabdau na bhavataḥ sādhanīya dūṣaṇīya arthau sva para śabdau iti ced atha api idam syāt sādhanīyaḥ sva pakṣaḥ dūṣaṇīyaḥ para pakṣaḥ iti aho śāstra artha kauśalam sādhanīyaḥ sādhyaḥ syāt sādhanīyaḥ sva pakṣaḥ iti kutas etat lakṣaṇam ca etat pakṣasya sādhaitum iṣṭaḥ pakṣaḥ iti sādhanīya śabdena api tat eva ucyate vyavaccheda artham ca idam ucyate sva pakṣaḥ para pakṣaḥ iti 
NV_1.2.1^12	 para pakṣāt ca ayam sva śabdena vyavacchidyamānaḥ na samānam artham śaknoti vaktum vyartham vā viśeṣaṇam sāmānya śabdāḥ api viśeṣe vartante iti dṛṣṭam etat na te sāmānya śabdāḥ ye viśeṣeṣu vartante iti kim tu prakaraṇa ādi bheda anuvidhāyinaḥ viśeṣa śabdāḥ eva te api ca sādhanīyaḥ pakṣaḥ sva pakṣaḥ dūṣaṇīyaḥ pakṣaḥ para pakṣaḥ iti etat api na buddhyāmahe sādhanasya pakṣa viṣaya tvāt sādhanīyaḥ pakṣaḥ svaḥ bhavatu dūṣaṇam tu na kim cit para pakṣena sambadhyate para pakṣasya tādavasthyāt atha dūṣaṇasya kaḥ viṣayaḥ kasya cit sthāpanāḥ viṣayaḥ iti kim cit dūṣaṇam sthāpanayā saṃbadhyate kim cit sva para pakṣābhyām asambaddham eva katamat punar dūṣaṇam sthāpanayā sambadhyate kā ca iyam sthāpana iti sthāpanā nāma pañca avayavam pakṣa sādhakam vākyam vākya doṣaḥ dūṣaṇam 
NV_1.2.1^13	 tat vākyam nyūnam ca adhikam ca bhavati avayava ābhāsa upapannam ca tad udbhāvanam dūṣaṇam etat sthāpanayā sambadhyate tad viṣaya tvāt śeṣam tu dūṣaṇam na sthāpanayā na sva para pakṣābhyām sambaddham uttara doṣaḥ ākṣepa bhāvāḥ ca iti satyam na sākṣāt pakṣasya dūṣaṇena abhisambandhaḥ sthāpanā nivṛtti dvāreṇa tu pravartamānam dūṣaṇam na pakṣam nivartayati sthāpanā nivṛtteḥ para pakṣam dūṣayati iti ucyate upacarita śabda prayogaḥ lakṣaṇe anupapannaḥ lakṣaṇasya tattva viṣaya tvāt tattva vyavacchedakam lakṣaṇam na punar upacarita śabda prayogeṇa vyavasthā asti yadi ca pāramparyeṇa pravṛttyā pravartamānam dūṣaṇam para pakṣam nivartayati tadā eva yuktam kartum para pakṣa asiddhi artham vacanam vādaḥ iti evam abhidhīyamāne kim bhaviṣyati laghu ca sūtram bhavati iti ubhayoḥ ca sādhana dūṣaṇayoḥ pāramparyeṇa para pakṣa asiddhi artha tā iti 
NV_1.2.1^14	 atha mā bhūt ubhayatra pāramparyam iti svarūpataḥ evam sūtram vaktavyam pakṣa sthāpanayoḥ siddhi asiddhi artham vacanam vādaḥ iti evam hi spaṣṭa tā lakṣaṇasya yathā viṣayam ca abhisambandhaḥ iti sthāpanā api na sarvam dūṣaṇam sambadhyate iti doṣa tādavasthyam na doṣatāt avasthyam kasya cit sambhavāt kim cit dūṣaṇam sthāpanayā sambaddhi atas iti uktam sāmānya abhidhāne api sāmarthyāt niyamaḥ tasmāt idam api anupapannam sādhanīya dūṣaṇīya arthau sva para śabdau iti sva para śabdau pūrva uttara pakṣa arthau bhaviṣyate iti yat uktam bhavati pūrva pakṣa uttara pakṣau iti tat uktam bhavati sva para pakṣau iti na yuktam etat api iti sādhana dūṣaṇayoḥ niyama abhyupagamāt te sādhana dūṣaṇaiḥ iti etasmin sūtre sādhandūṣaṇayoḥ niyama abhidhānam sva pakṣe sādhanam para pakṣe dūṣaṇam iti 
NV_1.2.1^15	 etasmin ca niyamaḥ uttara pakṣa viṣayam dūṣaṇam prāpnoti tena uttara pakṣa vādī svam eva pakṣam dūṣayati iti prāptam sva pakṣaḥ ca uttara pakṣa vādinaḥ pūrva pakṣāt anyaḥ iti sva para śabdābhyām ca pūrva uttara pakṣayoḥ abhidhānam iti na padārthaḥ na paribhāṣā na ca rūḍhiḥ etena pakṣa pratipakṣa artha tā prathama dvitīya pakṣa artha tā ca vyākhyātāḥ ekaḥ eva ayam pakṣaḥ iti viśeṣaṇa dvaya yogāt sādhya tayā dūṣya tayā ca viśeṣyamāṇaḥ sva para pakṣa śabda vācyaḥ iti yuktam etat dvivacanam tu na yuktam ekasya aneka viśeṣaṇa yogaḥ na pratiṣidhyate dvivacanam tu na bhavati iti brūmaḥ na hi ekasya aneka viśeṣaṇa abhisambandhe sati dvi vacana bahuvacane bhavataḥ na hi devadattam chatra daṇḍābhyām saṃbaddham samupalabhya vaktāraḥ bhavanti chatri daṇḍinau āgatau iti 
NV_1.2.1^16	 tat evam vikalpa anupapatteḥ sva para śabda anupapattiḥ samāsāsambhavāt ca sva para pakṣaḥ iti samāsapadam etat tatra tāvat viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya svarūpa anavadhṛteḥ na ṣaṣṭhī samāsaḥ yatra khalu ṣaṣṭhī samasyate tatra viśeṣaṇam viśeṣyāt pṛthak avadhāryate yathā rāja puruṣaḥ iti bhedāt ca yatra ca viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ bhavati tatra bhedaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ rāja puruṣa vat eva asati api bhede dṛṣṭaḥ iti ced asati api bhede dṛṣṭaḥ ṣaṣṭhī samāsaḥ tat yathā senāpatiḥ pānaka aṅgam iti tat ca na anabhyupagamāt kaḥ hi svastha ātmā pānakam aṅgebhyaḥ na artha antaram pratipadyate senām ca sainikebhyaḥ iti yathā ca senā ādīni artha antara bhūtāni tathā uktam guṇa guṇivādaḥ iti atha manyase sva arthaḥ sva śabdasya arthaḥ sādhanīya arthaḥ ca pakṣa śabdasya iti 
NV_1.2.1^17	 tat na apodita tvāt yathā sva artha vācakaḥ sva śabdaḥ na bhavati tathā uktam tasmāt na ṣaṣṭhī samāsaḥ etena karmadhārayaḥ pratyuktaḥ svaḥ ca asau pakṣaḥ ca iti viśeṣaṇa svarūpa asiddheḥ bheda abhāvāt ca etena bahuvrīhiḥ api pratyuktaḥ sādhayitṛ viṣayam ca sādhanam prāpnoti atas na bahuvrīhiḥ nanu ca sādhanīya artha tā sva arthaḥ pakṣa viśeṣaṇa tvena sambhavati na sambhavati paryāya tvāt sādhanīyaḥ pakṣaḥ iti paryāyaḥ eva na ca paryāya śabdaiḥ samāna adhikaraṇaḥ bahuvrīhiḥ vā sambhavati na hi bhavati vṛkṣa tarum chinatti iti virodhāt ca yadi tāvat ayam pakṣa śabdaḥ sva pakṣāt bhidyate para pakṣa vacanam pratijñā iti vyāghātaḥ kim kāraṇam pratijñāyāḥ sva pakṣa viṣaya tvāt atha abhinnaḥ tathā api idam na prāpnoti sva para pakṣayoḥ siddhi asiddhi artham vacanam vādaḥ iti 
NV_1.2.1^18	 na ca anyaḥ samāsaḥ sambhavati na ca idam vākyam tasmāt sva para pakṣayoḥ iti asāram etat āstām tāvat sva para śabda arthaḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ ca sva para śabdayoḥ atha samāsaḥ kasmāt na kriyate sva para pakṣa siddhi asiddhi artham vacanam vādaḥ iti kim evam kṛte bhaviṣyati saḥ eva arthaḥ lāghavam ca atra ke cit parihāram bruvate yadi kila samāsaḥ kriyataḥ ubhaya āśrite siddhi asiddhī prāpnutaḥ na doṣa tādavasthyāt na ayam doṣaḥ asamāsa karaṇena parihriyate katham iti sva pakṣa siddhi asiddhyā artham vacanam para pakṣasya ca siddhi asiddhi artham sva para pakṣayoḥ siddhi asiddhi artham iti na asāmarthyāt na hi ayam samāsaḥ samarthaḥ sva pakṣasya para pakṣasya ca siddhi asiddhi artham iti kasmāt vyāhata tvāt yadi siddhi artham yatate siddhi artham iti vyāghātaḥ 
NV_1.2.1^19	 yadi asiddhi artham yatate siddhi artham iti vyāghātaḥ yadi asāmarthyāt na samāsaḥ samāse api tarhi asāmarthyān na ubhaya pakṣa siddhi asiddhi prasaṅgaḥ eka vacana bahuvacana prasaṅgaḥ iti anye yadi kila samāsaḥ kriyeta samāsaḥ anabhivyakta vacana bhedaḥ tasmāt vacana bheda vyakti nimittam asamāsaḥ katham nāma sva para pakṣayoe eva siddhi asiddhi artham vacanam vādaḥ syāt na sva para pakṣāṇām na sva para pakṣasya iti na asambhavāt ekasya tāvat siddhi asiddhi artham vacanam na eva asti sva para pakṣāṇām sādhanam anumānam ekam iti kathā api eṣā na asti atas asthānaḥ āśaṅkā anityaḥ samāsa vidhiḥ iti apare apare punar samāsa vidheḥ anitya tām varṇayantī evam āhuḥ na ayam avaśyam vidhiḥ sarvatra samāsaḥ iti kva cit samāsaḥ bhavati kva cit ca vākyam 
NV_1.2.1^20	 yathā ca rājñaḥ puruṣaḥ rāja puruṣaḥ iti yadi ubhaya prāptiḥ asamāsaḥ kasmāt anityaḥ samāsa vidhiḥ iti evam bruvata etat uktam bhavati prāptam ubhayam atha ubhaya prāptau kasmāt asamāsaḥ iti samāsaḥ kasmāt iti anivṛttaḥ anuyogaḥ na anivṛttaḥ lāghava artha tvāt samāse lāghavam asamāse gauḥ evam artha gati artham ca śabdānām upādānam iti guru abhidhāne prāyoganam vācyam varṇe gurulāghava anabhyupagamaḥ iti ced na ayam parihāraḥ anuyogasya anivṛtteḥ varṇe gurulāghava anuyogam na pratipadyāmahe iti ced na nivartate anuyogaḥ kasmāt iti śāstra tvena ca vāda avidhānam abhyupagamyate na ca varṇe gurulāghavam āśrīyate iti na yuktam siddhi asiddhi artham iti etat api na yuktam kasmāt dvedhā anupapatteḥ ayam khalu siddhi śabdaḥ kalpyamānaḥ dvedhā kalpyeta vyaktau utpattau vā 
NV_1.2.1^21	 tat na tāvat utpattau yujyate pratijña ādikasya sādhanasya sādhana bhāva hāni prasaṅgāt na hi pratijña ādi sādhanena vastu utpādyate kim tu vidyamāna prakāśaka tvam sādhana arthaḥ sa hīyate siddhau utpattau kalpitāyām iti vyaktau iti ced na adhikaraṇa ādhāra tvāt atha manyase siddhiḥ vyaktiḥ na utpattiḥ yuktam etat uttaram tu vyāhatam bhavati adhikaraṇa pratyāyanam siddhi asiddhī iti ye ca ete adhikaraṇa pratyāyana lakṣaṇe siddhi asiddhī te adhikaraṇe vartamāne katham pakṣasya bhavataḥ iti ṣaṣṭhī arthaḥ vācyaḥ na ayam durvacaḥ tad viṣaya tvāt tayoḥ siddhi asiddhyoḥ pakṣaḥ viṣayaḥ atas tad viṣaya tvāt tasya iti na yuktam etat ye te siddhi asiddhī pakṣa viṣaye te kim tāvat pakṣe siddhe uta asiddhe yadi tāvat siddhe na adhikaraṇa pratyāyanam siddhiḥ kim tarhi 
NV_1.2.1^22	 yatas tat pratyāyanam sā siddhiḥ kutas ca tat bhavati arthasya tathā abhāvāt yasmāt saḥ arthaḥ tathā bhavati katham tathā bhavati yathā pramāṇaiḥ upasampannaḥ iti yat tat pramāṇa avisaṃvādi tvam sa tathā abhāvaḥ atha asiddhe pakṣe adhikaraṇa pratyāyanam bhavati sādhana prayogāt prāk adhikaraṇa pratyāyanam bhavati iti vāda vaiyarthyam syāt pakṣasya siddhiḥ adhikaraṇa pratyāyanam bhavatu asiddhiḥ tu katham na hi para pakṣa asiddhiḥ dūṣaṇena kriyate iti uktam sthāpanā nivṛtteḥ upacāraḥ iti ced syāt matiḥ dūṣaṇam prayujyamānam sākṣāt sthāpanām nivartayati sthāpanā nivṛtteḥ tu para pakṣa nivṛttiḥ upacaryate iti na prayojana abhāvāt na hi prayojanam antareṇa mukhya artha vyatikramaḥ labhyate api tu pramāṇa asambhavena upacāraḥ mañcāḥ kroṣanti iti yathā 
NV_1.2.1^23	 loka prayukta śabda viṣayaḥ ca upacāraḥ loka gatyā śabda arthaḥ na ca idam laukikam vākyam sva para pakṣayoḥ siddhi asiddhi artham vacanam vādaḥ apare tu pratijñāta artha ājñāpanam pakṣasya asiddhim varṇayanti tat yadi adhikaraṇa viṣayam na nivartate prasaṅgaḥ katham pakṣasya asiddhiḥ iti siddhi vat prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt siddhi asiddhī pakṣa dharmau eva yatas etat bhavati siddhaḥ pakṣaḥ asiddhaḥ ca iti evam sati draṣṭṛ sthe siddhi asiddhī iti vyāghātaḥ yadi siddhi asiddhī pakṣa dharmau draṣṭṛ sthe siddhi asiddhī iti vyāhatam bhavati atha mā bhūt vyāghātaḥ iti draṣṭṛ sthaḥ eva te tathā api pakṣasya vyakti avyaktī siddhi asiddhī iti vyāhatam bhavati atha tathā tathāte padārthasya siddhi asiddhī tathā api adhikaraṇa pratyāyanam siddhi asiddhī iti vyāhatam bhavati 
NV_1.2.1^24	 ke punar ete vyakti avyaktī vastu dharmau abhidhāna pratyaya hetū yatas etau abhidhāna pratyayau vyaktaḥ avyaktaḥ ca iti bhavataḥ te vyakti avyaktī iti artha śabda anupapattiḥ vikalpa anupapatteḥ artha śabdaḥ khalu pravartamānaḥ tredhā pravartate uddeśa prayojana abhidheya viṣaya tvena uddeśe tāvat artha śabdaḥ yathā brāhmaṇa artham bhaktam iti evam ca caturvidha vākya asaṅgrahaḥ prayojane artha śabdaḥ kim artham āgataḥ asi iti abhidheya artha śabdaḥ yathā gauḥ iti abhidhānasya kaḥ arthaḥ iti tat na tāvat uddeśe sambhavati yukta ayukta tvena viśeṣita tvāt sva pakṣasya yukta tvena para pakṣasya ayukta tvena iti evam viśeṣite kutas uddeśe artha śabdaḥ na hi ayam yuktā yukta śabdaḥ dūṣaṇa ābhāse sādhana ābhāse vā sambhavati iti sādhana yogaḥ yukta tā dūṣaṇa yogaḥ ayukta tā iti 
NV_1.2.1^25	 atha punar padārthasya tathā tva ātathā tve yukta ayukta tve yukta tvam tathā abhāvaḥ ayukta tvam atathā bhāvaḥ iti tathā api tayoḥ karma taya upādānāt yukta tvena adhikaraṇa pratyāyanam ayukta tvena ca iti vyāghātaḥ na hi pratyāyam pratyāyanam bhavati iti atha prayojane artha śabdaḥ tathā api sādhana dūṣaṇa ābhāsa vādinaḥ avāditā prāpnoti kim kāraṇam sādhana dūṣaṇa ābhāsayoḥ siddhi asiddhi aprayojana tvāt na hi sādhana dūṣaṇa ābhāsayoḥ siddhi asiddhī prayojanam evam ca tad vādī na vādī syāt tathā ca avādī nigṛhyate iti doṣaḥ atha abhidheye artha śabdaḥ abhidhāna svabhāva anavadhṛteḥ na yuktam etat api na hi granthakāra bhāṣya kārābhyām viśeṣitam evam prakāram abhidhānam siddhi asiddhyoḥ vācakam iti nanu ca viśeṣitam yena siddhi asiddhī abhidhīyete tat tayoḥ vācakam iti satyam uktam 
NV_1.2.1^26	 evam tu siddhi asiddhī iti ete abhidhāne vādaḥ prāptaḥ na ca anyaḥ artha śabdasya viṣaya tasmāt artha śabdaḥ api ayuktaḥ siddhi asiddhi artham vacanam vādaḥ iti bruvāṇena na pūrva uttaram avalokitam naiyāyika hetu pratiṣedhena viśeṣyam vacanam iti abhyupagatam idam punar sūtram samastam vacana viśeṣaṇa artham iti vyāghātaḥ tat evam etāni sūtra padāni vicāryamāṇāni svatantra vyāghātakāni iti lokam ca bādhantaḥ iti evam tāvat sautrāṇi padāni svena nyāyena asambaddhāni yathā ca vṛtti padāni asambaddhāni tathā idam ucyate svasya pakṣasya iti sva artha asiddheḥ ayuktam sva arthaḥ ca pratiṣiddhaḥ atas ayuktam svasya pakṣasya iti yat api ṣaṣṭhī saptamī vacanayoḥ tulya rūpa tvāt ṣaṣṭhi artha jñāpana artham svasya pakṣasya iti tat api ayuktam adhikaraṇa artha asambhavāt 
NV_1.2.1^27	 na hi pakṣa vyatirekeṇa pakṣe kim cit sādhyam sambhavati tasmāt ayuktam saptamī arthaḥ tad aprasaktau viśeṣaṇa ānarthakyam iti yukta ayukta tva anupapattiḥ ca vikalpa anupapatteḥ yukta ayukta tve khalu sādhana dūṣaṇe vā syātām sādhana dūṣaṇābhyām vā yogaḥ padārthasya vā tathā ātatathāte ca iti tat na tāvat sādhana dūṣaṇe yukta ayukta tve kasmāt sādhana dūṣaṇayoḥ pṛthak abhidhānāt te sādhana dūṣaṇaiḥ iti atra pṛthak ukte sādhana dūṣaṇe yukta ayukta śabdābhyām ca sādhana dūṣaṇayoḥ abhidhānam iti te sādhana dūṣaṇaiḥ iti sūtram anuccārya caritārtha tvāt iti atha manyase tayoḥ eva yukta ayuktayoḥ viśeṣaṇa artham te sādhana dūṣaṇaiḥ iti na prathama abhidhāna prasaṅgāt yadi yukta ayukta tva viśeṣaṇa artham te sādhana dūṣaṇaiḥ iti sūtram prathamā eva nyāyā te sādhana dūṣaṇāni iti 
NV_1.2.1^28	 na hi viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāve bhavati nīlam utpalaiḥ iti yogaḥ iti ced atha sādhana dūṣaṇābhyām yogaḥ yukta tva ayukta tve iti evam ced manyase tat na anirdeśāt na sādhana dūṣaṇābhyām yogaḥ nirdiṣṭaḥ evaṃvidhaḥ iti anirdeśāt ayuktam etat sādhanena yogaḥ iti ca kadā bhavati yadā asau nirṇītaḥ padārthaḥ tadā ca na sādhanasya arthaḥ kaḥ cit asti iti na yukta ayukta tvena adhikaraṇa pratyāyanam iti vyāghātaḥ atas na yuktaḥ yogaḥ atha padārthasya tathā ātā tathā tve yukta ayukta tve tat api na karaṇa artha asambhavāt ye tathā tvā tathā tva lakṣaṇe yukta ayukta tve te vyavacchedye na vyavacchedasya sādhane tasmāt karaṇa arthaḥ na asti atas yukta ayukta tvasya iti yuktam vaktum iti adhikaraṇa pratyāyanam iti ca na yuktam śāstra sambandha asaṅgata tvāt 
NV_1.2.1^29	 śāstra sambandham kurvāṇena uktam sandeha viparyaya pratiṣedha arthaḥ śāstrasya ārambhaḥ iti etat nirapekṣena idam abhidhīyate adhikaraṇa pratyāyanam siddhi asiddhī iti na ca prāśnikeṣu saṃśaya viparyayau staḥ paricchedaka tvāt tasmāt na prāśnikāḥ pratyāyāḥ iti yat ca uktam prāśnika pratyāyanāt eva prativādi pratyāyanam kṛtam bhaviṣyati iti kim kāraṇam tad pratyāyanāt prativādi pratyāyanam prativādī kila sva pakṣa rāgāt santam api artham na pratipadyate santam artham na pratipadyate ca iti vyāhatam ucyate katham ca anyathā pratipannaḥ san iti abhidhīyate atha pratipadyamānaḥ api parasya na kāmakāram dadāti tathā api na pratipadyate iti vyāhatam yat ca prāśnika pratyāyanāt tat pratyāyanam iti tat api na pratīteḥ karaṇa bhedāt 
NV_1.2.1^30	 prāśnika pratīteḥ anyāni kāraṇāni anyāni prativādi pratīteḥ iti na ca anya viṣayasya karaṇasya anyasya kriyā iti niyama abhāvāt ca na ca ayam niyamaḥ prāśnika pratyāyana arthaḥ eva vādaḥ prāśnikān antareṇa api guru ādibhiḥ saha vādaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti yadā tu na ayam tattva bubhutsuḥ lābha pūjā khyāti kāmaḥ vādam ārabhate tadā prāśnikaiḥ prayojanam asti iti satyam asti prayojanam vādaḥ tu na bhavati iti na traividhyā anabhyupagamāt ekaḥ eva ayam kathā mārgaḥ tasya prayojanam tattva avabodhaḥ lābha ādayaḥ ca na pratiṣedhāt prasiddhaḥ stuti māna lābha lipsoḥ vādaḥ yat api idam ucyate na traividhyā anabhyupagamāt iti na anabhyupagama āyattaḥ padārtha sadbhāvaḥ api tu sadbhāve sati abhyupagamaḥ iti yathā ca traividhyam kathā mārgasya tathā lakṣaṇa bhedāt vādāt jalpa vitaṇḍayoḥ bhedam upadarśayiṣyāmaḥ 
NV_1.2.1^31	 tasmāt ajñātvā viśeṣam ucyate traividhyā anabhyupagamāt iti yat ca uktam pakṣa siddhi viṣayam pratyāyanam pakṣa siddhi śabdena upacaritam yathā śūnyatā viṣayaḥ samādhiḥ śūnyatā iti na kāmatas upacāraḥ labhyate api tu pramāṇa asambhavena loka prayukta śabdānvā ākhyānam upacāraḥ uktam ca na upacarita śabda prayogaḥ lakṣaṇaḥ upapannaḥ iti tad artham vacanam iti etat api kila caturvidha vākya jñāpana artham uktam sādhanam sādhana ābhāsaḥ dūṣaṇam dūṣaṇa ābhāsaḥ ca sambhantsyate iti tat ayuktam yukta ayukta tvena iti viśeṣita tvāt evam viśeṣite etasmin kutas caturvidha vākya saṃgrahaḥ iti adhikaraṇam punar yaḥ vādi prativādibhyām adhikṛtaḥ iti atra adhikaraṇa arthaḥ vaktavyaḥ na hi vāde prāśnika ādhāra āram kim cit asti iti pratyāyana ādhāra tvāt adhikaraṇam iti ced na ukta uttara tvāt 
NV_1.2.1^32	 ukta uttaram etat pakṣa viṣayam pratyāyanam na prāśnika viṣayam iti tasmin sati bhāvāt iti ced na anyathā api darśanāt anyathā api guru ādibhiḥ saha dṛṣṭaḥ vādaḥ iti tat vāde parīkṣā kā kasya kva iti vaktavyam sādhana dūṣaṇa prayogaḥ pakṣa sthāpanā viṣayaḥ vādaḥ tasya parīkṣā sādhana dūṣaṇa tad ābhāsa parijñānam tad artham adhikāraḥ tasmin iti saptamī arthaḥ na asti yat api prāśnika prativādinoḥ priya apriya vacasi vāda prasaṅgaḥ iti ca udyam kṛtvā pratisamādhānam uktam tat siddhi asiddhibhyām sākṣāt pāramparyeṇa asambandhāt yukta ayukta viśeṣaṇāt ca asambaddham uttareṇa tu asaṅgata padārtha abhidhāyinaḥ dattaḥ sva hastaḥ pūrva aparayoḥ asambandhāt iti yadi tu asaṅgatasya api uttaram vākyam tatas evam vaktavyam na sūtra artha aparijñānāt iti tat etat sūtram vicāryamāṇam saha vārttikam na yuktyā saṅgacchate iti yathānyāyam eva astu 
NV_1.2.2^1	 samastam vāda lakṣaṇam chala ja ati nigraha sthāna sādhana upālambhaḥ jalpaḥ iti yathā ukta upapannaḥ iti na yuktam jalpe nigraha sthāna niyamasya anabhyupagamāt yadi evam ucyeta pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambhaḥ siddhānta aviruddhaḥ pañca avayava upapannaḥ pakṣa pratipakṣa parigrahaḥ chala ja ati nigraha sthāna sādhana upālambhaḥ jalpaḥ iti na yuktam evam bhavitum siddhānta aviruddhaḥ pañca avayava upapannaḥ iti ca padayoḥ upālambha grahaṇāt samasta nigraha sthāna pasaktau niyama artha tvāt niyama arthe ete pade siddhānta aviruddhaḥ pañca avayava upapannaḥ iti jalpe ca niyantavyam na kim cit asti tasmāt niyama arthe ete pade na atideṣṭavye iti atas na vaktavyam yathā ukta upapannaḥ iti na eṣa doṣaḥ sambhavataḥ atideśāt yat atra sambadhyate tat atidiśyate kim ca sambadhyate pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambhaḥ iti etat tasmāt yathā ukta upapannaḥ iti lakṣaṇa mātrasya atideśaḥ 
NV_1.2.2^2	 yathā anyatra aneka dravyeṇa dravyeṇa samavāyāt rūpa viśeṣāt ca rūpa aupalabdhiḥ anena rasa gandha sparśeṣu jñānam vyākhyātam iti na sva rūpa viśeṣaḥ atidiśyate api tu aneka dravyeṇa dravyeṇa samavāya mātram svagataḥ viśeṣaḥ sāmarthyāt tathā iha api yat samartham tat atidiśyate samartham ca lakṣaṇam tasmāt lakṣaṇam ati disyate na niyama arthe pade niyantavyasya abhāvāt atha vā yathā ukta upapannena upapannaḥ yathā ukta upapanna upannaḥ iti prāpte gamyamāna tvāt ekasya upapanna śabdasya lopaḥ yathā gorathaḥ iti kena punar ayam gamyate iti uktam sāmarthyena iti na hi niyama arthayoḥ padayoḥ jalpe sambhavaḥ tasmāt na te ati diśyete iti bhāvyam idānīm katham na sūtra pāṭhā anukrama jñāpana artha tvāt bhāṣyasya etasmin sūtre yat upapannam lakṣaṇa tvena tat atidiśyate iti chala ja ati nigraha sthānaiḥ na kasya cit sādhanam upālambhaḥ vā yuktaḥ ayukta uttara tvāt 
NV_1.2.2^3	 chalam tāvat na sādhanāya na upālambhāya vā alam kasmāt ayukta uttara tvāt ayuktam uttaram chalena abhidhīyate yat ca ayuktaḥ uttaram tat na alam sādhana upālambhāya vā iti evam jātiḥ aṅga bhāvaḥ iti ced atha api idam syāt yat tat pramāṇa tarkaiḥ sādhanam yaḥ ca upālambhaḥ tasya etāni prayujyamānāni chala jāti nigraha sthānāni rakṣaṇa artha tvāt aṅgam bhavanti iti etat api ayukta uttara tvāt eva anupapannam kim artham tarhi prayogaḥ yadi etāni chala jāti nigraha sthānāni sādhana upālambhayoḥ na sādhanam na aṅgam vā kim artham eteṣām upapādanam iti sādhana vighāta artham sādhanam vihaniṣyāmi iti anayā dhiyā apahṛtaḥ pravartate yatra ca etāni chala jāti nigraha sthānāni prayujyante na sa vādaḥ na punar etat abhidhīyate chala jāti nigraha sthānāni sādhanam aṅgam ca iti sādhu sādhana upādāne ca parena ākulīkṛta buddhiḥ chala ādīni prayuṅkte kadā cit śala ādibhiḥ ākulīkṛtasya parasya parājayaḥ api syāt iti 
NV_1.2.2^4	 na punar etāni tattva bubhutsunā vaktavyāni kim tu vijigīṣuṇā iti saḥ ayam pakṣa pratipakṣa parigrahaḥ chala ja ati nigraha sthāna prayoga aprayogābhyām bhidyamānaḥ vādaḥ jalpaḥ vitaṇḍā ca bhavati atra api viruddhau dharmau eka adhikaraṇa sthau iti samānam viruddhayoḥ dharmayoḥ eka adhikaraṇa tva anupapattiḥ ubhaya ātmaka vastu svabhāva asambhavāt yadi viruddhau eka adhikaraṇau dharmau bhavataḥ nanu ekam vastu ubhaya svabhāvam prāptam na ca etat asti tasmāt na viruddhau dharmau eka adhikaraṇau iti na adhyāropita svarūpa dharma saṃpratipattyā tad upapatteḥ ekaḥ tu dharmaḥ svarūpataḥ ekaḥ tu adhyāropita svarūpa pravṛttiḥ tasmāt ubhaya dharmāḥ dharmī iti siddham eka dharmi sthau viruddha arthau iti etat api na buddhyāmahe kaḥ viruddha arthaḥ iti na sva rūpa viparyaya upapatteḥ sva rūpa mātra viparyayaḥ virodhaḥ na punar bādhā vadhya ghātaka bhāvaḥ vā iti 
NV_1.2.3	 pratipakṣa sthāpanā hīnaḥ iti dvitīya pakṣa sthāpanā hīnaḥ iti yāvat uktam bhavati dvitīya pakṣa vādī vaitaṇḍikaḥ na kim cit pakṣam sthāpayati iti apare tu bruvate dūṣaṇa mātram vitaṇḍa iti dūṣaṇa mātram iti mātra śabda prayogāt vaitaṇḍikasya pakṣaḥ api na asti iti ayuktam ca etat caturvargasya abhyupagamāt dūṣaṇam abhyupagacchan dūṣyam abhyupaiti ayathārtha avabodham pratipadyate pratipādayitāram pratipattāram ca dūṣaṇa mātra abhyupagame sati sarvam etat na syāt dūṣaṇa mātra abhidhānāt śeṣam arthataḥ avagamyate iti ced vitaṇḍā vitaṇḍa iti eva vaktavyam yayā vitaṇḍyate sā vitaṇḍa iti anugata arthayā saṃjñayā eva parasya pakṣasya pratvṛtti vyāghātaḥ kriyate iti tasmāt yathānyāsam eva astu nyāyam 
NV_1.2.4^1	 hetu lakṣaṇa abhāvāt ahetavaḥ hetu sāmānyāt dhetu vat avabhāsamānāḥ te ime savyabhicāra viruddha prakaraṇa sama sādhya sama kāla atītāḥ hetvābhāsāḥ kim punar hetubhiḥ ahetūnām sāmānyam yena hetu vat ābhāsantaḥ iti pratijñā anantaram prayogaḥ sāmānyam yathā eva hetavaḥ pratijñā anantaram prayujyante evam hetvābhāsāḥ api iti etat sāmānyam anyatama liṅga dharma anuvidhānam vā yat vā yat sādhanasya liṅgasya trailakṣaṇyam dharmaḥ tatra ekatama dharma anuvidhānam dvi lakṣaṇasya anyatara dharma anuvidhānam vā vivakṣitam sādhaka asādhaka tve tu viśeṣaḥ hetoḥ sādhaka tvam dharmaḥ asādhaka tvam hetvābhāsasya kim punar tat 
NV_1.2.4^2	 samasta lakṣaṇa upapattiḥ asamasta lakṣaṇa upapattiḥ ca kaḥ punar asya sūtrasya arthaḥ vibhāga uddeśaḥ niyama arthaḥ iti uktam kim punar anena vibhāga uddeśena niyantavyam anekadhā prasṛtasya hetu hetvābhāsasya vistaraḥ saṃkṣeptavyaḥ iti kiyatā punar bhedena ayam hetu hetvābhāsaḥ prasṛtaḥ iti kāla puruṣa vastu bheda anuvidhānena aparisaṃkhyeyaḥ sāmānyatas sādhya vastu upagraheṇa hetu hetu ābhāsa bhedaḥ prapañcyamānaḥ ṣaṭsaptati śatam tatra sādhya vyāpaka dharma bhedaḥ ṣoḍaśadhā sādhya eka deśa vṛtti dharmaḥ api evam evam sādhya āvṛtti dharma bhedaḥ iti viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya asiddhi bhedāt catuḥṣaṣṭiḥ evam samarthāsamartha viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhedāt iti 
NV_1.2.4^3	 tatra sādhya vyāpaka dharma bhedānām ṣoḍaśānām udāharaṇāni tatrasādhya tad jātīyāni avyāpakaḥ prameya tvāt nityaḥ anityaḥ vā iti sādhya tajjātīya vyāpakaḥ vipakṣa eka deśa vṛttiḥ gauḥ ayam viṣāṇi tvāt sādhya tajjātīya vyāpakaḥ vipakṣa āvṛttiḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ utpatti dharmaka tvāt sādhya vyāpakaḥ tad jātīya āvṛttiḥ vipakṣa vyāpakaḥ nityaḥ śabdaḥ utpatti dharmaka tvāt sādhya vyāpakaḥ tad jātīya āvṛttiḥ vipakṣa eka deśa vṛttiḥ nityaḥ śabdaḥ sāmānya viśeṣavataḥ asmad ādi bāhya karaṇa pratyakṣa tvāt dvi aṇuka vat sādhya vyāpakaḥ tad jātīya vipakṣa āvṛttiḥ yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ sāmānya viśeṣavat tve sati śrāvaṇa tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat 
NV_1.2.4^4	 sādhya vyāpakaḥ tad jātīya eka deśa vṛttiḥ vipakṣa vyāpakaḥ ca agauḥ ayam viṣāṇi tvāt sādhya vyāpakaḥ tad jātīya vipakṣa eka deśa vṛttiḥ nityaḥ śabdaḥ asparśavat tvāt sādhya vyāpakaḥ tad jātīya eka deśa vṛttiḥ vipakṣa āvṛttiḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ sāmānya viśeṣavataḥ asmad ādi bāhya karaṇa pratyakṣa tvāt sāmānya viśeṣa vat iti sāmānya viśeṣa samavāyānām nirākaraṇam asmad ādi pratyakṣa tvāt iti paramāṇūnām bāhya karaṇa pratyakṣa tvāt iti ātmanaḥ sādhya tajjātīya vyāpakaḥ avidyamāna vipakṣaḥ siddhānta bheda āśrayaṇena ekānta vādinaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ utpatti dharmaka tvāt sādhya vyāpakaḥ tad jātīya eka deśa vṛttiḥ avidhyamāna vipakṣaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ bāhya indriya pratyakṣa tvāt 
NV_1.2.4^5	 sādhya vyāpakaḥ tad jātīya āvṛttiḥ avidyamāna vipakṣaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ śrāvaṇa tvāt sādhya vyāpakaḥ avidya mānasajātīyaḥ vipakṣa vyāpakaḥ nityaḥ śabdaḥ utpatti dharmaka tvāt sādhya vyāpakaḥ avidya mānasajātīyaḥ vipakṣa eka deśa vṛttiḥ nityaḥ śabdaḥ bāhya indriya pratyakṣa tvāt sādhya vyāpakaḥ avidyamānasajātīyaḥ vipakṣa āvṛttiḥ na idam nirātmakam jīvat śarīram anindriya adhiṣṭhāna tva prasaṅgāt pakṣa vyāpakaḥ avidya mānasapakṣa vipakṣaḥ sarvam nityam prameya tvāt te ete pakṣa vyāpakāḥ ṣoḍaśa eṣām pañca hetavaḥ śeṣāḥ hetvābhāsāḥ tatra anvaya vyatirekiṇau dvau vipakṣa āvṛttī tṛtīyanavamau ekānta vādinaḥ anvayinau eva daśama ekādaśau 
NV_1.2.4^6	 vyatireki pañcadaśaḥ iti atha sādhya eka deśa vṛttayaḥ sādhya eka deśa vṛttiḥ tad jātīya vipakṣa vyāpakaḥ pṛthivī ap tejaḥ vāyu ākāśāni anityāni agandhavat tvāt sādhya eka deśa vṛttiḥ tad jātīya vyāpakaḥ vipakṣa eka deśa vṛttiḥ ca sāmānya viśeṣa vat asmad ādi bāhya karaṇa pratyakṣe vāc manase anitya tvāt sādhya eka deśa vṛttiḥ tad jātīya vyāpakaḥ vipakṣa āvṛttiḥ anitye vāc manase utpatti dharmaka tvāt sādhya eka deśa vṛttiḥ tad jātīya āvṛttiḥ vipakṣa vyāpakaḥ anitye vāc manase utpatti dharmaka tvāt sādhya eka deśa vṛttiḥ tad jātīya āvṛttiḥ vipakṣa eka deśa vṛttiḥ sāmānya viśeṣa vat asmad ādi bāhya karaṇa pratyakṣe vāc manase nitya tvāt 
NV_1.2.4^7	 sādhya eka deśa vṛttiḥ tad jātīya vipakṣa āvṛttiḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ vibhāga ja vibhāgā samavāyi kāraṇa tvāt sādhya tajjātīya eka deśa vṛttiḥ vipakṣa vyāpakaḥ anityāḥ paramāṇavaḥ agandhavat tvāt sādhya tajjātīya vipakṣa eka deśa vṛttiḥ anitye vāc manase amūrta tvāt sādhya tajjātīya eka deśa vṛttiḥ vipakṣa āvṛttiḥ anitye vāc manase sāmānya viśeṣavataḥ asmad ādi bāhya karaṇa pratyakṣa tvāt sādhya eka deśa vṛttiḥ tad jātīya vyāpakaḥ avidhyamāna vipakṣaḥ siddhānta bheda āśrayaṇena anitye rūpa vijñāne amūrta tvāt vedanā ādi vat sādhya tajjātīya eka deśa vṛttiḥ avidyamāna vipakṣaḥ anitye cakṣuḥ vijñāne amūrta tvāt rūpa ādi vat 
NV_1.2.4^8	 sādhya eka deśa vṛttiḥ tad jātīya āvṛttiḥ avidyamāna vipakṣaḥ anitye vāc manase śrāvaṇa tvāt sādhya eka deśa vṛttiḥ avidyamāna sajātiḥ vipakṣa vyāpakaḥ nitye vāc manase utpatti dharmaka tvāt sādhya eka deśa vṛttiḥ avidyamāna sa jātiḥ vipakṣa eka deśa āvṛttiḥ nitye cakṣuḥ vijñāne amūrta tvāt sādhya eka deśa vṛttiḥ avidyamāna sa jātiḥ vipakṣa āvṛttiḥ na idam nirātmakam śarīram anindriya adhiṣṭhāna tva prasaṅgāt sādhya eka deśa vṛttiḥ avidyamāna sapakṣa vipakṣaḥ sarvam anityam mūrta tvāt iti ete ca sādhya eka deśa vṛttayaḥ ṣoḍaśa yathā uktāḥ sarve hetvābhāsāḥ atha sādhya āvṛttayaḥ sādhya āvṛttiḥ tad jātīya vipakṣa vyāpakaḥ anityā pṛthivī agandhavat tvāt 
NV_1.2.4^9	 sādhya āvṛttiḥ tad jātīya vyāpakaḥ vipakṣa eka deśa vṛttiḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ aśrāvaṇa tvāt sādhya āvṛttiḥ tad jātīya vyāpakaḥ vipakṣa āvṛttiḥ arthaḥ śabdaḥ aśrotra grāhya sāmānyavat tvāt sādhya tajjātīya āvṛttiḥ vipakṣa vyāpakaḥ arthaḥ śabdaḥ asāmānyavat tvāt sādhya tajjātīya āvṛttiḥ vipakṣa eka deśa vṛttiḥ ca kāraṇavān śabdaḥ artha tvāt sādhya tajjātīya vipakṣa āvṛttiḥ nityaḥ śabdaḥ asattvāt sādhya āvṛttiḥ tad jātīya eka deśa vṛttiḥ vipakṣa vyāpakaḥ asparśaḥ śabdaḥ dravya tvāt sādhya āvṛttiḥ tad jātīya vipakṣa eka deśa vṛttiḥ kāraṇavān śabdaḥ mūrta tvāt sādhya āvṛttiḥ tad jātīya eka deśa vṛttiḥ vipakṣa āvṛttiḥ āśrayavān śabdaḥ cākṣuṣa tvāt aulūkya pakṣe 
NV_1.2.4^10	 sādhya āvṛttiḥ tad jātīya vyāpakaḥ avidyamāna vipakṣaḥ siddhānta bheda āśrayeṇa anityaḥ śabdaḥ aśrāvaṇa tvāt sādhya āvṛttiḥ tad jātīya eka deśa vṛttiḥ avidyamāna vipakṣaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ mūrta tvāt sādhya tajjātīya āvṛttiḥ avidyamāna vipakṣaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ asattvāt sādhya āvṛttiḥ avidyamāna sapakṣaḥ vipakṣa vyāpakaḥ nityaḥ śabdaḥ aśrāvaṇa tvāt sādhya āvṛttiḥ avidyamāna sa jātiḥ vipakṣa eka deśa vṛttiḥ nityaḥ śabdaḥ mūrta tvāt sādhya āvṛttiḥ avidyamāna sa jātiḥ vipakṣa āvṛttiḥ nityaḥ śabdaḥ asattvāt sādhya āvṛttiḥ avidya māsa pakṣa vipakṣaḥ anityam sarvam asattvāt te ete ṣoḍaśa sādhya āvṛttayaḥ hetvābhāsāḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya asiddha bhedāt catuḥṣaṣṭi bhedāḥ bhavanti iti uktam 
NV_1.2.4^11	 tat katham vyāpaka avyāpaka viśeṣaṇa yogāt ye sādhya vyāpakāḥ ṣoḍaśa ye ca pakṣa eka deśa vṛttayaḥ te ete viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya asiddha bhedena catuḥṣaṣṭiḥ bhavanti iti tatra vyāpakānām tāvat udāharaṇāni anityaḥ śabdaḥ anabhidheya tve sati prameya tvāt iti viśeṣaṇa asiddhaḥ prameya tve sati anabhidheya tvāt iti viśeṣya asiddhaḥ evam sarveṣu sādhya vyāpakeṣu viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya asiddhi bhedaḥ vaktavyaḥ tāni eva ca udāharaṇāni sādhya eka deśa vṛttīnām tu udāharaṇam pṛthivī ap tejaḥ vāyu ākāśāni anityāni anabhidheya tve sati agandhavat tvāt viśeṣaṇa asiddheḥ agandhavat tve sati anabhidheya tvāt iti viśeṣya asiddhiḥ 
NV_1.2.4^12	 evam sarveṣu sādhya eka deśa vṛttiṣu evam asamartha viśeṣaṇā samartha viśeṣyāḥ catuḥṣaṣṭiḥ eva draṣṭavyāḥ yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tve sati prameya tvāt prameya tve sati kṛtaka tvāt iti evam sarveṣu sādhya eka deśa vṛttiṣu evam sandigdha viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhedāḥ api draṣṭavyāḥ yathā mayūra śabdaḥ ayam ṣaḍja ādimattve sati avarṇa ātmaka tvāt avarṇa ātmaka tve sati ṣaḍja ādimattvāt te ete ubhaya pakṣa sampratipannāḥ vidyamāna sādhya dharmāḥ udāhṛtāḥ iti evam anyatara asiddhā vyāpaka avyāpaka bhedena dvātriṃśakam śatam te ca punar vyadhikaraṇa viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya sandigdhā samartha viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhedena dvānavatam śatam draṣṭavyāj 
NV_1.2.4^13	 evam aprasiddha āśrayaḥ bhaya anyatara pakṣa aprasiddhyā dvātriṃśakam śatam te ca punar pūrvavat eva dvānavatam śatam yathā agnimān deśaḥ dhūmavat tvāt asti ca ātma icchā ādi guṇa tvāt asamartha avyāpaka asiddha viśeṣaṇānām udāharaṇam anityaḥ śabdaḥ prayatna anantarīyaka tve sati kṛtaka tvāt avyāpa kāsam artha viśeṣyāṇām udāharaṇam anityaḥ śabdaḥ pratyaya bheda bhedi tvena upalabhyamāna tvāt vyadhikaraṇa viśeṣyāṇām udāharaṇam asti pradhānam bhedānām anvaya darśanāt vyadhikaraṇa viśeṣaṇānām udāharaṇam rūpa rasa gandha sparśa śabdāḥ candana śabdāt atyantam vibhinna arthāḥ samudāya samudāyya sambhave sati tena vyapadiśyamāna tvāt 
NV_1.2.4^14	 etat eva vyadhikaraṇa viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyasya udāharaṇam viparyayena anyathā siddha udāharaṇam anyeṣām abhyāsāt nityaḥ śabdaḥ sandigdha aprasiddha viśeṣaṇānām udāharaṇam yathā sandihyamāna dhūma ādi bhāve agnimān deśaḥ dhūmavat tve sati prakāśaka tvāt viparyayeṇa sandigdha viśeṣyāḥ draṣṭavyāḥ evam sandigdha aprasiddha aprasiddhāḥ ubhaya anyatara siddhāḥ vyāpaka avyāpaka bhedena catuḥṣaṣṭiḥ bhavanti iti te ca punar pūrvavat bhedena śata trayam caturaśītam evam anyathā siddha bhedaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ evam viruddha viśeṣaṇā viruddha viśeṣyāḥ ca sarvatra draṣṭavyāḥ iti eṣām tu udāharaṇāni hetvābhāsa vārttike draṣṭavyāni svayam ca abhyūhyāni 
NV_1.2.4^15	 te ete hetavaḥ hetvābhāsāḥ ca asaṅkīrṇa viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhedena dve sahasre dvātriṃśike asiddha ādi samuccayena anantaḥ bhedaḥ iti sādhya āvṛttayaḥ tu asattvāt na viśeṣaṇa yoginaḥ iti atas na abhidhīyante iti te ete vidyamāna sādhya vyāpaka avyāpaka dharmāḥ prapañcataḥ uktāḥ tatra mukhya asiddha bhedāḥ ṣoḍaśa te ete pakṣa āvṛttayaḥ anaikāntikāḥ tu asaṅkīrṇā mukhyatas ṣaṭ eva sādhya vyāpaka varge viruddhāḥ catvāraḥ eva tasmin antimaḥ tu pakṣa mātra dharma tvāt anupasaṅhāryaḥ śeṣāḥ hetvābhāsāḥ te asiddha anaikāntika viruddha avyāpaka asiddha bhedena saṅkīrṇāḥ udāharaṇeṣu svayam abhyūhyāḥ iti ke cit tu viruddha avyabhicāriṇam anaikāntikam varṇayanti 
NV_1.2.4^16	 tat na asattvāt na ayam asti iti uktam upetya tasya pañcaviṃśatidhā bhedam pañcānām hetūnām sarūpa asa rūpa pratibandhānāt pañca pañcakāḥ bhavanti iti teṣām tu sarveṣām na udāharaṇāni santi iti tena na udāhriyante te ete hetvābhāsāḥ saṃkṣepeṇa īya tāḥ bhedena bhedavantaḥ teṣām saṃgraha artham hetvābhāsānām vibhāga uddeśa artham sūtram lakṣaṇataḥ eva pañcatvam gamyate iti ced yāni etāni pañca hetvābhāsānām lakṣaṇa sūtrāṇi taiḥ eva pañcatvam gamyate iti niyama artham sūtram anarthakam na anarthakam lakṣaṇasya itaretara vyavacchedaka tvāt itaretara vyavacchedakam lakṣaṇam na punar niyama artham na hi niyamaḥ lakṣaṇena gamyate iti 
NV_1.2.5^1	 teṣām anaikāntikaḥ savyabhicāraḥ etasmin ante niyataḥ aikāntikaḥ viparyayāt anaikāntikaḥ kaḥ punar ayam vyabhicāraḥ sādhya tajjātīyāni avṛtti tvam yat khalu sādhya tajjātīya vṛtti tve sati anyatra vartate tat vyabhicāri tad vṛtti tvam vyabhicāraḥ sarvaḥ ayam padārtha bhedaḥ anta dvaye avatiṣṭhate anyatra prameyāt nityaḥ ca anityaḥ ca vyāpakaḥ ca avyāpakaḥ ca iti evam ādiḥ tatra yaḥ hetuḥ upāttaḥ ubhau antau āśritya pravartate saḥ anaikāntikaḥ anaikāntikaḥ iti kim punar ayam paryudāsaḥ uta prasajya pratiṣedhaḥ iti kim ca atas yadi paryudāsaḥ sarva anaikāntika taikāntikāt anyaḥ anaikāntikaḥ iti bruvataḥ sarvaḥ anaikāntikaḥ prāptaḥ evam ca ekaḥ hetvābhāse iti prāptam atha prasajya pratiṣedhaḥ tathā api aikāntika abhāvaḥ anaikāntikaḥ iti prāptam tasya ca vyabhicāraḥ arthaḥ na asti iti ayuktaḥ anaikāntikaḥ hetvābhāsaḥ 
NV_1.2.5^2	 na ayam paryudāsa pakṣaḥ kim tu prasajya pratiṣedhaḥ prasajya pratiṣedhe abhāvaḥ iti ced na abhāvaḥ dharma viśeṣaka tvāt dharmaḥ ayam viśiṣyate yaḥ ekānte sanniyataḥ dharmaḥ iti na bhavati na punar abhāvaḥ abhāve viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyā sambhavān na abhāvaḥ ekānta sanniyataḥ na anaikāntikaḥ sanniyate iti katham abrāhmaṇa vat iti yathā brāhmaṇa śabdaḥ prasajya pratiṣedha viṣaya tvena pravartamānaḥ yat uttaram padam tat pratiṣedhati na punar ayam abhāvam pratipādayati tathā iha api iti adoṣaḥ udāharaṇam nityaḥ śabdaḥ asparśavat tvāt śabdasya asparśa tvam iti ṣaṣṭhyā bhedaḥ pradarśyate kim punar tat sparśa anādhārasya sva ātma satta anubhavaḥ asparśa tvam sparśa anādhārasya sattā sambandhaḥ vā ubhayam ca śabda vyatiriktam iti arthavatī ṣaṣṭhī kutas punar etat tad bhāve bhāvāt tad abhāve abhāvāt iti 
NV_1.2.5^3	 yat khalu sparśa vat sattām anubhavati na tatra asparśa śabdaḥ prasajyate yat ca asat tatra api na prayujyate iti yat asparśa vat sattām anubhāvati tatra prayujyate iti vākya artha anujñānāt ca padārtha abhyanujñā sparśānādhārasya vastunaḥ sattyā sambandhaḥ iti yaḥ vākya arthaḥ saḥ eva asparśa tva śabdasya arthaḥ atideśa anupapattiḥ anukta tvāt iti ced anaikāntikaḥ savyabhicāraḥ iti na kva cit anaikāntikaḥ uktaḥ yatas iha anaikāntika grahaṇāt savyabhicāraḥ gamyeta atas na yuktam anaikāntikaḥ savyabhicāraḥ iti na idam ayuktam lokataḥ tad adhigateḥ yat vastu lokataḥ na gamyate tatra śāstram arthavat yat punar lokataḥ eva gamyate tatra upadeśaḥ anarthakaḥ lokataḥ ca etat gamyate ubhayānta sanniyataḥ anaikāntikaaḥ iti yadi ca yat lokataḥ gamyate tat anuktam iti manyase duḥkha ādīni api deśayitavyāni kim idam duḥkham iti 
NV_1.2.5^4	 tasmāt paripelavam etat iti avyāpaka tvāt alakṣaṇam etat iti ced atha api idam syāt anaikāntika lakṣaṇena na sarvaḥ anaikāntikaḥ vyāpyate yathā asādhāraṇaḥ iti na anena eva saṃgrahāt katham iti vyāvṛtti dvāreṇa abhidhīyamānaḥ ayam ubhaya anta vyāvṛtteḥ anaikāntikaḥ iti apare punar prakaraṇa samam anaikāntikaḥ eva antar bhāvayanti katham iti nityaḥ ātmā śarīrāt anya tvāt iti śarīrāt kila anyat nityam anityam ca dṛṣṭam atas anaikāntikaḥ iti taiḥ tu na lakṣaṇa vyabhicāraḥ avagataḥ na udāharaṇa vyabhicāraḥ iti anaikāntikaḥ savyabhicāraḥ iti etat lakṣaṇam vyabhicāriṇaḥ yadi ca anena prakaraṇa sama saṃgrahaḥ bhavati prāptaḥ tāvatā lakṣaṇasya vyabhicāraḥ na punar udāharaṇa vyabhicārāt anaikāntika lakṣaṇa vyabhicāraḥ iti lakṣaṇasya tu ubhayam doṣaḥ lakṣya avyāptiḥ alakṣya vyāptiḥ ca iti vakṣyamāṇakam ca prakaraṇa samasya lakṣaṇam īkṣitavyam 
NV_1.2.6^1	 siddhāntam abhyupetya tad virodhī viruddhaḥ iti kaḥ asya sūtrasya arthaḥ abhyupagata artha virodhī viruddhaḥ evam ca sarva an ukta viruddha saṃgrahaḥ yāvān kaḥ cit viruddha bhedaḥ sarvaḥ asau anena saṃgṛhītaḥ yasmāt abhyupagatam bādhate abhyupagatena vā bādhyate nanu evam ekaḥ hetvābhāsaḥ viruddhaḥ prāpnoti satyam ekaḥ eva hetvābhāsaḥ viruddhaḥ tasya tu sāmānyena viruddha tvena saṃgṛhītasya pañcadhā upadeśaḥ yathā prameyam iti anena ṣoḍaśa padārthāḥ iti pṛthak abhidhānam tarhi viruddhasya na kartavyam 
NV_1.2.6^2	 na na kartavyam sāmānyatas adhigatasya viśeṣa jñāpana artham yathā prameyasya eva tatra anaikāntika ādi hetu ābhāsaḥ dvi rūpaḥ anaikāntika ādiḥ viruddhaḥ ca etasmin tu viruddha tā eva iti asādhāraṇa tayā tṛṇa ulapa ādi nyāyena niṣkṛṣya abhidhīyate tasmāt anaikāntika ādiṣu nimitta dvaya samāveśāt saṃjñā dvaya samāveśaḥ vivakṣita tad jātīyāni avṛtti tvena anaikāntika tvam hetu viṣaya svarūpa bādhā rūpeṇa tu viruddhaḥ evam sarvatra udāharaṇam tat etat trailokyam vyakteḥ apaiti nitya tva pratiṣedhāt apetam api asti vināśa pratiṣedhāt iti 
NV_1.2.6^3	 vināśa pratiṣedhāt iti anena vākyena nityam abhyanujñātam nitya tva pratiṣedhāt iti anena pratiṣiddham ete te vākye paraspara artha bādhite tayoḥ ca paraspara artha bādhāḥ virodhaḥ pratijñā hetvoḥ vā virodhaḥ yaḥ vā pratijñā hetvoḥ virodhaḥ sa viruddha hetu ābhāsaḥ nanu pratijñā hetvoḥ virodhaḥ pṛthak upadiṣṭaḥ nigraha sthāne pṛthak ca hetvābhāsaḥ tasmāt na pratijñā hetvoḥ virodhaḥ vaktavyaḥ iti na eṣa doṣaḥ ubhaya āśrita tvāt virodhasya vivakṣātaḥ anyatara nirdeśaḥ pratijñā hetvoḥ virodhaḥ iti pratijñā hetū āśritya ubhayāśritaḥ bhavati tatra yadā pratijñayā virodhaḥ vivakṣitaḥ tadā pratijñā virodhaḥ iti ucyate 
NV_1.2.6^4	 yadā pratijñāyāḥ hetu virodhaḥ hetoḥ vā pratijñā virodhaka tvam tadā viruddhaḥ hetuḥ iti atas pratijñā virodhaḥ vā hetu virodhaḥ vā iti adoṣaḥ hetu virodha udāharaṇam nityaḥ śabdaḥ utpatti dharmaka tvāt iti pratijñā virodhasya udāharaṇam na asti ātmā iti pratijñā hetu virodha udāharaṇam guṇa vyatiriktam dravyam artha antarasya anupalabdheḥ iti hetu virodha udāharaṇam na asti ekaḥ bhāvaḥ samūhe bhāva śabda prayogāt iti samūhaḥ iti bruvāṇenāikaḥ abhyupagataḥ bhāvaḥ bhavati ekatva samuccayaḥ hi samūhaḥ iti 
NV_1.2.7^1	 kasmāt prakaraṇa cintā tattva anupalabdheḥ yasmāt upalabdha tattve arthe nivartate cintā tasmāt sāmānyena adhigatasya yā viśeṣataḥ anupalabdhiḥ sā prakaraṇa cintām pravartayati iti udāharaṇam nityaḥ śabdaḥ anitya dharma anupalabdheḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ nitya dharma anupalabdheḥ atas eva prakaraṇam iti atas na hetuḥ nanu ayam sādhya aviśiṣṭaḥ eva yathā śabdasya nitya tvam sādhyam tathā anitya dharma anupalabdhiḥ api iti na aviśiṣṭaḥ tasya eva prakaraṇa pravṛtti hetoḥ dharmasya hetu tvena upādānāt yatra sādhyena samānaḥ dharmaḥ hetu tvena upādīyate sa sādhya aviśiṣṭaḥ yatra punar prakaraṇa pravṛtti hetuḥ eva prakaraṇa samaḥ ye tu saṃśaya hetu tvāt prakaraṇa samāna aikāntikayoḥ abhedam varṇayanti teṣām pratyakṣa anaikāntika prakaraṇa samānām abhedaḥ prāpnoti pratyakṣam api saṃśaya kāraṇam iti samūhaḥ saṃśayasya kāraṇam iti atas na pratyakṣe prasaṅgaḥ 
NV_1.2.7^2	 sāmānya darśanam viśeṣa avyavasthā viśeṣa smṛtiḥ ca samūhaḥ iti saṃśayasya kāraṇam na ekam pratyakṣam atas na pratyakṣe prasaṅgaḥ samūhaḥ kāraṇam iti abhidhānāt apratiṣedhaḥ samūhaḥ kāraṇam iti evam bruvatā na pratyakṣasya saṃśaya kāraṇa tvam pratiṣiddham bhavati tasmāt prasaṅgataḥ tad avasthaḥ eva iti ubhaya dharma anupalabdhau anyatara dharma upādānam prakaraṇa samsya arthaḥ yatra khalu ubhaya viśeṣa anupalabdhi ḥ tatra anyatara viśeṣasya upādānam yat prakaraṇa apanodāya sa prakaraṇa samaḥ hetvābhāse ubhaya viśeṣaṇa anupalabdheḥ abhidhāna aśakya tvāt na hi ubhaya viśeṣa anupalabdhiḥ śakyā pradarśayitum śarīrāt anya tvam tu na sūtra arthaḥ na hi ayam śarīrāt anya tvam upalabhamānaḥ api yadā tattvam upalabhate tadā pravartate iti yadā tu tattvam na upalabhate śarīrāt anya tvam upalabhamānaḥ api tadā pravartate iti śarīrāt anya tvam ca anāika antikam atas ca na sūtra arthaḥ 
NV_1.2.8^1	 sādhyena aviśiṣṭaḥ yaḥ sādhana dharmaḥ sādhya vat prajñāpayitavyaḥ sa sādhya samaḥ hetvābhāsaḥ tasya udāharaṇam dravyam chāyā gatimat tvāt iti yathā eva dravya tvam chāyāyāḥ sādhyam tathā gatimat tvam api iti gatimat tvam deśa antare darśanāt iti ced atha api idam syāt gatimatī iyam chāyā deśa antare darśanāt iti yat khalu deśa antareṣu upalabhyate tat gatimat yathā kumbhaḥ tathā ca chāyā tasmāt gatimatī iti na āśraya asiddha tvāt evam api ayam āśraya asiddhaḥ hetuḥ sati dravya bhāve chāyāyāḥ deśa antare darśanam samartham syāt dravya bhāvaḥ ca asiddhaḥ tasmāt āśraya asiddheḥ na hetuḥ abhyupetya deśa antare darśanam tasya anyathā siddheḥ asiddhaḥ 
NV_1.2.8^2	 yat eva deśa antare darśanam chāyāyāḥ tat anyathā saṃbhavati anyathā ca bhavat na artham sādhayati iti katham anyathā āvaraṇa santānāt asannidhi santānaḥ tejasaḥ iti āvarake dravye sarpati tejasaḥ asannidhi viśiṣṭam dravyam yat yat upalabhyate tat tat śāyā iti ucyate saḥ ayam asiddhaḥ tredhā bhavati prajñāpanīya dharma samānaḥ āśraya asiddha anyathā asiddhaḥ ca iti nityaḥ śabdaḥ asparśavat tvāt iti etat na udāharaṇam na hi asparśa tvam śabdasya jñāpanīyam na āśraya asiddham na anyathā siddham iti yathā tu asmābhiḥ sūtram varṇitam tathā ca udāhṛtam tathā ayam asambaddhaḥ doṣaḥ na sūtra arthaḥ vijñātaḥ na akṣara arthaḥ na hetvābhāsaḥ na dṛṣṭānta ābhāsaḥ iti 
NV_1.2.9^1	 yasya apadiśyamānasya kāla atyayena eka deśaḥ yujyate saḥ eka deśa atyayāt kāla atyaya apadiṣṭaḥ kāla atītaḥ iti ucyate udāharaṇam nityaḥ śabdaḥ saṃyoga vyaṅgya tvāt iti upalabdhi kāle saṃyogaḥ na asti saḥ ayam saṃyogaḥ hetu viśeṣaṇa tvena upāttaḥ upalabdhi kālam atyeti yadā upalabhyate tadā saṃyogaḥ na asti dāru vraścane dāruparaśu saṃyoga nivṛttau śabda upalabdhi iti nanu ayam anaikāntikaḥ eva saṃyoga vyaṅgya tvāt iti anityam api saṃyogena vyajyamānam dṛṣṭam yathā ghaṭaḥ iti na saṃyoga vyaṅgya tvena anavasthānasya sādhya tvāt na brūmaḥ nityaḥ śabdaḥ iti api tu avatiṣṭhate śabdaḥ iti ayam pratijñā arthaḥ tathā ca saṃyoga vyaṅgya tvāt iti ayam hetuḥ na anaikāntikaḥ na hi anavasthitam kim cit saṃyogena vyajyamānam dṛṣṭam iti avayava viparyāsa vacanam api na sūtra arthaḥ sāmarthyāt 
NV_1.2.9^2	 na hi paścāt abhidhīyamānaḥ hetuḥ udāharaṇa sādharmyāt iti etat dhetu lakṣaṇam jahāti ajahat dhetu lakṣaṇam na hetvābhāsaḥ bhavitum arhati iti avayava viparyāsa vacanam aprāpta kālam iti nigraha sthānam uktam tat eva punar ucyate iti samīkṛte abhidhānāt nigraha sthānam iti ced atha manyase yasmāt samīkṛte pakṣe paścāt abhidhīyate tatas nigraha sthānam iti kena samīkṛtaḥ iti vaktavyam hetu anabhidhānena yadi hetu anabhidhānena samīkṛtaḥ kim atra hetoḥ asāmarthyam etat asya asāmarthyam yat ayam paścāt abhidhīyate iti na etat dhetoḥ asāmarthyam yat ayam paścāt abhidhīyate iti api tu vaktuḥ iti na hi svatantraḥ hetuḥ sādhanam api tu sādhayitṛ tantraḥ tantra tvāt na hetu doṣaḥ sāmarthyāt ca iti uktam tasmāt avayava viparyāsa vacanam na sūtra arthaḥ na samīkṛta abhidhānam iti 
NV_1.2.10–1.2.12^1	 vacana vighātaḥ yaḥ kriyate sāmānya śabdasya viśeṣa aneka sambandhi tve sati avivakṣita adhyāropeṇa chalam tat veditavyam tat trividham iti niyama artham pūrvavat anekadhā bhinnam chalam saṃgṛhyate iti aviśeṣa abhihite arthe iti sūtram aviśeṣa abhihitam sāmānya śruti vākyam padam vā aviśeṣa abhihitam ucyate vākyam sāmānya śruti yathā nava kambalaḥ ayam iti padam sāmānya śruti yathā aśvaḥ aśvaḥ iti aviśeṣa śabdān abhidhānam prayoga abhāvāt na hi aviśeṣa śabdena kasya cit abhidhānam saṃbhavati na ca asya prayogaḥ yuktaḥ iti vākyam ca sarvam uccarat viśeṣam eva pratyāyayati iti sāmānya pratyāyanam ayuktam na prakaraṇa ādīn antareṇa śruti mātrāt tad upapatteḥ yadā prakaraṇa ādi nirapekṣam vākyam uccāryate śvetaḥ dhāvati iti tadā vākya śruti sāmānyāt śrotuḥ sandehaḥ 
NV_1.2.12^2	 sandehe sati avivakṣitam artham adhyāropya pratiṣedhati evam pade api iti artha grahaṇam śabda nirākaraṇa artham artha viṣayam chalam na śabda viṣayam iti na hi ayam pratiṣeddhum śaknoti na ayam nava kambala śabdaḥ iti tasya pratyavasthānam jñātvā ajñātvā vā prayogāt pratiṣedha anupapattiḥ yadi tāvat nava kambalasya artham buddhvā na ayam nava kambalaḥ iti pratyavatiṣṭhate tadā artha antaram āha anyat buddhyate anyat pratiṣidhyate iti atha punar na eva nava kambalasya artham budhyate tathā api ajñānam iti 
NV_1.2.13	 sambhavataḥ arthasya ati sāmānya yogāt asambhūta artha kalpanā sāmānyacchalam sāmānyasya vivakṣita artha atikramaḥ atisāmānyam udāharaṇam vidyā caraṇa sampannaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ iti paraḥ tu brāhmaṇa tvam vidyā caraṇa sampadaḥ hetuḥ iti kṛtvā pratyavatiṣṭhate stuti arthe vākye anyathā ākāram pratyavasthānam ubhayathā doṣaḥ buddhvā abuddhvā vā iti 
NV_1.2.14	 dharma vikalpa nirdeśe iti sūtram dharma vikalpa nirdeśa śabdena abhidhāna dharmaḥ dvedhā abhidhīyate pradhānam bhāktaḥ ca mañcāḥ iti kāṣṭha saṃghāteṣu pradhānaḥ mañca śabdaḥ krośana kriyāyāḥ asambhavam īkṣitvā sthāniṣu puruṣeṣu bhāktaḥ saḥ ayam abhidhāna abhidheya vyavahāraḥ evam vyavasthitaḥ yaḥ etasmin anyathā ākāram pratiṣedhaḥ tat upacāra= chalam iti asya api pūrvavat pratiṣedhaḥ jñātvā ajñātvā vā iti 
NV_1.2.15–1.2.16	 vākchalam eva upacāra= chalam tat aviśeṣāt iti sūtram eka tvam aviśeṣāt kaḥ aviśeṣaḥ iha api artha antara kalpanā tatra api iti aviśeṣāt iti asya hetoḥ anena sūtreṇa asiddha tām udbhāvayati katham asiddhiḥ ekatra vastu sadbhāvaḥ pratiṣidhyate na eva kroṣṭāraḥ mañcā iti ekatra vastu abhyanujñāya kambala yogam abhyupagamya kambalasya aneka tā dharmaḥ pratiṣidhyate iti yatra dharmaḥ pratiṣidhyate yatra ca dharmī saḥ ayam ati mahān viśeṣaḥ 
NV_1.2.17	 atha manuṣe kim naḥ anena viśeṣaṇena iha api artha antara kalpanā tatra api iti aviśeṣe vā kiñcid sādharmyāt eka= chala prasaṅgaḥ kaḥ asya sūtrasya arthaḥ virodhaḥ dvi tvam abhyanujñātam nivartate iti katamena punar nyāyena dvi tvam abhyanujñātam vāc chala upacāra= chalayoḥ eka tvam bruvatā sāmānyacchalam anyat iti abhyanujñātam bhavati viśeṣaṇa ānarthakyam vā yadi sarvam chalam evam eva iti abhyupagamaḥ vākchalam eva upacāra= chalam tat aviśeṣāt iti vyartham viśeṣaṇam katham ekatva prasaṅgaḥ kim cit sādharmyāt yadi anartha antara kalpanā viśeṣāt eka tvam sarvam chalam ekam prāpnoti kim cit sādharmyāt iti kim punar tat vacana vighātaḥ artha vikalpa upapattiḥ ca sarvasmin chalaḥ iti 
NV_1.2.18	 sādharmyeṇa pratyavasthānam vaidharmyeṇa pratyavasthānam jātiḥ iti prathama pakṣa anuyogam darśayati sthāpanāyām satyām pratīpam avasthānam pratyavasthānam pratipakṣa vat iti sūtra arthaḥ tu yathāśruti na punar udāharaṇa sādharmyeṇa udāharaṇa vaidharmyeṇa vā iti kim artham idam ucyate vyāpana artham yadi yathāśruti sūtra arthaḥ bhavati tadā sarva jātayaḥ vyāpyante yena kena cit sādharmyam yena kena cit vaidharmyam iti lakṣaṇe jātīnām avyāpaka tvam tu doṣaḥ bhāṣye tu udāharaṇa sādharmyam udāharaṇa vaidharmyam ca udāharaṇa artham iti yathā ca udāharaṇena evam anudāharaṇena api iti 
NV_1.2.19	 anyathā sthitasya anyathā abhihitasya apratipattiḥ vipratipattiḥ sva para artha uttara asamvittiḥ apratipattiḥ samarthe sādhane nigraha sthāna prāptau katham apratipattiḥ vipratipattiḥ yadā ayam sādhayitā samarthena sādhanena upāttena pareṇa jāti ādibhiḥ ākulīkṛta uttaram na pratipadyate tadā katham apratipattiḥ katham vā vipratipattiḥ iti tadā api sādhanasya eva sāmarthya aparijñānāt asamartham etat sādhanam iti apratipattiḥ vipratipattiḥ iti 
NV_1.2.20	 tāḥ etāḥ jātayaḥ kiyatyaḥ bhavanti kiyanti vā nigraha sthānāni iti vastu avadhāraṇa artham āha tad vikalpāt jāti nigraha sthāna bahu tvam iti sādharmya vaidharmyābhyām pratyavasthānasya vikalpāt tayoḥ ca vipratipatti apratipattyoḥ vikalpāt bahvaḥ jātayaḥ bahūni ca nigraha sthānāni bhavanti iti katamāḥ jātayaḥ sādharmya pratyavasthānāt katamāḥ ca vaidharmya pratyavasthānāt katamāni nigraha sthānāni vipratipatti vikalpāt katamāni vā apratipatti vikalpāt bhavanti iti pratiyoge viśeṣa lakṣaṇeṣu utprekṣaṇīyāni iti ete pramāṇa ādayaḥ padārthāḥ uddiṣṭāḥ lakṣitāḥ ca yathoddeśam ca yathālakṣaṇam ca parīkṣā vartiṣyate iti tantra pratijñā saṃsāraḥ tad nivṛttiḥ ca saṃvidā uddeśaḥ lakṣaṇam ca eva tattvānām iha kīrtitam 
NV_2.1.1^1	 trividhā ca asya śāstrasya pravṛttiḥ uddeśaḥ lakṣaṇam parīkṣā ca iti uktam tatra uddeśa lakṣaṇe pūrvā asmin adhyāyaḥ eva vyākhyāte parīkṣā vartiṣyate iti tatra yathoddeśaḥ tathā lakṣaṇam tathā parīkṣā iti sthānavatām parīkṣā vacanam iti pūrvam pramāṇam uddiṣṭam lakṣitam ca pūrvam eva tat parīkṣyate iti avasara prāptāni pramāṇāni vilaṅghya saṃśayaḥ parīkṣyate iti kim artham krama bhedaḥ parīkṣā aṅga tvāt saṃśayasya pūrvam saṃśayaḥ parīkṣyate tathā ca uktam vimṛśya pakṣa pratipakṣābhyām artha avadhāraṇam nirṇayaḥ iti nanu ca uktam na ayam nirṇaye niyamaḥ vimṛṣya pakṣa pratipakṣābhyām sarvatra nirṇayaḥ iti vāde pakṣa pratipakṣābhyām eva śāstre ca vimarṣa varjam iti śāstre ca ayam vicāraḥ tasmāt na saṃśaya pūrvakaḥ iti 
NV_2.1.1^2	 saṃśaya pūrvakaḥ hi vicāraḥ tarka viṣayaḥ eva na ayam tarka viṣayaḥ iti satyam na ayam nirṇaye niyamaḥ vicāre hi niyamaḥ nirṇayaḥ evam ca anyathā ca vicāraḥ saṃśaya pūrvakaḥ eva yat api uktam vāde śāstre ca vimarṣa varjam iti vādi prativādinau adhikṛtya tat uktam śāstra abhyupagame ca vādi prativādinoḥ na saṃśayaḥ ubhayoḥ niścita tvāt śāstre ca na saṃśayaḥ niścitasya vastunaḥ śāstra abhyupagamena abhyupagamāt tatra vādi prativādinau tāvat vicārayataḥ kim nitya sādhanam balīyaḥ āho anitya sādhanam iti śāstre api ca vicāraḥ sādhanasya sāmarthya asāmarthya parijñāna artham tatra ca saṃśayaḥ iti tasmāt saṃśaya pūrvakaḥ eva vicāraḥ tad mūlaka tvāt parīkṣā vidheḥ iti saṃśayaḥ pūrvam parīkṣyate iti tatra saṃśayaḥ vastu svarūpa anavadhāraṇa ātmakaḥ pratyayaḥ 
NV_2.1.1^3	 nirukta vyāghātaḥ iti ced anavadhāraṇa ātmakaḥ ca pratyayaḥ ca iti vyāhatam na pratyayasya svarūpa anavadhāraṇāt avyavaccheda ātmakam sva rūpam asya paricchidyate na punar anena viṣaya svarūpam avadhāryate iti saḥ ayam saṃśayaḥ samāna dharma upapatteḥ iti evam ādiyaḥ tasya ākṣepaḥ samāna aneka dharma adhyavasāyāt iti evam ādi sūtram tasya yathāśruti utthānam iti samānasya dharmasya adhyavasāyāt saṃśayaḥ na samāna dharma mātrāt upalabhyamānaḥ dharmaḥ saṃśaya hetuḥ iti dharma dharmi grahaṇena vā saṃśaya abhāvaḥ iti samānam anayoḥ dharmam upalabhaḥ iti dharma dharmi grahaṇe kva saṃśayaḥ iti dharmiṇaḥ artha antara bhāvāt vā na saṃśayaḥ na hi anyasmin upalabdhe anyatra saṃśayaḥ iti 
NV_2.1.1^4–2.1.5^1	 atha vā na samāna dharmasya adhyavasāyaḥ saṃśayasya kāraṇam vyavaccheda ātmaka tvāt saṃśaye ca tad abhāvāt iti etena aneka dharma adhyavasāyāt iti vyākhyātam adhigatān adhigatayoḥ na saṃśayaḥ adhigate ca vastuni saṃśayaḥ na yuktaḥ nirṇīta tvāt na anadhigate adṛṣṭa tvāt na samāna dharma adhyavasāyāt eva saṃśayaḥ sati api abhāvāt sati api samāna dharma adhyavasāye na dṛṣṭaḥ saṃśayaḥ yathā kṛtaka tvāt śabde na samāna dharma adhyavasāyāt eva saṃśayaḥ anyathā api bhāvāt anyathā api dṛṣṭaḥ saṃśayaḥ yathā viruddha avyabhicāri dharma dvaya sannipāte 
NV_2.1.1^4–2.1.5^2	 tattva anupalabdheḥ ca saṃśayaḥ yathā prakaraṇa same eka vṛtti tvāt ca na ayam samānaḥ eka vṛttiḥ ayam dharmaḥ na ca eka vṛttiḥ samānaḥ bhavitum arhati etena vipratipatti avyavasthā adhyavasāyāt iti pratyuktam na vipratipatti avyavasthā adhyavasāyāt iti prāk uktam vipratipatti avyavasthā adhyavasāyāt saṃśayaḥ na vipratipatti mātrāt avyavasthā mātrāt vā na vipratipattiḥ asti iti sūtra arthaḥ avyavasthā na vedyate iti sūtra arthaḥ samāna dharma ādīnām dharmāṇām sātatyāt nityam saṃśayaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NV_2.1.6^1	 asya uttaram yathā ukta adhyavasāyāt eva tad viśeṣa apekṣāt saṃśaye na asaṃśayaḥ na atyanta saṃśayaḥ vā na sūtra artha aparijñānāt iti sūtra arthaḥ yat punar etat dharma dharmi grahaṇe saṃśaya abhāvaḥ iti tat na aparijñānāt na brūmaḥ yaḥ asau dharmī upalabhyate tasya dharmam upalabhaḥ iti api tu yau mayā pūrvam sthāṇu puruṣau upalabdhau tayoḥ ayam samānaḥ dharmaḥ upalabhyate iti etena eka vṛtti tvāt iti parihṛtam yat punar etat na artha antara adhyavasāyāt anyatra saṃśayaḥ iti tat na anabhyupagamāt na artha antara bhāva mātram mayā saṃśaya hetu tvena upādīyate kim tu artha antara viśeṣaḥ kaḥ punar asau viśeṣaḥ dharma dharmi bhāvaḥ dharmaḥ upalabdhe dharmiṇi saṃśayaḥ iti parihāram manyate na punā rūpa sparśayoḥ dharma dharmi bhāvaḥ iti ayam ca na parihāraḥ iti paśyāmaḥ kim kāraṇam artha antara tva anivṛtteḥ yathā eva rūpa sparśayoḥ artha antara bhāvaḥ tathā dharma dharmiṇoḥ iti na yuktaḥ artha antara darśanāt artha antare saṃśayaḥ 
NV_2.1.6^2	 atra api tat eva uttaram na anabhyupagamāt iti na brūmaḥ artha antara darśanāt artha antare dharmiṇi saṃśayaḥ api tu samāna dharma ādi viśiṣṭa dharmi darśanāt viśeṣavati dharmiṇi eva saṃśayaḥ iti yat api etat sārūpya abhāvāt iti viśeṣān avadhāraṇam ubhayoḥ sārūpyam yathā eva samāna dharma darśanena viśeṣaḥ na avadhāryate tathā saṃśayena api iti kāraṇa sadbhāvāt ca kārya sadbhāvaḥ iti na sārūpya nirdeśaḥ ayam api tu kārya kāraṇa dharma nirdeśaḥ tathā ca kārya antareṣu api etat asti iti na hi kim cit kāryam kāraṇa sadbhāvam antareṇa sambhavati iti etena aneka dharma adhyavasāyāt iti pratiṣedhaḥ parihṛtaḥ yaḥ eva samāna dharma adhyavasāye parihāraḥ saḥ eva aneka dharma adhyavasāye api iti yat punar etat adhigatān adhigatayoḥ abhāvāt iti na samāna artha aparijñānāt iti na brūmaḥ anyasmin adhigate anyatra saṃśayaḥ iti api tu sāmānyatas a dhik ate dharmiṇi viśeṣa an avadhāraṇa ātmakaḥ pratyayaḥ saṃśayaḥ iti yat punar etat sati api abhāvāt iti na samāna artha aparijñānāt 
NV_2.1.6^3	 na hi kṛtaka tvam samānaḥ dharmaḥ anyathā samāna dharmasya abhidhānāt samānaḥ dharmaḥ iti yaḥ vivakṣita tad jātīya anyavṛttiḥ sa samānaḥ na punar kṛtaka tvam evam yat punar etat na samāna dharma adhyavasāyāt eva anyathā api darśanāt iti tat na pratiṣedhāt anavadhāraṇāt ca viruddha avyabhicāri dharma adhyavasāyāt saṃśayaḥ iti pratiṣiddham etat na ca etat avadhāryate samāna dharma adhyavasāyāt eva na anyasmāt iti anyasmāt api saṃśayaḥ aneka dharma adhyavasāyāt iti uktam anavadhāraṇena eva tattva anupalabdhiḥ iti pratyuktam vipratipatti avyavasthā adhyavasāyāt eva iti anena eva pratyuktam na evam brūmaḥ vipratipatti mātrāt avyavasthā mātrāt vā saṃśayaḥ iti na ca avyavasthātaḥ saṃśayaḥ upalabdhi anupalabdhi avyavasthāyāḥ pūrva pada viśeṣaṇa tvāt pūrva pada viśeṣaṇaḥ upalabdhi anupalabdhī na svatantre saṃśaya kāraṇam tat ca sūtre eva uktam iti yat punar etat vipratipattau ca sampratipatteḥ iti na saṃjñā anyathā tvāt arthasya anyathātvam 
NV_2.1.6^4–2.1.7^1	 yasmāt vipratipatti śabdasya nimitta antara sannipāte sampratipattiḥ iti nāma kṛtam na tāvatā vipratipattiḥ na asti vipratipatteḥ ca tathā abhāvāt saṃśaya hetu tvam yat punar etat avyavasthā ātmani vyavasthita tvāt ca avyavasthāyāḥ na avyavasthā asti iti tat api na vyāghātāt avyavasthā na asti avyavasthā ātmani vyavasthitā iti vyāghātaḥ na ca nimitta antara sannipātena arthasya saṃjñā antara karaṇam arthasya tathā abhāvam bādhate yathābhūtaḥ eva arthaḥ saṃjñā antara karaṇe tathābhūtaḥ eva akaraṇe api iti yat punar etat tathā atyanta saṃśayaḥ tad dharma sātatya upapatteḥ iti tat api na sūtra artha aparijñānāt iti uktam 
NV_2.1.6^4–2.1.7^2	 na ayam samāna dharma ādibhyaḥ eva saṃśayaḥ kim tu tad viṣayāt adhyavasāyāt upalabdhi anupalabdhi avyavasthāne ca sati viśeṣa smṛti sahitāt evam ca na asaṃśayaḥ na api atyanta saṃśayaḥ anyatara dharma adhyavasāt iti ca ayuktam na eva tasmāt saṃśayaḥ iti na hi kadā cit anyatara dharma adhyavasāye sati saṃśayaḥ anyatara dharma adhyavasāyasya nirṇaya hetu tvāt iti kaḥ asya sūtrasya arthaḥ svayam na saṃśayaḥ pratiṣeddhavyaḥ pareṇa tu saṃśaye pratiṣiddhaḥ evam uttaram vācyam iti śiṣyam śikṣyati 
NV_2.1.8	 atha idānīm avasara prāptāni pramāṇāni parīkṣyante iti kim punar eṣām parīkṣyam ādau tāvat sambhavaḥ kim pramāṇāni santi uta na santi iti sat asatoḥ sāmānyāt prameya tvāt viśeṣa adarśanāt ca saṃśayaḥ vyudasya saṃśayam paraḥ pakṣa parigraheṇa pratyavatiṣṭhate pratyakṣa ādīnām aprāmāṇyam traikālya asiddheḥ iti asya arthaḥ triṣu api kāleṣu pramāṇāni na artham sādhayanti iti 
NV_2.1.9–2.1.10	 pūrvam hi pramāṇa siddhau iti sūtram na indriya artha sannikarṣa apekṣam jñānam utpadyate iti sūtra arthe vyāghātaḥ doṣaḥ yadi pūrvam jñānam naḥ indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ tasya kāraṇam iti yat uktam indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam jñānam iti tat vyāhanyate paścāt siddhau iti sūtram na pramāṇa nimittā prameya saṃjñā iti vyāhatam pramāṇam antareṇa prameyam ātmānam labhate iti na pramāṇa āyattā prameya siddhiḥ 
NV_2.1.11^1	 yugapad siddhau iti sūtram indriya arthānām buddhīnām ca sannipāte sati yugapad bhāve sati krama vṛtti tvam dṛṣṭam na syāt iti vyāghātaḥ doṣaḥ yugapad jñāna anutpattiḥ iti ca uktam tat vyāhanyate iti atra samādhiḥ upalabdhi hetoḥ upalabdhi viṣayasya ca arthasya pūrva apara sahabhāva aniyamāt iti vākyasya asiddha tā udbhāvanam arthaḥ pratyakṣa ādīnām aprāmāṇyam iti ca pratijñā padayoḥ vyāghātaḥ pratyakṣa ādīni na artham sādhayanti iti ayam arthaḥ ayam ca vyāhataḥ katham iti 
NV_2.1.11^2	 pratyakṣa ādīni na artham sādhayanti iti ca yathā idam vastu naḥ upalabhyate iti idam ca naḥ upalabhyate iti vyāghātaḥ evam pratyakṣa ādīni ca na artham sādhayanti iti ca katham ca anyathā pratyakṣa ādīni na hi ete pratyakṣa ādi śabdāḥ artha sādhaka bhāvam antareṇa kṛtārthāḥ bhavanti iti dharma pratiṣedhāt ca pratyakṣa ādi abhyupagamaḥ pratyakṣa ādīnām aprāmāṇyam iti evam bruvatā na pratyakṣa ādīni pratiṣiddhāni api tu pramāṇa tvam dharmaḥ iti atha bhāvasya asvatantra tvāt tāni api pratiṣiddhāni pratyakṣa ādīnām aprāmāṇyam iti bhāva abhidhānam etat 
NV_2.1.11^3	 asvatantraḥ ca bhāvaḥ iti bhāva pratiṣedhāt tadvatām pratiṣedhaḥ iti evam api anivṛttaḥ vyāghātaḥ pratyakṣa ādīnām abhāvaḥ pratipādyaḥ pratyakṣa ādīni ca na santi iti kena abhāvam pratipādayasi na pratyakṣa ādi abhāve anyaḥ pratipādana upāyaḥ kaḥ cit asti viśeṣa pratiṣedhāt ca pramāṇa antara abhyanujñā pratyakṣa ādīnām aprāmāṇyam iti evam bruvatā pratyakṣa ādi vyatireki pramāṇam abhyanujñātam bhavati vyartham vā viśeṣaṇam pratyakṣa ādīnām aprāmāṇyam iti atha na pramāṇa antaram abhyanujñāyate kim asya viśeṣaṇasya sāmarthyam pratyakṣa ādīni na pramāṇāni iti 
NV_2.1.11^4	 na eva pramāṇāni santi iti evam vaktavyam iti etat api vyāhatam pramāṇāni naḥ eva santi pratipādayasi ca iti yat api tad pramāṇa antaram abhyanujñeyam tatra api traikālya asiddheḥ iti ayam anuṣaktaḥ hetuḥ yat ca triṣu api kāleṣu na pratipādayati katham tasya pramāṇa tvam iti anivṛttaḥ vyāghātaḥ atha dharma pratiṣedhaḥ eva ayam tathā api yāni tāni prāmāṇya vyatiriktāni pratyakṣa ādīni abhyanujñāyante rāja puruṣa pratiṣedha nyāyena teṣām kaḥ svabhāvaḥ iti anivṛttaḥ anuyogaḥ vyāghātaḥ ca 
NV_2.1.11^5	 artha antara anabhyupagame ṣaṣṭhyāḥ tad hitasya ca arthaḥ vaktavyaḥ yadi pratyakṣa ādi vyatiriktam na prāmāṇyam asti pratyakṣa ādīnām iti kaḥ ṣaṣṭhī arthaḥ atas avaśyam vidhīyamānaḥ pratiṣiddha mānaḥ vā dharmaḥ abhyupeyaḥ tad abhyupagame ca pratyakṣa ādīnām pṛthak svarūpam vaktavyam iti anivṛttaḥ vyāghātaḥ etena tad hita arthaḥ vyākhyātaḥ yaḥ ca ayam hetuḥ traikālya asiddheḥ iti ayam api vyadhikaraṇaḥ traikāla viṣaya tvāt iti tri kālasya bhāvaḥ traikālyam tasya asiddhiḥ iti na pramāṇa dharmaḥ 
NV_2.1.11^6	 atha ayam arthaḥ triṣu api kāleṣu pramāṇāni na artham sādhayanti iti tathā api hetu arthaḥ na asti pratijñā arthena ākṣipta tvāt yaḥ eva pratijñā arthaḥ na pramāṇāni artham sādhayanti iti saḥ eva hetu arthaḥ triṣu api kāleṣu na artham sādhayanti iti yat punar etat pramāṇena pramīyamānaḥ arthaḥ prameyam iti evam bhavati iti samākhyā hetoḥ traikālya yogāt apratiṣedhaḥ pramāṇam iti prameyam iti ca asyāḥ samākhyāyāḥ nimittam tri kāla yogi pramāsyate pramīyate prāmāyi vā anena iti pramāṇam pramāsyate pramīyate prāmāyi vā iti prameyam 
NV_2.1.11^7	 evam ca sati pramāsyate ayam arthaḥ bhaviṣyati asmin hetutaḥ upalabdheḥ iti prameyam iti etat sidhyati anabhyanujñāne ca vyavahāra anupapattiḥ iti virodhaḥ doṣaḥ yaḥ ca traikālikam pramāṇa prameya vyavahāram na pratipadyate tasya pācakam ānayaḥ iti evam ādi loka vyavahāraḥ virudhyate iti pratyakṣa ādīnām aprāmāṇyam traikālya asiddheḥ iti evam ādi vākyam pramāṇa pratiṣedhaḥ atha anena pratyakṣa ādīnām kim kriyate kim sambhavaḥ nivartyate atha asambhavaḥ jñāpyate iti kim ca atas 
NV_2.1.11^8	 yadi tāvat sambhavaḥ nivartyate tat na yuktam vyāghātāt pratiṣedha artha aparijñānāt ca sambhavaḥ nivartyate iti evam bruvāṇena pramāṇāni abhyupagatāni bhavanti na hi asataḥ nivṛttiḥ na ca pratiṣedhasya etat sāmarthyam yat vidyamānam padārtham anyathā kuryāt jñāpaka tvāt ca na sambhava nivṛttiḥ jñāpakaḥ ayam pratiṣedhaḥ na sambhava nivartakaḥ iti atha asambhavaḥ jñāpyate iti ced pramāṇa lakṣaṇa prāptaḥ tarhi pratiṣedhaḥ atas vyāghātaḥ iti pramāṇāni na artham sādhayanti iti pratiṣedhasya pramāṇa lakṣaṇa abhyanujñānāt iti 
NV_2.1.12^1	 evam ca traikālya asiddheḥ pratiṣedha anupapattiḥ iti ayam api pratiṣedhah triṣu api kāleṣu naḥ upapannaḥ iti ayam sūtra arthaḥ traikālya asiddheḥ pratiṣedha anupapattiḥ iti evam abhidadhānena abhyupagatam bhavati pratyakṣa ādīnām aprāmāṇyam traikālya asiddheḥ iti na eṣaḥ doṣaḥ tasya sva vacana vyāghāta codanāt sva vacana vyāghātaḥ mayā codyate na abhyupagamyate katham iti yat khalu triṣu api kāleṣu asādhakam tat asādhanam iti bruvatā pratiṣedhasya asādhaka tvam sva vācāḥ eva abhyupatam bhavati yathā nāma kaḥ cit sva aṅguli jvālayā param didhakṣuḥ sa ca param dahet mā vā sva aṅguli dāham tāvat anubhavati iti yaḥ ca ayam pratiṣedhaḥ pratyakṣa ādīni na artham sādhayanti iti kim ayam pratyakṣa ādīnām sāmarthya pratiṣedhaḥ uta sattā pratiṣedhaḥ 
NV_2.1.12^2	 yadi sāmarthya pratiṣedhaḥ na pratyakṣa ādīni pratiṣiddhāni teṣām ca sāmarthya pratiṣedhāt anyat pratyakṣa ādīnām svarūpam vyaktavyam iti pūrvavat prasaṅgaḥ atha sattā pratiṣedhaḥ tatra api katham na santi iti kim sāmānyatas atha viśeṣataḥ iti yadi sāmānyatas pratyakṣa ādi grahaṇam vyartham evam vaktavyam na pramāṇāni santi iti na ca dharmiṇām pratiṣedhe kaḥ cit nyāyaḥ iti atha viśeṣa pratiṣedhaḥ tathā api pramāṇa antara abhyupagamaḥ na hi anabhyupagata sāmānyasya viśeṣa pratiṣedhaḥ avakāśam labhate pratyakṣa ādīnām aprāmāṇyam traikālya asiddheḥ pratyakṣa ādīnām prāmāṇyam traikālya siddheḥ iti ca vākyayoḥ ekārtha tā vā syāt bhinna artha tā vā yadi ekārtha tā pratyakṣa ādīnām prāmāṇyam traikālya siddheḥ iti evam eva vaktavyam abhinna arthe ca ete vākye iti ca kutas pratipattiḥ 
NV_2.1.12^3	 yadi pramāṇataḥ anivṛttaḥ vyāghātaḥ atha anyatas tat pramāṇam iti saṃjñā bheda mātram atha bhinna arthe tat kena jñātam traikālya asiddeḥ traikālya siddheḥ iti ca anayoḥ vākyayoḥ bhinnaḥ arthaḥ iti pratyakṣa ādīni na santi iti ca nāstinā samāna adhikaraṇaḥ pratyakṣa ādi śabdaḥ na pratyakṣa ādīnām abhāvam śaknoti pratipādayitum na hi ayam nāstinā ghaṭa śabdaḥ samāna adhikaraṇaḥ ghaṭa abhāvam pratipādayati api tu geha ghaṭa saṃyogam vā sāmarthyam vā kāla viśeṣam vā ghaṭasya pratiṣedhati evam anena api pramāṇa samāna adhikaraṇena nāstinā pramāṇānām na abhāvaḥ śakyaḥ pratipādayitum api tu anena api tantra antara abhyupagatānām vā pratiṣedhaḥ sāmarthya pratiṣedhaḥ vā kāla viśeṣe vā pratiṣedhaḥ iti sarvathā pramāṇāni abhyupagatāni bhavanti tāni ca abhyupagatāni anena pratiṣedhena pratiṣidhyante iti vyāghātaḥ 
NV_2.1.12^4	 pramāṇānām ca asattvam pratipādyamānam katham pratipādyate kasya pratipādyate kaḥ ca pratipādayitā apratipannaḥ pratipādyate iti pratipannaḥ ca pratipādayati kena pratipannaḥ yadi pramāṇena vyāghātaḥ pramāṇa anabhyupagamāt atha anyathā na dṛṣṭāntaḥ asti pratipādya pratipādakayoḥ ca bheda abhyupagame vyāghātaḥ yadi pratipādyam pratipādayitāram ca bhedena pratipadyate bheda pratipādaka pramāṇa abhyupagamāt vyāghātaḥ atha bhedam na pratipadyase kva kim pratipādyate iti anivṛttaḥ vyāghātaḥ pramāṇāni na santi iti pratijānānaḥ paryanuyojyaḥ katham na santi iti yadi pramāṇam bravīti vyāghātaḥ atha na bravīti arthaḥ asya na sidhyati tat evam etat vākyam yāvat yāvat vicāryate tāvat tāvat pravilīyate iti 
NV_2.1.13	 traikālya asiddheḥ iti asya hetoḥ udāharaṇam upādīyate na vā yadi upādīyate tadā vyāghātaḥ bhavati pratyakṣa ādīnām ca aprāmāṇya abhyupagamāt upādīyamānam api na artham sādhayati iti vyartham atha sādhayati iti vyāghātaḥ atha naḥ upādīyate apradarśitam hetu arthasya sādhaka tvam iti anupasaṃhṛtaḥ ca hetu dṛṣṭānte na sādhakaḥ iti saḥ ayam hetuḥ sarvaiḥ pramāṇaiḥ vipratiṣiddhaḥ viruddhaḥ bhavati siddhāntam abhyupetya tad virodhī viruddhaḥ iti vākya arthaḥ hi asya siddhāntaḥ sa ca vākya arthaḥ pramāṇāni na artham sādhayanti iti idam ca pramāṇānām upādānam artha sādhanāya pratyakṣa ādīnām aprāmāṇyam traikālya asiddheḥ iti buddhi vivakṣā prayatna vāyu udīraṇa tālu abhighāta oṣṭha praspanda ādīn avarjayan buddhyā vākyam uccārayasi sthāṇu kaṇṭaka sarpa ādīn ca pariharan pāda viharaṇa ādi karoṣi te ete vākya pravṛttī pramāṇa pratiṣedhāt na sambhavataḥ iti 
NV_2.1.14	 atha sva vākya āśrita pramāṇa vyatirekeṇa pramāṇāni pratiṣidhyante evam sati na sarvam pramāṇam pratiṣiddham bhavati yaḥ ca nyāyaḥ sva vākya āśrita pramāṇa abhyupagame saḥ eva anya vākya āśrita pramāṇa abhyupagame api iti vi iti ayam upasargaḥ viśeṣa pratiṣedhe na vyāghāte kim uktam bhavati kāni cit pramāṇāni pratiṣidhyante kāni cit abhyanujñāyante iti yāni sva vākya āśritāni tāni abhyanujñāyante yāni para vākya āśritāni tāni pratiṣidhyante iti yat ca idam vākyam pratyakṣa ādīnām aprāmāṇyam traikālya asiddheḥ iti kim idam pramāṇa svarūpam atha na yadi pramāṇa svarūpam tadā vyāghātaḥ atha na tathā api na anena kaḥ cit arthaḥ pratipādyate iti vyartham 
NV_2.1.15	 traikālya apratiṣedhaḥ ca śabdāt ātodya siddhi vat tad siddheḥ iti sūtram yat tat pūrvam uktam upalabdhi hetoḥ upalabdhi viṣayasya ca arthasya pūrva apara sahabhāva aniyamāt yathādarśanam vibhāga vacanam iti tad utthāna jñāpana artham iti itas sūtrāntasya utthānam iti kasmāt punar tatra eva idam sūtram naḥ uktam iti aviśeṣāt tatra ca abhidhīyate iha vā na kaḥ cit viśeṣaḥ iti sarvathā tāvat ayam arthaḥ prakāśayitavyaḥ iti ekām ca vidhām udāharati śabdāt ātodya siddhi vat iti śeṣayoḥ tu vidhayoḥ yathā ukte udāharaṇe veditavye yathā pūrva siddham ātodyam paścāt siddhena śabdena anumīyate vīṇā vādyate veṇuḥ pūryyate iti yaḥ asau vīṇā veṇu śabdayoḥ asādhāraṇaḥ dharmaḥ vīṇā ādi nimitta tvam tad upalabhamānaḥ śabdasya vīṇā śabdaḥ veṇu śabdaḥ iti pratipadyate pūrva siddham ātodyam paścāt siddhaḥ śabdaḥ iti sahabhāve udāharaṇam dhūma darśanāt agnim dhūma viśeṣaṇam pratipadyate pūrva siddhaḥ upalabdhi hetuḥ ādityaḥ paścāt siddhānām ghaṭa ādīnām prakāśakaḥ iti 
NV_2.1.16^1	 pramāṇam prameyam iti ca iyam samākhyā samāveśena vartate samākhyā nimitta vaśāt samāveśaḥ aniyamaḥ samākhyā nimitta vaśāt samākhyā nimitta tantra tvāt iti pramāṇa prameya saṃjñayoḥ nimittam upalabdhi sādhana tvam upalabdhi viṣaya tvam ca yadā punar ekam vastu aneka nimitta sambandhi bhavati tadā katham tadā nimitta tantra tvāt samākhyāyāḥ tat vastu anekena nimittena sambandhe sati aneka śabda abhilāpyam asya ca arthasya jñāpana artham sūtram prameyā ca tulā prāmāṇya vat iti kim uktam bhavati yathā guru tva parimāṇa jñāna sādhanam tulā dravyam samāhāra guru tvasya iyattā pariccheda nimitta tvāt pramāṇam suvarṇa ādinā ca paricchidyamāneyattā eṣā tulā iti pariccheda viṣaya tvena vyavatiṣṭhamānā prameyam udāharaṇa mātram ca etat evam anavayavena tantra arthaḥ veditavyaḥ yathā ca pramāṇa prameya samākhye tathā sarve kāraka śabdāḥ nimitta samāveśa niyamena vartante tathā ca laukikam udāharaṇam ekam anekena kāraka śabdena abhidhīyate 
NV_2.1.16^2	 vṛkṣaḥ tiṣṭhati iti sva sthitau svātantryāt kartā kim punar vṛkṣasya sva sthitau svātantryam kāraka antara anapekṣa tvam na hi vṛkṣaḥ tiṣṭhan sva sthitau kāraka antaram prayuṅkte yadā ayam sthiti śabdaḥ gati pratiṣedha vacanaḥ bhavati tadā evam yadā api asteḥ abhidhāyakaḥ tadā api asteḥ vyakti nimitta tvena avatiṣṭhamānaḥ asti vyanakti iti kartā iti ucyate yadā api geha sambandha ādi abhidhāyakaḥ bhavati asti śabdaḥ yathā devadattaḥ gehe tiṣṭhati iti pratinirdiṣṭe asti iti gamyate tadā na sattām āha gati pratiṣedham api tu deva datta geha sambandham tadā api deva datta geha sambandha anubhava kriyā tasyām api na kāraka antarāṇi prayuṅkte iti svatantraḥ bhavati yadā api ayam abhagna vacanaḥ sthiti śabdaḥ tiṣṭhati vṛkṣaḥ na bhagnaḥ iti tadā api sva sthitau na kāraka antarāṇi prayuṅkte iti svatantraḥ bhavati samudāya eka deśam vā sva sthitau prayuṅkte vṛkṣaḥ mūlaiḥ tiṣṭhati iti prāsādaḥ stambhaiḥ ghriyate iti pūrva apara pratyaya eka viṣaya tā vā sthitiḥ 
NV_2.1.16^3	 yat vastu prāk prasiddham punar nimitta antara sannipāte sati upalabhyate yat tasya anekā yugapad kāla pratyaya viṣaya tvam sā sthitiḥ tasyām sthitau asya yat sahakāri sādhanam cakṣuḥ ādi tat karaṇam iti cakra bhrānti pradīpa pratyaya vat mithyā pratyayaḥ saḥ iti ced na pramāṇa abhāvāt atha manyase naḥ eva kim cit vastu ayugapad kāla aneka pratyaya viṣayaḥ bhavati yadi na bhavati katham tarhi saḥ eva ayam vṛkṣaḥ tiṣṭhati iti pratyayaḥ na hi kadā cit ādyena darśanena saḥ eva ayam vṛkṣaḥ tiṣṭhati iti pratyayaḥ bhavati dṛṣṭaḥ anya tve api sthiti pratyayaḥ cakram bhramat tiṣṭhati iti pradīpaḥ jvalan tiṣṭhati iti anavasthiteṣu nānā bhūteṣu cakra bhrānti pradīpa ādiṣu ye ete tad bhāva pratyayāḥ atasmin tat iti mithyā pratyayāḥ ete yathā ca ete mithyā pratyayāḥ evam vṛkṣa ādi sthitiṣu api iti na pramāṇa abhāvān na hi bhavatā pramāṇam kim cit vṛkṣa ādīnām nānā tva sthāpakakam abhidhīyate iti mithyā pratyayāḥ ca samyak pratyaya anusāreṇa bhavanti iti kva amī samyak pratyayāḥ bhavanti iti vaktavyam 
NV_2.1.16^4	 atha bhavataḥ kāla antara avasthāne kim pramāṇam uktam pramāṇam rūpa rasa gandha sparśa pratyayānām eka aneka nimitta tvam pratisandhānāt iti kāryasya ādhāra tvena vā kāraṇasya kārya kāla anubhavanam iti yat yasya ādhāraḥ bhavati tat tasya sadbhāva kālam anubhavati yathā kṣīrasya kuṇḍam kāraṇam ca kārya adhikaraṇam atas tena api kārya kālaḥ anubhavanīyaḥ iti anādhāram eva iti ced atha manyase apratītya kāraṇam kāryam utpadyate iti kva kim vartate iti tatra dṛṣṭānta abhāvāt 
NV_2.1.16^5	 na hi kaḥ cit ubhaya pakṣa sampratipannaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ asti kāryam anādhāram asti iti samānam kāryam ādhāra vat iti atra api na dṛṣṭāntaḥ asti samānam iti anuttaram abhyupagamāt abhyupagatam tāvat bhavatā na asmad pakṣe dṛṣṭāntaḥ asti kim tu bhavat pakṣe api na asti iti virodhaḥ iti ced atha manyase na mayā abhyupagamyate dṛṣṭānta abhāvaḥ kim tu bhavat pakṣe virodhaḥ codyate katham iti yaḥ anupapadyamāna dṛṣṭāntaḥ pakṣaḥ sa asādhīyān iti bruvāṇaḥ sva siddhāntam bādhate iti tat na aparijñānāt na bhavatā asmad pakṣaḥ vyajñāyi na sva pakṣaḥ 
NV_2.1.16^6	 asmad pakṣe tāvat kāryam ādhāra vat iti etat prasiddham bhavat pakṣe api rūpa ādayaḥ kāryāḥ ca ādhāravantaḥ ca iti abhyupagama virodhaḥ vā bhūta bhautika samudāyaḥ dravyam iti yadi rūpa ādīn anāśritāt na pratipadyase kaḥ asya tat hitasya arthaḥ bhautikāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ iti yat ca uktam maṇiḥ prabhāyāḥ āśrayaḥ tad gati sthiti vikāra anuvidhānāt kuṇḍam badarāṇām āśrayaḥ tad vaśena āpātāt tailasya tilaḥ āśrayaḥ tad vaśena asyandanāt iti evam ādi tat vyāhanyate anāśritāḥ ca rūpa ādayaḥ svatantrāḥ ekam upanibandhanam vastu antareṇa tila mudga māṣa ādi vat vibhajyeran na tu vibhajyante tasmāt paratantrāḥ iti
