NV_2.1.16^7	 tasmāt vyavasthitam etat smṛtyā saha pūrva apara pratyaya eka viṣaya tā vā sthitiḥ iti darśanena āptum iṣyamāṇa tvāt vṛkṣaḥ karma karmaṇi kaḥ kāraka arthaḥ kriyā viṣaya tvam yat khalu kriyāyāḥ viṣaya bhāvena vyavatiṣṭhate iti tat karma anena karma lakṣaṇena tathā yuktam ca anīpsitam iti saṃgṛhītam ānantarya pratipattiḥ karaṇasya sādhakatama tva arthaḥ vṛkṣeṇa candramasam jñāpayati iti vṛkṣam gṛhītvā atha anantaram candramasam pratipadyate iti vṛkṣaḥ karaṇa kāraka śabda vācyaḥ 
NV_2.1.16^8	 karmaṇā āptum abhīṣṭam sampradānam yat vastu karmaṇā abhiprepsitam bhavati tat sampradāna saṃjñakam vṛkṣāya udakam āsiñcati iti āsicyamānam udakam karma tena karmaṇā udakena vṛkṣam prāpnoti iti vṛkṣaḥ sampradānam bhavati apagacchati avatiṣṭhate yat tat apādānam yathā vṛkṣāt patati vṛkṣaḥ upādāna saṃjñakaḥ yat patati tat apagacchati tasmin apagacchati avatiṣṭhate vṛkṣaḥ iti dhṛti hetuḥ adhikaraṇam yasmin yat ādheyam tasya ādheyasya yat dhṛti hetuḥ tat adhikaraṇam yathā vṛkṣe vayāṃsi iti vṛkṣa sambandhaḥ vayasām guru tva pratibandhe kāraṇam iti vṛkṣaḥ adhikaraṇa śabda vācyaḥ evam ca sati na dravya mātram kārakam na kriyā mātram kim uktam bhavati na ayam kāraka śabdaḥ kriyā mātre pravartate na dravya mātre na hi dravyam śuddham upalabhamānaḥ kāraka śabdam prayuṅkte na api kriyām kevalām api tu yadā kriyā dravya sambandham upalabhate tadā sāmānyena kāraka śabdena abhidhatte kārakam iti sāmānyam ca kārakāṇām kriyā nimitta tvam 
NV_2.1.16^9	 avivakṣite viśeṣe kriyā nimitta tve kevale vivakṣite kārakam iti śabdaḥ pravartate yadā tu viśeṣaḥ vivakṣyate tadā tu asādhāraṇena kāraka dharmena itaretara vyāvṛttena svātantrya ādinā viśeṣena viśiṣyamāṇam vastu kartā karma karaṇam iti ca vyapadiśyate sarvasya ca kārakasya sva kriyā nimittaḥ kartṛ vyapadeśaḥ pradhāna kriyā sa vyapekṣaḥ tu kāraka śabda prayogaḥ evam ca śāstram kārake janake nirvartake kasyāḥ kriyāyāḥ iti tathā vyapadeśaḥ tasmāt naḥ idam sva kriyā mātram apekṣya uktam kim tu pradhāna kriyām 
NV_2.1.16^10	 tasyām eva pradhāna kriyāyām kim cit ārāt upakārakam kim cit āsanna upakārakam iti kim cit katham cit upakaroti tad apekṣāḥ ca kartṛ ādi śabdāḥ iti tat uktam purastāt yadi kriyā sambandha nimittakaḥ kāraka śabda prayogaḥ pacati eva pācaka śabdaḥ pravarteta na apākṣīt pācakaḥ pakṣyati iti vā pācakaḥ iti na śakteḥ traikālya avasthānāt śaktiḥ triṣu api kāleṣu avatiṣṭhate śakti apekṣaḥ ca atīta anāgatayoḥ kāraka śabda vyapadeśaḥ pacati apākṣīt pakṣyati iti śakteḥ traikālya avasthānāt traikālya vyaktiḥ ayuktā yathā 
NV_2.1.16^11	 yathā eva hi dravyam tri kāla yogi tathā śaktiḥ api iti yathā dravye traikālyam na vyajyate evam śaktau api iti apacati api pacati iti syāt pakṣyati pācakaḥ apākṣīt pācakaḥ iti etat na syāt na eṣaḥ doṣaḥ kriyā sambandhasya śakti vyakti hetu tvāt kriyāḥ iti anena śabdena dhātu arthaḥ abhidhīyate tasya yat pradhānam sādhanam sa kartā sa ayam kartā yadā anayā kriyayā sambadhyate tadā śaktim vyanakti kā punar iyam śaktiḥ kriyā kartṛ vyatiriktaḥ kartṛ dharmaḥ sāmarthyam upāya parijñānam ca kriyā sambandhena vyajyate yadā upāya parijñānam sāmarthyam kriyā sambandhaḥ tadā mukhyaḥ śabdaḥ pravartate pacati pācakaḥ iti yadā tu kriyā sambandham antareṇa upāya parijñāna sāmarthya mātra upādāne anyatam avaikalyāt pācaka śabdaḥ pravartate tadā upacārataḥ apākṣīt pācakaḥ pakṣyati pācakaḥ iti kāraka śabdaḥ ca ayam pramāṇam prameyam iti kutas kriyā viśeṣa yogāt yathā eva amī pācaka ādi śabdāḥ kriyā viśeṣa yoge sati pravartante tathā pramāṇa prameya śabdau api iti 
NV_2.1.17–2.1.18	 asti bhoḥ kāraka śabdānām nimitta samāveśāt niyamaḥ pratyakṣa ādīni pramāṇāni saṃvedyamānāni ca prameyam upalabdhi viṣaya tvāt tatra idam cintyate kim etāni pratyakṣa ādīni sva upalabdhau pratyakṣa ādi vyatiriktam pramāṇa antaram prayojayanti atha niḥsādhanāḥ eva pramāṇa upalabdhiḥ iti kim ca atas pramāṇataḥ siddheḥ pramāṇānām pramāṇa antara siddhi prasaṅgaḥ pramāṇa viṣayāyāḥ siddheḥ yadi pramāṇam sādhanam pramāṇa antaram prāpnoti pratyakṣa ādīnām sādhya tvāt na sādhyam sādhanam bhavati iti atha pramāṇam antareṇa niḥsādhanāḥ eva pramāṇeṣu upalabdhiḥ tad vinivṛtteḥ vā pramāṇa siddhi vat prameya siddhiḥ yathā pramāṇāni sva upalabdhau nivartante evam prameya siddhau api iti 
NV_2.1.19^1	 asya uttaram na pradīpa prakāśa siddhi vat tad siddheḥ iti pradīpa prakāśa vat tad siddheḥ iti pradīpa prakāśaḥ ghaṭa ādi upalabdhi sādhanasya aṅga tvāt pramāṇam sa ca pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ eva upalabhyate na asau ātma upalabdhau pratyakṣa ādi vyatireki pramāṇam prayojayati taiḥ eva upalabhyate tathā pramāṇāni api pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ eva upalabhyante iti dṛṣṭānta mātram etat kaḥ atra nyāyaḥ iti ayam nyāyaḥ ucyate pratyakṣa ādīni sva upalabdhau pramāṇa antara aprayojakāni pariccheda sādhana tvāt pradīpa vat yathā pradīpaḥ pariccheda sādhanam sva upalabdhau na pramāṇa antaram prayojayati tathā pramāṇāni 
NV_2.1.19^2	 tasmāt tāni api pramāṇa antara aprayojakāni iti siddham sāmānya viśeṣavat tvāt ca yat sāmānya viśeṣa vat tat sva upalabdhau na pratyakṣa ādi vyatireki pramāṇam prayojayati yathā pradīpaḥ iti saṃvedya tvāt ca yat saṃvedyam tat pratyakṣa ādi vyatirikta pramāṇa aprayojakam yathā pradīpaḥ iti āśrita tvāt kāraṇa tvāt ca iti evam ādi pradīpa vat indriya ādayaḥ api pratyakṣa aṅga tvāt pratyakṣa ādi vyatirikta pramāṇa antara aprayojakāḥ iti samānam tena eva tasya agrahaṇam iti ced atha manuṣe pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ pratyakṣa ādīnām upalabdhau tena eva tat eva gṛhyate iti prāptam 
NV_2.1.19^3	 na ca etat asti na hi sādhyam sādhanam bhavati iti na eṣaḥ doṣaḥ artha bhedasya lakṣaṇa sāmānyāt pramāṇa lakṣaṇena anekaḥ arthaḥ saṃgṛhītaḥ tatra kena cit kasya cit grahaṇam iti adoṣaḥ yathā uddhṛtena udakena āśaya sthasya yathā uddhṛtam udakam gṛhītvā āśaya stham api evam bhūtam iti pratipadyate iti na punar evam abhidhīyate tena eva tasya grahaṇam api tu tathābhūtena tathābhūtasya na ca ayam ekāntaḥ na tena eva tasya grahaṇam bhavati iti bhavati api kadā cit saḥ eva jñātā jñeyaḥ bhavati yadā ātmānam jānīte iti nimitta bhedaḥ atra iti ced 
NV_2.1.19^4	 atha manyase yadā ayam ātmā jñātā tadā anya nimittam yadā jñeyaḥ tat anyat iti samānam yathā eva jñātā sukha ādi sambandha apekṣaḥ tat viśeṣaṇam ātmānam pratipadyate aham sukhī aham duḥkhī ca iti tathā pramāṇam api pramāṇa viṣaya tvena avatiṣṭhamānam prameyam iti pratyakṣa ādīnām ca aviṣayasya anupapatteḥ yadi kaḥ cit viṣayaḥ pratyakṣa ādi viṣayaḥ syāt pratipadyemahi pratyakṣa ādi vyatiriktam pramāṇam sa ca na śakyaḥ kena cit pratipādayitum sarvam idam sat ca asat ca pratyakṣa ādīnām eva viṣayaḥ tasmāt pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ eva upalabhyate 
NV_2.1.20^1	 apare tu hetu viśeṣa parigraham antareṇa dṛṣṭānta mātram pradīpa prakāśa sūtreṇa upādadate yathā kila pradīpa prakāśaḥ pradīpa antara prakāśam antareṇa gṛhyate tathā pramāṇāni api pramāṇa antaram antareṇa grahīṣyante iti tān prati idam ucyate kvacid nivṛtti darśanāt anivṛtti darśanāt ca kvacid anekāntaḥ yathā pradīpa prakāśaḥ tathā pramāṇāni na punar yathā sthālī ādi rūpam tathā pramāṇāni iti kaḥ atra niyama hetuḥ sthālī ādi rūpa prakāśane ca pradīpa prakāśaḥ na nivartate kasmāt evam na pramāṇāni ayam ca pradīpa prakāśaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ pramāṇa pakṣe bhavatu mā bhūt prameya pakṣe iti tatra api niyama hetuḥ vaktavyaḥ pradīpa prakāśaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ bhavatu mā bhūt sthālī ādi rūpam dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti atra api niyama hetuḥ vaktavyaḥ iti sa ayam ubhayathā anekāntaḥ viśeṣa hetu parigraham antareṇa dṛṣṭāntaḥ prasaktaḥ viśeṣa hetu parigrahe sati upasaṃhāra abhyanujñānāt apratiṣedhaḥ 
NV_2.1.20^2	 yadi punar ayam pradīpa prakāśa dṛṣṭāntaḥ viśeṣa hetunā prakāśaka tva ādinā saṃgṛhītaḥ tatas ekasmin pakṣe abhyanujñāyamānaḥ na śakyaḥ pratiṣeddhum iti anekāntaḥ iti ayam doṣaḥ na bhavati iti pratyakṣa ādīnām pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ upalabdhau anavasthā iti ced yadi pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ pratyakṣa ādīni upalabhyante tāni api anyaiḥ tāni api anyaiḥ iti anavasthā anavasthāyām ca ādya pramāṇa adhigamaḥ na syāt atha vyavasthā asti ādya pramāṇa adhigatiḥ apramāṇā prasajyate na eṣaḥ doṣaḥ saṃvitti viṣaya saṃvitti nimittānām upalabdhyāḥ vyavahāra siddheḥ 
NV_2.1.20^3	 saṃvitti viṣayam saṃvitti nimittam ca upalabhamānasya saṃvitti viṣayaḥ prameyam saṃvitti nimittam pramāṇam pramāṇa prameyayoḥ upalabdhau sarvaḥ vyavahāraḥ sidhyati dharma artha sukha apavarga prayojanaḥ tad pratyanīka parivarjana prayojanaḥ ca na tu anavasthā sādhanīyam kim cit prayojanam asti yena ayam prayuktaḥ anavasthām upādadīta tasmāt pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ pratyakṣa ādīnām upalabdhiḥ na ca anavasthāḥ iti evam tāvat sāmānyatas samadhigatam etat santi pramāṇāni prameya sādhanāni iti 
NV_2.1.21^1	 atha idānīm sāmānyatas adhigatānām viśeṣa parīkṣā tatra pratyakṣam ādau uktam tat parīkṣyate iti pratyakṣa lakṣaṇa anupapattiḥ asamagra vacanāt yat idam bhavatā pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam ucyate indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam iti tat asamagram kasmāt anyāni api pratyakṣasya kāraṇāni santi tāni na uktāni yathā ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ iti evam ādīni atha indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam iti etat lakṣaṇam iti lakṣaṇam api etat na bhavati kasmāt utpatti kāraṇa apadeśāt indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam iti etat kāraṇam apadiśyate na ca kāraṇa apadeśaḥ vastunaḥ lakṣaṇam na hi ghaṭa ādeḥ kāryasya mṛd piṇḍa ādi krama utpattiḥ tad lakṣaṇam iti na ubhayathā api adoṣāt yadi kāraṇam tathā api na doṣaḥ 
NV_2.1.21^2	 atha lakṣaṇam tathā api na doṣaḥ katham kāraṇa pakṣe tāvat uktam bhavati naḥ idam kāraṇa avadhāraṇa artham sūtram iti api tu pratyakṣasya pramāṇasya yat asādhāraṇam anumāna ādi vyavacchedakam tat uktam iti naḥ ātma manaḥ saṃyoga ādiṣu prasaṅgaḥ indriya manaḥ saṃyogaḥ tarhi upasaṃkhyeyaḥ yadi asādhāraṇa kāraṇa tvāt indriya artha sannikarṣasya grahaṇam na tu etasmāt eva indriya manaḥ sannikarṣaḥ api upasaṃkhyeyaḥ iti na ukta tvāt uktam atra api na yāvat asādhāraṇam kāraṇam tat sarvam vaktavyam iti api tu anyatara grahaṇena api viśeṣitam etat lakṣaṇa pakṣe api na doṣaḥ asādhāraṇa tvāt indriya artha sannikarṣasya iti indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ pratyakṣa utpādaka tvāt kāraṇam ca samāna asamāna jātīyebhyaḥ viśeṣaka tvāt lakṣaṇam ca iti 
NV_2.1.22	 arthataḥ vai abhidhānam ātma manaḥ saṃyogasya indriya manaḥ saṃyogasya ca katham iti jñāna utpatti darśanāt na asaṃyukte dravye saṃyoga jasya guṇasya utpattiḥ iti manaḥ saṃyoga anapekṣam ca indriyam pravartate iti yugapad aneka upalabdhiḥ syāt na tu bhavati atas manaḥ sannikarṣaḥ api kāraṇam iti tat idam sūtram ukta bhāṣyam na ātma manasoḥ sannikarṣa abhāve pratyakṣa utpattiḥ iti ātma manasoḥ sannikarṣa abhāve na utpadyate buddhiḥ indriya artha sannikarṣa abhāva vat iti na ukta uttara tvāt ukta uttaram etat na idam kāraṇa avadhāraṇa artham sūtram api tu viśiṣṭa kāraṇa vacanam iti 
NV_2.1.23^1	 ye tu sati bhāvāt kāraṇa bhāvam varṇayanti yasmāt kila indriya artha sannikarṣe sati jñānam bhavati asati ca na bhavati tasmāt indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ kāraṇam iti teṣām diś deśa kāla ākāśeṣu api evam prasaṅgaḥ diś deśa kāla ākāśeṣu satsu api jñānam bhavati sati bhāvāt tāni api kāraṇam iti prāptam katamena punar nyāyena diś ādya kāraṇam sāmarthya anupalabdheḥ na hi jñāna utpattau diś ādeḥ sāmarthyam upalabhyate tasmāt akāraṇam sannidhi mātrāt iti ced atha manyase diś ādiḥ sannidhi mātreṇa jñāna utpatteḥ kāraṇam bhavati tat ayuktam sannidheḥ avarjanīya tvāt nityam diś ādi vyāpakam ca iti nitya tvāt vyāpaka tvāt ca na śakyaḥ sannidhiḥ parivarjayitum iti tatra kāraṇa bhāve hetuḥ vaktavyaḥ 
NV_2.1.23^2	 na hi sannidhi mātram hetu tve kāraṇam katham rūpa upalabdheḥ tejaḥ sparśa sadbhāva vat iti yathā rūpa upalabdhau tejasaḥ rūpa viśeṣaḥ hetuḥ na punar tejasaḥ sparśaḥ sannidhi mātreṇa sāmarthya adarśanāt rūpasya punar dṛṣṭam sāmarthyam tad bhāva abhāva anuvidhānāt upalabdheḥ yasmāt yatra rūpam bhavati tatra upalabdhiḥ yatra na bhavati na tatra upalabhyate tasmāt rūpam eva upalabdheḥ kāraṇam na sparśaḥ iti yathā cāndramasam rūpam vinā tejaḥ sparśena auṣṇyena prakāśayati apavaraka ādi sthitam ca āuṣṇyam vinā rūpeṇa na prakāśayati evam ātma indriya manaḥ artha sannikarṣebhyaḥ jñānam bhavat na diś ādibhyaḥ bhavati sannidhi mātra tvāt itareṣām ca sāmartha adarśanāt iti 
NV_2.1.24	 yadi evam ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ tarhi upasaṃkhyeyaḥ na upasaṃkhyeyaḥ gamyamāna tvāt kena gamyamāna tvāt jñāna liṅga tvāt ātmanaḥ na anavarodhaḥ jñānam ātma liṅgam iti uktam tena ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ anuktaḥ api anumeyaḥ katham punar jñānam ātmanaḥ liṅgam tad guṇa tvāt guṇa bhāva asiddhiḥ iti ced atha manuṣe guṇa abhāvaḥ eva tasya asiddhaḥ kutas ātma guṇa tvam setsyati iti na ātma samavāyāt sukha ādi vat iti na hi dravyam karma vā ātmani samavaiti tasmāt na dravyam na karma ātmani ca samavāyaḥ jñānasya sukha ādi vat tasmāt ātma guṇaḥ na pṛthivī ādi guṇaḥ sva saṃvedya tvāt yat pratyakṣam sva saṃvedyam na tat pṛthivī ādi guṇaḥ bhavati yat ca pratyakṣam sva para saṃvedyam tat pṛthivī ādi guṇaḥ yathā rūpa ādi na ca evam jñānam tasmāt ātma guṇaḥ iti uktam ca atra kim uktam na yāvat pratyakṣasya kāraṇam sarvam tat vaktavyam iti 
NV_2.1.25	 atha indriya manaḥ sannikarṣaḥ kasmāt na abhidhīyate iti tad ayaugapadya liṅga tvāt ca na manasaḥ yugapad jñāna anutpattiḥ manasaḥ liṅgam iti uktam tena manasaḥ api avarodhaḥ iti na yugapad anutpatti sūtrasya anya artha tvāt yat idam ucyate yugapad jñāna anupapattiḥ manasaḥ liṅgam iti atra jñāna kāraṇam manaḥ iti tat ayuktam anya artha tvāt anya artham tat sūtram na punar tena jñāna kāraṇa tvam manasaḥ abhidhīyate anya arthasya api tad artha prakāśaka tvam upapatti sāmarthyāt yadi api tasmin sūtre na manasaḥ jñāna kāraṇa tvam sākṣāt uktam tathā api upapatti sāmarthyāt jñāna kāraṇa tā manasaḥ iti gamyate na hi jñānam svatantram na ca cakṣuḥ ādi svatantram iti 
NV_2.1.26–2.1.28	 atha kasmāt indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ abhidhīyate katham ca naḥ ātma manaḥ sannikarṣaḥ indriya manaḥ sannikarṣaḥ vā iti pratyakṣa nimitta tvāt ca indriya arthayoḥ sannikarṣasya sva śabdena vacanam indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ pratyakṣasya eva nimittam ātma manaḥ sannikarṣaḥ pratyakṣasya anyasya ca iti indriya artha sannikarṣeṇa samāna tvāt indriya manaḥ saṃyogaḥ vaktavyaḥ yadi sādhāraṇa tvāt ātma manaḥ saṃyogasya na abhidhānam indriya manaḥ saṃyogaḥ asādhāraṇa tvāt indriya artha sannikarṣa vat vaktavyaḥ naḥ idam kāraṇa avadhāraṇa artham iti uktam na ca yāvat asādhāraṇam sarvam tat vaktavyam api tu sādhāraṇam na vaktavyam iti ayam sūtra arthaḥ indriya artha sannikarṣasya prādhānya pradarśana param idam sūtram śeṣam bhāṣye prādhānye ca hetu antaram taiḥ ca apadeśaḥ jñāna viśeṣāṇām yasmāt idam pratyakṣa jñānam utpadyamānam viṣayeṇa vā kāraṇena vā indriyeṇa vyapadiśyate iti yat ca asādhāraṇam tena vyapadeśaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yathā yava aṅkuraḥ iti 
NV_2.1.29	 vyāhata tvāt iti anena tri sūtrīm pratyācaṣṭe pratyakṣa nimitta tvāt ca indriya arthayoḥ sannikarṣasya supta vyāsakta manasām ca indriya arthayoḥ sannikarṣa nimitta tvāt taiḥ ca apadeśaḥ jñāna viśeṣāṇām iti iyam kila trisūtrī ātma manaḥ sannikarṣasya jñāna kāraṇa tvam pratiṣedhati iti vyāhatam idam bhavati jñāna liṅga tvāt ātmanaḥ na anavarodhaḥ tad ayaugapadya liṅga tvāt ca na manasaḥ iti manaḥ saṃyoga anapekṣāyām ca yugapad jñāna utpatti prasaṅgaḥ iti dṛṣṭa vyāghātaḥ atha mā bhūt vyāghātaḥ iti sarvam jñānam ātma manaḥ saṃyogāt utpadyate codya avastham eva etat kasmāt ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ na abhidhīyate iti atra uktam kim uktam na idam kāraṇa avadhāraṇa artham sūtram iti api tu viśiṣṭa kāraṇa vacanam iti 
NV_2.1.30	 yā api iyam trisūtrī pratyakṣa nimitta tvāt ca indriya arthayoḥ sannikarṣasya iti evam ādi iyam api na artha viśeṣa prābalyāt na anayā tri sūtryā ātma manaḥ saṃyogasya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ pratiṣidyate api tu prādhānyam indriya artha sannikarṣasya upapādyate prādhānyam ca upapādayatyāḥ naḥ ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ pratiṣiddhaḥ bhavati manasi kriyā kāraṇa abhidhānam supta vyāsakta manasām ca indriya arthayoḥ sannikarṣa nimitta tvāt iti abhidhānena ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ api kāraṇam iti uktam tatra manasi kriyā kāraṇam vācyam iti atha sukha duḥkha upabhogasya adṛṣṭa nimitta tvāt adṛṣṭam kāraṇam yathā eva ātmani guṇa antaram icchā janitam prayatna lakṣaṇam kriyā hetuḥ tathā ātmani saṃskāraḥ dharma adharma samākhyātaḥ vartate tena preritam manaḥ saṃyujyate vibhajyate vā tena hi apreryamāṇe manasi tatas anyasya kriyā hetoḥ abhāvāt sarva artha tā tasya guṇasya nivarteta na hi dharma adharmau antareṇa manasi ca kaḥ cit anyaḥ kriyā hetuḥ ādau sambhavati iti atas adṛṣṭam kāraṇam iti evam tāvat samadhigatam pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam 
NV_2.1.31^1	 atas param idānīm pratyakṣasya anumāne antarbhāvam kurvāṇaḥ idam āha pratyakṣam anumānam eka deśa grahaṇāt upalabdheḥ yat idam indriya artha sannikarṣāt utpadyate jñānam ayam vṛkṣaḥ iti etat kila pratyakṣam tat tu anumānam eva kasmāt eka deśa grahaṇāt vṛkṣa upalabdheḥ eka deśam ayam gṛhītvā vṛkṣam upalabhate na ca eka deśaḥ vṛkṣaḥ tatra yathā anyasya darśanāt anyasmin pratipattiḥ anumānam evam eka deśa grahaṇāt vṛkṣa pratipattiḥ anumānam iti tat yathā dhūmam gṛhītvā agni pratipattiḥ evam eka deśam gṛhītvā vṛkṣa pratipattiḥ iti 
NV_2.1.31^2	 na yaha asaṃbhavam vikalpa anupapatteḥ eka deśa grahaṇāt artha antaram pratipadyate iti kim tad artha antaram yat eka deśa grahaṇāt pratipadyate iti avayava samūha pakṣe tāvat avayava antarāṇi dravya antara utpatti pakṣe tāni ca avayavī ca iti yadi tāvat avayava samūha mātram vṛkṣam adhikṛtya ucyate etasmin pakṣe gṛhyamāṇa avayava vyatirekeṇa yāni agṛhyamāṇā anyāvayava antarāṇi sa vṛkṣaḥ atha dravya antara utpatti pakṣe āśrīyate tathā api arvāc bhāgaḥ vyavahitāni avayava antarāṇi artha antaram ca sa vṛkṣaḥ iti 
NV_2.1.31^3	 kim punar atra eka deśa grahaṇāt ayam pratipadyate kim tāvat avayava antarāṇi atha dravya antaram iti avayava samūha pakṣe tāvat vṛkṣa buddheḥ abhāvaḥ para bhāgasya avṛkṣa tvāt arvāc bhāga vat yathā eva ayam arvāc bhāgaḥ na vṛkṣaḥ evam madhya para bhāgau api na vṛkṣaḥ sā iyam avayava samūha pakṣe avṛkṣe vṛkṣa buddhiḥ utpadyamānā nirviṣayā arvāc bhāgaḥ para bhāgaḥ madhya bhāgaḥ iti etat ca na asti katham bhāgaḥ iti avayavasya etat nāma yaḥ punar artha antaram avayavinam na pratipadyate tasya avayavaḥ iti nirabhidheyam vākyam avayavaḥ ca para bhāgaḥ madhya māgaḥ arvāc bhāgaḥ ca sa ca avayavi pratyākhyānāt na yuktaḥ iti atha eka deśaḥ bhāgaḥ iti ucyate kaḥ ayam eka deśaḥ eka deśaḥ hi avayavinaḥ ādhāraḥ avayavinam ca pratyācakṣāṇena eka deśaḥ api pratyākhyātaḥ atha akārya kāraṇa bhūtānām paraspara pratyāsatti upagraheṇa eka deśa avasthānam avayava arthaḥ aho śabda artha kauśalam akārya kāraṇa bhūtāḥ ca paraspara pratyāsatti upagraheṇa ca vartante iti na ca paraspara upakāram kurvanti avayavāḥ ca abhidhīyante iti citram 
NV_2.1.31^4	 apare tu arvāc bhāga darśanena para bhāga anumānam kṛtvā pratisandhāna pratyaya jām avṛkṣe vṛkṣa buddhim adhyavasyanti etasmin pakṣe vṛkṣa buddheḥ abhāvaḥ eva katham arvāc bhāgasya para bhāgasya ca avṛkṣa tvāt na ca avṛkṣa pratisandhāna jā vṛkṣa buddhiḥ utpattum arhati iti na ca etasmin pakṣe anumānam bhavati iti arvāc bhāgam ayam gṛhītvā para bhāgam anumimīte iti na anumānasya viṣayaḥ parijñātaḥ katham aparijñātaḥ yadi tāvat evam anumimīte vṛkṣaḥ ayam arvāk bhāgavat tvāt katamaḥ asau vṛkṣaḥ yasya arvāk bhāgavat tvam dharmaḥ anabhyupagata artha antarauvayavinaḥ arvāc bhāga mātram pratyakṣam na ca dharmiṇi anupalabdhe anumānam pravartate na ca ayam jātu api dharmiṇam upalabhate avidhyamāna tvena abhyupagamāt na ca anumānam anumāne evaṃvidhasya pratisandhānasya abhāvāt na hi anumāne evaṃvidham pratisandhānam asti na ayam anumātā pūrvam anupalabhya agnim dhūma viśeṣaṇam pratipadya pratisandhatte ayam dhūmaḥ ayam ca agniḥ iti na ca pratisandhāya anumimīte agninā atra bhavitavyam iti kim kāraṇam 
NV_2.1.31^5	 vaiyarthyāt vyartham anumānam etasyām avasthāyām agneḥ viśeṣaṇa bhūtasya pratīta tvāt tasmāt na anumāne pratisandhānam asti pratisandhāya api ca na samudāye pratisandhānam na vṛkṣe na hi ayam eka deśa darśanāt samudāyam pratipadyate na vṛkṣam kim tu śeṣam samudāyinam eva kim kāraṇam samudāyi vyatirekeṇa samudāyasya asattā abhyupagamāt na hi bhavantaḥ samudāyi vyatiriktam samudāyam pratipadyante na ca āsan samudāyaḥ anumātum śakyaḥ kim ca arvāc bhāgam ayam gṛhītvā kim anyat anumimīte ayam arvāc bhāgaḥ para bhāgavān iti na yuktam anumātum arvāk bhāgasya para bhāgavat tva asambhavāt na hi arvāc bhāgaḥ para bhāgavān bhāgasya bhāga asambhavāt na hi bhāgasya aparaḥ bhāgaḥ vidyate iti atha bhāgam bhāgavantam pratipadyase na asau bhāgaḥ bhāgavān bhāgī eva asau bhāgi viṣayam ca anumānam iti na yuktam ubhayoḥ pratyakṣa tvāt ubhayam hi asya pratyakṣam arvāc bhāgaḥ ca bhāgī ca tatra arvāc bhāgavat tvena bhāginaḥ para bhāga anumānam asmad pakṣe yuktam bhavat pakṣe tu bhāga mātra darśanāt na yuktam iti 
NV_2.1.31^6	 yat ca tad arvāc bhāga darśanam na tasya liṅga liṅgi sambandha smṛti anugrahaḥ asti sambaddhayoḥ arvāc bhāga para bhāgayoḥ adṛṣṭa tvāt na hi ayam draṣṭā arvāc bhāga para bhāgayoḥ sambandham paśyati na ca arvāc bhāga para bhāgau sambaddhau na ca anubhavam antareṇa smṛtiḥ na ca smṛtim antareṇa liṅga darśanam kevalam anumānam katham punar ayam arvāc bhāga para bhāgau sambaddhau na paśyati nityam arvāc bhāgena para bhāgasya ca vyavadhānāt nityam arvāc bhāgam eva kevalam upalabhate para bhāgam tu na katham canārvāc bhāga vyavahita tvāt 
NV_2.1.31^7	 satyam na ubhayoḥ upalabdhiḥ asti ubhau tu sambaddhau satyam sambaddhau anumānam ca na śakyam ubhayoḥ adarśanāt arvāc bhāga para bhāgayoḥ ca dharma dharmi bhāva anupapatteḥ na anumānam yatra khalu anumānam bhavati tatra dharmiṇaḥ dharma prasiddhau dharma antara viṣayam anumānam na punar arvāc bhāgasya para bhāgaḥ dharmaḥ para bhāgasya na arvāc bhāgaḥ atas ca na anumānam yat ca idam ucyate pratisandhāna pratyaya jā vṛkṣa buddhiḥ iti tat ayuktam vṛkṣasya asiddhatvena abhyupagamāt na pratisandhānam 
NV_2.1.31^8	 pratisandhānam hi nāma pūrvavastu anurañjitaḥ pratyayaḥ piṇḍa antare bhavati yathā rūpam ca mayā upalabdham rasaḥ ca iti bhavat pakṣe punar arvāc bhāgam gṛhītvā para bhāgam anumāya arvāc bhāga para bhāgau iti etāvān pratisandhāna pratyayaḥ yuktaḥ vṛkṣa buddhiḥ tu kutas na tāvat arvāc bhāgaḥ vṛkṣaḥ na para bhāgaḥ iti arvāc bhāga para bhāgayoḥ ca avṛkṣa bhūtayoḥ yā vṛkṣa buddhiḥ sā atasmin tat iti pratyayaḥ atasmin tat iti pratyayaḥ na anumānāt bhavitum arhati iti pramāṇasya yathābhūta artha paricchedaka tvāt 
NV_2.1.31^9	 yaḥ ca ayam atasmin tat iti pratyayaḥ sa pradhāna anukāreṇa bhavati iti vṛkṣa buddheḥ pradhānam vaktavyam na hi agṛhīta sāmānyasya anadhyāropita tad viparīta dharmaṇaḥ vā atasmin tat iti pratyayaḥ bhavati pradhānam ca na asti vṛkṣasya anabhyupagamāt tasmāt na anumāna pratisandhānāt vṛkṣa buddhiḥ etena arvāc bhāga para bhāga pratyayāḥ api pratyuktāḥ anabhyupagata antyauvayavinaḥ cārvāc bhāgaḥ para bhāgaḥ iti etat api na asti kasmāt mahataḥ dravyasya upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya para bhāga vyavadhāyakasya etat nāma arvāc bhāgaḥ iti 
NV_2.1.31^10	 tathābhūtasya eva vyavahitasya para bhāgaḥ iti na ca bhavatā kim cit dravyam avayavi bhūtam pratipadyate yat arvāc bhāga para bhāga śabda vācyam syāt iti paramāṇuṣu tathā asanniviṣṭeṣu arvāc bhāga para bhāga vṛkṣa ādi pratyayāḥ iti ced atha manuṣe na asmābhiḥ avayavi dravyāṇi kāni cit pratipadyante kim tu teṣu eva parama aṇuṣu paraspara pratyāsatti upasaṃgraheṇa saṃsthāna viśeṣa avasthiteṣu ete śabdāḥ pravartante arvāc bhāgaḥ iti para bhāgaḥ iti ca vṛkṣaḥ iti ca iti na tathā aśabdasya artha an abhidhānāt 
NV_2.1.31^11	 tathā asanniviṣṭeṣu iti etat abhidhānam pravartate pūrva prasiddhau satyām na ca paramāṇuṣu pūrva apara bhāga ādi śabda pravṛtteḥ bījam asti yathā prasiddhe gavi gavayaḥ tathārūpaḥ iti evam tāvat avayava samūha pakṣe vṛkṣa buddheḥ abhāvaḥ iti uktam dravya antara utpatti pakṣe tu na avaya vi anumeyaḥ pratyakṣa tvāt arvāc bhāga vat yathā eva ayam arvāc bhāgam indriya sambaddham pratyakṣataḥ upalabhate tathā vṛkṣam api iti na anumeyaḥ vṛkṣaḥ atha indriya sambaddham api vṛkṣam anumeyam eva pratipadyase vṛkṣa vat arvāc bhāgaḥ api anumeyaḥ prasajyate 
NV_2.1.31^12	 tathā ca vyāhatam bhavati arvāc bhāgam ayam gṛhītvā vṛkṣam pratipadyate iti sarvam eva anumānam iti etasmin api ca pakṣe anumāna abhāvaḥ pratyakṣataḥ anadhigata tvāt dharmiṇaḥ na hi dharmiṇi pratyakṣatas anadhigate anumānam pravartate yat api atīndriyeṣu artheṣu anumānam uktam tat api na asti iti uktam na hi atīndriyah arthaḥ anumātum śakyaḥ katham iti dharmiṇaḥ anadhigata tvāt iti uktam kaḥ punar sāmānyatas dṛṣṭasya pratyakṣa pūrvaka anumānāt viśeṣaḥ yadi sarvam pratyakṣa pūrvakam eva anumānam iti ayam viśeṣaḥ pratyakṣa pūrvakam trika prasiddhau pravartate sādhya sādhana dharmī upalabdhau yatra ayam sādhyam sādhanam ca dharmiṇam ca pūrvam gṛhītvā punar dharma dharmi darśanena dharma antaram anumimīte tat pratyakṣa pūrvakam yat punar sādhana dharmam dharmiṇam ca upalabhya atyanta parokṣam dharma antaram anumimīte tat sāmānyatas dṛṣṭam iti bhavat pakṣe tu na sāmānyatas dṛṣṭāt anumānāt vṛkṣa buddhiḥ na pratyakṣa pūrvakāt dharmiṇaḥ anabhyupagamāt pratyakṣa pratiṣedhāt ca iti 
NV_2.1.32^1	 viruddhaḥ ca ayam hetuḥ eka deśa grahaṇāt vṛkṣa upalabdheḥ iti katham iti na pratyakṣeṇa yāvat tāvat api upalambhāt pratyakṣam anumānam iti evam bruvatā pratyakṣam apahnūyate pratyakṣa apahnavāt ca yat eka deśa grahaṇam pratyakṣam tat vyāhatam bhavati katham iti yat tat eka deśa grahaṇam bhavatā āśrīyate pratyakṣam tat tāvatā api ca pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam sidhyati iti na ca idam pratijñāyate sarvam pratyakṣasya viṣayaḥ kim tu yāvat indriya artha sannikarṣāt upalabhyate tāvat pratyakṣasya viṣayaḥ iti athāḥ api na pratyakṣam anumānam aprakāravat tvāt prakāra vat anumānam aprakāra vat pratyakṣam tat uktam anumāna sūtram varṇayadbhiḥ iti tri kāla viṣaya tvāt ca na anumānam pratyakṣam tri kāla viṣayam anumānam na ca evam pratyakṣam iti liṅga liṅgi sambandha smṛti anapekṣa tvāt ca na anumānam pratyakṣam 
NV_2.1.32^2	 liṅga parāmarśa jñānasya liṅga liṅgi sambandha smṛti anugrahaḥ asti na ca evam pratyakṣasya tasmāt na pratyakṣam anumānam itas ca na pratyakṣasya anumāna tva prasaṅgaḥ tad pūrvaka tvāt pratyakṣa pūrvakam anumānam na tu pratyakṣam ayam ca anayoḥ viśeṣaḥ iti indriya sambaddhāt ca na ca indriyasya anumeyena arthena sannikarṣāt utpadyate jñānam yat anumānam iti ucyate sa ayam pramāṇa dṛṣṭaḥ pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ ekatvam āsan jayatā bhedaḥ pratyākhyāyate iti na ca eka deśa upalabdhiḥ avayavi sadbhāvāt yat idam bhavatā abhidhīyate eka deśa grahaṇāt ayam vṛkṣaḥ pratipadyate iti tat anupapannam yasmāt eka deśa upalabdhiḥ ca tad sahacarita avayavī upalabdhiḥ ca na hi indriyeṇa sannikṛṣyamāṇe eka deśe tad sahacaritaḥ avayavī na sannikṛṣṭaḥ tena yathā eka deśaḥ sva sannikarṣāt upalabhyate evam avayavī api svasannikarṣāt upalabhyate iti kasmāt avayavi sadbhāvāt 
NV_2.1.32^3	 asti hi ayam eka deśa vyatiriktaḥ avayavī tasya avayava sthānasya upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya eka deśa upalabdhau anupalabdhiḥ anupapannāḥ kim kāraṇam mahat aneka dravya rūpāṇi upalambhakāni tāni eka deśa vat eka deśini api vartante tasmāt eka deśaḥ upalabhyate na eka deśī iti ayuktam na avayavinaḥ upalabdhiḥ yuktāḥ kasmāt vikalpa anupapatteḥ ayam khalu avayavī avayaveṣu vartamānaḥ ekasmin kārtsnaḥ vā vartate eka deśena vā kim ca atas yadi ekasmin kṛtsnaḥ vartate śeṣa avayava vaiyarthyam na hi śeṣaiḥ avayavaiḥ kim cana avayavinaḥ kriyante iti eka dravyaḥ ca asau avayavī bhavat naḥ upalabhyeta kim kāraṇam mahat aneka dravyavat tvasya upalambhaka tvāt na ca asya vināśaḥ prāpnoti kāraṇa dravya vibhāga asambhavāt na hi ekasya vibhāgaḥ sambhavati na ca ekena ārabhyamāṇasya mahat tvam yuktam kāraṇa bahu tva mahat tva pracaya asambhavāt 
NV_2.1.32^4	 tasmāt ekasmin na kārtsnaḥ vartate iti na api eka deśena vartate na hi asya kāraṇa vyatirekeṇa anye eka deśāḥ santi sa ayam eka deśa upalabdhau avayavi upalabhyamānaḥ na kṛtsnaḥ upalabhyate sā iyam eka deśa upalabdhiḥ nivṛttāḥ iti atha upalabhyamānaḥ avayavī katham upalabhyeta yadi gṛhyamāṇeṣu avayaveṣu kṛtsnaḥ parisamāptaḥ syāt na ca ayam gṛhyamāṇeṣu parisamāptaḥ śeṣa avayava vaiyarthyāt iti uktam aśeṣa avayava upalabdhiḥ api na asti madhya para bhāgayoḥ arvāc bhāgena vyavadhānāt tena avayavinaḥ na grahaṇa vikalpaḥ na api vṛtti vikalpaḥ ekasmin kṛtsna eka deśa śabda asambhavāt apraśnaḥ kim avayavī eka deśena vartate atha kṛtsnaḥ vartate iti na yuktaḥ praśnaḥ na avayavī kṛtsnaḥ naḥ eka deśaḥ kṛtsnam iti khalu ekasya aśeṣasya abhidhānam eka deśaḥ iti ca aneka tve sati kasya cit abhidhānam tau imau kṛtsna eka deśa śabdau ekasmin avayavini anupapannau 
NV_2.1.32^5	 katham tarhi avayaveṣu avayavī vartate iti āśraya āśrayi bhāvena āśritaḥ avayavī āśrayāḥ avayavāḥ iti kā punar iyam vācaḥ yuktiḥ naḥ eka deśena vartate na ca kārtsnyena vartate atha ca vartate iti yat yathābhūtam vastu tat tathā nirdiśyate iti eṣā vācaḥ yuktiḥ kṛtsna eka deśa śabdau ca avayavini na staḥ tasya eka tvāt iti uktam tasmāt āśraya āśrita dharmi nirdeśa mātram avayavi avayaveṣu vartate iti kā punar iyam vṛttiḥ ekasya anekatra āśraya āśrita bhāva lakṣaṇā prāptiḥ api ca ekam anekatra vartate iti pratijānānaḥ na anuyoktavyaḥ kasmāt ubhayena vyāghātāt ekam anekatra vartate iti bruvāṇaḥ kim eka deśena vartate uta sarva ātmanā iti na anuyoktavyaḥ kasmāt ubhayena vyāghātāt yadi ekam anekatra vartamānam pratyavayavam sarva ātmanā vartate naḥ ekam anekatra vartate anekam anekatra vartate iti āpannam 
NV_2.1.32^6	 evam ca anuyoge adhikaraṇa vyāghātaḥ atha ekam anekatra vartamānam pratyavayavam eka deśena vartate tathā api na ekam anekatra vartate iti prāptam anekam anekatra vartate iti āpannam ye ca te eka deśāḥ pratyekam avayaveṣu vartante te avayavinaḥ iti prāptam ekasmin api pakṣe naḥ ekam anekatra vartate kim tarhi anekam anekatra iti atha pratyekam parisamāptyā vartate iti ayam arthaḥ anekam anekatra vartate iti tathā api anuyoga adhikaraṇam nivartate iti ye eva khalu ayam arthaḥ anekam anekatra vartate saḥ eva ayam arthaḥ pratyekam parisamāptyā vartate iti sarvathā anuyoga adhikaraṇam nivartate iti anuyogasya adhikaraṇa bādhaka tvāt ayam khalu anuyogaḥ kriyamāṇaḥ adhikaraṇam bādhate atas dharma vikalpa bhāvena na vartate na ayam vikalpaḥ kva cit api āśrayavān iti atas na anuyoktavyaḥ iti 
NV_2.1.32^7	 evam sarveṣu aneka dravya vṛttiṣu saṃkhyā pṛthaktva saṃyoga vibhāga sāmāni ādiṣu anuyoga adhikaraṇa vyāvṛtti doṣaḥ vaktavyaḥ grahaṇa agrahaṇa bhedāt bhedaḥ avayava vat iti ced yathā gṛhyamāṇānām agṛhyamāṇānām ca avayavānām bhedaḥ tathā avayavinaḥ api gṛhyamāṇā gṛhyamāṇauvayava āśritasya bhedaḥ prāptaḥ tatas ca naḥ ekaḥ avayavī na bhedaḥ ekasmin api darśanāt ekasmin api gṛhyamāṇe grahaṇam agrahaṇam ca dṛṣṭam devadatta ādi vat iti yathā devadatta ādiḥ kena cit saha gṛhyate kena cit saha na gṛhyate na tāvatā tasya bhedaḥ tathā avayavinaḥ api iti adoṣaḥ gṛhīta tvāt ca yat idam bhavatā abhidhīyate eka deśa grahaṇāt asya grahaṇam eka deśa agrahaṇāt ca agrahaṇam iti ayam anāspadaḥ vikalpaḥ avayavinaḥ gṛhīta tvāt eka deśa sahacaritaḥ avayavī gṛhītaḥ iti kim asya agṛhītam yena grahaṇa agrahaṇa vikalpaḥ āspadavān syāt iti 
NV_2.1.32^8	 madhya bhāga para bhāgau na gṛhītau iti ced na tayoḥ avayavinaḥ anya tvāt anyaḥ avayavī anyau madhya bhāga para bhāgau iti anya tvāt avayavinaḥ madhya bhāga para bhāgau na gṛhyete iti kim kāraṇam grahaṇa hetu abhāvāt yathā arvāc bhāgena saha avayavinaḥ indriya prāptiḥ upalabdhi nimittam asti naḥ evam madhya bhāga para bhāgābhyām saha tasmāt arvāc bhāgena saha upalabhyate na madhya bhāga para bhāgābhyām iti avayava samūha pakṣe tu sarvathā vṛkṣa buddheḥ abhāvaḥ katham mūla skandha śākhā palāśānām samūhaḥ vā vṛkṣaḥ syāt prāptiḥ vā samudāyinām ubhayathā ca vṛkṣa buddheḥ abhāvaḥ avayavaiḥ avayava antara vyavadhānāt aśeṣa grahaṇam na asti prāpti grahaṇam api ayuktam prāptimatām agrahaṇāt na hi prāptimati agṛhyamāṇe prāpteḥ grahaṇam asti bhavati hi idam anena saṃyuktam iti sā iyam eka deśa grahaṇa sahacaritā vṛkṣa buddhiḥ dravya antara utpatti pakṣe kalpate na samudāya mātre iti 
NV_2.1.33^1	 kāraṇebhyaḥ dravya antaram utpadyate iti sādhyam etat kim punar atra sādhyam kim avyatirekaḥ atha avayavī iti yadi avayavī na liṅgam asti dharmiṇi vipratipatteḥ na hi dharmiṇi vipratipadyamānaḥ kutas cit abhyanujñām labdhum arhati na ca dharmiṇi vipratipatteḥ bījam asti sādṛśya abhāvāt na hi sādṛśyam antareṇa vipratipatti kāraṇam kim cit asti kim kāraṇam vipratipattiḥ nāma viparītā pratipattiḥ tasyāḥ ca kāraṇam samāna dharma upalabdhau anavagata viśeṣasya tad viparīta dharma adhyāropaḥ na ca anabhyupagata artha antarauvayavinaḥ avayavini sāmānyam kim cit asti 
NV_2.1.33^2	 na api tad viparīta dharma adhyāropaḥ tasmāt na vipratipattiḥ atha avyatirekaḥ sādhyaḥ tatra avyatireka pratipādakam pramāṇam vaktavyam na hi aprāmāṇikī kā cit pratipattiḥ asti idam pramāṇam artha antara anavayava tvam artha antaram artha antarasya avayavaḥ na bhavati yathā na gauḥ aśva avayavaḥ avayavāḥ ca tantavaḥ avayavī ca paṭaḥ tasmāt na asau tebhyaḥ artha antaram iti idam tāvat yathāśruti vākyam hetu hīnam na hi atra hetuḥ asti iti nanu ca upanayena vyajyamānaḥ hetuḥ avayava tvam asti na artha antaram paṭāt tantavaḥ tad avayava tvāt iti 
NV_2.1.33^3	 na vyāghātāt anartha antara bhāve na avayava tvam tantūnām siddhi ati iti kim kāraṇam avayavi apekṣa tvāt avayavi apekṣaḥ hi avayavaḥ na ca avayavi pratyākhyāne avayava tve kim cit bījam asti artha antare ca darśanāt viruddhaḥ syāt dṛṣṭaḥ avayavaḥ artha antara bhāve na anartha antaraḥ iti yathā tantu avayavāḥ ghaṭāt artha antaram iti ṣaṣṭhī viśeṣaṇāt aprasaṅgaḥ iti ced paṭasya avayavāḥ iti ukte ghaṭa ādiṣu kaḥ prasaṅgaḥ nanu atra uktam kim uktam vyāghātāt iti na hi anartha antara bhāve avayava tvam tantūnām sidhyati na ca ṣaṣṭhī 
NV_2.1.33^4	 na tantuḥ tantoḥ avayavaḥ na api ṣaṣṭhi arthaḥ na tantuḥ tantoḥ avayavaḥ iti upetyāḥ avayava tvam tantūnām tasya na anvayaḥ na vyatirekaḥ iti asādhāraṇa tvāt ahetuḥ na artha antaram paṭāt tantavaḥ iti ca tantūn pakṣīkṛtya tad avayava tvāt iti bruvāṇaḥ tantūnām tantu avayava tvam bravīti etat ca viruddham na tantavaḥ tantūnām avayavāḥ iti atha paṭaḥ pakṣīkriyate tathā api vyadhikaraṇaḥ hetuḥ avayava tvasya tantu dharma tvāt tantu dharmaḥ avayava tvam na paṭa dharmaḥ iti avayava śabdasya ca kāraṇa viśeṣa vācaka tvāt asati avayavini vyāghātaḥ 
NV_2.1.33^5	 yadi avayavinam artha antaram na pratipadyase kasya tantavaḥ kāraṇam na hi kāraṇam ātmānam nirvartayati iti na eva hi naḥ kim cit nirvartyam asti te eva tantavaḥ saṃsthāna viśeṣa avasthitāḥ paṭa ākhyām labhante iti apaṭāḥ tantavaḥ paṭa śabdena abhidhīyante iti etat uktam bhavati etat ca viruddham mukhya abhāvāt na hi tantūnām apaṭānām paṭena kim cit sāmānyam asti na ca asati sāmānye mithyā pratyayasya bījam asti iti uktam yat ca idam ucyate saṃsthāna viśeṣa avasthānam iti kim tad artha antaram āho naḥ iti yadi artha antara bhūtam kim tat iti vaktavyam 
NV_2.1.33^6	 atha na artha antaram śūnyam tarhi idam vākyam saṃsthāna viśeṣa avasthānam iti asmākam tu saṃsthāna viśeṣaḥ saṃyogaḥ sa ca artha antaram na anabhyupagamāt na mayā artha antaram saṃyogaḥ pratipādyate anya asaṃyogāt iti anyat anyasya saṃyogaḥ na bhavati yathā na gauḥ aśvasya saṃyogaḥ aṅgulyoḥ tu saṃyogaḥ tasmāt na artha antaram iti na ukta uttara tvāt ukta uttaram etat kim iti artha antara anartha antarayoḥ vyāvṛtta tvāt saṃyogaḥ asādhāraṇaḥ pratijña eka deśaḥ ca na artha antaram saṃyogaḥ saṃyoga tvāt iti viśeṣaṇa bhāvāt ca artha antaram saṃyogaḥ 
NV_2.1.33^7	 saṃyukte dravye āharaḥ iti ukte yayoḥ dravyayoḥ saṃyogam paśyati te itarebhyaḥ viśiṣya saṃyukte āharati na viśeṣaṇasya anyathā siddha tvāt yat idam bhavatā abhidhīyate saṃyukte dravye āharaḥ iti viśeṣaṇa bhāvāt artha antaram saṃyogaḥ iti tat anyathā sambhavati katham anyathā pratyāsattau pratīghāta avasānāyām saṃyoga vyavahāraḥ tāvat dravyāṇi pratyāsīdanti yāvat prahatāni bhavanti tasmin pratīghāte saṃyoga vyavahāraḥ na artha antaraḥ iti anabhyupagata artha antara saṃyogena pratyāsatti pratīghātau vaktavyau tatra saṃyukta saṃyoga alpīyaḥ tvam pratyāsattiḥ mūrta sparśa vat dravya saṃyogaḥ pratīghātaḥ 
NV_2.1.33^8	 yaḥ punar saṃyogam na pratipadyate tena pratyāsatteḥ pratīghātasya ca arthaḥ vacanīyaḥ iti yadi ca artha antaram saṃyogaḥ na syāt kṣetra udaka bīja agni in dhana ādīni sarvatra avasthitāni sarvadā aṅkura pāka ja ādi kāryam kuryuḥ tāni eva tāni iti tasmāt yaḥ taiḥ apekṣyate sa arthaḥ anyaḥ tasmin saṃyogaḥ iti saṃjñā iti kṣetra udaka bīja agni in dhanāni aṅkura pāka ja ādi kārya utpattau sa apekṣāṇi sarvadā tad kārya anārambhāt daṇḍa ādi vat yathā daṇḍa ādi anekam kāraṇam saṃyoga ādi nimitta antara apekṣam na sadā ghaṭa ādi kāryam karoti tathā bīja ādi api 
NV_2.1.33^9	 tasmāt tat api sa apekṣam iti yat tu atra pareṇaḥ ucyate kārya utpattiḥ vinā tena śabda ayaska anta karma vat iti asya arthaḥ yathā kila śabdaḥ śabda antaram ārabhamāṇaḥ vinā saṃyogena ārabhate yathā ca ayaskāntaḥ ayaḥ samākarṣati vinā saṃyogena yathā ca karma saṃyogam saṃyogena vinā karoti tathā anyā api kārya utpattiḥ vinā saṃyogena bhaviṣyati iti na hetu artha aparijñānāt na brūmaḥ asti saṃyogaḥ kārya utpatteḥ api tu kṣetra udaka bīja agni in dhanāni sa apekṣāṇi iti yadi ca nirapekṣam kim cit kāraṇam sarvadā ārambhakam syāt bhavet anaikāntika tvam hetoḥ 
NV_2.1.33^10	 tat tu na kena cit śakyam pratipādayitum śabdaḥ śabda antaram ārabhamāṇaḥ sva paricchinna ākāśa deśa pratyāsatti apekṣaḥ ārabhate śabdasya ākāśa avyāpaka tvāt ayaskāntaḥ api ayaḥ samākarṣati sva āśraya pratyāsatti apekṣaḥ eva yadi ca nirapekṣaḥ ākarṣet na kva cit ayaṃsi avatiṣṭheran tasmāt na nirpakṣaḥ karma api āśraya pratyāsattyā abhimukhya apekṣam saṃyogam karoti na nirapekṣam karma na pratilomam iti yadi anapekṣam karma saṃyogam kuryāt pāṇḍya mathurā sambandhini devadatte utpannam karma takṣaśilā sambandhini yajñadatte saṃyogam kuryāt na tu idam asti 
NV_2.1.33^11	 na ca evam pratijñāyate sarvasya kāraṇam saṃyogaḥ iti api tu sa apekṣam ārabhate iti sūtra vyāghātaḥ iti ced atha manuṣe yadi karma api sa apekṣam saṃyogam karoti nanu pāramarṣam sūtram vyāhanyeta eka dravyam aguṇam saṃyoga vibhāgayoḥ anapekṣa kāraṇam karma iti na vyāghātaḥ sūtra artha aparijñānāt na bhavatā sūtra arthaḥ vyajñāyi na ayam sūtra arthaḥ nirapekṣam karma saṃyoga kāraṇam āśraya ādi api na apekṣate iti api tu carama bhāvi nimitta antaram na apekṣate iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NV_2.1.33^12	 yathā dravya jātam utpannam carama bhāvinam saṃyogam apekṣamāṇam paścāt ārabhate yathā vā saṃyogaḥ guṇa karmasu ārabdhavyeṣu paścātbhāvi saṃskāra prayatna adṛṣṭa ākhyam nimittam apekṣate yathā vā kāraṇeṣu vartamānāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ kārya rūpa ādiṣu ārabdhavyeṣu dravya utpattim apekṣante utpādyasya ādhāra bhāvāt yat utpādyam dravyam tat teṣām ādhāraḥ iti na tu karma paścāt bhā vi nimittam apekṣate iti anapekṣa tvam karmaṇaḥ śāstre uktam na punar karma āśraya ādi api na apekṣate iti saṃyoge sa apekṣa tva prasaṅgaḥ iti ced yadi paścāt bhā vi nimitta antara anapekṣa tvam karmaṇaḥ nirapekṣa tva arthaḥ api tarhi saṃyoge kartavye karma sa apekṣam prāpnoti vibhāga apekṣi tvāt 
NV_2.1.33^13	 na hi asati vibhāge karma saṃyogam karoti tasmāt vibhāga apekṣi tvam karmaṇaḥ prasaktam tatas ca tad avasthaḥ sūtra vyāghāta doṣaḥ na sandehāt kim vibhāga apekṣeṇa karmaṇā saṃyogaḥ janyate uta pratibandhakaḥ vibhāgena nivartyate iti sandihyate vayam tu brūmaḥ vibhāgaḥ utpannaḥ pūrva saṃyoga nivṛttim karoti nivṛtte ca saṃyoge pratibandha apagamāt karma saṃyogam karoti yathā guru tvam nirapekṣam karma kāraṇam iti uddiṣṭam śāstre atha ca vṛnta phala vibhāgāt nivṛtte vṛnta phala saṃyoge guru tvam labdha vṛtti patana karma karoti tathā karma api iti adoṣaḥ 
NV_2.1.33^14	 yathā vā saṃyogaḥ sādhāraṇa kārya dravya saṃyoga vināśa uttara kālam dravya antara ārambhe nirapekṣaḥ kāraṇam iti na vibhāga apekṣaḥ dravyam ārabhate tathā karma saṃyogam ārabhamāṇam na vibhāgam apekṣiṣyate iti atas api na sūtra vyāghātaḥ yat api uktam karma vinā saṃyogena saṃyogam karoti tat api na vyāghātāt na ca saṃyogaḥ asti karma ca saṃyogam karoti iti vyāhatam na hi asati saṃyoge vākyam etat arthavat tāyām vyavatiṣṭhate iti athavā anena vyāghātaḥ gati vibhāga saṃyoga saṃyogāḥ ca pratiṣidhyante atha ca karma saṃyogam karoti iti vyāhatam 
NV_2.1.33^15	 atha manuṣe paramata vyapekṣaḥ ayam saṃyoga vibhāga karmaṇām pratiṣedhaḥ na asmābhiḥ saṃyoga vibhāga karmāṇi abhyupagamyante iti evam api anivṛttaḥ vyāghātaḥ yāni tāni para pakṣa abhyupagatāni saṃyoga vibhāga karmāṇi tāni bhavatā katham pratipadyante yadi pramāṇataḥ katham para pakṣa abhyupagatāni atha pramāṇam antareṇa katham pratipadyase na hi pramāṇam antareṇa kā cit pratipattiḥ yuktāḥ iti atha naḥ evam pratipadyase vyāhatam tarhi etat bhavati para pakṣa prasiddhāni saṃyoga vibhāga karmāṇi iti 
NV_2.1.33^16	 atha brūṣe yāni bhavatā abhyupagamyante saṃyoga vibhāga karmāṇi tāni na santi na punar saṃyoga vibhāga karmaṇām pratiṣedhaḥ katham deśa antare avirala dravya utpāde gati vyavahāraḥ yaḥ santānaḥ aviralaḥ deśa antareṣu utpadyate tatra gati vyavahāraḥ nirantara utpāde saṃyoga vyavahāraḥ ye vastunī nirantaram utpadyete tayoḥ yaḥ nirantara utpādaḥ sa saṃyogaḥ viparyayāt vibhāgaḥ iti atra tāvat uktam vṛkṣa sthitam bhāvayadbhiḥ na pramāṇa abhāvāt iti na hi kṣaṇika tve pramāṇam asti iti sāntara nirantara buddhyoḥ ca nimittam vaktavyam 
NV_2.1.33^17	 yadi saṃyogam vibhāgam vā na artha antaram pratipadyase sāntaram iti buddheḥ nirantaram iti buddheḥ bhede nimittam vaktavyam na hi nimitta bhedam antareṇa buddhīnām bhedaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ rūpa ādi vat iti yā ca iyam acalati calati iti buddhiḥ yā asaṃyukte saṃyuktam iti yā avibhakte vibhaktam iti ca sā ca pradhānam antareṇa na bhavati sarvāḥ etāḥ mithyā buddhayaḥ mithyā buddhayaḥ ca pradhāna anukāreṇa bhavanti iti pradhānam vaktavyam na hi niṣpradhānam bhāktam dṛṣṭam sthāṇu puruṣa vat yathā sthāṇau sati puruṣe sthāṇu buddhiḥ puruṣe ca sati sthāṇau puruṣa buddhiḥ iti 
NV_2.1.33^18	 yadi ca artha antaram saṃyogaḥ na syāt kuṇḍalī iti etasyāḥ buddheḥ kim nimittam avaśyam vidhīyamānam pratiṣidhyamānam vā nimitta antaram upādeyam na tāvat iyam kuṇḍala nimittā buddhiḥ na devadatta nimittāḥ na ca bhavatā nimitta antaram pratipadyate nimitta antaram ca antareṇa yathā katham cit vyavasthitābhyām devadatta kuṇḍalābhyām kuṇḍalī iti buddhyā bhavitavyam tasmāt avaśyam vidhīyamānam pratiṣidhyamānam vā nimitta antaram abhyupagantavyam yadi pratiṣidhyamānam yat anyatra bhavati tat anyatra pratiṣidhyate iti pratiṣidhyamānasya viṣayaḥ vaktavyaḥ 
NV_2.1.33^19	 tasmāt na katham cana saṃyogaḥ pratiṣeddhum śakyate ihabuddhi nimitta tvāt ca iyam ihabuddhiḥ pravartamānā na ṛte sambandhāt pravartate yathā iha kuṇḍe badarāṇi iti na iyam badara mātra nimittāḥ na kuṇḍa mātra nimittāḥ iti yat asyāḥ nimittam sa saṃyogaḥ iti iha iti buddhiḥ yadi saṃyogāt aniyamaḥ na prāpnoti yadi saṃyogāt ihabuddhiḥ bhavati asati saṃyoge ihabuddhiḥ na syāt yathā santi iha vane tilakāḥ santi iha vane kiṃśukāḥ iti dūrāt ca antaram apaśyatām kiṃkṛtā ihabuddhiḥ na hi tatra asti saṃyogaḥ iti na ihabuddheḥ ubhaya nimitta tvāt 
NV_2.1.33^20	 ubhayam ihabuddheḥ nimittam saṃyogaḥ vibhāga adarśanam ca tatra ekā mukhyāḥ ekā bhāktā yā saṃyogāt sā tattva buddhiḥ yā vibhāga adarśanāt sā bhāktāḥ iti yā ca iyam bhāktā sā pradhāna sāmānya darśanāt upajāyate na sā pradhānam pratyācaṣte na hi pradhāna pratyākhyānena bhāktā buddhiḥ bhavitum arhati iti sarvāḥ eva bhaktāḥ bhaviṣyanti iti na yuktam pradhāna apekṣi tvāt iti uktam yat api idam ucyate vinā saṃyogena ihabuddhiḥ dṛṣṭā yathā santi iha vane tilakāḥ santi kiṃśukāḥ iti tat atra saṃdhāryam kim tatra sambandhaḥ na asti uta saṃyogaḥ na asti iti 
NV_2.1.33^21	 vayam tu brūmaḥ saṃyogaḥ na asti na sambandhaḥ sambaddham hi vanam tilaka ādibhiḥ api iti kim punar idam vanam nāma na idam durvacam uktam etat bahu tva saṃkhyā sa viśeṣaṇāḥ iti ūrdhava avasthayoḥ satyām ihabuddhiḥ kasmāt na bhavati tayoḥ eva dravyayoḥ tasmin eva saṃyoge sati na bhavati iti kiṃkṛtaḥ aniyamaḥ na aparijñānāt sambandham antareṇa nirnimittāḥ ihabuddhiḥ na bhavati iti brūmaḥ na punar bhavati eva ihabuddhiḥ sati saṃyoge iti na ca uttara adharatā anapekṣeṇa saṃyogena ihabuddhiḥ na kriyate iti tad pūrvikā na bhavati 
NV_2.1.33^22	 yat punar etat asati sambandhe asya dravyasya iha samavāyaḥ iti ihabuddhiḥ na prāpnoti yathā iha tantuṣu paṭaḥ iti buddheḥ samavāyaḥ nimittam na punar samavāyasya samavāyaḥ asti iti iha samavāyaḥ iti na syāt atra uktam kim uktam mithyā pratyayaḥ eva eṣaḥ iti kim punar samavāyavadbhiḥ dravyaiḥ samavāyasya sāmānyam yad apekṣayā sa mithyā pratyayaḥ pravartate bheda adarśanam yāni samavāyavanti na teṣām bhedaḥ dṛśyate samavāye ca etat asti iti yuktaḥ mithyā pratyayaḥ vākya dharma bhedāt ca aniyamaḥ na ca ekasmin vākye dharmaḥ sa vākya antare api bhavati 
NV_2.1.33^23	 yathā rājñaḥ puruṣaḥ gacchati iti trīṇi padāni trīṇi api svena svena svena arthena arthavanti bhavanti iti udakasya bhāvaḥ bhavati iti naḥ etat vākya sāmānyāt ekasmin api vākye trīṇi api padāni pṛthak arthāni bhavitum arhanti kaḥ punar asya vākyasya arthaḥ udakasya bhāvaḥ bhavati iti yāvat uktam bhavati udakam bhavati iti tāvat uktam bhavati udakasya bhāvaḥ bhavati iti evam anyāni api vākyāni yathā kuṇḍe badarāṇām vṛttiḥ iti vṛttau coditāyām vṛttimatsu badareṣu sampratyayaḥ 
NV_2.1.33^24	 etat uktam bhavati kuṇḍe badarāṇi vartante iti tathā iha dravye dravyasya samavāyaḥ iti bruvāṇena uktam bhavati atra dravyam dravye vartate iti tasmāt ajñātvā vākya artha vibhāgam idam ucyate asya dravyasya iha samavāyaḥ asati nimitte iti tasmāt upapannam artha antaram saṃyogaḥ iti tad upapattau ca na saṃsthāna viśeṣeṇa avasthitāḥ tantavaḥ paṭa buddheḥ kāraṇam bhavanti iti apare punar anyathā artha antara anavayava tvāt iti etat vākyam varṇayanti avayava avayavi bhāvāt iti etat tu taiḥ kutas labhyate na hi ayam arthaḥ artha antara anavayava tvāt iti etasmin vākye śrūyate 
NV_2.1.33^25	 upanayena labhyate iti āha yasmāt ayam upanayaḥ avayavāḥ ca tantavaḥ avayavī ca paṭaḥ iti upanayena avayava avayavi tvāt iti hetuḥ labhyate satyam labhyate viruddhaḥ tu bhavati na hi tantavaḥ sva ātmanaḥ avayavāḥ ca avayavī ca na paṭaḥ sva ātmanaḥ avayavaḥ avayavī ca iti kim kāraṇam avayava avayavi śabdayoḥ sambandhi śabda tvāt sambandhi śabdau etau avayavaḥ avayavī ca iti na ca anyatara pratyākhyāne sambandhi śabda pravṛttiḥ asti tasmāt ayam api na sūtra arthaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ anartha antare api pradeśa pradeśi vyavahāraḥ yathā ākāśasya pradeśaḥ iti na ukta uttara tvāt ukta uttaram etat 
NV_2.1.33^26	 anyaḥ avayava arthaḥ anyaḥ ca pradeśa arthaḥ iti kaḥ avayava arthaḥ kāraṇa viseṣa abhidhānam avayavaḥ iti ādhāra abhidhānam pradeśaḥ pradiśyate asmin iti na ca ākāśam kva cit pradiśyate na ca ākāśasya kim cit kāraṇam asti tasmāt na kāraṇa arthaḥ naḥ ādhāra arthaḥ iti saḥ ayam ākāśe pradeśa śabdaḥ pradeśa vat dravya sāmānyāt draṣṭavyaḥ kim punar pradeśavatā dravyeṇa sāmānyam saṃyogasya avyāpya vṛtti tvam etam ca artham upariṣṭāt vakṣyāmaḥ iti tad pradeśa ātmaka tvāt iti ced atha manuṣe ayam anyaḥ hetuḥ avayavinaḥ anartha antara tva prasādhakaḥ tad pradeśa ātmaka tvam kaḥ asya arthaḥ 
NV_2.1.33^27	 anartha antaram paṭāt tantavaḥ tad pradeśa vyapadeśa viṣaya tvāt iha ye yasya pradeśa tvena vyapadiśyante te tasya ātmānaḥ bhavanti yathā ākāśasya pradeśāḥ paṭasya ca pradeśa tvena vyapadiśyante tantavaḥ tasmāt paṭa ātmānaḥ iti idam tāvat yathāśruti vākyam pūrvavat hetu hīnam tad pradeśa ātmaka tvasya artha antara anartha antarayoḥ adarśanāt asādhāraṇaḥ pradeśa śabdasya kāraṇa paryāya tvāt viruddhaḥ tad pradeśa vyapadeśa viṣaya tvasya tantubhiḥ asambandhāt asiddhaḥ yaḥ api ayam dṛṣṭāntaḥ ākāśasya pradeśaḥ iti saḥ api asiddhaḥ 
NV_2.1.33^28	 katham iti ākāśasya pradeśaḥ iti saṃyogasya avyāpya vṛtti tvam ucyate na ca saṃyogasya avyāpya vṛtti tva mātram ākāśam tasmāt asiddhaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ dravya antarebhyaḥ dravya antara aniṣpatteḥ na anyaḥ avayavī avayavebhyaḥ na kila dravya antarebhyaḥ dravya antaram utpadyamānam dṛṣṭam na ca go hasti aśvebhyaḥ puruṣaḥ utpadyate tantubhyaḥ tu utpadyate paṭaḥ tasmāt na asau tebhyaḥ artha antaram iti asya api pūrvavat hetuni ūna tā upanayena vyajyamānaḥ tebhyaḥ tu utpatteḥ iti hetuḥ ayam api artha antara anartha antarayoḥ vyāvṛtteḥ asādhāraṇaḥ 
NV_2.1.33^29	 artha antarāt ca turya ādeḥ artha antarasya paṭasya utpatti darśanāt viruddhaḥ paṭa pakṣīkaraṇe asambaddha arthaḥ na paṭaḥ paṭāt utpadyate iti atas tad śabdena tantavaḥ sambaddhi ante tantubhyaḥ paṭaḥ utpadyate iti tathā api viruddhaḥ na tantuḥ tantubhyaḥ bhavati paṭaḥ tu bhavati na anyaḥ avayavī avayavebhyaḥ avayavi antara avayavānām avayavi antara artha antara bhāvāt iha ye avayavinaḥ artha antaram bhavanti te avayavi antara avayavāh bhavanti yathā cakra ādayaḥ ratha avayavāḥ iti te artha antaram paṭāt yadi ca tantavaḥ api paṭāt artha antaram syuḥ te api paṭavyatirekeṇa avaya vi antara avayavāḥ syuḥ 
NV_2.1.33^30	 na tu te tad vyatirekeṇa avaya vi antara avayavāḥ tasmāt na artha antaram iti vākya mātre hetuni ūna tā asādhāraṇa tā ca doṣaḥ hetuḥ tu tad vyatirekeṇa anyān a vayava tvāt na tantavaḥ tantūnām avayavāḥ iti viruddhaḥ artha antara pratyākhyānāt ca avayavaḥ avayavī iti etat na syāt yat api idam ucyate ye avayavāḥ avayavinaḥ artha antaram bhavanti te tad vyatirekeṇa anya avayavāḥ bhavanti yathā cakra ādayaḥ iti tat api na ubhayena vyāghātāt cakra ādayaḥ avayavāḥ iti bruvatā abhyupagatam artha antaram bhavati 
NV_2.1.33^31	 anabhyupagame vā kaḥ asya vākyasya arthaḥ cakra ādayaḥ ratha avayavāḥ iti ye ca cakra ādayaḥ ratha avayava tvena abhyupagamyante te api artha antara pratiṣedhāt na rathasya na api anyasya avayavāḥ iti ucchinnaḥ avayava avayavi śabdasya viṣayaḥ tasmāt ahetuḥ ayam na anyaḥ avayavī avayavebhyaḥ dravya antara utpatti deśa vyavacchedāt yat ubhaya pakṣa sampratipannam artha antara tvena tat tasmāt bhinna deśam utpadyamānam dṛṣṭam yathā gauḥ aśvāt na tu tantubhyaḥ bhinna deśaḥ paṭaḥ utpadyate tasmāt na asau tebhyaḥ artha antaram iti atra api hetuni ūna tā ca asādhāraṇa tā ca pūrvavat 
NV_2.1.33^32	 tad deśa utpatteḥ iti hetuḥ na tantuḥ tantu deśe utpadyate iti viruddhaḥ utpatti pratyākhyānam vā paṭa pratiṣedhāt yadi tantubhyaḥ paṭaḥ naḥ utpadyate kaḥ punar utpatti śabda arthaḥ na tantuḥ utpadyate na paṭaḥ iti utpatti deśa vyavacchedāt utpatti śabdasya arthaḥ vaktavyaḥ sa ca nirūpyamāṇah vyakti ādi dharma bhedena apūrvam janma āha iti viruddhaḥ na anyaḥ avayavī avayavebhyaḥ avayava antara avayavinaḥ avayava antara artha antara bhāvāt iha yaḥ avayava antarāṇām avayavinī bhavati sa avayava antarebhyaḥ artha antaram bhavati yathā cakra ādibhyaḥ ghaṭaḥ 
NV_2.1.33^33	 cakra ādibhyaḥ avayavebhyaḥ artha antaram ghaṭaḥ iti cakra ādi avayava vyatirekeṇa avayava antarāṇām avayavī bhavati na tu paṭah tantu vyatirekeṇa avayava antarāṇām avayavī tasmāt na asau tantubhyaḥ artha antaram atra api asādhāraṇa tā hetuni ūna tā ca pūrvavat avayava antarāṇām avayavī iti bruvatā avayavi artha antara bhūtaḥ abhyanujñātaḥ bhavati śūnyam vā vākyam atha na abhyanujñāyate kaḥ asya vākyasya arthaḥ avayava antarāṇām avayavī iti na hi avayavi pratyākhyāne etat vākyam arthavat tāyām śakyam vyavasthāpayitum tad vyatirekeṇa anyāna vayavi tvam hetu arthaḥ 
NV_2.1.33^34	 asya api prasaṅgaḥ pūrvavat na anyaḥ avayavī avayavebhyaḥ sati anya kartuḥ artha antara bhāvāt iha ye yasmin sati anyat kurvanti te tasmāt artha antaram bhavanti yathā kaṭāt tantavaḥ sati kaṭe arthāntaram paṭam kurvanti kaṭāt artha antaram bhavanti na punar tantavaḥ sati paṭe dravya antaram kurvanti tasmāt na te na artha antaram iti asya api hetu arthaḥ sati anya akaraṇāt asya api asādhāraṇa tā nyūna tā ca pūrvavat sati kaṭe tantavaḥ paṭam kurvanti iti brūṣe paṭam ca kurvanti na ca artha antaram iti vyāhatam na hi tantavaḥ ātmānam kurvanti 
NV_2.1.33^35	 paṭam api artha antara abhāvāt na kurvanti iti ced na kriyā viṣaya uccheda prasaṅgaḥ na tantavaḥ ātmānam kurvanti na ca artha antaram kurvanti iti kriyā viṣayaḥ ucchinnaḥ bhavati iti na anyaḥ avayavī avayavebhyaḥ sva ātma saṃyoga vyatireka bhāvya vaya vī anya tvāt iha ye yasmāt artha antaram bhavanti te sva ātma saṃyoga vyatirekeṇa bhavanti tat yathā tantu saṃyoga vyatirekeṇa kaṭaḥ bhavati na ca tantu saṃyoga vyatirekeṇa paṭaḥ bhavati tasmāt na asau tebhyaḥ artha antaram asya api hetu arthaḥ tantu saṃyogebhyaḥ tad utpattiḥ iti asya api asādhāraṇa tā hetunyūna tā ca pūrvavat eva 
NV_2.1.33^36	 tantu saṃyogebhyaḥ tad utpattiḥ iti bruvatā tantu vyatiriktaḥ saṃyogaḥ ca avayavī ca tantu vyatiriktaḥ abhyupagataḥ bhavati anabhyupagame ca tantu saṃyogebhyaḥ tad utpatteḥ iti vākya arthaḥ hīyate na anyaḥ avayavī avayavebhyaḥ dravya antara guṇa āmām dravya antara guṇa akāraṇa tve aguṇa tva prasaṅgāt na kila dravya antara guṇebhyaḥ dravya antara guṇānām utpādaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yathā na go guṇebhyaḥ aśva guṇānām tantu guṇebhyaḥ ca paṭa guṇānām utpattiḥ tasmāt na asau tebhyaḥ artha antaram iti saḥ ayam apanyāyaḥ vartate kaḥ atra apa nyāyaḥ 
NV_2.1.33^37	 tantu guṇebhyaḥ ca paṭa guṇānām utpattim pratipadyase na ca artha antaram paṭaḥ iti na ca tantu guṇebhyaḥ tantu guṇānām utpattiḥ iti tantu guṇebhyaḥ tad guṇa utpattiḥ iti hetu viruddhaḥ na anyaḥ avayavī avayavebhyaḥ apratyakṣa tva prasaṅgāt pratyakṣa apratyakṣa vṛttiḥ avayavī apratyakṣaḥ syāt yadi avayavī artha antaram syāt yathā garbha mātṛ śarīra saṃyogaḥ pratyakṣa apratyakṣa vṛttiḥ apratyakṣaḥ pratyakṣaḥ tu avayavī tasmāt na asau tebhyaḥ artha antaram pratyakṣa tvāt eva artha antaram iti viruddhaḥ hetuḥ 
NV_2.1.33^38	 garbha mātṛ śarīra saṃyogaḥ ca apratyakṣaḥ iti kim ayam pratyakṣa apratyakṣābhyām ārambhāt apratyakṣaḥ uta pratyakṣa apratyakṣa vṛtti tvāt apratyakṣaḥ iti yadi pratyakṣa apratyakṣābhyām ārambhāt apratyakṣaḥ iti himavat paramāṇukam apratyakṣam prāpnoti tasya hi ekaḥ avayavaḥ pratyakṣaḥ ekaḥ apratyakṣah iti atha pratyakṣa apratyakṣa vṛtti tvāt apratyakṣah bhāvaḥ apratyakṣaḥ prāpnoti sa hi pratyakṣa apratyakṣa vṛttiḥ iti na ca ayam pakṣaḥ asti avayavānām pratyakṣa tvāt avayavī pratyakṣaḥ iti uktam ca atra kim uktam yeṣām indriyeṇa sannikarṣaḥ asti avayavānām taiḥ saha avayavī gṛhyate yeṣām na asti taiḥ saha na gṛhyate 
NV_2.1.33^39	 na ca etat kṛtaḥ asti bhedaḥ avayavānām apratyakṣa tvāt avayavinaḥ apratyakṣa tvam bruvataḥ sarvam atīndriyam prāpnoti na hi kasya cit madhya bhāga apara bhāgau upalabhyete iti saḥ ayam pratyakṣasya viṣayaḥ ucchinnaḥ bhavati pratyakṣa tvāt iti bruvāṇena avayava vyatiriktaḥ avayavī abhyupagataḥ bhavati paramāṇūnām atīndriya tvāt na hi paramāṇavaḥ kadā cit kena cit upalabhyante iti na paramāṇavaḥ atīndriyāḥ rūpa ādimatām atīndriya tva nivṛtteḥ na hi rūpa ādimat kim cit atīndriyam dṛṣṭam iti dṛṣṭam tu rūpa ādimat aindriyakam ghaṭa ādi 
NV_2.1.33^40	 aindriyakāḥ paramāṇavaḥ iti kaḥ arthaḥ kim tāvat indriya karaṇa pratyakṣāḥ uta indriya sambaddhāḥ iti kim ca atas yadi indriya karaṇa pratyakṣāḥ aindriyakāḥ iti tat na yuktam na hi indriyam anyasya anyathā artham prakāśayati anyathā anyasya iti indriya vṛttīnām avikalpita tvāt bhavatām ca paramāṇavaḥ aindriyakāḥ asmad ādīnām api aindriyakāḥ syuḥ atha indriya sambaddhāḥ aindriyakāḥ iti tasmāt na virodhaḥ na hi paramāṇavaḥ indriyeṇa na sambadhyante iti tasmāt indriya sannikarṣe sati api mahat tva abhāvāt na paramāṇavaḥ upalabhyante iti 
NV_2.1.33^41	 katham punar avagamyate mahat tvam api upalambhe rūpavat kāraṇam iti bhāva abhāvayoḥ tadvat tvāt yasmāt sati mahat tve rūpe ca upalabdhiḥ bhavati asati ca na bhavati tasmāt ubhayam kāraṇam iti yat tu atra uktam tejaḥ sparśa vat iti sati tejaḥ sparśe upalabdhiḥ bhavati asati ca na bhavati na ca tejaḥ sparśaḥ api rūpavat dravya upalabdheḥ kāraṇam iti tat na vyabhicārāt vyabhicārī sparśaḥ upalabdheḥ na kāraṇam na punar rūpa mahat tve kva cit vyabhicarataḥ tasmāt rūpa mahat tve eva upalabdheḥ kāraṇam iti ayam ca arthaḥ sūtrakāreṇa sūtra dvayena uktaḥ 
NV_2.1.33^42	 adravya tvāt paramāṇau= anupalabdhiḥ rūpa saṃskāra abhāvāt vāyau= anupalabdhiḥ iti rūpa saṃskāraḥ rūpa samavāyaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ atha punar sparśasya api rūpa mahat tva vat avyabhicāraḥ kasmāt sparśaḥ na kāraṇam iti vaktavyam samavadhārya ca etat bhavatā abhidhīyate sparśa vat etat syāt iti yena ca pramāṇena avadhṛtam etat sparśaḥ na kāraṇam iti mayā api tatas eva akāraṇa tvam atha akāraṇa tva pratipādakam na pramāṇam asti kaḥ hi asya vākyasya arthah sparśa vat etat syāt iti tad bhāva bhāvi tvam ca vyabhicārayatā kārya kāraṇa dharmaḥ ucchinnaḥ bhavati 
NV_2.1.33^43	 idam asya kāryam idam asya kāraṇam iti pareṇa paryanuyuktaḥ tad bhāva bhāvi tva vyatirekeṇa kena anyena na pratipādayasi atas virodhāt anuttaram etat yat punar etat atīndriya saṃyoga atīndriya tvāt iti atīndriyayoḥ kila ātma manasoḥ yaḥ saṃyogaḥ saḥ api atīndriyaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti yadi ca paramāṇavaḥ atīndriyāḥ syuḥ tad kāryam api atīndriyam syāt aindriyakam ca dṛṣṭam tasmāt aindriyakāḥ iti saḥ ayam dṛṣṭānta prayogaḥ atīndriya saṃyoga atīndriya tvāt iti dṛṣṭānta prayoga mātre ca hetuni ūna tā 
NV_2.1.33^44	 yaḥ api atra katham cit hetuḥ labhyate na atīndriya kāryam mahābhūta ādi vyaktam aindriyaka tvāt ghaṭa vat iti ghaṭa ādi aindriyakam aindriyaka kāryam dṛṣṭam tathā ca mahābhūta ādi vyaktam aindriyakam tasmāt tat api aindriyaka kāryam iti ayam api pratyakṣa virodhāt viruddhaḥ anuṣṇaḥ agniḥ kṛtaka tvāt iti yathā eke tu vātāyana= chidra dṛśyam truṭim pamāṇum varṇayanti tat na yuktam tasya bhedya tvāt abhedyaḥ paramāṇuḥ bhidhyate truṭiḥ iti katham avagamyate bhidyate iti dravya tve sati asmad ādi bāhya karaṇa pratyakṣa tvāt ghaṭa vat iti katham ca anyathā abhedyaḥ san paramāṇuḥ iti ucyate 
NV_2.1.33^45	 anitya tvāt ca na paramāṇuḥ sāmānya viśeṣavataḥ asmad ādi bāhya karaṇa pratyakṣa tvāt ca tasmāt na aindriyakāḥ paramāṇavaḥ teṣām atīndriya tvāt yat pratyakṣam tat anyat iti viruddhaḥ hetuḥ saṃhatānām utpatti nirodhāt na asaṃhtaḥ paramāṇuḥ asti iti apare apare ca saṃhatam paramāṇum varṇayanti saṃhatāḥ eva utpadyante niruddhi ante ca asaṃhatāḥ tu paramāṇavaḥ na santi eva iti tat ayuktam saṃhata arthasya anukta tvāt asaṃhatāḥ paramāṇavaḥ na santi iti bruvatā saṃhata śabdasya arthaḥ vaktavyaḥ saṃghātaḥ hi nāma bahūnām akārya kāraṇa bhūtānām saṃyuktānām avasthānam 
NV_2.1.33^46	 na ca asaṃhata pratiṣedhe saṃghātasya nimittam asti saṃhanyamāna tantra tvāt nityam ayam saṃghātaḥ saṃhanyamāna tantraḥ bhavati na ca asaṃhata pratiṣedhe saṃhanyamānam asti tasmāt na asaṃghātaḥ asti iti vyāghātāt na kim cit etat eka pratiṣedhāt aneka abhyupagama vat yathā nāma kaḥ cit mugdhaḥ eka pratiṣedhāt anekam abhyupeyāt tasya ca eka pratiṣedhāt anekam nivartate eka samudāya tvāt anekasya tathāvidham idam bhavati iti itas ca na anyaḥ avayavī avayavebhyaḥ saṃyoga aprāpti abhāvāt yat kahlu yasmāt artha antaram bhavati tasya tena saṃyogaḥ bhavati 
NV_2.1.33^47	 aprāptiḥ vā yathā gavāśvasya na punar tantubhiḥ paṭasya saṃyogaḥ na api aprāptiḥ tasmāt na asau tebhyaḥ artha antaram iti avayavinaḥ pakṣīkaraṇe saṃyoga vibhāga abhāvasya saṃyoga vibhāga viṣaya tvāt asambaddham atha asaṃyogitva avibhāgi tve hetū te api asiddhe saṃyujyate ca ayam vibhajyate ca ayam iti atha sva avayavena asaṃyogi tvāt saḥ api anupasaṃhāryaḥ na asya anvayaḥ na vyatirekaḥ iti atha api sarpa kuṇḍalaka ādi udāharaṇam syāt yathā sarpa kuṇḍalaka ādi kila sva kāraṇena asaṃyogi na ca artha antaram iti tat asiddham yathā ca artha antaram sarpa kuṇḍalaka ādi tathā uktam purastāt iti 
NV_2.1.33^48	 yat api sva kāraṇena asaṃyogi iti tat atra cintyam kim guṇa tvāt sva kāraṇena asaṃyogi atha anartha antara bhāvāt vayam tu brūmaḥ guṇa tvāt na anartha antara bhāvāt iti guṇaḥ ca sarpa kuṇḍalaka saṃyogaḥ sa ca artha antaram iti pratipāditam etat artha antara bhāve ca darśanāt viruddhaḥ sattva rajaḥ tamāṃsi bhavatām pakṣe mithas artha antara bhūtāni teṣām ca na saṃyogaḥ na aprāptiḥ iti pradhāna puruṣayoḥ ca na saṃyogaḥ na aprāptiḥ ubhayoḥ vyāpaka tvāt iti viruddhaḥ iti na anyaḥ avayavī avayavebhyaḥ guru tva antara kārya agrahaṇāt iti 
NV_2.1.33^49	 guru tva antara kārya agrahaṇāt iti etat na katham cit api pakṣeṇa sambadhyate kva ca na anyaḥ avayavī avayavebhyaḥ kva ca guru tva antara kārya agrahaṇam guru tva antara kārya agrahaṇāt ca guru tva antara kāryam na syāt na guru tvam na guru tva antaram na avayavī na udaka pratiṣedhāt kamaṇḍaloḥ kapālānām vā pratiṣedhaḥ yuktaḥ eke tu guru tva antara kārya agrahaṇāt iti anena guṇa antara ārambham pratiṣedhati udāharaṇa mātra artha tvāt guru tva antara ārambha pratiṣedhasya katham iti na kāryam kāraṇa rūpa ādi pūrvaka rūpa ādimat guru tva antaravat tva prasaṅgāt 
NV_2.1.33^50	 yadi kāraṇa gatāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ kārye rūpa ādīni ārabheran api tarhi kāraṇa gatāni api guru tvāni kārye guru tva antaram ārabheran tatas ca guru tva antara vat kāryam upalabhyeta na tu upalabhyate tasmāt na kāraṇa rūpa ādi pūrvaka rūpa ādimat kāryam iti satyam upapāditaḥ pakṣa dharmaḥ sa tu pratyakṣa virodhāt na kim cit katham iti abhyupetya kāryam rūpa ādayaḥ kārye pratiṣiddhi ante kārya abhyupagamāt ca pratiṣedhyam anujñātam bhavati kāraṇa rūpa ādayaḥ ca kārye rūpa ādīn naḥ ārabhante iti bruvataḥ kāryam aguṇam syāt na tu idam aguṇam dṛśyate tatas ca virodhāt ayam ahetuḥ 
NV_2.1.33^51	 atha kāryam naḥ eva asti na kāryam kāraṇa rūpa ādi pūrvaka rūpa ādimat iti anarthakam na hi kamaṇḍaloḥ abhāve anudakaḥ kamaṇḍaluḥ iti yuktam uktam etena kārye rūpa ādi pratipattiḥ pratyuktāḥ yaḥ ca ayam hetuḥ guru tva antaravat tva prasaṅgāt iti ayam api abhyupagamāt na kim cit nābhyupagamāḥ eva doṣa tvena na udyante yadi tarhi guru tva antara vat kārya dravyam rūpa ādi antara vat ca tatas guru tva antara kāryam upalabhyeta yathā rūpa ādi antarakāryam na tu upalabhyate na hi tulāyām vibhakta piṇḍa dvaya upanyāsa vat sambaddhayoḥ api kārya bhedam paśyāmaḥ tasmāt vibhaktayoḥ iva tayoḥ saṃyuktayoḥ api na asti dravya antara ārambhaḥ 
NV_2.1.33^52	 ke cit tu na guru tva antara vat kārya dravyavatī tulā iti pakṣayitvā avana mana viśeṣa abhāvāt iti hetum bruvate saḥ ayam vyadhikaraṇaḥ avana mana viśeṣa abhāvasya atulā dharma tvāt na hi avanamana viśeṣa abhāvaḥ tulā dharmaḥ iti evam tu yuktam utpaśyāmaḥ avanamana viśeṣa anādhāra tvāt na guru tva antara vat kārya dravyavatī tulā iti asiddhaḥ tāvat ayam hetuḥ avana mana viśeṣa anādhāra tvasya atulā vṛtti tvāt na tadvatā anupalabdheḥ ayam api anaikāntāt ahetuḥ guru tva antara vat dravya sannipāte sati avana mana viśeṣa anādhāra tvasya dṛṣṭa tvāt 
NV_2.1.33^53	 yathā gurutvavati dravye unmīyamāne truṭi bhūte rajasi gurutvavati sannipatitaḥ iti mahā guru tve ca unmīyamāne guru tva mātra upahitānām api avanati viśeṣam na karoti sama hīna adhika prasaṅgaḥ iti ced yadi tāvat kāraṇa guru tvaiḥ samam kārya guru tvam yāvat dvi palābhyām asambaddhe avanamanam dvis tāvat sambandhe sati syāt atha kāraṇa guru tva adhikam kārya guru tvam tathā api adhikataram prasajyeta atha kāraṇa guru tvāt hīnam kārya guru tvam tathā api viśeṣaḥ gṛhyeta na tu idam asti tasmāt na kārya guru tvam asti 
NV_2.1.33^54	 na kārya kāraṇa gurutveyattān avadhāraṇāt yadi etat avadhāritam syāt etāvat kāraṇeṣu guru tvam iyat kāryaḥ iti tat etat yujyeta vaktum sama hīna adhika prasaṅgaḥ iti tat tu na avadhāritam iyat kāraṇe guru tvam iyat kāryaḥ iti yadi kārya kāraṇa guru tvam na avadhāryete yaḥ ayam pratyayaḥ tulayā unmīyamāne dravye dvi palam pañca palam iti sa na prāpnoti na na prāpnoti dravya samāhāra guru tva avadhāraṇāt yat idam bhavān manyate dvi palam pañca palam iti na atra kārya kāraṇa guru tve avadhāryete kim tu ā caramāt ā ca paramāṇoḥ dravya samāhārah unmīyate 
NV_2.1.33^55	 tat manuṣya dharmaṇaḥ na yuktam vaktum iyat kāraṇa guru tvam iyat kārya guru tvam iti na ca samāhāraḥ kāraṇam api tu anārabdha kāryam caram a dravyam kāraṇam iti ke cit tu ārabhyaḥ ārabhante iti pratipadyante tān prati idam ucyate na pūrva uttara kārya dravye samāna deśe mūrtimat tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat iti śeṣaḥ tu ārabhya ārambhaka vicāraḥ na aprastuta tvāt nirākriyate iti niranumānam tarhi kārya guru tvam yadi guru tva antara vat dravya upacaye sati kārye bhedaḥ na gṛhyate niranumānam tarhi kārya guru tvam katham pratipattavyam iti kaḥ evam āha kārya guru tvam na gṛhyate iti 
NV_2.1.33^56	 yadi gṛhyate kim tat patanam na hi kārya guru tvam antareṇa kārya pāte anyaḥ hetuḥ asti tasmāt guru tva antara vat kāryam iti etena tulā vanati viśeṣasya agrahaṇāt kārye na gauravam iti pratyuktam atha manyase kāraṇa guru tvaiḥ eva kāryam pātyate na kārye guru tvam asti atas kārya pātasya anya nimitta tvāt na sidhyati guru tva antara vat kāryam iti na kārya kāraṇa yoḥasaṃyogāt yatra guru tvam āśraya antare pāta hetuḥ bhavati tatra saṃyogaḥ upakaraṇam yathā tulā paṭalaka guru tva vat dravya saṃyogaḥ iti na kārya kāraṇayoḥ saṃyogāt 
NV_2.1.33^57	 yatra guru tvam āśraya antare pāta hetuḥ bhavati tatra saṃyogaḥ upakaraṇam yathā tulā paṭalake guru tva vat dravya saṃyogaḥ iti na tu kārya kāraṇayoḥ saṃyogaḥ asti ayutasiddha tvāt yuta siddhiḥ asambaddhasya vidyamāna tā na punar kāryam kāraṇa asambaddham vidyate jātam sambaddhaḥ ca iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tasmāt na kārya kāraṇe saṃyukte samavāya upakaraṇam guru tvam pātayiṣyati iti ced na asaṃkīrtanāt virodhāt ca atha manayse satyam na kārya kāraṇayoḥ saṃyogaḥ asti api tu samavāyaḥ samavāyaḥ guru tva apekṣaḥ kāryam pātayiṣyati iti na sidhyati kārya guru tvam 
NV_2.1.33^58	 na asaṃkīrtanāt na samavāyaḥ kva cit api kriyā hetu tvena saṃkīrtitaḥ sūtrakāreṇa yathā saṃyogaḥ nodana abhighātāt saṃyukta saṃyogāt ca pṛthivyām karma iti na kevalam asaṃkīrtanāt eva virodhāt ca yadi ca samavāyaḥ kriyā hetuḥ syāt kāraṇa rūpa ādayaḥ api kāryeṇa eka artha samavāyāt pateyuḥ patantu rūpa ādayaḥ api kim naḥ bādhyate iti ced na guru tvasya api pāta prasaṅgāt yathā rūpa ādayaḥ kārya dravyam patat anupatanti tathā guru tvam api anupatet guru tvam ca anupatat kutas patati iti vaktavyam na guru tvasya guru tva antaram pāta hetuḥ asti 
NV_2.1.33^59	 tasmāt na guru tvam patati na rūpa ādayaḥ patanti iti yadi rūpa ādayaḥ na patanti dravye patati tiṣṭheyuḥ iti adravyāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ syuḥ dravyam ca rūpa ādi hīnam upalabhyeta atha dravye patati patanti kriyāvantaḥ rūpa ādayaḥ prāpnuvanti atha na tiṣṭhanti na patanti saḥ ayam yukti virodhaḥ avaśyam bhavatā abhyupagantavyaḥ patati patanti patati vā tiṣṭhanti iti veda punarbhavān yukta ayuktayoḥ nānā kāraṇam vedmi iti paraḥ yuktam pramitam ayuktam apramitam ayuktam tarhi idam patati patanti patati vā tiṣṭḥanti iti 
NV_2.1.33^60	 tat ca uktam guru tvasya guru tva antara prasaṅgāt rūpa ādi śūnyasya ca dravyasya adarśanāt adravyāṇām ca rūpa ādīnām adarśanāt iti yat ca patati gacchati vā tat prāptam jahāti aprāptam ca prāpnoti na punar rūpa ādayaḥ prāptam jahati aprāptam vā prāpnuvanti rūpa ādayaḥ aprāptam na prāpnuvanti iti na yuktam bhavati hi idam dravyayoḥ prāptayoḥ rūpe api prāpte iti na sandehāt kim ayam prāpti pratyayaḥ prāpti nimittaḥ āho aprāpteḥ adarśana nimittaḥ iti sandihyate vayam tu brūmaḥ aprāpteḥ adarśana nimittaḥ iti na hi dravyayoḥ prāptayoḥ rūpayoḥ ayam aprāptim paśyati dravyayoḥ api evam eva iti ced 
NV_2.1.33^61	 atha manyase yathā rūpayoḥ prāpti pratyayaḥ aprāpteḥ adarśana nimittaḥ evam dravyayoḥ aprāpti adarśana nimittaḥ bhaviṣyati na prāpti nimittaḥ iti na eṣaḥ doṣaḥ pratyaya dvaitasya aneka nimitta tvāt iha khalu pratyaya dvaitam eka nimittam dṛṣṭam tat yathā citra gatāsu pratikṛtiṣu krodha bhaya parihāre api kruddha bhīta pratyayāḥ bhavanti iti na tāvatā puruṣeṣu api krodha bhaya abhāve kruddha bhīta pratyayāḥ prādurbhavitum arhanti iti evam ayam prāpti pratyayaḥ kva cit saṃyoga nimittaḥ kva cit aprāpteḥ darśana nimittaḥ iti tasmāt vyavasthitam na guru tvam patati na rūpa ādayaḥ patanti iti 
NV_2.1.33^62	 apare tu kārya guru tvena kāraṇa guru tva pratibandham bruvate kārya guru tvena kila kāraṇa guru tvāni pratibaddhāni atas avanati viśeṣaḥ na bhavati iti etat tu na yuktam iti paśyāmaḥ kutas kārya kāraṇayoḥ pāta darśanāt yadi kārye patati kāraṇam avatiṣṭheta pratipadyemahi kārya guru tvena kāraṇa guru tvam paratibaddham iti na tu idam asti atas na yuktam etat anādhāra tva prasaṅgāt ca yadi kārya guru tvena kāraṇa guru tvam pratibaddham na kāraṇe kriyām ārabheta kārye patati na kāraṇam patet iti kāryam anādhāram syāt 
NV_2.1.33^63	 etena kārya guru tvena kāraṇa guru tva vināśaḥ api vyākhyātaḥ vibhaktānām ca pātaḥ na syāt iti adhikam yadi ca kārya guru tvena kāraṇa guru tvam vināśyeta kārya dravya vināśe kāraṇānām vibhaktānām pātaḥ na syāt guru tvam eva ca na syāt yadi kārya guru tvena kāraṇa guru tvam vinaśyeta api tarhi na kva cit guru tvam syāt na hi kasya cit paramāṇoḥ atītam kāryam na asti iti atas aguravaḥ paramāṇavaḥ syuḥ paramāṇuṣu ca guru tva abhāvāt kārye guru tvam kutas utpadyeta tasmāt apratiṣedhaḥ ayam kārya guru tvaiḥ kāraṇa guru tvānām vināśa pratibandhau iti 
NV_2.1.33^64	 atas pūrvaḥ eva pratiṣedhaḥ nānā ekāntāt iti kārya kāraṇa guru tva anavadhāraṇāt ca tat evam avayavinaḥ asattva avyatireka pratipādakam na pramāṇam asti iti atas sādhya tvāt avayavini sandehaḥ iti ayuktam itas ca sādhya tvāt avayavini sandehaḥ iti na yuktam asaṃkīrtanāt na hi sādhya tvam saṃśaya hetuḥ iti saṃkīrtitam kva cit api atas na saṃsabhavati sādhya tvāt saṃśayaḥ kaḥ evam āha sādhya tvāt saṃśayaḥ api tu sādhya tvāt vipratipattiḥ vipratipatteḥ saṃśayaḥ iti sādhya tva kāryāyām vipratipattau sādhya tvam adhyāropya uktam sādhya tvāt avayavini sandehaḥ iti 
NV_2.1.34^1	 saṃśaya apākaraṇa artham sūtram sarva agrahaṇam avayavi asiddheḥ iti sarveṣām arthānām agrahaṇam prasajyetayadi avayavī artha antara bhūtaḥ avayavebhyaḥ na asti iti katham iti pramāṇavaḥ tāvat darśana viṣaya bhāvam naḥ āpadyante atīndriya tvāt iti uktam avayavi dravyāṇi ca bhavadbhiḥ na pratipadyante tad anabhyupagame ca yaḥ ayam dravya pratyayaḥ kumbhaḥ iti guṇa pratyayaḥ śyāmaḥ iti kriyā pratyayaḥ calati iti sāmānya pratyayaḥ asti iti viśeṣa pratyayaḥ kalaśaḥ iti samavāya pratyayaḥ iha ghaṭe rūpa ādayaḥ iti tathā anye api pratyayāḥ ekaḥ mahān saṃyuktaḥ vibhaktaḥ pṛthak paraḥ aparaḥ iti ca na syuḥ 
NV_2.1.34^2	 asti ca sarvasya grahaṇam dravya guṇa karma ādi prapañcasya tena sarvasya grahaṇāt paśyāmaḥ avayava atiriktaḥ asti avayavī iti atha vā sarva agrahaṇam iti sarvaiḥ pramāṇaiḥ agrahaṇam katham pratyakṣasya vartamāna mahat viṣaya tvāt yat vartamānam mahat ca tat bāhya karaṇa pratyakṣam ghaṭa ādi avayavi pratyākhyāne ca na bāhya karaṇa pratyakṣa viṣayaḥ asti tasya abhāvāt anumāna ādeḥ api abhāvaḥ sā iyam sarva pramāṇa nivṛttiḥ upalabhyante ca arthāḥ pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ pramāṇaiḥ taiḥ sarvaiḥ grahaṇāt paśyāmaḥ asti avayavī iti tat idam sūtram avayavi anabhyupagame virodha pradarśana param saḥ ayam sarva ākāraḥ virodhaḥ loka paridṛṣṭa pratyaya ucchedaḥ iti 
NV_2.1.35^1	 avayavī artha antara bhūtaḥ iti ca arthaḥ kim idam dhāraṇam nāma eka deśa grahaṇa sāhacrye sati avayavi ninaḥ deśa antara prāpti pratiṣedhaḥ dhāraṇam yadā ayam avayavinaḥ eka deśam gṛhṇāti tadā eka deśa grahaṇena saha avayavinam api gṛhṇāti tena ca grahaṇena yat avayavinaḥ deśa antara prāpti nivāraṇam tat dhāraṇam ākarṣaṇam nāma eka deśa grahaṇa sāhacaryeṇa yat avayavinaḥ deśa antara prāpaṇam pūrvavat kutas etat lokataḥ lokaḥ khalu dhāraṇa ākarṣaṇe evam prayuṅkte iti te ete dhāraṇa ākarṣaṇe avayavinam sādhayataḥ katham iti niravayave avayave ca adarśanāt 
NV_2.1.35^2	 na hi dhāraṇa ākarṣaṇe niravayave avayave ca dṛṣṭe dṛṣṭe ca dhāraṇa ākarṣaṇe tasmāt avayavi dharmau iti yat tu atra uktam saṃgraha kārite vai dhāraṇa ākarṣaṇe na avaya vikārite pāṃśu rāśi prabhṛtiṣu abhāvāt tṛṇa upalaka aṣṭḥa ādiṣu jatu saṃgṛhīteṣu darśanāt iti tat na anavadhāraṇāt na brūmaḥ sarvasmin avayavini dhāraṇa ākarṣaṇe bhavataḥ api tu anyatra na bhavataḥ na ca virodhaḥ avayaviṣu eva darśanāt yāni tāni tṛṇa upala kāṣṭhāni jatu saṃgṛhītāni ākṛṣyante dhāryante ca iti manyase avayavinaḥ eva te yadi tu niravayave avayave vā dhāraṇa ākarṣaṇe syātām syāt virodhaḥ 
NV_2.1.35^3	 yat idam ucyate saṃgraha kārite te iti na viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt saṃgraha kārite dhāraṇa ākarṣaṇe na avaya vikārite iti na bhavatā viśeṣa hetuḥ apadiśyate pāṃśu rāśi prabhṛtiṣu ca kasmāt saṃgrahaḥ na asti iti vācyam yaḥ eva atra saṃgraha abhāve bhavataḥ hetuḥ saḥ eva avayavinaḥ vidyamānasya dhāraṇa ākarṣaṇayoḥ abhāvaḥ iti kaḥ punar asau uktaḥ asau eka deśa gṛhītasya tad sahacaritasya sambandha viśeṣaḥ iti sa ca pāṃśu rāśi prabhṛtiṣu na asti tasmāt na tatra dhāraṇa ākarṣaṇe iti saḥ ayam vyatirekī hetuḥ 
NV_2.1.35^4	 atha idānīm anvayinaḥ hetoḥ prayogam upanyasiṣyan idam āha atha avayavinam pratyācakṣāṇakaḥ mā bhūt pratyakṣa lopaḥ iti aṇu sañcayam darśana viṣayam pratijānānaḥ kim anuyoktavyaḥ iti ekabuddheḥ viṣayam paryanuyojyaḥ yā iyam buddhiḥ ekam idam dravyam idam iti kim iyam nānā viṣayāḥ uta abhinna viṣayāḥ iti yadi nānā viṣayāḥ bahuṣu adarśanāt ayuktā na hi bahuṣu ekam idam iti yuktaḥ pratyayaḥ atha abhinna artha viṣayāḥ yaḥ asau ekabuddheḥ viṣayaḥ saḥ avayavī iti eka aneka buddhī bhinna viṣaye viśeṣavat tvāt rūpa ādi viṣaya buddhi vat iti atha vā api eka aneka buddhī bhinna viṣaye samuccitā samuccita viṣaya tvāt idam iti idam ca idam vā iti yathā 
NV_2.1.36^1	 senā vana vat grahaṇam iti ced na atīndriya tvāt aṇūnām iti senā vana vat grahaṇam iti ced atha manyase asati artha antara bhāve asati ca eka aneka vibhede dṛṣṭaḥ buddhi viśeṣaḥ yathā anyā senā buddhiḥ anyāḥ gaja ādi buddhayaḥ iti tathā anyāḥ dhava ādi buddhayaḥ anyā ca vana buddhiḥ iti na ca tāvatā senā vanam ca anartha antaram tasmāt anaikāntika tvāt ahetuḥ iti idam tāvat sūtram sādhana pakṣe dṛṣṭānta mātra tvāt asambaddham anaikāntikīkaraṇa pakṣe tu na asiddha tvāt kena senā vanayoḥ anartha antara bhāvaḥ abhyupagamyate yathā ca senā vanāni artha antara bhūtāni tathā uktam abheda pratyayasya ca aneka nimitta tvāt na yuktam asti ayam abheda pratyayaḥ abhinnaḥ eva asti ca bhinne upalabhyamāne bhedasya adarśanāt abhinne tāvat eka pratyayaḥ yat ekam ubhaya pakṣa sampratipattyā vyavasthitam ekam na asti iti aneka pratyayaḥ vyāhataḥ eka samuccayaḥ hi anekam iti 
NV_2.1.36^2	 anekasmin upalabhyamāne api bhedasya adarśanāt abheda pratyayaḥ bhavati bhedasya adarśnamārāt nimittāt yathā senā ādiṣu yāni tāni senā aṅgāni hasti ādīni tāni ekaśas upalabhyamāna pṛthaktvāni ārāt nimittāt bhedam naḥ upalambhayanti bheda anupalambhe bhinne vastuni abhinna pratyayaḥ na tu pramāṇavaḥ kena cit upalabhyante kasmāt atīndriya tvāt aṇūnām iti atīndriyāḥ paramāṇavaḥ iti pratipāditam etat yaḥ ca āindriyakaḥ padārthaḥ saḥ upalabhya pṛthaktvaḥ san ārāt pṛthaktu asya agrahaṇe abheda pratyaya nimittam bhavati yathā upalabhyamāna jātīyānām ārāt na jāti grahaṇam upalabhyamāna praspandānām ca naḥ ārāt praspanda grahaṇam iti gṛhyamāṇā grahaṇasya ca anya nimitta tvāt yat ca idam gṛhyamāṇasya padārthasya agrahaṇam tat anya nimittam dṛṣṭam yathā teṣām eva senā vana aṅgānām na tu paramāṇavaḥ gṛhyante atīndriya tvāt tasmāt na teṣām anya nimittam agrahaṇam iti anupajāta viśeṣāṇām ca buddhi bheda ahetu tvāt virodhaḥ 
NV_2.1.36^3	 yasya paramāṇavaḥ ghaṭa ādi buddhi hetavaḥ bhavanti saḥ idam praṣṭavyaḥ kim paramāṇavaḥ upajāta viśeṣāḥ buddhi viśeṣam kurvanti uta anupajāta viśeṣāḥ iti kim ca atas yadi upajāta viśeṣāḥ yaḥ asau viśeṣaḥ saḥ avayavī iti prāptam atha anupajāta viśeṣāḥ te eva atīndriyāḥ aindriyakāḥ ca iti ati mahān virodhaḥ viśeṣaḥ saṃyogaḥ paramāṇūnām te paraspara pratyāsattau satyām saṃyoga upakaraṇāḥ upalapsyante iti na atīndriya tvāt aṇūnām na atīndriyānām saṃyogaḥ pratyakṣaḥ bhavitum arhati bhavati hi idam anena saṃyuktam iti tasmāt na saṃyogaḥ viśeṣaḥ yaḥ ca ayam anekasmin eka pratyayaḥ sa mithyā pratyayaḥ mithyā pratyaya nimittam ca sāmānya darśanam viśeṣa anupalabdhiḥ avidyamāna viśeṣa darśana dvāreṇa adhyāropita tad viparīta dharma tā na ca atīndriya tvāt aṇūnām sāmānya darśanam asti tad abhāve kutas viśeṣa adarśanam sāmānya darśane viśeṣa adarśane vā asati na tad viparīta dharma adhyāropaḥ 
NV_2.1.36^4	 na ca nimittam antareṇa naimittakasya mithyā pratyayasya prādurbhāvaḥ yuktaḥ iti etena bhāktaḥ aupamikaḥ ca pratyayaḥ vyākhyātaḥ bhaktiḥ nāma atathābhūtasya tathā bhāvibhiḥ sāmānyam ubhayena bhajyate iti bhaktiḥ yathā vāhīkasya mandām saṃjñām upādāya vāhīkaḥ gauḥ iti na tu atīndriya tvāt paramāṇūnām etat asti upamāna pratyayaḥ api na yuktaḥ atadbhāvinaḥ tad bhāvibhiḥ asāmānyāt yasya atathābhūtasya tathā bhāvibhiḥ sāmānyam tatra upamā pratyayaḥ yuktaḥ yathā siṃhaḥ māṇavakaḥ iti siṃhaḥ iva siṃhaḥ kim punar atra upamīyate śauryam na tu paramāṇūnām atīndriya tvāt mithyā pratyayānām nimittam asti iti mithyā pratyayāḥ api ete na bhavanti pradhāna abhāvāt indriya antara viṣayeṣu abheda pratyayaḥ pradhānam iti ced atha manyase indriya antara viṣayeṣu śabda ādiṣu eka ādi pratyayāḥ pradhānam bhavanti tad abhāve tu mithyā pratyayāḥ iti 
NV_2.1.36^5	 viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt dṛṣṭānta avyavasthā evam sati dṛṣṭānta upādānam na vyavatiṣṭḥate tasmin tat iti pratyayaḥ atasmin tat iti ca pratyayaḥ asti ca ayam paramāṇuṣu sañciteṣu tat iti pratyayaḥ kim ayam atasmin tat iti āhosvit atasmin tat iti sandihyate śabda ādiṣu eka pratyayaḥ pradhānam ghaṭa ādiṣu tu eka pratyayaḥ mithyā pratyayaḥ iti bruvāṇaḥ ghaṭa ādīn abhyupaiti na hi anabhyupagateṣu ghaṭa ādiṣu śabda ādi sāmānyam eka pratyaya bījam ghaṭa ādiṣu asti atha manyase na asmābhiḥ ghaṭa ādayaḥ abhyupagamyante kim tu paramāṇūnām sañcitānām śabdena sāmānyāt eka pratyaya utpatti nimitta tvam iti atra uktam na atīndriya tvāt aṇūnām iti yān ca śabda ādīn pradhāna pratyaya nimitta tvena bhavān pratipadyate te api sañcitāḥ eva sañcita tvāt teṣu api ayam eka pratyayaḥ na yuktaḥ śabda ādiṣu ca eka pratyayaḥ samuccaya nivṛtti nimittaḥ ekatva vat dravya sāmānyāt bhāktaḥ 
NV_2.1.36^6	 yāni ekatvavanti dravyāṇi teṣām samuccaya nivṛttiḥ dharmaḥ asti ca śabda ādiṣu samuccaya nivṛttiḥ tena ekatva vat dravya sāmānyāt śabda ādiṣu eka pratyayaḥ bhāktaḥ iti sarvatra samuccaya nivṛtti nimittaḥ eva iti ced na dve iti atra eka aneka matau sandehaḥ na syāt yadi sarvatra ayam samuccaya nivṛtti nimittaḥ eva eka pratyayaḥ bhavati na dve iti atra kim ekam anekam iti dvi pratiṣedha sāmānyāt sandehaḥ na syāt sati ca sandehe ekam iti niyama artham yatas niyamaḥ tat eka tvam yatas tri ādi pratyayāḥ te tritva ādayaḥ iti evam dvi tva ādi pratyayāḥ api śabda ādiṣu samuccaya nimittāḥ draṣṭavyāḥ kasmāt dvi tva ādimad dravya sāmānyāt dvi tva ādimatā dravyeṇa śabda ādīnām samuccayaḥ sāmānyam sarvatra samuccayāt eva iti ced na ekam iti atra sāmānya matau na saṃśayaḥ syāt yadi ca sarvatra samuccayatantrāḥ dvi ādi pratyayāḥ bhavanti na ekam iti pratiṣedhe dve trīṇi iti sāmānya gatau na saṃśayaḥ syāt 
NV_2.1.36^7	 tasmāt yatas vyavasthā te dvi tva ādayaḥ iti yaḥ punar eka tvam dvi tva ādīn ca na pratipadyate tasya na samuccayaḥ na samuccaya nivṛttiḥ anabhyupagata eka tvasya kasya samuccayaḥ anabhyupagata dvi tvasya ca kasya pratiṣedhaḥ eka tva dvi tva ādīn ca artha antara bhūtān anabhyupagacchataḥ ekam śatam ekam dvi tvam iti eka pratyayaḥ na syāt bhedasya agrahaṇāt ca śabda ādiṣu eka pratyayaḥ yasmāt śabda ādiṣu bhedaḥ na gṛhyate upalabhyamāneṣu eka pratyayaḥ na punar paramāṇuṣu abheda grahaṇasya nimittam asti atīndriya tvāt aṇūnām iti uktam udāharaṇa mātra tvāt ca eka pratyaya paryanuyogasya eka pratyaya vat aneka pratyayam api anuyoktavyaḥ yaḥ avayavinam artha antaram na pratipadyate tasya yathā eka pratyayaḥ anupapannaḥ tathā aneka pratyayāḥ api naḥ āpnuvanti yathā ca eka aneka pratyayān evam sarvān eva ghaṭa ādi pratyayān paryanuyojyaḥ 
NV_2.1.36^8	 evam parimāṇa saṃyoga praspanda jāti viśeṣa pratyayān api anuyoktavyaḥ teṣu ca evam prasaṅgaḥ yadi avayavinam artha antaram na pratipadyase mahat iti saṃyuktaḥ iti calati aśvaḥ gauḥ gacchati iti pratyayāḥ na prāpnuvanti na hi atīndriyeṣu paramāṇuṣu ete pratyayāḥ yujyante iti kim ete eka ādi pratyayāḥ aṇu sañcaya mātre āhosvit artha antara bhāve iti sandihyate sandehe sati viśeṣa hetuḥ vaktavyaḥ iti ayam viśeṣa hetuḥ mahat pratyaya sāmānādhikaraṇyāt eka pratyayasya eka pratyayaḥ mahati yaḥ khalu yad samāna adhikaraṇaḥ pratyayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ sa tad dharma yuktaḥ bhavati yathā nīlam utpalam iti ubhaya dharma yogini nīlotpala pratyayaḥ pravartate asti ca mahat pratyaya sāmānādhikaraṇyam eka pratyayasya tasmāt mahati eka pratyayaḥ iti aṇu samūhe atiśaya grahaṇam mahat pratyayaḥ iti ced atha manyase na asmābhiḥ avayavī artha antara bhūtaḥ abhyupagamyate 
NV_2.1.36^9	 api tu aṇu samūham upalabhya aṇu samūha antare atiśayam gṛhṇataḥ mahat pratyayaḥ bhavati saḥ ayam atasmin tat iti pratyayaḥ iti pūrvavat prasaṅgaḥ iti amahatsu aṇuṣu amahatsu vai aṇu samūheṣu yaḥ ayam mahat pratyayaḥ saḥ atasmin tat iti mithyā pratyayaḥ mithyā pratyayaḥ ca pradhānam antareṇa na bhavati iti pūrvavat eva prasaṅgaḥ aṇuḥ śabdaḥ mahān iti ca vyavasāyāt pradhāna siddhiḥ iti ced atha manyase mahān śabdaḥ aṇuḥ ca śabdaḥ iti śabde dṛṣṭaḥ mahat aṇu pratyayaḥ pradhānam anyatra mahat aṇu pratyayasya iti na ca mandatīvra tā grahaṇam iyattā an avadhāraṇāt na śabde mahat tvam ca aṇu tvam guṇa tvāt aṇu mahat pratyayaḥ tarhi śabde na prāpnoti na na prāpnoti anya nimitta tvāt kim nimittam manda tā tīvra tā ca kasmāt iyattā an avadhāraṇāt na hi ayam mahān śabdaḥ iti vyavasyan iyān iti avadhārayati yathā kuvala āmalaka vilvāni iti adhārayati
