NV_2.1.36^10	 kuvalāt āmalakam mahat āmalakāt ca vilvam tāni ca iyat tayā paricchinatti iyat parimāṇam etat iti na punar śabdeṣu etat asti śabdeṣu api pūrva anubhūta śabdam upalabhya tasmāt śabdāt ayam śabdaḥ mahān aṇuḥ vā iti avadhāryate na avadhāraṇam pratiṣidhyate iti idam tu cintyate yaḥ ayam śabde aṇu mahat pratyayaḥ kim ayam parimāṇa yogāt uta anyasmāt nimittāt iti anyasmāt nimittāt iti yuktam guṇasya guṇa antara sambandha anupalabdheḥ na hi guṇasya guṇa antara sambandhaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yatas parimāṇa sambandhaḥ api gamyeta mahat pratyayāt eva guṇavān śabdaḥ dravya vat iti ced na yathā ayam mahat pratyayaḥ dravyeṣu bhavat mahat parimāṇa yogāt bhavati śabde api ca ayam mahat pratyayaḥ asti atas mahat pratyaya viṣaya tvāt mahat parimāṇa yuktaḥ śabdaḥ iti nānā ekāntāt mahat pratyaya viṣaya tve tulye api mahat parimāṇa yogaḥ na dṛṣṭaḥ yathā mahat parimāṇaḥ iti 
NV_2.1.36^11	 dravye tarhi mahat pratyayaḥ katham yadi tāvat mahat pratyaya viṣaya tve sati api mahat parimāṇa yogam na pratipadyase mahat parimāṇa yuktam dravyam iti etat katham na mahat pratyaya viṣaya tvāt mahat parimāṇa yuktam dravyam api tu mahat parimāṇa yoge sati mahat pratyayaḥ dravye iti mahat parimāṇa yogaḥ tu dravyasya viśeṣa pratyayānām anākasmika tvena yadi viśeṣa pratyayānām anākasmika tvena mahat parimāṇa yogaḥ dravye śabde api evam śabde api aṇu mahat pratyayaḥ asti tena api na akasmāt bhavitavyam kaḥ ca evam āha śabde api ayam ākasmikaḥ iti kim nimittaḥ mandatīvra tā nimittaḥ mandatīvra tā ca śabda dharmaḥ tatas aṇu mahat pratyayaḥ śabde iti kā punar iyam manda tā tīvra tā ca aṇu dravya sāmānyāt sāmānya pratyaya viṣaya tvam manda tā mahat dravya sāmānyāt ca sāmānya viśeṣa buddhi viṣaya tvam tīvra tā pāṭavam iti saṃyukte iti ca dvi tva samāna āśrayam prāpti grahaṇam avayavinaḥ pratipādakam katham iti 
NV_2.1.36^12	 saṃyukta mahat pratyayau eka viṣayau pratisandhānāt nīlotpala pratyaya vat yathā ca nīlam ca tat utpalam ca iti pratisandhīyamānau pratyayau eka viṣayau bhavataḥ tathā saṃyukte mahatī iti ca pratisandhānam asti tasmāt pratisandhānāt eka viṣayau iti etena ekam mahat calam mahat khadiram mahat iti mahat ādi pratyayāḥ vyākhyātāḥ samudāya dvaya apekṣaḥ iti ced atha manyase dvau samudāyau āśritya saṃyukta mahat pratyayau bhavataḥ tathā eka ādi mahat pratyayāḥ api eka samudāya apekṣāḥ iti ced na vikalpa anupapatteḥ samudāya apekṣāḥ saṃyukta mahat ādi pratyayāḥ iti kaḥ ayam samudāyaḥ kim anekaḥ samudāyī uta anekasya prāptiḥ iti anekasya prāptiḥ samudāyaḥ iti ced prāptī prāpte iti pratyayaḥ syāt kim kāraṇam samudāyasya prāpti tvena abhyupagamāt saṃyukte ime vastunī iti ca na syāt prāptī prāpte iti ca syāt samudāyaḥ ca samudāya antara prāptau ekībhūtaḥ iti prāpti pratyayaḥ na syāt samudāyasya eka tvāt 
NV_2.1.36^13	 atha anekaḥ samudāyī samudāyaḥ iti dvi tvena sāmānādhikaraṇyam na syāt saṃyukte ime vastunī iti dvi tva samāna adhikaraṇaḥ pratyayaḥ na syāt tasmāt mahatī dvi tva āśraya bhūte dravye saṃyogasya sthānam iti na saṃyogaḥ asti iti ced uktam atra yathā artha antaram saṃyogaḥ iti idam tāvat avayava samudāya vādī praṣṭavyaḥ yaḥ ayam gauḥ aśvaḥ puruṣaḥ iti jāti nimittaḥ pratyayaḥ sa kva bhavati iti na eva jātiḥ asti kutas jāti nimittaḥ pratyayaḥ bhaviṣyati iti jāti viśeṣasya pratyaya anuvṛtti liṅgasya apratyākhyānam na jāti viśeṣam antareṇa pratyaya anuvṛtteḥ nimittam asti na ca nirnimittaḥ pratyayaḥ vyavasthātum arhati asti ca ayam anuvṛttaḥ pratyayaḥ imāni kuṇḍalāni iti asti ca vyāvṛttaḥ pratyayaḥ naḥ imāni kuṇḍalāni iti tasmāt jāti viśeṣaḥ na pratyaya ākhyeyaḥ vyadhikaraṇasya anabhivyakteḥ adhikaraṇa vacanam na ayam jāti viśeṣaḥ anadhikaraṇaḥ vyajyate iti adhikaraṇam avaśyam vaktavyam 
NV_2.1.36^14	 aṇu samavasthānam adhikaraṇam iti ced atha manyase paramāṇavaḥ eva kena cit samavasthānena avatiṣṭhamānāḥ tām tām jātim vyañjayanti atas na avayavī sidhyati iti atra tāvat uktam samavasthānam saṃyogaḥ artha antaram iti yat ca samavasthānam jāti viśeṣam vyanakti iti manyase kim tat cakṣuṣā prāptam vyanakti āhosvit aprāptam iti prāptam vyanakti iti ced madhya para bhāgayoḥ aprāpta tvāt anabhivyaktiḥ sa yadi prāpte samavasthāne jāti viśeṣaḥ vyajyate madhya para bhāgayoḥ arvāc bhāga vyavadhānāt aprāptau anabhivyaktiḥ yāvat prāptam tāvati abhivyaktiḥ iti ced na tāvataḥ adhikaraṇa tvam atha manyase yāvat cakṣuṣā samavasthānam prāptam tāvati jāti vyaktiḥ tāvat eva tarhi adhikaraṇam jāteḥ prāptam evam sati pratīyamāna bhedaḥ yaḥ ayam vṛkṣaḥ iti samudāyaḥ pratīyate tasya vṛkṣasya bhedaḥ prāpnoti kim kāraṇam 
NV_2.1.36^15	 yāvati jātiḥ vyajyate sa vṛkṣaḥ iti prāpnoti tatas ca ekaḥ vṛkṣaḥ anekaḥ iti pratīyeta iti eka pratyayaḥ na syāt arvāc bhāgasya ca avṛkṣa tvāt na kva cit vṛkṣaḥ iti vṛkṣa buddheḥ viṣayaḥ vaktavyaḥ tasmāt samudita aṇu sthānasya ātma antarasya jāti viśeṣa vyakti hetu tvāt avayavī artha antara bhūtaḥ iti samuditāḥ aṇavaḥ sthānam yasya saḥ ayam samudita aṇu sthānaḥ samudita aṇu sthānaḥ ca asau ātma antaram ca tasya jāti viśeṣa vyakti hetu tvam na aṇūnām iti sidhyati avayavī artha antara bhūtaḥ anabhyupagata artha antarauvayavinā ca paramāṇu śabdasya arthaḥ vaktavyaḥ paramāṇu śabdasya parama apakarṣa vāci tvāt na hi asati mahati na ca asati aṇau paramāṇuḥ iti viśeṣaṇam yuktam parimāṇa prakarṣa yoge sati paramāṇuḥ iti viśeṣaṇam arthavat asati anarthakam iti sa ca ayam parimāṇa prakarṣa yogaḥ sati avayavini sidhyati iti sattva rajaḥ tamasām sarva apakṛṣṭaḥ saṃghātaḥ paramāṇuḥ iti kasya cit darśanam 
NV_2.1.36^16	 tat na yuktam iti paśyāmaḥ vyāghātāt sarva apakṛṣṭaḥ ca saṃghātaḥ ca iti vyāhataḥ na hi saṃhanyamānam antareṇa saṃghātaḥ sadhyati iti artha antaram paṭāt tantavaḥ tad kāraṇa tvāt turya ādi vat iti turya ādi paṭasya kāraṇam iti artha antaram dṛṣṭam tathā ca tantavaḥ tasmāt artha antaram iti sāmarthya bhedāt viṣa agada vat bhinna pratyaya viṣaya tvāt rūpa sparśa vat tantu paṭa rūpe bhinna kāraṇe viśeṣavat tvāt rūpa sparśa vat eke tu bhinna rūpa tvāt iti evam hetum kṛtvā paramāṇunā pratyavatiṣṭhante ekasmin api paramāṇau rūpa bhedaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ raktaḥ śyāmaḥ iti ca sa tu evam pratyavastheyaḥ na hetu artha aparijñānāt iti na brūmaḥ bhinna rūpa tvāt anyaḥ avayavī avayavebhyaḥ api tu tantu paṭa rūpe bhinna kāraṇe iti pakṣayitvā viśeṣavat tvāt iti hetum brūmaḥ tathā ca ayam apratiṣedhaḥ iti ati bahu grantha visāriṇī tu eṣā kathā iti uparamyate 
NV_2.1.37^1	 prasaṃgataḥ parīkṣitam pratyakṣam atha idānīm avasara prāptam anumānam parīkṣyate kim punar idam anumānam uktam tad pūrvakam anumānam iti tatra pūrvavat ādeḥ udāharaṇāni nadī pūraḥ pipīlikā aṇḍa sañcāraṇam mayūra vāsitam iti etat udāharaṇa vyabhicāra dvārakam sūtram rodha upaghāta sādṛśyebhyaḥ vyabhicārāt anumānam apramāṇam iti tatra rodhaḥ nāma apām syandamānānām drava tva pratibandha hetuḥ upaghātaḥ nāma pipīlikā gṛhāṇām upamardaḥ sādṛśyam nāma mayūra puruṣa śabdayoḥ samāna pratyaya kartṛ tvam ebhyaḥ vyabhicārāt anumānam apramāṇam iti śeṣam bhāṣye yat tāvat uktam anumānam apramāṇam iti tat ayuktam pratijñā padayoḥ vyāghātāt anumānam iti sambaddhasya atīndriya artha sādhakasya etat nāma apramāṇam iti tasya pratiṣedhaḥ saḥ ayam pratijñā padayoḥ vyāghātaḥ anujñāta pratiṣiddhayoḥ ekatva anupapatteḥ 
NV_2.1.37^2	 pratijñā hetvoḥ ca virodhaḥ anumānam apramāṇam iti pratijñā rodha upaghāta sādṛśyebhyaḥ vyabhicārāt iti hetuḥ yat vyabhicāri tat apramāṇam yathā go siddhau viṣāṇi tvam saḥ ayam hetuḥ pratijñām vyāhanti pratijñā ca hetum iti yat ca idam ucyate anumānam apramāṇam iti tat kim anumāna mātrasya apramāṇa tvam uta anumāna viśeṣasya iti kim ca atas yadi anumāna mātram apramāṇam iti pakṣaḥ hetoḥ eka deśa vṛtti tvāt avyāpaka tvam samastam anumānam pakṣīkṛtya na sarvasmin anumāne vyabhicāraḥ asti na hi vyabhicārasya apramāṇa tva sādhanasya vyabhicāraḥ śakyaḥ pradarśayitum na hi vyabhicārasya vyabhicāre kim cit pramāṇam asti iti avyāpaka tvāt ahetuḥ atha yat vyabhicāri tat apramāṇam iti brūṣe pratijñā viśeṣaṇa tvāt hetoḥ hetu antaram vacanīyam siddha sādhanam ca etat yat vyabhicāri tat pramāṇam na bhavati 
NV_2.1.38	 yāni api etāni udāharaṇāni vyabhicārīṇi iti ucyante teṣu api vyabhicāraḥ na asti iti asiddha tā udbhāvana dvārakam sūtram na eka deśa trāsa sādṛśyebhyaḥ artha antara bhāvāt yat tāvat rodhāt api nadī pūraḥ bhavati iti na atra nadī pūra mātreṇa upari vṛṣṭimat deśa sambandhi tvam nadyāḥ sādhyate api tu pūra viśeṣeṇa tasya ca vyabhicāraḥ asiddhaḥ upaghātāt pipīlikā aṇḍa sañcāraṇa mātrasya ca vyabhicāraḥ na sañcāraṇa viśeṣasya kaḥ punar asau viśeṣaḥ avitrastānām bhūyasīnām bhūyaḥsu sthāneṣu pipīlikā piṇḍa bhūyaḥ tvena ūrdhva sañcāraṇam yat tat anāgata vṛṣṭi avinābhāvi śabda vyabhicāraḥ api na asti yasmāt na śabda mātram anumānam mayūra astitve na ca atra mayūraḥ sādhyate api tu śabda gatāt viśeṣāt ṣaḍja ādi śabdaḥ eva mayūra guṇa viśiṣṭaḥ anumīyate iti evam ca vyabhicāraḥ na asti iti asiddhaḥ hetuḥ 
NV_2.1.39^1	 tri kāla viṣayam anumānam traikālya grahaṇāt iti uktam tatra tāvat kālaḥ eva na asti iti ke cit tat ca na pramāṇa abhāvāt na hi kāla asattve pramāṇam asti nanu ca anupalabdhiḥ kāla asattvam pratipādayati na pratipādayati vyabhicārāt tri kāraṇāḥ iyam anupalabdhiḥ tatra anupalabdhyā kāraṇa vaikalyam gamyeta na tu upalabhyam eva na asti iti etat atha upalabhyamānasya abhāvāt anupalabdhiḥ iti ayam pratijñā arthaḥ tathā api hetuḥ na asti pratijñā arthena ākṣipta tvāt ākṣiptaḥ hetuḥ pratijñā arthaḥ iti na ca asati dharmiṇi dharmaḥ sambhavati āśraya abhāvāt atha dharmaḥ api na asti sādhana arthaḥ hīyate na hi asataḥ sādhana artham paśyāmaḥ iti parāpara ādi pratyayānām ca sa nimitta tvāt kāla pratiṣedhaḥ na yuktaḥ yaḥ ca kālam na pratipadyate tena parāpara ādi pratyayānām nimittam vaktavyam na hi asati nimitte naimittikān viśeṣavataḥ pratyayān paśyāmaḥ rūpa ādi pratyaya vat 
NV_2.1.39^2	 kāla eka tvāt pratyaya bheda anupapattiḥ iti ced atha manyase kālasya eka tve sati na yuktaḥ parāpara ādi pratyaya bhedaḥ na abhinnam nimittam bhinnam kāryam karoti iti na sa apekṣa tvāt pitṛ ādi pratyaya bheda vat yathā ekasmin puruṣe aneka sambandha bheda anuvidhāyini abhinne api pitā putraḥ bhrātā iti pratyayāḥ bhavanti tathā ekaḥ kālaḥ kārya kāraṇa viśeṣa apekṣaḥ parāpara ādi pratyaye hetuḥ iti evam upapāditaḥ kālaḥ tasya upapannasya vartamāna kāla pratiṣedha artham sūtram vartamāna abhāvaḥ patataḥ patita patitavya kāla upapatteḥ vṛntāt pracyutasya phalasya bhūmim pratyāsīdataḥ yat ūrdhvam phalam avadhim kṛtvā yāvat vṛntam iti sa patitaḥ adhvā yat adhastāt phalam eva avadhim kṛtvā yāvat bhūmiḥ iti sa patitavyaḥ adhvā na idānīm tṛtīyaḥ adhvā vidyate yatra patati iti syāt na ca adhvānam antareṇa kāla vyaktiḥ asti tasmāt na vartamāna kālaḥ asti iti 
NV_2.1.40^1	 na virodhāt vartamānaḥ kālaḥ na asti iti bruvan abhyupagatau kālau bādhate etat anujñāpana artham ca sūtram tayoḥ api abhāvaḥ vartamāna abhāve tad apekṣa tvāt vartamāna kāla apekṣau itarau kālau yasya vartamānaḥ na asti tasya vartamāna anabhyupagame abhyupagatayoḥ kālayoḥ abhāvaḥ iti na ca ayam kālaḥ adhvavyaṅgyaḥ kim tarhi kriyā vyaṅgyaḥ patati iti yadā dravyam kriyā sambandham upalabhate saḥ ayam sambandha viśiṣṭaḥ kālaḥ vartamānaḥ iti ucyate kriyā sambandha atikramāt ca atītaḥ 
NV_2.1.40^2	 yadā tu kriyā kāraṇāni abhimukhyena avasthitāni apratibaddha śaktikāni tadā bhaviṣyati kriyāḥ iti anāgataḥ kālaḥ iti yadi ca ayam vartamānām kriyām na pratipadyate kasmāt atītatām anāgatatām ca pratipadyate na kālaḥ atītaḥ na phalam atītam kālasya sarvadā vartamāna tvāt phalasya ca apatat patati patiṣyati iti kriyā viśeṣaṇa tvena pratyaya viśeṣa viṣaya tvāt kriyāyām sambhavaḥ na phale iti tasmāt kriyā kāla abhivyakti nimittam na adhvā gantavyasya tādavasthyāt yaḥ asau gantavyaḥ deśaḥ sa yathābhūtaḥ eva anutpanna kriye phale tathābhūtaḥ eva utpanna kriyaḥ iti abhedāt na adhvā kāla bheda vyakti hetuḥ 
NV_2.1.41	 atha manyase vartamāna kāla anabhyupagame api atīta anāgatau itaretara apekṣau setsyataḥ etat pratiṣedha artham sūtram na atīta anāgatayoḥ itaretara apekṣā siddhiḥ iti na hi atīta anāgatau itaretara apekṣau siddhi atas katham iti vartamāna abhāve kim atītam katham ca kim anāgatam katham ca iti na śakyate nirvaktum avyākaraṇīyam etat vartamāna lopaḥ iti viśeṣa pratiṣedhāt ca vartamānaḥ abhyupagataḥ yasmāt ayam viśeṣa pratiṣedhaḥ patataḥ patita patitavya kāla upapattiḥ iti na ca vartamāna kāla anabhyupagame patataḥ iti padasya arthaḥ asti iti na ca etat padārtha anabhyupagame patataḥ iti yuktam vaktum saḥ ayam vyāghātaḥ vartamānaḥ ca na asti patataḥ iti ca prayogaḥ na ca itaretara apekṣā kasya cit siddhiḥ asti yasmāt eka abhāve anyatara abhāvāt ubhaya abhāvaḥ yadi itaretara apekṣā siddhiḥ syāt yāvat itarat na asti tāvat itarat na asti iti ubhayoḥ abhāvaḥ 
NV_2.1.42	 artha sadbhāva vyaṅgyaḥ ca vartamānaḥ kālaḥ vidyate dravyam vidyate guṇaḥ karma iti yasya ca ayam na asti tasya vartamāna abhāve sarva agrahaṇam pratyakṣa anupapatteḥ sūtra arthaḥ virodhaḥ katham punar vartamāna abhāve pratyakṣa anupapattiḥ yasmāt idam pratyakṣam vartamāna ādhāram kāryatvāt kṣīra vat iti yat kāryam tat vartamāna adharam dṛṣṭam yathā kṣīram kāryam ca pratyakṣam tasmāt tat api vartamāna ādhāram iti vartamāna kāla anabhyupagamāt anādhāram pratyakṣam prāpnoti anādhāram ca kāryam na asti iti pratyakṣa anupapattiḥ pratyakṣa anupapatteḥ ca sarva pramāṇa lopaḥ sarva pramāṇa lope ca sarvasya grahaṇam na syāt asti ca sarvasya grahaṇam te vayam sarvasya grahaṇāt paśyāmaḥ asti vartamānaḥ pratyakṣa nimittam pratyakṣa viṣayaḥ pratyakṣam ca iti saḥ ayam vartamānaḥ kālaḥ upapannaḥ 
NV_2.1.43^1	 upapannaḥ ca san dvidhā bhidyate kva cit kriyā mātra vyaṅgyaḥ kva cit kriyā santāna vyaṅgyaḥ kriyā mātra vyaṅgyaḥ vidyate dravyam iti kriyā santāna vyaṅgyaḥ pacati chinatti iti kriyā santānaḥ api dvidhā bhavati eka ākāra kriyaḥ nānā ākāra kriyaḥ ca iti eka ākāra kriyaḥ chinatti iti yathā tatra hi udyamya udyamya nipātana kriyā eka ākārāḥ nānā ākāra kriyaḥ ca santānaḥ pacati iti tatra hi anekā kriyā aneka ākārā ca yathā edha upādānam agni abhijvālanam sthālī adhiśrayaṇam udaka āsecanam taṇḍulā vapanam darvī ghaṭṭanam avaśrāvaṇam avatāraṇam iti eṣaḥ hi evambhūtaḥ kriyā santānaḥ pacati iti anena ekena śabdena abhidhīyate kriyā santānasya hi atra avicchedaḥ vivakṣitaḥ na anā ārambhaḥ naḥ uparamaḥ iti santāna ārambha vivakṣāyām pakṣyati iti uparama vivakṣāyām apākṣīt iti 
NV_2.1.43^2	 yat ca idam chidyamānam tat kriyamāṇam tasmin akriyamāṇe kṛta tā kartavyatā upapatteḥ tu ubha yathā grahaṇam kasya vartamānasya katham ubhayathā kevalasya vyapavṛktasya atīta anāgatābhyām sampṛktasya ca tābhyām iti kva punar vyapavṛktasya vidyate dravyam iti atra hi kevalaḥ śuddhaḥ vartamānaḥ abhidhīyate pacati chinatti iti atra sampṛktaḥ katham saṃpṛktaḥ kāḥ cit tatra kriyāḥ vyatītāḥ kāḥ cit anāgatāḥ ekā ca vartamānāḥ iti anyaḥ ca loke pratyāsatti prabhṛteḥ arthasya vivakṣāyām aneka prakāraḥ vartamānasya prayogaḥ kadā cit ayam vartamānam atīte prayuṅkte āgataḥ san bravīti eṣaḥ āgacchāmi iti kadā cit anāgate prayuṅkte yathā sthitaḥ san bravīti eṣaḥ gacchāmi iti evam anyeṣu prayogeṣu utprekṣitavyaḥ 
NV_2.1.44	 atha idānīm upamānam avasara prāptam parīkṣyate kim punar upamānam prasiddha sādharmyāt sādhya sādhanam upamānam iti uktam tasya ākṣepaḥ atyanta prāya eka deśa sādharmyāt upamāna asiddhiḥ iti na atyanta sādharmyāt upamānam bhavati yathā gauḥ evam gauḥ iti bhūyas sādharmyāt api na upamānam siddhyati na hi bhavati yathā gauḥ evam mahiṣaḥ iti eka deśa sādharmyāt api na bhavati na hi bhavati yathā meruḥ tathā sarṣapaḥ iti na ca anyā gatiḥ asti tasmāt naḥ upamānam sidhyati atyanta ādi sādharmyāt upamāna pratiṣedhe naḥ upamāna pratiṣedhaḥ iti yat atyanta prāya eka deśa sādharmyāt upamānam tat pratiṣiddhyate tena sūtreṇa na punar upamāna mātrasya pratiṣedhaḥ tathā sati yat anyathā upapmānam tasya sva rūpam vaktavyam atha naḥ eva anyathā upamānam asti iti pratipadyase vyartham tarhi idam vākyam atyanta prāya eka deśa sādharmyāt upamāna asiddhiḥ iti anabhyupagacchatā hi upamānam evam vaktavyam upamānam apramāṇam artha apratipādaka tvāt iti 
NV_2.1.45	 prasiddha sādharmyasya vaidharmyasya ca upamāna hetu tvāt apratiṣedhaḥ yaḥ ayam bhavatā pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate atyanta ādi sādharmyāt upamānam na sidhyati iti ayam anupapannaḥ anabhyupagamāt kaḥ khalu evam āha atyanta ādi sādharmyāt upamānam iti api tu prasiddha sādharmyāt upamānam sādhya sādhana bhāvam āśritya pravartate tathā ca ayam apratiṣedhaḥ sarvathā asaṃbhavāt atyanta sādharmyāt upamānam sidhyati yadā tad kriyayā eva tad kriyā upamīyate yathā rāma rāvaṇayoḥ yuddham rāma rāvaṇayoḥ iva iti prāyas sādharmyeṇa api yadā goḥ bala prakarṣa jijñāsā bhavati tadā bhūyas sādharmyeṇa upamānam yathā mahiṣaḥ tathā gauḥ iti eka deśa sādharmyāt api bhavati yadā tu sat mātram jijñāpayiṣitavyam bhavati meroḥ sattā kiṃrūpāḥ iti tadā yathā sarṣapasya tathā meroḥ tasmāt apratiṣedhaḥ ayam iti 
NV_2.1.46–2.1.47	 astu tarhi upamānam anumānam pratyakṣeṇa apratyakṣa siddheḥ yathā pratyakṣeṇa dhūma dharmeṇa ūrdhva gati ādinā apratyakṣaḥ dhūma dharmaḥ agniḥ anumīyate tathā pratyakṣeṇa gavā apratyakṣasya gavayasya pratipattiḥ iti apratyakṣa artha pratipādaka tvāt upamānam anumānam iti na aparijñānāt na bhavatā upamāna lakṣaṇam vyajñāyi na ca apratyakṣe gavaye upamāna artham paśyāmaḥ na apratyakṣe gavaye pramāṇa artham upamānasya paśyāmaḥ atha pratyakṣe gavaye kaḥ upamāna arthaḥ yā asau saṃjñā saṃjñi sambandha pratipattiḥ saḥ upamāna arthaḥ evam ca naḥ upamānam āgamaḥ na pratyakṣam na hi ayam āgamāt pratyakṣāt vai ayam gavayaḥ iti pratipadyate iti 
NV_2.1.48	 para artha tvāt ca para artham ca upamānam bhavati na hi yathā gauḥ evam gavayaḥ iti etat āgamam antareṇa sārūpya mātra parijñānam upamānam uktam na hi āgama mātram sārūpya parijñānam antareṇa upamānam bhavitum arhati na ca evam anumānam tasmāt yathā liṅga liṅgi saṃbandha smṛti anugrahe sati liṅga parāmarśaḥ anumānam tat ca pratyakṣam tathā āgama āhita saṃskāra smṛti apekṣam sārūpya pratyakṣam upamānam iti pratipatti bhedāt ca na anumānam evam bhavati yathā dhūmaḥ tathā agniḥ iti asti tu upamāne yathā gauḥ evam gavayaḥ iti yatra ca pratipatti bhedaḥ tat pramāṇa antaram yathā pratyakṣāt anumānam apūrvān adhigamāt upamānam na bhavati iti anena pratyuktam 
NV_2.1.49^1	 atha avasara prāptaḥ śabdaḥ parīkṣyate kaḥ punar ayam śabdaḥ āpta upadeśaḥ śabdaḥ iti uktam tasya ākṣepaḥ na śabdaḥ pramāṇam sati api aprasiddheḥ yasmāt vidyamānaḥ api ayam śabdaḥ aśrūyamāṇaḥ na pratipatti hetuḥ pratipatti hetuḥ ca pramāṇam iti viṣaya abhāvāt ca na ca pratyakṣa anumāna viṣaya vyatirekī viṣayaḥ śabdasya asti na ca aviṣayam pramāṇam iti avijñāna ātmaka tvāt ca na pramāṇam yat pramāṇam tat vijñāna ātmakam pratyakṣa ādi avijñāna ātmakam ca na pramāṇam ghaṭāt bāhya karaṇa pratyakṣa tvāt ca ghaṭa ādi vat eva na pramāṇam ātmani asamavāyāt na ghaṭa ādi vat eva pramāṇam ākāśa guṇa tvāt tat saṃkhyā ādi vat na pramāṇam yat tāvat sati api apramiteḥ iti tat na asiddha tvāt na hi kadā cit śabdaḥ upalabhyamāne na pramā bhavati anupalabhyamāne na bhavati iti na asau pramāṇam tadā pramāṇam hi nāma yena pramīyate kadā ca tena pramīyate yadā upalabhyate yat punar etat viṣaya abhāvāt iti kaḥ evam āha pratyakṣa anumāna vyatirekī viṣayaḥ na asti iti ayam api asiddhaḥ hetuḥ 
NV_2.1.49^2	 yathā ca pratyakṣa ādibhyaḥ viṣaya bhedaḥ tathā uktam yat punar etat avijñāna ātmaka tvāt bāhya karaṇa grāhya tvāt ātmani asamavāyāt ca iti na anekāntāt pradīpa vat pradīpe etat sarvam asti pramāṇam ca pradīpaḥ pratyakṣa aṅga tvāt iti uktam tasmāt anaikāntika tvāt ahetavaḥ eva iti yat punar etat ākāśa guṇa tvāt ayam api anaikāntikaḥ eva yathā ākāśe yat parimāṇam tat mahat pratyaya kartṛ tvāt pramāṇam bhavati tasmāt ākāśa guṇa tvāt iti ayam api ahetuḥ anumānam śabdaḥ smṛti apekṣa tvāt yasya smṛti apekṣi tvam tat anumānam 
NV_2.1.49^3	 smṛti apekṣaḥ ca śabdaḥ artha pratyāyane tasmāt anumānam tri kāla viṣaya tvāt ca tri kāla viṣayam anumānam tathā ca śabdaḥ tasmāt anumānam anvaya vyatireka upapatteḥ ca yat anvayavyatireki tat anumānam dṛṣṭam yathā dhūma viśeṣa darśanam agni mat dhūma viśeṣa pratipattau tathā ca śabdaḥ anvaya vyatirekābhyām eva artham pratipādayati tasmāt anumānam itas ca śabdaḥ anumānam śabdaḥ anumānam arthasya anupalabdheḥ anumeya tvāt pratyakṣeṇa anupalabhyamāna artha viṣaya tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NV_2.1.50–2.1.51	 itas ca anumānam upalabdheḥ at vipravṛtti tvāt pramāṇa antara bhāve upalabdhi bhedaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yathā pratyakṣe anumāne ca anyathā hi pratyakṣe upalabdhiḥ anyathā anumāne na tu evam śabde iti tasmāt na pramāṇa antaram sambaddha artha pratipādaka tvāt ca iti sūtra arthaḥ sambaddha artha pratipādakam anumānam tathā ca śabdaḥ iti 
NV_2.1.52^1	 yat tāvat smṛti apekṣa tvāt anumānam śabdaḥ iti tat na anaikāntika tvāt anumāne api smṛti apekṣi tvam asti yathā saṃśaye yathā tarke yathā upamāne iti etena tri kāla viṣaya tvam pratyuktam yat punar etat anvaya vyatireka upapatteḥ iti anvaya vyatireka upapattiḥ pratyakṣe api yathā yatra ghaṭaḥ tatra ghaṭa jñānan yatra na asti tatra tad abhāvaḥ iti yat punar etat anupalabhyamāna artha viṣaya tvāt iti satyam anupalabhyamāna artha viṣayam anumānam na punar svarga apūrva devatā ādi artheṣu laukikasya pratyakṣam anumānam vā api tu āpta upadeśa sāmarthyāt śabdāt artha saṃpratyayaḥ na hi ayam śabda mātrāt svarga ādīn pratipadyate kim tu puruṣa viśeṣa abhihita tvena pramāṇa tvam pratipadyate 
NV_2.1.52^2	 tathābhūtāt śabdāt svarga ādīn pratipadyate na ca evam anumāne tasmāt na anumānam śabdaḥ iti śabdam ca ullikhantī pratipattiḥ śabdāt na anumānāt iti etena advipravṛtti tvam vyākhyātam yat punar etat sambandhāt ca iti asti śabda arthayoḥ sambandhaḥ anujñātaḥ asti ca pratiṣiddhaḥ vācya vācaka bhāva lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ anujñātaḥ asya śabdasya ayam arthaḥ vācyaḥ iti yaḥ punar ayam svābhāvikaḥ śabda arthayoḥ sambandhaḥ iti kaiḥ cit abhyupagamyate sa pratiṣiddhaḥ na svābhāvikaḥ śabda arthayoḥ sambandhaḥ asti katham na asti pramāṇataḥ anupalabdheḥ tatra pratyakṣeṇa tāvat śabda artha saṃbandhasya anupalabdhiḥ atīndriya viṣaya tvāt yasmāt śabdasya atīndriyaḥ api arthaḥ viṣayaḥ tasmāt na pratyakṣeṇa upalabdhiḥ iti 
NV_2.1.53^1	 anumānena upalapsyate iti ced na anumānena api vikalpa anupapatteḥ śabdaḥ vā artha deśam upasampadyate arthaḥ vā śabda deśam ubhayam vā na tāvat arthaḥ śabda deśam upasampadyate pūraṇa pradāha pāṭana anupalabdheḥ pūraṇa pradāha pāṭana anupalabdheḥ ca sambandha abhāvaḥ āsyaḥ eka deśa sthāna karaṇa uccāraṇīyaḥ śabdaḥ iti anna agni asi śabda uccāraṇe pūraṇa pradāha pāṭanāni gṛhyeran mūrtimān ca mahān padārthaḥ modaka ādiḥ gavā ādi vat āgacchan upalabhyeta tatas ca śabdena loka vyavahāraḥ ucchidyeta atha śabdaḥ artha antikam upasampadyate tasya api anupapattiḥ vyāghātāt nityaḥ ca śabdaḥ santāna vṛttyā ca āgacchati iti vyāhatam atha naḥ āgacchati artha deśe eva bhavati iti nityaḥ ca bhavati ca iti anivṛttaḥ vyāghātaḥ 
NV_2.1.53^2	 sthāna karaṇa prayatna asambhavāt ca artha deśe na bhavati atha na gacchati na bhavati tatra vyajyate ekaḥ vitatya avasthitaḥ iti ced na sarva artha upalabdhi prasaṅgāt yadi sarva śabdāḥ eva vitatya avasthitāḥ sthāna karaṇa ādi nimitta sannidhāne sati vyajyante iti manyase sarva arthānām upalabdhiḥ prāptā yat ekasya śabdasya vyañjakam tat śabda antarāṇām api iti vitatya avasthitasya śabdaḥ vyajyataḥ iti sva viṣaya vyāpti avasthāne sati yatra kva cana avasthitānām go śabda abhivyaktau kakudādimad artha pratyāyanam syāt atha sāmānya vat etat syāt yathā sāmānyam sva viṣayam vyāpya avasthitam na ca sarvatra upalabhyate tathā śabde api sva viṣayam vyāpya avasthite niyamaḥ bhaviṣyati iti na yuktam evam bhavitum sāmānyasya āśraya upalabdhiḥ vyakti hetuḥ 
NV_2.1.53^3	 na punar śabdasya āśraya upalabdhiḥ asti na ca vācye vṛttiḥ tasmāt asamaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ yadi ca vācya artha vṛttiḥ śabdaḥ syāt vācya upalabdhau akṛta samayena api pratipādyeta yathā sāmānyam akṛta samayaḥ api pratipadyate iti tasmāt na anumānāt api pratipadyate itas ca sva āśrayāt anyena na sambandhī śabdaḥ guṇa tvāt anyena gavā ādinā śabdam prati samavāyaḥ na asti śabdasya ākāśa vṛtti tvāt na api śabda arthayoḥ eka artha samavāyaḥ sva ātmani ekasya anārambhāt upamānāt pratipatsyate iti na upamānasya api na viṣayaḥ āgamāt pratipatsyate iti ced saḥ eva atra vicāryate kim śabda arthau sambaddhau āhosvit asambaddhau iti yat tu idam bhavatā abhidhīyate smṛti ādi apekṣa tvāt anumāna sādharmyāt anumānam śabdaḥ iti tasmāt eva na anumānam 
NV_2.1.53^4	 na hi tena eva tasya sādharmyam iti atha smṛti ādi sādharmyāt śabda anumānayoḥ eka tvam eva tarhi ekam pramāṇam prāpnoti asti hi artha paricchedaka tvam sarva pramāṇānām sādharmyam iti bhavatu ekam pramāṇam kim naḥ bādhyate iti katham na bādhyate iti yat abhīṣṭam tat nivartate kim ca abhīṣṭam pratyakṣa anumāne bhinne iti atha sāmānyam āśritya abhedaḥ deśyate tadā upekṣayā vartitavyam sāmānyam āśritya abhedaḥ viśeṣam āśritya bhedaḥ iti na kim cit bādhitam na ca anumānam śabdaḥ sva para ātma pratyāyaka tvāt yat sva para ātma pratyāyakam tat anumānam na bhavati yathā pradīpaḥ pradīpaḥ yena kriyate tasya api upalabdhi sādhanam bhavati itarasya api śabdaḥ api evam tasmāt na anumānam iti 
NV_2.1.54	 yadi śabda arthau asambaddhau syātām śabda artha pratyaya vyavasthā na syāt śabdaḥ sambaddhaḥ artham pratipādayati pratyaya niyama hetu tvāt pradīpa vat yaḥ pratyaya niyama hetuḥ sa sambaddhaḥ artha pratipādakaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yathā pradīpaḥ śabdaḥ ca evaṃdharmā tasmāt śabdaḥ api sambaddha artha pratipādakaḥ iti pratyayaḥ vā pakṣīkartavyaḥ sambaddhābhyām śabda arthābhyām vastu pratyayaḥ bhavati niyamāt kuṇḍalī iti pratyaya vat 
NV_2.1.55	 na sambandha kāritam śabda artha vyavasthānam kim tarhi samaya kāritam kaḥ punar ayam samayaḥ abhidhāna abhidheya niyama niyogaḥ tasmin upayukte śabda artha vyavasthā bhavati kaḥ cit ca sambandhaḥ anujñātaḥ iti yat avocāma samayam tat avocāmaḥ iti sā iyam śabda artha vyavasthāḥ anyathā api bhavati iti ahetuḥ ayam ca vācya vācaka bhāva lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ svābhāvika śabda artha sambandha vādinā abhyanujñeyaḥ na hi svābhāvika sambandha vādinaḥ anupayukta śabda artha sambandhasya śabda śravaṇāt viśeṣa pratyayaḥ bhavati sa punar samayaḥ kutas pratyetavyaḥ pada jñānāt lokataḥ ca iti tat hi śāstram samayasya avilopa artham praṇītam lokataḥ ca samayaḥ boddhavyaḥ mātrā ādīn teṣu teṣu artheṣu tān tān śabdān prayuñjānān upalabhya saḥ api tathā eva śikṣitaḥ tān eva śabdān teṣu teṣu artheṣu prayuṅkte na punar enam kaḥ cit lipim iva śikṣayati iti 
NV_2.1.56	 na svābhāvikaḥ śabda arthayoḥ sambandhaḥ yadi svābhāvikaḥ śabda arthayoḥ sambandhaḥ abhaviṣyan na jāti viśeṣe śabda artha vyavasthā abhaviṣyat asti tu yathākāmam prayogaḥ jāti viśeṣe yathākāmam prayogaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ na punar svābhāvikena sambandhena sambaddhānām jāti viśeṣe vyabhicāraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ na hi pradīpaḥ asmākam anyathā prakāśayati anyathā jāti viśeṣaḥ iti jāti viśeṣa śabdena punar deśaḥ abhidhīyate iti 
NV_2.1.57^1	 tad aprāmāṇyam anṛta vyāghāta punarukta doṣebhyaḥ iti sūtram tat iti adhikṛta śabda abhidhānāt śabda viśeṣa adhikāraḥ yasmāt prāptam api prakaraṇena śabdam tad śabdena punar abhidhatte tat jñāpayati śabda viśeṣam prati iyam cintā na tu śabda mātram prati anyathā evam vaktavyam apramāṇam śabdaḥ anṛta vyāghāta punarukta doṣebhyaḥ iti aprāmāṇyam arthasya apratyāyaka tvam anṛta tvam ayathārtha abhidhānam vyāghātaḥ padayoḥ vākyayoḥ vā saha asambhavaḥ punaruktam pūrva abhihita artha abhidhānam udāharaṇāni bhāṣye tatra anṛta tve hetuḥ phala adarśanam 
NV_2.1.57^2	 agnihotram juhuyāt iti vidhi vākyam asya vyāghātaḥ kālāsambhavena udita anudita samaya adhyuṣita pratiṣedhāt na ca anyaḥ kālaḥ vidyate yatra agni hotra havanam syāt udita anudita samaya adhyuṣita vākyānām vā paraspara virodhaḥ prathama uttamayoḥ sāmidhenyoḥ tris abhidhānam punar uktam udāharaṇam ca bhāṣye dṛṣṭānta tvena etāni vākyāni upanyasya eka kartṛka tvena śeṣa vākyānām apramāṇa tvam iti agnihotra ādi vākyānām vā pramāṇa tva pratiṣedhaḥ veda eka deśa tvena tad anya vākya vat punarukta tāyām pūrvam uttaram vā na vākyam ekena pratīyamāna tvāt 
NV_2.1.58^1	 yat tāvat anṛta tvāt apramāṇam veda vākyāni phala adarśanāt iti tat atra sampradhāryam kim phala adarśanam veda vākyānām apramāṇa tvāt āho karma kartṛ sādhana vaiguṇyāt iti vayam tu brūmaḥ karma kartṛ sādhana vaiguṇyāt iti phala adarśanāt ca kāraṇānām asāmagyram gamyate iṣṭeḥ karaṇa sādhana tvena abhyupagamāt ca doṣaḥ na ca iyam iṣṭiḥ mayā sākṣāt putra kāraṇa tvena abhyupagamyate api tu pitarau iṣṭyā saṃprayujyamānau putram janayataḥ tatra na jñāyate kim pitroḥ asāt guṇyāt putra janma na bhavati āhosvit iṣṭeḥ asāt guṇyāt iti mantrāh ca iṣṭa sādhana tvena prayujyamānāḥ iṣṭi aṅgam bhavanti tatra api na jñāyate kim iṣṭiḥ mantrāṇām vaiguṇyāt na sampannāḥ āhosvit darbha idhma ādeḥ kāraṇasya vaiguṇyāt iti 
NV_2.1.58^2	 yathā eva mantrāṇām nyūna adhika bhāvena prayujyamānānām iṣṭiḥ na nirvartate tathā darbha idhma ādeḥ api sādhanasya vaiguṇyāt iti na kevalam sādhana vaikalyāt eva iṣṭeḥ anabhinirvṛttiḥ tathā iṣṭeḥ sādhayituḥ karmaṇaḥ ca asāt guṇyāt iti upetya iṣṭi sampadam na kevalāḥ eva iṣṭiḥ kāraṇam iti uktam tatra putra janma adarśanena na yuktam vaktum manuṣya dharmaṇā mantrāṇām asāmarthyāt puttra anutpattiḥ iti ubhayathā dṛṣṭa tvāt sandehaḥ iti ced na abhyupeta hāneḥ atha manyase tri kāraṇam putra janma tatra anyatara kāraṇa vaikalyāt putraḥ na bhavati iti kāraṇa vaikalyam gamyate tatra yathā eva pitryoḥ vaiguṇyāt putra an utpattiḥ tathā mantrāṇām api apramāṇa tvāt iti sandihyate 
NV_2.1.58^3	 na abhyupeta hāneḥ pūrvam bhavatā abhyadhāyi vedaḥ apramāṇam iti adhunā tu abhidhīyate sandigdham pramāṇa tvam iti evam ca bruvatā pūrvaḥ vādaḥ tyaktaḥ bhavati samānam iti ced atha manyase samānam etat bhavataḥ api kim pitroḥ vaiguṇyāt putra ajanmaḥ uta aho veda vākyānām apramāṇa tvāt iti sandihyate nāsādhanāt na mayā etat sādhyate veda vākyāni pramāṇam apramāṇam vā iti bhavatā tu sādhyate tatra mayā bhavataḥ sādhanāni atara vaiguṇyāt putra janma na bhavati iti sandigdhaḥ hetuḥ apadiśyate tad sahakāri tvāt ca upadeśaḥ dāru mathana vat iti na iyam iṣṭiḥ sākṣāt kāraṇa tvena putra janmanaḥ upadiśyate api tu putra kāmaḥ iṣṭim kurvīta iti 
NV_2.1.58^4	 yathā agni kāmaḥ dāruṇī mathnīyāt iti upadeśaḥ tatra ca kartṛ karmaṇoḥ vaiguṇyāt agniḥ na bhavati iti naḥ upadeśa vaiyarthyam tathā iha api iti adoṣaḥ sāmastye phala niṣpatti darśanāt ca yatra ca samastāni kāraṇāni tatra phala abhinirvṛttiḥ dṛṣṭāḥ iti adoṣaḥ yat ca idam vākyam tad aprāmāṇyam anṛta vyāghāta punarukta doṣebhyaḥ iti tat api veda vākyasya pakṣīkṛta tvāt avyāpakam atha yāni evaṃdharmakāṇi vākyāni tāni pakṣīkriyante teṣu api eṣām dharmāṇām viśeṣaṇa tvena upayukta tvāt aprāmāṇya pratipādakaḥ hetuḥ vaktavyaḥ anṛta tvāt aprāmāṇyam iti ced kim idam anṛta tvam nāma yadi ayathārtha abhidhānam nanu ayam eva pratijñā arthaḥ apramāṇam iti anṛta tvam ca asiddham iti uktam etat 
NV_2.1.59^1	 yat punar etat vyāghāta doṣāt iti abhyupetya kāla bhede doṣa vacanāt na vyāghātaḥ agni ādhāna kāle eva ayam niyama parigrahaḥ udite hotavyam anudite hotavyam samaya adhyuṣite hotavyam iti saḥ ayam abhyupetya kālam yadā atikrāmati tadā abhyupeta kāla atikramāt nindyate nindā vacane ca na vyāghātaḥ ubhaya pratiṣedha anabhidhānāt na idam anyathā yadi punar etat ubhaya pratiṣedha abhidhānam syāt bhavet ayam prasaṅgaḥ vyāghātaḥ iti na punar etāni pratiṣedha vākyāni udite hotavyam iti evam ādīni tasmāt aprasaṅgaḥ ayam iti 
NV_2.1.59^2	 atha punar etāni vākyāni homa vidhi pratiṣedhakāni syuḥ tadā udita ādi grahaṇam vyartham evam eva vaktavyam iti agnihotram juhuyāt iti yat vākyam tat na kartavyam iti evam ca saṃgata artha tā yathā etat vyākhyātam evam pūrva uttare ca vākye saṅgate bhavataḥ havanam anūdya kāla viśeṣa vidhānāt iti evam etat na punar yathā asmābhiḥ vyāghātaḥ abhidhīyate iti niyama hetuḥ vaktavyaḥ idam eva udita ādi vākyam niyama hetuḥ katham iti idam eva udita ādi vākyam kāmataḥ vā vikalpya ita abhihitam vā anūdyate iti abhihita anuvādaḥ nyāyaḥ tatra hi pramāṇānām avisaṃvādaḥ itaratra vyāghātaḥ iti 
NV_2.1.60	 yat punar etat punar ukta doṣāt iti na punar ukta doṣaḥ anuvāda upapatteḥ punaruktam nāma tasya eva arthasya anaṅgīkṛta viśeṣasya yat punarvacanam anuvādaḥ tu punar śruti sāmānyāt aṅgīkṛta viśeṣasya arthasya vādaḥ evam ca sati yathā uktaḥ na doṣaḥ udāharaṇam bhāṣye putra kāma iṣṭi ādi vākyāni pramā veda eka deśa tvāt bhūmiḥ āvapanam mahat iti vākya vat itas ca pada ādi niyamāt dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ iti vākya vat itas ca kartṛ viśeṣa abhihita tvāt agniḥ himasya bheṣajam iti vākya vat 
NV_2.1.61–2.1.62	 samastāni vā veda vākyāni pakṣīkṛtya abhidhīyante pramāṇam veda vākyāni artha vibhāgavat tvāt manu ādi vākya vat yathā manu ādi vākyāni artha vibhāgavanti artha vibhāgavat tve sati prāmāṇyam tathā ca veda vākyāni artha vibhāgavanti tasmāt pramāṇam iti vibhāgaḥ ca trividhaḥ bhavati vidhi artha vāda anuvāda vacana viniyogāt tridhā khalu brāhmaṇa vākyāni bhavanti vidhi vacanāni arthavāda vacanāni anuvāda vacanāni ca 
NV_2.1.63–2.1.66	 tatra vidhiḥ vidhāyakaḥ yat vākyam vidhāyakam deśakam sa vidhiḥ vidhiḥ tu niyogaḥ anujñā vā yat vākyam vidhatte idam kuryāt iti sa niyogaḥ anujñā tu yat kurvāṇukam anujānāti tat anujñā vākyam yathā agnihotra vākyam eva tad sādhana avāpti pravṛtti pūrvaka tvam anujānāti eṣām udāharaṇāni bhāṣye vidhi anuvacanam ca anuvādaḥ vihita anuvacanam ca pūrvaḥ śabda anuvādaḥ paraḥ artha anuvādaḥ yathā punaruktam dvividham śabda punaruktam artha punaruktam ca śabda punaruktam anityaḥ nityaḥ iti artha punaruktam anityaḥ nirodha dharmakaḥ iti kaḥ asya sūtrasya arthaḥ pratīta artha śabda abhyāsaḥ anuvāda punaruktayoḥ sāmyam punaruktaḥ api pratīta arthaḥ śabdaḥ abhyasyate anuvāde api evam atas pratīta artha śabda abhyāsāt ubhayam asādhu iti 
NV_2.1.67^1	 śīghratara gamana upadeśa vat abhyāsāt na aviśeṣaḥ iti yathā śīghram gamyatām śīghrataram gamyatām iti ca tarapā kriyā atiśayaḥ abhidhīyate tathā anuvāda lakṣaṇena api abhyāsena kriyā atiśayaḥ abhidhīyate iti asya prayogaḥ arthavān anuvāda lakṣaṇaḥ abhyāsaḥ pratyaya viśeṣa hetu tvāt śīghratara gamana upadeśa vat yathā śīghra śabdāt śīghratara śabdaḥ prayujyamānaḥ pratyaya viśeṣa hetu tvāt na punar ukta doṣam labhate tathā anuvāda lakṣaṇaḥ abhyāsaḥ pratyaya viśeṣa hetu tvāt na punarukta doṣam lapsyate iti kaḥ punar asau viśeṣaḥ bhavati iti vaktavyam tat ucyate 
NV_2.1.67^2	 ādye pacati śabda prayoge pākaḥ nirvartanīyaḥ iti paktuḥ pratyayaḥ bhavati dvitīyāt tu pacati śabdāt avadhāraṇa pratyayaḥ bhavati mayā eva paktavyam iti sātatya pratyayaḥ vā bhavati satatam mayā paktavayam iti adhyeṣaṇa pratyayaḥ vā bhavati mām eva ayam adhikurutaḥ iti āśu pratyayaḥ vā bhavati āśu mayā paktavyam iti evam śrotuḥ yathā ca śrotuḥ tathā ca vaktuḥ api ete eva pratyayāḥ bhavanti iti punarukte tu na kaḥ cit viśeṣaḥ gamyate iti asti mahān viśeṣaḥ punar ukta anuvādayoḥ evam anyaḥ api anuvādasya prayogaḥ loke boddhavyaḥ iti 
NV_2.1.68^1	 kim punar pratiṣedha hetu uddhārāt eva pramāṇa tā veda vākyānām siddhāḥ na kim kāraṇam na sādhanam antareṇa siddhiḥ asti iti kutas tarhi pramāṇataḥ kim tat pramāṇam artha vibhāgavat tvam mantra āyurveda prāmāṇya vat ca tad prāmāṇyam āpta prāmāṇyāt ca śabdaḥ pūrva hetu anukarṣaṇa arthaḥ yathā mantra āyurveda vākyāni puruṣa viśeṣa abhihita tvāt pramāṇam tathā veda vākyāni iti puruṣa viśeṣa abhihita tvam hetuḥ kim āyurvedasya prāmāṇyam yat tat āyurvedena upadiśyate idam kṛtvā iṣṭam adhigacchati idam kṛtvā aniṣṭam jahāti tasya anuṣṭhīyamānasya tathā abhāvaḥ aviparyayaḥ etat prāmāṇyam kiṃkṛtam etat 
NV_2.1.68^2	 āpta prāmāṇya kṛtam kim punar āptānām pramāṇa tvam sākṣāt kṛta dharmatā yam te padārtham upadiśanti sa taiḥ sākṣāt kṛtaḥ bhavati iti bhūta dayā ca yasmai ca upadiśanti tam pratyeṣām anukampā bhavati yathā parijñāna artha cikhyā payiṣā ca asya bhavati etena trividhena viśeṣaṇena viśiṣṭaḥ vaktā āptaḥ tena yaḥ upadeśaḥ kriyate sa pramāṇam iti dṛṣṭa artha vākya avisaṃvādena vā śeṣa anumānam yat vākyam dṛṣṭa artham yathā grāma kāmaḥ yajeta iti evam ādi tena śeṣa anumānam pramāṇam iti laukikam api vākyam anenaḥ eva tri prakāreṇa viśeṣaṇena viśiṣṭasya vaktuḥ pramāṇam bhavati asya prayogaḥ 
NV_2.1.68^3	 pramāṇam veda vākyāni vaktṛ viśeṣa abhihita tvāt mantra āyurveda vākya vat iti eka kartṛka tvena vā mantra āyurveda vākyāni pakṣīkṛtya alaukika viṣaya pratipādaka tvena vaidharmya hetuḥ vaktavyaḥ pauruṣeya tvam asiddham nitya tvāt iti ced atha manyase nityāni veda vākyāni nitya tvāt ca eṣām prāmāṇyam tasmāt pauruṣeya tvam asiddham na asiddha tvāt siddhe nitya tve etat yuktam vaktum tat tu na siddham iti atas na yuktam etat yadi na nityāni katham pramāṇam pratipādaka tvāt pramāṇam na nitya tvāt ke cit tu bruvate na kim cit nityam pramāṇam asti iti pramāṇa tvāt eva anityāni iti tat tu na samyak iti paśyāmaḥ 
NV_2.1.68^4	 nityam api pramāṇam yathā manaḥ ātmā ca pramāṇa śabdasya samudāya vāci tvāt ayam khalu pramāṇa śabdaḥ samudāye vartate tatra ca nityam anityam ca anekam samudāyi pramāṇasya aṅga tvāt pramāṇam iti ucyate yathā pradīpaḥ evam ca nityam api pramāṇam asti iti yadā ca paramāṇu ādi nityam itara vastu sādhaka tvena upādīyate tadā paramāṇu ādeḥ nityasya pramāṇa bhāvāt pramāṇa tvāt anityaḥ iti anekāntaḥ bhavati iti anuttaram etat tasmāt yuktam artha vibhāgavat tvāt antiya tvam laukika vākya vat iti yathārtha vibhāgavanti laukika vākyāni tathā ca veda vākyāni tasmāt na nityāni iti 
NV_2.1.68^5	 laukika vākyāni api nityāni iti ced atha manyase yāni api etāni laukika vākyāni artha vibhāgavanti tāni api nityāni iti artha visaṃvādaḥ na syāt yaḥ ayam artha visaṃvādaḥ laukike vākye sa na syāt dṛṣṭaḥ tu tāni anityāni iti ced viśeṣa hetuḥ vaktavyaḥ tulye artha vibhāgavat tve tulye ca artha pratipādaka tve laukikāni anityāni vaidikāni nityāni iti viśeṣa hetuḥ vaktavyaḥ tulyam bhavataḥ api anitya tve viśeṣa hetuḥ vaktavyaḥ iti uktaḥ artha vibhāgavat tvam hetuḥ itas ca varṇavat tvāt varṇavanti laukikāni vākyāni anityāni ca tathā ca veda vākyāni tasmāt tāni api anityāni 
NV_2.1.68^6	 itas ca sāmānya viśeṣavat tve sati śrotra grāhya tvāt laukika vākya vat eva itas ca pada ādi niyamāt laukika vākya vat darśanasya para artha tvāt iti ced atha manyase darśanam para artham dṛṣṭam darśana śabdaḥ uccāraṇa arthaḥ tat ca uccāraṇam para pratipādana artham na hi kaḥ cit ātma pratipattaye śabdam uccārayati yadi ca ayam nityaḥ bhavati tatas śabdāt artha pratyayaḥ yuktaḥ atha anityaḥ utpanna pradhvaṃsī tatas asya śrotuḥ nityam apūrvaḥ śabdaḥ śrotra viṣayam iti na ca apūrva śabda śravaṇāt sampratipattiḥ yuktāḥ na hi nārikela dvīpa vāsinaḥ aprasiddha go śabdasya go śabda śravaṇāt kakudādimad artha pratipattiḥ bhavati 
NV_2.1.68^7	 tathā ca anitya vādinaḥ sarve śabdāḥ tasmāt asya api śabdāt pratyaya niyamaḥ na prāptaḥ iti na anekāntāt kṣaṇa vidhvaṃsiṣu api pradīpeṣu para pratyāyanam dṛṣṭam iti na udāharaṇa vaidharmyāt pradīpaḥ anākhyātaḥ prakāśanīya artha sambandhāt prakāśanīya artha sampratipattim karoti na punar anākhyātaḥ śabdaḥ iti kaḥ evam āha anākhyātaḥ śabdaḥ pratipādayati iti sambandhasya adarśanāt ākhyānam anupapannam uktam etat yathā na śabda arthayoḥ prāpti lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ asti iti vācya vācaka bhāva lakṣaṇaḥ tu pauruṣeyaḥ sambandhaḥ sa ca kṛtakaḥ iti sa ca saṃsāra anādi tvāt lokataḥ avagamyate 
NV_2.1.68^8	 ye tu saṃsāram anādimantam varṇayanti te evam upālabhyāḥ atha yaḥ ayam abhilāpaḥ nityāḥ vedāḥ iti sa katham sampradāyasya avicchedāt tāni eva veda vākyāni manvantara catur yuga antareṣu sampradāya abhyāsa avi= chedena pravartante tad apekṣayā laukikāḥ śabdāt na prayuñjate nityāḥ vedāḥ iti yathā nityāḥ saritaḥ nityāḥ parvatāḥ iti etat ca manu ādi vākyeṣu samānam kutas etat sampradāya abhyāsa avi= chedāt nitya tvam na punar nitya tvāt eva anitya tve pramāṇa avighātāt yāni mayā anitya tve pramāṇāni upadiṣṭāni tāni na vihanyante teṣām avighātāt anitya tve sati sampradāya abhyāsa avi= chedāt nitya tva upacāraḥ iti 
NV_2.2.1^1	 pratyakṣa anumāna upamāna śabdāḥ pramāṇāni iti sūtram tasya apekṣaḥ na catuṣṭvam aitihya arthāpatti sambhava abhāva prāmāṇyāt asya arthaḥ ayathārthaḥ ayam pramāṇa uddeśaḥ iti na catvāri eva pramāṇāni aitihya arthāpatti sambhava abhāvāḥ api pramāṇāni iti saṃśaya vyudāsa artham vai aitihya ādayaḥ upakṣipya pratiṣidhyante pratyakṣa ādīni ca pramāṇāni iti aitihya ādīni ca iti ke cit manyante tatra śrotuḥ saṃśayaḥ syāt kim vidyamānāḥ aitihi ādayaḥ na abhihitāḥ uta avidyamānāḥ iti vidhini ūna tā parihāra artham vā prakaraṇam vidyamānāni aitihyādīni na abhihitāni iti vidhi hīnam śāstram syāt doṣavatām doṣa an abhidhānāt doṣa hīnam vā śāstram syāt iti atas uddiśya nivartyante doṣavantaḥ aitihi āt ayaḥ iti atas na abhidhīyante iti doṣaḥ tarhi vaktavyaḥ atha doṣaḥ na abhidhīyate doṣa hīnam śāstram iti tad parihāra artham prakaraṇam upadiśyate pratyakṣa ādiṣu antarbhāva pradarśana artham vā aitihya ādīni pratyakṣa ādiṣu antar bhāvayitum ye yatra antarbhavanti tatra teṣām pradarśana artham prakaraṇam iti 
NV_2.2.1^2	 siddha tvāt anārambhaḥ nanu ayam arthaḥ catvāri eva pramāṇāni iti etasmin eva vibhāga uddeśa sūtre siddhaḥ iti siddha tvāt punar anārambhaḥ iti na avadhāraṇa prayojanasya itas siddheḥ yena nyāyena catvāri eva pramāṇāni iti etat avasthāpyate sa nyāyaḥ iha prakaraṇe varṇyate tasmāt ārabhyam eva iti kim idam aitihyam nāma anirdiṣṭa pravaktṛkam pravāda pāramparyam iti ha ūcuḥ vṛddhāḥ kathayanti iti arthāt āpattiḥ arthāpattiḥ āpattiḥ prāptiḥ prasaṅgaḥ yasmin vākye abhidhīyamānāt arthāt anyaḥ arthaḥ āpadyate sārtha āpattiḥ yathā asatsu megheṣu vṛṣṭiḥ na bhavati iti kim atra arthāt āpadayte satsu bhavati iti sambhavaḥ nāma āvina abhāvavartinaḥ padārthasya grahaṇāt anyasya sattā vijñānam yathā droṇasya sattā grahaṇāt āḍhakasya sattā iti abhāvaḥ pratyanīkasya grahaṇāt tad virodhinaḥ grahaṇam yathā vidhārake vāyu abhra saṃyoge sati guru tva pratibandhāt apām apātar pratiṣiddhaḥ tad apām apātena virodhinam vāyu abhra saṃyogam pratipadyate iti 
NV_2.2.2^1	 tāni etāni aitihya ādīni iti evaṃbhūtāni lakṣaṇa bhedāt eteṣu eva antarbhavanti iti na pṛthak ucyante viṣaya abhāvāt ca na hi pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇa vyatirekī viṣayaḥ aitihya ādīnām sambhavati atas ca na pramāṇa antarāṇi atha prayojana bhedāt bhedam pratipadyase evam tarhi aṣṭa tvam nivartate yat abhyupagatam pramāṇa aṣṭa tvam tat nivartate prayojana bhedāt pramāṇa bhedam abhyupagacchate iti eka karaṇa nimittaḥ ca prayojana bhedaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti anekāntaḥ yathā ekam cakṣuḥ aneka nīla ādi bhinna rūpa grahaṇa prayojanam iti indriya aneka tvam vā atha prayojana bhedāt bhedam manyase ekam indriyam anekam prāpnoti atha viṣaya sāmānya avyatirekāt ekam indriyam 
NV_2.2.2^2	 na yuktaḥ tarhi pratiṣedhaḥ na catuṣṭvam aitihya arthāpatti sambhava abhāva prāmāṇyāt iti yadi etāni pramāṇāni na pramāṇa antarāṇi tarhi kva antarbhavanti iti vaktavyam antarbhāva pradarśana artham sūtram śabdaḥ aitihya anartha antara bhāvāt anumāne arthāpatti sambhava abhāva anartha antara bhāvāt ca apratiṣedhaḥ śabde aitihyam antarbhavati samāna lakṣaṇa tvāt na śabda lakṣaṇam aitihyāt nivartate saḥ ayam bhedaḥ sāmānyena saṃgṛhītaḥ anumāne arthāpatti sambhava abhāvānām antara bhāvaḥ samāna lakṣaṇa tvāt anumāne arthāpatti sambhava abhāvāḥ antarbhavanti katham arthāpattiḥ anumānena saṃgṛhyate dvayoḥ ekatara pratiṣedhasya dvitīya abhyanujñā viṣaya tvāt 
NV_2.2.2^3	 yatra yatra dvayoḥ vastunoḥ ekatarat vastu pratiṣidhyate tatra tatra dvitīya abhyanujñā dṛṣṭāḥ yathā divā na bhuṅkte iti abhidhānāt rātrau bhuṅkte iti gamyate eke tu bruvate naḥ iyam arthāpattiḥ divā na bhuṅkte iti atra kila avadhāraṇa dvayam divā na bhuṅkte eva divā eva na bhuṅkte iti ca ubhaya prāptau na vaktavyam rātrau bhuṅkte iti etat tu na samyak asambhavāt divā na bhuṅkte eva iti ayam arthaḥ asambhavena nirākṛtaḥ na hi kaḥ cit divā bhuṅkte eva bhuñjānaḥ api tāvat na bhuṅkte eva kim punar abhuñjānaḥ iti tasmāt asambhavena asya arthasya nirākṛta tvāt kāla pratiṣedhaḥ anena vākyena divā na bhuṅkte iti 
NV_2.2.2^4	 anyathā anarthakam syāt kriyā antara nivṛtteḥ asambhavena nirākṛta tvāt kāla pratiṣedhasya ca anabhyupagamāt anarthakam vākyam bhavatu anarthakam vākyam kim naḥ bādhyate katham na bādhyate yat abhyupetam tat nivartate kim ca abhyupetam kriyā antara pratiṣedhaḥ yam na kāla pratiṣedhaḥ iti na ca idam anarthakam tasmāt ubhayoḥ sāmarthya prāptayoḥ ekatara pratiṣedhe dvitīya abhyanujñānāt anumānam eva artha āpattiḥ katamat anumānam sāmānyatodṛṣṭam etena sambhava abhāvau vyākhyātau sambhavaḥ anumānam abhāvaḥ api evam eva tat ca varṇitam anayoḥ api sāmānyatodṛṣṭe eva antarbhāvaḥ iti tat evam antarbhāvāt pṛthak anapadeśaḥ iti 
NV_2.2.3^1	 satyam etāni pramāṇāni na tu pramāṇa antarāṇi iti uktam tatra artha āpatteḥ pramāṇa bhāva abhyanujñā naḥ upapadyate tathā iha iyam arthāpattiḥ apramāṇam anaikāntika tvāt yā iyam bhavatā arthāpattiḥ pramāṇa tvena pratipādyate sā na pramāṇam apramāṇam iti na arthasya ekadā api pratipādikā yathā megheṣu asatsu vṛṣṭiḥ na bhavati satsu bhavati iti arthāt āpannam satsu api ekadā na bhavati iti anaikāntikī arthāpattiḥ arthāpatti mātrasya pakṣīkaraṇe anaikāntika tvam avyāpakam 
NV_2.2.3^2	 yadi tāvat arthāpatti mātram pakṣayasi tatas arthāpatteḥ anaikāntika tvam aśakyam darśayitum atha anaikāntikī yā sā pakṣīkriyate tadā abhyupagamaḥ vayam api brūmaḥ anaikāntikī apramāṇam iti hetuḥ ca na asti hetoḥ pratijñā viśeṣaṇa tvāt yā anaikāntikī sā apramāṇam iti pratijñā tatra hetuḥ na asti na ca ayam arthaḥ sādhyaḥ iti hetu abhāvaḥ vyāghātaḥ ca abhyupagamāt anaikāntikī yā arthāpattiḥ sā pramāṇam na bhavati iti bruvatā yā aikāntikī sā pramāṇam iti abhyupagatam bhavati anarthakam ca idam abhidhānam yā anaikāntikī arthāpattiḥ sā na pramāṇam iti 
NV_2.2.4	 yām api bhavān anaikāntikīm arthāpattim manyate sā api na anaikāntikī anartha āpattau arthāpatti abhimānāt na iyam arthāpattiḥ anaikāntikī arthāpattiḥ ca satsu megheṣu vṛṣṭiḥ bhavati iti sā iyam anaikāntikī katham na satsu bhavati eva api tu satsu eva bhavati iti yat tu satsu megheṣu vṛṣṭiḥ na bhavati iti kāraṇa pratibandhaḥ asau na tat arthāpatteḥ prameyam kim punar asyāḥ prameyam kāraṇe sati kāryam bhavati iti sā iyam anaikāntikī katham syāt yadi asati api kāraṇe kāryam utpadyate tat tu na dṛṣṭam iti na kadā cit anaikāntika tvam 
NV_2.2.5	 yaḥ ayam bhavatā pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate arthāpattiḥ na pramāṇam anaikāntika tvāt iti ayam api anaikāntikaḥ sattā pratiṣedhāt na anena pratiṣedhena arthāpatteḥ sattā pratiṣidhyate katham na sattā pratiṣidhyate yasmāt arthāpatteḥ viśeṣaḥ pratiṣidhyate na arthāpatti mātram tena sattā pratiṣedhāt anaikāntikaḥ bhavati iti 
NV_2.2.6	 atha manyase na pratiṣedhasya sattvam viṣayaḥ kim tu pramāṇa tvam saḥ ayam pratiṣedhaḥ sva viṣaye pravartamānaḥ na anaikāntikaḥ bhavitum arhati iti anaikāntikaḥ hi nāma sa jñeyaḥ yaḥ sva viṣaya tajjātīya anyavṛttiḥ na ca anaikāntikam prāmāṇya pratiṣedhe asti tasmāt na anaikāntikaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ iti tad prāmāṇye vā na artha apatti aprāmāṇyam yadi sva viṣaya tajjātīya anyavṛttim anaikāntikam manyase arthāpattiḥ api tarhi anaikāntikī na bhavati na hi asati kāraṇe kvacid api kāryam utpadyamānam dṛṣṭam iti tat idam sūtram vyāghāta deśana artham yat uktam bhavatā sva viṣayāt anyatra vartamānam anaikāntikam na bhavati arthāpattiḥ ca anaikāntikī iti vyāhatam ajñānam vā atha abuddhvā ekāntikān aikāntika vyavahāram idam ucyate arthāpattiḥ apramāṇam anaikāntika tvāt iti tadā upekṣayā vartitavyam na unmatta vākyāni pratisamādheyāni iti 
NV_2.2.7–2.2.8	 na abhāvaḥ pramāṇam viṣaya abhāvāt yat aviṣayam tat apramāṇam yathā go śabdaḥ aśva pratipādane tathā ca abhāvaḥ tasmāt apramāṇam kaḥ ca evam āha abhāvaḥ pramāṇam iti api tu abhāva viṣayā pratipattiḥ pramāṇam tayā pratīyate iti kaḥ punar asyāḥ viṣayaḥ abhāvaḥ iti uktam tatra anekadhā bhinnasya abhāva prapañcasya udāharaṇa artham sūtram lakṣiteṣu alakṣaṇa lakṣita tvāt alakṣitānām tat prameya siddhiḥ alakṣitāni vāsāṃsi ānayaḥ iti prayuktaḥ ubhaya sannidhau yeṣu vāsaḥsu lakṣaṇāni na paśyati tāni lakṣaṇa abhāvena eva pratipadyate praiṣa sampratipattyoḥ eka viṣaya tvāt pratipadya ca ānayati pratipatti hetuḥ ca pramāṇam tasmāt sidhyati abhāvasya pramāṇa tvam 
NV_2.2.9	 asati arthe na abhāvaḥ iti ced atha manyase yatra yat bhavati tat tatra na bhavati na ca ālakṣiteṣu vāsaḥsu lakṣaṇāni bhavanti tasmāt na tatra na bhavanti iti na aparijñānāt na bhavatā asmad abhiprāyaḥ abodhi na brūmaḥ yat yatra bhavati tatra tat na bhavati iti api tu lakṣitāni vāsāṃsi upalabhamānaḥ itarāṇi lakṣaṇa abhāva viśiṣṭāni pratipadyate iti ayathārthaḥ ayam upala ambhaḥ iti atas ukta artham sūtram na anya lakṣaṇa upapatteḥ iti 
NV_2.2.10–2.2.11	 yāni tāni lakṣiteṣu vāsaḥsu lakṣaṇāni tāni na kasya cit na santi iti yāni ca santi teṣām abhāvaḥ vyāhataḥ atra uktam na aparijñānāt iti asya ca arthasya jñāpana artham sūtram na lakṣaṇa avasthita apekṣa siddheḥ na brūmaḥ yāni bhavanti teṣām tatra eva abhāvaḥ iti api tu keṣu cit lakṣaṇāni avasthitāni apekṣya yeṣu tāni na bahvanti tāni lakṣaṇa abhāvena pratipadyate iti 
NV_2.2.12	 abhāva dvaitam khalu bhavati iti prāk ca utpatteḥ avidyamāna tā ūrdhvam ca vināśāt avidyamāna tā iti tatra yaḥ ayam vināśāt abhāvaḥ lakṣaṇānām alakṣiteṣu vāsaḥsu saḥ anupapannaḥ naḥ itaraḥ iti asati arthe na abhāvaḥ tad siddheḥ alakṣiteṣu ahetuḥ iti ca ubhe api ete chala sūtre chalasya uktam uttaram jñātvā ajñātvā vā asambaddham ajñānam vā tasmāt aprayojyam chalam iti 
NV_2.2.13^1	 āpta upadeśaḥ śabdaḥ iti pramāṇa bhāve viśeṣaṇam bruvatā nānā prakāraḥ śabdaḥ iti jñāpyate katham na asati bhede viśeṣaṇam arthavat na ca anarthakam viśeṣaṇam yuktam iti yuktam nānā bhūtaḥ śabdaḥ viśeṣaṇa sāmarthyāt iti tasmin sāmānyena vicāraḥ nityaḥ anityaḥ vā vicāraḥ parīkṣā vimarśa hetu anuyoge ca vipratipatteḥ saṃśayaḥ viparti patti śabdasya uktaḥ arthaḥ tatra ākāśa guṇaḥ śabdaḥ mahattva vat abhivyakti dharmā iti eke eke tāvat bruvate nityaḥ śabdaḥ iti avinaśyat ādhāra eka dravya ākāśa guṇa tvāt yat avinaśyat ādhāram eka dravyam ākāśa guṇaḥ ca tat nityam dṛṣṭam yathā ākāśa mahat tvam 
NV_2.2.13^2	 tathā ca śabdaḥ tasmāt nityaḥ iti saḥ ayam nityaḥ san abhivyakti dharmā tasya abhivyañjakāḥ saṃyoga vibhāga nādāḥ iti gandha ādi saha vṛttiḥ dravyeṣu sanniviṣṭaḥ gandha ādi vat avasthitaḥ abhivyakti dharmā iti apare apare punar bruvate gandha ādibhiḥ saha sanniviṣṭaḥ śabdaḥ gandha ādi vat eva abhivyajyate tasya abhivyañjakāḥ bhūta viśeṣa abhighātāḥ iti ākāśa guṇaḥ śabdaḥ utpatti nirodha dharmakaḥ iti ca anye anye punar varṇayanti anityaḥ śabdaḥ ākāśa guṇaḥ utpatti nirodha dharmakaḥ iti mahābhūta saṃkṣobha jaḥ śabdaḥ na āśritaḥ utpatti nirodha dharmakaḥ iti ca apare atas saṃśayaḥ kim atra tattvam iti anityaḥ iti etat tattvam 
NV_2.2.13^3	 kim idam anitya tvam nāma yatas anityaḥ iti bhavati kim punar tat prāc pradhvaṃsa abhāvau iti eke eke tāvat varṇayanti yasya prāc pradhvaṃsa abhāvau staḥ tat anityam iti na sambandhāt na hi prāc pradhvaṃsa abhāvābhyām bhāvaḥ sambadhyate iti anutpanna vinaṣṭayoḥ ca prasaṅgāt yadi ca prāc pradhvaṃsa abhāvau anitya tā iti manyase anutpanne vastuni prāc abhāvaḥ asti ūrdhvam ca vastunaḥ pradhvaṃsa abhāvaḥ asti iti ghaṭa ādau asati prāc pradhvaṃsa abhāva nimittataḥ anitya pratyayaḥ syāt anityasya bhāvaḥ anitya tā iti prāk pradhvaṃsayoḥ abhāva tvāt bhāva śabdena anabhidhānam anityam nāma yasya na asti atyantam bhāvaḥ 
NV_2.2.13^4	 tasya anityasya yaḥ bhāvaḥ sā anitya tā prāc pradhvaṃsa abhāvau ca bhāva pratiṣedhau na ca abhāvaḥ bhāva abhidhānena vaktum yuktau tasmāt na prāc pradhvaṃsa abhāvau anitya tā iti ṣaṣṭhī arthah ca na asti iti tasya bhāvaḥ tu atalau iti tasya iti dharmī apadiśyate bhāvaḥ iti dharmiṇaḥ dharmaḥ na ca abhāvaḥ dharmaḥ na ca dharma kāle tad śabda vācyaḥ dharmī vidyate na ca avidhyamānasya ṣaṣṭhyā yogaḥ iti atha yat bhavati tat prāk na bhavati ūrdhvam ca na prabhavati iti manyase evam api na kim cit pratiṣiddham vayam api brūmaḥ yat prāk na bhavati tat ūrdhvam na bhavati iti ṣaṣṭhī arthaḥ tu pūrvavat na asti 
NV_2.2.13^5	 ghaṭasya prāc abhāvaḥ ghaṭasya pradhvaṃsa abhāvaḥ iti etat katham na atra ṣaṣṭhyā sambandhaḥ abhidhīyate api tu prāk idam vastu na asti paścāt jātam iti arthaḥ ūrdhvam ca vināśāt idam vastu na bhaviṣyati iti anityam iti ucyate tasya ca bhāvaḥ anitya tā iti vartamāne ca asambhavāt yadi ca prāc pradhvaṃsa abhāvau anitya tā iti manyase vartamāne vastuni na prāc abhāvaḥ na pradhvaṃsa abhāvaḥ iti anitya abhilāpaḥ na syāt pācaka ādi śabda vat iti ced atha manyase yathā amī pācaka ādi śabdāḥ tri kāla viṣayāḥ tathā ayam anitya śabdaḥ tri kāla viṣayaḥ bhaviṣyati iti na ṇvulaḥ tri kāla viṣaya tvāt ṇvulaḥ prayogaḥ tri kāla viṣayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ 
NV_2.2.13^6	 pācakaḥ bhavati pācakaḥ bhaviṣyati pācakaḥ abhūt iti tyapaḥ api tri kāla viṣaya tvam iti ced atha manyase tyapaḥ api tri kāla viṣaya tvam iti tat ca na adarśanāt na hi asati anitye anityaḥ iti prayogam paśyāmaḥ tasmāt tyapaḥ tri kāla viṣaya tvam ayuktam iti atas na prāc pradhvaṃsa abhāvau anitya tā iti vināśa hetu bhāvaḥ iti anye apare punar bruvate vināśa hetoḥ astitvam anitya tā iti etat tu na yuktam asati bhāvāt prāk vināśa hetu bhāvāt anityaḥ iti pratyayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ anupajāta kapāla vibhāgeṣu ghaṭa ādiṣu yadi punar vināśa hetu bhāvaḥ anitya tā syāt vartamāneṣu ghaṭa ādiṣu na syāt 
NV_2.2.13^7	 na hi asati jvare jvaritaḥ iti pratyayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ vināśa hetu bhāvāt ca vināśasya hetuḥ asti iti pratyayaḥ yuktaḥ na anityaḥ iti na hi go tvāt aśva pratyayaḥ bhavati iti atha manyase yasya vināśa hetuḥ asti tad vināśa vat yat ca vināśa vat tat anityam iti etat api na budhyāmahe yasya vināśa hetuḥ asti tad vināśa vat iti kim tu yasya vināśa hetuḥ asti tad vināśa hetumat iti vaktum yuktam na ca anyena yogāt anya nimittaḥ pratyayaḥ yuktaḥ na hi daṇḍa yogāt kuṇḍalī iti bhavati vināśa vat śarīram iti prayoga darśanāt yuktam iti ced atha manyase vināśa vat śarīram iti dṛṣṭaḥ prayogaḥ 
NV_2.2.13^8	 na ca asati sambandhe prayogaḥ bhavitum arhati na matupaḥ asatsu a darśanāt na ayam matubh kva cit api asatsu dṛṣṭaḥ na hi asatā kuṇḍalena kuṇḍalī iti bhavati na ca bhāvasya vināśena yogaḥ asti tasmāt vināśa vat śarīram iti ayuktaḥ prayogaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti ced atha manyase dṛṣṭaḥ ayam prayogaḥ vināśi etat śarīrakam adhruvāḥ ete viṣayāḥ iti na upacārāt vināśi iti upacāreṇa prayogaḥ vināśaḥ asya avaśyantayā iti adhruvā iti anitya tā eva ucyate tasmāt na vināśa hetu bhāvaḥ anitya tā upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya atyanta tiraḥ bhāvaḥ anitya tā iti anye anye punar anitya tā śabdasya artham anyathā varṇayanti 
NV_2.2.13^9	 yat upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam vastu tena eva ātmanā atyantam tirobhūtam naḥ upalabhyate tat anityam iti ucyate etat tu śūnyam abhidhānam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam atyanta tiraḥ bhūtam naḥ upalabhyate iti bruvāṇaḥ siddhāntam bādhate na hi kim cit vastu atyantam naḥ upalabhyate iti siddhāntaḥ anupajāta viśeṣasya ca vastunaḥ tirobhāvaḥ na yuktaḥ iti anekadhā varṇitam tasmāt iyam anitya tā na yuktāḥ ye punar varṇayanti saḥ eva ca bhāvaḥ abhūtvā bhavan bhūtvā ca abhavan anityaḥ iti ucyate sā ca avasthāḥ bhāva pratyayena anitya tā iti abhidhīyate etat tu na yuktam sva arthe bhāva pratyayasya adarśanāt 
NV_2.2.13^10	 na hi kaḥ cit sva arthe bhāva pratyayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ vinaya ādi pāṭhāt iti ced nanu ca vinaya ādibhyaḥ ṭhak iti sva arthe pratyayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ vinayaḥ eva vainayikam iti na anabhyupagamāt na ayam sva arthe pratyayaḥ kim tarhi vinayena yogaḥ vainayikam iti ucyate evam sarvatra draṣṭavyam anupalabhyamāna bhedānām api anumānataḥ bhedaḥ anumeyaḥ yān ca api bhavān anupalabhyamāna bhedān pratyayān sva arthe manyate teṣu api anumānataḥ bhedah anumeyaḥ kim anumānam ṣaṣṭhyā bheda viṣaya tvam sarvā ṣaṣṭhī bhede dṛṣṭāḥ iti yathā ca anartha antare ṣaṣṭhī na asti tathā uktam guṇa guṇivāde iti tat kim idānīm anitya tā iti ayam śabdaḥ anabhidheyaḥ eva 
NV_2.2.13^11	 na anabhidheyaḥ avadhya pekṣā anapekṣā bhedāt sattā eva ubhayathā yāḥ ubhayānta paricchinna vastu sattā sā anitya tā iti yā aparicchinna vastu sattā sā nityatā iti yathā samavāyaḥ ekaḥ san sa ca kāryeṇa viśiṣyamāṇaḥ kāraṇa tvam iti abhidhīyate kāraṇena viśiṣyamāṇaḥ kāryatvam iti abhidhīyate katham iti kāraṇam iti ayam pratyayaḥ na animittakaḥ kadā cit bhāvāt na vastu nimittaḥ avastu pratyayaḥ vyatireki tvāt na sattātaḥ vailakṣaṇyāt sattātaḥ sat iti syāt ayam tu sattā pratyayāt vilakṣaṇaḥ tasmāt na sattātaḥ iha viśeṣaṇa nimitta tvāt ca sambandha nimittaḥ iha tantuṣu paṭaḥ iti ādhāra viśiṣṭaḥ pratyayaḥ upajāyate 
NV_2.2.13^12	 na ca asati sambandhe ihapratyayena śakyam bhavitum yatas ayam ihapratyayaḥ sa samavāyaḥ kārya samavāye sati kāraṇam iti abhidhīyate yasya guṇasya yogāt yasmin arthe śabda niveśaḥ tad abhidhāne tu atalau kārya samavāyasya ca bhāvāt etat bhavati iti kārya samavāyaḥ kāraṇa tvam etena kāryatvam vyākhyātam kārya ātma lābha hetuḥ samavāyaḥ kāraṇa viśiṣṭaḥ kāryatvam yathā samavāyaḥ evam sattā api ekā satī ubhaya anta paricchinna vastu sambandhi tve sati anitya tā iti ucyate viparyayāt nityatā iti etayā anitya tayā yogāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti ādimattvāt aindriyaka tvāt kṛtaka vat upacārāt ca 
NV_2.2.13^13	 ādimattvāt ādiḥ yoniḥ kāraṇam iti kāraṇavat tvāt anityaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ kim punar idam kāraṇavat tvam nāma nimitta kāraṇa bheda anuvidhānam utpatti dharmaka tvam iti tad abhivyaṅgyeṣu na asti na hi kim cit abhivyajyamānam nimitta kāraṇa bheda anuvidhāyi dṛṣṭam iti saṃyoga vibhāga anantaram upalabdheḥ sandehaḥ iti ced atha manyase saṃyoga vibhāga anantaram upalabhyate śabdaḥ sā ca tad anantara upalabdhiḥ vyajyamānasya api yuktāḥ atas sandehaḥ kim ayam saṃyoga vibhāgābhyām vyajyate atha kriyate iti na vyajyate aindriyaka tvāt kim idam aindriyaka tvam indriya pratyāsatti grāhyaḥ aindriyakaḥ iti tatas kim 
NV_2.2.13^14	 yadi indriya pratyāsatti grāhyaḥ aindriyakaḥ tatas na vyajyate na hi vyajyamānasya indriyeṇa prāptiḥ yuktāḥ katham iti śrotram tāvat śabda deśam na gacchati amūrta tvāt yat amūrtam tat niṣkriyam dṛṣṭam yathā rūpa ādi amūrtam ca ākāśam tasmāt niṣkriyam iti kriyā kāraṇa guṇa samavāyāt kriyāvat tvam iti ced atha manyase yasmin kriyā kāraṇam guṇaḥ vartate tat kriyāvat dṛṣṭam yathā loṣṭa ādi tathā ca ākāśam tasmāt tat api kriyāvat iti na anekāntāt kriyā kāraṇam ca guṇaḥ ātmani na ca kriyāvān ātmā iti anekāntaḥ vidyamānasya api na kriyā hetu tvam mahā parimāṇa pratibandhāt vidyamānaḥ api ākāśe abhighātaḥ na kriyā hetuḥ mahat parimāṇa pratibandhāt 
NV_2.2.13^15	 yat ākāśe vartate mahat tvam tena eka artha samavetena tad vṛttiḥ abhighātaḥ pratibadhyate iti yathā loṣṭa guru tvam tad eka artha vṛttinā saṃyogena iti saṃyoga pratibandhāt guru tvasya sa apekṣa tva prasaṅgaḥ iti ced atha manyase yadi saṃyogena pratibadhyamānam guru tvam kriyām naḥ ārabhate tat pratibandha apagama apekṣam ārabhate iti nanu evam guru tvam sa apekṣam kriyā kāraṇam iti prāptam evam ca śāstra vyāghātaḥ nirapekṣam guru tvam karma kāraṇam iti hi śāstram na nirapekṣasya anyathā vyākhyānāt na ayam nirapekṣa arthaḥ guru tvam na kim cit apekṣate iti 
NV_2.2.13^16	 api tu carama bhāvi nimitta antaram na apekṣate iti nirapekṣam guru tvam karma kāraṇam iti na asti vyāghātaḥ tathā ca śāstram saṃyoga abhāve guru tvāt patanam iti viṣaya abhāvāt ca na kriyā kāraṇa guṇa samavāya mātram kriyāvat tve hetuḥ api tu kriyā kāraṇa guṇa samavāye sati yadi kriyā viṣayaḥ mūrtiḥ bhavati kriyā kāraṇam ca guṇaḥ apratibaddhaḥ bhavati tadā kriyā utpadyate iti tasmāt niṣkriya tvāt ākāśam tāvat na gacchati śabdaḥ api na āgacchati niṣkriya tvāt eva na ca aprāptasya grahaṇam asti sarva śabda upalabdhi prasaṅgāt pariśeṣāt tu santāna siddhiḥ tatra ādyaḥ śabdaḥ saṃyoga vibhāga hetukaḥ tasmāt śabda antarāṇi kadamba golaka nyāyena sarva dikkāni 
NV_2.2.13^17	 tebhyaḥ api pratyekam ekaikaḥ śabdaḥ mandataratamādi nyāyena āśraya apratibandham anuvidhīyamānaḥ prādur asti tatas antyasya atimāndyāt śabda antara utpatti śakti vyāghātaḥ yena kena cit pratibandhāt bhavati iti atas śabda santāna ucchedaḥ tatra yaḥ karṇa śaṣkulīm antam ākāśa deśam prāpnoti saḥ upalabhyate naḥ itaraḥ iti tasmāt aindriyaka tvam tat ca anyathā na yuktam iti atas anityaḥ iti ekaḥ eva iti ced atha manyase ne eva śabda antarāṇi mayā abhyupagamyante api tu ekaḥ eva ayam śabdaḥ vitati a ākāśam avatiṣṭhate saṃyoga vibhāgābhyām vyaktaḥ san upalabhyate yathā ghaṭa ādi apavaraka ādiṣu avasthitam pradīpa saṃyogena iti 
NV_2.2.13^18	 tat ca na sarvaiḥ upalabdhi prasaṅgāt yadi ekaḥ śabdaḥ vitatya avasthitaḥ saṃyogena vyaktaḥ śrotravataḥ artha pratyayam karoti iti manyase tadā yena kena cit yatra tatra avasthitena śabdaḥ vyaktaḥ iti sarvaiḥ śrotravadbhiḥ upalabhyeta na ca upalabhyate tasmāt akalpanā iyam eka deśa abhivyaktiḥ iti ced atha manyase satyam vitatya avasthitaḥ śabdaḥ tasya tu avasthitasya eka deśaḥ nimittena vyajyate iti na kimaḥ tādātmya anupapatteḥ yān tān eka deśān śabdasya manyase te kim śabda ātmakāḥ āho naḥ iti kim ca atas yadi śabda ātmakāḥ tatas aneke śabdāḥ iti vyāghātaḥ 
NV_2.2.13^19	 atha aśabda ātmakāḥ na śabdāt artha pratyayaḥ iti prāptam teṣām ca svabhāvaḥ vaktavyaḥ eka deśa artha anabhidhānāt ca eka deśaḥ iti samāsapadam etat ekaḥ ca asau deśaḥ ca iti tatra deśaḥ ādhāra arthaḥ kāraṇa arthaḥ vā syāt tatra ādhāra arthaḥ tāvat na yuktaḥ śabdasya ākāśa vṛtti tvāt ākāśa vṛttiḥ śabdaḥ tad guṇa tvāt tasmāt ākāśa vyatiriktaḥ naḥ ādhāraḥ iti kāraṇa arthaḥ api na asti akṛtaka tva abhyupagamāt akṛtakaḥ śabdaḥ iti svayam pratipadyamānāḥ bhavantaḥ na arhanti vaktum kāraṇam eka deśaḥ iti na ca anyaḥ eka deśa arthaḥ sambhavati iti śūnyam abhidhānam eka deśaḥ śabdasya vyajyate iti 
NV_2.2.13^20	 eka deśa abhivyaktau ca artha pratyayaḥ na syāt varṇa vat varṇāḥ sarve eva vyāpakāḥ bhavanti iti etasmin pakṣe varṇa eka deśa vyaktiḥ na ca varṇa eka deśaḥ śakyaḥ nirūpayitum na ca nirūpitāt api tasmāt artha pratipattiḥ sambhavati varṇānām api artha pratyāyaka tva anabhyupagamāt varṇāḥ eva tāvat ekaikaśas artha pratyāyakāḥ na bhavanti kutas tat eka deśāḥ iti etena bahu tvam pratyuktam yathā ekasya śabdasya vyaktau doṣaḥ evam aneka śabdasya api vyāpi tve doṣaḥ iti kolāhalam ca syāt yadi ca aneka śabdāḥ ākāśe vartante yugapad vartante iti pratipadyase eka śabda abhivyañjaka upādāne samāna deśānām śabdānām vyaktiḥ iti kolāhalam syāt 
NV_2.2.13^21	 yathā malla naṭaraṅga samājeṣu prayoga karaṇa atiśaya āvarjiteṣu nadatsu na tu bhavati tasmāt na anekaḥ vyāpakaḥ iti niyamaḥ ca na syāt yadi ca aneke śabdāḥ yugapad ākāśe vartante iti evam ca yat kim cit vyañjakam upāttam samāna deśān sarva śabdān abhivyanakti iti yadā vīṇā vādyate tadā rāsabha dhvaniḥ api śrūyate na hi samāna aindriya grāhyāṇām samāna deśānām vyañjakeṣu niyamaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yat yasya vyañjakam tena tasya vyaktiḥ iti ced tat na adṛṣṭa tvāt atha manyase aneka śabda sannipāte api vyañjakāni bhidyante vyañjaka bheda anuvidhāyinyaḥ vyaktayaḥ pratiśabdam upajāyante iti tat na adṛṣṭa tvāt 
NV_2.2.13^22	 na hi samāna deśānām eka indriya grāhyāṇām vyañjakeṣu niyamaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti na hi pradīpaḥ eka indriya grāhyam anekam artham yugapad sannipatitam na prakāśayati iti sāmānya vat etat syāt iti ced na anabhyupagamāt atha manyase aneka artha sannipāte sati sarvābhiḥ vyaktibhiḥ sāmānyāni sambadhyante aneka artha sambandhe sati api sāmānyasya kena cit arthena kim cit sāmānyam vyajyate evam aneka śabda sannipāte sati kim cit vyañjakam kim cit śabdam vyanakti iti na anabhyupagamāt sāmānyam anekena bhinna jātīyena arthena sambadhyate iti na abhyupagamyate api tu sva viṣaya sarva gatam sāmānyam go tvam goṣu eva na aśva ādiṣu aśva tvam aśveṣu eva na gavā ādiṣu 
NV_2.2.13^23	 tasmāt asamaḥ ayam dṛṣṭāntaḥ vyañjaka abhāve ca upalabdheḥ na vyajyate śabdaḥ yadi ca saṃyoga vibhāgābhyām vyaktaḥ śabdaḥ upalabhyate iti manyase saḥ api saṃyoga abhāve na upalabhyeta upalabhyate ca dāruvraścane dāruparaśu saṃyoga nivṛttau iti abhighātāt vāyuḥ iti ced atha manyase dāru paraśvoḥ abhighātāt vāyuḥ jāyate sa vāyuḥ santāna vṛttyā vartate santāna vṛttyā ca vartamānaḥ karṇa śaṣkulīm antam ākāśa deśam prāpnoti tad prāptau tatrasthaḥ śabdaḥ vyajyate iti atra uktam yathā ekaḥ śabdaḥ karṇa śaṣkulīm ati ākāśa deśe vartate tathā sarve eva śabdāḥ vartante iti 
NV_2.2.13^24	 yat kim cit vyañjakam upāttam yasya kasya cit śabdasya vyañjakam syāt iti sarva śabda upalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ niyamaḥ ca na syāt iti nimitta sannidhāne ca sarvatra upalabdheḥ na vyajyate yat khalu vyajyate tat nimitta sannidhāne sati api na sarvatra vyajyamānam dṛṣṭam yathā ghaṭa arthinaḥ vibhrāṇāḥ pradīpam ghaṭa ādi rahita anapavaraka ādīn praviśya na ghaṭa ādīn upalabhante iti abhivyaktim ghaṭa ādīnām pratipadyante na punar tālu ādi abhighāta bhūta sannidhāne sati kva cit api śabdāt na paśyāmaḥ tasmāt na vyajyate iti sarvatra santi iti ced na ukta uttara tvāt atha manyase yasya eka deśa vṛttayaḥ śabdāḥ tam pratyayam upālambhaḥ asmākam tu sarve eva vyāpakāḥ 
NV_2.2.13^25	 tasmāt naḥ eṣaḥ doṣaḥ iti na ukta uttara tvāt ukta uttaram etat vākyam na punar pratisamādhānam prayojayati iti tasmāt na vyajyate iti nāda upalabdhau ca viprakṛṣṭa deśa avasthitena nāda samāna deśasya śabda anupalabdheḥ na vyañjakaḥ nādaḥ etena vāyavīyāḥ saṃyoga vibhāgāḥ śabda vyañjakāḥ iti pratyuktam kṛtaka vat upacārāt ca tīvram mandam iti kṛtakam upacaryate tīvram sukham duḥkham mandam sukham duḥkham iti upacaryate tīvraḥ śabdaḥ mandaḥ śabdaḥ iti atra prayogaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ tīvra manda viṣaya tvāt sukha duḥkha vat iti kṛtaka vat upacārāt iti anena sūtreṇa sarva anitya tva dharma sādhana saṃgrahaḥ 
NV_2.2.13^26	 kṛtaka vat grahaṇasya udāharaṇa artha tvāt yathā sāmānya viśeṣavataḥ asmad ādi bāhya karaṇa pratyakṣa tvāt upalabhyasya anupalabdhi kāraṇa abhāve sati anupalabdhiḥ guṇasya sataḥ asmad ādi bāhya karaṇa pratyakṣa tvam iti evam ādi tīvra śabdasya tīvra artha viṣaya tvāt na śabda ādi viṣaya tvam iti ced atha manyase tīvra śabdena tīvra arthaḥ abhidhīyate na śabdaḥ na ca anya viṣayaḥ śabdaḥ anyasya arthasya pratipādakaḥ iti na śabda śabda samāna adhikaraṇasya tīvra śabdasya abhidhānāt satyam ayam tīvra śabdaḥ kevalaḥ uccaran dravya guṇa karmaṇām samānam dharmam pratipādayati śabda śabdaḥ api uccaran aneka dharma yoginam śabdam abhidhatte 
NV_2.2.13^27	 yadā punar etau tīvra śabda śabdau viśeṣaṇā viśeṣya bhāva āpannau abhidhīyete tadā tīvra śabdena dharma antarāṇi vyavacchidyante śabda śabdena ca dharmi antarāṇi iti ubhaya śabda prayogāt śabdaḥ gamyate tasmāt upapannam tīvra manda śabda viṣaya tvāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti vyañjakasya tathā abhāvāt grahaṇasya tīvra manda tā rūpavat iti ced na abhibhava upapatteḥ śeṣam bhāṣye grahaṇam nimitta bheda anuvidhāyi iti ced na grahaṇa bhedasya ekatra adṛṣṭa tvāt atha manyase na śabdaḥ bhidyate śabde tu abhinne grahaṇam nimitta bheda anuvidhāyi bhavati grahaṇbhedāt ca abhibhavaḥ iti na grahaṇa bhedasya ekatra adṛṣṭa tvāt 
NV_2.2.13^28	 yadi abhinnaḥ śabdaḥ grahaṇa bhedaḥ na prāpnoti na hi abhinne viṣaye bheda grahaṇam paśyāmaḥ atha abhinne viṣaye grahaṇāni bhidyante iti manyase nityam grahaṇa bhedaḥ syāt tatas ca bhinnaḥ abhinnaḥ iti bhinna abhinna pratyayau na syātām abhibhava anupapattiḥ ca grahaṇayoḥ yūgapad asambhavāt na hi grahaṇe yugapad bhavataḥ na ca ekam grahaṇam ātmanaḥ eva abhibhāvakam na ca ayam abhibhavaḥ na asti tasmāt bhidyate śabdaḥ abhibhava anupapattiḥ ca vyañjaka samāna deśasya abhivyaktau prāpti abhāvāt vyañjakena samāna deśaḥ ayam vyajyate iti etasmin pakṣe naḥ upapadyate abhibhavaḥ kasmāt vyañjaka samāna deśa tvāt 
NV_2.2.13^29	 na hi vyañjaka samāna deśena śabdena aprāptaḥ śabdaḥ abhibhavitum śakyaḥ aprāpta tvāt na hi aprāptam abhibhāvakam bhavati atha aprāptam abhibhavati iti manyase vīṇā ādi śabdānām agrahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ aprāptāḥ śaṅkha rāsabha ādi śabdāḥ abhibhāvakāḥ iti na kadā cit vīṇā ādi śabdāḥ śrūyeran sarvatra santi iti ced na pūrva doṣa anuvṛtteḥ atha manyase yaḥ vyañjaka samāna deśam śabdam abhyupaiti tasya eṣaḥ doṣaḥ asmākam tu sarve eva śabdāḥ samāna deśāḥ tasmāt adoṣaḥ ayam iti na pūrva doṣān ativṛtteḥ samāna deśa tve śabdānām vyañjakeṣu niyamaḥ na asti iti yat kim cit vyañjakam upāttam sarva śabda vyakti hetuḥ iti pūrva doṣa anivṛttiḥ 
NV_2.2.13^30	 samāna deśa tve ca vīṇā veṇu śaṅkha śabdānām nityam saṅkha śabdena vīṇā veṇu śabdayoḥ abhibhavaḥ iti vīṇā ādi śabda aśravaṇa prasaṅgaḥ tad avasthaḥ tasmāt śabdāḥ eva bhidyante iti teṣām tu bhinnānām santāna vṛtti tve sati ye karṇa śaṣkulīm ati ākāśa deśe yugapad samavayanti tatra yaḥ paṭuḥ śabdaḥ saḥ itarasya abhibhāvakaḥ iti abhibhavaḥ ca nāma mandasya paṭīyasoḥ grahaṇāt agrahaṇam iti yadi santāna vṛttiḥ śabdaḥ karṇa śaṣkulīmat ākāśa deśam prāptaḥ ca gṛhyate diś deśa pratyayaḥ na prāpnoti iti pūrveṇa śabdaḥ uttareṇa śabdaḥ iti na hi viṣayeṣu pratyāsīdatsu diś deśa pratyayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ gandha ādi vat iti 
NV_2.2.13^31	 na upādāna nimitta tvāt diś deśa vyapadeśasya yaḥ ayam śabdeṣu diś deśa vyapadeśaḥ na ayam śabda nimittaḥ pūrva apara ādi bhinnebhyaḥ nimittebhyaḥ upajāyamānānām eka deśa grahaṇāt tulyaḥ diś deśa vyapadeśaḥ syāt tasmāt na śabda nimittaḥ kutas tarhi ayam bhavati iti vācyam nimitta bhedāt yāni tāni śabda nimittāni śabda kāraṇasya saṃyogasya anugrahakāṇi tāni diś deśavanti teṣām nimittānām bhedāt diś deśa pratyayāḥ iti nimitta deśa grahaṇāt ye upalabhyamāna nimittāḥ śabdāḥ teṣu etat yuktam vaktum yeṣām tu śabdānām nimittāni naḥ upalabhyante teṣu diś deśa pratyayaḥ na yuktaḥ na na yuktaḥ śabda santānasya nimitta bheda abhimukhyena ādau prāpteḥ 
NV_2.2.13^32	 yaḥ śabda santānaḥ yasmāt nimittāt upajāyate sa samantāt śabda antarāṇi santanoti tatra yaḥ śabda viśesaḥ ādau karṇa śaṣkulīm atas ākāśa deśasya tad abhimukhena bhāgena sambadhyate tad nimittaḥ pūrva apara ādi śabda vyapadeśaḥ iti yadā punar ādya śabda paricchedaḥ na asti tadā viparyayaḥ iti eke tu bruvate naḥ eva śabdeṣu diś deśa pratyayāḥ santi kutas cakṣuḥ viṣaya siddhau diś deśa vyavasāyāt iti tathā hi jāti andhānām pūrva apara ādi pratyayāḥ śabdeṣu na santi iti apare tu diś deśa vyapadeśena cakṣuḥ śrotre aprāpya kāriṇī iti bruvate teṣām uktam uttaram pratyakṣa sūtram varṇayadbhiḥ iti 
NV_2.2.14–2.2.16	 sūtrasya pūrva hetūnām anaikāntika tva jñāpanam arthaḥ śeṣam bhāṣye nitya tvam iti atra kim tāvat tattvam ubhaya anta aparicchinna sattā saṃbandhaḥ iti viparyayāt anitya tvam etat ca abhāve na asti bhāktam tu tat bhavati nityaḥ iva nityaḥ ghaṭa abhāvaḥ na punar nityaḥ eva kāla dvaya anavasthānāt pradhvaṃsa abhāvaḥ na prāk asti na ghaṭa kāle asti prāc abhāvaḥ na pradhvaṃsa kāle na ghaṭa kāle iti katham tarhi nityaḥ iti nityaḥ iva nityaḥ iti ucyate bhaktyā kā punar iyam bhaktiḥ prāgabhāvasya kāraṇa abhāvaḥ pradhvaṃsa abhāvasya avināśaḥ ubhayam ca etat nitya viṣayam iti etat sāmānyāt nityaḥ iva nityaḥ na punar nityaḥ eva iti indriya pratyāsatti grāhyaḥ aindriyakaḥ iti santāna anumāna viśeṣaṇāt avyabhicāraḥ na vayam aindriyaka tvāt iti anena śabda anitya tām sādhayāmaḥ api tu aindriyaka tvāt iti anena śabdasya vyaktim pratiṣedhāmaḥ na hi vyajyamānasya aindriyaka tvam yuktam iti purastāt uktam 
NV_2.2.17^1	 nityeṣu api avyabhicāraḥ na hi nityānām dravyāṇām pradeśa śabdena kāraṇam ucyate ākāśasya pradeśaḥ ātmanaḥ pradeśaḥ iti na atra ākāśa ātmanoḥ kāraṇa dravyam abhidhīyate yathā kṛtakasya kim iti na abhidhīyate avidyamāna tvāt na hi vidyante ākāśa ādeḥ pradeśāḥ iti katham na vidyante pramāṇataḥ anupalabdheḥ yadi ākāśa ādeḥ pradeśāḥ syuḥ pramāṇataḥ upalabhyeran iti katham pramāṇataḥ anupalabdhiḥ vikalpa anupapatteḥ pradeśa śabdena kāraṇam vai abhidhīyate ādhāraḥ vā na kāraṇam akṛtaka tvāt yasmāt akṛtakam ākāśam atas na kāraṇa arthaḥ pradeśa śabdena ucyate na ādhāraḥ anāśrita tvāt anāśritam ākāśam tasya ādhāra arthaḥ api na śakyaḥ vaktum iti loka virodhaḥ iti ced 
NV_2.2.17^2	 na anyathā tad upapatteḥ yadi ākāśam niṣpradeśam pratipadyase nanu lokaḥ viruddhyate pūrva bhāgena nabhasaḥ ādityaḥ iti madhya bhāge nabhasaḥ ādityaḥ iti na anyathā tad upapatteḥ saṃyogasya avyāpya vṛtti tve pradeśa śabdena abhidhīyamāne na loka virodhaḥ yasmāt yat tat saṃyogasya avyāpya vṛtti tvam tat pradeśa śabdena abhidhīyate etat ca pradeśavatā dravyeṇa ākāśa sāmānyam ye khalu paricchinne dravye āmalaka ādike bhavataḥ tayoḥ yaḥ saṃyogaḥ vartate sa te na vyāpnoti pradeśavatī ca te ākāśa saṃyogaḥ api na ākāśam vyāpnoti iti pradeśa vat dravya sāmānyāt pradeśa vat ākāśam iti bhāktaḥ pratyayaḥ kā punar iyam bhaktiḥ atathābhūtasya tathā bhāvibhiḥ sāmānyam ubhayena bhajyate iti bhaktiḥ 
NV_2.2.17^3	 etat sāmānyāt adhyāropita pradeśa vṛttiḥ pradeśa śabdaḥ yasmāt ākāśasya pradeśavadbhiḥ dravyaiḥ sāmānyam saṃyogasya avyāpya vṛtti tvam asti atas pradeśa śabdaḥ ākāśe prayujyate evam etat na tattvataḥ iti ced na pramāṇam asti iti ced na pramāṇataḥ anupalabdheḥ atha manyase ākāśa pradeśāḥ pradeśa vat dravya sāmānyāt ākāśe upacaryante na punar tattvataḥ santi iti na pramāṇam asti na pradeśasya pramāṇataḥ anupalabdheḥ na hi ākāśa ādi pradeśa pratipādakam pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇam sambhavati iti sva rūpeṇa anabhidhānāt ca yadi ca ākāśasya pradeśāḥ syuḥ te sva rūpeṇa vyapadiśyeran yathā paṭasya pradeśāḥ ke tantavaḥ iti na punar ākāśasya pradeśāḥ ke iti ukte sva rūpeṇa vyapadeṣṭum śakyāḥ iti 
NV_2.2.17^4	 kimaḥ anupapatteḥ ca pūrvavat yān ca ākāśa pradeśān bhavān manyate te kim ākāśa ātmakāḥ uta naḥ iti kim ca atas yadi ākāśa ātmakāḥ anekam ākāśam iti prāptam atha na teṣām svabhāvaḥ vaktavyaḥ katham ca te tasya pradeśāḥ iti vaktavyam anākāśa ātmakāḥ santaḥ ākāśasya pradeśāḥ iti kena arthena abhidhīyate tat yathā tantavaḥ paṭa pradeśāḥ iti ukte kāraṇa arthaḥ ādhāra arthaḥ ca gamyate na punar ākāśasya pradeśeṣu etat asti pradeśa abhāvāt anādhāraḥ saṃyogaḥ iti ced nānā dhāraḥ ākāśa vṛtti tvāt atha manuṣe yadi ākāśasya pradeśāḥ na santi ākāśa deśa āśrayaḥ saṃyogaḥ anādhāraḥ prāpnoti nānā dhāraḥ ākāśa vṛtti tvāt asya yasmāt tvayā eva ucyate ākāśa āśrayaḥ iti tasmāt nānā dhāraḥ iti 
NV_2.2.17^5	 samāna deśāḥ iti ced na ābādhanāt atha manyase mūrtimat dravya saṃyogāḥ ye ākāśe nanu te pradeśa abhāvāt sarve eva samāna deśāḥ prāpnuvanti evam ca samāna deśa tve sati na kim cit bādhyate tat evam pradeśa vat dravya sāmānyāt ākāśasya pradeśāḥ iti bhāktaḥ pratyayaḥ niṣpradeśa tvāt sarva śabda upalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ iti ced na ukta uttara tvāt atha manyase yadi niṣpradeśam ākāśam tena ca tarhi sarve eva śabdāḥ samāna deśāḥ iti sarvaiḥ sarvaḥ śabdaḥ upalabhyeta na tu upalabhyate tasmāt anyonya vṛttayaḥ śabdāḥ sarvaiḥ agrahaṇāt aṅguli rūpa ādi vat iti guṇa tvāt vyāpakam iti eke eke tu guṇa tvāt hetoḥ śabda saṃyoga ādi aṅguli rūpavat vyāpakam pratipadyante 
NV_2.2.17^6	 te idam praṣṭavyāḥ vyāpaka tvam iti kaḥ arthaḥ yadi āśraya vṛtti tvam vyāptiḥ na kim cit bādhyate atha anyat tat na vidmaḥ vayam tu vyāptim aṅguli rūpasya āśraya upalabdhau upalabhya tvam brūmaḥ na punar śabda ādayaḥ āśraya upalabdhau upalabhyante iti tasmāt aṅguli rūpavat na vyāpakāḥ iti samudita sthānānām eka samudāyī upalabdhau upalabdhi anupalabdhī vyāpti avyāptī eka āśrayāṇām āśraya upalabdhau iti atha ye ākāśe mūrtimatām saṃyogāḥ teṣām kān cit ke cit kṛtakān pratipadyante kān cit akṛtakān iti tatra kārya dravya saṃyogaḥ kṛtakaḥ saṃyoga ja tvāt utpadyamānasya kāraṇa sambandhibhiḥ kāryasya saṃyoga jaḥ saṃyogaḥ iti kriyājam tu ke cit naḥ icchanti yāvat dravya bhāvi tvāt saṃyogasya 
NV_2.2.17^7	 avibhaktasya ca saṃyogaḥ na asti iti na asti ākāśe kriyājaḥ saṃyogaḥ aṇu ākāśa saṃyogam tu akṛtakam icchanti tatra aṇvākāśa saṃyogasya tāvat kṛtaka tve anumānam ākāśena kṛtaka sambandha sambandhī paramāṇuḥ mūrtimat tva ādibhyaḥ ghaṭa vat iti kārya ākāśa saṃyogaḥ api vipratipatti viṣayaḥ na yāvat dravya bhāvī avinaśyat ādhāra tve kriyāvat dravya vṛtti tve ca aprāpti pratidvandvi tvāt mūrtimat itara dravya saṃyoga vat tasmāt kārya dravyeṇa ākāśasya saṃyoga jaḥ ca saṃyogaḥ kriyājaḥ ca paramāṇoḥ tu kriyājaḥ iti vipratipatti viṣaya avibhāginaḥ ākāśa ādayaḥ kriyāvat dravya saṃyogi tvāt paramāṇu vat yathā paramāṇoḥ kriyāvat dravya saṃyogāḥ ayāvat dravya bhāvinaḥ saṃyoga vat śabda buddhi ādayaḥ ca ātmani avyāpakāḥ saṃyogasya ca avyāpya vṛtti tvam ātmanaḥ pradeśa arthaḥ iti vyākhyātam 
NV_2.2.17^8	 ekasya ca aneka mūrta pradeśa vat dravya sambandhi tvam pradeśa arthaḥ yat vā yat ākāśasya ekasya sataḥ pradeśavatā anekena sambandhi tvam tat pradeśa vat dravya sāmānyam yathā ghaṭasya iti kasmāt punar sūtrakārasya asmin arthe sūtram na śrūyate iti katam asmin arthe niṣpradeśam ākāśam niṣpradeśaḥ ātmā iti etasmin arthataḥ adhigateḥ na sūtram yasmāt ayam arthaḥ arthataḥ adhigamyate atas na sūtritaḥ iti śabda santāna pratipādane vā na sūtram arthataḥ adhigateḥ śāstra siddhāntāt vā tad adhigatiḥ śāstra siddhāntaḥ tu nyāya samākhyātam bahu śākham anumānam tena anuktam api gamyate iti na sūtryate 
NV_2.2.18^1	 atha api khalu idam asti idam na asti iti bhāṣyam yaḥ ayam paryanuyogaḥ tasya kaḥ viṣayaḥ iti anupalabhyamāna śabda astitvam ye śabdam nitya tvam kalpayanti te idam paryanuyojyāḥ idam asti idam na asti iti etat bhavantaḥ katham pratipadyante iti evam anuyuktāḥ santaḥ pratibruvate pramāṇataḥ upalabdheḥ anupalabdheḥ ca iti avidyamānaḥ tarhi śabdaḥ prāk uccāraṇāt anupalabdheḥ āvaraṇa ādi anupalabdheḥ ca yat ca ubhaya pakṣa sampratipannam ghaṭa ādi anitya tvena tena ca anuyojyāḥ iti yat idam anityam ghaṭa ādi bhavadbhiḥ pratipadyate tat katham anityam iti 
NV_2.2.18^2	 saḥ evam anuyuktaḥ yadi ghaṭa ādi anitya tve nyāyam bravīti sa śabde api iti sūtram sataḥ anupalabdhi kāraṇa abhāve kadā cit upalabdheḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ śeṣam bhāṣye vyañjaka abhāvāt agrahaṇam iti ced na ukta uttara tvāt atha manyase śabdasya uccāraṇam vyañjakam vyañjaka abhāvāt naḥ upalabhyate iti asiddham viśeṣaṇam anupalabdhi kāraṇa abhāvaḥ iti kim idam uccāraṇam nāma vivakṣā janitena prayatnena kauṣṭhyasya vāyoḥ preritasya kaṇṭha ādi sthāneṣu pratighātaḥ tat naḥ ukta uttara tvāt vāyu gata vega apekṣaḥ vāyunā tālu ādi saṃyogaḥ abhighātaḥ saṃyogasya ca vyañjaka tvam prāk pratiṣiddham iti 
NV_2.2.19	 evam ca sati tattvam pāṃśubhiḥ iva avakiran āha kaḥ asya arthaḥ tattve ukte jātyā pratyavatiṣṭhate iti sā ca jātiḥ tad anupalabdheḥ anupalambhāt āvaraṇa upapattiḥ kaḥ asya vākyasya arthaḥ āvaraṇa ādi anupalabdhyā anekāntaḥ iti ayam arthaḥ yathā āvaraṇa anupalabdhiḥ anupalabhyamānāḥ api asti tathā āvaraṇam iti anekāntaḥ atha anupalabdhiḥ anupalabhyamānā na asti tad abhāvāt upalabdhiḥ asti na ca avidyamānasya upalabdhiḥ iti siddham āvaraṇam katham punar bhavān jānīyate na āvaraṇa anupalabdhiḥ upalabhyate iti kim atra jñeyam pratyātma vedanīya tvāt pratyātmam eva ayam āvaraṇa upalabdhi vat āvaraṇa anupalabdhim ca vedayate evam ca sati apahṛta viṣayam uttaram vākyam iti apahṛta viṣayam iti na asya utthānam asti iti 
NV_2.2.20–2.2.21	 abhyanujñā vādena tu ucyate anupalambhāt api anupalabdhi sadbhāvāt na āvaraṇa anupapattiḥ anupalambhāt iti asya sūtrasya anupalabdheḥ anaikāntika tvam arthaḥ atathā jātīyena pratyavasthānāt anuttaram iti sūtra arthaḥ yathājātīyaḥ śabdaḥ anityaḥ tathā ajātīyam kim cit nityam na dṛṣṭam iti uktam ca atra kim uktam ubhaya anta aparicchinna sattā sambandhaḥ nityatā iti tasmāt ayathārtha pratyavasthānāt na kim cit etat anityaḥ śabdaḥ guṇa tve sati asmad ādi pratyakṣa tvāt buddhi vat iti avyāpakasya vyāpaka dravya samavāyi tve sati pratyakṣa tvāt sukha vat ākāśa niṣpradeśa tve hetuḥ niṣpradeśam ākāśam vyāpaka tvāt ātma vat dravyasya sataḥ sarvadā amūrta tvāt ātma vat eva vyāpaka tvāt eva akṛtaka tvam vyāpaka tvam ca dravyasya sataḥ sarvadā amūrta tvāt etena diś kālau vyākhyātau evam tāvat sva sādhana sthityā vyavasthitam anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti 
NV_2.2.22	 atha śabdasya nitya tvam pratijānānāḥ iti bhāṣyam vipratipatteḥ pramāṇa mūla tvāt hetau paripraśnaḥ vipratipattiḥ nāma dvayoḥ eka dharma viṣayā viruddha dharma sampratipattiḥ na ca vipratipattiḥ pramāṇa antaram antareṇa yuktāḥ iti nitya tve pramāṇam vaktavyam iti nityaḥ śabdaḥ asparśa tvāt anupalabdha vipakṣa eka deśasya prayogaḥ ākāśa vat iti 
NV_2.2.23–2.2.26	 tasya vyabhicāra darśana artham sūtram na karma anitya tvāt iti śeṣam asya bhāṣye na aṇu nitya tvāt ayam anyaḥ hetuḥ śabda nitya tve sampradānāt na hi kim cit nityam sampradīyamānam dṛṣṭam iti anvayinaḥ dṛṣṭāntasya abhāvāt viruddhaḥ atha ayam pratijñā arthaḥ avatiṣṭhate śabdaḥ sampradānāt ghaṭa ādi vat iti evam api nitya tvam na sidhyati tad antarāla anupalabdheḥ ahetuḥ avatiṣṭhamānaḥ hi dātṛ pratigrahītroḥ antarāle upalabhyeta iti iti virodhaḥ sūtra arthaḥ 
NV_2.2.27–2.2.28	 na virodhaḥ anumānātaḥ upalabdheḥ na hi pratyakṣataḥ anupalabhyamānasya anumānena upalabdhiḥ sattām bādhate kim anumānam adhyāpanam kim idam adhyāpanam nāma dīyamānasya sampradāna prāptiḥ dātṛ pratigrahītroḥ antarāle śabdaḥ asti adhāpanāt śara ādi vat iti na śabdasya adhyāpanam pratiṣidhyate api tu nṛtya upadeśa vat anityasya eva ādhyāpanam iti yat punar etat dātṛ pratigrahītroḥ antarāle śabdaḥ asti iti siddha sādhanam etat vayam api brūmaḥ dātrā uccaritaḥ śabdaḥ santāna vṛttyā sampradānam prāpnoti tasmāt sampradānam avasthāne na hetuḥ 
NV_2.2.29	 ayam tarhi hetuḥ abhyāsāt vīṇā ādi vat iti anityeṣu eva laṅghana plavana ādiṣu abhyāsaḥ iti viruddhaḥ atha avasthānam abhyāsāt sādhyeta tathā api anavasthiteṣu teṣu eva abhyāsaḥ iti anekāntaḥ abhyāsa svarūpa anavadhāraṇāt asiddhaḥ ca abhyāsaḥ hi nāma eka viṣayaḥ aneka jñāna utpādaḥ eka ākāra viṣayaḥ vā tatra ayam abhyāsaḥ eka viṣayaḥ eka ākāra viṣayaḥ vā iti sandigdha asiddhaḥ
