NV_2.2.30–2.2.31	 abhyāsā siddhau abhyāsa upacāra viṣaya tvena sādhanam tasya anaikāntika tva jñāpana artham na anya tve api abhyāsa upacāraḥ anya tva pratiṣedha artham api abhyāsasya upacārāt etat sūtram anya tva pratiṣedha artham yat idam anyat iti manyase idam anyasmāt ananyat vā syāt ananyat vā yadi anyat ananyat na bhavati yathā brāhmaṇāt anyaḥ na brāhmaṇaḥ iti atha ananyat tathā api anyat na bhavati ananya tvāt yat ananyat tat katham anyat bhavati iti 
NV_2.2.32^1	 sūtrasya arthaḥ virodhaḥ ananya tvam abhyupagatam nivartate iti katham nivartate pratiṣedhasya anya viṣaya tvāt anya abhāve ananyat na asti na hi brāhmaṇa abhāve abrāhmaṇaḥ sidhyati iti ayam tarhi hetuḥ pratyabhijñānāt tad abhāve pratyabhijñānam dṛṣṭam maṇi ādiṣu asti ca pratyabhijñānam śabde tasmāt pratyabhijñānāt avatiṣṭhate śabdaḥ iti kim idam pratyabhijñānam tad pratyaya viṣaya tvam tad pratyaya viṣaya tvam anya tve api iti anekāntaḥ atha pratyabhijñānam tad pratyaya viṣayasya avyabhicāraḥ na hi kadā cit tad pratyaya viṣaya vyabhicāraḥ asti yaḥ punar sadṛśe tad pratyayaḥ sa viśeṣa darśanāt nivartate atas yā asu tad pratyayasya śabde avyāvṛttiḥ tat pratyabhijñānam iti na tad pratyayasya avyāvṛttiḥ asiddhāḥ ayam tāvat tad pratyayaḥ puruṣa antare nivartamānaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yat punar etat viśeṣa darśanāt tad sadṛśe tad bhāva pratyayaḥ nivartate iti satyam eva tat śabde tu kim viśeṣasya adarśanāt tad sadṛśe tad pratyayaḥ uta tad bhāvāt eva tad pratyayaḥ iti sandihyate 
NV_2.2.32^2	 atha pratyabhijñānam tad bhāvāt bhavati iti pakṣaḥ tathā api anyaḥ hetuḥ vaktavyaḥ kim kāraṇam pratyabhijñānasya pakṣa viśeṣaṇa tvena upayukta tvāt yat punar etat go śabdena go śabdaḥ iti pratyayasya avyāvṛttiḥ asti iti na ca go śabdasya go pratyaya kartṛ tva vyabhicāraḥ iti etat api sandihyate kim kāraṇa sāmānyāt go śabde go pratyayasya avyāvṛttiḥ āhosvit tad bhāvāt iti etena tad pratyaya kartṛ tvam vyākhyātam yuktam tu kāraṇa sāmānyāt tad pratyayasya avyāvṛttiḥ katham iti go buddhau go buddhi pratyayaḥ na vyāvartate na ca asyāḥ go śabda buddheḥ tad pratyaya kartṛ tvam nivartate tasmāt tad pratyaya hetu tve pratyabhijñānam ahetuḥ yaḥ ca anupalabdha viśeṣaḥ eva nivartate tam prati tasya vastunaḥ kim viśeṣaḥ asti na asti iti bhavantaḥ eva praṣṭavyāḥ yadi asti viśeṣaḥ tad pratyaya avyāvṛttiḥ ahetuḥ anekāntāt atha na asti viśeṣaḥ ekam vastu dvi ātmakam iti prāptam virodhāt ahetuḥ pratyaya avi āvṛttiḥ ca aśeṣa puruṣa viṣaya tayā asiddhā puruṣa viśeṣa viṣaya tayā anaikāntikī iti 
NV_2.2.33–2.2.35^1^1	 ayam tarhi hetuḥ vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ yat anityam tasya vināśa kāraṇam upalabhyate yathā loṣṭasya kāraṇa dravya vibhāgaḥ na tu śabdasya tasmāt nityaḥ śabdaḥ iti aśravaṇa kāraṇa anupapatteḥ satatam śravaṇa prasaṅgaḥ iti śeṣam bhāṣye anumānena śabdasya vināśa kāraṇam upalabhyate yat ca anumānena upalabhyate na tat na asti kim anumānam santāna upapatteḥ iti varṇitam tasmāt anapadeśaḥ ayam vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ iti yathā viṣāṇī tasmāt aśvaḥ iti kim punar atra asat kim viṣāṇam āhosvit aśva viṣāṇa sambandhaḥ iti ubhayam iti āha 
NV_2.2.33–2.2.35^1^2	 nanu yadā viṣāṇinam aśva tvena sādhayati tadā viṣāṇam asti eva na viṣāṇam pratiṣidhyate aśva viṣāṇa sambandhasya abhāvāt anumānam asat iti yuktam vaktum asattvāt anapedeśaḥ iti karma vat iti ced na āśraya anitya tvāt atha manyase nityasya api upalabhyamānasya atyantam agrahaṇam dṛṣṭam yathā karma tvasya iti tat ca naḥ āśraya anitya tvāt āśrayasya nitya tvāt aśravaṇa kāraṇa anupapatteḥ iti brūmaḥ karma tvasya punar agrahaṇa kāraṇam āśraya anitya tvam asti tasmāt aprasaṅgaḥ iti ghaṇṭāyām abhihanyamānāyām tāraḥ tārataraḥ mandaḥ mandataraḥ iti śruti bhedāt nānā śabda santānaḥ hi avicchedena śrūyate tatra idam cintyate 
NV_2.2.35^2	 śabdasya vyajyamānasya yat vyakti kāraṇam tat kim ghaṇṭā stham āhosvit anya vṛtti iti yadi ghaṇṭā stham kim avasthitam uta santāna vṛtti iti anya vṛtti tve api kim avasthitam uta santāna vṛtti iti yadi ghaṇṭā stham avasthitam ca śruti bhedaḥ na prāpnoti iti atha ghaṇṭā stham santāna vṛtti ca yugapad aneka śabdvyakti prasaṅgaḥ yāvān śabdaḥ ghaṇṭā sthena avasthitena santāna vṛttinā vā vyaṅgyaḥ sa sarvaḥ ekasmin kāle upalabhyeta ghaṇṭā stham ca abhivyakti kāraṇam katham anyatra vartamānam śabdam vyanakti iti vācyam atha anya āgatam avasthitam santāna vṛtti vā śabda abhivyakti kāraṇam manyase tadā ekasyām ghaṇṭāyām abhihatāyām śabdān vyanakti na pratyāsanna deśa vṛttiṣu ghaṇṭā antareṣu iti niyama hetuḥ vaktavyaḥ asati ca śabda bhede śrutīnām bhedaḥ upapādayitavyaḥ tāraḥ mandaḥ iti nādaḥ bhidyate na śabdaḥ tāraḥ mandaḥ iti ced na śabda samāna ādhikaraṇyasya grahaṇāt śabda śabda samāna adhikaraṇaḥ ayam tāra manda ādi śabdaḥ pravartate 
NV_2.2.35^3	 na ca asati śabda viṣaya tve śabda samāna adhikaraṇa tvam yuktam nīlotpala vat iti vyāmoha pratyayaḥ saḥ iti ced na nimitta an abhidhānāt atha manyase tāraḥ mandaḥ iti śabda samāna adhikaraṇaḥ vyāmoha pratyayaḥ bhavati yathā dīrghaḥ śabdaḥ mahān śabdaḥ iti na viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt vyāmoha pratyayaḥ ayam iti na viśeṣa hetuḥ asti yadi ca ayam vyāmoha pratyayaḥ bhavati vyāmoha pratyayasya nimittam vācyam yathā dīrghaḥ śabdaḥ iti avirata śabda santāna śrutau śabde dīrgha pratyayaḥ bhavati yāni khalu dīrghāṇi dravyāṇi bhavanti teṣām avayava upacaye sati grahaṇa santati viṣaya tvam tad sāmānyāt śabde dīrgha pratyayaḥ na tu nitya śabda vādinaḥ vyāmoha pratyaya bījam asti iti ayuktam etat tulyam iti ced na tad nimittasya kadā cit bhāvāt atha manyase yasya api anityaḥ śabdaḥ tena api ghaṇṭā stham avasthitam santāna vṛtti vai anya stham avasthitam santāna vṛtti vai utpatti kāraṇam vācyam 
NV_2.2.35^4	 ghaṇṭā stham utpatti kāraṇam kadā cit śabdān utpādayati kadā cit naḥ iti nitya vat prasaṅgaḥ na prasaṅgaḥ nimittasya kadā cit bhāvāt yat tu tat śabda utpatti kāraṇam ghaṇṭā vṛtti tat kadā cit bhavati kadā cit bhāve api sati santāna vṛtti tasmāt nimitta bheda anuvidhāyinaḥ śabdāḥ kadā cit bhavanti santāna vṛtti tvāt ca mandataratama ādi bhinna rūpa anuvidhāyinam śabdam utpādayanti iti tat ca kāraṇam saṃskāraḥ iti kutas tad utpattiḥ pāṇi saṃśleṣam apekṣamāṇāt karmaṇaḥ pāṇi ghaṇṭā saṃśleṣāt pāṇi gata vega apekṣāt ghaṇṭāyām karma tat karma pāṇi abhighātam apekṣamāṇam vibhāga sama kālam saṃskāram karoti sā calanti ādhyātmikam vāyum upagṛhṇāti sā vāyunā abhihatā punar karma karoti tatas saṃskāraḥ saṃskāreṇa punar karma punar vāyu upagrahaṇam iti evam mandataratamādi nyāyena saṃskāraḥ upapadyate iti tatra antyasya atimāndyāt ghaṇṭāyām mahābhūta saṃkṣobha śakteḥ abhāvaḥ tatas vāyu upagraha ucchedaḥ tatas saṃskāra kṣayaḥ iti 
NV_2.2.36	 na saṃskāraḥ asti anupalabdheḥ iti ced atha manyase naḥ eva saṃskāraḥ asti anupalabdheḥ iti tat ca asat pāṇi nimitta praśleṣāt śabda abhāve na anupalabdhiḥ ukta artham sūtram yadi saṃskāram śabda utpatti nimittam na pratipadyase pāṇi ghaṇṭā saṃśleṣāt śabdesantāna ucchedaḥ na prāpnoti atha ghaṇṭā sthaḥ saṃskāraḥ pāṇi saṃśleṣāt nivartate tathā api katham śabda santāna ucchedaḥ iti na brūmaḥ pāṇi ghaṇṭā saṃśleṣaḥ śabdam ucchinatti iti api tu pāṇi ghaṇṭā saṃśleṣāt tad vṛttiḥ saṃskāraḥ sparśavat dravya saṃyoga virodhi tvāt nivartate nivṛtte ca tasmin kāraṇa abhāvāt kārya abhāvaḥ iti santāna ucchedaḥ 
NV_2.2.37	 yat idam ucyate vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ nityaḥ śabdaḥ iti yadi yasya vināśa kāraṇam na upalabhyate tat nityam yāni imāni śabda grahaṇāni teṣām na bhavatā vināśa kāraṇam upapādyate anupapādanāt avasthānāt nitya tvam iti atha anupalabdha vināśa kāraṇāni api śabda grahaṇāni anityāni śabdaḥ api evam iti anekāntaḥ atha anumānataḥ śabda grahaṇānām vināśa kāraṇam gamyante tad samānam śabdaḥ iti na kim cit bādhitam bhavati 
NV_2.2.38	 vyadhikaraṇa tvāt ayuktam iti ced atha manyase vyadhikaraṇaḥ śabdaḥ katham anya vṛttinā saṃśleṣeṇa nivartyate atha vyadhikaraṇam api nivartayati sarva ghaṇṭā śabda uccheda prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt pāṇi ghaṇṭā saṃśleṣa samāna adhikaraṇaḥ śabdaḥ iti asparśa tvāt apratiṣedhaḥ asparśa vyāpi dravya āśrayaḥ śabdaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ katham anyatara vartamānasya pāṇi ghaṇṭā saṃśleṣaḥ nivartakaḥ iti na ukta uttara tvāt ukta uttaram etat kāraṇa abhāvāt anya śabda an utpādaḥ yaḥ tu utpannaḥ śabdaḥ sa mandataratamādi nyāyena antyasya atimāndyāt yena kena cit virodhi tvāt kṣīyate yaḥ ayam saṃskāraḥ śabda kāraṇa tvena samadhigataḥ sa kim ekaḥ anekaḥ vā iti sandihyate anekaḥ saṃskāraḥ iti etat tattvam śabda bhedāt kāraṇa bhede sati kārya bhedaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti yasya ca ekaḥ saṃskāraḥ tasya eṣoḥ pātaḥ prāpnoti agatvā eva yāvat gantavyam iti atha apratibadhyamāne saṃskāre dravyam gacchati na kadā cit pātaḥ prāpnoti dṛṣṭaḥ ca pātaḥ tasmāt anekaḥ saṃskāraḥ iti 
NV_2.2.39	 tasmāt na ayam śabdaḥ gandha ādibhiḥ saha sanniviṣṭaḥ vyajyante vibhakti antara upapatteḥ vibhāgaḥ ca vibhāgānataram ca iti vibhakti antaram vidharmāṇaḥ śabdāḥ nānā rūpāḥ sarūpāḥ ca eka dravyāḥ śrūyante samāsaḥ samudāyaḥ etat ca sparśavat dravya vṛttiṣu śabdeṣu na prāpnoti gandha ādi vat yathā pratidravyam ekaḥ gandhaḥ evam pratidravyam ekaḥ śabdaḥ iti santāna upapatteḥ ca iti ca arthaḥ yadi ayam gandha ādibhiḥ saha sanniviṣṭaḥ syāt na anyatra vartamānaḥ śrotraḥ upalabhyeta tasmāt santāna vṛtti tvāt ākāśa āśrayaḥ śabdaḥ iti 
NV_2.2.40–2.2.44	 iti saṃśaya jñāpana artham sūtram iti sūtram prakṛti anuvidhānāt iti sūtra arthaḥ vikāre prakṛti anuvidhānam dṛṣṭam iti iti sādhana pakṣe dṛṣṭānta mātra tvāt ahetuḥ dvividhasya api hetoḥ abhāvāt asādhanam dṛṣṭāntaḥ dūṣaṇa pakṣe na atulya prakṛtīnām vikāra vikalpāt iti asambaddham atulyāyāḥ prakṛteḥ vikalpyante vikārāḥ hrasva dīrgha anuvidhānam tu yakāre na asti iti 
NV_2.2.45–2.2.49	 yathā dravya bhāvena tulyāyāḥ prakṛteḥ vikāra vikalpaḥ bhavati evam varṇa bhāvena tulyāyāḥ prakṛteḥ vikāra vikalpaḥ syāt iti iti parihāraḥ iti yadi vikriyante varṇāḥ punar āpattiḥ na prāpnoti vikāra prāptānām punar āpattiḥ darśanāt anekāntaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ sarva avastham suvarṇa darśanam na punar ikāraya kārayoḥ kaḥ cit varṇa ātmā vyavasthitaḥ asti yaḥ itvam hitvā yatvam āpadyate iti varṇa tva avyatirekāt varṇa vikārāṇām apratiṣedhaḥ varṇa vikārāḥ api varṇa tvāt na vyatiricyante iti asti varṇa tvam sāmānyam iti sāmānyavataḥ dharma yogaḥ na sāmānyasya iti parihāraḥ 
NV_2.2.50–2.2.52	 varṇa vikāra anupapattiḥ nitya tve avikārāt anitya tve ca anavasthānāt nityāḥ varṇāḥ iti na yuktaḥ vikāraḥ vyāghātāt anityāḥ varṇāḥ iti na yuktaḥ vikāraḥ anavasthitānām vikāra adarśanāt nityānām api atīndriya tva darśanāt tad dharma vikalpāt ca varṇa vikārāṇām apratiṣedhah iti vikalpa samā jātiḥ iti sādharmya samā jātiḥ 
NV_2.2.53–2.2.54	 ubhayoḥ api uttaram vikāra dharmi tve nitya tva abhāvāt kāla antare vikāra upapatteḥ ca apratiṣedhaḥ nityāḥ varṇāḥ vikriyante iti vyāghātaḥ doṣaḥ upalabhyamānasya ca ikārasya yatvā anupapatteḥ varṇa aupalabdhi vat iti asambaddham itas ca varṇa vikāra anupapattiḥ prakṛti aniyamāt vikāre prakṛtīnām niyamaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ ikāraya kārayoḥ tu aniyamaḥ tasmāt aniyamāt na vikriyante iti 
NV_2.2.55–2.2.57	 sūtra arthaḥ aniyamaḥ na asti iti anujñāta pratiṣiddhayoḥ ekatva anupapatteḥ iti virodhaḥ sūtra arthaḥ tasmāt anupalabhyamāna pṛthak dharmi viśeṣāṇām ādeśaḥ iti yadi ete varṇāḥ vikriyeran tatas pṛthak vikāra lakṣaṇebhyaḥ dharmebhyaḥ dharmī upalabhyeta na tu upalabhyate tasmāt na varṇāḥ vikriyante iti atha vikriyante iti evam vikāraḥ bhavati guṇa antara āpatti upamarda hrāsa vṛddhi leśa śleṣebhyaḥ tu vikāra upapatteḥ varṇa vikārāḥ sūtra arthaḥ guṇa antara āpatti ādinā deśaḥ iti ayam ca vikāra ādeśa upadeśa vikāraḥ bhāṣya kāreṇa eva samyak nirūpitaḥ iti sūtra artha mātram varṇitam iti 
NV_2.2.58	 te varṇāḥ yathādarśanam vikṛtāḥ vibhakti antāḥ pada saṃjñakāḥ bhavanti artha pratyayaḥ tarhi na prāpnoti na na prāpnoti antya varṇa pratyayāt pūrva varṇa pratisandhāna pratyaya apekṣāt artha pratyayaḥ iti vibhaktiḥ dvayī nāmikī ca ākhyātikī ca nāmikī sva ādayaḥ ākhyātikī tiba ādayaḥ tayā viśiṣyamāṇam padam dvedhā bhavati nāma ca ākhyātam ca abhidheyasya kriyā antara yogāt viśiṣyamāṇa rūpaḥ sabdaḥ nāma yathā brāhmaṇaḥ iti kriyā kāraka samudāyaḥ kāraka saṃkhyā viśiṣṭaḥ kriyā kāla yoga abhidhāyi kriyā pradhānam ākhyātam pacati iti yathā yadi dvayī vibhaktiḥ upasarga nipātāḥ tarhi na pada saṃjñakāḥ na nāmni antarbhāvāt upasarga nipātāḥ nāmnā saṃgṛhītāḥ yasmāt āha avyayāt lopaḥ iti tena subanta tvāt tena eva saṃgṛhītāḥ iti 
NV_2.2.59^1	 padena vyavahāraḥ iti padārthaḥ cintyate nāma padam ca adhikṛtya vyavahāraḥ iti nāma padam cintyate nāmnaḥ ca adhikāraḥ vyāpaka tvāt yasmāt nāmnā sarva padam vyāpyate tasmāt gauḥ iti asya padasya arthaḥ cintyate na padātartha adhigatiḥ viśeṣe anavasthānāt na hi pade uccarite kaḥ cit viśeṣaḥ gamyate tasmāt padam avācakam iti na padasya viśeṣa aviṣaya tvāt kaḥ evam āha padena viśeṣaḥ gamyate api tu sāmānya varti padam viśeṣa varti vākyam na ca sāmānya abhidhānāt anarthakam bhavitum arhati iti na sāmānyasya vyavahāra aviṣaya tvāt sarvaḥ upadeṣṭā viśeṣa pratipatti artham padam uccārayati na ca sāmānye paiṣaḥ na sampratipattiḥ tasmāt padam avācakam eva iti na sāmānya viṣaya tve sati viśeṣa śruteḥ niyāmaka tvāt yadi padāni avācakāni syuḥ na ca pada śravaṇāt sāmānyam gamyeta yat avācakam na tasmāt sāmānyam viśeṣaḥ vā gamyate yathā arthāt gamyate ca padāt sāmānyam sāmānya śruteḥ ca viśeṣa śrutiḥ niyāmikā bhavati 
NV_2.2.59^2	 yathā gauḥ iti sāmānya adhigatau tiṣṭḥati gacchati iti viśeṣa śrutyā gamyate iti katham punar iyam viśeṣa śrutiḥ gacchati tiṣṭhati iti na eva iyam kevalāt viśeṣa śrutiḥ kim tu pūrva pada apekṣayā viśeṣa pratyaya hetutvāt viśeṣa śrutiḥ iti ucyate bhavatu vā padāt eva ubhayam etasmāt eva vā go śabdāt ubhayam gamyate kriyā ca tad sādhanam ca pradhāna upasarjana bhāvasya aniyamena yadā ayam go śabdaḥ go tva nimittaḥ go tva yogāt gauḥ iti tadā go śabdāt pradhānam sādhanam gauḥ gamyate kriyā tu aṅga bhūtāḥ viśeṣaka tvāt yadā punar kriyā pradhānam padam goḥ bhāvaḥ go tvam iti tadā api gauḥ aṅga bhūtaḥ viśeṣaka tvāt gamyate pradhānam go tvam iti tat evam pradhāna upasarjana bhāvasya aniyamena go tvam iti ca pade gauḥ iti ca ubhayam gamyate iti tatra pradhāna upasarjana bhāvam āśritya tad arthe vyakti ākṛti jāti sannidhau upacārāt saṃśayaḥ yasmāt ayam go śabdaḥ vyakti ākṛti jātiṣu avinā abhāvena vartamānāsu prayujyate avinā abhāva vṛttiḥ ca sannidhiḥ atas na jñāyate kim vyaktiḥ padārthaḥ uta ākṛtiḥ uta jātiḥ iti 
NV_2.2.60	 śabdasya prayoga sāmarthyāt padārtha avadhāraṇam iti prayoga pradarśana artham yā śabda ādi sūtram nāmī yā śabda ādayaḥ iti jātau prayujyante kasmāt abhedāt ekā jātiḥ tasyāḥ viśeṣaṇam anarthakam yā gauḥ tiṣṭhati iti yā gauḥ niṣaṇṇāḥ iti evam śeṣeṣu ākṛteḥ api abhidhāyakam etat na bhavati niṣkriya tvāt ākṛteḥ na hi niṣkriyāḥ gacchati tiṣṭhati vā iti evam sarvatra yasya ca anena viśeṣeṇa tiṣṭhati ādinā yogaḥ tam go śabdaḥ abhidhātum arhati iti kutas viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvasya eka viṣaya tvāt yadi ca go śabdasya tiṣṭhati śabdasya ca ekam abhidheyam bhavati tatas go śabdena dharmi antarāṇi nirākriyante tiṣṭhati śabdena ca kriyā antarāṇi iti viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva āpannayoḥ tiṣṭhati go śabdayoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyam yujyate anyathā naḥ iti dravyam vyaktiḥ iti na artha antaram tiṣṭhati śabda sannihitena go śabdena vyaktiḥ abhidhīyate iti 
NV_2.2.61–2.2.62^1	 tad pratiṣedha artham sūtram na tad anavasthānāt iti na anena go śabdena vyakti mātram śuddham ucyate yadi ayam vyakti mātra abhidhāyakaḥ abhaviṣyat tena yasyām kasyām cit vyaktau pratyayaḥ abhaviṣyat iti sūtra arthaḥ yadi vyaktiḥ na padārthaḥ katham vyaktau prayogaḥ yā gauḥ tiṣṭhati iti evam ādiḥ nimittāt atadbhāve api tad upacāraḥ kva punar nimittāt atadbhāve api tadvat upacāraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti tasya upapādana artham sūtram sahacaraṇa sthāna tādarthya vṛtta māna dhāraṇa sāmīpya yoga sādhana ādhipatyebhyaḥ brāhmaṇa mañca kaṭa rāja saktu candana gaṅgā śāṭaka anna puruṣeṣu atadbhāve api tad upacāraḥ iti atadbhāve api tad upacāraḥ iti atad śabdasya tad śabdena abhidhānam upacāraḥ yathā yaṣṭikā śabdena dravya viśeṣaḥ abhidhīyate yaṣṭi yogāt punar sāhacaryāt brāhmaṇaḥ abhidhīyate yaṣṭikāḥ praveśaya iti evam sarvatra 
NV_2.2.62^2	 kim punar atra upacāra bījam yaṣṭikāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ iti na hi upacāra bījam antareṇa upacāraḥ labhyate nanu uktam sāhacaryam iti sāhacaryam nāma yaṣṭikayā nitya sambandhaḥ yaṣṭikā sambandhāt ca yaṣṭikāvān iti syāt na yaṣṭikāḥ iti yaṣṭikāvān iti ca ayam śabdaḥ mukhyaḥ eva tasmāt upacāra bījam anyat vaktavyam iti yaṣṭikāyām tāvat ayam yaṣṭikā śabdaḥ jāti nimittaḥ yaṣṭikā tvam jātiḥ sā yaṣṭikāyām vartate iti tayā yaṣṭikā tu a yuktayā yaṣṭikayā brāhmaṇasya yogaḥ sāhacaryāt saṃyukta samavetām jātim adhyāropya brāhmaṇam yaṣṭikāḥ iti āha evam śeṣāṇi upacāra bījāni svayam utprekṣaṇīyāni iti 
NV_2.2.63	 yadi tarhi gauḥ iti padasya na vyaktiḥ arthaḥ astu tarhi ākṛtiḥ tad apekṣa tvāt sattva vyavasthāna siddheḥ ākṛtiḥ padārthaḥ kasmāt tad apekṣa tvāt sattva vyavasthānasya gauḥ aśvaḥ puruṣaḥ iti evam ādi sattva vyavasthānam ākṛti apekṣam sidhyati yad apekṣā ca sattva vyavasthāna siddhiḥ sa go śabdasya viṣayaḥ iti atra api tat eva upasthitam na tad anavasthānāt iti yasya ca jātyā yogaḥ sa go śabdasya viṣayaḥ na ākṛtiḥ jātya yogāt kasya punar jāti yogaḥ niyata avayava vyūhasya āvayavinaḥ niyataḥ avayava vyūhaḥ yasya sa bhavati niyata avayava vyūhaḥ anya pad arthena bahu vrīhiṇā avayavī abhidhīyate iti 
NV_2.2.64^1	 astu tarhi jātiḥ padārthaḥ vyakti ākṛti yukte api aprasaṅgāt prokṣaṇa ādīnām mṛd gavake jātiḥ yasmāt mṛd gavake vyakti ākṛtī staḥ na ca tatra prokṣaṇa ādīni prayujyante na hi gām ānaya gām prokṣaya gām dehī iti mṛd gavake praiṣa sampratipattī bhavataḥ yat abhāvāt tatra na sampratyayaḥ sa go śabdasya arthaḥ kasya ca abhāvāt na tatra sampratyayaḥ jāteḥ atha mṛd gavake kasmāt go tvam na jātiḥ yasmāt mṛdgavakaḥ gauḥ na bhavati yaḥ ca gauḥ na bhavati na tatra go tvam vartate yathā aśvaḥ iti atha mṛdgavakaḥ kasmāt gauḥ na bhavati atas eva na bhavati yasmāt mṛdgavakaḥ iti na ca ayam yuktaḥ praśnaḥ mṛdgavakaḥ kasmāt gauḥ na bhavati iti kim kāraṇam pratipatti bādhita tvāt bhavān api etam artham pratipadyate na ayam gauḥ iti pratipattyā ca praśnaḥ bādhyate iti atha mṛdgavake go śabdaḥ kutas ākṛti sāmānyāt citra ādi vat iti 
NV_2.2.64^2	 sarva gatāḥ iti ced atha manyase sarva gatā jātiḥ sā utpadyamānena yathā gavā sambaddhyate tathā mṛd gavakena api iti asti mṛd gavake go tvam tat na anabhyupagamāt kena sarva gata tvam jāteḥ abhyupagamyate api tu sva viṣaye sarvatra vartate iti sarva gatāḥ iti ucyate kaḥ punar go tvasya svaḥ viṣayaḥ yatra go tvam vartate kva punar go tvam vartate yatra go tva nimittaḥ anuvṛtta pratyayaḥ bhavati kva punar anuvṛtta pratyayam go tvam karoti yat tasya sādhanam kaḥ punar nitye go tve goḥ sādhana arthaḥ yat tena vyajyate na hi kakudādi mad artha vyatirekeṇa go tvasya vyaktiḥ asti na hi piṇḍebhyaḥ artha antaram go tvam piṇḍa antarāleṣu agrahaṇāt iti ke cit tat na vikalpa anupapatteḥ piṇḍa antarāleṣu adarśanāt iti brūvāṇaḥ piṇḍa antarālam paryanuyojyaḥ kim idam piṇḍa antarālam kim ākāśam āhosvit abhāvaḥ uta dravya antaram iti 
NV_2.2.64^3	 yadi ākāśam na tatra go tvam na hi ākāśam gauḥ iti etena abhāvaḥ dravya antaram ca vyākhyātam viśeṣa pratyayānām anākasmika tvāt ca ayam ca piṇḍa pratyaya vyatireka bhāj pratyayaḥ upajāyamānaḥ nimitta antarāt bhavati dṛṣṭā khalu piṇḍa pratyaya vyatireka bhājām pratyayānām nimitta antarāt utpattiḥ yathā vastra carma kambaleṣu nīla pratyayaḥ iti ākṛti sāmānyāt iti ced atha manyase satyam ayam piṇḍa vyatirekāt nimitta antarāt anuvṛtti pratyayaḥ bhavati na punar asya jātiḥ nimittam api tu yat śiraḥ pāṇi pāda ākṛti sāmānyam tasmāt anuvṛtti pratyayaḥ iti na piṇḍa vat asādhāraṇa tvāt ākṛteḥ yathā eva piṇḍāḥ piṇḍa antara vṛttayaḥ na bhavanti tathā ākṛtiḥ api eka piṇḍa varti tvāt piṇḍa antara vartinī na bhavati atha ākṛteḥ piṇḍa antara varti tvam abhyupagamyate nāmni vivādaḥ na arthaḥ iti atha piṇḍa vyatiriktam sāmānyam na abhyupagamyate tathā api eka sāmānya nirākaraṇāt samāna pratyaya bījam anyat vaktavyam syāt 
NV_2.2.64^4	 na hi asati sāmānye samāna pratyayam paśyāmaḥ iti asati api sāmānye dṛṣṭaḥ sāmānya pratyayaḥ iti ced atha manyase yathā sāmānyeṣu asati sāmānya ānatare anuvṛtti pratyayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ go tva aśva tva ghaṭa tveṣu idam sāmānyam idam sāmānyam iti tasmāt anaikāntika tvāt anuvṛtti pratyayaḥ asādhanam artha antara nimitta pratipādane iti na anabhyupagamāt na mayā go tva aśva tva ghaṭa tveṣu nirnimittaḥ sāmānya pratyayaḥ abhyupagamyate tasmāt anuttaram etat sūtra vyāghātaḥ iti ced yadi manyase sāmānyeṣu api sāmānyam asti iti nanu sūtra vyāghātaḥ sāmānya viśeṣeṣu sāmānya viśeṣa abhāvāt tatas eva jñānam iti na sūtra artha aparijñānāt ayam sūtra arthaḥ yathā dravyam iti pratyayaḥ dravya tva viśeṣaṇe dravye bhavati na punar sāmānya viśeṣeṣu evam iti na punar ayam sūtra arthaḥ nirnimittaḥ anuvṛtti pratyayaḥ iti 
NV_2.2.64^5	 kim nimittam iti ced atha manyase go tva ādiṣu anuvṛtti pratyayasya kim nimittam yatas sāmānyam iti bhavati kutas ca sāmānyam iti bhavati aneka artha samāvāyāt yathā go tvam aneka artha samavāyi tathā aśva tva ādi iti aneka arthaiḥ tad samavāyasya samāna tvāt go tva ādiṣu anuvṛtti pratyayaḥ iti pācaka ādi śabda vat iti ced atha manyase yathā pācaka ādi śabdāḥ anuvṛtti pratyayāḥ ca bhavanti na ca pācaka tvam nāma sāmānyam asti tathā gavā ādiṣu anuvṛtti pratyayaḥ iti na hetu artha aparijñānāt viśeṣa pratyayānām ākasmika tvāt iti asya hetoḥ piṇḍa pratyaya vyatiriktasya pratyayasya nimitta antarāt utpādaḥ iti ayam arthaḥ na punar sarvaḥ anuvṛtti pratyayaḥ sāmānyāt eva bhavati iti evam ca sati pacana kriyāyāḥ yat pradhānam sādhanam tat pācaka śabdena ucyate tat ca prādhānyam pācaka antareṣu api asti iti na doṣaḥ yadi aneka artha vṛtti go tvam tat kim pratipiṇḍam parisamāptyā vartate atha eka deśena iti 
NV_2.2.64^6	 kim ca atas yadi pratipiṇḍam parisamāptyā vartate piṇḍa vadasā dhāraṇa tvāt na sāmānyam bhavitum arhati atha eka deśena vartate tathā api na ekam anekatra vartate kim tu anekam anekatra iti yasmāt pradeśāḥ sāmānyasya vartante iti ye ca te eka deśāḥ sāmānyasya pratyekam piṇḍeṣu vartante te kim sāmānya ātmakāḥ uta naḥ iti yadi sāmānya ātmakāḥ na ekam anekatra pravartate iti prāptam na ca anekam anekatra pravartamānam sāmānyam iti yuktam vaktum atha na sāmānya ātmakāḥ śūnyam abhidhānam sāmānyasya eka deśāḥ pratyekam vartante iti taiḥ api deśaiḥ sāmānyam vartate iti pūrvavat prasaṅgaḥ na ca anyā gatiḥ asti tasmāt na aneka vṛtti sāmānyam iti na vikalpa anabhyupagamāt na ayam vikalpaḥ asti go tvam pratyekam piṇḍeṣu parisamāptya vartate atha eka deśena vartate iti tasmāt vikalpa anabhyupagamāt apraśnaḥ ayam 
NV_2.2.64^7	 kasmāt go tvasya avayavi samudāya tva anabhyupagamāt na go tvam avayavī na samudāyaḥ samudāyasya bhāgaḥ eka deśa śabdaḥ avayavinaḥ ca avayave yadā na kim cit parihāṇya aśeṣam abhidhīyate tadā avayavinaḥ avayavān apekṣya kṛtsna śabdaḥ samudāye ca samudāyinaḥ apekṣya na ca go tvam avayavī na samudāyaḥ tasmāt na tatra kṛtsna eka deśa śabdau staḥ na ced tatra etau śabdau staḥ tasmāt go tvam kim kārtsnyena vartate uta eka deśena iti na yuktaḥ praśnaḥ uktam ca atra ekam anekatra vartate iti pratijānānaḥ na anuyoktavyaḥ kasmāt ubhayena vyāghātāt iti katham tarhi go tvam goṣu vartate āśraya āśrayi bhāvena kaḥ punar āśraya āśrayi bhāvaḥ samavāyaḥ tatra vṛttimat go tvam vṛttiḥ samavāyaḥ iti ihapratyaya hetu tvāt iti uktam gavya gavi vṛtti abhāvāt iti ced atha manyase yat idam go tvam goṣu anuvṛtti pratyaya kāraṇam tat kim gavi vartate 
NV_2.2.64^8	 āhosvit agavi yadi tāvat gavi prāk go tva yogāt gauḥ eva asau iti vyartham go tvam atha āgavi tena aśva ādi api go tva yogāt gauḥ prāpnoti na ca anyā gatiḥ asti tasmāt na go tvāt anuvṛtti pratyayaḥ iti na vikalpa anabhyupagamāt na gavi go tvam nāgavi prāk go tvāt na asau gauḥ na api agauḥ iti kim kāraṇam ubhau etau viśeṣya pratyayau na ca viśeṣya pratyayau viśeṣaṇa sambandham antareṇa bhavataḥ na ca prāk go tva yogāt vastu vidyate na ca avidyamānam gauḥ iti agauḥ iti vā śakyam vyapadeṣṭum yadā eva vastu tadā eva go tvena abhisambadhyate iti anāspadaḥ vikalpaḥ etena sattā sambandhasya sat asat vikalpaḥ vyākhyātaḥ na sataḥ sattā sambandhaḥ na asataḥ yadā eva vastu tadā eva sat tayā sambadhyate iti sat asat āśraya doṣaḥ anupapannaḥ tasmāt upapannā jātiḥ na ca asau mṛdgavake iti yat abhāvāt tatra asampratyayaḥ sa padārthaḥ iti 
NV_2.2.65	 jāteḥ abhivyaktiḥ ākṛti vyaktī apekṣate vyakti ākṛtī iti prāpte prādhānyāt ākṛteḥ pūrva nipātaḥ kim punar prādhānyam ākṛti viśeṣaṇa tvam vyakteḥ yasmāt vyaktyai ākṛti viśeṣyamāṇāḥ jāteḥ liṅgam bhavati tasmāt pradhānam ākṛtiḥ na ca āgṛhyamāṇāyām ākṛtau vyaktau ca jāti mātram śuddham śabdāt gamyate tasmāt na jātiḥ eva padārthaḥ 
NV_2.2.66^1	 na ca vai padārthena na śakyam bhavitum kaḥ tarhi padārthaḥ vyakti ākṛti jātayaḥ tu padārthaḥ tuśabdaḥ viśeṣaṇa arthaḥ kim viśiṣyate pradhāna upasarjana bhāvasya aniyamena padārtha tvam yadā bheda vivakṣā viśeṣa gatiḥ ca gauḥ tiṣṭḥati gauḥ niṣaṇṇāḥ iti tadā vyaktiḥ padārthaḥ aṅgam jāti ākṛtī jātau ākṛtau ca sthāna gamana asambhavāt yatra sambhavaḥ sa padārthaḥ iti yadā punar bhedaḥ na vivakṣitaḥ sāmānya gatiḥ ca tadā jātiḥ padārthaḥ yathā gauḥ na padā spraṣṭavyāḥ iti ākṛteḥ tu pradhāna bhāvaḥ utprekṣitavyaḥ iti svayam utprekṣya iti ayam arthaḥ 
NV_2.2.66^2	 kva punar ākṛteḥ prādhānyam dṛṣṭam yathā piṣṭaka mayaḥ gāvaḥ kriyantām iti tat etat bahulam prayogeṣu pradhāna upasarjana bhāvaḥ svayam utprekṣya iti na vyakti ākṛti jātayaḥ padārthaḥ iti ke cit kutas vikalpa anupapatteḥ sat iti etat eva vyāpaka tvāt upādāya cintyate sat iti anena padena jātiḥ vai abhidhīyate piṇḍaḥ vā sambandhaḥ vā jātimān vā arthaḥ tatra na tāvat jātiḥ abhidhīyate bheda arthaiḥ abhinna vibhaktika tvāt yadi ayam jāti vācakaḥ sat śabdaḥ bhavati sat dravyam iti bheda vācinā dravya śabdena sāmānya adhikaraṇyam na prāpnoti 
NV_2.2.66^3	 na hi bhinna artha vācakānām śabdānām sāmānya adhikaraṇyam paśyāmaḥ na hi gavāśvam iti sāmānya adhikaraṇyam dṛṣṭam iti atha dravya ādi vṛtti tvāt sattāyāḥ dravya ādi śabdaiḥ saha sāmānādhikaraṇyam tathā api pāratantryāt sattā guṇaḥ guṇī abhidhāyinoḥ ca śabdayoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyam yathā śaṅkhasya śauklyam iti etena sambandhaḥ vyākhyātaḥ sat śabdaḥ piṇḍānām vācakaḥ bhavati iti na yuktam piṇḍānām ānantyāt na hi ekasya sat śabdasya anekena dravya guṇa karma prapañcena sambandhaḥ ākhyātum śakyaḥ 
NV_2.2.66^4	 na ca anākhyāte śabda artha sambandhe śabdāt artha pratipattiḥ yuktā sva rūpa mātra pratīteḥ vyabhicārāt ca sat śabda śravaṇāt dravya guṇa karmāṇi iti pariplavate buddhiḥ na ca yasmāt abhidhānāt pariplavate buddhiḥ tad abhidhānam iti yuktam vaktum tasmāt na sat śabdaḥ bhedānām vācakaḥ jātimat mātrā abhidhāyakaḥ api sat śabdaḥ na bhavati kasmāt asvatantra tvāt na hi sat śabdāt tad bhedāḥ ghaṭa ādayaḥ gamyante iti tad gata ghaṭa ādi bhedān ākṣepāt sāmānādhikaraṇya abhāvaḥ atha vā asvatantra tvāt iti sat śabdaḥ prādhānyena sattāyām vartate tatra vartamānaḥ tadvat iti upacaryate 
NV_2.2.66^5	 yat ca yatra vartamānam anyatra upacaryate na tat tasya abhidhāyakam yuktam mañca śabda vat iti uktam ca atra kim uktam tadvatām ānantyāt na sat śabdena abhidhānam yuktam iti tadvati ca na guṇa sārūpyāt pratyaya saṅkrāntiḥ yathā svāmi śabdasya bhṛtye na guṇa uparāgāt yathā nīlaḥ sphaṭikaḥ iti krama vṛtti abhāvāt ca yugapad a sambhavāt ca ayathārtha jñāna utpatti prasaṅgāt ca tasmāt na jātimat mātrā abhidhāyakaḥ api asādhāraṇa viśeṣa abhidhāyakaḥ bhaviṣyati iti na yuktam anyatra pratyaya abhāva prasaṅgāt na ca anyā gatiḥ asti tasmāt anya artha apoha kṛta śrutiḥ iti anya śabda artha antara apoham sva arthe kurvatī śrutiḥ abhidhatte iti atra asmābhiḥ vyakti ākṛti jātayaḥ padārthaḥ iti pradhāna upasarjana bhāvasya aniyamena vyavasthāpitam ekānta vādinaḥ ca ete doṣāḥ iti na ca ete doṣāḥ katham iti yat tāvat sattā śabdaḥ sattāyāḥ na vācakaḥ iti tat na vyāghātāt sattā śabdaḥ na sattāyāḥ vācakaḥ iti vyāhatam ucyate katham ca tad avācaka tve sati sattā śabdaḥ iti abhidhīyate bhavat abhiprāyeṇa abhidhīyate iti ced 
NV_2.2.66^6	 atha manyase naḥ eva naḥ kṛtānte sattā ādi śabdāḥ santi kim tu bhavadbhiḥ sattā śabdaḥ dravya guṇa karma śabdāḥ iti ca parikalpya vyavahāraḥ kriyate tatas asmābhiḥ api yuṣmad abhiprāya anuvidhānena sattā śabdāḥ iti vācaḥ uccaryante iti na vyāghāta anivṛtteḥ sat iti evam ādīni padāni loka prasiddhāni tāni keṣu artheṣu vartante iti ubhayoḥ vicāraḥ vayam tu brūmaḥ sattā śabdaḥ sattāyām vartate tvam punar bravīṣi sattā śabdaḥ na sattāyām iti evam bruvāṇaḥ mayā virodhena pratyavasthīyase virodha uddhāram ca anuktvā tu anmatyāḥ mayā abhidhīyate iti brūvāṇaḥ na vyāghātam ativartase 
NV_2.2.66^7	 yat ca idam ucyate tvayā parikalpitāḥ sattā ādi śabdāḥ iti tat api na parikalpya viṣaya anabhidhānāt parikalpyasya viṣayaḥ atathābhūtasya tathā bhāvibhiḥ sāmānye sati adhyāropita tad dharmaṇaḥ pradhāna artha pratipattiḥ yathā sthāṇau puruṣaḥ iti yadi ca amī sattā ādi śabdāḥ parikalpitāḥ bhavanti pradhānam eṣām vācyam na hi niṣpradhānam parikalpyam paśyāmaḥ iti yat punar etat bheda arthaiḥ abhinna vibhaktika tvāt iti tat na samāna artha aparijñānāt na brūmaḥ sattā ādi śabdena dravya śabdasya sāmānādhikaraṇyam api tu sattāyāḥ pradhāna sādhana vācinā sat śabdena dravya guṇa karmāṇi abhidhīyante dravya guṇa karma śabdaiḥ api itaretara viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva āpannaiḥ tāni 
NV_2.2.66^8	 evam sati yuktam sāmānādhikaraṇyam ubhayoḥ sat dravya śabdayoḥ eka viṣaya tvāt yadā punar ayam sattā śabdaḥ sattā pradhānaḥ eva aṅga bhūtam sādhanam abhidhatte na tadā sāmānādhikaraṇyam dravyasya sattā iti bhavati tasmāt sāmānādhikaraṇya anupapattiḥ adoṣaḥ vibhakti bheda niyamāt guṇa guṇī abhidhāyinoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyasya asiddhiḥ sat dravya śabdayoḥ iti etat anena pratyuktam etena sambandhaḥ vyākhyātaḥ katham iti na sat śabdena sambandhaḥ abhidhīyate api tu sambandha śabdena eva sambandhaḥ ca guṇaḥ tad śabdaḥ guṇa śabdaḥ 
NV_2.2.66^9	 na ca guṇa śabdena dravya vācinaḥ śabdasya sāmānādhikaraṇyam asti iti yat punar etat ānatyāt na jāti śabdaḥ bhedānām vācakaḥ iti svayam prakptām vācoyuktim bhavān pratiṣedhati kaḥ ca evam āha jāti śabdaḥ bhedānām vācakaḥ iti yadi tarhi jāti śabdaḥ na bhedānām vācakaḥ katham sat śabdena dravya guṇa karmāṇi abhidhīyante na ayam bhoḥ sat śabdaḥ jāti śabdaḥ api tu bheda śabdaḥ eva ayam bheda śabdena ca bhedāḥ abhidhīyante iti na kim cit bādhyate katham na bādhyate yadā sat śabdaḥ ekaḥ bhedānām ānantyam tad avastham eva na ca ekasya anekena sambandhaḥ śakyaḥ ākhyātum 
NV_2.2.66^10	 na ca anākhyāte śabda artha sambandhe śabda artha pratipattiḥ yuktāḥ iti na kevalānām anabhidhānāt yaḥ hi sat śabdena nirviśeṣaṇāni dravya guṇa karmāṇi abhidhīyante iti abhidhatte tam prati eṣaḥ doṣaḥ asmākam tu dravya guṇa karmāṇi sattā viśeṣaṇāni abhidhīyante yatra yatra sattām paśyati tatra tatra sat śabdam prayuṅkte ekā ca sattā tad pratyayasya anuvṛtteḥ tasmāt bhedānām ānantyam na doṣaḥ kaḥ ca ayam evambhūtaḥ sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ śabdam pakṣayasi ānantyāt iti vastu dharmam hetu tvena abhidhatse iti 
NV_2.2.66^11	 atha bhedāḥ eva jāti dharma śava acyatvena pakṣīkriyante tathā api na anvayī na vyatirekī dṛṣṭāntaḥ asti iti ahetuḥ ānantyāt iti atha api eka deśān pakṣīkritya ānantyāt iti hetuḥ śeṣaḥ eka deśaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti ayam api na virodhāt evam ca sati na kaḥ cit padārthaḥ vācyaḥ na kaḥ cit śabdaḥ vācakaḥ iti vācya vācaka bhāva nivṛttau viśeṣaṇam anarthakam ete na vācyāḥ ete na vācakāḥ iti yat punar etat vyabhicārāt iti na vyabhicāra viṣaya aparijñānāt vyabhicārī hi nāma sa jñeyaḥ yaḥ sva viṣaya tajjātīya vṛtti tve sati anyatra vartate na punar ayam sat śabdaḥ sva viṣaya vyatirekeṇa asati vartate 
NV_2.2.66^12	 tasmāt asthāne vyabhicāra codanāḥ iti hetu bhāva anabhyupagamāt ca kena ca atra hetuḥ abhidhīyate dravyam guṇaḥ karma vā sattvāt iti tasmāt ayuktam etat api bheda vācaka tva pratiṣedhāt sat dravya śabdayoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyam iti na vaktavyam vyāghātāt na ca kaḥ cit śabdaḥ dravya vācakaḥ dravya sat śabdayoḥ ca sāmānādhikaraṇyam iti vyāhatam yat punar etat na tadvatas asvatantra tvāt iti na kila sat śabdena tad bhedāḥ ghaṭa ādayaḥ gamyante tad gata ghaṭa ādi bhedān ākṣepāt sāmānādhikaraṇya abhāvaḥ iti tat naḥ ukta uttara tvāt 
NV_2.2.66^13	 ukta uttaram etat sat dravya śabdayoḥ eka viṣaya tvāt sāmānādhikaraṇyam iti tad gata ghaṭa ādi bhedān ākṣepaḥ iti ca na yuktam sat śabdena sattā sādhanānām dravya guṇa karmaṇām ākṣepāt sattā śabdena dravya guṇa karmāṇi naḥ ākṣipyante na punar sat śabdena śakyam vaktum sattā śabdena api guṇa bhūtāni gamyante iti sat iti ca ayam abhidhāna śabdaḥ kaḥ tasya abhidheyaḥ yaḥ asmāt pratīyate sa tasya arthaḥ iti kaḥ asya arthaḥ sa vibhajyate sattā tad yogaḥ artha antaram iti trayaḥ arthāḥ tat pradhāna upasarjana bhāvasya aniyamena vivakṣāyām pradhānam sādhanam gamyate aṅgam sattā ca tad yogaḥ ca 
NV_2.2.66^14	 kimkṛtaḥ pradhāna aṅga bhāvaḥ artha kṛtaḥ yadā satā kim cit kurvati tadā sattā viśeṣaṇam padārtham upādāya kim cit karoti yena karoti tad pradhānam aṅgam apradhānam pratyaya hetu tvāt yasmāt sat tayā padārthaḥ viśiṣyate aṅga hīne pratyaya nivṛtteḥ yatra tad aṅgam sattā ādikam na asti tatra na sat iti pratyayaḥ tat evam tad gata ghaṭa ādi bhedān ākṣepāt iti ayuktam yat punar etat sat śabdaḥ sattāyām prādhānyena vartate tatra vartamānaḥ tadvatī upacaryate iti tat na sat śabda viṣaya aparijñānāt na bhavatā sat śabdasya viṣayaḥ vyajñāyi 
NV_2.2.66^15	 kaḥ evam āha sat śabdaḥ sattāyām prādhānyena vartate iti yathā ca sat śabdasya dravya guṇa karmāṇi sattā sādhana bhāvāt viṣayaḥ iti tathā uktam etena bhedānām ānantyam pratyuktam sat śabdasya viṣayaḥ sattā sādhanam viṣayaḥ ca sattā sādhana bhūtaḥ ekaḥ eva iti yat punar etat tadvati ca na guṇa sārūpyāt pratyaya saṅkrāntiḥ yathā svāmi śabdasya bhṛtyaḥ iti asya arthaḥ svāmi anukāri tvāt bhṛtye svāmi śabdaḥ iti etat tu na buddhyāmahe pratyayānām saṅkrāntiḥ iti yadi svāmi pratyaya viṣaya tvam tat na pratyaya saṅkrāntiḥ na hi svāmi pratyayaḥ bhṛtyasya bhavati 
NV_2.2.66^16	 kevalam guru tām vā priya tām vā paśyan svāmi śabdam guṇa bhūtam tatra prayuṅkte yathā ca bhṛtyaḥ svāmi artha kāri tvāt svāmī iti ucyate na punar evam sattā śabdaḥ kadā cit api dravya ādiṣu vartate iti yadā tu satām bhāvaḥ sattā iti satām sattā viśeṣaka tvāt guṇa bhūtānām sattā śabdena abhidhānam viśeṣaka tvam upacāraḥ etena eva guṇa uparāgāt yathā nīlaḥ sphaṭikaḥ iti pratyuktam yat punar etat krama vṛtti abhāvāt yugapad a sambhavāt ca iti asya arthaḥ sattā śabdaḥ kila sattāyām varti tvāt tadvati vartate iti na ca evam paśyāmaḥ yugapad api na sambhavati 
NV_2.2.66^17	 sattā pratyayaḥ ca dravya pratyayaḥ ca na yugapad bhavataḥ etat api na ukta uttara tvāt ukta uttaram etat na atra kramaḥ na yugapad pratyayaḥ sat pratyayasya sādhana viṣaya tvāt etena ayatha artha jñāna utpatti prasaṅgāt iti pratyuktam evam hi kuhetu pradhāna nirāsāt vyavasthitam vyakti ākṛti jātayaḥ padārthaḥ iti na jāti śabdaḥ bhedānām vācakaḥ iti viśeṣaṇa ānarthakyam na hi kaḥ cit śabdaḥ bhavatā bhedānām vacaka tvena abhyupagamyate viśeṣaṇam hi nāma viśeṣye sati sāmānya pratipattau ca na ca asya kim cit viśeṣyam asti na ca jāti śabdasya kaḥ cit padārthaḥ vācyaḥ abhyupagamyate 
NV_2.2.66^18	 tasmāt viśeṣaṇa ānarthakyam virodhāt ca yadi ca ayam jāti śabdaḥ bhedānām vācakaḥ abhaviṣyat api tarhi jāti śabdaḥ eva na abhaviṣyat na hi anya padārtha vācakānām śabdānām tad śabda tvam sambhavati katham ca bheda vācaka tve sati jāti śabdaḥ iti ucyate yat ca ucyate na jāti sabdaḥ bhedānām vācakaḥ iti tathā tat kaḥ hi svastha ātmā jāti śabda vācyān bhedān abhyupaiti yadi ca jāti śabda vācyāḥ bhedāḥ na bhavanti anya śabda vācyāḥ tarhi bhedāḥ prāpnuvanti 
NV_2.2.66^19	 atha anya śabda vācyāḥ api bhedāḥ na bhavanti tena na jāti sabda vācyāḥ na anya śabda vācyāḥ iti ubhayathā avācya tve kim asya viśeṣaṇasya sāmarthyam na jāti śabdaḥ bhedānām vācakaḥ iti atas evam vaktavyam avācyāḥ bhedāḥ avācakāḥ śabdāḥ iti atha manyase paramata vyapekṣayā etat ucyate na jāti śabdaḥ bhedānām vācakaḥ iti na anabhyupagamāt na hi kaḥ cit tantrikaḥ asti yaḥ jāti śabda vācyān bhedān pratipadyate jāteḥ api avācaka tve vyāghātaḥ jāti śabdaḥ iti na hi yaḥ yasya avācakaḥ sa tad śabdaḥ iti śakyam vaktum na jāti śabdaḥ bhedānām vācakaḥ iti kasya tarhi vācakaḥ bheda vācaka tva pratiṣedhāt anya vācaka tvam āyātam 
NV_2.2.66^20	 atha anya vācaka tvam api naḥ iṣyate vyartham viśeṣaṇam jāti sabdaḥ bhedānām na vācakaḥ iti sarve eva ca śabdāḥ arthānām na vācakāḥ iti yuktam vaktum atha avācakāḥ śabdāḥ avācyāḥ padārthāḥ iti ayuktam ca etat vyāghātāt avācakāḥ śabdāḥ bhavanti avācaka tvam ca śabdānām śabdaiḥ eva pratipādyate iti avācaka tve ca śabdānām pratijñā hetvoḥ vyāghātaḥ na jāti sabdaḥ bhedānām vācakaḥ iti pratijnnāḥ hetuḥ ānantyāt iti ubhayam ca vacana ātmakam iti ubhayasya avācaka tvāt vyāghātaḥ śabdān ca āvācakān pratipadyamānena laukika pratipādana upāyaḥ anyaḥ vaktavyaḥ 
NV_2.2.66^21	 anyathā abhyupagate iti ced atha manyase na mayā avācakāḥ śabdāḥ abhyupagamyante na api arthāḥ avācyāḥ api tu yaḥ bhavadbhiḥ vācya vācaka nyāyaḥ abhyupagamyate saḥ asmābhiḥ nirākriyate asmākam tu śabdena anya apoha lakṣaṇā jātiḥ abhidhīyate iti viśiṣya vaktavyam yadi anyathā śabdāḥ arthānām vācakāḥ bhavanti viśiṣya vaktavyam asmad prakpta jāti ādi vyatirekeṇa jāti ādi śabdāḥ na jāti ādīnām na vācakāḥ iti svarūpa anabhidhānāt ca na ca samāna pratyaya kāraṇa tā vyatirekeṇa jāteḥ svarūpam nirdeṣṭum śakyam na ca anuvṛtti pratyayaḥ pratyākhyātum śakyaḥ 
NV_2.2.66^22	 na ca viśeṣa pratyayena akasmāt śakyam bhavitum yatas ayam pratyayaḥ sā jātiḥ iti nāmni vivādaḥ evam tāvat yathāśruti vākye doṣaḥ atha jāti śabda avācya tvena bhedāḥ eva pakṣīkriyante etasmin api pratijñā arthe yāvantaḥ ete vākya doṣāḥ te sarve prasajyante iti evam eka deśa pakṣīkaraṇe api viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva anupapatteḥ pūrva doṣa anuvṛttiḥ yat api idam ucyate sat dravya śabdayoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyam iti tat api na vyāghātāt dravya sat śabdayoḥ ca sāmānādhikaraṇyam na ca bheda vācakāḥ śabdāḥ iti vyāhatam upacārataḥ na vyāghātaḥ iti ced 
NV_2.2.66^23	 atha manyase sat dravya śabdau iti upacārataḥ abhidhīyete katham iti dravya śabdena adravya vyudāsaḥ sat śabdena asat vyudāsaḥ tau etau asat dravya vyudāsa rūpeṇa pravartamānau ekam artham brute iti samāna adhikaraṇau iti ucyate mukhyatas tu na kaḥ cit vidhānataḥ śabdaḥ vācakaḥ iti na mukhyā sambhavāt mukhyatas sat dravya śabda prayoge sati tena sāmānyāt atathābhūte upacāraḥ iti yuktam vaktum na tu evam vādinām pradhānam asti na ca pradhānam antareṇa upacāraḥ sambhavati na ca anya apoha pakṣe upacāraḥ yuktaḥ ubhayoḥ pradhāna śabda tvāt 
NV_2.2.66^24	 yathā siṃha śabdaḥ siṃhe vartate asiṃha rūpa vyudāsena tathā māṇavake api iti tulya rūpa tvāt tasmāt naḥ upacāraḥ iti yat punar etat anya śabda artha apohaḥ śabda arthaḥ iti tat api ayuktam vidhānataḥ śabda artha asambhave sati ādya apratipatteḥ yadi vidhānataḥ śabda arthaḥ bhavati tatas vidhīyamāna śabda artha pratipattau satyām tasya anyatra pratiṣedhaḥ iti upapannaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ yasya punar vidhīyamānaḥ padārthaḥ na asti tasya ādyām pratipattim antareṇa katham pratiṣedhaḥ yāvat ca itarat na pratipadyate tāvat itarat na pratiṣedhati iti 
NV_2.2.66^25	 yathā gauḥ iti padasya arthaḥ agauḥ na bhavati yāvat ca agām na pratipadyate na tāvat gavi pratipattiḥ yuktā yāvat ca gām na pratipadyate tāvat agavi iti ubhaya pratipatti abhāvaḥ yaḥ ca ayam anya apohaḥ agauḥ na bhavati iti go śabdasya arthaḥ sa kim bhāvaḥ atha abhāvaḥ iti yadi bhāvaḥ kim gauḥ agauḥ iti yadi gauḥ na asti vivādaḥ atha agauḥ go śabdasya agauḥ arthaḥ iti aho śabda artha kauśalam atha abhāvaḥ tat na yuktam praiṣa sampratipattyoḥ aviṣaya tvāt na hi go śabda śrāvaṇāt abhāve praiṣaḥ na vā sampratipattiḥ śabda arthaḥ ca pratipatrā pratīyate 
NV_2.2.66^26	 na ca go śabdāt abhāvam kaḥ cit pratipadyate iti anya apohaḥ ca śabda arthaḥ iti ayuktam avyāpaka tvāt yatra dvairāśyam bhavati tatra itara pratiṣedhāt itarat pratīyate yathā gauḥ iti pade gauḥ pratīyamānaḥ agauḥ pratiṣidhyamānaḥ na punar sarva pade etat asti na hi asarvam nāma kim cit asti yat sarva śabdena nivartyeta eka ādi vyudāsāt vyāpaka tvam iti ced atha manyase eka ādi a sarvam tat sarva śabdena nivartyate tat na sva artha apavāda doṣa prasaṅgāt evam sati eka ādi vyudāsena pravartamānaḥ sarva śabdaḥ aṅgasya pratiṣedhāt aṅga vyatiriktasya ca aṅginaḥ anabhyupagamāt anarthakaḥ syāt 
NV_2.2.66^27	 evam sarve samudāya śabdāḥ eka deśa pratiṣedha rūpeṇa pravartamānāḥ samudāyi vyatirikta samudāya anabhyupagamāt anarthakāḥ prāpnuvanti dvi ādi śabdānām ca samuccaya viṣaya tvāt eka ādi pratiṣedhe pratiṣidhyamānānām asamuccayāt dvi ādi śabdānām anarthaka tvam kriyā rūpa tvāt ca apohasya viṣayaḥ vaktavyaḥ agauḥ na bhavati iti ayam apohaḥ kim go viṣayaḥ atha ago viṣayaḥ iti yadi go viṣayaḥ katham goḥ gavi eva abhāvaḥ atha ago viṣayaḥ katham anya viṣayāt apohāt anyatra pratipattiḥ na hi khadire chidyamāne palāśe chidā bhavati 
NV_2.2.66^28	 atha āgoḥ gavi pratiṣedhaḥ agauḥ gauḥ na bhavati iti kena goḥ ago tvam prasañjitam yat pratiṣidhyate katham ca agavi goḥ pratipattim antareṇa pratiṣedhaḥ na hi uttara padārtha pratipattim antareṇa pratiṣedham paśyāmaḥ iti uktam ca atra ādyā pratipattiḥ na prāpnoti iti ādi pratipattim ca antareṇa na pratiṣedhaḥ iti itas ca na yuktaḥ apohaḥ arthaḥ vikalpa anupapatteḥ yaḥ ayam apohaḥ gavi sa kim goḥ vyatiriktaḥ āhosvit avyatiriktaḥ iti yadi vyatiriktaḥ kim āśritaḥ anāśritaḥ vā iti yadi āśritaḥ āśrita tvāt guṇaḥ iti go śabdena guṇaḥ abhidhīyate na gauḥ iti gauḥ tiṣṭhati iti sāmānādhikaraṇyam na prāptam 
NV_2.2.66^29	 atha anāśritaḥ kena arthena ṣaṣṭhī goḥ apohaḥ iti atha avyatiriktaḥ gauḥ eva asau iti na kim cit kṛtam bhavati ayam ca apohaḥ prativastu ekaḥ anekaḥ vā iti vaktavyam yadi ekaḥ aneka go sambandhī ca go tvam tat iti atha anekaḥ tatas piṇḍa vat ānantyāt ākhyāna anupapatteḥ artha pratyayaḥ api na yuktaḥ idam ca tāvat praṣṭavyaḥ bhavān kim ayam apohaḥ vācyaḥ atha avācyaḥ iti yadi vācyaḥ anaikāntikaḥ śabda arthaḥ anya apohaḥ śabdasya arthaḥ iti anavasthā vā yadi anapoha vyudāsa rūpeṇa abhidhīyate apohaḥ tasya api anyaḥ iti anavasthā 
NV_2.2.66^30	 atha avācyaḥ anya śabda artha apoham karoti iti vyāhatam yadi ca śabdasya apohaḥ nābhidheyaḥ arthaḥ abhidheya arthavytirekeṇa sva arthaḥ vaktavyaḥ atha saḥ eva asya sva arthaḥ tathā api vyāhatam anya śabda antara artha apoham sva arthe kurvatī śrutiḥ abhidhatte iti ucyate iti asya vākyasya ayam arthaḥ tadānīm bhavati anyat anabhidhānaḥ abhidhatte iti anekam iti ca asya padasya dvi ādi viṣaya tvāt sāmānya gatau viśeṣaḥ āśrayitavyaḥ na hi asati viśeṣa āśrayaṇe sāmānya śabdāt viśeṣa pratipattiḥ yuktāḥ iti 
NV_2.2.66^31	 nīlotpala śabdayoḥ ca pradhāna tvāt viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva anupapattau viśeṣaṇasya pūrva nipātaḥ iti ubhayoḥ pradhāna tvāt na prāptaḥ etena rāja puruṣa śabdau vyākhyātau samāna adhikaraṇa arthaḥ ca anya apoha vādinā vācyaḥ yasya ca anya apohaḥ śabda arthaḥ tena anīla anutpala vyudāsau katham samāna adhikaraṇau iti vācyam yasya punar vidhīyamānaḥ śabda arthaḥ tasya jāti guṇa viśiṣṭam nīlotpala śabdābhyām dravyam ucyate jāti guṇau ca dravye vartete na punar anīla an utpala vyudāsau tasmāt samāna adhikaraṇa arthaḥ na asti iti tat evam anya apohaḥ yathā yathā vikalpyate tathā tathā pramāṇa vṛttam bādhate iti 
NV_2.2.67^1	 katham punar jñāyate nānā vyakti ākṛti jātayaḥ iti adhigata tvāt praśna anupapattiḥ iti ced adhigatāḥ vyakti ākṛti jātayaḥ yā śabda ādi sūtraiḥ adhigata tvāt praśnaḥ anupapannaḥ na nimitta traividhye sati tad viśeṣa viṣaya jñāpana artha tvāt praśnasya go śabdaḥ uccaryamāṇaḥ pradhāna upasarjana bhāvena nimitta trayam pratipādayati iti yā śabda ādi sūtrāṇām arthaḥ evam ca sati tad viśeṣa viṣaya jñāpana artham yuktaḥ praśnaḥ katamā atra vyaktiḥ katama ākṛtiḥ katamā jātiḥ iti vyakti ākṛti jātīnām bhedaḥ lakṣaṇa bhedāt 
NV_2.2.67^2	 kim punar vyakteḥ lakṣaṇam iti vyakteḥ lakṣaṇa pratipādana artham vyaktiḥ guṇa viśeṣa āśrayaḥ mūrtiḥ iti sūtram tatra vyajyate iti vyaktiḥ indriya grāhyāḥ iti yat dravyam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam sparśa paryantānām guṇānām āśrayaḥ tat mūrcchita avayava tvāt mūrtiḥ iti ca ucyate vyaktiḥ iti ca etat tu na buddhyāmahe kim idam avayavi dravyasya lakṣaṇam āho padārtha tvena trayāṇām prasaktānām jāti ākṛti vyavacchedakam vyakti lakṣaṇam iti vayam tu brūmaḥ na atra avayavī vyavacchedyaḥ api tu jāti ākṛti pada vyatiriktasya vyakti padasya arthaḥ vaktavyaḥ iti 
NV_2.2.67^3	 sā ca vyaktiḥ yā na ākṛtiḥ na jātiḥ tasyāḥ anena sūtreṇa saṃgrahaḥ vyaktiḥ guṇa viśeṣa āśrayaḥ mūrtiḥ iti guṇa viśeṣāḥ ca tad āśrayaḥ ca atra tad śabda lopāt guṇa viśeṣa āśraya śabdena dravyam ucyate karma api guṇa viśeṣa śabdāt labhyate guṇebhyaḥ viśeṣaḥ guṇa viśeṣaḥ iti guṇa viśeṣa grahaṇam kim artham guṇa śabdena saṃgṛhītāyāḥ ākṛteḥ nirākaraṇa artham ākṛtiḥ saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ sā ca guṇa grahaṇena gṛhyate tat nirākaraṇa artham guṇa viśeṣa grahaṇam guṇa viśeṣaḥ iti ca atra dvi rūpaḥ vigrahaḥ guṇāḥ ca te viśeṣāḥ iti ca guṇebhyaḥ ca viśeṣāḥ iti ca 
NV_2.2.67^4	 āśraya samāna adhikaraṇaḥ mūrti śabdaḥ dravye mūrcchate iti mūrti śabdena dravyam ucyate evam ca pratipadam vyakti lakṣaṇam sidhyati evam ca rūpa ādi ākāśa ādi avarodhaḥ yadi ca pratipadam vyakti lakṣaṇam sidhyati evam ca rūpa ādi ākāśa ādi avarodhaḥ yadi pratipadam etat vyakti lakṣaṇam bhavati tatas rūpa ādayaḥ ca ākāśa ādayaḥ ca vyāpyate anyathā tu lakṣaṇam avyāpakam syāt atha vā guṇa viśeṣāṇām āśrayaḥ iti guṇāḥ ca viśeṣāḥ ca guṇa viśeṣāḥ teṣām āśrayaḥ dravyam tatra mūrcchate iti rūpa ādayaḥ api mūrtiḥ 
NV_2.2.68	 jātiḥ jāti liṅgāni ca prakhyāyante yayā tām ākṛtim vidyāt sā ca na anyā sattva avayavānām tad avayavānām ca niyatāt vyūhāt niyata avayava vyūhāḥ khalu avayavāḥ jātim anumāpayanti śiraḥ pāṇi ādi mad a ākāra sāmānyena go tvam vyajyate śiraḥ pāṇi ādīnām ca avayavānām avayava viśeṣa darśanena kadācid punar iyam ākṛtiḥ padārtha tvam jahāti kva punar jahāti yatra ākṛti vyaṅgyā jātiḥ na bhavati yathā mṛd suvarṇam rajatam iti ākṛtau niyamaḥ na jātau sarva ākṛtiḥ jāti liṅgaym iti na punar sarvā jātiḥ ākṛtyai 
NV_2.2.69	 yayā bhinnāni anekāni vastūni itaretarataḥ anuvṛtti vyāvṛtti pratyaya hetu bhāvena vyavatiṣṭḥante sā jātiḥ yathā imāni kuṇḍāni iti anuvartante naḥ imāni kuṇḍāni iti vyāvartante tat ekam sannimittam anuvṛtti vyāvṛtti kāraṇam yat tat sāmānya viśeṣaḥ sā jātiḥ iti samāna pratyaya utpatti kāraṇam jātiḥ iti jātau niyamaḥ na samāna pratyaya utpattau jātim antareṇa api dṛṣṭa tvāt jātim antareṇa api samāna pratyayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yathā pāca kākiṣu tasmāt vyavasthitam vyakti ākṛti jātayaḥ padārthaḥ iti gavā ādiṣu anuvṛtti pratyayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ piṇḍavyariktāt nimittāt bhavati viśeṣavat tvāt nīla ādi pratyaya vat iti gotaḥ artha antaram go tvam bhinna pratyaya viṣaya tvāt rūpa sparśa pratyaya vat gotaḥ artha antaram go tvam vyapadeśa śabda viṣaya tvāt caitra aśva vat goḥ go tva anuvṛtti pratyayaḥ bhinna nimittaḥ viśeṣavat tvāt rūpa ādi pratyaya vat iti saṃśayasya pramāṇānām vicāraḥ tad vyavasthitiḥ śabdasya tattvam prāmāṇyam padārthāḥ ca iha kīrtitāḥ 
NV_3.1.1^1	 ānantaryāt prameya parīkṣā yat viṣayaḥ ahaṅkāraḥ saṃsāram pratanoti yat viṣayam ca samyak jñānam saṃsāra nivṛtti hetuḥ bhavati tadā anantaryāt parīkṣyate tat ca ātma ādi iti ātmā vicāryate kim punar asya vicāryam kim śarīra indriya manaḥ buddhi vyatiriktaḥ āho naḥ iti na dharmya prasiddheḥ vyatireka avyatirekau ātma dharmau sati dharmiṇi dharmau bhavataḥ iti dharmī ca atra aprasiddhaḥ na ca aprasiddhe dharmiṇi dharmayoḥ vicāraḥ yuktaḥ tasmāt dharmī eva tāvat pratipādyatām iti na icchā ādi sūtrāt ātma prasiddheḥ icchā ādi sūtre ātma sadbhāvaḥ pratipāditaḥ pratipādita tvāt anantaraḥ dharma vicāraḥ yuktaḥ iti 
NV_3.1.1^2	 avipratipatteḥ ca na hi kaḥ cit vādī ātma sattve vipratipadyate kim tu viśeṣe vipratipadyate iti śarīra mātram ātmā indriya mātram ātmā buddhi ādayaḥ ātmā saṅghātaḥ ātmā tad vyatiriktaḥ ātmā iti iyam ca dharma viśeṣe vipratipattiḥ apratipanna ātma sattvānām na yuktāḥ iti yuktaḥ dharma vicāraḥ asattva pratipādaka pramāṇa asambhavāt ca na ca ātmā sattva pratipādakam pramāṇam asti iti atas ca sadbhāve na vipratipadyate iti na na asti ajāta tvāt iti eke na asti ātmā ajāta tvāt śaśa viṣāṇa vat iti tatra na asti ātmā iti pade tāvat vyāhate nāsti śabda samāna adhikaraṇaḥ ayam ātma śabdaḥ naḥ ātmanaḥ asattvam pratipādayati 
NV_3.1.1^3	 kim kāraṇam ātmā iti vastu abhidhīyate na asti iti tasya pratiṣedhaḥ yat ca yatra pratiṣidhyate tat tasmāt anyatra asti iti yathā nāstinā samāna adhikaraṇaḥ ghaṭa śabdaḥ na ghaṭa abhāvam pratipādayitum śaknoti api tu deśa kāla viśeṣe pratiṣedhaḥ na asti ghaṭaḥ iti deśa viśeṣe vā pratiṣedhaḥ gehe na asti iti kāla viśeṣe vā pratiṣedhaḥ idānīm na asti iti prāk na asti ūrdhvam na asti iti sarvaḥ ca ayam pratiṣedhaḥ na anabhyupagata ghaṭa sattvasya yuktaḥ tathā na asti ātmā iti kim ayam deśa viśeṣe pratiṣidhyate uta kāla viśeṣe iti yadi tāvat deśa viśeṣe pratiṣiddhaḥ saḥ ātmani na yuktaḥ adeśa tvāt ātmanaḥ 
NV_3.1.1^4	 na ca deśa viśeṣa pratiṣedhāt ātmā pratiṣiddhaḥ bhavati atha ayam bhavatām abhiprāyaḥ śarīram ātmā na bhavati iti kasya vā śarīram ātmā yam prati pratiṣedhaḥ śarīre na asti ātmā iti evam pratiṣedhaḥ iti ced kasya vā śarīre ātmā yam prati pratiṣedhaḥ iti kva tarhi ayam ātmā na kva cit ātmā kim ayam na asti eva na na asti viśeṣa pratiṣedhāt kā iyam vācoyuktiḥ na ca śarīram na ca śarīre ca anyatra na ca na asti eṣā eṣā vacaḥ yuktiḥ yat yathābhūtam tat tathā nirdiśyate iti na ca ayam ātmā kva cit api iti tasmāt tathā eva nirdeśaḥ na ca kāla viśeṣa pratiṣedhaḥ api yuktaḥ ātmani traikālyasya anabhivyakteḥ 
NV_3.1.1^5	 na hi ātmani traikālyam abhivyajyate nitya tvāt nityaḥ ātmā iti upariṣṭāt pūrva abhyasta sūtre pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ tasmāt na kāla viśeṣa pratiṣedhaḥ api asti iti ātma pratiṣedham ca kurvāṇena ātma śabdasya viṣayaḥ vaktavyaḥ na hi ekam padam nirathakam paśyāmaḥ atha api śarīra ādi viṣayam ātma śabdam pratipadyethāḥ evam api anivṛttaḥ vyāghātaḥ katham iti na asti ātmā iti asya vākyasya tadānīm ayam arthaḥ bhavati śarīra ādayaḥ na santi iti atha yam bhavantaḥ ātmānam kalpayanti sa na asti iti na vayam ātmānam kalpayāmaḥ kalpanā hi nāma atathā bhūtasya tathā bhāvibhiḥ sāmānyāt tad dharma adhyāropeṇa tad pratyayaḥ 
NV_3.1.1^6	 na ca ātmānam evambhūtam pratipadyāmahe yam bhavantaḥ ātmānam kalpayanti iti ca bruvāṇaḥ bhavān praṣṭavyaḥ jāyate katham vayam ātmānam kalpayāmaḥ iti kim sattvena atha asattvena vā yadi sattvena kim asataḥ satā sādharmyam yena kalpanā viṣayaḥ ātmā ātma sāmānyam ca anātmanaḥ bruvatā ātmā abhyupagataḥ bhavati na hi asataḥ satā sāmānyam asti atha śarīra ādi viṣayam ahaṅkāram ātmani kalpayitvā viparyeti evam ca śarīra ādi vyatirikta ahaṅkāra viṣaya sattva abhyupagamāt anivṛttaḥ vyāghātaḥ atha manyase eka padasya na avaśyam arthena bhavitavyam iti yathā śūnyam tamaḥ iti ca tat na vyāghāta anivṛtteḥ 
NV_3.1.1^7	 śūnya śabdasya tāvat ayam arthaḥ yasya rakṣitā dravyasya na vidyate tat dravyam śvabhyaḥ hita tvāt śūnyam iti ucyate tamaḥ śabdasya api anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptāni dravya guṇa karmāṇi viṣayaḥ yatra yatra asannidhiḥ tejasaḥ tatra tatra dravya ādi tamaḥ śabdena abhidhīyate tamaḥ śabdaḥ ca anarthakaḥ iti bruvāṇaḥ sva siddhāntam bādhate catūrṇām upādāna rūpa tvāt tamasaḥ iti tasmāt na anarthakam ekam padam iti na asti ātmā iti ca evam bruvāṇaḥ siddhāntam bādhate katham iti rūpam bhadantaḥ na aham vedanā saṃjñā saṃskāraḥ vijñānam vā bhadantaḥ na aham iti evam etat bhikṣaḥ rūpam na tvam vedanā saṃjñā saṃskāraḥ vijñānam vā na tvam asi iti 
NV_3.1.1^8	 te ete skandhāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ ahaṃkāra viṣaya tvena pratiṣiddhāḥ viśeṣa pratiṣedhaḥ ca ayam na sāmānya pratiṣedhaḥ ātmānam anabhyupagacchatā sāmānyam eva pratiṣeddhavyam na aham naḥ eva tvam asi iti atha ekaśas pratiṣedhena samudāya viṣayaḥ ahaṅkāraḥ iti tathā api rūpa ādi skandha pañcaka vyatirekeṇa samudāyaḥ vaktavyaḥ yaḥ ahaṅkāra viṣayaḥ tat vyatiriktam ca samudāyam ahaṅkāra viṣayam abhyupagacchatā saṃjñā bhidyate ātmā samudāyaḥ iti atha avyatiriktaḥ eka pratyayaḥ na prāpnoti aham iti na hi bahuṣu eka pratyayam paśyāmaḥ iti na ca rūpa ādayaḥ skandhāḥ ekaśas samuditāḥ vā ātmānaḥ iti ahaṅkāra pratyayaḥ atasmin tat iti prāptaḥ 
NV_3.1.1^9	 bhavatu mithyā pratyayaḥ kim naḥ bādhyate iti katham na bādhyate yadā samyak pratyaya anukāreṇa mithyā pratyayāḥ bhavanti na ca ātmānam anabhyupagacchatā tathāgata darśanam arthavat tāyām śakyam vyavasthāpayitum na ca idam vacanam na asti sarva abhisamaya sūtre abhidhānāt tasmāt na asti ātmā iti evam bruvāṇaḥ siddhāntam bādhate iti tathā ca bhāram ca vaḥ bhikṣavaḥ deṣayiṣyāmi bhāra hāram ca bhāraḥ ca pañca skandhāḥ bhārahāraḥ ca pudgalaḥ iti yaḥ ca ātmā na asti iti bravīti sa mithyādṛṣṭikaḥ bhavati iti sūtram yaḥ api ayam hetuḥ ajāta tvāt iti ayam api rāśi antara vyavaccheda hetutvāt viruddhaḥ 
NV_3.1.1^10	 jātam ajātam iti ca vastu dharmau etau kim punar jātam kim vā jātam iti yasya kāraṇavataḥ sattā tat jātam yasya akāraṇavataḥ sattā tat ajātam iti kim kāraṇam nañaḥ janma pratiṣedha viṣaya tvāt ayam khalu nan pravatamānaḥ janmanaḥ pratiṣedham karoti na asya janma vidyate iti tat idam ajātam iti ātmanaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ na bhavati yathā anudakaḥ kamaṇḍaluḥ iti atha ayam bhāva pratiṣedhaḥ eva ajātam iti tathā api pratijñā hetvoḥ eka tvam ajāta tvam iti ca ayam dharmaḥ na ca dharmaḥ svatantraḥ yuktaḥ anyatra samavāyāt yat tantraḥ ayam dharmaḥ saḥ ātmā iti viruddhaḥ hetuḥ atha dharmaḥ asti na dharmī iti 
NV_3.1.1^11	 tathā api anivṛttaḥ vyāghātaḥ svatantrasya dharmasya adarśanāt iti kaḥ ca ayam arthaḥ ajāta tvāt iti yadi tāvat ayam arthaḥ na asya janma iti tatas asiddhaḥ janmavān ātmā kim punar ātmanaḥ janma śarīra indriya buddhi vedanābhiḥ nikāya viśiṣṭābhiḥ apūrvābhiḥ abhisambandhaḥ atha ajātatvam akāraṇa tvam tathā api na kaḥ cit bādhyate viruddhaḥ ca hetuḥ akāraṇasya nitya tvāt asattvam sādhayataḥ nityatām āpādyate iti viruddhaḥ hetuḥ pratijñā hetvoḥ ca virodhaḥ pratijñāyāḥ viṣayaḥ na asti ātmā iti hetoḥ viṣayaḥ ātyantika sattā sambandhaḥ tau etau pratijñā hetū asataḥ sat viṣaya tvāt viruddhau 
NV_3.1.1^12	 etena nirhetuka tvāt janma hetu anupādānāt akārya tvāt akāraṇa tvāt iti evam ādayaḥ tulya doṣāḥ iti pratyuktāḥ yat api idam ucyate śaśa viṣāṇa vat iti ayam api asiddhaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ katham iti śaśa viṣāṇa śabdasya sambandha viṣaya tvāt sambandha pratiṣedhaḥ na viṣāṇa pratiṣedhaḥ śaśa viṣāṇa sambandhaḥ udāharaṇam bhaviṣyati iti sa api na yuktaḥ kadā cit viṣāṇena śaśasya sambandha upapatteḥ loka virodhaḥ iti ced atha manyase yadi śaśe viṣāṇam asti nanu lokaḥ virudhyate iti na virudhyate kārya kāraṇa bhāva pratiṣedha dvāreṇa laukika pravṛtteḥ lokaḥ tāvat kāryam kāraṇam vā śaśasya viṣāṇam na asti iti evam pratiṣedhati 
NV_3.1.1^13	 yathā goḥ viṣāṇasya ca kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ na evam śaśasya viṣāṇasya ca kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ na ca kārya kāraṇa bhāva pratiṣedhāt asattvam na hi yat yasya na kāryam na kāraṇam tat na asti yathā devadattasya paṭaḥ iti idam ca śaśa viṣāṇam na asti iti bruvāṇaḥ praṣṭavyaḥ kim ayam sāmānya pratiṣedhaḥ atha viśeṣa pratiṣedhaḥ iti yadi sāmānya pratiṣedhaḥ tat na yuktam aśakya tvāt śaśasya viṣāṇam na asti iti gavā ādi viṣāṇāni api śaśasya na santi iti prāptam etat ca aśakyam na hi tāni na santi iti atha viśeṣa pratiṣedhaḥ kim cit viṣāṇam śaśasya pratiṣidhyate yasya śaśaḥ na kāryam yat ca śaśasya na kāraṇam iti 
NV_3.1.1^14	 saḥ ayam kārya kāraṇa sambandhaḥ eva pratiṣidhyate kārya kāraṇa sambandhaḥ tu anyatra dṛṣṭaḥ iha pratiṣidhyate iti na atyantā sattva pratipādane dṛṣṭāntaḥ bhavati etena kha puṣpa ādi asattvam vyākhyātam veditavyam na asti ātmā anupalabdheḥ iti ced atra api pratijñā doṣaḥ dṛṣṭānta doṣaḥ ca pūrvavat yat api anupalabdheḥ iti tat api ayuktam sā api anupalabdhiḥ asiddhā pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇa viṣaya tvāt ātmanaḥ pratyakṣeṇa tāvat ātmā upalabhyate katham pratyakṣeṇa liṅga liṅgi sambandha smṛti anapekṣam viṣaya svabhāva bheda anuvidhāyi aham iti vijñānam rūpa ādi jñāna vat pratyakṣam 
NV_3.1.1^15	 yat ca api bhavān mukta saṃśayam pratyakṣam pratipadyate tasya kutas pratyakṣa tvam iti avaśyam bhavatā jñānam eva liṅga ādi sambandha nirapekṣam sva ātma saṃvedyam pratipattavyam atha manyase asti ayam aham pratyayaḥ na punar asya ātmā viṣayaḥ hantaḥ tarhi nirdiśyatām viṣayaḥ rūpa ādiḥ viṣayaḥ iti ced atha manyase rūpa ādayaḥ eva ahaṅkārasya viṣayaḥ tathā ca uktam ahaṅkāra ālambana utpatti nimit tvāt ātmā iti ucyate iti tat na pratiṣedhāt asattvāt ca pratiṣiddhaḥ ahaṅkāraḥ rūpa ādiṣu rūpam na aham evam etat bhikṣaḥ rūpam na tvam asi tasmāt rūpa ādayaḥ eva tāvat ahaṅkārasya viṣayāḥ na bhavanti na ca ayam ahaṅkāraḥ rūpa ādiṣu kadā cit api dṛṣṭaḥ 
NV_3.1.1^16	 na hi bhavati kadā cit aham rūpam aham vedanā ādayaḥ iti nanu bhavati aham gauraḥ aham kṛṣṇaḥ iti na bhavati iti brūmaḥ katham na hi etasya draṣṭuḥ yat etat mama rūpam gauram etat aham iti pratyayaḥ bhavati kevalam matublopam kṛtvā aham gauraḥ iti ṣaṣṭhī artham nirdiśati evam etat na tattvataḥ iti kutas iti ced atha manyase matublopāt ayam ṣaṣṭhī artha vyapadeśaḥ na tattvataḥ iti atra kaḥ hetuḥ iti mama pratyaya samāna adhikaraṇasya nirdeśāt yasmin arthe mama pratyayaḥ asya bhavati tatra eva ayam ahaṅkāraḥ api iti mama pratyaya sāmānādhikaraṇyāt gamyate matublopaḥ iti mama pratyaya samāna adhikaraṇaḥ ca ayam ahaṃkāraḥ anya tve dṛṣṭaḥ upakāraka tvāt 
NV_3.1.1^17	 upakārake vastuni mama pratyaya samāna adhikaraṇaḥ aham pratyayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yaḥ ayam saḥ aham iti uktam ca atra rūpa ādi skandheṣu ahaṃkāraḥ atasmin tat iti pratyayaḥ iti tat evam ahaṃkāraya viṣaya tvāt ātmā tāvat pratyakṣaḥ anumānena api yathā ātmā upalabhyate tathā uktam icchā ādi sūtre iti āgamaḥ api asti eva tāni evam trīṇi pramāṇāni eka viṣaya tayā pratisandhīyamānāni ātmānam pratipādayanti na ca pramāṇa antaram vipratipatti hetuḥ asti iti tasmāt anupalabdheḥ iti asiddhaḥ hetuḥ sandigdhaḥ ca anupalabdheḥ tri kāraṇa tvāt anupalabdhi kāraṇāni trīṇi upalabdhā upalambhanam upalabhyam iti tatra iyam anupalabdhiḥ bhavantī kasya abhāvāt bhavati iti sandihyate 
NV_3.1.1^18	 yadi brūṣe upalabhyasya abhāvāt iti nanu ayam pratijñā arthaḥ eva na ca pratijñā pratijñā artham sādhayati iti anupalabdhiḥ ahetuḥ yā ca iyam anupalabdhiḥ ātma asattva pratipadanāya upādīyate tasyāḥ kaḥ āśrayaḥ yadi ātmānam pratipadyase vyāhatam bhavati āśrayaḥ ca na asti ca iti atha anāśrayā kaḥ sādhana arthaḥ na hi anāśrayaḥ dharmaḥ sādhyam sādhayitum śaknoti atha anupalabdhiḥ api na asti kaḥ sādhana arthaḥ anupalabdheḥ iti na hi asat sādhanam bhavitum arhati iti atha kalpitasya anupalabdhiḥ dharmaḥ iti katham kalpitasya iti vācyam kim sattvena atha asattvena yadi sattvena na anupalabdhiḥ tasya dharmaḥ 
NV_3.1.1^19	 na hi sthāṇoḥ puruṣa tayā kalpitasya sthāṇu dharmāḥ pratyavabhāsante atha asattvena kalpitasya anupalabdhiḥ dharmaḥ sidhyati anupalabdhiḥ dharmaḥ vṛthā tu kalpanā kim kāraṇam kalpanāyāḥ atatha abhāvāt kalpanā hi nāma atathā bhāvaḥ asattvena ca ātmā kalpitaḥ iti asattvena ātmā na asti asattvena ced na asti vṛthā kalpanā kim artham ca ayam ātmā asattvena kalpyate yadi hetu artham upapannaḥ hetuḥ yat artham upāttar sa punar arthaḥ na sidhyati na hi yaḥ puruṣe sthāṇu dharmān adhyāropya hetu tvena vyapadiśati tasya asau sthāṇuḥ syāt iti tat evam api anupalabdhiḥ ahetuḥ 
NV_3.1.1^20	 rūpa ādi skandha vācaka śabda viṣaya vyatirikta viṣayaḥ ātma śabdaḥ rūpa ādi śabdebhyaḥ anya tve sati eka pada tvāt ghaṭa śabda vat iti etena aham pratyayaḥ vyākhyātaḥ asiddhaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti ced atra uktam yathā guṇa vyatiriktaḥ guṇī iti tamaḥ śabda ādibhiḥ anaikāntikaḥ iti ced atha manyase yathā rūpa ādi śabdebhyaḥ anya tve sati eka pada tve ca tamaḥ śabdasya artha antara aviṣaya tvam evam ātma śabdasya api iti tat na virodhāt tamaḥ śabdaḥ nirviṣayaḥ iti bruvāṇaḥ siddhāntam bādhate upādāya rūpa tvāt tamasaḥ na ca etat asmābhiḥ abhyupagamyate tamaḥ śabdaḥ nirviṣayaḥ iti tamaḥ śabdasya sa viṣaya tve sūtra vyāghātaḥ dravya guṇa karma niṣpatti vaidharmyāt bhābhāvaḥ tamasḥ iti 
NV_3.1.1^21	 na sūtra artha aparijñānāt nirākṛta tejaḥ sambandhīni dravya guṇa karmāṇi tamaḥ śabdena abhidhīyante tasmāt na sūtra vyāghātaḥ apare tu jīva vat śarīram nirātmaka tvena pakṣayitvā sattvāt iti evam ādikam hetum bruvate tat na vikalpa anupapatteḥ nirātmakam iti kaḥ arthaḥ yadi tāvat ātmanaḥ anupakārakam iti na dṛṣṭāntaḥ asti na hi kim cit ātmanaḥ anupakārakam asti atha ātma pratiṣedhaḥ nirātmakam śarīram ātmā śarīram na bhavati iti kasya vā ātmā śarīram uttara pada viṣaya tvāt ca nisaḥ kim sā ātmakam iti vācyam na hi asati uttara pade nisaḥ prayogam paśyāmaḥ yathā nirmaśakam iti 
NV_3.1.1^22	 atha śarīre ātmā pratiṣidhyate siddham sādhayati kasya vā śarīre ātmā vidyate atha śarīram ātma sambandhi na bhavati punar dṛṣṭāntaḥ na asti sarve ca ete viśeṣa pratiṣedhāḥ viśeṣa pratiṣedhāt ca sāmānyam avagamyate evam ca sati yat pratiṣeddhavyam tat abhyanujñātam bhavati atha ātma śabdaḥ anitya viṣayaḥ varṇa ātmaka tvāt tathā api nitya śabdena anaikāntikam śarīra ādīnām ca ātma śabda vācya tvāt siddha sādhanam atha śarīra ādi vyatirikta viṣayaḥ ātma śabdaḥ anitya viṣayaḥ tathā api rūpa ādi vyatirikta viṣaya abhyupagamāt virodhaḥ tat evam yathā yathā ātma asattvam pratijñā kriyate tathā tathā nyāyam na sahate iti 
NV_3.1.1^23	 para arthāḥ cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ saṅghāta tvāt śayana āsana ādi vat iti saṅghātāḥ saṅghāta antara arthāḥ iti ced atha manyase satyam saṅghātāḥ para arthāḥ bhavanti te tu saṅghāta antara arthāḥ yathā śayana ādayaḥ iti na saṅghātasya abhyupagame virodhāt na hi rūpa ādi skandha vyatiriktam saṅghātam bhavantaḥ pratipadyante na ca asati saṅghāta antare saṅghātānām saṅghāta antara artha tā sidhyati atha pratipadyate vyāhatam bhavati aniṣṭa prasaṅgaḥ iti ced atha manyase mayā saṅghāta antaram pratipadyate api tu asmin hetau sati idam aniṣṭam prāpnoti iti para arthasya saṅghāta antara avinābhāvi tvāt 
NV_3.1.1^24	 yāvat para artham bhavati sarvam tat saṅghāta antara artham dṛṣṭam iti na virodhāt anabhyupagamāt ca na hi kaḥ cit vyatirikta ātma vādinaḥ saṅghātaḥ saṅghātasya para artham karoti tad ubhaya pakṣe saṃpratipanne na aniṣṭa āpādanam dṛṣṭam iti virodhāt ca yadi vivakṣita artha vyatirekeṇa anumānasya avivakṣitam api viṣayaḥ nanu etasyām prakalpanāyām sarvam anumānam vyāhanyeta katham iti yat iṣṭam anumāna tvena tat api te na anumānam prāptam yathā śabda anitya tve kṛtaka tvam kim kāraṇam yathā kṛtaka tvam anitya tvena āvinābhūtam anitya tvam sādhayati evam duḥkha śūnyān ātma ādi api sādhayati anātma ādi vat aśrāvaṇa tvam api sādhayiṣyati 
NV_3.1.1^25	 na śrotra grāhyaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat iti atha anumānena bādhyate ayam pratijñā arthaḥ iti atas na hetuḥ nanu ayam api saṅghāta antara arthāḥ cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ iti āgamena anumānena ca bādhyate iti yat ca api bhavān saṅghāta antaram pratipadyate tatra api anivṛttam saṅghāta tvam iti tena api saṅghāta antara arthena bhavitavyam iti evam ca anavasthā na ca enām śaktaḥ kaḥ cit pratipādayitum iti yatas eṣā nivartate tat asaṃhatam atha asaṃhatam na eva asti asaṃhata anabhyupagame saṅghāta anupapatteḥ vyāghātaḥ na hi kadā cit asaṃhata pratiṣedhe saṅghātaḥ sidhyati iti atha anumānam na eva asti iti paraḥ pratipadyeta 
NV_3.1.1^26	 sa katham na pratipadyate iti praṣṭavyaḥ yadi anumāna bādhita tvāt anumānam na asti ati nyāyaḥ ayam anumānena ca bādhyate anumānam ca na asti iti atīndriya artha adhigatiḥ ca katham yadi anumānam na asti katham atīndriya arthaḥ adhigamyate āgamāt atīndriya artha adhigatiḥ bhaviṣyati iti na yuktam āgama vyatirikta viṣaya tvāt kasmāt anumānasya āgama vyatiriktaḥ viṣayaḥ yathā stanayitnu śabdasya hetau na hi tatra pratyakṣam naḥ āgamaḥ iti tat evam ātmā asti iti samadhigatam tasmin vyapadeśasya ubhayathā siddheḥ saṃśayaḥ kaḥ punar ayam vyapadeśaḥ kriyā karaṇayoḥ kartrā sambandha abhidhānam vyapadeśaḥ darśanam kriyā karaṇam cakṣuḥ 
NV_3.1.1^27	 karaṇasya ca kriyāyāḥ ca kartrā sambandhaḥ cakṣuṣā paśyati iti sa ca ayam vyapadeśaḥ dvedhā bhavati avayavena samudāyasya yathā mūlaiḥ vṛkṣaḥ tiṣṭhati iti atra samudāya śabdena avayavī vṛkṣaḥ abhidhīyate eka deśena ca eka deśa antarāṇām yat bhinna jātīyaiḥ ārabhyate tatra hi eka deśa darśanāt eka deśa antarāṇi pratipadyante tatra api vyapadeśa stambhaiḥ prāsādaḥ dhriyate iti anyena ca anyasya vyapadeśaḥ paraśunā vṛścati iti paraśuḥ karaṇam vṛścanam kriyā tābhyām kartuḥ abhisambandhaḥ paraśunā vṛścati iti asti ca ayam iha api vyapadeśaḥ cakṣuṣā paśyati iti tat kim anyena anyasya vyapadeśaḥ atha avayavena avayavinaḥ atha eka deśena eka deśa antarāṇām iti 
NV_3.1.1^28	 kriyā karaṇa karmaṇām vā kartrā sambandhaḥ vyapadeśaḥ cakṣuṣā vṛkṣam paśyati iti kriyā karaṇa karmaṇām kartrā sambandhaḥ asti ca ayam iha api vyapadeśaḥ śarīreṇa sukha duḥkham anubhavati tatra na jñāyate kim tattvam iti anyena ayam anyasya vyapadeśaḥ iti etat tattvam katham darśana sparśanābhyām eka artha grahaṇāt dṛśyate anena iti darśanam cakṣuḥ spṛśati anena ātmā spraṣṭavyam artham iti sparśanam tvac indriyam ucyate darśanena dṛṣṭam artham sparśanena pratyabhijānāti yam aham adrākṣam tam spṛśāmi yam asprākṣam tam paśyāmi iti eka viṣayau etau pratyayau pratisandhīyete 
NV_3.1.1^29	 pratisandhānam ca nāma smṛtyā saha eka viṣaya tvam darśana sparśana pratyayayoḥ ghaṭa ādi viṣaya tvāt asambandhaḥ iti ced atha manyase yau etau darśana sparśana pratyayau tau ghaṭa ādi viṣayau atas na vyatirekam ātmanaḥ vyadhikaraṇa tvāt gamayate iti na sūtra artha aparijñānāt darśana sparśana pratyayau eka kartṛkau iti sūtra arthaḥ yadi ca anuṣaktam guṇa vyatirekam api eka viṣaya tvena sādhayataḥ na kaḥ cit doṣaḥ guṇa vyatirekaḥ asiddhaḥ iti ced uktam atra yathā guṇa vyatiriktaḥ kaḥ cit doṣaḥ guṇa vyatirekaḥ asiddhaḥ iti ced uktam atra yathā guṇa vyatiriktaḥ guṇī iti kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt pratisandhānam iti ced 
NV_3.1.1^30	 ukta uttaram etat icchā ādi sūtre iti akārya kāraṇa bhūtānām ca pratisandhānāt anekāntaḥ bhāvasya bhavitrapekṣa tvāt ca iti sūtra arthaḥ dṛṣṭiḥ darśanam spṛṣṭiḥ sparśanam iti bhāva rūpau etau pratyayau bhavitāram pratipādayataḥ na hi bhāvam anādhāram paśyāmaḥ utpatti vat iti karma ādhāraḥ bhaviṣyati iti na yuktam karmaṇi asati darśanāt asati api karmaṇi smṛteḥ bhāvaḥ bhavati na tu vinaṣṭam karma bhāvasya ādhāraḥ yuktaḥ tatas yat ādhāraḥ bhāvaḥ saḥ ātmā darśana sparśana grahaṇayoḥ rūpa asparśa ādi viṣaya tvāt na ghaṭa ādi viṣaya tvam na rūpa sparśa anupalabdhau tad viśiṣṭa pratyaya darśanāt 
NV_3.1.1^31	 yadā ayam anupalabhyamāna rūpa ādikam vastu upalabhyate tadā asya tad viśiṣṭaḥ pratyayaḥ ūpa jāyate yathā nīla ādi upahite sphaṭike pratyayaḥ rūpa ādi anupalabdhau bhavati rātrau ca balākāyām śukla rūpa ādi agrahaṇāt pakṣi pratyayaḥ tasmāt rūpa sparśa vyatirikta nimittaḥ ghaṭa pratyayaḥ pratisandhānāt ca vyatirikta nimitta tvam na hi nānā viṣayau pratyayau pratisandhīyete asti ca pratisandhānam yam adrākṣam tam spṛśāmi yam ca asprākṣam tam paśyāmi iti tasmāt eka viṣaya tvam saṅghāta kartṛkau darśana sparśana pratyayau bhaviṣyate iti na yuktam saṅghātasya nānātva ābādhanāt 
NV_3.1.1^32	 saṅghātaḥ saṃhanyamāna tantraḥ bhavati saṃhanyamānam ca anekam anekam ca pratisandhāna pratyaya kāraṇam na yuktam nānā kartṛkāṇām nānā viṣayāṇām ca pratyayānām apratisandhānāt eka indriya kṛtakau iti ced atha manyase yat eva indriyam darśana pratyayasya kāraṇam tat eva sparśana pratyayasya api iti tat na aviṣaya tvāt cakṣuṣaḥ cakṣuḥ khalu sva viṣaya grahaṇam pratisandhātum arhati yam adrākṣam saḥ eva ayam arthaḥ iti na punar indriya antara viṣaya grahaṇam aviṣaya tvāt iti indriya antara vaiyarthyam vā atha ekaikam eva indriyam aneka viṣaya grahaṇam pratisandhatte indriya antara utpādānam vyartham 
NV_3.1.2	 cetanāni indriyāṇi viṣaya vyavasthānāt viṣaya vyavasthānāt iti asya ayam arthaḥ karaṇa viṣaya niyamāt iti sati cakṣuṣi rūpa grahaṇam bhavati asati na bhavati yat ca yasmin sati bhavati asati ca na bhavati tasya tat sati ca cakṣuṣi rūpa grahaṇam bhavati tasmāt rūpa grahaṇam cakṣuṣaḥ evam śeṣeṣu api evam ca sati kim anyena cetanena iti ced na sandigdha tvāt ahetuḥ kim ayam indriyāṇām viṣaya niyamaḥ cetana tvāt āho cetanā upakaraṇa tvāt iti sandihyate cetana upakaraṇa tve api sati indriyāṇām etat bhavitum arhati yathā pradīpasya sadbhāve rūpa grahaṇam bhavati asati na bhavati na ca rūpa grahaṇam pradīpasya viparyaya prasādhakaḥ ca ayam hetuḥ viṣaya vyavasthānāt iti 
NV_3.1.3^1	 viparyaya sādhaka tva jñāpana artham ca tad vyavasthānāt eva ātma sadbhāvāt apratiṣedhaḥ iti sūtram yasmāt eva etāni indriyāṇi vyavasthita viṣayāṇi atas eva anyena atra avyavasthita viṣayeṇa bhavitavyam yadi hi kim cit ekam indriyam aneka artha grāhya vyavasthita viṣayam syāt kaḥ tatas anyam cetanam anumātum śaknuyāt caitanyam tu ātmanaḥ svātantrye sati avyavasthānāt cakṣuḥ ādi vat iti na acetanaḥ ātmā asvātantrya prasaṅgāt cakṣuḥ ādi vat iti anvaya abhāvāt ayuktam iti ced atha manyase ātmanaḥ caitanya sādhanasya avyavasthānasya na anvayaḥ asti na ca anvayam antareṇa hetuḥ sidhyati iti 
NV_3.1.3^2	 na viparyaya sambandhasya avyabhicārāt na ayam anvaya hetuḥ api tu vyatireka hetuḥ vyatireka hetoḥ ca viparyaya sambandha avi abhicāraḥ sāmarthyam yat ca acetanam tat sarvam vyavasthita viṣayam dṛṣṭam iti pṛthivī ādi nitya tva sādhane gandhavat tva ādi prasaṅgaḥ iti ced atha manyase yadi vyatirekī hetuḥ bhavati anvayam antareṇa atha pṛthivī ādi nitya tve sādhye gandhavat tvam kasmāt na hetuḥ na hetuḥ ubhaya vyāvṛtteḥ yasmāt gandhavat tvam nityāt ca anityāt ca vyāvartate na punar avyavasthānam evam tasmāt avyavasthānam hetuḥ na gandhavat tvam iti 
NV_3.1.4^1	 itas ca śarīra ādi vyatiriktaḥ ātmā na śarīra ādi saṅghāta mātram śarīra dāhe pātaka abhāvāt śarīra grahaṇena śarīra indriya buddhi vedanā saṅghātaḥ prāṇi bhūtaḥ gṛhyate śarīram prāṇi bhūtam dahataḥ prāṇi hiṃsā kṛtam pāpam pātakam iti ucyate tasya abhāvaḥ akartuḥ phalena sambandhaḥ kartuḥ ca asambandhaḥ iti kasmāt anabhyupagata artha antarātmanaḥ anyaḥ śarīra indriya buddhi vedanā saṃghātaḥ kartā anyaḥ ca tad phalasya bhoktā iti tat evam akṛta abhyāgama kṛta nāśa doṣa prasaṅgaḥ aniṣṭaḥ ca ayam tasmāt yaḥ kartā bhoktā ca yaḥ saḥ ātmā iti tat idam sūtram yasya ātmā na asti tasya ayam doṣaḥ iti doṣa pratipādana artham na sādhana artham iti hetu phala bhāvāt smṛti vat kartṛ bhoktṛ vyavahāraḥ iti ced yathā hetu phala bhāvena vyavasthitāyām santatau yasyām eva bhāvanā upajāyate tasyām eva santatau smṛtiḥ bhavati 
NV_3.1.4^2	 evam yat kāya citta santāna prabhavam karma tat kāya citta santāna prabhavam phalam iti na asti akṛta abhyāgama kṛta nāśa doṣaḥ sa ca katham syāt yadi anyasyām santatau kṛtam karma anyasyām phalam dadyāt yadi ca bhavān evam artham pratipādayitum śaknuyāt yaḥ eva karoti saḥ eva phalam bhuṅkte iti ubhayam ca na asti tasmāt akṛta abhyāgama ādiḥ na doṣaḥ na ukta uttara tvāt na santānaḥ nānātvam bādhate iti ukta uttaram etat yat punar etat ekasmin adarśanāt iti atra api uktam eka nimittānām pratyayānām pratisandhānāt iti śalya ādi bīja vat iti ced atha manyase yathā śāli bījāt aṅkuraḥ upajāyate aṅkura upamada uttara kālam nāla kāṇḍa ādi bhāvena mahābhūta anugraha vaśāt śālibījam prādurbhavati na ca tatra ekam kim cit anubaddham nimittam asti 
NV_3.1.4^3	 atha ca niyamaḥ śali bīja pūrkāt aṅkurāt śāli bījam evam ca sati hetu phala bhāvena vyavasthitāyām santatau āntare cetasi pariṇāma viśeṣa prāptāt karmaṇaḥ phalam iti tat na bīja avayava anuvṛtteḥ śāli bīja vat iti ayam asiddhaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ tatra api ye bīja avayavāḥ te pūrva vyūha parityāgena vyūha antaram āpadyante vyūha antara āpattau ca pṛthivī dhātuḥ abdhātunā saṃgṛhītaḥ āntareṇa tejasā pacyamānaḥ rasa dravyam nirvartayati sa rasaḥ pūrva avayava sahitaḥ aṅkura ādi bhāvam āpadyate tasmāt bīja avayava anuvṛtteḥ asiddham idam ucyate yathā śāli bījāt vinaṣṭāt aṅkuraḥ utpadyate atha ca pratisandhānam iti paramāṇu avastha tvāt bīja avayavānām yathā ukta doṣa āpattiḥ iti ced atha manyase asya api bīja avayavāḥ pūrva vyūham jahati vyūha antaram vā āpadyante tasya api paramāṇu avastha tvāt bījasya paramāṇu mātram śiṣyate iti 
NV_3.1.4^4	 na ca paramāṇuṣu apara jātayaḥ vidyante iti na hi śāli bīja paramāṇūnām yava bīja paramāṇūnām ca kaḥ cit viśeṣaḥ yathā anupajāta viśeṣāḥ paramāṇavaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva niyamāt tad pūrvaka tayā śāli aṅkuram abhinirvartayanti tathā mama api kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt niyamaḥ iti na anabhyupagamāt paramāṇu avasthāni bījāni bhavanti iti etat na pratipadyāmahe sarva avasthā upalabdheḥ yasmāt śāli ādi bījam ucchūna avasthām ādim kṛtvā yāvat upāntyam śāli bīja kāryam tāvat na kadācid paramāṇu avastham bhavati yadi ca syāt kadā cit naḥ upalabhyeta yadi tarhi āparamāṇoḥ vibhāgaḥ na asti kalpa ādau utpattiḥ na prāpnoti paramāṇu avastha tvāt jagataḥ paramāṇu avasthe ca jagati na śāli ādi jāti vyaktiḥ asti iti punar utpāde jāti vyakti hetavaḥ paramāṇavaḥ eva iti abhyupagantavyam yathā ca kalpa ādau evam paramāṇu avasthe bīje api iti na anena eva ukta uttara tvāt 
NV_3.1.4^5	 anena eva sarva avasthā upalabdheḥ iti ukta uttaram etat sarga ādau ca śāli jāti vyakti hetuḥ adṛṣṭa viśeṣaḥ yena adṛṣṭena prāṇinām upabhogāya śāli ādayaḥ nirvartyante tam adṛṣṭa viśeṣam apekṣamāṇaḥ īśvaraḥ tān tān paramāṇūn tathā tathā saṅghātayati yathā yathā śāli ādi jāti vyaktiḥ iti etena ghaṭa ādi pākaḥ vyākhyātaḥ na aparamāṇu antaḥ vibhāgaḥ sarva avasthā upalabdheḥ iti ā madhyāt pāka anupapattiḥ iti ced atha manyase yadi kārya kāraṇa dravye pacyete ā madhyāt pākaḥ na prāpnoti pācakena tejasā aprāpta tvāt na apratibandhāt bhavet api eṣaḥ doṣaḥ yadi tejasaḥ anupraveśam avayavī pratibadhnīyāt sa tu na pratibadhnāti apratibaddham tejaḥ anupraviśati iti na pratibadhnāti iti na hetuḥ asti iti na na asti parisrava ādimataḥ ghaṭasya upalabdheḥ 
NV_3.1.4^6	 yasmāt parisrava ādimataḥ ghaṭasya drava tva pratibandhaḥ na dṛṣṭaḥ apratibandhena drava tvam parisrutim karoti tat ca pratyakṣataḥ upalabhyate yadi ca ayam avayava anupraveśaḥ dravyasya vināśakaḥ syāt na parisrava ādimān ghaṭaḥ upalabhyeta parisravamāṇa tvāt ca bhājana gatānām apām avasthānam na syāt vināśe ca kārya dravyāṇām vyavahita avyavahitayoḥ tulya upalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ yadi ca anupraviśya dravyam dravya antaram vyatibhinatti tena cākṣuṣasya raśmeḥ anupraveśāt sphaṭika ādi vinaṣṭam iti vyavahite ca avyavahite ca tulya upalabdhiḥ prāpnoti tasmāt śāli bījam adṛṣṭāntaḥ yasya ca pūrva skandha nirodha sama kālāni skandha antarāṇi prādurbhavanti tasya teṣām skandha antarāṇām akarma nimittaḥ sargaḥ prāpnoti akarma nimittena sattva sargeṇa śubha aśubha phala prāpti arthā kriyā na prāpnoti sukhī syām iti tad kriyā iti ced 
NV_3.1.4^7	 atha manyase svayam karmāṇi karoti katham aham sukhī syām duḥkhī na syām iti tat na ananubhūta tvāt yena sukham anubhūtam sukha sādhana sambandha anusmṛtiḥ ca yasya sa tad sādhanam upādatte yasya punar pratikṣaṇa pradhvaṃsinaḥ saṃskārāḥ tasya sukha sādhana sambandha anusmṛteḥ abhāvāt sukhī syām iti kriyā anupapattiḥ muktyrthaḥ ca prayāsaḥ naḥ upapadyate ayatna siddha tvāt jāta mātraḥ eva ayam mucyate iti mukti arthaḥ brahmacarya vāsaḥ vyarthaḥ paripṛcchā ca na prāpnoti tathāgatena bhikṣavaḥ paripṛcchyante kaccit yūyam mayā vinītāḥ iti te ca āhuḥ aṅga vinītāḥ smaḥ iti atīta anāgata vartamānānām anupakārya tvāt ye tāvat anāgatāḥ saṃskārāḥ te tāvat asattvāt naḥ upakriyante ye api atītāḥ te api evam ye tu vartamānāḥ teṣu saṃskāra ādhānam aśakyam vartamāna lakṣaṇasya anupakārya tvāt 
NV_3.1.4^8	 na hi tasya avasthāna kālaḥ asti yasmin upakriyā syāt saṃskārya saṃskārakayoḥ saha utpādāt yuktam idam iti ced na saṃskārya saṃskārakayoḥ saha utpāde niyama anupapatteḥ iti idam saṃskārakam idam saṃskāryam iti niyamaḥ naḥ upapadyate atha saṃskārakam apekṣamāṇam saṃskāryam vilakṣaṇam kāryam karoti vilakṣaṇa kārya utpādaḥ ca saṃskāraḥ iti ucyate na saṃskārya artha anabhidhānāt idam saṃskārakam idam saṃskāryam iti etat katham na hi yaḥ yasya viśeṣam na ādatte sa tad saṃskārakaḥ iti vā saṃskāryaḥ iti vā śakyam vyapadeṣṭum atha api upadeśena saṃskārāṇām anāgatānām anutpattiḥ kriyate nānāgatānām anutpatteḥ sattvāt yā asau anāgatānām saṃskārāṇām anutpattiḥ na asau kadā cit na asti iti kim tasyāḥ kriyate tasmāt mukti arthaḥ brahmacarya vāsaḥ iti anupapannam tat evam anabhyupagata artha antarātmanaḥ doṣaḥ iti 
NV_3.1.5^1	 yasya api ātmā nityaḥ tasya api hiṃsā phale na prāpnutaḥ hiṃsā tāvat na prāpnoti nitya tvāt phalam api ātmanaḥ na yuktam anupakārya tvāt asya ca arthasya jñāpikām kārikām udāharanti varṣa ātapābhyām kim vyomnaḥ carmaṇi asti tayoḥ phalam carma upamaḥ ced saḥ anityaḥ kha tulyaḥ ced asat phalaḥ tat evam ekasmin pakṣe hiṃsā niṣphalāḥ ekasmin tu pakṣe anupapannā niṣphalā ca iti iyam ca hiṃsā sāṃkhya pakṣe sambhavati buddheḥ pariṇāmi tvāt kārya kāraṇa saṃghātaḥ pariṇāmi tvāt ucchidyate saḥ eva ca tad phalāni bhuṅkte tad phalasya tatra vyakteḥ iti na pūrva avasthā parityāgāt 
NV_3.1.5^2	 yathā eva ātmā pūrva avasthām na jahāti iti tatra phalam naḥ iṣyate tathā buddhiḥ api nitya tvāt pūrva avasthām na jahāti iti tatra phalam naḥ iṣyate atha manyase pūrva avasthām jahāti iti nitya tvam virudhyate pūrva avasthā parityāgena buddhi nitya tvam viruddham atha api avasthā bhidyate iti manyase tathā api anivṛttaḥ vyāghātaḥ avasthābhyaḥ avasthāvataḥ ananya tvāt na hi avasthābhyaḥ avasthāvān anyaḥ iti avasthā bhede avasthāvān bhidyate iti yaḥ eva bauddhasya pratikṣaṇam dhvaṃsiṣu saṃskāreṣu doṣaḥ saḥ eva pratikṣaṇa vipariṇāmiṣu api iti ṛju vakra tā vat iti ced 
NV_3.1.5^3	 atha manyase ṛju vakra tā ādi bhede yathā aṅguli dravyam na bhidyate na ca aṅgulitaḥ anye te tathā avasthā bhede buddheḥ abhedah iti na anya tvāt anye ṛju vakrate yuktam ca yat anya bhede anya abhedaḥ iti na punar avasthātaḥ avasthāvataḥ anya tvam tasmāt asamaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ kim punar vakra tvam ṛju tvam vā guṇaḥ ākuñcana jam vakra tvam prasāraṇa jam ṛju tvam guṇaḥ ca guṇinaḥ artha antaram iti pratipāditam etat buddheḥ api evam iti ced atha manayse buddheḥ api ye te avasthe bhidyete tayoḥ bhede buddhiḥ na bhidyate iti anya avasthātaḥ buddhiḥ 
NV_3.1.5^4	 tat na siddhānta virodhāt na bhavatām pakṣe dharma dharmiṇoḥ bhedaḥ iti bhedam ca abhyupagacchatā siddhāntaḥ tyaktaḥ bhavati tasmāt yathā ātma nitya tve sukha duḥkha anupabhogaḥ doṣaḥ iti na tatra sukha duḥkhe kalpyete tathā buddhi nitya tve iti buddhau api na kalpanīye samānam nitya tvam iti atha ātmanaḥ nityasya puṇya pāpābhyām kim kriyate iti sukha duḥkhe puṇya pāpābhyām ātmanaḥ nityasya kriyete atha tābhyām sukha duḥkhābhyām ātmanaḥ kim kriyate pratyayaḥ ye ātmani sukha duḥkhe tad viṣayaḥ pratyayaḥ ātmani bhavati iti etāvat kriyate sa ca pratyayaḥ bhogaḥ 
NV_3.1.5^5	 yat punar etat varṣa ātapābhyām kim vyomnaḥ iti yat eva carmaṇaḥ carmaṇaḥ varṣa ātapābhyām yat kriyate tat eva vyomnaḥ atha carmaṇaḥ kim kriyate sambandhaḥ yathā carma varṣa ātapābhyām sambadhyate tathā vyama api varṣa ātapa sambandhāt carma vat anityam vyomaḥ iti ced atha manyase yathā carma varṣa ātapa sambandhāt vikriyate tathā vyoma varṣa ātapa sambandhāt vikariṣyate na anekāntāt varṣa ātapa sambandhī paramāṇuḥ atha ca nityaḥ iti anekāntaḥ carmaṇaḥ ca anitya tvam kim varṣa ātapa sambandhāt atha kāraṇa vibhāgāt atha āśraya vināśāt iti 
NV_3.1.5^6	 vayam tu brūmaḥ kāraṇavataḥ tad vibhāgāt tad vināśāt ca yuktaḥ vināśaḥ na punar ākāśasya kāraṇam asti iti ubhaya abhāvaḥ iti tadvatām ca avasthānāt na sambandhaḥ vināśa hetuḥ yadi ca ayam sambandhah vināśa hetuḥ abhaviṣyat na tadvatām avasthānam abhaviṣyat avatiṣṭhante tu bhāvāḥ tāvat yāvat na vināśa kāraṇa sannipātaḥ iti atha manyase varṣa ātapābhyām carmaṇaḥ saṅkoca vikāśau bhavataḥ na tu ākāśasya iti tat na vikalpa anupapatteḥ saṅkoca vikāśau carmaṇaḥ iti kaḥ arthaḥ kim tāvat alpa tva mahat tve uta saṃyoga vibhāgau iti 
NV_3.1.5^7	 tat na tāvat saṅkoca vikāśau alpa tva mahat tve yāvat dravya bhāvi tvāt parimāṇasya yāvat dravyam hi parimāṇam tat sati na nivartitum arhati iti atha carmaṇaḥ saṃyoga vibhāgau saṅkoca vikāśau iti tat api na yuktam eka tvāt na hi ekasya saṃyoga vibhāgau sambhavataḥ iti katham tarhi idam ucyate carmaṇaḥ saṅkocaḥ carmaṇaḥ vikāśaḥ iti carma kāraṇānām avinaśyat kāryāṇām avayavānām ātapa sambandha apekṣāṇām yāḥ paraspareṇa prāptayaḥ ārabdha kāryāṇām dravya antara anārambhikāḥ tāḥ itaretara upaśleṣeṇa avayaveṣu vartamānāḥ tad eka artha samavāyini carmaṇi upacaryante 
NV_3.1.5^8	 tad apekṣam ca idam ucyate carmaṇaḥ saṅkocaḥ na punar carma saṅkucati iti etena tad avayavānām eva udaka sambandha apekṣāṇām avinaśyat kāryāṇām parasparataḥ vibhāgaḥ vikāśaḥ iti vikriyāyām ca dṛṣṭānta abhāvaḥ tat eva vastu avinaśyat vikriyām āpadyate iti na dṛṣṭāntaḥ asti vikriyā tu padārtha antara utpādaḥ yathā pūrvarūpa ādi nivṛttau rūpa antara utpāde vikṛtaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti yadi evaṃbhūtaḥ vikāraḥ ātmani api vikāraḥ asti tatra api sukha nivṛttau duḥkha prādurbhāvaḥ iti sukha pratyaya nivṛttau duḥkha pratyayaḥ iti tasmāt nityasya ātmanaḥ sukha duḥkha upabhogaḥ iti siddham
