NV_3.1.6^1	 nitya tvāt ātmanaḥ hiṃsā doṣaḥ aparihāryaḥ na anyathā tad upapatteḥ ātma nitya tve api anyathā hiṃsā bhavati asya arthasya jñāpanāya na kārya āśraya kartṛ vadhāt iti sūtram na brūmaḥ nityasya sattvasya vadhaḥ hiṃsā iti api tu anucchitti dharmakasya sattvasya yat śarīram yāni ca sukha duḥkha saṃvitti sādhanāni indriyāṇi asādhāraṇāni teṣām pīḍā vaikalyam pramāpaṇam vā hiṃsā iti kutas etat pratipattavyam iti hiṃsāyāḥ phala bhogasya ca ubhaya pakṣa sampratipanna tvāt hiṃsā phala upabhogaḥ ca ubhaya pakṣa sampratipannaḥ sā iyam hiṃsā ekasmine pakṣe sambhavati yasya tāvat pratikṣaṇa vināśinaḥ saṃskārāḥ tasya kim hiṃsyate nirhetuka tvāt vināśasya kasya vyāpāraḥ asti atha vilakṣaṇa utpatti nimitta tvena vyavatiṣṭhamānaḥ paraḥ hinasti iti ucyate nanu upacāraḥ bhavati na bhavataḥ pradhānam asti yena śarīra utpādakaḥ upacaryate 
NV_3.1.6^2	 na samāna tvāt bhavatām api pakṣe na pradhānam hiṃsyate iti satyam mama api kārya āśraya kartṛ vadhaḥ hiṃsā iti tulyam ayam tu viśeṣaḥ ekasmin pakṣe yaḥ eva ayam ātmā śarīra ādi sādhanaḥ karma karoti saḥ eva tad phalam upabhuṅkte iti akṛta abhyāgama doṣaḥ na asti bhavatām tu akṛta abhyāgama kṛta praṇāśaḥ ca iti pariśeṣāt ātma nitya tve hiṃsā iti vyavasthitam tatra kārya āśraya śabdena śarīram ucyate tad nimitta tvāt upabhogasya iti kartṝṇi indriyāṇi tad sādhana tvāt atha vā samāna adhikaraṇa samāsāt śarīram eva kārya āśraya kartṛ śabdābhyām ucyate iti kartā bhoktā ca ātman kim punar idam kartṛ tvam kim vā bhoktṛ tvam iti jñāna cikīrṣā prayatnānām samavāyaḥ kartṛ tvam sukha duḥkha saṃvid samavāyaḥ bhoktṛ tvam etat ca na śarīre nimitta tvāt tu kartṛ śarīram ucyate 
NV_3.1.7^1	 itas ca deha vyatiriktaḥ ātmā savya dṛṣṭasya itareṇa pratyabhijñānāt savyena cakṣuṣā dṛṣṭam itareṇa pratyabhijānāti iti sūtra arthaḥ tat ca pratyabhijñānam smṛti pūrvaka tvāt pratisandhānam pratisandhānāt ca eka kartṛ tvam pratyayānām sidhyati iti siddha tvāt anārambhaḥ iti darśana sparśanābhyām eka artha grahaṇāt iti etasmin prakaraṇe siddhaḥ ātma vyatirekaḥ siddha tvāt anārambhyam prakaraṇam iti indriya vyatireka jñāpana artham iti eke eke idam prakaraṇam indriya vyatireka jñāpana artham varṇayanti tat na tatas eva siddheḥ pūrva prakaraṇena eva indriya śarīra vyatirekaḥ siddhaḥ iti samuccaya artham iti apare apare tu samuccaya artham savya dṛṣṭasya itareṇa pratyabhijñānāt iti hetum bruvate yuktaḥ anyaḥ samuccayaḥ ayam tu na yuktaḥ virodhāt 
NV_3.1.7^2	 savya dṛṣṭasya itareṇa pratyabhijñānāt iti hetum bruvāṇaḥ yuktim bādhate kā punar iyam yukti bādhāḥ aneka tvāt indriyasya yugapad adhiṣṭhāna asambhavaḥ aṇu manaḥ anekam cakṣuḥ na ca anoḥ manasaḥ yugapad anekena cakṣuṣā sambandhaḥ sambhavati atha asambaddham api dvitīyam cakṣuḥ arthān ālocayati evam ca sati dvitīya cakṣuḥ vat itara cakṣuḥ api manasā anadhiṣṭhitam eva pravartiṣyate iti vyartham manas prāptam anadhiṣṭhitam ca pravartamānam indriyam karaṇa tvam bādhate na hi karaṇam anadhiṣṭhitam pravartamānam dṛṣṭam iti sama grāsam agra cakṣuṣoḥ ca tulya upalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ na hi anadhiṣṭhitam indriyam pravartate iti aṇu tvāt manasaḥ nityam idam ekena eva sambadhyate iti vikala avikalayoḥ tulya upalabdhiḥ prāptā prakaraṇa virodhaḥ ca indriya artha pañcatvāt iti indriya pañcatva pratipādakam prakaraṇam virudhyate iti 
NV_3.1.8	 yadi tarhi ekam indriyam katham dvi tva upalabdhiḥ dvi tva upalabdhi pratipādana artham na ekasmin nāsā asthi vyavahite dvi tva abhimānāt iti sūtram ekam indriya dravyam dvi adhiṣṭhānam abhinnam kaḥ adhiṣṭhāna arthaḥ taijasasya cakṣuṣaḥ pārthivena kṛṣṇasāreṇa upakāra vikāra bheda anuvidhānam yasmāt kṛṣṇasāre upakriyamāṇaḥ upakriyate vikriyamāṇe vikriyate tiṣṭhati tiṣṭhati naśyati naśyati iti tasmāt asya kṛṣṇasāram adhiṣṭhānam iti ucyate etat ca vyākhyātam śarīra sūtre tasya antau gṛhyamāṇau dvi tva abhimānam prayojayataḥ yathā dīrghasya dravyasya madhye vyavahitasya antau upalabhyamānau dvi tva abhimānam prayojayate iti 
NV_3.1.9	 ekasmin vinaṣṭe uddhṛte vā dvitīyam avatiṣṭhate viṣaya grahaṇa liṅgam na anyathā tad utpatteḥ dvitīyam avatiṣṭhate iti naḥ etat kasya cit pratyakṣam pratyaya mātram tu vinaṣṭe api ekasmin adhiṣṭhāne yat avatiṣṭhate tena bhavati na ca adhiṣṭhānam indriyam api tu yat tad anuvidhāyi tat ekam anuvidhatte iti yathā bahu vātāyanasya veśmanaḥ eka pidhāne itareṇa grahaṇam iti 
NV_3.1.10–3.1.11	 apare tu avayava vināśe api avayavi upalabdheḥ ahetuḥ iti parihāram varṇayanti tasya uttaram dṛṣṭānta virodhāt apratiṣedhaḥ iti sūtram asya arthaḥ na kāraṇa dravya vināśe kārya dravyam avatiṣṭḥate iti yadi na avatiṣṭhate katham kāraṇa dravya vināśe kāryam upalabhyate iti kaḥ evam āha upalabhyate iti api tu bahuṣu avayaviṣu yasya kāraṇāni vibhaktāni tat vinaṣṭam yasya na vibhaktāni tat upalabhyate iti śeṣam bhāṣye 
NV_3.1.12	 anumīyate ca ayam deha ādi vyatiriktaḥ cetanaḥ indriya antara vikārāt kasya cit amlasya phalasya gṛhīta sāhacarye rūpe gandhe vā kenacid indriyeṇa gṛhyamāṇe rasanā indriya vikāraḥ kaḥ punar vikāraḥ rasa anusmṛtau rasa ga ṛddhi pravarttitaḥ gaṛddhiḥ tṛṣṇā rasa tṛṣṇā pravarttitaḥ danta antara pariśrutābhiḥ adbhiḥ rasanā indriyasya sambandhaḥ saṃplavaḥ vikāraḥ iti ucyate sā ca iyam smṛtiḥ indriya caitanye na prāpnoti na ca pratikṣaṇa vināśiṣu saṃskāreṣu anya anubhūtasya anyena asmaraṇāt iti indriya antara vikāraḥ indriya antara dharmaḥ sa katham vyadhikaraṇa tvāt ātma vyatirekam pratipādayati na indriya antara vikāraḥ ātma vyatireka pratipatti kāraṇam api tu smṛtiḥ na hi ekam anubhavitāram antareṇa smṛtiḥ prāpnoti smṛtiḥ ca bhāva tvāt bhavitṛ apekṣāḥ utpatti vat iti nyāyaḥ na ca smṛtim antareṇa indriya vikāraḥ sambhavati iti pratyakṣaḥ indriya antara vikāraḥ upādīyate ananubhūta rasasya indriya antara vikāra abhāvāt iti vyatireka hetuḥ 
NV_3.1.13–3.1.14^1	 smṛtiḥ nāma dharmaḥ tasyāḥ smartavyaḥ arthaḥ viṣayaḥ sā iyam smartavya artha sannidhānāt upajāyamānāḥ aparidṛṣṭa sāmarthyam na smartāram pratipādayiṣyati na hi sva kāraṇa sannidhānāt prādurbhavan aṅkuraḥ aparidṛṣṭa sāmarthyam stambha ādikam artham pratipādayati na smartavya mātrāt smṛtiḥ utpadyate iti yadā ayam atītam artham smarati tadā smṛtiḥ anādhārā prāpnoti na ca iyam anādhārā yuktāḥ guṇa tvāt na hi kaḥ cit guṇaḥ anādhāraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti na ca iyam indriyeṣu sambhavati ananubhūta tvāt na viṣaye tasya asattvāt na śarīre śarīra guṇānām pratyakṣāṇām sva ātma parātma pratyakṣa tvāt na ca iyam anādhārāḥ guṇa tvāt iti uktam na ca iyam na asti na ca ātmani asati asyāḥ sadbhāvaḥ yuktaḥ iti tebhyaḥ anyasya tad utpattau sāmarthyam gamyate katham iti etat anena eva pratyuktam asti ātmanaḥ sāmarthyam smṛteḥ ādhāra bhāvaḥ na ca iyam anādhārā kāryatvāt sarvam kāryam ādhāra vat kṣīrnīḥ ādi dṛṣṭam iti etena na tat cakṣuṣi naḥ rūpe na antarāle tayoḥ sthitam 
NV_3.1.14^2	 na tat asti na tat na asti yatra tat niṣṭhitam bhavet bauddhasya iti pratyuktam na tat asti na tat na asti iti vyāhatam na ca anayā kārikayā vijñānasya āśrayi bhāvaḥ pratiṣeddhum śakyaḥ kim kāraṇam viśeṣa pratiṣedhāt na cakṣuṣi naḥ rūpe iti evam ādiḥ viśeṣa pratiṣedhaḥ atha anāśritam eva vijñānam vyartham vākyam na tat cakṣuṣi naḥ rūpe iti kasya vā cakṣuṣi rūpe vā vijñānam vartate iti siddham yam prati pratiṣedhaḥ ayam ca vijñānasya āśraya āśraya bhāva pratiṣedhaḥ vicāryamāṇaḥ ātma sattvam pratipādayati na hi vijñānasya ātma āśrita tvam antareṇa vākyam etat arthavat tāyām vyavatiṣṭhate iti atha vai ekasya aneka viṣaya upalabdhi pratisandhānam anena sūtreṇa pradarśyate iti ukta nyāyam śeṣam bhāṣye iti 
NV_3.1.15–3.1.16	 ye ete bhavatā ātma pratipādakāḥ hetavaḥ upadiṣṭāḥ sarve ete manasi sambhavanti evam ca na manaḥ vyatiriktaḥ ātmā sidhyati yathā jñātāram abhyupagacchatā jñānasya sādhanāni cakṣuḥ ādīni pratipadyante tathā mantāram pratipadyamānena mati sādhanam abhyupeyam yat ca tat mati sādhanam tad manaḥ iti saṃjñā bheda mātram atha mantā niḥsādhanaḥ matim karoti evam ayam jñātā niḥsādhanaḥ jñāptam kariṣyati iti sarva indriya vilopa prasaṅgaḥ 
NV_3.1.17^1	 yaḥ ayam niyamaḥ āśrīyate matiḥ asādhanā na punar jñāptiḥ iti niyamaḥ ayam niranumānaḥ jñapti vat mateḥ na niḥsādhana tve anumānam asti asti tu sa sādhana tve sukha ādayaḥ ca rūpa ādibhyaḥ viṣaya antaram iti tad viṣayāyāḥ upalabdheḥ sādhanena bhavitavyam na hi kim cit sa viṣayam vijñānam asādhanam dṛṣṭam rūpa ādi jñāna vat iti niranumānaḥ niyamaḥ ca sukha ādi vijñānāni niḥsādhanāni bhavantu mā bhūvan rūpa ādi viṣayāṇi iti yadi sarvam vijñānam sa sādhanam utpadyate manasi api karaṇa antaram prāpnoti viṣaya tvāt om iti ucyate asti manasi karaṇam 
NV_3.1.17^2	 kim punar tat yena manaḥ adhigamyate kena punar manaḥ adhigamyate ayugapad jñāna utpattyā yasya tu manaḥ pratyakṣam bhavati tasya ca yoga ja dharma anugṛhītaḥ ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ karaṇam yogi dharmāṇām ca acintya tvāt katham te manaḥ gṛhṇanti iti avicāraṇīyam etat etena ātma vijñānam pratyuktam ātma manaḥ saṃyogasya karaṇa bhāvāt iti evam tāvat ātmanaḥ astitva vyatirekau siddhau bahu tvam ca atas eva darśana sparśanābhyām eka artha grahaṇāt na anya dṛṣṭam anyaḥ smarati iti śarīra dāhe pātaka abhāvāt iti ca tena sarvā vyavasthā śarīra bhede sati sambhavati iti 
NV_3.1.18^1	 kim punar ayam deha ādi saṅghātāt anyaḥ nityaḥ atha anityaḥ iti etasmin arthe ubhayathā dṛṣṭa tvāt iti saṃśayam upapādayati anupapanna rūpaḥ ca ayam saṃśayaḥ ātma astitva vyatireka hetubhiḥ śarīra bhede api abhede ātmani siddhaḥ siddha tvāt prakaraṇam anārabhyam iti nānārabhyam katham janma prabhṛti yāvat prāyaṇam etasmāt ekaḥ sidhyati na punar śarīra vināśāt ūrdhvam bhavati iti evam sidhyati iti etasya arthasya jñāpana artham pūrva abhyasta smṛti anubandhāt jātasya harṣa bhaya śoka sampratipatteḥ iti sūtram asya arthaḥ jātaḥ khalu ayam kumārakaḥ viṣaya avagamā samartheṣu indriyeṣu harṣa bhaya śokān sampratipadyamānaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ smita kampa rudita anumeyān 
NV_3.1.18^2	 te ca smṛti anubandhāt utpadyante smṛti anubandhaḥ ca na antareṇa pūrva śarīram iti tatra janma nikāya viśiṣṭābhiḥ apūrvābhiḥ śarīra indriya buddhi vedanābhiḥ sambandhaḥ abhipreta viṣaya prārthanā prāpatau sukha anubhavaḥ harṣaḥ aniṣṭa viṣaya sādhana sannipāte tad jihāsoḥ hāna aśakya tā bhayam iṣṭa viṣaya viyoge sati tad prāpti aśakya prārthanā śokaḥ tad anubhavaḥ sampratipattiḥ eka viṣaya aneka vijñāna utpādaḥ abhyāsaḥ eka ākāra viṣayaḥ vā yathā śālayaḥ anena abhyastāḥ iti pratyakṣa buddhi nirodhena tad anusandhāna viṣayaḥ pratyayaḥ smṛtiḥ 
NV_3.1.18^3	 tad anugṛhītaḥ tad anusandhāna viṣayaḥ pratyayaḥ tad bhāva viṣayaḥ pratyabhijñānam anubandhaḥ bhāvanā ākhyaḥ smṛti hetuḥ saṃskāraḥ iṣṭa viṣaya anusmaraṇāt nayana ādi prasādaḥ smitam aniṣṭa viṣaya anusmaraṇāt tad sādhana jihāsā anuṣṭhāna lakṣaṇaḥ hasta ādi vikṣepavataḥ aśru vimocana sahacaritaḥ śabda viśeṣaḥ ruditam smita rudite vyadhikaraṇa tvāt asādhanam atha manyase smita rudite bālya avasthāyām bhavataḥ na ca bālya avasthā ātmanaḥ tasmāt vyadhikaraṇa tvāt asādhanam iti na śoka ādimada ātmavatyāḥ bālya avasthāyāḥ sādhya tvāt śoka ādi vat ātmavatī bālya avasthā iti sādhyam smita rudita ādimattvāt iti bālya avasthāyāḥ dharmaḥ yauvana avasthāvat 
NV_3.1.18^4	 etena smṛti saṃskāra anubhava pūrva śarīra sambandha vat ātmavat tvam vyākhyātam katham iti yathā smita ruditavat tvena śoka ādimadātmavatī bālya avasthā sādhyate evam śoka ādimada ātmavat tvena smṛtimada ātmavatī bālya avasthā sādhyāḥ tathā smṛtimada ātmavat tvena saṃskāra vat ātmavatī bālya avasthā sādhyāḥ saṃskāra vat ātmavat tvena pūrva anubhava vat ātmavatī pūrva anubhava vat ātmavat tvena pūrva śarīra sambandha vat ātmavatī iti sarvatra pūrva anubhava vat ātmavat tvena pūrva śarīra sambandha vat ātmavatī sādhyāḥ sarvatra yauvana avasthāḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ sā hi smita ruditavatī bhavati iti śoka ādimadātmavatī ca iti sarvatra yojyam 
NV_3.1.19^1	 anitye api vikāra darśanāt anekāntaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ kaḥ punar ayam prabodhaḥ kim vā sammīlanam iti padma pattra avayava vibhāgaḥ avinaśyat kāryaḥ prabodhaḥ padma pattra avayavānām eva ārabdha kāryāṇām yāḥ punar paraspareṇa prāptayaḥ tāḥ sammīlanam iti na vikalpa anupapatteḥ padma ādiṣu prabodha sammīlana vikāra ādi vat tad vikāraḥ iti kim ayam dṛṣṭāntaḥ sādhana pakṣe uta anaikāntika pakṣaḥ iti yadi sādhana pakṣe hetuḥ asti na ca hetum antareṇa dṛṣṭānta mātram sādhakam iti asādhanam dṛṣṭāntaḥ atha dūṣaṇam tat kim dṛṣṭa kāraṇa pratyākhyānam atha kāraṇa antara upapādanam atha ātmani utpatti nirodha kāraṇa anumānam atha ākasmika tvam iti 
NV_3.1.19^2	 tat yadi tāvat dṛṣṭa kāraṇa pratyākhyānam tat na yuktam dṛṣṭena viśeṣita tvāt yauvana ādi avasthāsu smita rudita vat tvam śoka ādimadātmavat tvam ca dṛṣṭam dṛṣṭena smita ruditavat tvena śoka ādimada ātmavat tvam bālya avasthāyām gamyate iti na doṣaḥ atha kāraṇa antara upapādanam tat api na yuktam atas eva dṛṣṭena viśeṣita tvāt iti atha ātmanaḥ utpatti nirodha kāraṇa anumānam tat na yuktam dravyasya sataḥ sarvadā amūrta tvāt akāraṇaḥ ātmā ākāśa ādi vat iti ātmānam ca kṛtakam pratipadyamānena kāraṇam asya vācyam kutas kāryasya kāraṇavat tvāt sarvam kāryam kāraṇa vat dṛṣṭam iti 
NV_3.1.20	 atha padma ādi prabodha sammīlana vikāraḥ akasmāt bhavati iti tat na uṣṇa śīta varṣā kāla nimitta tvāt pañca ātmaka vikārāṇām na ayam ākasmikaḥ padma ādi prabodha sammīlana vikāraḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ evam ca sati na kim cit dṛṣṭāntena pratiṣidhyate pañca ātmaka vikārāṇām iti na pañca ātmakāni padma ādīni api tu pañcānām bhūtānām anugrahe sati bhavanti iti pañca ātmakāni iti ucyante mukhyatas tu na pañca ātmakam asti iti upariṣṭāt vakṣyāmaḥ 
NV_3.2.21	 jāta mātrasya vatsasya pravṛttyā stanya abhilāṣaḥ gamyate stanya prāptau nivṛtteḥ pravṛtti anumeyaḥ stanya abhilāṣaḥ tena smṛtiḥ tayā saṃskāraḥ tena anubhavaḥ tena pūrva śarīram iti pūrvavat prayogaḥ kim artham punar idam sūtram ārabhyate yadā ayam arthaḥ pūrva abhyasta sūtre eva adhigataḥ sāmānyatas adhigatasya viśeṣa jñāpana artham sūtram iti adoṣaḥ 
NV_3.1.22–3.1.23	 pravṛtti mātrasya anaikāntika tva jñāpana artham ayasaḥ ayaskānta abhigamana vat tad upasarpaṇam iti sūtram na vikalpa anupapatteḥ kim idam ayasaḥ ayaskānta abhigamanam sa nimittam āho nirnimittam iti yadi sa nimittam tat kena avagamyate niyamena ayaḥ ayaskāntam eva upasarpati iti na tu loṣṭa ādīn na ca loṣṭa ādayaḥ upasarpanti saḥ ayam kārya niyamaḥ kāraṇa niyamāt gamyate etena ākasmika tvam pratiṣiddham tat idam ayasām upasarpaṇam kim dṛṣṭa kāraṇa pratyākhyāna artham upanyastam atha kāraṇa antara upapādana artham atha ātmanaḥ utpatti nirodhaka anumānam iti pūrvavat prasaṅgaḥ ākasmika tva pratiṣedha artham ca na anyatra pravṛtti abhāvāt iti sūtram 
NV_3.1.24	 nityaḥ ātmā vīta rāga janma adarśanāt na hi kaḥ cit jāta mātraḥ vīta rāgaḥ dṛśyate vīta rāgāṇām janma adarśanāt sa rāgaḥ jāyate iti gamyate janma vyākhyātam tatas kim rāgasya pūrva anubhūta viṣaya anucintanam yoniḥ na ca viṣaya avagamā samartheṣu indriyeṣu rāgaḥ sambhavati na ca smṛtim antareṇa pūrva anubhūta viṣaya anucintanam yuktam pūrva anubhūta viṣaya prārthanā saṃkalpaḥ adṛṣṭāt iti ced atha manyase na pūrva śarīra yogaḥ rāgāt gamyate api tu adṛṣṭāt rāgah iti nābhi prāya aparijñānāt na ayam abhiprāyaḥ kāraṇa niyamena rāgaḥ api tu pūrva śarīra sambandha mātra pratipādanam sūtra arthaḥ na ca adṛṣṭāt rāgaḥ iti bruvatā tat pratiṣidhyate iti kim cit uktam 
NV_3.1.25–3.1.26	 iti anaikāntika pakṣe sūtram na ukta uttara tvāt ukta uttaram etat atra api pūrvavat saṃkalpa smṛti saṃskāra anubhava pūrva śarīra vat ātmavat tvāni yojyāni iti tad maya tvāt rāgaḥ iti viṣaya abhyāsaḥ khalu ayam bhāvanā hetuḥ tad maya tvam ucyate jāti viśeṣāt ca rāga viśeṣaḥ iti karma khalu idam jāti viśeṣasya nirvartakam tādarthyāt tāt śabdyam labhyate vīraṇa ādi vat evam ca anādiḥ saṃsāraḥ apavarga antaḥ sidhyati iti vyavasthitam etat asti ātmā vyatiriktaḥ anekaḥ nityaḥ ca iti 
NV_3.1.27–3.1.29	 ātma anantaram śarīram avasara prāptam tat parīkṣyate atha vā anādiḥ cetanasya śarīra yogaḥ iti śarīram parīkṣyate tasmin parīkṣyamāṇe ātma adhikāraḥ eva ayam parisamāptaḥ bhavati iti kim punar asya parīkṣyam kim ghrāṇa ādi vat eka prakṛti uta nānā prakṛti iti vipratipatteḥ saṃśayaḥ śrūyate khalu atra vipratipattiḥ tatra idam tattvam pārthivam guṇa antara upalabdheḥ mānuṣam śarīram pārthivam iti mānuṣam iti kim artham viśiṣyate loka antara śarīrāṇi na pārthivāni iti yuktam viśeṣaṇam gandhavat tvāt paramāṇu vat gandhavān paramāṇuḥ eka ātmakah dṛṣṭaḥ gandha vat ca śarīram tasmāt eka ātmakam iti eka ātmakam iti eka svabhāvam iti na tu idam abādibhiḥ asaṃpṛktayā pṛthivī ārabdham ca iṣṭa indriya artha āśraya bhāvena kalpyate iti bhūta saṃsargaḥ avipratiṣiddhaḥ mithas pañcānām iti 
NV_3.1.30^1	 evam ca sati pārthiva āpya taijasam tad guṇa upalabdheḥ niḥśvāsa ucchvāsa upalabdheḥ cāturbhautikam gandha kleda pāka vyūha avakāśa dānebhyaḥ pāñcabhautikam iti pratyuktam tatra sannihitānām tad guṇa upalabdheḥ iti tat idam aneka bhūta prakṛti śarīram arasam agandham arasam arūpam asparśam ca prakṛti anuvidhānāt syāt iti bhāṣyam tasya vyākhyānam pṛthivī udakābhyām ārabhyamāṇam agandham kāraṇa gandhasya ekasya anārambhaka tvāt pṛthivī analābhyām ārabhyamāṇam agandham ca arasam ca kāraṇa gandha rasayoḥ kevalayoḥ anārambhaka tvāt pṛthivī anilābhyām agandham ca arasam ca arūpam ca vāyoḥ agandha rasa rūpa tvāt pṛthivī ākāśābhyām agandham arasam arūpam asparśam ca ākāśe gandha ādi abhāvāt sarvatra samānaḥ nyāyaḥ kāraṇa guṇasya kevalasya anārambhaka tvāt iti jala analābhyām agandham ca arasam ca jala vāyubhyām agandham ca arasam ca arūpam ca 
NV_3.1.30^2	 jala ākāśābhyām agandham arasam arūpam asparśam ca tejaḥ anilābhyām agandham ca arasam ca arūpam ca anala ākāśābhyām agandham arasam arūpam asparśam ca anila ākāśābhyām evam eva bhū jala analaiḥ agandham eva bhū jala anilaiḥ evam eva bhū jala ākāśaiḥ evam eva pṛthivī anila analaiḥ agandham arasam ca pṛthivī anala ākāśaiḥ evam eva pṛthivī anila ākāśaiḥ agandham arasam arūpam ca jala anala anilaiḥ agandham arasam ca jala anala ākāśaiḥ evam eva jala anila ākāśaiḥ agandham ca arasam ca arūpam ca anala anila ākāśaiḥ evam eva pṛthivī udaka tejaḥ vāyubhiḥ agandham pṛthivī udaka jvalana ākāśaiḥ evam eva pṛthivī jala anila ākāśaiḥ evam eva pṛthivī anala anila ākāśaiḥ agandham arūpam ca jala anala anila ākāśaiḥ evam eva pṛthivī udaka tejaḥ vāyu ākāśaiḥ agandham kāraṇa gūṇasya ekasya anārambhaka tvāt iti sāmānam eka kāraṇaka tve tu satata utpatti anupalabdhi nitya tva prasaṅgaḥ iti uktam 
NV_3.1.31	 sūryam te cakṣuḥ spṛṇomi iti asya mantrasya ante pṛthivīm te śarīram iti sā iyam spṛtiḥ kāraṇāt kāraṇāt kārya utpattim darśayati sūryaḥ cakṣuṣaḥ kāraṇam pṛthivī śarīrasya iti antya iṣṭa kāle ca mantraḥ sūryam te cakṣuḥ gacchatu pṛthivīm śarīram iti asya api mantrasya arthaḥ yat yasmāt āyātam tat tasmin eva pralayam gacchatu iti prakṛtau vikārasya pralaya abhidhānam pralaya śabdena ca kārya śūnyam kāraṇam abhidhīyate na punar kāryasya kāraṇe layaḥ pralayaḥ evam ca sati asat utpadyate sannirudhyate iti ayam arthaḥ uktaḥ bhavati 
NV_3.1.32^1	 atha idānīm indriyāṇi prameya krameṇa vicāryante kim āvyaktikāni āhaṃkārikāṇi āho bhautikāni iti saṃśaya kāraṇa pratipādana artham sūtram kṛṣṇasāre sati upalambhāt vyatiricya ca upalambhāt saṃśayaḥ kṛṣṇasāram bhautikam tasmin anupahate viṣaya upalabdhiḥ kṛṣṇasāra vyatirekeṇa ca viprakṛṣṭa deśa avasthitasya viṣayasya upalabdhiḥ sā iyam vyatireka upalabdhiḥ abhautika dharmaḥ tat evam ubhaya dharma upalabdheḥ saṃśayaḥ iti kṛṣṇasāram eva cakṣuḥ tasmin sati bhāvāt rūpa grahaṇasya yasmāt idam rūpa grahaṇam sati kṛṣṇāre bhavati asati na bhavati 
NV_3.1.32^2	 yat ca yasmin sati bhavati asati na bhavati tasya tat iti yathā kārya dravyasya rūpa ādayaḥ iti na pradīpa ādibhiḥ anekāntāt pradīpe sati rūpa upalabdhiḥ bhavati na ca pradīpasya rūpa upalabdhiḥ iti anekāntaḥ yasya ca kṛṣṇasāram cakṣuḥ tasya sannikṛṣṭa viprakṛṣṭayoḥ tulya upalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ kṛṣṇasāram ca viṣayam na prāpnoti aprāpti aviśeṣāt sannikṛṣṭa viprakṣṭayoḥ tulya upalabdhiḥ prāpnoti viṣayībhāvāt iti ced atha manyase sannikṛṣṭam asya viṣayī bhavati viprakṛṣṭam aviṣayaḥ evam ca na tulya upalabdhiḥ iti na ukta uttara tvāt ukta uttaram etat pratyakṣa sūtre iti 
NV_3.1.33^1	 abhautikāni iti apare mahat aṇu grahaṇāt mahat iti mahattaram mahattamam ca ucyate aṇu iti aṇutaram aṇutamam iti tat idam ubhayam cakṣuṣā upalabhyamānam bhautika tvam cakṣuṣaḥ bādhate bhautikam hi yāvat bhavati tāvat eva vyāpnoti abhautikam tu vyāpaka tvāt sarvasya vyāpakam iti na bhautikeṣu pradīpa ādiṣu dṛṣṭa tvāt bhautikāḥ pradīpa ādayaḥ mahat aṇvoḥ prakāśakāḥ bhavanti iti anekāntaḥ pradīpa ādi anabhyupagame vā mahat aṇu prakāśaka tvam cakṣuṣaḥ eva iti asādhāraṇa tvāt ahetuḥ bhautikā bhautikayoḥ nivṛtteḥ nanu ca abhautike vijñāne mahat aṇu prakāśaka tvam dṛṣṭam na dṛṣṭam na hi buddhyā mahat aṇunī prakāśyete api tu prakāśaḥ buddhiḥ na prakāśanam iti avadhāritasya tu arthasya hāna upādāna upekṣā buddhīnām sādhanam buddhiḥ iti nābhautikam mahat aṇu prakāśakam asti nanu ca manaḥ vidyate satyam manaḥ vidyate na punar tat bhautikam na api abhautikam iti etena ātmā vyākhyātaḥ na asau bhautikaḥ na api abhautikaḥ iti 
NV_3.1.33^2	 yadi manaḥ nābhutikam yat uktam bhautikāni indriyāṇi abhautikam manaḥ iti tat vyāhatam nābhautika tva arthasya abhūtātmaka paryāya tvāt abhautikam manaḥ iti abhūta ātmakam manaḥ iti yāvat uktam bhavati mukhyatas tu manaḥ na bhautikam na api abhautikam iti na indriye api samāna tvāt indriyam abhautikam iti abhūta ātmakam iti yāvat uktam syāt abhūta ātmakam vyāpakam ca indriyam pratipadyamānaḥ idam paryanuyojyaḥ vyavahita artha grahaṇam kasmāt na bhavati iti kim kāraṇam vyāpaka tvāt indriyasya kuḍya kaṭa ādeḥ āvaraṇasya na sāmarthyam asti iti vṛttiḥ pratibadhyate iti ced atha manyase satyam vyāpakam indriyam tasya tu puruṣa arthena hetunā kṣobhyamānasya mahā hradāt budbudāḥ tad vṛttayaḥ niścaranti tāḥ kuḍya ādibhiḥ pratibadhyante iti na vṛtti vyatirekeṇa indriyasya sattve pramāṇa abhāvāt yā iyam viṣaya grahaṇa ātmikā vṛttiḥ tām tyaktvā tad vyatiriktam indriyam iti kim pramāṇām 
NV_3.1.33^3	 na ca aprāmāṇikaḥ arthaḥ śakyaḥ pratipattum na ca pratibadhyamāna apratiṣidhyamānayoḥ ekatvam eka tve ca anarthakam vṛttiḥ pratibadhyate niścarati ca iti avyatirekāt ca tad utpatti vināśa dharmakam yadi ca vṛtti avyatireki indriyam yathā vṛtteḥ utpāda vināśau evam indriyasya api prāpnutaḥ vṛtteḥ vyaktiḥ naḥ utpattiḥ iti ced atha manyase na mayā vṛtteḥ utpattiḥ abhyupagamyate api tu vyaktiḥ na nirodhaḥ vināśaḥ api tu tirobhāvaḥ iti na utpatti viśeṣa tvāt vyaktiḥ utpatti viśeṣaḥ katham iti na anupajāta viśeṣasya vyaktiḥ iti atha anupajāta viśeṣam vyajyate iti manyase nityam vyaktiḥ syāt etena vināśaḥ vyākhyātaḥ tirobhāvaḥ iti vidyamānam na kim cit nivṛttam na hi anivṛtta viśeṣasya agrahaṇam sambhavati iti na ca sarva nitya tā vādinaḥ grahaṇa agrahaṇe yukte viśeṣasya anupajananāt na grahaṇam viśeṣasya anupacaryāt na agrahaṇam iti nityam vyāpakam ca indriyam abhyupagacchataḥ kāraṇa arthaḥ hīyate 
NV_3.1.33^4	 kāraṇam hi nāma yasya anantaram yat bhavati kāraṇam ca nityam kāryam ca nityam iti kim kasya anantaram kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ ca katham ubhayoḥ nitya tvāt kāraka śabda arthaḥ ca vācyaḥ nanu ca karoti iti kārakam satyam karoti iti kārakam na punar nitya vādinaḥ kim cit kartavyam asti na ca asati kartavye kāraka artham paśyāmaḥ vyaktau kāraka arthaḥ iti ced vyaktau api tulyam vyaktiḥ api vyaṅgya vat nityāḥ iti vyaktau api na kāraka arthaḥ asti yugapad aneka vijñāna prasaṅgāt ca yadi ca vṛttiḥ vṛttimataḥ na anyā bhavati vṛttimataḥ avasthānāt vṛttīnām avasthānam iti yugapad aneka vijñāna prasaṅgaḥ vṛtti aneka tve ca ekam indriyam anekam prāpnoti vṛttibhyaḥ ananya tvāt atha mā bhūt indriya bhedaḥ iti vṛttīnām tarhi eka tvam prāpnoti vṛtti vṛttimatoḥ ananya tvāt atha mā bhūt eṣaḥ doṣaḥ iti ubhayam naḥ iṣyate bhedaḥ tarhi vṛtti vṛttimatoḥ iti na ca anyā gatiḥ asti tasmāt ayuktam vyāpakam indriyam nityam ca iti 
NV_3.1.34^1	 mahat aṇu grahaṇasya ca anyathā siddheḥ ahetuḥ yaḥ api ayam hetuḥ mahat aṇu grahaṇāt abhautikāni indriyāṇi iti ayam api anyathā siddhiḥ na mahat aṇu grahaṇa mātrāt abhautika tvam vyāpaka tvam ca indriyāṇām śakyam pratipattum kasmāt yasmāt idam raśmi artha sannikarṣa viśeṣāt tad grahaṇam yasmāt raśmi artha sannikarṣa viśeṣāt mahat aṇvoḥ grahaṇam cakṣūraśmeḥ ca arthasya ca sannikarṣa viśeṣāt mahat aṇvoḥ grahaṇam bhavati tatra sannikarṣa mātrāt sāmānya grahaṇam sannikarṣa viśeṣāt viśeṣa grahaṇam kaḥ punar sannikarṣasya viśeṣaḥ 
NV_3.1.34^2	 bhūyas avayava sannikarṣa anugrahaḥ yasmāt ayam sannikarṣaḥ viśeṣa pratipatti hetuḥ bhūyobhiḥ avayava saṃyogaiḥ anugṛhyate saḥ ayam avayava antara saṃyoga apekṣaḥ avayavi indriya sannikarṣaḥ sannikarṣa viśeṣaḥ iti ucyate sa ca raśmi artha sannikarṣa viśeṣaḥ aṇoḥ mahataḥ ca tulyaḥ bhavati iti anyathā mahat aṇvoḥ grahaṇam sidhyati raśmi artha sannikarṣaḥ ca āvaraṇa liṅgaḥ kuḍya ādi vyavahitānām aprakāśaka tvāt aprāpya kāri tve tu na kuḍya ādeḥ āvaraṇasya sāmarthyam asti iti asti ca akṣaṣaḥ raśmiḥ yathā pradīpa raśmiḥ iti 
NV_3.1.35	 āvaraṇa anumeya tve sati idam āha tad anupalabdheḥ ahetuḥ na cākṣuṣaḥ raśmiḥ vidyate iti sūtra arthaḥ katham iti upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tvāt anumāna anupapattiḥ yat khalu upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam naḥ upalabhyate tat na asti yathā ghaṭa ādi ghaṭa ādeḥ mahat aneka dravyavat tva rūpāni upalambhakāni santi iti upalabhyante ghaṭa ādayaḥ tathā ca mahat aneka dravya rūpavān cākṣuṣaḥ raśmiḥ kasmāt pratyakṣataḥ naḥ upalabhyate iti vācyam mahat tvam tāvat kāraṇa mahat tva bahutva pracayebhyaḥ aneka dravyavat tvam api kāraṇa bahu tvāt eva rūpa sparśa vat dhi tejaḥ iti na arūpam tat evam aśeṣa upalabdhi kāraṇa sannidhāne sati yena naḥ upalabhyate tena gamyate na asti iti 
NV_3.1.36	 yat pratyakṣataḥ naḥ upalabhyate tat anumānena upalabhyamānam na asti iti ayuktam vaktum yathā candramasaḥ para bhāgasya pṛthivyāḥ ca adhobhāgasya iti yathā candramasaḥ pṛthivyāḥ ca para bhāga adhobhāgau upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptau api na pratyakṣataḥ upalabhyete na ca anumānena upalabdheḥ tau na staḥ kim punar anumānam arvāk bhāgavat tvam ubhaya pratipattau tathā cākṣuṣasya raśmeḥ kuḍya ādi āvaraṇam anumānam sambhavati iti 
NV_3.1.37^1	 apare tu mahat tvāt aneka dravyavat tvāt rūpāt ca upalabdhiḥ iti upalabdhau niyamam varṇayanti na upalabhyamānaḥ iti kim uktam bhavati na brūmaḥ yatra yatra mahat aneka dravyavat tva rūpāṇi santi tat tat upalabhyate iti api tu yat yat upalabhyate tatra tatra mahat aneka dravyavat tva rūpāṇi santi iti evam tarhi idam sūtram naḥ upalabdheḥ kāraṇa pratipādakam satsu abhāvāt iti satsu mahat aneka dravya rūpeṣu upalabdhiḥ na bhavati iti naḥ etāṇi upalabdhi kāraṇāni dravya guṇa dharma bhedāt ca upalabdhi niyamaḥ iti śeṣam bhāṣye kasmāt tarhi cākṣuṣaḥ raśmeḥ naḥ upalabhyate upalabdhi kāraṇa abhāvāt iti na etāvat eva upalabdhi kāraṇam yat uta mahat aneka dravya rūpāṇi api tu rūpa grahaṇena rūpa viśeṣah abhidhīyate na rūpa mātram evam ca sūtram aneka dravyeṇa dravyeṇa samavāyāt rūpa viśeṣāt ca rūpa upalabdhiḥ iti 
NV_3.1.37^2	 atra rūpa viśeṣa grahaṇena rūpa dharmaḥ udbhava samākhyātaḥ abhidhīyate na rūpa tvam rūpa antarāt rūpam viśinaṣṭi api tu udbhavaḥ viśeṣaka tvāt viśeṣaḥ iti ucyate yathā brāhmaṇa viśeṣaḥ iti na brāhmaṇa tvam brāhmaṇa viśeṣaḥ evam yat samāna jātīya viśeṣaka tvam tat viśeṣaḥ iti ucyate udbhavaḥ ca kārya gamyaḥ yasya abhāvāt viṣakta avayavam āpyam dravyam hemante na gṛhyate taijasam ca grīṣme yasya ca bhāvāt pradīpa raśmiḥ upalabhyate āditya raśmiḥ ca saḥ udbhavaḥ nāma rūpa viśeṣaḥ sa tasmin na ayane raśmau rūpa viśeṣaḥ na asti iti atas cākṣuṣaḥ raśminā upalabhyate iti dṛṣṭaḥ ca tejasaḥ dharma bhedaḥ caturvidham ca tejaḥ bhavati udbhūta rūpa sparśam yathā āditya raśmiḥ udbhūta rūpam anudbhūta sparśam yathā pradīpa raśmiḥ ubhayam ca pratyakṣam rūpasya udbhūta tvāt udbhūta sparśam anudbhūta rūpam yathā vāri sthitam tejaḥ anudbhūta rūpa sparśam yathā na ayanaḥ raśmiḥ ubhayam ca apratyakṣam rūpasya anudbhūteḥ 
NV_3.1.38^1	 śeṣam bhāṣye rūpa sparśa anabhivyaktiḥ ca vyavahāra prakpta arthāḥ yadi na ayanaḥ raśmiḥ udbhūta rūpa sparśaḥ bhavet tena dṛśya viśeṣe aneka raśmi sannipāte ca sati dravyam dahyeta aneka raśmi sannipāte ca sati vyavahita tvāt dravyasya anupalabdhyā bhavitavyam atha manyase yathā āditya raśmi sambaddhe arthe na ayanaḥ raśmiḥ na vyavadhīyate evam raśmi antara sannipāte api iti tat na vyatibhedāt anugrāhaka tvāt vyatibhidya āditya raśmim tad sambaddhena dravyeṇa sambadhyate udbhūta rūpa sparśavat tve ca cakṣuṣaḥ yasya pūrvam sannipatitam cakṣuḥ tad itareṇa avyatibhinnam iti na artham gṛhṇīyāt atha aneka raśmi sannipāte sati samāna jātīya dravyebhyaḥ dravya antaram raśmiḥ utpadyate iti evam ca samagrāsam agra cakṣuṣoḥ rūpa upalabdhiḥ samānā prāpnoti 
NV_3.1.38^2–3.1.39	 na ce etat iṣṭam anupalabdheḥ iti tena sarvaḥ vyavahāraḥ na kalpate vyavahāra prakpti artham ca na ayanasya raśmeḥ anudbhūta rūpa sparśa vat tvam iti sarva dravyāṇām ca viśva rūpaḥ vyūhaḥ puruṣa artha tantraḥ karma kāritaḥ iti karma tu dharma adharma bhūtam cetanasya upabhoga artham iti avyabhicārī tu pratīghātaḥ bhautika dharmaḥ bhautikam cakṣuḥ kuḍya ādibhiḥ pratīghāta darśanāt ghaṭa ādi vat iti apratīghātāt abhautikam iti ced atha manyase yadi pratīghātāt bhautikam apratīghātāt tarhi abhautikam iti dṛṣṭaḥ ca apratīghātaḥ kāca abhra paṭala sphaṭika antarita upalabdheḥ iti na anekāntāt pradīpa raśmi vat iti bhautikasya api apratīghātaḥ yathā pradīpa raśmeḥ iti sthālī ādiṣu ca pācakasya tejasaḥ apratīghātāt iti upapadyate ca anupalabdhiḥ kāraṇa bhedāt madhyandina ulkā prakāśa anupalabdhi vat tad anupalabdhiḥ yathā upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya madhyandine ulkā prakāśasya nimittāt agrahaṇam abhibhavāt tathā upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya cākṣuṣasya raśmeḥ agrahaṇam nimittāt rūpasya anudbhūteḥ iti 
NV_3.1.40	 madhyandina ulkā prakāśaḥ naḥ upalabhyate āditya prakāśa abhibhavāt iti ayuktam sarva raśmivat tva prasaṅgāt evam sati sarvam loṣṭa ādi raśmi vat prāpnoti atha loṣṭa ādi raśmayaḥ kasmāt naḥ upalabhyante iti atra anuyuktaḥ bruyāt āditya raśmi abhibhavāt iti etat uttara dvārakam sūtram na rātrau api anupalabdheḥ yadi loṣṭa ādi ḥ aśmayah syuḥ divā ditya prakāśa abhibhavāt ca naḥ upalabhyante iti rātrau tarhi upalabhyeran rātrau api naḥ upalabhyante vyañjaka abhāvāt iti ced na hi yat yasya abhibhāvakam tat tasya abhivyañjakam iti prāptaḥ loṣṭa raśmīnām upalambhaḥ anumānataḥ ca naḥ upalabhyate loṣṭe raśmiḥ iti api śabdāt gamyate tat evam sarva pramāṇa vinivṛttena vidyate loṣṭe raśmiḥ na punar evam cākṣuṣaḥ raśmiḥ niranumānaḥ kuḍya ādeḥ āvaraṇasya sāmarthyāt iti 
NV_3.1.41	 tasya vidyamānasya bāhya prakāśa anugrahāt viṣaya upalabdheḥ anabhivyaktitaḥ anupalabdhiḥ dṛṣṭānta sthāne eva etat sūtram kim uktam bhavati yat khalu bāhya prakāśa anugraham apekṣate tasya anupalabdhiḥ rūpasya anabhivyaktitaḥ iti anudbhūteḥ yathā viṣakta avayavasya api adravyasya rūpsyān udbhūteḥ agrahaṇam tathā cākṣuṣaḥ raśmiḥ bāhya prakāśa anugraham apekṣate tasmāt asya api rūpasya anudbhūteḥ agrahaṇam iti 
NV_3.1.42	 kasmāt punar na ayanasya raśmeḥ anupalabdheḥ abhibhavaḥ naḥ ucyate iti abhivyaktau ca abhibhavāt yat udbhūta rūpam bāhya prakāśa anugrahaṇam ca na apekṣate tat abhibhūyate yathā madhyandine ulkā prakāśaḥ anudbhūta rūpaḥ ca nāyanaḥ raśmiḥ bāhya prakāśa anugrahaṇam ca apekṣate yat anudbhūta rūpam tat na abhibhūyate yathā tat eva viṣakta avayavam āpyam dravyam yat ca bāhya prakāśa anugraha apekṣam udbhūta rūpam api tat na abhibhūyate yathā ghaṭa ādi dravyam iti saḥ ayam ubhaya viṣayaḥ abhibhavaḥ na ayana raśmau anupapannaḥ iti vipratipatti viṣayaḥ kṛṣṇasāram raśmi vat dravya tve sati rūpa upalabdhau niyatasya sādhana aṅgasya nimitta tvāt pradīpa vat iti atha vā raśmimat cakṣuḥ dravya tve sati niyatasya sādhana aṅga tve ca sati sphaṭika ādi vyavahita artha prakāśaka tvāt pradīpa vat iti 
NV_3.1.43	 iti dṛṣṭānta sūtram mānuṣam cakṣuḥ raśmimat aprāpti svabhāva tve sati rūpa ādi upalabdhi nimitta tvāt naktañcara cakṣuḥ vat iti jāti bheda vat indriya prabhedaḥ iti ced atha manyase viḍāla tvam jātiḥ vṛṣadaṃśe vartate na manuṣye evam raśmimat viḍālasya eva cakṣuḥ bhaviṣyati na mānuṣasya iti na āvaraṇa sāmarthyāt sati etasmin jāti bhede yathā vṛṣadaṃśa prabhṛtīnām kuḍya ādibhiḥ rāsmayaḥ āvriyante tathā manuṣyāṇām api iti samānam eva itas ca bhautikāni indriyāṇi pratighāti tvāt ghaṭa vat iti bhūtam śrotram dravya tve sati bāhya artha prakāśaka tvāt ghrāṇa ādi vat iti 
NV_3.1.44–3.1.46	 raśmi artha sannikarṣa viśeṣāt tad grahaṇam ayuktam anyathā api grahaṇāt aprāpya grahaṇam kāca abhra paṭala sphaṭika antarita upalabdheḥ tṛṇa ādi sarpat dravyam kāce abhra paṭale vā vyāhanyate yadi ca cākṣuṣaḥ raśmiḥ prāpta artha prakāśakaḥ syāt kāca abhra paṭala sphaṭika vyavahita artha prakāśakaḥ na syāt asti tu tasmāt na prāpya kāri cakṣuḥ iti atas eva ca abhautikam prāpya kāri tvam hi bhautika dharmaḥ aprāpya kāri tve indriyasya na kuḍya ādi āvaraṇasya sāmarthyam asti iti uktam śeṣam bhāṣye na kācaḥ abhra paṭalam vā raśmim viṣṭabhnāti saḥ apratihanyamānaḥ vyatibhidya arthena sambadhyate 
NV_3.1.47	 yat ca manyeta na bhautikasya asti apratīghātaḥ iti sarvam bhautikam pratīghāta dharmakam iti tat na āditya raśmeḥ sphaṭika antarite api dāhye avighātāt na āditya raśmeḥ avighātāt sphaṭika antarite api avighātāt dāhye api avighātāt avighātāt iti ca pada abhisambandhbhedāt vākya bhedaḥ na ekam vākyam aneka artham prativākyam ca artha bhedaḥ śeṣam bhāṣye kaḥ ayam avighātaḥ avyuhyamāna avayava dravya anupraveśaḥ yasya dravyasya avayavāḥ na vyuhyante tasya antara avayavaiḥ avyuhyamānasya yaḥ abhisambandhaḥ saḥ avighātaḥ iti antar vyavasthitasya vā dravyasya avyuhyamāna avayavasya bahis avasthita dravya prāptiḥ dṛṣṭam hi kalase niṣiktānām apām bahis śīta sparśasya grahaṇam na ca guṇasya asvatantrasya guṇinam antareṇa bahis nirgamanam yuktam iti tatra praspandaḥ tiryak gamanam parisravaḥ pātaḥ iti 
NV_3.1.48–3.1.49	 itara dharmaḥ itaratra prayujyate iti itara dharmaḥ ca itaratra yadi avighātaḥ cakṣūraśmeḥ sphaṭika ādibhiḥ kuṭādibhiḥ api prāpnoti kuḍya ādibhiḥ vā pratīghātaḥ iti sphaṭika ādibhiḥ api prāpnoti na eṣaḥ doṣaḥ ādarśa udakayoḥ prasāda svābhāvyāt rūpa upalabdhi vat tad upalabdhiḥ ādarśa udakayoḥ prasādaḥ rūpa viśeṣaḥ sa ca svar bhavati niyamāt kaḥ punar ayam rūpa viśeṣaḥ dravya antara asaṃpṛkta dravya samavāyaḥ tasya vā rūpa upalambhana sāmarthyam svar dharmaḥ sa ca svabhāvaḥ tasya yā vidyamāna todaka ādiṣu tat svābhāvyam prasāda svabhāva tvāt ādarśa udaka ādiṣu nayana raśmiḥ pratihanyate sa ca pratihataḥ pratinivṛtya sva mukha ādinā sambadhyate tasya ca agra sambandhāt yat abhimukham agram tat abhimukham mukha ādi paśyati iti yathā agratas vyavasthitasya puruṣasya iti ādarśa mukha grahaṇam tu krameṇa bhavat api āśu bhāvāt na vibhāvyate iti ādarśa rūpa anugrahaṇāt tad anurañcitaḥ pratyayaḥ śeṣam bhāṣye 
NV_3.1.50	 pramāṇasya tattva viṣaya tvāt dṛṣṭa anumitāḥ khalu ime dravya dharmāḥ yathābhūtāḥ bhavanti tathābhūtāḥ eva pramāṇena pratipādyante iti imau ca bhavatā niyoga pratiṣedhau deśitau kva viṣaye syātām na ca etat yuktam na hi yathā dhūmena agni pratipattiḥ tathā udaka pratipattiḥ api bhavatu iti na ca udaka pratipatti dhūmena bhavati iti agni pratipattiḥ api na yuktāḥ arthān ca niyuñjānaḥ bhavān upekṣaṇīyaḥ pratighāta apratighātayoḥ khalu upalabdhi anupalabdhī vyavasthāpike vyavahita upalabdhyā anumīyate sphaṭika ādibhiḥ apratīghātaḥ vyavahita anupalabdhyā ca kuḍya ādibhiḥ pratighātaḥ īt yadi prāpya kāri cakṣuḥ bhavati atha kasmāt añjana śalāka ādi naḥ upalabhyate iti na indriyeṇa asambandhāt indriyeṇa sambaddhāḥ arthāḥ upalabhyante na ca añjana śalāka ādi indriyeṇa sambaddham adhiṣṭhānasya anindriya tvāt raśmiḥ indriyam na adhiṣṭhānam na ca raśmiḥ añjana śalāka ādi sambaddhaḥ iti evam tāvat bhautikāni indriyāṇi iti vyavasthitam 
NV_3.1.51	 kim punar ekam indriyam āho anekam iti eke tu sthāna anya tve nānātvāt avayavi nānā sthāna tvāt ca saṃśayaḥ sthāna anya tve nānātvam dṛṣṭam yathā bahūnām ghaṭa ādīnām ekasya ca nānā sthāna tvam yathā avayavinaḥ iti anupapanna rūpaḥ ca ayam saṃśayaḥ katham iti yadi tāvat evam kriyate sthāna anya tve nānātva ekatva darśanāt iti tadā eka tve sthāna anyatvasya adarśanāt na samāna dharmaḥ atha nānā sthāna tve sati eka aneka tva darśanāt saṃśayaḥ iti tadā dravyam nānā sthānam anekam na kim cit dṛṣṭam iti na samāna dharma tvam yat tu ghaṭa ādi anekam na tat nānā sthānam api tu sthāna anya tvam tasya saḥ ayam saṃśayaḥ ubhayathā anupapannaḥ indriyeṣu sthāneṣu tu yuktaḥ kim nānā sthānāni uta nānā sthānam iti indriyeṣu tu na sthāna nānā tvāt sambhavati na api nānā sthāna tvāt iti śarīra vyatirekāt sattvāt ca saṃśayaḥ śarīra vyatiriktam ubhayathā dṛṣṭam ekam anekam ca yathā ākāśam ghaṭa ādi ca sat ca ubhayathā dṛṣṭam ekam anekam ca tat evam ubhayam ca indriyeṣu śarīra vyatirekaḥ sattvam ca tena sandihyate iti 
NV_3.1.52^1	 ekam indriyam kim punar tat tvac avyatirekāt kaḥ punar ayam avyatirekaḥ sarva adhiṣṭhāna sambandhaḥ na hi na kim cit indriya adhiṣṭhānam tvacā na prāptam sati bhāvaḥ vā na hi asatyām tvaci kim cit viṣaya grahaṇam bhavati tasmāt tvac ekam indriyam na indriya antara artha anupalabdheḥ iti loka virodhaḥ ekam indriyam iti bruvāṇaḥ lokam viruṇaddhi vidyamāne tvac indriye sparśa upalabdhi liṅge indriya antara arthāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ andha ādibhiḥ api upalabhyeran na tu upalabhyante tasmāt na ekam indriyam iti yat api avyatirekāt iti tat api na anekāntāt anekena ca anindriyeṇa sarvāṇi indriya adhiṣṭhānāni pṛthivī ādinā prāptāni iti anekāntaḥ avayava upaghātāt iti ced 
NV_3.1.52^2	 atha bhavet etat tvac avayavaḥ kaḥ cit upahataḥ bhavati tad upaghātāt andha ādibhiḥ naḥ upalabhyante rūpa ādayaḥ iti yathā tvac avayava viśeṣeṇa dhūma upalabdhiḥ yaḥ cakṣuṣi tvac avayava viśeṣaḥ tad upaghātāt dhūma sparśa anupalabdhiḥ iti na vyāghātāt tvac avayava viśeṣaṇa dhūma upalabdhi vat rūpa ādi upalabdhim bruvatā yat uktam ekam indriyam iti tat vyāhatam bhavati prāk ekam indriyam tvac iti abhyupagamya idānīm tvac avayava viśeṣāḥ rūpa ādi grāhakāḥ iti bruvāṇaḥ pratiṣedhyam abhyanujānāti na hi avayavi anatiriktāḥ avayavāḥ iti yān ca avayavān rūpa ādi grāhakān tvacaḥ manyase te kim indriya ātmakāḥ uta naḥ iti kim ca atas yadi indriya ātmakāḥ na ekam indriyam atha indriya ātmakāḥ na bhavanti na tarhi indriya grāhyāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ iti 
NV_3.1.53^1	 sūtreṇa ca abhisambandhaḥ na yugapad artha anupalabdheḥ yasya ekam indriyam tasya yugapad arthānām upalabdhiḥ prasajyate katham iti ātmā manasā sambadhyate manaḥ indriyeṇa indriyam sarva arthaiḥ sannihitaiḥ iti ātma indriya manaḥ artha sannikarṣebhyaḥ yugapad buddhayaḥ prāduḥṣyuḥ iti na ekaindriya grāhyāṇām yugapad upalabdhi prasaṅgāt yathā eka indriya vādinaḥ yugapad aneka artha sannikarṣe sati yugapad upalabdhiḥ doṣaḥ bhavati iti tathā aneka indriya vādinaḥ api eka indriya grāhyeṣu yugapad upalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ 
NV_3.1.53^2	 yaḥ eva atra parīhāraḥ saḥ eva mama api bhaviṣyati iti atha ayam aduṣṭaḥ pakṣaḥ acodyam tarhi etat yugapad upalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ iti atra ke cit parihāram varṇayanti bubhutsā bhedāt na yugapad upalabdhiḥ iti mama api evam yadi bubhutsā bhedāt na yugapad upalabdhiḥ labhyate mama api na bubhutsā bhedaḥ na daṇḍa vāritaḥ iti satyām ca bubhutsāyām ayugapad upalabdhau anyaḥ nyāyaḥ avadhāraṇīyaḥ iti karaṇa tvāt iti anye anye tu parihāram bruvate karaṇa tvāt iti karaṇasya kila ayam dharmaḥ adhiṣṭhitam api anekām kriyām na yugapad śaknoti kartum 
NV_3.1.53^3	 andhiṣṭhitam ca na pravartate iti tulyam yasya api ekam indriyam tasya api karaṇa tvam na nivāryate iti tasmāt yugapad artha anupalabdhiḥ iti adoṣaḥ ayam iti evam bruvāṇaḥ eka indriya vādī vikalpataḥ paryanuyojyaḥ yat tat ekam indriyam sarva artham iti manyase tat kim prāpya kāri āho naḥ iti kim ca atas yadi prāpya kāri kim tat iti vaktavyam yadi tvac tvacā aprāptānām rūpāṇām agrahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ atha aprāptam rūpam gṛhṇāti sparśa ādiṣu api evam prasaṅgaḥ atha sāmikārī indriyam kim cit prāptam gṛhṇāti kim cit ca aprāptam evam sati karaṇa dharma atikramaḥ bhavatu karaṇa dharma atikramaḥ kim naḥ bādhyate iti etasmin pakṣe na yugapad upalabdhi prasaṅgāt iti sūtram yathā aneka indriya vādinaḥ eka indriya grāhyeṣu yugapad upalabdhi para saṅge karaṇa tvāt iti parihāraḥ saḥ asyāḥ na bhavati karaṇa dharma atikrama abhyupagamāt vyāhatam ca etat karaṇam prāpya kāri ca aprāpya kāri ca iti asāha caryāt ca na tvac sāhacaryam nāma yasya ekam viṣaya grahaṇam tasya dvitīyam api iti andha badhira ādi abhāva prasaṅgaḥ 
NV_3.1.54	 śeṣam bhāṣye eka upaghāte tad vināśe vā sarva anupalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ atha ekam indriyam bhavati tad upaghāte tad vināśe vā sarva anupalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ āvaraṇa anupapattiḥ ca yadi tvac ekam indriyam bhavati na āvaraṇasya sāmarthyam asti iti vyavahita avasthita rūpa upalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ dūra antika anuvidhānam ca upalabdhi anupalabdhyoḥ na syāt aprāpya kāri tve tvac indriyasya antike grahaṇam dūre ca agrahaṇam iti etat na syāt 
NV_3.1.55^1	 pratiṣedhāt ca nānātva siddhau sthāpanā hetuḥ api upādīyate pratiṣedhāt nānātvam sidhyati iti na buddhyāmahe pratiṣedhāt eka tva sādhanam na syāt nānātvam tu katham sidhyati iti na asādhanā kriyāḥ iti eka tvam ca katham pratiṣeddhum śakyate pratiṣedhāt eka tva sādhanam anumānam nivartate na punar eka tvam aneka tvam vā nivartate iti katham tarhi ayam granthaḥ grāhyaḥ pratiṣedhāt ca anantaram nānātva siddhau sthāpanā hetuḥ api upādīyate indriya artha pañcatvāt atha vā pratiṣedhāt ca nānātva siddhau iti pratiṣedha hetunā eka tva pratiṣedhe kṛte arthān nānātvam sidhyati iti ayam arthaḥ katamaḥ punar asau pratiṣedha hetuḥ yugapad artha upalabdhi prasaṅgāt iti ayam anena eka tvam pratiṣiddham tat evam avīta siddhau vīta darśana artham idam ucyate indriya artha pañcatvāt iti sūtram arthaḥ prayojanam iti evam ādi bhāṣye 
NV_3.1.55^2	 idam ca sūtram na katham cana nyāyena sambadhyate katham iti vidhīyamānaḥ arthaḥ sādhyaḥ pañca indriyāṇi iti indriya artha pañcatvāt iti asambaddham atha prayojana pañcatvam tat api evam eva atha grahaṇāni pakṣīkriyante tatra api aikāntikaḥ hetuḥ na asti iti etena viṣayāḥ vyākhyātāḥ idam tu sūtram evam syāt rūpa rasa gandha sparśa śabdeṣu nānā sādhana kriyaḥ kartā eka viṣayau= asitau viṣaya antara siddhyai karaṇa antara apekṣi tvāt yasya kartuḥ anekaḥ viṣayaḥ tasya anyatama viṣaya avasāye viṣaya antara siddhau sādhana antara apekṣi tvam dṛṣṭam yathā aneka śilpa paryavadātasya puruṣasya ratha kriyā vasāye ghaṭa ādi kriyāyām karaṇa antara apekṣi tvam tathā ca rūpa ādi anyatama viṣaya avasāye viṣaya antara siddhyai sādhana antara apekṣi tvam asti iti tasmāt rūpa rasa gandha sparśa śabdeṣu nānā sādhana kriyaḥ kartā iti 
NV_3.1.56	 asya yathāśruti utthānam asya ca arthaḥ indriya pañcatva virodhaḥ na virodhāt artha bahu tvāt indriya bahu tvam prāpnoti iti bruvāṇaḥ yat abhyupagatam ekam indriyam iti tat bādhate nāsādhanāt na mayā artha bahu tvāt indriya bahu tvam sādhyate yatas me virodhaḥ syāt api tu bhavatā indriya artha pañcatvāt pañca indriyāṇi iti yat sādhanam uktam tasya mayā virodhaḥ deśyate yadi indriya artha pañcatvāt pañca indriyāṇi bhavanti indriya artha bahu tvāt bahūni indriyāṇi iti prasajyante iti 
NV_3.1.57–3.1.58	 asya uttara dvārakam sūtram gandha tva ādi avyatirekāt gandha ādīnām apratiṣedhaḥ iti gandha tva ādibhiḥ sva sāmānyaiḥ kṛta vyavasthāḥ gandha ādayaḥ na sva karaṇa vyatirekeṇa karaṇa antarāṇi prayojayanti yāvatsu gandha tvam vartate tāvatām eka sādhana sādhya tvāt yaḥ punar apara jāti bhedaḥ iṣṭa aniṣṭa upekṣaṇīya tva ādiḥ na asau karaṇa antaram prayojayati evam sarvatra śeṣam bhāṣye yadi sāṃānyam saṃgrāhakam prāptam indriyāṇām viṣaya tva avyatirekāt eka tvam asya api arthaḥ avirodhaḥ eva na ukta uttara tvāt indriya artha pañcatvāt iti asya arthena ukta uttaram etat 
NV_3.1.59^1	 asya ca arthasya jñāpana artham na buddhi lakṣaṇa adhiṣṭhāna gati ākṛti jāti pañcatvebhyaḥ iti sūtram tatra buddhayaḥ eva lakṣaṇāni iti asya arthaḥ varṇitaḥ indriya artha pañcatvāt iti nānā indriyam bhinna adhiṣṭhāna tvāt yasya adhiṣṭhānam bhinnam tat anekam dṛṣṭam yathā ghaṭa ādi adhiṣṭhāna bhedaḥ ca indriyāṇām asti tasmāt nānā iti adhiṣṭhāna bhedaḥ asiddhaḥ iti ced na asiddhaḥ andha badhira ādyabhāva prasaṅgāt iti yasya punar adhiṣṭhāna bhedaḥ tasya eka adhiṣṭhāna vināśe adhiṣṭhāna antara āśrayasya indriyasya avasthānam iti na doṣaḥ gati bhedāt api indriya bhedaḥ bhinna gati tvāt iti prayogaḥ pūrvavat ākṛtiḥ parimāṇam iyattā sva sthāna parimāṇāni ghrāṇa rasana sparśanāni 
NV_3.1.59^2	 cakṣuḥ bahis viniḥsṛtam viṣaya vyāpi tat mahat śrotram tu ākāśam tad adhiṣṭhāna niyamena pravartate dharma adharma saṃskṛtayā iṣṭa aniṣṭa upekṣaṇīya śabda sādhana bhūtayā karṇa śaṣkulyāḥ yaḥ ākāśasya sambandhaḥ tad sambandha anuvidhāyi ākāśam na vivara antareṇa asya ādinā śabdam upalambhayati na anyatra iti tad upakāra pratīkāra bhedāt vā upakriyate pratikriyate ca iti na punar ākāśam nitya tvāt upakriyate na pratikriyate iti prakṛṣṭa aprakṛṣṭa śrotra bhedaḥ api atas eva jātiḥ iti yonim pracakṣmahe pañca khalu imāḥ indriya yonayaḥ pṛthiva ādīni bhūtāni indriyāṇām yonayaḥ iti yoniḥ tādātmyam na punar tad kārya tvam ākāśe asambhavāt iti tat nitya tvāt 
NV_3.1.60	 katham punar jñāyate bhūta prakṛti indriyāṇi na avyakta prakṛtīni iti na ukta uttara tvāt na avyakta prakṛtīni indriyāṇi iti ukta uttaram etat bhūta guṇa viśeṣa upalabdheḥ tādātmyam bhūta guṇa viśeṣāḥ gandha rasa rūpa sparśa śabdāḥ viśeṣaka tvāt viśeṣāḥ iti ucyante yasmāt gandhena pṛthivī abādibhyaḥ viśiṣyate rasa ādibhiḥ ap ādayaḥ iti dṛṣṭaḥ hi bāhyānām ubhaya pakṣa sampratipannānām pṛthivī ādi bhūtānām sva guṇa abhivyakti niyamaḥ asti ca ghrāṇa ādibhiḥ api gandha ādi abhivyakti niyamaḥ tena bhūta guṇa viśeṣa upalabdheḥ bhūta prakṛtīni indriyāṇi iti kim kim ātmakam iti yena yat guṇa abhivyaktiḥ tatra pārthivam ghrāṇam gandha abhivyakti hetu tvāt bāhya pārthiva vat iti evam śeṣeṣu 
NV_3.1.61–3.1.62^1	 gandha ādayaḥ pṛthivī ādi guṇāḥ iti uddiṣṭam uddeśaḥ ca niyoga vikalpa samuccayaiḥ samānaḥ tatra niyogaḥ ekaika guṇa tvam vikalpaḥ kasya cit ekaḥ kasya cit dvau iti evam ādiḥ samuccayaḥ sarve sarvatra atas viśeṣaṇa artham gandha rasa rūpa sparśa śabdānām sparśa paryantāḥ pṛthivyāḥ ap tejaḥ vāyūnām pūrvam pūrvam apohya ākāśasya uttaraḥ niyama arthe sūtre catvāraḥ pṛthivyāḥ ekaikaśas apakarṣaḥ uttareṣu sparśa paryantānām iti vibhakti vipariṇāmaḥ tena kim kṛtam bhavati sparśa paryāntānām guṇānām viniyuktānām yaḥ uttaraḥ saḥ ākāśasya iti 
NV_3.1.62^2	 ākāśasya uttaraḥ śabdaḥ uttaraḥ iti ayam tarabniḥ deśaḥ na yuktaḥ dvayoḥ dṛṣṭa tvāt iha punar prakarṣa vāci tve sati uttamaḥ iti syāt na ayam bhoḥ tarabniḥ deśaḥ api tu para abhidhānam etat yat uktam bhavati paraḥ iti tat uktam bhavati uttaraḥ iti tarabh vā sparśasya vivakṣita tvāt bhavatu vā tarabniḥ desaḥ nanu uktam uttamaḥ iti prāpnoti na sparśasya vivakṣita tvāt gandha ādibhyaḥ paraḥ sparśaḥ para ādayaḥ paraḥ iti yāvat uktam bhavati tāvat idam uktam bhavati uttaraḥ iti 
NV_3.1.63–3.1.64	 na ayam guṇa viniyogaḥ sādhuḥ kasmāt pārthivena ghrāṇena pārthivānām gandha ādīnām upalabdhi prasaṅgāt evam āpyena rasanena trayāṇām taijasena cakṣuṣā dvayoḥ iti katham tarhi ime guṇāḥ viniyoktavyāḥ ekaika śyena uttara uttara guṇa sadbhāvāt uttara uttarāṇām tad anupalabdhiḥ yasmāt ekaika guṇāni bhūtāni tasmāt ekaika guṇa grahaṇam iti ekaikaśyenaḥ iti sautraḥ nirdeśaḥ katham tarhi aneka guṇāni bhūtāni gṛhyante iti saṃsargāt tu aneka guṇa grahaṇam saṃsṛṣṭa āba ādibhiḥ pṛthivī tasmāt aneka guṇāḥ gṛhyate iti evam śeṣeṣu 
NV_3.1.65–3.1.66	 saṃyogaḥ tu apratiṣiddhaḥ mithas pañcānām ca iti niyamaḥ tarhi na prāpnoti pṛthivyām catvāraḥ naḥ itareṣu saṃsargasya aniyamāt iti na na prāpnoti kasmāt viṣṭam hi aparam pareṇa aparam pareṇa viṣṭam ap ādinā na apareṇa pṛthivī ādinā parama bādi viṣṭam viṣṭa tvam saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ na pārthiva āpyayoḥ pratyakṣa tvāt iti na iti tri sūtrīm anantara uktām anena sūtreṇa pratyācaṣṭe yasya ekaika guṇāni bhūtāni tasya taijasam eva dravyam rūpavat tvāt pratyakṣam prāpnoti na pārthivam āpyam vai arūpa tvāt asya sūtrasya vikalpataḥ anekaḥ sūtra arthaḥ prakalpyate iti bhāṣye varṇitam 
NV_3.1.67	 tat eva nyāya viruddham pravādam pratiṣidhya na sarva guṇa anupalabdheḥ iti yat deśitam tat samādhīyate pūrvam pūrvam guṇa utkarṣāt tad tad pradhānam tasmāt na sarva guṇa upalabdhiḥ ghrāṇa ādīnām indriyāṇām pūrvam pūrvam indriyam yasmāt parasmāt parasmāt pradhānam kā pradhāna tā caturguṇa tva ādikāḥ kaḥ guṇa utkarṣaḥ sva guṇa abhivyakti sāmarthyam yena guṇena yat dravyam utkṛṣyate sa tad jātīya abhivyañjaka tvāt utkṛṣṭaḥ bhavati yathā bāhyāṇām dravyānām iti asti ca indriyāṇām api sva guṇa abhivyakti niyamaḥ tasmāt na sarva guṇa upalabdhiḥ yaḥ punar gandha guṇa tvāt ghrāṇam gandha grāhakam iti pratijānīte tasya sarva guṇa upalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ 
NV_3.1.68–3.1.69	 kasmāt punar na sarvam pārthivam ghrāṇam iti vyavasthā niyama jñāpana artham tad vyavasthānam na bhūyaḥ tvāt iti sūtram kim punar idam bhūyas tvam artha nirvṛtti samarthasya pravibhaktasya dravyasya saṃsargaḥ puruṣa saṃskāra kāritaḥ bhūyas tvam dṛṣṭaḥ hi prakarṣe bhūyas tva śabdaḥ yathā loke prakṛṣṭaḥ viṣayaḥ bhūyān iti ucyate tathā ca pṛthak artha kriyā samarthāni puruṣa saṃskāra upagrahāt viṣa oṣadhi maṇi prabhṛtīni dravyāṇi nirvartyante iti sva guṇāt naḥ upalabhante indriyāṇi kasmāt iti ced kena kāraṇena svān gandha ādīn indriyāṇi naḥ upalabhante iti sa guṇānām indriya bhāvāt saha guṇena indriyam indriyam bhavati nirguṇam tu naḥ indriyam atas na gṛhṇāti 
NV_3.1.70–3.1.71	 yadi punar indriyasya sahakārī ca gandhaḥ syāt grāhyaḥ ca iti tena eva tasya agrahaṇāt ca yadi indriyam sva gandham gṛhṇīyāt te na asau indriya gandhaḥ atha indriya gandhaḥ na indriya grāhyaḥ syāt gandham ca gṛhṇat indriyam ātmānam gṛhṇīyāt ātmā hi asya gandhaḥ iti na ca ātma sādhanam karaṇam asti iti dṛṣṭa virodhaḥ na ca etat pratyakṣam yat uta ghrāṇa gandhaḥ ghrāṇa grāhyaḥ iti kasmāt punar idam na deśyate ghrāṇena ghrāṇam kasmāt na gṛhyate iti na deśyate adṛṣṭa tvāt na dṛṣṭam ghrāṇena ghrāṇasya grahaṇam iti atas na deśyate iti tulyam ghrāṇena svasya gandhasya agrahaṇam iti etat api adeśanīyam sva guṇān naḥ upalabhante indriyāṇi kasmāt iti tulyaḥ hi ubhayatra pratipatti hetu abhāvaḥ sva guṇān naḥ upalabhante indriyāṇi iti etat ayuktam sva guṇaḥ upalabhyate śrotreṇa śabdaḥ iti 
NV_3.1.72^1	 satyam upalabhyate na punar śrotram sa śabdam indriyam iti yathā itarāṇi sa guṇāni indriyāṇi ne evam ākāśam iti kasmāt śabdasya itara guṇa vaidharmyāt ākāśasya itara dravya vaidharmyāt asya arthasya jñāpana artham tad upalabdhiḥ itaretara dravya guṇa vaidharmyāt iti sūtram na śabdaḥ śabdasya vyañjakaḥ na ākāśam sa guṇam indriyam iti kim punar idam śrotram ākāśam pariśeṣāt tatra ātmā tāvat na śrotram kartṛ tvāt śrotā ātmā na śrotram manaḥ śrotram bhaviṣyati iti api na manasaḥ śrotra tve bādhirya abhāvaḥ sarva viṣaya tvāt ca manasaḥ sarva viṣayam ca śrotram prāpnoti pṛthivī ādi api na śrotram ghrāṇa ādiṣu viniyogāt ghrāṇa ādiṣu viniyuktāḥ pṛthivī ādayaḥ śrotra bhāve ca ghrāṇa ādīnām tad vaikalye śabda anupalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ 
NV_3.1.72^2	 tvacaḥ śrotra bhāve badhira abhāvaḥ sarva upaghāte ca prāyaṇam diś kālayoḥ śrotra bhāve ca śabdasya anya guṇa tvāt agrahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ tad guṇa tvam eva iti ced nāmni vivādaḥ yasya śabdaḥ guṇaḥ tat ākāśam bhavatā tu saṃjñā mātram bhidyate tau diś kālau iti ākāśa pratyākhyānam ca anya guṇa tvāt śabdasya yadi tu śabdaḥ diś kāla guṇaḥ bhavati ākāśam tarhi pratyākhyātam na hi śabdam antareṇa ākāśa astitve liṅgam asti yathā diś kālayoḥ parāpara ādi liṅgam iti na ca dravya antaram śiṣyate na ca guṇānām śrotra bhāvaḥ yuktaḥ na ca karmaṇām na ca sāmānya viśeṣa samavāyānām sāmarthya anupalabdheḥ na ca idam śrotram na asti śabda upalabdhi liṅgam śiṣyate ca ākāśam tasmāt ākāśam śrotram iti 
NV_3.2.1	 parīkṣitāni indriyāṇi arthāḥ ca buddheḥ idānīm parīkṣā kramaḥ sā kim anityāḥ nityāḥ vā iti dharma vicāraḥ sattvasya adhigata tvāt tasyām ca saṃśayam upapādayati karma ākāśa sādharmyāt saṃśayaḥ ubhābhyām sādharmyam asparśavat tvam viśeṣaḥ upajanana apāya dharmaka tvam viparyayaḥ ca buddhau naḥ upalabhyate tatas saṃśayaḥ 
NV_3.2.2	 anupapanna rūpaḥ khalu ayam saṃśayaḥ sarva śarīriṇām pratyātma vedanīya tvāt sarva śarīriṇām pratykṣam etat yat uta anityā buddhiḥ iti traikālya vyakteḥ ca buddhau traikālyam vyajyamānam dṛṣṭam jānāmi jñāsyāmi ajñāsiṣam iti na ca upajana apāyau antareṇa traikālya vyaktiḥ na hi anupajana apāya dharmeṣu ākāśa ādiṣu traikālyam vyajyate na ca viśeṣa darśane sati yuktaḥ saṃśayaḥ tasmāt saṃśaya prakriyā anupapattiḥ iti śeṣam bhāṣye dṛṣṭi pravāda upalambha artham tu prakaraṇam na buddheḥ anitya tvam pratipādyam api tu parasya darśanam nivartanīyam iti evam hi paśyantaḥ pravadanti saṃkhyāḥ nityā buddhiḥ iti sādhanam ca pracakṣate viṣaya pratyabhijñānāt iti yam pūrvam ajñāsiṣam tam imam jānāmi iti jñānayoḥ samane arthe pratisandhānam avasthitāyāḥ buddheḥ upapannam buddhi nānātve tu pratyabhijñāna anupapattiḥ yathā puruṣa antara buddhiṣu 
NV_3.2.3^1	 yathā eva buddheḥ nitya tvam sādhyam tathā buddheḥ pratyabhijñānam api sādhyam kasmāt cetana dharmasya karaṇe anupapatteḥ puruṣa dharmaḥ khalu ayam jñānam darśanam upalabdhi bodhaḥ iti cetanaḥ hi pūrva jñātam artham pratyabhijānāti tasya etasmāt hetoḥ nitya tvam yuktam kriyā anādhāra tvāt ca karaṇasya na hi karaṇam kriyāyāḥ ādhāraḥ bhavati upalabdhiḥ ca kriyā sā ca na karaṇe bhavitum arhati iti sva kriyā ādhāra tvāt ayuktam iti ced atha manyase sarvam kārakam sva kriyāyāḥ ādhāraḥ bhavati iti atas ayuktam karaṇam kriyāyāḥ na ādhāraḥ iti satyam bhavati sva kriyādhāraḥ na punar sva kriyātaḥ karaṇa vyapadeśaḥ 
NV_3.2.3^2	 sva kriyāsu sarvam kārakam kartṛ bhavati karaṇa bhāvam ca āśritya buddhau vicāraḥ tasmāt ayuktam etat sarva kartṛ tva prasaṅgaḥ iti ced yadi punar sva kriyā nimittakaḥ kartṛ vyapadeśaḥ sarvam kārakam kartṛ prāptam satyam evam etat nābhyupagamāḥ eva doṣa tvena deśyante iti kartṛ karaṇa ādi vyapadeśaḥ ca katham pradhāna kriyā apekṣaḥ kartṛ karaṇa ādi vyapadeśaḥ yat artham karakam upādīyate sā pradhāna kriyā tasyāḥ sādhana bhāve sāmānyena vivakṣite bhede ca avivakṣite kārakam iti anena śabdena abhilapyante kartṛ ādayaḥ yadā tu bhedaḥ vivakṣitaḥ tadā kartṛ karaṇa karma śabda vācyāni iti 
NV_3.2.3^3	 kāraka śabdena api sāmānyena abhidhīyamāneṣu karakeṣu yaḥ sva gataḥ viṣayaḥ itaretara vyāvṛttaḥ saḥ abhidhīyate anyasya asambhavāt pradhāna kriyā vyapekṣam tu kārakāṇām kartṛ ādi abhidhānam iti tatra yat aparā prayojyam itara kāraka prayoktṛ ca tat kartṛ kārakam evam śeṣeṣu kāraka śabdāḥ pūrvavat vaktavyāḥ yadi anya kāraka prayojya tvam kartṛ tvam nanu ayam api kārakopādānena prayujyate na prayujyate phalasya prayojaka tvāt phalam kartāram prayojayati na kārakam karaṇa ādi na ca phalam kārakam iti teṣām tat na antarīyakam upādānam 
NV_3.2.3^4	 na hi karaṇa ādi kāra kopa ādānam antareṇa kriyā sambhavati iti tat na antarīyaka tvāt karaṇa ādīni upādīyante iti tasmāt cetana dharmaḥ karaṇe na sambhavati iti upetya pratyabhijñānam antaḥkaraṇe tasya eka aneka vyāvṛtteḥ asādhāraṇa tā na hi pratyabhijñānam eka tve dṛṣṭam na nānātve iti pratyabhijñāna svarūpa avadhāraṇe ca sati viruddhaḥ yadā ca idam pratyabhijñānam nirūpyate tadā buddhi bhedam pratipādayati katham iti pratyabhijñānam hi nāma ādya pratyakṣa nirodhe dvitīya darśane prāc āhita saṃśkāra abhivyaktau smṛti pūrvam tṛtīyam darśanam na ca buddhi abheda vādinaḥ dvitīyam api tāvat darśanam sambhavati kutas tṛtīyam iti 
NV_3.2.3^5	 pratyaya bhedaḥ iti ced atha manyase avasthitāyāḥ buddheḥ pratyayāḥ tirobhavanti vyajyante ca tatra ādya darśana tirobhāve pratyaya antara āvirbhāve ca pratyabhijñānam iti tat na yuktam tad vyatirekeṇa buddhi svabhāvān avadhāraṇāt yām tām pratyaya vyatiriktām buddhim bhavantaḥ kalpayanti tasyāḥ kaḥ svabhāvaḥ iti vaktavyam asmākam tu pratyaya mātram buddhiḥ artha grahaṇam hi buddhiḥ iti darśana dṛṣṭasya sparśanena pratyabhijñānāt nānātve pratyabhijñānam iti viruddhaḥ pradīpa antara dṛṣṭasya ca pradīpa antareṇa iti yadi buddhiḥ adhyavasyati atha buddhau vartamānena jñānena cetanaḥ kim karoti 
NV_3.2.3^6	 cetayate iti ced kaḥ cetayate yadi yasya adhyavasāyaḥ sa cetayate viruddham etat atha ātmā cetayate katham buddhau vartamānena pratyayena ātmā cetayate na hi anyatra vartamānayā kriyayā anyasya tadvat tā bhavati atha puruṣaḥ cetayate buddhiḥ jānīte iti na idam jñānāt artha antaram ucyate yāvat uktam bhavati cetayate tāvat uktam bhavati jānīte iti buddhiḥ jñāpayati iti ced atha manyase buddhiḥ jñāpayati ātmā jānīte iti addhā jānīte puruṣaḥ buddhiḥ jñāpayati iti adhyavasāya cetanayoḥ ca svabhāva bhedaḥ vaktavyaḥ 
NV_3.2.3^7	 bhavatā api eka tvam vaktavyam deśa kāla svabhāva abhedāt yasmāt avideśam avikālam ca buddhyā adhyavasitam ātmā adhyavasyati iti svabhāva abhedaḥ asiddhaḥ iti ced atha manyase satyam abhinna kālam abhinna deśam ca buddhyā adhyavasitam ātmā api adhyavasyati iti na punar yā eva cetanā saḥ eva adhyavasāyaḥ iti na pratiśarīram aneka puruṣa prasaṅgāt yadi anyaḥ cetayitā anyaḥ ca adhyavasātā bhavati anyaḥ pratijānīte anyaḥ paśyati anyaḥ śṛṇoti mantā iti evam ādiṣu puruṣa antarāṇi khalu imāni draṣṭā śrotāḥ mantā iti naḥ ekasya ete dharmāḥ iti tatra bhavatām kim vaktavyam 
NV_3.2.3^8	 abhinna arthāḥ ete śabdāḥ iti etat vaktavyam abhinna arthāḥ ced śabdāḥ bhavanti nanu atra api arthaḥ na bhidhyate cetanaḥ adhyavasātā mantā boddhā iti tasmāt ayuktam etat buddhiḥ adhyavasyati ātmā cetayate iti yadi punar idam pratyabhijñānam manasaḥ nitya tva sādhakam syāt na yuktam evam bhavitum manasaḥ nitya tvasya abhyupagamāt abhyupagamyate manasaḥ nitya tvam iti tatra sādhanam anarthakam anekāntāt ca na ca pratyabhijñānāt karaṇa eka tvam sidhyati dṛṣṭam karaṇa bhede api pratyabhijñānam jñātuḥ eka tvāt darśana dṛṣṭasya sparśanena pratyabhijñānāt pradīpa dṛṣṭasya ca pradīpa antareṇa iti 
NV_3.2.4–3.2.7	 yat ca idam manyate buddheḥ avasthitāyāḥ yathā viṣayam vṛttayaḥ prādurbhavanti vṛttiḥ ca vṛttimataḥ na anyāḥ iti etat ca na yugapad agrahaṇāt vṛttimataḥ avasthānāt vṛtteḥ avasthānam iti sūtra arthaḥ vṛttīnām apagame vṛttimataḥ api apagamaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ avibhu ca ekam manaḥ paryāyeṇa indriyaiḥ sambadhyate iti krama vṛtti tvāt ayugapad grahaṇam vṛtti vṛttimatoḥ nānā tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ vṛtti vṛttimatoḥ eka tve prādurbhāva tirobhāvayoḥ abhāvaḥ iti apratyabhijñānam ca viṣaya antara vyāsaṅgāt iti vṛtti vṛttimatoḥ bhede sati upapadyate iti eka tve tu anarthakaḥ vyāsaṅgaḥ iti 
NV_3.2.8^1	 vibhu tve ca antaḥkaraṇasya paryāyeṇa indriyaiḥ saṃyogaḥ na gati abhāvāt vyāptāni antaḥkaraṇena indriyāṇi iti sūtra arthaḥ vyāpi tve ca yugapad aneka indriya sambandhāt yugapad grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ doṣaḥ aṇau api manasi eka indriya grāhyeṣu yugapad upalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ iti ced karaṇa tvāt na yugapad grahaṇam mama api evam kasmāt na parihāraḥ na karaṇa bhede dṛṣṭa tvāt yāni khalu bhinnāni karaṇāni tāni ekena eva adhiṣṭhāyakena adhiṣṭhitāni yugapad pravartamānāni dṛṣṭāni yathā ubhaya hasta adhiṣṭhite vā asyau pravartete tathā ca indriyāṇi vyāpakena antaḥkaraṇena adhiṣṭhīyante iti yugapad pravṛttiḥ prasaktā tad prasaktau ca yugapad grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ iti gati abhāvāt ca vibhunaḥ antaḥkaraṇasya prāpti arthasya gamanasya abhāvāt na ayugapad pratyaya utpattau pramāṇam asti yena pramāṇena pratiṣiddham api pratyaya ayaugapadyam pratipadyeta yathā kim cit pratiṣiddham api pratipadyate yathā cakṣuṣaḥ gatiḥ pratiṣiddhā kena cit sannikarṣa viprakarṣayoḥ tulya kāla grahaṇāt 
NV_3.2.8^2	 yasmāt sannikṛṣṭam pāṇim viprakṛṣṭam ca candramasam ekasmin kāle cakṣuṣā pratipadyate tasmāt na gatimat cakṣuḥ iti pratiṣiddhā api satī gatiḥ vyavadhāna pratighātena anumīyate iti na ca yugapad pratyaya utpattau pramāṇam asti saḥ ayam na antaḥkaraṇe vivādaḥ na tasya nitya tve kva tarhi vivādaḥ tasya vibhu tve tat ca pramāṇataḥ anupalabdheḥ na asti na hi antaḥkaraṇasya vibhu tva pratipādakam pramāṇam asti ekam antaḥkaraṇam nānā ca imāḥ cakṣuḥ vijñāna ādi ātmikāḥ vṛttayah iti etat ca vṛtti vṛttimatoḥ eka tve anupapannam yasya punar vṛtti vṛttimatoḥ nānātvam tasya antaḥkaraṇa sādhanaḥ cakṣuḥ ādi sādhanaḥ ca ātmā arthān upalabhate iti yuktam etena viṣaya antara vyāsaṅgaḥ pratyuktaḥ puruṣaḥ jānīte na antaḥkaraṇam iti kaḥ punar ayam vyāsaṅgaḥ abhīṣṭa viṣayaḥ aneka vijñāna utpādaḥ sa ca puruṣasya na antaḥkaraṇasya yaḥ punar ayam sannidhāna āsannidhāna lakṣaṇaḥ antaḥkaraṇasya vyāsaṅgaḥ saḥ anujñātah iti 
NV_3.2.9^1	 ekam antaḥkaraṇam nānā vṛttayaḥ iti naḥ etat nyāya vid saṃcakṣāṇakaḥ pratipattum arhati yathā eva antaḥkaraṇam ekam tathā eva ekā vṛttiḥ iti dṛṣṭa virodhaḥ iti ced atha manyase yadi ca antaḥkaraṇāt na vṛttiḥ bhidyate na tu dṛṣṭam virudhyate rūpam rasaḥ gandhaḥ sparśaḥ iti dṛṣṭaḥ pratyaya bhedaḥ na syāt na na syāt viṣaya bheda anuvidhānāt vṛttiḥ abhinnāḥ api viṣaya bhedam anuvidhīyamānāḥ bhinnāḥ iva khyāti yathā upadhāna bhedam anuvidhīyamānam sphaṭika ādi dravyam bhinnam iva prakāśate asya ca arthasya jñāpana artham sphaṭika anyatva abhimāna vat tad anyatva abhimānaḥ iti sūtram na anekāntāt ubhayathā khalu ayam nānātva abhimānaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ nānā bhūteṣu ca gandha ādiṣu abhinne ca sphaṭike iti yathāśruti sūtre hetu abhāvaḥ dṛṣṭānta mātra tvāt dṛṣṭānta mātram etat na atra hetuḥ asti iti vikalpa anupapatteḥ ca 
NV_3.2.9^2	 yaḥ ca ayam dṛṣṭāntaḥ sphaṭika vat iti vikalpaḥ atra kim ayam sphaṭikaḥ upadhāna bhedena bhidyate uta naḥ iti kim ca atas yadi bhidyate na dṛṣṭāntaḥ atha na bhidyate nānātva abhimānaḥ katham yadi upadhāna bhedāt bhinnam upadhānam iti katham pratipadyate yadi pratyaya bhedāt vyāghātaḥ abhinnā vṛttiḥ pratyayaḥ ca bhinnaḥ iti vyāhataḥ pratyaya paryāya tvāt vṛtteḥ atha bhavatām vṛttīnām bhede kim pramāṇam jñānānām krameṇa upajana apāya darśanam krameṇa jñānāni upajāyante apayanti ca iti dṛśyate eka aneka viṣaya tvāt ca pratyaya nānātva abhimānasya eka aneka viṣaya adhigatiḥ katham ekasmin ca viṣaye nānātva abhimānaḥ sphaṭike dṛṣṭaḥ nānā bhūteṣu ca gandha ādiṣu nānātva abhimānaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tena nānātva abhimānasya ubhayathā dṛṣṭa tvāt idam ekam idam anekam iti na yuktaḥ pratyayaḥ iti 
NV_3.2.9^3	 yaḥ ca ayam abhinne sphaṭike bheda pratyayaḥ saḥ api pratyaybhedam antareṇa na yuktaḥ na hi pratyaya abheda vādinaḥ sphaṭike nīla ādi pratyaya bhedaḥ yuktaḥ iti sphaṭike nīla ādi pratyayaḥ asambandhāt na yuktaḥ na hi nīlam dravyam cakṣuḥ sannikṛṣṭam iti atha sannikṛṣṭam tat eva nīlam na sphaṭikaḥ iti sphaṭika samāna adhikaraṇaḥ sphaṭike nīla pratyayaḥ na yuktaḥ na nairantarya darśanāt nairantaryeṇa avasthite sphaṭika nīla dravye cakṣuṣā sannikṛśyete tatas sannikarṣāt nīla guṇa adhyāropeṇa sphaṭike mithyā pratyayaḥ nīlaḥ iti yathā sāntareṣu antarāla adarśanāt saṃyukta pratyayaḥ iti yasya ca pratyayaḥ na bhidyate tasya trīṇi pramāṇāni iti śāstram vyāhanyate na hi pratyaya abhede pramāṇa bhedaḥ sambhavati viṣaya bhedāt tritvam iti ced 
NV_3.2.9^4	 atha manyase viṣayaḥ tredhā bhinnaḥ tena anurañjitaḥ pratyayaḥ tredhā eva bhavati tat na yuktam pramāṇa abhede viṣaya bhedān adhigateḥ na hi pramāṇa bhedam antareṇa viṣaya bhedaḥ adhigantum śakyate iti viṣaya tādātmyāt iti ced atha manyase viṣayaḥ eva asau tathā vyavasthitaḥ tādātmyāt tathā khyāti iti tat na pramāṇa vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt evam ca sati vyartham pramāṇam na viṣaya bhedam pramāṇa bhedaḥ avagamayati viṣayaḥ tu tādātmyāt tathā vyavatiṣṭhate iti yathā adhyavasyati tathā cetayate iti ca vyāghātaḥ aprakāravat tvāt prakāravati etat yuktam aprakāre na yuktam buddhiḥ tam pratyayam upalabhate iti ca virodhaḥ adhikaraṇa ādheyayoḥ abhedāt yaḥ pratyayaḥ sā buddhiḥ iti adhikaraṇa ādheyayoḥ abhedaḥ evam ca sati buddhi stham pratyayam upalabhate iti vyāhatam 
NV_3.2.10	 sphaṭika anyatva abhimāna vat tad anyatva abhimānaḥ iti etat amṛṣyamāṇaḥ kṣaṇika vādī āha sphaṭike api apara apara utpatteḥ kṣaṇika tvāt vyaktīnām ahetuḥ sphaṭikasya abhedena avasthitasya anyatva abhimānaḥ iti ayuktam kṣaṇika tvāt vyaktīnām kṣaṇika tvam upacaya apacaya prabandha darśanāt yasmāt śarīra ādiṣu pakti nirvṛttam rasa dravyam pratikṣaṇam upacīyate ca apacīyate ca upacayāt vyaktīnām utpādaḥ apacayāt vyakti nirodhaḥ tau ca utpāda nirodhau asya kāla antareṇa dṛṣṭau atas avagamyate pratikṣaṇam upacīyate ca apacīyate ca śarīram iti yasya khalu pratikṣaṇam upacaya apacayau na dṛṣṭau tasya kāla antareṇa api na bhavataḥ yathā bhūmeḥ apacyamānāyāḥ pāka jānām iti pacyamāna bhūmi pākaja vat ca pratikṣaṇam viśeṣaḥ iti asya prayogaḥ pratikṣaṇam śarīram anyat ca anyat ca bhavati bāhya pratyaya abhede sati ante viśeṣa darśanāt pacyamāna bhūmi pākaja vat apacyamāna bhūmi pākaja vat ca iti 
NV_3.2.11^1	 tat idam upacaya apacaya prabandha darśanam śarīre dṛṣṭa tvāt śarīrasya anya tvam sādhayatu na punar anupalabhyamāna upacaya apacaya viśeṣāṇām sphaṭika ādīnām etasmāt anya tvam sidhyati iti ahetuḥ yatra upalabdhiḥ tasya anya tvam iti ced atha manyase naḥ eva asmābhiḥ upacaya apacaya prabandha darśanena sarva bhāvānām kṣaṇika tvam sādhyate api tu yatra tat asti tasmin kṣaṇika tvam iti satyam yasya yasya upacaya apacaya prabandhaḥ upalabhyate tasya tasya anya tvam iti na tu kṣaṇika tvam upacaya apacaya prabandha darśanam ca anyathā bhavat ahetuḥ kṣaṇika tve 
NV_3.2.11^2	 katham anyathā pūrvśarīra avayava sahitāḥ āhāra avayavāḥ pūrva vyūha parityāgena vyūha antaram āpadyamānāḥ śarīra antaram utpādayanti iti yuktaḥ bhedaḥ iti ahetuḥ eṣaḥ tulyam pakṣa pratijñānam iti ced atha manyase apūrva āhāra avayava upayoge sati śarīra avayavāḥ śarīra antaram ārabhante pūrva vyūha parityāgena na punar kṣaṇika tvāt anyat jātam iti atra kaḥ hetuḥ iti nāsādhanāt na mayā āhāra upacaya apacaya yogāt śarīrasya anya tā sādhyate api tu bhavatā viśeṣa darśanāt śarīrasya anya tvam abhyadhāyi tatas ca kṣaṇika tvam iti viśeṣa darśanam kṣaṇika tva sādhanam tat asmābhiḥ viśeṣa darśanam anyathā bhavat kṣaṇika tve na sādhanam iti etāvat mātrakam ucyate na sādhanam abhidhīyate iti 
NV_3.2.12^1	 atha avaśyam sādhanam vaktavyam idam brūmaḥ naḥ utpatti vināśa kāraṇa upalabdheḥ utpatti kāraṇam vināśa kāraṇam ca upacaya apacayau valmīka ghaṭa ādīnām dṛṣṭau iti tat ubhayam kṣaṇika tve na syāt upacayaḥ iti ca vṛddhiḥ avardhata gauḥ iti apacayaḥ iti hrāsaḥ apacitaḥ gauḥ iti ubhayam ca etat avasthita vastu viṣayam na hi apūrvam jāyamānam vardhate iti ucyate na api vinaśyat apacitam iti ucyate upacaya apacaya utpatti vināśa kāraṇa upalabdheḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ athavā kāraṇam iti ādhāraḥ abhidhīyate kāryam iti ādheyam na ca kṣanika tve ādhāra ādheya bhāvaḥ sambhavati na ca ādhāra ādheya bhāvam antareṇa kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ tasmāt kārya kāraṇa bhāva upalabdheḥ akṣaṇika tvam iti asya prayogaḥ 
NV_3.2.12^2	 kārya kāraṇe eka kāla anubhāvinī ādhāra ādheya bhāvāt kṣīrakuṇḍa vat iti kṣīram kuṇḍe vartate tat ca kuṇḍakālam anubhavati tathā ca kāryam kāraṇe vartate iti tasmāt tat api kāraṇa kālam anubhavati na ādhāra ādheya bhāvasya asiddha tvāt iti ced atha manyase asiddhaḥ kārya kāraṇayoḥ ādhāra ādheya bhāvaḥ kāryasya anādhāra tvāt na eva hi naḥ kim cit kāryam ādhāra vat dṛṣṭam iti na anekāntāt na ayam ekāntaḥ sarvam kāryam anādhāram iti yathā ubhaya pakṣa sampratipattyā rūpam kāryam ca ādhāra vat ca sparśaḥ tad āśrayaḥ iti vyāghātaḥ yadi ca rūpam anāśritam bhavati sparśaḥ tad āśrayaḥ iti vyāhatam anena ca rūpa dṛṣṭāntena yāvat yāvat samāna kāla tayā sādhyate sarvam tat eka kāla anubhāvi bhavati iti siddhaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ kṣaṇikeṣu api 
NV_3.2.12^3	 nāśa utpādayoḥ eka kāla tvāt tulā anta nāma unnāma vat iti ced atha manyase kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ kṣaṇikeṣu api sambhavati iti kāraṇa vināśa sama kālam kārya bhāvāt yadā kāraṇam vinaśyati tadā kāryam utpadyate iti vinaśyat ca kāraṇam asti kāraṇa vināśena ca abhinna kālaḥ kārya utpādaḥ yathā tulāyāḥ antayoḥ nāma unnāmau iti na hetu artha aparijñānāt na brūmaḥ kṣaṇikeṣu kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ na asti api tu kṣaṇikeṣu ādhāra ādheya bhāvaḥ bhinna kāla tvāt kārya kāraṇayoḥ na yuktaḥ kāryam ca anādhāram iti na dṛṣṭāntaḥ asti asmat pakṣe kāryam ādhāra vat iti asti dṛṣṭāntaḥ rūpa ādi tulādhārasya ca karmaṇaḥ nāma unnāma bhāvena anabhyupagamāt yugapad bhāva anupapattiḥ eka tvāt yadi tāvat tulām adhikṛtya bravīṣi tadā ekam karma bhramaṇa ākhyam eka tvāt ca yugapad bhāvaḥ na yuktaḥ 
NV_3.2.12^4–3.2.13	 na hi ekam yugapad bhavati iti atha avayava karmaṇī tayoḥ api kārya kāraṇa bhāvena anabhyupagamāt kim kena sambadhyate atha yugapad bhāva mātram vivakṣitam iti yugapad bhāvaḥ kāraṇa yaugapadyāt yāvatām arthānām kāraṇāni yuga padyena bhavanti tāvatām ekasmin kāle bhavaḥ iti nāma unnāmau asambaddhau kāraṇa yaugapadyam tu guru tva prayatna saṃyogāḥ unnateḥ avanateḥ api guru tva vat dravya saṃyoga anugṛhītaḥ rajju tulā saṃyogaḥ atha api na karma artha antaram saṃyogam vā paraḥ pratipadyate tasya api uktam uttaram saṃyogaḥ api artha antaram iti saṃyoga kāraṇa tvena ca karma api artha antaram iti yathā ca bhāvānām utpatti vināśa kāraṇam upalabhyate naḥ evam sphaṭikasya na ca anupalabhyamānam śakyam abhyanujñātum iti yathā kṣīrasya vināśa kāraṇam anupalabhyamānam abhyanujñāyate dadhnaḥ ca utpatti kāraṇam evam sphaṭika ādi vyaktīnām upalabhyamāne utpatti vināśa kāraṇe abhyanujñeye iti 
NV_3.2.14^1	 yat liṅgataḥ upalabhyate na tat na asti iti viparyayaḥ tu sphaṭika ādiṣu na hi sphaṭika ādi vyaktīnām apara apara utpattau liṅgam asti iti na na asti śīta uṣṇa sparśa bhedasya nānā tva sādhana tvāt śīta uṣṇa sparśa bhedaḥ nānātve dṛṣṭaḥ yathā agnau udake ca asti ayam śīta uṣṇa sparśa bhedaḥ sphaṭike sa tu nimitta antarāt bhavati kim punar nimittam ap tejaḥ avayava anupraveśaḥ udaka avayava anupraveśāt śītaḥ tejaḥ avayava anupraveśāt ca uṣṇaḥ iti ap tejaḥ avayava anupraveśaḥ na yuktaḥ alpatara bahutara anupraveśe hetu abhāvāt hemante hi ākāśe paryuṣitānām kāṣṭha bhūmi aśma lohānām śaityasya uttarottara viśeṣaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tathā punar grīṣma ātapa santāpitānām teṣām eva āuṣṇyasya na hi teṣu alpatara bahutara praveśe kāraṇam paśyāmaḥ 
NV_3.2.14^2	 tasmāt sva gata mahābhūta viśeṣa apekṣāṇi āsādita bāhya nimittāni bhūtāni eva tathā tathā utpadyante iti yuktam na yuktam na hi ap tejaḥ avayava anupraveśena bhūta svabhāvaḥ nivāryate bhūta svabhāvasya ubhaya pakṣa sāmyāt asādhanam bhūta svabhāvaḥ iti viruddhaḥ ca ayam hetuḥ yadi avayava anupraveśam na pratipadyase khara sneha uṣṇa īraṇa ātmakāni bhūtāni iti vyāhanyate katham iti yat kaṭhinam tat ekasmin kāle uṣṇam api bhavati iti yat ca uṣṇam tat kaṭhinam gacchati iti tat ekam vastu dvi svabhāvakam tri svabhāvakam ca prāpnoti yasya punar avayava anupraveśaḥ tasya eṣaḥ doṣaḥ na asti anyatra avasthitasya saṃyukta samavetasya auṣṇyasya grahaṇāt iti viruddhaḥ ca ayam hetuḥ katham ekasya viśeṣa abhyupagamāt ekam tat vastu ekasmin kāle kaṭhinam uṣṇam gacchati ca iti tri svabhāvakam 
NV_3.2.14^3	 tatas ca viśeṣa darśanāt iti ayam hetuḥ siddhāntam abhyupetya tad virodhī viruddhaḥ iti viruddhaḥ bhavati atha manyase na viśeṣa mātram nānātvam pratipādayati api tu virodhī viśeṣaḥ nānātve sādhanam iti nābhi prāya aparijñānāt vayam api na brūmaīḥ viśeṣa mātram nānātvam api tu bhūtānām yaḥ viśeṣaḥ itaretara vyāvṛttaḥ lakṣaṇa tvena upāttar sa viruddhaḥ yadi aviruddhaḥ syāt na lakṣaṇam syāt eka vṛtti tve vā lakṣaṇa trayasya tat tat vastu kim abhidhīyate yadi tāvat pṛthivī tat na yuktam auṣṇyasya darśanāt atha tejaḥ tat api na yuktam kāṭhinyasya darśanāt etena vāyuḥ vyākhyātaḥ saḥ ayam hetu bhūta lakṣaṇam vā bādhate nānā tva sādhanam vā na bhavati etena jale tāpa viśeṣa grahaṇam pratyuktam 
NV_3.2.14^4	 tatra api auṣṇyam snigdha teraṇa bhāvaḥ ca yugapad bhavati iti jale agni rūpa grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ tu na yuktaḥ abhibhavāt tat na siddhānta aparijñānāt na ayam siddhāntaḥ jala rūpena agni rūpam abhibhūyate iti api tu tejasaḥ cāturvidhyāt tatra na rūpa agrahaṇam caturvidham tejaḥ iti etat pratipāditam indriya prakaraṇe iti yā ca iyam pratijñāḥ anyaḥ ca anyaḥ ca sphaṭikaḥ iti asyāḥ ca kaḥ arthaḥ yadi tāvat anya tva mātram tatas siddha sādhanam bhavati stambha ādibhyaḥ anyaḥ sphaṭikaḥ iti atha sphaṭika antarāt anyaḥ iti etat api tādṛś eva atha pūrva sphaṭikāt anyaḥ katamaḥ asau pūrvaḥ sphaṭikaḥ yatas ayam anyaḥ iti vyavacchedasya aśakya tvāt anabhidhānam yathā ubhaya pakṣa sampratipannāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ tebhyaḥ anya an anya vicāraḥ ghaṭa ādeḥ yuktaḥ 
NV_3.2.14^5	 na punar iha pūrva sphaṭika antaram ubhaya pakṣa sampratipannam yatas vartamānaḥ anya tvena sādhyate atha ubhaya pakṣa sampratipannam pūrvam sphaṭika antaram vyartham sādhanam atha vartamānam sphaṭikam abhyupagamya yat atītam sphaṭika antaram tat anyat iti sādhyate evam sati śīta uṣṇa sparśa bhedaḥ na tad dharmaḥ vartamāna sphaṭika dharma tvāt vartamānāt ca sphaṭikāt anyat atītam sphaṭika antaram iti kena etat na pratipannam atha tat eva anyat iti vyāghātaḥ tat eva anyat ca iti evam yathā yathā anya tvam vicāryate tathā tathā siddha sādhanam bhavati siddhāntam ca bādhate iti atha ayugapad kāla pratyayānām ālambanam sphaṭikaḥ na bhavati iti ayam pratijñā arthaḥ etasmin api pratijñā arthe na dṛṣṭāntaḥ asti na na asti pradīpa ādiḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti 
NV_3.2.14^6	 pradīpaḥ ayugapadtkāla pratyaya anālambanam sat ādi dharmāḥ ca iti vidyate dṛṣṭāntaḥ na asiddha tvāt asiddham etat ayugapad kāla pratyaya anālambanāḥ pradīpa ādayaḥ teṣām aneka kṣaṇa avasthānāt pradīpasya tāvat sva kāraṇa sattā sambandha kālaḥ sāmānya abhivyakti kālaḥ avayava karma kālaḥ tad anantaram tad vināśa kālaḥ tad anantaram tad saṃyoga vināśa kālaḥ tatas dravya nāśaḥ iti yathā ca pradīpaḥ evam sarve bhāvāḥ sva kāraṇa sattā sambandha abhivyakti tad virodhyāśraya vināśa anuvidhānena vinaśyanti akāraṇasya vināśānasya anabhyupagamāt na hi naḥ kim cit niṣkāraṇam vinaśyati iti vinaśyat avastha dravya karma vat etat syāt na karmaṇaḥ anabhyupagame virodhāt anabhyupagamāt ca vināśa hetu abhāvāt iti ced atha manyase na atra vināśasya kāraṇam asti tasmāt utpanna mātraḥ eva ayam bhāvaḥ vinaśyati iti 
NV_3.2.14^7	 na vikalpa anupapatteḥ vināśasya hetuḥ na asti iti bruvāṇaḥ paryanuyoktavyaḥ kim akāraṇa tvāt vināśaḥ na asti uta akāraṇa tvāt nityaḥ iti bhavatām pakṣe akāraṇam dvedhā nityam asat ca asmākam tu nityam eva tat yadi akāraṇa tvāt nityaḥ vināśaḥ kāryasya utpādaḥ na prāpnoti anutpannasya ca vināśaḥ bhāvasya vināśaḥ na saha avasthānam iti ca doṣaḥ tatas ca bhāvānām abhāva virodhi tvāt atyanta avasthānam iti atha āsan vināśaḥ evam api sarva nitya tvam vināśa abhāvāt yadi ca āsan vināśaḥ vinaśyati iti asati vināśe pratyayaḥ na prāpnoti nāsatyām gatau gacchati iti bhavati atha avināśi tvāt akāraṇaḥ vināśaḥ iti manyase vināśaḥ na vinaśyati iti kutas etat vinaṣṭānām punar anutpatteḥ iti ced 
NV_3.2.14^8	 atha manyase yadi vināśaḥ vinaśyet vinaṣṭaḥ punar utpadyate na yuktam etat na hi vināśa abhāva abhāvaḥ bhāvaḥ yatas asya vināśa avināśāt bhavet api tu kāraṇavān bhāvaḥ tasya yadā kāraṇam bhavati tadā utpādaḥ iti api ca vināśaḥ kāraṇavān ca na ca vinaśyati abhāva tvāt bhāva dharmaḥ eṣaḥ yat kāraṇa vat tat vinaśyati iti abhāvaḥ tu akāraṇaḥ api vinaśyati yathā prāgbhāvaḥ kāraṇavān api na vinaśyati yathā pradhvaṃsa abhāvaḥ yadi kāraṇavān vināśaḥ nanu janakam vināśakam prāpnoti yaḥ eva agni saṃyogaḥ pāka jānām utpādayitā saḥ eva pāka ja antara utpāde pūrva pāka jān ucchinatti iti janakam vināśakam prāptam na anavarodhāt na idam bhavatā kāśyapī iyam darśanam vyajñāyi na hi naḥ yaḥ eva agni saṃyogaḥ pāka jān utpādayati saḥ eva ca ucchinatti 
NV_3.2.14^9	 api tu agni saṃyoga antaram pūrvarūpa ādīn ucchinatti tad sama kālam rūpa ādīn ārabhate tatas tāni api anyaḥ tāni api anyaḥ iti evam janakasya vināśaka tva prasaṅgaḥ na asti atha manyase janaka sarūpam api vināśakam na bhavati iti na na bhavati dṛṣṭaḥ hi ap ādi saṃyogāt aṅkurasya utpādaḥ saḥ eva ābādi saṃyogaḥ tad vināśakaḥ iti na asti dṛṣṭe anupapannam nāma yaḥ ca akāraṇe vināśe doṣaḥ saḥ aparihāryaḥ iti atas evam ucyate janaka sarūpam vināśakam iti evam tāvat anya tve sādhye doṣaḥ uktaḥ ye tu kṣaṇika tvam sādhayanti ante viśeṣa darśanāt vināśa hetu abhāvāt ca tān prati idam ucyate kṣaṇikāḥ saṃskārāḥ iti bruvāṇaḥ kṣaṇika śabda artham praṣṭavyaḥ kim uktam bhavati kṣaṇikāḥ iti yadi vināśinaḥ iti siddha sādhanam atha āśu vināśinaḥ iti 
NV_3.2.14^10	 tadā api viśeṣaṇam siddhānta virodhi atha utpanna pradhvaṃsinaḥ iti etat api tādṛś eva utpannāḥ pradhvaṃsinaḥ iti siddha sādhanam atha utpannaḥ vinaṣṭam iti ekaḥ kālaḥ utpatti vināśau eka kālau iti tena yathā anutpannasya utpattiḥ evam anutpannasya vināśaḥ iti prāptam atha utpannam vinaśyati iti etasmin api pakṣe utpatti vat vināśaḥ kāraṇavān yathā utpattiḥ kriyā tvāt sa kāraṇā tathā vināśaḥ iti utpadya vināśa kāraṇam anubhavati tatas vinaśyati iti akāraṇe ca vināśe doṣaḥ uktaḥ yaḥ ca ayam matvarthīyaḥ kṣaṇikaḥ iti sa katham yadi nirukta nyāyena kṣayaḥ kṣaṇaḥ iti kṣaṇaḥ asya asti iti kṣaṇikaḥ iti tat na yuktam kāla bhedāt yadā kṣayaḥ na tadā kṣayī iti bhinna kālayoḥ na matu arthīyaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ 
NV_3.2.14^11	 atha punar bhāvaḥ eva anantara vināśena viśiṣyamāṇaḥ kṣaṇaḥ iti ucyate tathā api tena eva tat eva tadvat na bhavati iti na yuktaḥ matu arthīyaḥ atha kṣaṇa avasthiti kālāḥ kṣaṇikāḥ iti sarva antyam kālam kṣaṇa tvena pratipadya tatra avatiṣṭhante te kṣaṇikāḥ iti etat api na yuktam saṃjñā mātreṇa kālasya abhyupagamāt pañca bhikṣavaḥ saṃjñā bheda mātram iti śāstram na ca saṃjñā mātram vastu viśeṣaṇa tvena yuktam kṣaṇikāḥ id ca pratijñām kṛtvā na dṛṣṭāntaḥ asti iti uktam pradīpa ādeḥ asiddha tvāt ye api hetavaḥ ante viśeṣa darśanāt iti evam ādayaḥ te api asiddhāḥ vai anyathā siddhāḥ vā viruddhāḥ vā bhavanti iti ahetavaḥ upetya vā viśeṣavat tvam vartamāna eka kṣaṇa viśeṣavat tvena anaikāntikam ubhaya pakṣa sampratipattyā yaḥ eva kṣaṇaḥ vartamānaḥ sa viśeṣavān bhavati ekaḥ ca iti anekāntaḥ 
NV_3.2.14^12	 ante viśeṣa darśanāt iti ca viśeṣaṇa ānarthakyam anta artha anabhidhānāt katamasmin ante viśeṣa darśanam vaktavyam atha antar vināśaḥ naḥ etasmin viśeṣa darśanam asti atha antimam vastu eva anta śabda vācyam evam sati eksamin viśeṣaḥ iti viruddhaḥ hetuḥ yaḥ api ayam hetuḥ darśana adarśanāt iti asya arthaḥ nīyamānasya kila pradīpa ādeḥ dravyasya deśa antare utpādaḥ deśa antare ca nirodhaḥ tad kṛte darśana adarśane staḥ tathā ca gacchataḥ devadatta ādeḥ darśana adarśanāt tasmāt asya api pratikṣaṇam utpāda vināśau iti na etat nyāyam devadatta ādeḥ draśana adarśanayoḥ anya nimitta tvāt saṃyoga vibhāga kṛte darśana adarśane naḥ utpāda vināśa kṛte yasmin deśe saṃyogaḥ vinaṣṭaḥ tasmin saṃyogī na gṛhyate yasmin utpannaḥ tat na gṛhyate iti 
NV_3.2.14^13	 samyogāt hi dravye ihabuddhiḥ bhavati bhāva abhāvayoḥ tadvat tvāt iti atha saṃyoga vibhāgau na pratipadyte tasya api saṃyogaḥ artha antaram bhavati iti pratipāditam etena vibhāgaḥ vyākhyātaḥ tat evam saṃyoga vibhāga utpatteḥ dravyasya darśana adarśane bhavataḥ na anyathā iti yat punar etat pradīpasya desa antare utpādaḥ iti etat api na buddhyāmahe katham iti yat tāvat bhavatām pakṣe vastu utpannam yatra tatra eva tat dhvaṃsate yat utpatsu tat anāhita saṃskāram asattvāt deśa antare na utpattum arhati atha anāhita saṃskārasya api deśa antare utpādaḥ na kim cit vastu abhinna deśam utpadyate atha kāraṇam saṃskṛtam iti tad ādheya vaśāt kāryam api tathābhūtam eva utpadyate iti tulyam kāryeṇa yathā eva kārye saṃskāraḥ ādhātum aśakyaḥ tathā kāraṇe api iti tulyam 
NV_3.2.14^14	 nityam bhavatām pakṣe bhinna deśena kāryeṇa utpattavyam abhinna deśena vā etena eva atulya pātaḥ vyākhyātaḥ atulya pātāt kṣaṇika tvam iti na kila ākāśe patataḥ loṣṭa ādeḥ pratibandhakam kim cit asti yat anuvidhānena loṣṭa ādi kim cit cireṇa patati kim cit āśu iti tasmāt kṣaṇika tvāt kāḥ cit avasthāḥ tādṛśyaḥ utpadyante yāsām na bhavati adhas santāna utpattau sāmarthyam punar ca tādṛśyaḥ utpadyante yāsām bhavati iti etat api anyathā siddham eva tulyānām gurutvavatām dravyāṇām ekasya guru tva prayatna kṣepāḥ kāraṇam ekasya guru tva mātram ekasya guru tva prayatnau iti tat evam kāraṇa bheda anuvidhāyīni gurutvavanti dravyāṇi cira āśu pāta anuvidhāna bhāñji bhavati iti ahetuḥ atulya pātaḥ 
NV_3.2.14^15	 yat api idam iṣoḥ ca āpatanam bhavet iti saṃskāreka tva vādinaḥ doṣaḥ ayam api saṃskāreka tva anabhyupagamena pratyuktaḥ yathā ca anekaḥ saṃskāraḥ iti tathā uktam pāṇi nimitta praśleṣa sūtre iti ekaḥ ca saṃskāraḥ nimitta bhedāt kadā cit paṭūni karmāṇi karoti kadā cit mandāni iti guru tva vat draṣṭavyam yathā ekam guru tvam sahakāri saṃyoga apekṣam mandam pātam karoti tat eva pratibandha apagame paṭum karoti dṛṣṭaḥ hi grāvṇaḥ ākāse muktasya paṭuḥ pātaḥ mandaḥ apsvati tat evam atulya pātaḥ api ahetuḥ atha akṣaṇika tve kim pramāṇam uktam ādhāra ādheya bhāvāt eka kāla anubhāvīni kārya kāraṇe kuṇḍe badara vat iti atas ca vipratipannāḥ ayugapad kālāḥ pratyayāḥ eka viṣayāḥ avyutthāyi tat pratyaya sāmānādhikaraṇye sati samāna śabda vācya tvāt vartamāna eka kṣaṇa aneka puruṣa pratyaya vat 
NV_3.2.14^16	 yathā vartamāna eka kṣaṇa viṣayāṇām aneka puruṣa pratyayānām avyutthāyi tat pratyaya sāmānādhikaraṇye sati samāna śabda vācyānām eka viṣaya tvam tathā ca avyutthāyi tat pratyaya samāna adhikaraṇāḥ samāna śabda vācyāḥ ca vipratipannāḥ ayugapad kālāḥ pratyayāḥ tasmāt te api eka viṣayāḥ iti pratyātmam na aneka kartṛkāḥ pratyayāḥ apratisandhāna prasaṅgāt devadatta ādi pratyaya vat iti rūpa rasa gandha sparśa pratyayāḥ eka aneka nimittāḥ pratisandhānāt kṛta samayānām bahūnām vartamāna eka kṣaṇa aneka vijñāna vat iti hyastanāt yatanāni vijñānāni eka santatau eka aneka nimittāni mayā iti pratisandhānāt pūrvavat śāstra artha pratyayāḥ eka aneka nimittāḥ pratisandhānāt pūrvat iti nānā viṣayāṇām nānā kartṛkāṇām ca pratyayānām apratisandhānāt iti pūrvavat eva nyāyaḥ iti
