NV_3.2.15	 na evam kṣīram vinaśyati na api dadhi utpadyate api tu avasthitasya dravyasya pūrva dharma nivṛttau dharma antaram utpadyate iti eke varṇayanti apare tu avasthitasya dravyasya guṇa nivṛttau guṇa antaram utpadyate iti sa khalu ayam eka pakṣībhāvaḥ iva kaḥ upamāna arthaḥ ubhayatra dravyam avatiṣṭhate ekasya tirobhāva abhivyaktī ekasya vināśa prādurbhāvau iti upamāna arthaḥ 
NV_3.2.16	 ubhayoḥ api ca uttaram vyūha antarāt dravya antara utpatti darśanam pūrva dravya nivṛtteḥ anumānam śeṣam bhāṣye yat punar etat ekasya tirobhāva abhivyaktī ekasya vināśa prādurbhāvau iti tat na pūrva avasthā parityāgāt yadi vināśa utpādau nivṛtti prādurbhāvau atha api abhivyakti anabhivyaktī sarvathā pūrva avasthām jahāti dravyam iti na hi anapavṛktasya pūrva avasthātaḥ abhivyakti anabhivyaktī bhavataḥ vināśa prādurbhāvau vā iti tasmāt ayuktam avasthitasya pariṇāmaḥ iti 
NV_3.2.17^1	 abhyanujñāya ca niṣkāraṇam kṣīra vināśam niṣkāraṇam ca dadhi utpādam kvacid vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdeḥ kvacid ca upalabhdeḥ anekāntaḥ kṣīra dadhi vat niṣkāraṇau vināśa utpādau sphaṭika vyaktīnām na punar kumbha ādi vat sa kāraṇau iti na atra hetuḥ asti iti niradhiṣṭhānam ca dṛṣṭānta vacanam kaḥ adhiṣṭhāna arthaḥ āśrayaḥ kim uktam bhavati niradhiṣṭhānam iti dharmī na asti iti yāvat uktam bhavati na hi sphaṭikasya utpāda vināśau pratikṣaṇam upalabhyete yatas iyam cintā bhavet kim etau sa kāraṇau āhosvit akāraṇau iti yathā anabhyupagata śabda sattvam prati kaḥ cit brūyāt kṛtaka tvāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ tādṛś etat iti 
NV_3.2.17^2	 dharmya prasiddheḥ ca dṛṣṭānta abhāvaḥ iti ca samānam abhyanujñāya ca sphaṭikasya utpāda vināśau yaḥ atra sādhakaḥ tasya abhyanujñānāt apratiṣedhaḥ ubhau etau dṛṣṭāntau kṣīra dadhi vat kumbha ādi vat ca tatra kim kumbha ādi dṛṣṭāntaḥ bhavatu atha kṣīra dadhinī iti kumbha ādi vat iti yuktam kumbha ādi utpatti vināśa kāraṇasya dṛṣṭa tvāt kṣīra dadhi vat tu na yuktam anumānataḥ grahaṇāt iti siddham anityā buddhiḥ iti itas ca anityā buddhiḥ guṇa tve sati pratyakṣa tayā vyāpaka dravya samavāyāt śabda vat jātimat tve sati asmad ādi pratyakṣa tvāt āśrita tvāt ca śabda vat karaṇa bhāve sati ayogi pratyakṣa tvāt śabda vat eva 
NV_3.2.18	 sā tu iyam buddhiḥ kasya guṇaḥ iti etat cintyate na guṇa bhāva asiddheḥ anitya tve sati niyamena ācākṣuṣa pratyakṣa tvāt rasavat siddhaḥ guṇa bhāvaḥ sannikarṣa utpatteḥ saṃśayaḥ iti tatra ayam viśeṣaḥ na indriya arthayoḥ tad vināśe api jñāna avasthānāt bhavati khalu idam indriye arthe ca vinaṣṭe jñānam adrākṣam iti adrākṣam iti etat naḥ indriya artha sannikarṣāt smṛti tvāt smṛtiḥ eṣā naḥ indriya artha sannikarṣāt bhavitum arhati smṛtau api tulyam yathā jñātāram antareṇa jñānam na bhavati evam anubhavitari naṣṭe anubhavitāram antareṇa smṛtiḥ ayuktāḥ iti 
NV_3.2.19^1	 astu tarhi manaḥ guṇaḥ jñānam yugapad jñeya anupalabdheḥ ca na manasaḥ tat khalu yugapad jñeya anupalabdyā samadhigatam manaḥ na atas tasya guṇaḥ jñānam viśeṣaṇa upādānāt antaḥkaraṇa bahutva prasaṅgaḥ iti ced atha manyase yat khalu yugapad jñeya anupalabdhyā samadhigatam manaḥ na tasya guṇaḥ jñānam iti evam bruvāṇena bahūni antaḥkaraṇāni pratipannāni bhavanti na hi asati antaḥkaraṇa bahutve viśeṣaṇam arthavat iti na sarvasya indriyasya manana nimitta tvāt sarvam eva indriyam manana nimitta tvāt manaḥ iti abhidhīyate evam ca sati yuktam viśeṣaṇam yugapad jñeya anupalabdhyā yat samadhigatam manaḥ na tasya guṇaḥ jñānam iti evam api viśeṣaṇam vyartham anyasya anabhyupagamāt yadi tasya antaḥkaraṇasya na bhavati anyasya tarhi sādhanasya jñānam guṇaḥ iti prāptam anyasya anabhyupagamāt anyasya upapatteḥ apratiṣedhaḥ 
NV_3.2.19^2	 anavasthita tvāt pramāṇa prameya vyavahārasya yadā ayam yogī puruṣa antareṇa puruṣa antaram paricchinatti tadā puruṣa antara paricchede puruṣa antaram sādhanam iti tattva jñāna guṇam bhavati iti yuktam viśeṣaṇam iti tasmāt na tasya guṇaḥ jñānam iti kasya tarhi asya arthasya pradarśana artham jñāsya vaśitvāt vaśī jñātā vaśyam karaṇam iti na ca ayam jñātari niyamaḥ jñātā vaśī eva vaśyaḥ api bhavati iti acetane tu niyamaḥ acetanam tu sarvam vaśyam iti vaśyam manaḥ acetana tvāt ghrāṇa ādi vat iti jñāna guṇa tve ca saṃjñā bheda mātram vibhu ca antaḥkaraṇam jñāna guṇam ca iti saṃjñā mātram bhidyate yathā ca jñātuḥ jñāna sādhanam indriyam evam mantuḥ mati sādhanena avaśyam bhavitavyam iti ubhayoḥ cetanatve pratyaya vyavasthā anumānam na syāt vibhu ca antaḥkaraṇam jñāna guṇam iti sarva indriyaiḥ yugapad upalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ 
NV_3.2.20–3.2.22	 yasya api ātmā vibhuḥ ca jñāna guṇaḥ ca tasya api sarva indriyaiḥ sambandhasya apratiṣedhāt yugapad upalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ na prasaṅgaḥ kāraṇa antara bhāvāt indriya artha sannikarṣa vat indriya manaḥ sannikarṣaḥ api kāraṇam iti tasya ca ayaugapadyam aṇu tvāt manasaḥ iti yadi punar ātma indriya artha sannikarṣāt eva jñānam utpadyeta kim syāt na utpatti kāraṇa anapadeśāt asmāt eva utpadyatām iti na kāraṇam apadiśyate iti sūtra arthaḥ ātma indriya artha sannikarṣāt jñānam utpadyate iti ayugapad utpattau vā na kāraṇa antaram apadisyate videha pratyaya anutpattau vā yadā indriyam arthena bahis avasthitena sambadhyate ātma sambandhaḥ api tatra asti iti kasmāt videha pratyayaḥ na bhavati iti vaktavyam antaḥkaraṇa pratyākhyāne ca kevalam ātmā smṛti ādi kāraṇam iti kasmāt na yugapad utpattiḥ smṛtīnām yadā ca indriyam ātmā ca arthena yugapad sambaddhau tadā kim indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ kāraṇam uta ātma artha sannikarṣaḥ uta ātma indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ iti kāraṇa anapadeśaḥ 
NV_3.2.23	 tad ātma guṇa tve api tulyam iti etat anena samuccīyante yadi ātma guṇaḥ buddhiḥ bhavati vināśa kāraṇa abhāvāt nitya tvam asyāḥ prasajyeta katham iti guṇānām dvavidhaḥ vināśa hetuḥ āśraya abhāvaḥ virodhi guṇa prādurbhāvaḥ ca tatra nitya tvāt ātmanaḥ anupapannaḥ pūrvaḥ virodhī ca gunaḥ na asti iti nitya tva prasaṅgaḥ 
NV_3.2.24^1	 anityā buddhiḥ iti etat pratipāditam tatra asyāḥ buddhi antarāt vā saṃskārāt vā vināśaḥ iti pratipattavyam na dve buddhī saha iti ced atha manyase na dve buddhī saha bhavataḥ yatas parayā pūrvā nivartyate iti tat ca na yugapad utpatti pratiṣedhāt yugapad utpattiḥ pratiṣidhyate na sahabhāvaḥ na hi buddhyoḥ yugapad bhāve kim cit virudhyate iti labdha ātmakena ca kāryeṇa kāraṇasya vināśa abhyupagamāt yadā ca kāryam labdha ātmakam bhavati tadā kāraṇam vināśayati śabda vat yathā labdha ātmakaḥ kāryaḥ śabdaḥ kāraṇam śabdam nirmārṣṭi tathā buddhiḥ api iti antyayoḥ na syāt iti ced atha manyase yadi pūrvau buddhi śabdau parābhyām vināsyete antyayoḥ buddhi śabdayoḥ kim vināśa kāraṇam iti yathā ca antyau buddhi śabdau vināśa kāraṇam vinā vinaśyataḥ evam anyat api kāryam iti na sparśavat dravya saṃyogāt tad utpatteḥ 
NV_3.2.24^2	 sparśavat dravya saṃyogena antya śabdaḥ virudhyate ye kuḍya ādibhiḥ ākāraṇasya saṃyogāḥ te eka artha samavāyinam śabdam pratibadhnanti atah antyasya aśrutiḥ śabdasya iti antyā buddhiḥ sthiti hetu abhāvāt vinaśyati iti kālāt vā saṃskārāt vā katham kālāt yau antyasya janmanaḥ sthiti hetū dharma adharmau tayoḥ abhāvāt antyā buddhiḥ vinasyati iti kasmāt punar etat evam ucyate na punar ahetukaḥ vināśaḥ abhyupagamyate iti na abhyupagamyate ukta doṣāt nirhetuke vināśe uktaḥ doṣaḥ kṣaṇa bhaṅgam nirākurvadbhiḥ iti yadi kāraṇasya ayaugapadyāt buddhīnām ayugapad utpattiḥ yatra kāraṇasya yaugapadyam asti tatra yugapad utpatti prasaṅgaḥ yathā smṛtiṣu atra tāvat ekaḥ parihāraḥ karaṇasya eka kriyā nirvṛttau sāmarthyāt na hi karaṇam ekasmin kāle anekām kriyām nirvatayitum śaktam iti pariccheda tvāt ca smṛtīnām jñāna vat yugapad utpattiḥ iti 
NV_3.2.25–3.2.26	 apare tu kāraṇasya ayaugapadyam upapādayiṣyantaḥ jñāna samaveta ātma pradeśa sannikarṣāt manasaḥ smṛti utpatteḥ na yugapad utpattiḥ iti āhuḥ etat tu na samyak iti pratipādayitum āha na antar śarīra vṛtti tvāt manasaḥ antar śarīre manaḥ vartate iti kaḥ vṛtti arthaḥ na tāvat āśraya āśraya bhāvaḥ na hi manaḥ kva cit āśritam na api vṛttiḥ sva kārya sāmarthyam bahis kārya darśanāt manasā adhiṣṭhitam cakṣuḥ niḥsṛtya rūpa ādikam artham grāhayati cakṣuṣoḥ visarārvoḥ manasaḥ kāryam tad bhāva bhāvi tvāt na ca anyā vṛttiḥ sambhavati tasmāt na antar śarīra vṛtti manaḥ iti atra brūmaḥ na āśraya āśrita bhāvaḥ manasaḥ vṛttiḥ na api kārya pratilambhaḥ api tu na aśarīrasya manasaḥ kāryam iti manasaḥ vṛtti arthaḥ na hi aśarīram manaḥ puruṣasya artham karoti iti 
NV_3.2.27–3.2.30	 aśarīram manaḥ puruṣa artha asamartham iti sādhyam etat smaraṇa śarīra dhāraṇe yugapad bhavataḥ iti dṛṣṭam dṛṣṭam ca sarveṇa pratipattavyam cira niścarite ca manasi smarataḥ śarīra dhāraṇam na syāt ubhayam sidhyati smaraṇam dhāraṇam ca aniyataḥ smṛti kālaḥ atas ayuktam etat śarīra saṃyoga anapekṣam ca ātma manaḥ saṃyogam smṛti kāraṇam bruvataḥ śarīrasya upabhoga āyatana tvam nivartate tad nivṛttau ca śarīra utpatti vaiyarthyam iti 
NV_3.2.31–3.2.32	 apare tu ātma preraṇa yadṛcchā jña tābhiḥ ca na saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ iti parihāram bruvate eta ca vyāsakta manasaḥ pāda vyathanena saṃyoga viśeṣeṇa samānam bhavati iti aparihāraḥ karma adṛṣṭam upabhoga artham niyāmakam bhavati iti na yuktam samāna tvāt tasmāt pūrvaḥ eva parihāraḥ na antar śarīra vṛtti tvāt manasaḥ iti 
NV_3.2.33^1	 yadi tarhi jñāna samaveta ātma pradeśa sannikarṣasya ayaugapadyāt iti parihāraḥ na iṣyate prāptaḥ smṛtīnām yugapad utpādaḥ kāraṇasya yaugapadyāt iti praṇidhāna liṅga ādi jñānānām ayugapad bhāvāt yugapad asmaraṇam na apekṣā kāraṇasya ayugapad bhāvāt prātibhavat tu praṇidhāna ādi anapekṣe smārte yaugapadya prasaṅgaḥ yad praṇidhāna ādi ātma manaḥ saṃyogasya sahakāri kāraṇam tat na yugapad bhavati iti ayugapad utpattiḥ smṛtīnām yadi praṇidhāna ādi apekṣa ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ na yugapad smṛti kāraṇam yāḥ smṛtayaḥ praṇidhāna ādi sannidhānam antareṇa bhavanti tāsām yaugapadyam syāt na anabhyupagamāt na hi praṇidhāna ādi anapekṣam smārtam asti sataḥ smṛti hetoḥ tu asaṃvedanāt prātibhena samāna abhimānaḥ ayam iti prātibham tarhi yugapad bhavitum arhati na hi tasya asat nihitam kāraṇam iti na ukta uttara tvāt ukta uttaram etat na hi karaṇasya aneka kriyā nirvṛtti sāmarthyam asti prātibham ca anekam jñānam bhavat ekasmin arthe bhavet anekasmin vā tat na tāvat ekasmin vaiyarthyāt 
NV_3.2.33^2	 na anekasmin sāmarthya abhāvāt na ca ayam niyamaḥ pratyayānām yaugapadyam na bhavati iti jñātuḥ vikaraṇa dharmaṇaḥ deha nānā tve pratyaya yaugapadyāt iti yadi ca jñāna samaveta ātma pradeśa āsannikarṣāt na smṛtīnām yugapad utpattiḥ ye saṃskārāḥ eka deśāḥ teṣu avasthita śarīrasya aneka jñāna samavāyāt eka pradeśe yugapadaneka artha smaraṇam syāt na ca etat asti iti atas ca aparīhāraḥ iti avasthita śarīrasya saṃskārāḥ samāna deśāḥ iti ayuktam ātma pradeśānām adravya antara tvāt evam sati sarva saṃskārāṇām samāna deśa tve pratyaya yaugapadya prasaṅgaḥ aparihāryaḥ saṃskāra pratyāsattyā smṛti yaugapadyam na bhavati iti kā pratyāsattiḥ na hi saṃskārāṇām sannikṛṣṭa viprakṛṣṭa bhāvaḥ asti samāna deśa tvāt na brūmaḥ sannikṛṣṭa tā pratyāsattiḥ api tu saṃskārasya sahakāri kāraṇa samavadhānam pratyāsattiḥ śabda vat yathā śabdāḥ santāna vartinaḥ sarve eva ākāśe samavayanti samāna deśa tve api yasya upalabdheḥ kāraṇāni santi saḥ upalabhyate naḥ itare tathā saṃskāreṣu api iti 
NV_3.2.34–3.2.36	 puruṣasya jñānam icchā ādayaḥ antaḥkaraṇasya iti kasya cit darśanam tat pratiṣidhyate jñasya jñasya icchā dveṣa nimitta tvāt ārambha nivṛttyoḥ jñātuḥ eva icchā ādayaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ yadi antaḥkaraṇasya icchā ādayaḥ syuḥ na pratyakṣāḥ syuḥ na hi icchā ādayaḥ anyatra vartamānāḥ anyasya pratyakṣāḥ bhavitum arhanti iti nityam ca icchā ādayaḥ apratyakṣāḥ syuḥ manaḥ guṇānām nityam atīndriya tvāt ārambha nivṛttyoḥ ca pratyagātmani dṛṣṭa tvāt paratra anumānam pravṛtti nivṛttibhyām sāmānādhikaraṇyāt śarīra ādiṣu prasaṅgaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ iti anekāntaḥ vākya arthaḥ 
NV_3.2.37	 prayujyamāna bhūta viṣaya tvam pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ niyamaḥ yāni bhūtāni prayujayante teṣu pravṛtti nivṛttī bhavataḥ na sarveṣu iti yadi punar jña tvāt bhūtānām pravṛtti nivṛttī syātām bhūtamātre syātām yathā guru tva ādibhyaḥ bhūta guṇebhyaḥ yāni guru tva ādimanti bhūtāni tāni sva guṇāt patanti iti niyamaḥ ca dṛṣṭaḥ tasmāt na bhūtāni cetanāni iti eka śarīre ca jñātṛ bahu tvam niranumānam yasya bhūtāni cetanāni tasya eka śarīre bahūni bhūtāni iti bahavaḥ cetanāḥ syuḥ bhavantu bahavaḥ cetanāḥ kim naḥ bādhyate iti ced na bahu tve vyavasthāna anumānam na bhavet vyavasthām tu na paśyāmaḥ pratyayānām pratisandhānāt sarvaḥ pratyayaḥ pratisandhīyamānaḥ ekasmin kārya kāraṇa saṅghāte dṛṣṭaḥ iti anyathā abhidhānāt ca hita ahita prāpti parihāra arthaḥ parispandaḥ pravṛtti nivṛttī bhavatā tu kriyā mātram kriyā uparama mātram ca āśritya tad liṅga tvāt icchā dveṣayoḥ pārthiva ādyeṣu apratiṣedhaḥ iti uktam 
NV_3.2.38	 yathāvidhe ca pravṛtti nivṛttī prayujyamāna bhūta ādhāre dṛṣṭe na tathāvidhe bhūtamātre bhavataḥ iti bhūta indriya manasām samānaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ manaḥ tu udāharaṇa mātram yathā ukta hetu tvāt pāratantryāt sva kṛta abhyāgamāt ca na manasaḥ yathā ukta hetu tvāt iti darśana sparśanābhyām eka artha grahaṇāt iti evam ādīnām ātma pratipatti hetūnām apratiṣedhāt pāratantryāt iti paratantryāṇi śarīra indriya manāṃsi dhāraṇa preraṇa vyūhana kriyāsu prayatna vaśāt pravartante caitanye punar svatantrāṇi syuḥ sva kṛta abhyāgamāt ca cetana tvāt śarīra ādīnām taiḥ kṛtam karma puruṣena bhujyate iti akṛta kṛta āgama nāśa doṣa prasaṅgaḥ acetana tve tu tad sādhanasya sva kṛta karma phala upabhogaḥ iti 
NV_3.2.39	 atha ayam siddha upasaṅgrahaḥ pariśeṣāt yathā ukta hetu upapatteḥ ca ātmanaḥ guṇaḥ jñānam iti prakṛtam yathā ukta hetu upapatteḥ iti ātma pratipādakānām hetūnām apratiṣedhāt pariśeṣāt iti śarīra indriya manasām pratiṣedhāt anyasya ca śiṣyamāṇasya asambhavāt ātmanaḥ ca śiṣyamāṇa tvāt tasya guṇaḥ jñānam iti upapatteḥ iti vā svatantraḥ hetuḥ ātmanaḥ nitya tve iti kasya upapatteḥ saṃsāra apavargayoḥ upapatteḥ iti evam ādi bhāṣye 
NV_3.2.40–3.2.41	 smaraṇam tu ātmanaḥ jña svābhāvyāt smṛti hetūnām ayaugapadyāt ayugapad smaraṇam iti uktam atha kebhyaḥ smṛtiḥ utpadyate iti smṛti kāraṇānām ayaugapadya pratipādana artham praṇidhāna ādi sūtram p r a ṇ i d h ā n a n i b a n d h ā b h y ā s a l i ṅ g a l a k ṣ a ṇ a s ā d ṛ ś y a p a r i g r a h ā ś r a y ā ś r ita sambandha ānantarya viyoga eka kārya virodha atiśaya prāpti vyavadhāna sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa bhaya arthi tva kriyā rāga dharma adharma nimittebhyaḥ evam upapannam anityā buddhiḥ iti 
NV_3.2.42^1	 anityāyām ca buddhau utpanna apavargi tvāt kāla antara avasthāyi tvāt ca nityānām saṃśayaḥ kim utpannāpavargiṇī buddhiḥ śabda vat āho kāla antara avasthāyinī kumbha vat iti utpanna apavargiṇī iti yuktam kaḥ punar ayam arthaḥ utpanna apavargiṇī iti anyebhyaḥ vināśibhyaḥ āśutaram vinaśyati iti na tu ayam arthaḥ utpatti anantaram dhvaṃsate iti kaḥ punar atra nyāyaḥ āśutara vināśinī buddhiḥ jātimat tve sati asmad ādi pratyakṣa tāyāḥ vyāpaka dravya samavāyāt śabda vat pratikṣaṇam apūrva utpattau ayugapad utpattau ca karaṇa tve sati pratyartha prakāśaka tvāt 
NV_3.2.42^2	 yasya pratikṣaṇam apūrva utpanna padārtha prakāśaka tvam karaṇa tve sati tasya āśu vināśi tvam dṛṣṭam yathā pradīpasya pratikṣaṇam apūrva utpannāḥ ca pradhvaṃsinaḥ padārthān buddhiḥ pratyartha niyamena prakāśayati tasmāt iyam api āśutara vināśinī iti atha vā āśutara vināśinī buddhiḥ guṇa tve sati abāhya karaṇa pratyakṣa tvāt sukha vat iti asya arthasya jñāpana artham karma anavasthāyi grahaṇāt iti sūtram yadi tarhi anavasthāyiṣu padārtheṣu evaṃbhūtā buddhiḥ atha yadā avasthitam kumbha ādikam artham upalabhate tadā kim kumbha vat kāla antara avasthāyinī uta āśu vidhvaṃsinī iti 
NV_3.2.42^3	 avasthita grahaṇe api pratyakṣa nivṛtteḥ pradhvaṃsinī yadā api avasthitam kumbha ādikam artham upalabhate tadā api santānena eva buddhayaḥ vartante kasmāt vyavahite pratyakṣa nivṛtteḥ yadi kumbha vat kāla antara avasthāyinī buddhiḥ abhaviṣyat vyavahite api pratyakṣam avāsthāsyata na tu avatiṣṭhate tasmāt na kāla antara avasthāyinī iti smṛteḥ avatiṣṭhate iti ced yadi buddhiḥ pradhvaṃsinī syāt smṛtiḥ na syāt na hi buddhi bhede smṛtim paśyāmaḥ yathā puruṣa antara buddhiṣu asti ca smṛtiḥ tasmāt avatiṣṭhate buddhiḥ iti na atas eva atas eva na avatiṣṭhate 
NV_3.2.42^4	 na hi buddhau avasthitāyām smṛtiḥ sambhavati smṛtiḥ nāma pratyakṣa buddhi nirodhe tad pūrvakaḥ viṣaya pratisandhiḥ yathā idam adrākṣam iti adrākṣam iti ca na pratyakṣāyām buddhau avasthitāyām yuktam iti anyatas ca tad bhāvāt smṛtiḥ aliṅgam iti yā iyam smṛtiḥ buddhi avasthāna liṅga tvena abhyupagamyate naḥ iyam liṅgam anyatas tad bhāvāt avatiṣṭhate hi buddhi jaḥ saṃskāraḥ iti tatas praṇidhāna ādi nimitta apekṣāt smṛtiḥ iti hetu abhāvaḥ iti ced atha manyase saṃskārāt smṛtiḥ na buddhi avasthānāt iti atra kaḥ hetuḥ smṛtiḥ eva yadi avatiṣṭhate buddhiḥ smṛtiḥ na syāt iti uktam 
NV_3.2.43–3.2.44^1	 yadi anavasthāyinī buddhiḥ avyaktam vyaktasya grahaṇam prāpnoti yathā vidyutā prakāśitānām arthānām avyaktam grahaṇam iti na virodhāt avyakta grahaṇāt avasthāyinī buddhiḥ iti bruvāṇaḥ yat pratiṣeddhavyam anavasthāyinī buddhiḥ iti tat abhyanujānāti tasya ca abhyanujñānāt yat uktam kāla antara avasthāyinī buddhiḥ iti tat bādhitam bhavati avyakta grahaṇasya ca anya nimitta tvāt na avyakta grahaṇāt buddhi anavasthānam siddhyati yat tat avyaktam vyaktam ca grahaṇam na tat buddheḥ avasthāna anavasthānābhyām api tu grahaṇa hetoḥ bhedāt iti tad asambhavāt ca na ca avyaktam nāma grahaṇam asti kasmāt artha grahaṇa mātra tvāt buddheḥ artha grahaṇa mātram hi buddhiḥ tat ca artha grahaṇam sāmānyatas viśeṣataḥ ca 
NV_3.2.44^2–3.2.45	 yat ca sāmānya viṣayam tat sāmānyam prati vyaktam evam viśeṣa viṣayam evam tadvat viṣayam iti tat idam avyakta grahaṇam deśitam katamasmin viṣaye buddhi anavasthāna kāritam syāt loka virodhaḥ iti ced yadi tarhi vyakta avyakta grahaṇe na syātām yaḥ ayam vyavahāraḥ lokeṣu vyaktam paśyāmi iti sa katham na anyathā tad upapatteḥ na ayam sāmānya viśeṣa tadvatsu vyakta avyakta grahaṇa bhedaḥ api tu dharmiṇaḥ sāmānyatas adhigatasya viśeṣataḥ upalipsā dvārakam avyakta grahaṇam iti anekāntāt ca na ca ayam ekāntaḥ asti yat viṣaya grahaṇa hetoḥ grāhyasya ca anavasthānam tatra avyakta grahaṇam anavasthāyi tve api yathā pradīpa arciṣām sanatatyā vartamānānām grāhya anavasthānam grahaṇa anavasthānam ca bhavati bhavati ca vyaktam grahaṇam arcīṃṣi iti yathā arciḥṣu tathā anyatra api iti vyavasthitam kṣaṇikā buddhiḥ iti 
NV_3.2.46	 śarīra guṇaḥ cetanā sati śarīre bhāvāt asati ca abhāvāt iti yat ca yasmin sati bhavati asati ca na bhavati tasya tat iti vijñāyate yathā rūpa ādayaḥ iti na sati bhāvāt śarīra guṇa tvam cetanāyāḥ sidhyati sati bhāvasya anya guṇa tve api darśanāt na tāvat saṃyoga vibhāga ssaṃskārāḥ karma guṇāḥ atha ca sati karmaṇi bhāvaḥ asati ca abhāvaḥ iti saṃyoga vibhāga śabdeṣu ca satsu śabdaḥ bhavati atha ca na tad guṇaḥ iti tad guṇa tvam ca tatra upalabdhyā siddhyati yadi yatra vartamānam upalabhyate rūpa ādikam tat tasya guṇaḥ iti atha sati bhāvāt iti anena śarīre cetanā upalabdhim brūyāt tasya api asiddha tā doṣaḥ na hi naḥ śarīre cetanā upalabhyate cetanā mātram tu upalabhyate tat ca sandigdham kim śarīre uta anyasmin iti upetya śarīre cetanā upalabdhim kim śarīra guṇaḥ cetanāḥ uta dravya antara guṇaḥ iti dravye sva guṇa para guṇa upalabdheḥ saṃśayaḥ iti ukta artham sūtram 
NV_3.2.47^1	 na śarīra guṇaḥ cetanā yāvat śarīra bhāvi tvāt rūpa ādīnām dṛṣṭānta sūtram vaidharmyeṇa ye śarīra guṇāḥ bhavanti te yavat śarīram vartante yathā rūpa ādayaḥ na tu yavat śarīram cetanā vartate tasmāt na tad guṇaḥ iti sādharmyeṇa vā na tad guṇaḥ iti yathā apsu uṣṇa tā iti saṃskāra vat iti ced atha manyase yathā saṃskāraḥ śarīra guṇaḥ na ca yavat śarīram vartate tathā cetanāḥ api iti na kāraṇa anucchedāt saṃskārasya na śarīra mātram kāraṇam tasya nodana ādi kāraṇa sannidhāne tad abhāve ca bhāva abhāvau yuktau na tu cetanāyāḥ kāraṇa sannidhānam atas ayuktam etat iti cetanā nimittasya api asannidhānam iti ced 
NV_3.2.47^2	 atha manyase yathā eva saṃskārasya kāraṇam asannihitam evam cetanā kāraṇam api iti tat ayuktam vikalpa anupapatteḥ yat śarīre cetanā utpatti kāraṇam tat kim śarīra stham uta dravya antara stham śarīra stham api kim yavat śarīra bhāvi uta naimittikam iti yadi yavat śarīra bhāvi na kadā cit cetanā hīnam śarīram upalabhyeta tad nimittasya sannihita tvāt atha naimittikam yat tad śarīre cetanā utpatteḥ nimitta kāraṇam tatra api cetanāvat prasaṅgaḥ atha dravya antara stham dravya antara vṛtti nimittam śarīre cetanām karoti na dravya antareṣu iti atra api niyama hetuḥ vaktavyaḥ dravya antara stham ca etat nityam anityam vā anityam api kāla antara avasthāyi pratikṣaṇa pradhvaṃsi vā iti cetanā vat prasaṅgaḥ 
NV_3.2.48–3.2.49	 yat ca manyeta śyāma ādi guṇam ca dravyam bhavati na ca yāvat dravya bhāvinī śyāma tā iti tat ca na pāka ja guṇa antara utpatteḥ na atyantam śyāma rūpa uparame rūpa antara anutpādaḥ cetanā uparamaḥ tu atyantaḥ iti itas ca pratidvandvi siddheḥ pāka jānām apratiṣedhaḥ yāvatsu dravyeṣu pūrva guṇa pratiṣedhaḥ tāvatsu pratidvandvinaḥ guṇa antarasya darśanam yathā śyāma ādi nivṛttau rakta ādīnām iti na punar śarīre cetanā viparītam guṇa antaram upalabhyate cetanā mātra uparamaḥ tu atyantam iti atha manyase śarīre api acetana tvam nāma guṇa antaram iti tat na svarūpataḥ anirdeśāt yat tat acetana tvam nāma kim tat cetanā viparītam dharma bhūtam vastu uta cetanā pratiṣedha mātram iti yadi viparītam vastu cetanā vat saṃvedyam syāt atha cetanā pratiṣedha mātram tat na guṇaḥ iti 
NV_3.2.50	 itas ca na śarīra guṇaḥ cetanā śarīra vyāpi tvāt śarīra vat śarīra avayavāḥ cetanā utpattyā vyāpyante kaḥ vyāpti arthaḥ na kaḥ cit śarīra avayavaḥ cetanā hīnaḥ bhavati iti sarvasya cetanā nimitta tvāt śarīra vat śarīra avayavāḥ cetanāḥ prāpnuvanti bhavantu śarīra avayavāḥ api cetanāḥ na pratyaya vyavasthā prasaṅgāt śarīra vat śarīra avayavāḥ cetanā iti pratyaya vyavasthānam syāt 
NV_3.2.51–3.2.54	 na śarīra avayavāḥ cetanāḥ na keśa nakha ādiṣu anupalabdheḥ iti dṛṣṭānta sūtram saṃyogi dravyam keśa ādayaḥ iti na tu śarīra avayavāḥ iti tasmāt aprasaṅgaḥ ayam iti itas ca na śarīra guṇaḥ cetanā śarīra guṇa vaidharmyāt dvaye śarīra guṇāḥ bhavanti bāhya karaṇa pratyakṣāḥ ca rūpa ādayaḥ atīndriyam ca guru tvam vidha antaram tu cetanā na bāhya karaṇa pratyakṣāḥ antar saṃvedya tvāt na atīndriyāḥ manaḥ viṣaya tvāt tasmāt na śarīra guṇaḥ iti yathā itaretara vidharmāṇaḥ rūpa ādayaḥ na śarīra guṇa tvam ativartante tathā rūpa ādi vaidharmye api na cetanā śarīra guṇa tvam na hāsyati iti 
NV_3.2.55	 apratyakṣa tvāt ca dvaye śarīra guṇāḥ bhavanti iti uktaḥ sūtra arthaḥ rūpa ādīnām itaretara vaidharmyam ananu saṃhitam ca avyāvṛttam ca iti vaidharmya mātram anvayavyatireki tu cetanāyāḥ śarīra guṇa tva sādhanam na bhavati tasmāt asamam etat ye hetavaḥ anena prakaraṇena labhyante teṣām prayogaḥ na śarīra guṇaḥ cetanā nimitta antara abhāve virodhi guṇa adarśane ca sati ayāvat dravya bhāvi tvāt apsu auṣṇya vat iti śarīra vyāpi tvāt iti na sādhanam kim tu śarīre cetanām bruvataḥ doṣaḥ aneka cetana tva prasaṅgaḥ na śarīra guṇaḥ cetanā bāhya karaṇa apratyakṣa tvāt sukha ādi vat iti atha idam prakaraṇam nirṇīta artham kasmāt punar ārabhyam iti bahu parīkṣyamāṇam tattvam niścitataram bhavati iti atas ārabhyate iti 
NV_3.2.56	 parīkṣitā buddhiḥ manaḥ avasara prāptam parīkṣyate tat pratiśarīram ekam anekam iti vā avicāre jñāna ayaugapadyāt ekam manaḥ ayugapad jñānāni bhavanti iti etat pratyakṣam etat ca manasaḥ eka tvam sādhayati katham iti yadi bahūni manāṃsi syuḥ pratīndriyam manasaḥ sambandhaḥ iti yugapad aneka artha sannidhāne yugapad aneka vijñānāni bhaveyuḥ yat tu eka indriya grāhyeṣu artheṣu vijñānānām ayugapad janma tat na manasaḥ eka tve liṅgam anyatas tad bhāvāt anyathā hi karaṇa tvāt tat bhavati iti uktam 
NV_3.2.57–3.2.59	 iti śeṣam bhāṣye asya uttara dvārakam sūtram alāta cakra darśana vat tad upalabdhiḥ āśu sañcārāt yathā ālātasya bhramataḥ vidyamānaḥ kramaḥ naḥ upalabhyate tathā buddhīnām āśu bhāvāt vidyamānaḥ kramaḥ naḥ upalabhyate iti na ca asti ubhaya pakṣa sampratipannā buddhīnām yugapad utpattiḥ yayā bahu tvam manasaḥ pratipadyemahi iti yaḥ eva eka tve hetuḥ manasaḥ uktaḥ anena eva aṇu manaḥ adhyavasātavyam iti 
NV_3.2.60^1	 manasaḥ khalu bhoḥ sa indirya śarīre vṛttiḥ śarīre vicāryamāṇe manaḥ eva vicāritam bhavati atas punar śarīram vicāryate kim ayam śarīra sargaḥ karma nirapekṣaiḥ bhūtaiḥ ārabhyate āhosvit sa apekṣaiḥ iti vipratipatteḥ saṃśayaḥ śrūyate khalu atra vipratipattiḥ iti tatra idam tattvam pūrva kṛta phala anubandhāt tad utpattiḥ pūrva kṛtam iti pūrva śarīre yā pravṛttiḥ vāc buddhi śarīra ārambha lakṣaṇā tat pūrva kṛtam tasya phalam tad janitau dharma adharmau tayoḥ anubandhaḥ ātma samavetayoḥ pratibaddhayoḥ avasthānam vipāka kālasya aniyamāt iti aniyataḥ vipāka kālaḥ iha amutra jāti antare ca iti 
NV_3.2.60^2	 tena avasthitena prayuktebhyaḥ bhūtebhyaḥ pṛthivī ādibhyaḥ tasya śarīrasya utpattiḥ na svatantrebhyaḥ kasmāt punar karma dharma adharma saṃjñakam utpatti sama kālam phalam na dadāti kaḥ evam āha na dadāti iti vipāka kālasya aniyamāt yadā aśeṣa kāraṇa sannidhānam bhavati sannidhāne api ca yadā kāraṇāni apratibaddhāni bhavanti tadā dadāti api yadā punar na dadāti tadā vipacyamāna karma atiśaya pratibandhāt yaḥ vipacyamāna karma atiśayaḥ bhavati yasya dharma adharma samākhyātaḥ anupabhukta phalaḥ tena pratibandhāt vidyamānam api karma phalam na dadāti iti 
NV_3.2.60^3	 yāni ca prāṇi antarāṇi tasya karmaṇaḥ samāna upabhogāni teṣām vipacyamānaiḥ karma āśayaiḥ pratibandhāt yāni vā sattva antarāṇi tasya karmaṇaḥ phala bhogīni tasmin deśe teṣām tatra asannidhānāt yāni vā prāṇi antarāṇi bhāgīni tasya karmaṇaḥ tad karmabhiḥ pratibandhāt tasya vā karmaṇaḥ sahakāri dharma adharma lakṣaṇam nimittam na asti iti atas phalasya anārambhaḥ tasya vā sahakāriṇaḥ kāraṇasya pratibandhāt sattva antara karmaṇām vā sahakāriṇām utpatteḥ sattva antara karmaṇām vā sahakāriṇām pratibandhāt na sarvadā phalam dharma adharmau prayacchataḥ iti durvijñeyā ca karma gatiḥ sā na śakyāḥ manuṣya dharmaṇā avadhārayitum 
NV_3.2.60^4	 ākṛti mātram tu uktam iti kaḥ punar atra nyāyaḥ karma tantrāṇi bhūtāni śarīram ārabhante na nirapekṣāṇi iti ayam nyāyaḥ abhidhīyate puruṣa guṇa viśeṣa prerita bhūta pūrvakam śarīram puruṣa artha kriyā sāmarthyāt yat yat puruṣa artha kriyā samartham tat tat puruṣa guṇa viśeṣa prerita bhūta pūrvakam dṛṣṭam yathā ratha ādi puruṣa guṇena prayatnena preritaiḥ bhūtaiḥ ārabhyamāṇam puruṣa artha kriyā samartham dṛṣṭam tathā ca śarīram tasmāt idam api sa apekṣaiḥ bhūtaiḥ ārabhyate iti sukha duḥkha nimitvāt ghaṭa ādi vat iti itas ca kāryatvāt ratha ādi vat iti bāhya karaṇa grāhya tve sati rūpa ādimattvāt ghaṭa ādi vat eva 
NV_3.2.61	 atra nāstikaḥ evam āha bhūtebhyaḥ mūrti upādāna vat tad upādānam yathā karma nirapekṣebhyaḥ bhūtebhyaḥ nirvṛttāḥ mūrtayaḥ sikatā śarkarā gairi kāñcana prabhṛtayaḥ puruṣa artha kāri tvāt upādīyante tathā śarīra sargah api iti puruṣa artha kriyā sāmarthyāt iti asya hetoḥ anaikāntika tvadvārakam sūtram sādhana pakṣe dṛṣṭānta mātra tvāt asambaddham 
NV_3.2.62	 atha ayaḥ pakṣaḥ karma nirapekṣāṇi bhūtāni śarīram ārabhante puruṣa artha kriyā sāmarthyāt sikata ādi vat iti etat ca na sādhya sama tvāt yathā eva śarīra sargaḥ karma nirapekṣaiḥ bhūtaiḥ ārabhyate iti sādhyam tathā sikata ādīnām akarma nimittaḥ sargaḥ sādhyaḥ iti sikata ādīnām api ca karma nimittaḥ sargaḥ iti etasmāt eva hetoḥ sidhyati iti yathā ca ubhaya pakṣa sampratipannaḥ ratha ādi dṛṣṭāntaḥ puruṣa viśeṣa guṇa prerita bhūta pūrvakaḥ asti na tathā akarma nimitta sarga pakṣe dṛṣṭāntaḥ asti iti 
NV_3.2.63	 viṣamaḥ ca ayam upanyāsaḥ bhūtebhyaḥ mūrti upādāna vat iti na utpatti nimitta tvāt mātā pitroḥ mātā pitṛ śabdena lohita retasī bīja bhūte gṛhyete tatra pitroḥ putra phala anubhavanīye karmaṇī sattvasya ca garbha vāsa anubhavanīyam karma mātuḥ garbhāśaye śarīra utpattim prayojayanti tatra ca upapannam bīja anuvidhānam bīja anuvidhānāt ca yat jātīyau tasya pitarau tad jātīyaḥ sa bhavati iti 
NV_3.2.64–3.2.65	 utpatti nimitta tvāt iti prakṛtam etat api sikata ādibhiḥ vaidharmyam eva ucyate aśita pītam āhāraḥ tasya pākāt rasa dravyam nirvartate tad mātṛ śarīre upacīyate garbha śarīre ca upacitam kalala ādi bhāvena upacīyamānam karma sāpekṣaiḥ bhūtaiḥ peśya ādi bhāvam āpadyate yadi punar karma nirapekṣāṇi bhūtāni syuḥ sthālī ādi gatam iva annam pacyeta na tu idam asti tasmāt sa apekṣāṇi iti karma nirapekṣāṇi bhūtāni śarīram ārabhante iti sarvaḥ dampatyoḥ saṃyogaḥ putra ādi phalakaḥ syāt karmasāpekṣeṣu bhūteṣu upapannaḥ niyama abhāvaḥ iti 
NV_3.2.66^1	 sarva ātmabhiḥ sambandhāt sādhāraṇa vigrahavat tva prasaṅgaḥ niyama hetu abhāvāt iti ced atha manyase śarīram sarva ātmabhiḥ sambadhyate saṃyoga jena saṃyogena kriyā jena vā tatra śarīra ādi gataḥ na kaḥ cit niyama hetuḥ asti yena śarīram ekasya ātmanaḥ vyavatiṣṭheta na ca puruṣa gataḥ kaḥ cit atiśayaḥ vidyate yena śarīram ekasya puruṣasya upabhoga sādhanam bhavet asti ca niyamaḥ tasmāt vaktavyaḥ niyama hetuḥ iti etasya uttara dvārakam sūtram śarīra utpatti nimitta vat saṃyoga utpatti nimittam karma yena eva karmaṇā śarīram utpādyate tat eva tat śarīram niyamayati akarma nimitte tu śarīra sarge yathā uktaḥ doṣaḥ iti karmaṇaḥ tad sthatā kutas iti ced 
NV_3.2.66^2	 atha manyase yadi karma niyāmakam śarīra sargasya karmaṇi kutas niyamaḥ iti na sva saṃyoga utpatti niyamāt yaḥ yasya ātmanaḥ saṃyogaḥ tasmāt yat karma upajāyate tat tasya bhavati iti saṃyoge kutas niyamaḥ iti yathā eva karmaṇi paryanuyogaḥ na vyāvartate tathā saṃyoge api iti na manaḥ niyama hetu tvāt yasya ātmanaḥ yat manaḥ tena yaḥ saṃyogaḥ janyate sa tasya bhavati iti manasi api tulyam manasaḥ tarhi sarva ātmabhiḥ sambandhāt kim niyāmakam iti karmaṇaḥ niyāmaka tvāt yat manaḥ yadīyena karmaṇā upanibaddham tadīyam tat bhavati iti sarga ādau katham iti ced sarga ādeḥ anabhyupagamāt adeśyam anādiḥ saṃsāraḥ pūrva abhyasta sūtre pratipāditam etat ādimati saṃsāre eṣaḥ deśyaḥ nānā ādau iti 
NV_3.2.67	 kaḥ punar ayam niyamaḥ yathā ekasya ātmanaḥ śarīram tathā sarva ātmanam iti niyamaḥ anyasya anyathā anyasya anyathā iti aniyamaḥ bhedaḥ vyāvṛtti dṛṣṭaḥ śarīra bhedaḥ praṇinām aneka rūpaḥ sa ca karma nirapakṣaiḥ bhūtaiḥ śarīra ārambhe na yuktaḥ karmaṇām tu bhedāt śarīrāṇi bhidyante iti yuktam upapannaḥ ca tad viyogaḥ karma kṣaya upapatteḥ dve śarīrasya prakṛtī vyaktā ca avyaktā ca tatra avyaktāyāḥ karma samākhyāyāḥ prakṛteḥ upabhogāt prakṣayaḥ prakṣīṇe ca karmaṇi vidyamānāni api bhūtāni na śarīram utpādayanti iti upapannaḥ apavargaḥ karma nirapekṣeṣu bhūteṣu kasya prakṣayāt mokṣamāṇāḥ apavṛjyeran bhūta lakṣaṇāyāḥ prakṛteḥ anucchedāt 
NV_3.2.68^1	 tad adṛṣṭa kāritam iti ced atha manyase adṛṣṭa kāri tā śarīra utpattiḥ adṛṣṭa śabdena adarśanam ucyate adarśanam adṛṣṭam iti sarga ādau pradhānam puruṣa arthena hetunā pravartate tat pravartamānam mahat ādi bhāvena śarīram utpādayati utpanne śarīre draṣṭā dṛśyam paśyati dṛśyam ca dvedhāḥ viṣayāḥ nānātvam ca prakṛti puruṣayoḥ dṛṣṭena punar pradhānam caritārtha tvāt na pravartate iti tat evam adarśanam śarīra sarge hetuḥ tad bhāva bhāvi tvāt iti 
NV_3.2.68^2	 etasmin khalu darśane punar tad prasaṅgaḥ apavarge yā ca prāk pravṛtteḥ darśana nivṛttiḥ darśana abhimatā yā ca uttara kālam nivṛtteḥ sarge naḥ etayoḥ adarśanayoḥ kaḥ cit viśeṣaḥ adarśana nimittā ced śarīra utpattiḥ bhavati tena yathā prāk nānātva darśanāt pradhānam puruṣa artham pravartate tathā apavṛkte api iti na ca evam abhyupagamyate tasmāt na adarśanam sarge kāraṇam iti caritārtha tā viśeṣaḥ bhaviṣyati iti na yuktam carita arthānām acarita arthānām ca bhūtānām punar punar ārambha darśanāt ādyena śarīreṇa rūpa ādi upalabdheḥ kṛta tvāt dvitīya ādi śarīram śabda ādi upalabdhi sādhanam na syāt 
NV_3.2.68^3	 bhavati ca śabda ādi upalabdhi sādhanam dvitīya ādi śarīram tena gamyate caritārthāni api bhūtāni punar śarīram ārabhante iti puruṣa arthena ca hetunā punar śarīrāṇi ārabhante puruṣa arthaḥ ca puruṣa pradhāna nānā tva darśanam tasya ca akāraṇāt anarthakaḥ śarīra ārambhaḥ bhavati iti didṛkṣā viśeṣaḥ adarśanam iti ced atha manyase na adarśanam darśana abhāvaḥ kim tu didṛkṣā darśanam iti ucyate sā ca apavṛkte pradhāne dṛṣṭa tvāt na bhavati iti na prāk pravṛtteḥ tad abhāvāt yāvat pradhānam mahat ādi bhāvena na pariṇamate tāvat didṛkṣā na asti asatī katham kāraṇam bhaviṣyati pravṛtteḥ iti sarva śaktimat tvāt tadā api asti iti ced atha manyase sarvāḥ kāraṇa śaktayaḥ pradhāne vidyante tat idam ātma bhūtābhiḥ kāraṇa śaktibhiḥ sarva śaktimat pradhānam sarva śaktimat tvāt ca prāk api pravṛtteḥ pradhāne didṛkṣāḥ asti iti na apavarga abhāva prasaṅgāt 
NV_3.2.68^4	 didṛkṣā vat nānātva darśanam api asti iti apavarga abhāvaḥ vidyamāne ca nānātva darśane pradhānasya pravṛttiḥ ayuktā yadā ca nānātva darśanam tadā api didṛkṣā na vyāvartate na hi satā ātmānam jahāti iti vaḥ pakṣaḥ didṛkṣāyām ca satyām kutas apavargaḥ didṛkṣā nānātva darśane ca viruddhe katham ekasya ekasmin kāle bhavataḥ ajñānam adarśanam iti ca bruvāṇaḥ vikalpataḥ paryanuyojyaḥ kim jñāna abhāvaḥ ajñānam uta mithyājñānam ajñānam kim ca atas yadi abhāvaḥ apavargaḥ na prāpnoti prāk pravṛtteḥ apavṛkte ca pradhāne jñāna abhāvasya tulya tvāt atha mithyājñānam tat na yuktam prāk pravṛtteḥ tad abhāvāt katham abhāvaḥ buddhi dharmaka tvāt apavṛkte ca pradhāne na buddhiḥ asti katham tad dharmaḥ ajñānam bhaviṣyati iti satkārya vāda abhyupagamāt sarvadā asti iti bruvāṇaḥ mokṣam bādhate katham tattva jñānasya sarvadā bhāvāt tattva jñāna mithyā jñānayoḥ ca saha anavasthānāt pravṛtteḥ tādātmyam ayuktam 
NV_3.2.68^5	 na hi bhavatām pakṣe kim cit asat bhavati sat vā ātmānam jahāti iti sarva arthānām sambhavāt pradhānam kim artham pravartate iti vaktavyam atha abhivyakti nimittam pravṛttim pratipadyethāḥ sā api abhivyaktiḥ prāk pravṛtteḥ satī aho asatī iti pūrvavat prasaṅgaḥ yat ca prāk anupalabdham paścāt upalabhyate tat kim ūpa jāta viśeṣam uta anupajāta viśeṣam iti yadi viśeṣa upajananāt paścāt upalabhyate vyāhatam bhavati atha anupajāta viśeṣam kasmāt prāk naḥ upalabhyate iti vaktavyam satkārya vāda abhyupagame ca visphūrjatāḥ api na viśeṣa upajanaḥ śakyaḥ pratipādayitum na ca viśeṣa upajana pratyākhyāne vastunaḥ upalabdhi anupalabdhi bheda viṣaya tvam śakyam avagamayitum karma nimitte tu sarge dṛśya darśana artham bhūtāni śarīram puruṣa guṇa preritāni ārabhante iti yuktam na hi anutpanne śarīre draṣṭā nirāyatanaḥ dṛśyam paśyati iti apare tu adṛṣṭam paramāṇu guṇam varṇayanti teṣām api punar tad prasaṅgaḥ apavargaḥ iti paramāṇu guṇasya adṛṣṭasya śarīra utpatti nimitta tvāt punar tad prasaṅgaḥ apavargaḥ iti 
NV_3.2.69	 paramāṇavaḥ svakāt adṛṣṭāt saṃhanyante saṃhatāḥ ca dvi aṇuka ādinā prakrameṇa śarīram utpādayanti tat manaḥ sva guṇāt adṛṣṭāt upasarpati iti upasarpaṇa hetoḥ adṛṣṭasya nitya tvāt kimkṛtam apasarpaṇam iti karma āśaya kṣaye tu karma āśaya antarāt apasarpaṇam iti yuktam prāyaṇam ubhaya hetuḥ manaḥ vṛttiḥ adṛṣṭaḥ bhaviṣyati iti na yuktam ekasya jīvana prāyaṇa hetutva anupapatteḥ 
NV_3.2.70–3.2.71	 nitya tva prasaṅgaḥ iti prāyaṇa anupapattim brūmaḥ tat idam uktam upasarpaṇa hetoḥ adṛṣṭasya nitya tvāt apasarpaṇa hetoḥ ca adṛṣṭasya abhāvāt yādṛcchike tu prāyaṇe prāyaṇa bhedaḥ na syāt aṇu śyāma tā anitya tva vat etat syāt iti parihāram varṇayanti yathā kilāṇau śyāma tā nityāḥ atha ca agni saṃyogena pratiṣidhyate evam aṇu manasoḥ adṛṣṭaḥ samyak jñānena pratiṣetsyate iti 
NV_3.2.72	 etat ca na akṛta abhyāgama prasaṅgāt iti anupapanna pramāṇasya abhyupagamaḥ akṛta abhyupagamaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ yathāśruti vā sūtra arthaḥ akṛtasya karmaṇaḥ upabhoga prasaṅgāt iti etat ca vistareṇa uktam bhāṣye iti ātmā śarīram karaṇam arthaḥ buddhiḥ manaḥ tathā yat yathā vastu tattvena tat tathā iha upapāditam uddyota karasya 
NV_4.1.1	 manasaḥ anantaram pravṛttiḥ avasara prāptā parīkṣitavyāḥ iti atas āha pravṛttiḥ yathā uktā pravṛttiḥ yathā uktā tathā parīkṣitavyāḥ iti arthaḥ sūtrasya kim punar pravṛtteḥ parīkṣitavyam iti yāvat dharma adharma āśrayam parīkṣitam sarvā sā pravṛtteḥ parīkṣā tatra pravṛttiḥ dvayī bhavati kāraṇa rūpā kārya rūpā ca tatra kāraṇa rūpā pravṛttiḥ vāc buddhi śarīra ārambhaḥ iti kārya rūpā dharma adharma samākhyā duḥkha ādi sūtre varṇitā tatra kāraṇa rūpāyāḥ pravṛtteḥ viṃśatidhā bhedaḥ kārya rūpā tu pravṛttiḥ eka dravya abhyudayasya pratiniyamāt avasthitā vyāpaka kālasya niyamāt ātma samavāyāt guṇa bhūtāḥ anityā prāyaṇa ādi darśanāt tat uktam vipacyamāna karma āśaya prakṣaye prāyaṇam iti janmanaḥ kāraṇam pūrva kṛta phala anubandhāt tad utpattiḥ iti saṃsāra apavarga hetu bhūta tad bhāve saṃsāraḥ tad abhāve apavargaḥ iti evam ādi uktam 
NV_4.1.2	 pravṛtti anantarāḥ tarhi doṣāḥ iti abhidhīyantām iti atas āha tathā doṣāḥ uktāḥ iti buddhi samāna āśraya tvāt ātma guṇāḥ saṃsārasya anādi tvāt anādinā prabandhena pravartante samyak jñānāt ca mithyājñāna nivṛttau nivartante iti utpāda nirodha dharmakāḥ kāryatve sati asmad ādi indriya antara pratyakṣa tvāt acākṣuṣa pratyakṣa tvāt ca guṇāḥ 
NV_4.1.3^1	 pravartanā lakṣaṇāḥ doṣāḥ iti uktam tathā ca māna ādayaḥ pravartayanti iti lakṣaṇa sāmyāt te api upasaṃkhyeyāḥ iti na upasaṃkhyāynate saṃgṛhīta tvāt kena saṃgrahaḥ pravartanā lakṣaṇāḥ doṣāḥ iti anena eva tat trairāśyam rāga dveṣa moha artha antara bhāvāt teṣām tu lakṣaṇena saṃgṛhītānām tatrairāśyam rāga dveṣa moha artha antara bhāvāt teṣām doṣāṇām trayaḥ rāśayaḥ trayaḥ pakṣāḥ sambhavanti rāga pakṣaḥ dveṣapakṣaḥ moha pakṣaḥ iti tatra rāgapakṣaḥ kāmaḥ matsaraḥ spṛhā tṛṣṇā lobhaḥ iti dveṣapakṣaḥ krodhaḥ īrṣyāḥ asūyā drohaḥ amarṣaḥ iti moha pakṣaḥ mithyājñānam vicikitsā mānaḥ prasādaḥ iti kāmaḥ matsaraḥ iti evam ādi kim paryāya vacanam āho artha antara bhāvaḥ iti kim ca atas yadi paryāya vacanam trayaḥ rāśayaḥ iti na yuktam na hi paryāya śabdeṣu rāśi tvam sambhavati na hi indra śakra purandara śabdānām rāśi arthaḥ kaḥ cit asti 
NV_4.1.3^2	 artha antara bhāvaḥ tadā viśeṣaḥ vācyaḥ iti artha antara bhāvaḥ iti brūmaḥ tatra kāmaḥ strī gataḥ abhilāṣaḥ yā strī gatā prārthanā sā kāmaḥ iti evam ca āhuḥ na akāmayamānaḥ maṇḍayate iti akṣīyamāṇa vastu aparityāga icchā matsaraḥ yat vastu dīyamānam upabhujyamānam vā na kṣīyate tad aparityāga icchā sā matsaraḥ iti yathā rājakīyoda pānāt mā udakam pāḥ iti avastu ādāna icchā spṛhā yat vastu svam na bhavati tasya yā āditsā sā spṛhā punarbhava pratisandhāna hetu bhūtā tṛṣṇā yā punarbhava prārthanā sā tṛṣṇā iti pramāṇa viruddha para dravya ādāna icchā lobhaḥ pramāṇa viruddham para dravya ādānam kurvāṇaḥ lubdhaḥ iti ucyate iti eṣām ca sāmānyam rāgaḥ sāmānyena viśeṣaḥ saṃgṛhītaḥ iti śarīra indriya adhiṣṭhāna vaikṛtya hetuḥ krodhaḥ saṃjāte yasmin śarīra indriya adhiṣṭḥānāni vikṛtāni bhavanti sa krodhaḥ iti sādhāraṇe vastuni para abhiniveśa pratiṣedha icchā īrṣyā 
NV_4.1.3^3	 yat aparigṛhītam sādhāraṇam vastu tasmin yaḥ para abhiniveśa pratiṣedha abhiprāyaḥ sā īrṣyā para guṇa akṣamatā asūyā yā para guṇān śrutvā akṣamatā upajāyate sā asūyā para apakāra icchā drohaḥ aśaktasya yā param prati apacikīrṣā sā drohaḥ apakāra asahiṣṇu tā amarṣaḥ yā kṛta apakārasya asahiṣṇu tā saḥ amarṣaḥ asya ca dveṣaḥ sāmānyam tena saṃgrahaḥ viparyaya jñānam mithyājñānam atasmin tat iti pratyayaḥ viparyayaḥ iti saṃśayaḥ vicikitsā kim svid iti vidyamānā vidyamāna guṇa adhyāropeṇaḥ ātma utkarṣa pratyayaḥ mānaḥ āho aham asmi iti yathā śaktasya kartavyā karaṇam pramādaḥ yaḥ śaktaḥ sva kartavyam na karoti sa pramādaḥ iti asya ca sāmānyam mohaḥ tena saṃgrahaḥ iti atas trairāśyāt naḥ upasaṃkhyāyante iti kutas etat lokataḥ tad adhigateḥ lokataḥ ete kāma ādayaḥ evambhūteṣu abhiprāyeṣu prayujyante nābhi prāya mātre 
NV_4.1.3^4	 na hi bhikṣām prārthayamānaḥ kāmayate iti bhavati lakṣaṇasya tarhi abhedāt tritvam anupapannam ekam rāga dveṣa mohāḥ lakṣaṇa abhedāt rāga bheda vat iti na anupapannam rāga dveṣa moha artha antara bhāvāt sati api lakṣaṇasya abhede āntargaṇikam bhedakam lakṣaṇam asti tat upapatteḥ tritvam yathā rāga lakṣaṇena saṃgṛhītānām kāma ādīnām iti na ca sāmānyam eka tve kāraṇam sāmānyasya eva abhāvaḥ syāt yadi rāga dveṣa mohānām eka tvam syāt samānam etat lakṣaṇam iti etat eva na syāt iti na hi ekasya sāmānyam kim punar āntar gaṇikam lakṣaṇam iti sakti lakṣaṇaḥ rāgaḥ yaḥ viṣayeṣu abhiṣvaṅgaḥ sa rāgaḥ amarṣa lakṣaṇaḥ dveṣaḥ asahiṣṇu tā duḥkhasya duḥkha sādhanānām vā iti dveṣaḥ mithyā pratipatti lakṣaṇaḥ mohaḥ yathā avasthite padārthe atatha abhāva pratipattiḥ yā etat ca rāga dveṣa mohānām vyavacchedakam lakṣaṇam ātma pratyakṣam iti 
NV_4.1.4–4.1.5	 ekam rāga dveṣa mohāḥ eka pratyanīka tvāt vibhāga vat iti yathā vibhāgaḥ ekena eva saṃyogena virudhyamānaḥ ekaḥ bhavati tathā tattva jñānena ekena virudhyante rāga ādayaḥ tasmāt ekam rāga ādayaḥ iti eka pratyanīkāḥ ca rūpa ādayaḥ eka agni saṃyoga virodhinaḥ na ca eṣām eka tvam iti anaikāntikam eka yoni tvāt ekam rāga ādayaḥ śabda vat iti api anena eva pratyuktam eka yonayaḥ rūpa ādayaḥ na ca eṣām eka tvam iti 
NV_4.1.6	 sati ca artha antara bhāve teṣām mohaḥ pāpīyān na amūḍhasya itara utpatteḥ teṣām mohaḥ pāpīyān pāpatamaḥ pāpiṣṭhaḥ iti vā prāpte dvau dvau abhipretya pāpīyān iti ucyate rāga mohayoḥ mohaḥ pāpīyān dveṣa mohayoḥ mohaḥ pāpīyān iti kasmāt na amūḍhasya itara utpatteḥ na amūḍhasya itarau bhavataḥ mūḍhaḥ kupyati mūḍhaḥ rajyate mūḍhaḥ muhyati iti tattva jñānāt ca moha nivṛttau rāga ādi nivṛttiḥ iti eka pratyanīka tā yasmāt tattva jñānāt nivṛtte mohe na rāga dveṣau bhavataḥ atas eka pratyanīka tā na punar eka tvāt iti evam ca kṛtvā duḥkha ādīnām uttarottara apāye tad anantara abhāvāt apavargaḥ iti sidhyati 
NV_4.1.7–4.1.9	 prāptaḥ tarhi nimitta naimittika bhāvāt artha antara bhāvaḥ doṣebhyaḥ adoṣaḥ mohaḥ doṣa nimitta tvāt rūpa ādi vat iti na atra kārya kāraṇa bhāvena padārthānām tathā abhāvaḥ atatha abhāvaḥ vā sidhyati kim tu lakṣaṇasya abhedāt iti doṣa lakṣaṇam ca mohe asti iti doṣaḥ mohaḥ tulya jātīyāyām anekavidha vikalpaḥ nimitta naimittika bhāvaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti yathā buddhiḥ buddhi antarasya nimittam tulya jātīyā ca iti turya ādayaḥ dravyasya nimittam dravya jātīyāḥ nodana abhighāta saṃyukta saṃyogāḥ saṃskāraḥ ca guṇāḥ iti 
NV_4.1.10	 parīkṣitāḥ doṣāḥ doṣa an antaram pretyabhāvaḥ tasya asiddhiḥ ātmanaḥ nitya tvāt nityaḥ ātmā na jāyate na miryate ubhayam ca pretyabhāvaḥ mṛtvā punarjanma tatra ayam siddhārtha anuvādaḥ ātma nitya tve pretyabhāva siddhiḥ nityaḥ san ātmā praiti jāyate ca iti kim uktam bhavati mriyate iti pūrva utpannābhiḥ śarīra indriya buddhi vedanābhiḥ viyujyate iti kim ca uktam bhavati jāyate iti apūrvābhiḥ nikāya viśiṣṭābhiḥ śarīra indriya buddhi vedanābhiḥ sambadhyate iti na punar janma maraṇe ātmanaḥ utpāda nirodhau nitya tvāt ātmanaḥ nityaḥ ātmā iti etat pūrva abhyasta sūtre pratipāditam yasya punar ātmanaḥ utpāda nirodhau janma maraṇe tasya akṛta abhyāgama kṛta nāśa doṣa prasaṅgaḥ iti uktam śarīra dāhe pātaka abhāvāt iti sūtram varṇayadbhiḥ 
NV_4.1.11	 katham utpattiḥ iti ced kiṃdharmakāt kāraṇāt idam śarīra indriya mahābhūta ādi vyaktam utpadyate iti vyaktāt vyaktānām pratyakṣa prāmāṇyāt kim punar vyaktam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam rūpa ādi yuktam dravyam tad sāmānyāt paramāṇu lakṣaṇam api pṛthivī ādi kāraṇam vyaktam iti ucyate kim punar sāmānyam rūpa ādi yogaḥ rūpa ādi sāmānyāt paramāṇavaḥ api vyaktāḥ iti ucyante rūpa ādi yuktebhyaḥ paramāṇubhyaḥ ghaṭa ādi gavā ādi vyaktam utpadyate iti kaḥ punar atra nyāyaḥ pratyakṣa prāmāṇyāt dṛṣṭā rūpa ādi madbhyaḥ rūpa ādimatām utpattiḥ iti na anekāntāt na ayam ekāntaḥ rūpa ādi madbhyaḥ rūpa ādimataḥ utpattiḥ iti arūpāt api saṃyogāt rūpa ādimat utpadyamānam ghaṭa ādi gavā ādi dṛṣṭam iti na sūtra artha aparijñānāt na ayam sūtra arthaḥ rūpa ādimat rūpa ādimataḥ eva utpadyate iti api tu rūpa ādimad sāmagrī pūrvakam gavā ādi vyaktam iti sūtra arthaḥ evam ca sati na anekāntaḥ asti na hi arūpāyāḥ sāmagryāḥ rūpa ādimat kāryam iti 
NV_4.1.12–4.1.13	 sajātīyāt sajātīyam utpadyate iti matvā pratiṣedhaḥ na sūtra artha aparijñānāt iti na brūmaḥ sarvam sarvasya kāraṇam iti yaḥ ca sarvam sarvasya kāraṇa tvena abhyupeyāt saḥ evam pratyavastheyaḥ na ghaṭāt ghaṭaḥ utpadyamānaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti api tu vyaktāt ghaṭa niṣpatteḥ apratiṣedhaḥ yat api ghaṭa ādikam vyaktam utpadyate tat api vyaktāt eva kapāla ādeḥ vyaktāt ca utpadyamānam ghaṭa ādi na kimcid bādhyate iti rūpa ādimad sāmagrī pūrvakam gavā ādi vyaktam darśana sparśanābhyām eka artha grahaṇāt ghaṭa vat iti śabda vat vā vaidharmyeṇa tat etat tattvam 
NV_4.1.14	 atas param prāvādukānām darśanāni upanyasya kāni cit pratiṣidhyante kāni cit abhyanujñāyante iti tatra tāvat abhāvāt bhāva utpattiḥ na anupamṛdya prādurbhāvāt abhāvāt bhāvaḥ jāyate iti kasya cit darśanam tatra ca nyāyam bruvate na anupamṛdya prādurbhāvāt iti na kila avinaṣṭe kāraṇe kāryam utpadyate iti yathā bīja vināśa uttaram aṅkuraḥ prādurbhavati yadi ca bīja vināśaḥ aṅkura kāraṇam na abhaviṣyat avinaṣṭe api bīje aṅkuraḥ abhaviṣyat na ca evam asti tasmāt bīja vināśaḥ aṅkura kāraṇam iti 
NV_4.1.25	 upamṛdya prādurbhavati iti vyāghātaḥ yat upamṛdnāti tat asti na hi asat upamarda kāraṇam iti yat ca prādurbhavati tat na asti na hi sat utpadyate iti tat idam upamṛdnāti prādurbhavati ca iti vyāhatam ucyate kaḥ vyāghātaḥ saha asambhavaḥ yadi upamṛdnāti na jāyate atha jāyate naḥ upamṛdnāti 
NV_4.1.16^1	 atīte anāgate ca kāraka śabdāḥ prayujyamānāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ atīte tāvat bhinnam kumbham anuśocati bhinnasya kumbhasya kapālāni abhūt kumbhaḥ iti anāgate api putraḥ janiṣyate janiṣyamāṇam putram abhinandati janiṣyamāṇasya putrasya nāma karoti iti ajātāḥ putrāḥ sthaviram tāpayanti iti bahulam prayogāḥ bhāktāḥ evam ayam prādurbhaviṣyan aṅkuraḥ upamṛdnāti iti ucyate kaḥ punar upamarda arthaḥ ānantarya sāmarthyāt anantara utpatti arthaḥ yasmāt bīja upamardāt anantaram ayam prādurbhavati iti atra utkam vyāghātāt iti na ajātena upamardaḥ naḥ upamarda samarthaḥ jāyate iti 
NV_4.1.16^2	 yat api idam ucyate atīte ca anāgate ca kāraka śabdāḥ prayujyante iti na prayogaḥ vāryate api tu asataḥ kāraṇāt utpattiḥ na yuktāḥ iti kāraka śabdānām ca traikālikaḥ prayogaḥ tat uktam prāmāṇya sāmānya cintāyām vṛkṣaḥ tiṣṭhati iti yathā yat punar etat ānantarya sāmarthyāt upamṛdya prādurbhavati iti ucyate iti na bīja nāśaḥ aṅkurasya kāraṇam api tu vyāhata vyūhānām bīja avayavānām pūrva vyūha nivṛttau vyūha antaram utpadyate iti vyūha antarāt aṅkuraḥ āvirbhavati iti na ca avinaṣṭe pūrva vyūhe vyūha antareṇa śakyate bhavitum iti ānantaryam prādurbhāva arthaḥ evam ca bīja upādānam yuktam iti 
NV_4.1.17–4.1.18	 asya ca arthasya jñāpana artham sūtram na vinaṣṭebhyaḥ aniṣpatteḥ iti na hi bīja vināśaḥ aṅkurasya kāraṇam api tu bīja avayavāḥ pūrva vyūha parityāgena iti arthaḥ sūtrasya pūrvam bīja vināśaḥ paścāt aṅkura utpattiḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ abhāvaḥ ced aṅkura utpatti kāraṇam syāt sarvam sarvasmāt utpadyeta abhāvasya nirviśeṣa tvāt na hi śāli bīje vinaṣṭe kā cit anvaya śaktiḥ asti ananvitam ca kāryam sarvābhiḥ śaktibhiḥ utpadyeta anvitam tu dṛṣṭam tasmāt na abhāvaḥ kāraṇam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NV_4.1.19	 aparaḥ idānīm āha īśvaraḥ kāraṇam puruṣa karma aphalya darśanāt puruṣaḥ ayam samīhamānaḥ na avaśyam samīhā phalam āpnoti tena avagamyate para adhīnam puruṣasya karma phala avadhānam iti nirapekṣaḥ ced puruṣaḥ karma phala bhoge samarthaḥ syāt na kasya cit aphalā kriyā bhavet na kaḥ cit duḥkham kuryāt iti ubhayam ca dṛṣṭam tasmāt īśvaraḥ kāraṇam iti 
NV_4.1.20	 na puruṣa karma abhāve phala aniṣpatteḥ iti īśvaraḥ kāraṇam bhavet puruṣa karma antareṇa pi sukha duḥkha upabhogaḥ bhavet tatas ca kriyā vilopaḥ anirmokṣa prasaṅgaḥ ca īśvarasya eka rūpa tvāt eka rūpā kriyāḥ iti atha īśvaraḥ kāraṇa bheda anuvidhānena kāryam nirvartayati yat apekṣate tat na karoti iti prāptam na hi kulālaḥ daṇḍa ādi karoti evam karma ādi apekṣaḥ ced īśvaraḥ jagat utpatti kāraṇam syāt karmaṇi īśvaraḥ anīśvaraḥ syāt 
NV_4.1.21^1	 na brūmaḥ karma ādi anapekṣaḥ īśvaraḥ kāraṇam iti api tu puruṣa karma īśvaraḥ anugṛhṇāti kaḥ anugraha arthaḥ yat yathābhūtam yasya ca yadā paripāka kālaḥ tat tathā tadā ca viniyuṅkte iti yaḥ punar īśvaram karma anapekṣam kāraṇa tvena pratipadyate tasya anirmokṣa tva ādi doṣaḥ sa apekṣe tu īśvare yathā uktaḥ na doṣaḥ śeṣam bhāṣye tat kārita tvāt iti evam bruvatā nimitta kāraṇam īśvaraḥ iti upagatam bhavati yat ca nimittam tat itarayoḥ samavāyi kāraṇā samavāyi kāraṇayoḥ anugrāhakam yathā turya ādi tantūnām tad saṃyogānām ca iti īśvaraḥ ced jagataḥ nimittam yat jagataḥ sākṣāt upādānakāraṇam tat kim uktam pṛthivī ādi parama sūkṣmam paramāṇu saṃjñitam vyaktam kāraṇam iti vyakta kāraṇa abhyupagame ca sati nimitta viśeṣa vipratipattau īśvara prakriyā yasmāt nimitta kāraṇe vipratipadyante ke cit kālam ke cit īśvaram ke cit prakṛtam iti tat evam nimitta viśeṣa vipratipattau kim nyāyam iti īśvaraḥ eva nyāyam tatra hi pramāṇāni avighātena pravartante iti astitva asiddhiḥ iti ced 
NV_4.1.21^2	 atha manyase siddhe īśvarasya astitve kāraṇa antara nirākaraṇam nimitta kāraṇa bhāvaḥ ca siddhyet tat tu asiddham tasmāt ayuktam etat iti na atas eva tad upapatteḥ yena eva nyāyena īśvarasya kāraṇa tvam sidhyati tena eva astitvam iti na hi avidyamānam kāraṇam iti kaḥ punar īśvarasya kāraṇa tve nyāyaḥ ayam nyāyaḥ abhidhīyate pradhāna paramāṇu karmāṇi prāk pravṛtteḥ buddhimat kāraṇa adhiṣṭhitāni pravartante acetana tvāt vā asya ādi vat iti yathā vā asya ādi buddhimatā takṣṇāḥ adhiṣṭhitam acetana tvāt pravartate tathā pradhāna paramāṇu karmāṇi acetanāni pravartante 
NV_4.1.21^3	 tasmāt tāni api buddhimat kāraṇa adhiṣṭhitāni iti tatra pradhāna kāraṇikāh tāvat puruṣa artham adhiṣṭhāyakam pradhānasya varṇayanti puruṣa arthena prayuktam pradhānam pravartate iti puruṣa arthaḥ ca dvedhā bhavati śabda ādi upalabdhiḥ guṇa puruṣa antara darśanam ca iti tat ubhayam pradhāna pravṛttim vinā na bhavati iti na prāk pravṛtteḥ tad abhāvāt yāvat pradhānam mahat ādi bhāvena na pariṇamate tāvat na śabda ādi upalabdhiḥ asti na guṇa puruṣa antara upalabdhiḥ iti hetu abhāvāt pradhāna pravṛttiḥ ayuktā 
NV_4.1.21^4	 atha asti na asat ātmānam lambhate na san nirudhyate iti evam ca sati vidyamānaḥ puruṣa arthaḥ pradhānam pravartayati iti na puruṣa arthāya pradhānasya pravṛttiḥ na hi loke yat yasya bhavati sa tad artham punar yatate iti satatam ca pravṛttiḥ prāpnoti kāraṇasya sannihita tvāt puruṣa arthaḥ pravṛtteḥ kāraṇam iti puruṣa arthasya nitya tvāt satatam pravṛttyā bhavitavyam iti atha vidyamānaḥ api na pravartayati na tarhi puruṣa arthaḥ kāraṇam iti yasya abhāvāt pradhānam na pravartate yasya ca bhāvāt pravartate tat kāraṇam iti 
NV_4.1.21^5	 atha vidyamānaḥ pratibandhāt na pravartayati pratibandha apagamasya aśakya tvāt satatam apravṛttiḥ yaḥ tat pratibandha kāraṇam puruṣa arthasya tasya apagamaḥ kartum aśakyaḥ na tadā ātmānam jahāti iti pratibandhakasya ca nitya tvāt nityam apravṛttyā bhavitavyam yā ca bhavantaḥ sattva rajaḥ tamasām sāmya avasthām prakṛtim varṇayanti sā kutas nivartate iti vaktavyam na ca anivṛttāyām sāmya avasthāyām vaiṣamyeṇa śakyam bhavitum atha aṅga aṅgībhāvasya aniyamāt vaiṣamyam bhavati tatra api bhavantam paryanuyuñjmahe katham sāmyena avasthitam adhikam hīnam vā bhavati na apūrva upacayaḥ vidyate na pūrvahānam asti iti 
NV_4.1.21^6	 yān ca śabda ādīn prāc anupalabdha svarūpān puruṣaḥ upalabhate buddhiḥ upalambhayati iti te kim upajāta viśeṣāḥ uta anupajāta viśeṣāḥ iti yadi upajāta viśeṣāḥ upalabhyante iti vyāhatam bhavati na asat ātmānam labhate iti atha anupajāta viśeṣāḥ eva upalabhyate tathā api anivṛttaḥ vyāghātaḥ pradhānam puruṣa artham prati pravartayati iti sa ayam pradhāna vādaḥ yāvat yāvat vicāryate tāvat tāvat pramāṇa vṛttam bādhate iti ye api paramāṇūn puruṣa karma adhiṣṭhitān jagataḥ kāraṇa tvena varṇayanti tān prati idam ucyate paramāṇavaḥ pravartante iti satatam pravṛttyā bhavitavyam atha kāla viśeṣa apekṣāḥ pravartante pramāṇubhiḥ kālaḥ vyākhyātaḥ yathā acetana tvāt paramāṇavaḥ buddhimantam adhiṣṭḥātāram apekṣante tathā kālaḥ api iti na hi tatra acetana tvam nivartate iti kṣīra ādi vat acetanasya api pravṛttiḥ iti ced yathā apatya bharaṇa artham kṣīra ādeḥ acetanasya api pravṛttiḥ evam paramāṇavaḥ acetanāḥ santaḥ puruṣa artham pravartiṣyante iti tat na yuktam sādhya sama tvāt 
NV_4.1.21^7	 yathā eva paramāṇavaḥ svatantrāḥ pravartante iti sādhyam tathā kṣīra ādi acetanam svatantram pravartate iti yadi ca kṣīra ādi svatantram pravarteta mṛteṣu api pūrvavat pravarteta na tu pravartate atas avagamyate buddhimat kāraṇa adhiṣṭhitam tat api na ca ayam hetuḥ tasmāt na pravartate evam yāvat yāvat acetanam pravartate sarvam tat buddhimat kāraṇa adhiṣṭhitam iti ayam aparaḥ hetuḥ buddhimat kāraṇa adhiṣṭhitam mahābhūta ādi vyaktam iti sukha duḥkha ādi nimittam bhavati rūpa ādimattvāt turya ādi vat iti 
NV_4.1.21^8	 dharma adharmau buddhimat kāraṇa adhiṣṭhitau puruṣasya upabhogam kurutaḥ karaṇa tvāt vā asya ādi vat iti ātmā eva adhiṣṭhātā dharma adharmayoḥ bhaviṣyati iti ced yasya tau dharma adharmau saḥ eva adhiṣṭhātā bhaviṣyati iti na yuktam prāk kāya karaṇa utpatteḥ tad asambhavāt yāvat kāya karaṇa saṅghātaḥ naḥ upajāyate puruṣasya tāvat ayam ajñaḥ upasandhātā api upalabhyān api tāvat rūpa ādīn naḥ upalabhate kutas anupalabhyau dharma adharmau upalapsyate iti yadi ca puruṣaḥ svatantraḥ pravartate na duḥkham kuryāt na hi kaḥ cit ātmanaḥ duḥkham icchati iti 
NV_4.1.21^9	 yaḥ ca ātmanaḥ aṅga upaghātam śirascheda ādi vā karoti saḥ api tad vaikalye prāyaṇe vā hita buddhiḥ pravartate iti yadi punar dharma adharmābhyām eva adhiṣṭhitāḥ paramāṇavaḥ pravarteran na yuktam idam acetana tvāt na hi kim cit acetanam svatantram adhiṣṭhāyakam dṛṣṭam iti abhyupagamya api brūmaḥ dharma adharmayoḥ paramāṇuṣu vṛtti sāmarthyam na karaṇasya kevalasya kiryā nivṛttau asāmarthyāt na hi karaṇam kevalam kriyām nirvartayat upalabhyate atha paramāṇu apekṣābhyām dharma adharmābhyām kriyā janyate etat api na yuktam adṛṣṭa tvāt 
NV_4.1.21^10	 na hi karma karaṇābhyām kriyām janyamānām kva cit api paśyāmaḥ iti ātmā kartā bhaviṣyati iti uktam etat ajña tvāt iti akāraṇa utpattiḥ bhaviṣyati iti na yuktam adṛṣṭa tvāt iti na ca anyā gatiḥ asti tasmāt buddhimat kāraṇa adhiṣṭhitāḥ paramāṇavaḥ karmāṇi ca pravartante iti kriyānāveśāt akāraṇam iti ced atha manyase ye khalu kartāraḥ bhavanti te kriyā viṣṭhāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ kulāla ādayaḥ iti kriyā rahitaḥ ca īśvaraḥ tasmāt akāraṇam iti na vikalpa anupapatteḥ īśvaraḥ niṣkriyaḥ iti kām kriyām adhikṛtya ucyate 
NV_4.1.21^11	 dvayī hi naḥ śāstre kriyā utkṣepaṇa ādikā ca ākhyāta śabda vācyā ca yadi ākhyāta śabda vācyām adhikṛtya ucyate tadā asiddhaḥ hetuḥ svātantrya abhyupagamāt svātantryam hi bhagavati nityam asti kim punar svātantryam anya kāraka aprayojya tvam itara kāraka aprayoktṛ tvam ca tat uktam kārakāṇi varṇayadbhiḥ iti atha utkṣepaṇa ādikām adhikṛtya ucyate niṣkriyaḥ iti tadā anekāntaḥ kriyāvat ca kāraṇam dṛṣṭam niṣkriyam ca iti kadā cit dravyāṇi uparata kriyāṇi dravyam ārabhante saṃyogāt nivṛtte karmaṇi saṃyoga upakaraṇāni dravyāṇi dravyam ārabhante iti niṣkriyāṇām ārambhaḥ 
NV_4.1.21^12	 yadā ca yugapad bahūni dravyāṇi saṃhanyante tadā asādhāraṇa kārya vyāvṛttebhyaḥ saṃyogebhyaḥ ekam eva dravyam utpadyate eka avayava vibhāge tu dravya nivṛttau śeṣāṇi dravya antarāṇi dravyam ārabhante iti niṣkriyāṇām ārambhaḥ kāni cit punar kriyāvanti ārabhante tat yathā anyatara karma jāt saṃyogāt nivṛtte karmaṇi itarasmin dravye karma nivṛtti sama kālam eva dravyam utpadyate tadā kriyāvatā dravyeṇa kriyāvatām ārambhaḥ virodhaḥ ca utkṣepaṇa ādikāyāḥ kriyāyāḥ anabhyupagamāt iti 
NV_4.1.21^13	 na kāraṇam īśvaraḥ vikalpa anupapatteḥ kartā ced īśvaraḥ kim sa apekṣaḥ karoti uta nirapekṣaḥ iti kim ca atas yadi sa apekṣaḥ yat apekṣate tasya akartā iti evam anyatra api prasaṅgaḥ tat api sādhanam yena karoti tasya akartā iti atha ayam kim cit anapekṣya karoti tadvat anyatra api prasaṅgaḥ atha ayam sarvam anapekṣaḥ karoti evam api puruṣa karma aphalam prasajyate anirmokṣaḥ ca yaḥ ca akarma nimitte sarge doṣaḥ saḥ iha api prasajyate iti nirapekṣa kartṛ tvasya anabhyupagamāt dharma adharma vaiphalya ādi doṣaḥ na asti 
NV_4.1.21^14	 na ca akarma nimitte sarge doṣaḥ iti yena karoti na tasya akartā iti ced na anekāntāt na ayam ekāntaḥ asti yena karoti sa tat na karoti iti yathā aneka śilpa paryavadātaḥ puruṣaḥ karaṇa antara upādānaḥ vā asya ādi karoti vā asya ādi upādānaḥ daṇḍa ādi karoti tad upādānaḥ ghaṭa ādīn na ca paryāya kartṛ tve sati kartṛ tvam tathā īśvaraḥ api dharma adharma upādānaḥ śarīra sukha ādikam ātma manaḥ saṃyoga śuddha aśuddha abhisandhi sādhanaḥ ca dharma adharmau sukha duḥkha smṛti apekṣaḥ tad sādhana ādi apekṣaḥ ca śuddham aśuddham ca abhisandhim iti 
NV_4.1.21^15	 yadā karoti tadā sādhanasya akartā iti ced atha manyase yadā ayam sādhyam kim cit vastu nirvartayati tadā yena sādhayati tasya akartā prasajyate iti na etat evam na brūmaḥ sarvān arthān ayam ekasmin kāle karoti iti api tu paryāyeṇa paryāya kartṛ tve ca ayam adoṣaḥ yadā ādau karoti tasya asādhana utpattiḥ iti ced atha manyase yadi śarīra ādi kartṛ tvam dharma adharma ādi apekṣasya atha yat ādau karoti katham tat ādeḥ anabhyupagamāt acodyam anādiḥ ayam saṃsāraḥ iti pratipāditam etat dharma adharma sāphalyam ca evam 
NV_4.1.21^16	 yadi ca anādiḥ saṃsāraḥ sa apekṣaḥ kartā evam prāṇi antara samavāyinām dharma adharmāṇām sāphalyam atha ayam īśvaraḥ kurvāṇaḥ kim artham karoti iti loke hi ye kartāraḥ bhavanti te kim cit vastu uddiśya pravartante idam āpsyāmi idam hāsyāmi ca iti na punar īśvarasya heyam asti duḥkha abhāvāt naḥ upādeyam vaśi tvāt krīḍā artham iti eke eke tāvat bruvate krīḍā artham īśvaraḥ sṛjati iti nanu etat ayuktam krīdā hi nāma rati artham bhavati vinā krīdayā ratim avindatām na ca rati arthī bhagavān duḥkha abhāvāt iti uktam 
NV_4.1.21^17	 duḥkhinaḥ ca sukha upagama artham krīḍanti vibhūti khyāpana artham iti apare jagataḥ vaiśvarūpyam khyāpanīyam iti īśvaraḥ pravartate iti apare manyante etat api tādṛś eva na hi vibhūti khyāpanena kaḥ cit atiśayaḥ labhyate na ca asya ākhyāpanena kim cit hīyate iti kim artham tarhi karoti tad svābhāvyāt pravartate iti aduṣṭam yathā bhūmi ādīni bhūtāni dhāraṇa ādi kriyām tad svābhāvyāt kurvanti tathā īśvaraḥ api tad svābhāvyāt pravartate pravṛtti svabhāvakam tattvam iti tad svābhāvyāt satatam pravṛttiḥ iti ced 
NV_4.1.21^18	 atha manyase yadi pravṛtti svabhāvakam tat tattvam pravṛtti nivṛttī na prāpnutaḥ na hi pravṛtti svabhāvake tattve nivṛttiḥ yujyate iti krameṇa ca utpattiḥ na prāpnoti tattvasya eka rūpa tvāt idam idānīm bhavatu idam mā bhavatu iti etat na yuktam na hi eka rūpāt kāraṇāt kārya bhedaḥ paśyāmaḥ iti na eṣaḥ doṣaḥ buddhimat tva viśeṣaṇāt buddhimat tattvam iti etat pratipāditam buddhimat tayā ca viśiṣyamāṇam sa apekṣam sa apekṣam ca na sarvam pravartate na ca sarvam ekasmin kāle utpādayati yasya kāraṇa sānnidhyam tat bhavati 
NV_4.1.21^19	 yadā asannihita kāraṇam tat na bhavati iti na ca sarvasya yugapad kāraṇa sānnidhyam asti iti atas sarvasya yugapad utpādaḥ na prasaktaḥ sa khalu pravartamānaḥ dharma adharmayoḥ paripāka kālam apekṣate kāraṇa antara utpādam tad bhāginām ca sattvānām tatra sannidhānam tad bhāgi sattva dharma adharma paripākam ca tat apratibandham ca iti yat tat īśvarasya aiśvaryam kim tat nityam anityam vā iti yadi anityam tasya kāraṇam vaktavyam yasya ca anityam aiśvaryam tasya kāraṇtaḥ bhavati aṇima ādeḥ evam anyeṣām api iti anekaḥ īśvaraḥ prasajyate atha aneka tve kim bādhyate iti ekasmin vastuni vyāhata kāmayoḥ īśvarayoḥ pravṛttiḥ na prāpnoti atha ekam itaraḥ atiśete yaḥ atiśete saḥ īśvaraḥ naḥ itaraḥ iti atha nityam aiśvaryam dharma vaiyarthyam na tat dharmāt bhavati iti nityam iti brūmaḥ na ca dharma vaiyarthyam doṣaḥ tasya eva yaḥ dharmaḥ saḥ īśvare na asau tatra aiśvaryam karoti kim tu pratyātma vṛttīn dharma adharma sannicayān anugṛhṇāti na ca īśvare dharmaḥ asti iti acodyam etat 
NV_4.1.21^20	 tad svabhāva an avadhāraṇāt sandehaḥ īśvaraḥ kim dravyam āho guṇa ādīnām anyatamaḥ iti dravyam buddhi guṇa tvāt dravya antara vat iti buddhimat tvāt tarhi ātma antaram iti na ātma antaram guṇa bhedāt yathā guṇa bhede sati pṛthivī ādayaḥ na ātmānaḥ tathā guṇa bhinnaḥ īśvaraḥ tasmāt asau api naḥ ātmā iti kaḥ punar asya guṇa bhedaḥ eke tāvat bruvate dharma jñāna vairāgya aiśvaryāṇi atiśayavanti tasmin iti nitya tvam atiśayaḥ etat tu na buddhyāmahe yathā buddhi mat tāyām īśvarasya pramāṇa sadbhāvah naḥ evam dharma ādi nitya tve pramāṇam asti 
NV_4.1.21^21	 na ca aprāmāṇikam pratipattum śakyam iti atiśayaḥ tu buddhi nitya tvam guṇa bhedaḥ tatra hi nityā buddhiḥ saṃkhyā ādayaḥ ca sāmānya guṇāḥ ṣaḍguṇaḥ ākāśa vat īśvaraḥ iti atha asya buddhi nitya tve kim pramāṇam iti nanu idam eva buddhimat kāraṇa adhiṣṭhitāḥ paramāṇavaḥ pravartante iti buddhi mat tāyām etat sādhanam sā punar nityāḥ iti etat kutas pratyartha niyama asambhavāt ye khalu pratyartha niyatāḥ buddhi bhedāḥ te śarīra ādi kāraṇa sannidhāne sati bhavanti na tu iyam pratyartha niyatāḥ yugapad aneka kārya utpatti darśanāt 
NV_4.1.21^22	 tat yathā sthāvara bhedasya anekasya yugapad utpādaḥ iti sa ca pratyartha niyateṣu buddhi bhedeṣu īsvarasya na yuktaḥ saṃkhyā parimāṇa pṛthaktva saṃyoga vibhāga buddhayaḥ eva tasya guṇāḥ atha buddhimat tayā īśvarasya śarīra yogam api pratipadyate tena api pratipadyamānena śarīra ādayaḥ nityāḥ anityāḥ vā avaśyam eṣitavyāḥ yadi anityāḥ dharma adharma sadbhāvaḥ api abhyupeyaḥ tad abhyupagame ca tat tantra tvāt īśvaraḥ naḥ īśvaraḥ syāt atha nityāni śarīra ādīni kalpayasi evam api dṛṣṭa viparītam kalpitam bhavati 
NV_4.1.21^23	 dṛṣṭa viparyayam pratipadyamānena varam buddheḥ eva nitya tvam pratipattavyam iti atha santāna vartinīm anekām buddhim īśvare pratipadyeta evam api na yugapad utpādaḥ sthāvara ādīnām prāpnoti atha tāḥ santāna vartinyaḥ sarva artha abuddhayaḥ bhavanti iti evam api dṛṣṭa viparītam kalpitam bhavati evam ca kalpayatā buddhi nitya tvam eva pratipattavyam etāvat ca etat syāt nityā vā santāna vartinī vā santāna vartinī iti na yuktāḥ yadi guṇa bhedāt bhedaḥ yat abhinna guṇam tat ekam prāpnoti yathā diś kālau iti 
NV_4.1.21^24	 na anekāntāt guṇa bhedāt nānātvam brūmaḥ na punar guṇa abhedāt ekatvam iti tathā hi abhinna guṇānām ghaṭa ādīnām nānātvam dṛṣṭam diś kālayoḥ ca guṇa bhede api kārya bhedān nānātvam iti na ca buddhimat tayā vinā īśvarasya jagat utpādaḥ ghaṭate iti sā ca buddhiḥ sarva artha atīta anāgata vartamāna viṣayā pratyakṣā na ānumānikī naḥ āgamikī ca na hi tatra anumānam na āgamaḥ iti jñāna nitya tvāt ca na saṃskāraḥ nityam vijñānam īśvarasya iti na tatra saṃskāraḥ vidyate iti saṃskāra abhāvāt buddhi nitya tvāt ca na smṛtiḥ smṛteḥ abhāvāt ca na anumānam na duḥkham adharmasya abhāvāt atas eva na vairāgyam yatra duḥkham tatra vairāgyam iti duḥkha abhāvāt na virajyate iti atas eva na dveṣaḥ duḥkha abhāvāt iti icchā tu vidyate akliṣṭā avyāhatā sarva artheṣu yathā buddhiḥ iti atha kim ayam baddhaḥ muktaḥ iti na baddhaḥ duḥkha abhāvāt eva abaddha tvāt na muktaḥ iti bandhavān mucyate na ca bhagavati bandhanam asti iti atas na muktaḥ ātma antarāṇām asambandhāt adhiṣṭhātṛ tvam anupapannam iti ced 
NV_4.1.21^25	 atha manyase prāṇya antara samavāyinaḥ ye dharmāḥ ca adharmāḥ ca te na sākṣāt īśvareṇa sambadhyante na pāramparyeṇa na ca asaṃbaddham adhiṣṭhātum śakyate na ca anadhiṣṭhitayoḥ dharma adharmayoḥ pravṛttiḥ yuktāḥ iti tat ca na ajasambandha upapatteḥ ajaḥ sambandhaḥ ātma antarāṇām iti eke icchanti na ca etat iha pratiṣidhyate iti apratiṣedhāt upāttaḥ saḥ iti te tu ajam sambandham pramāṇataḥ pratipādayanti vyāpakaiḥ ākāśa ādibhiḥ sambaddhaḥ īśvaraḥ mūrtimat dravya sambandhi tvāt ghaṭa vat iti yathā ghaṭa ādi mūrtimatā ghaṭa ādinā sambandhi tvena vyāpakaiḥ ākāśa ādibhiḥ sambandhi bhavati tathā īśvaraḥ api mūrtimat sambandhī iti tasmāt ayam api vyāpakaiḥ ākāśa ādibhiḥ sambadhyate iti sa punar ātma īśvara sambandhaḥ kim vyāpakaḥ avyāpakaḥ vā iti artha abhāvāt avyākaraṇīyaḥ praśnaḥ ātma īśvara sambandhaḥ asti iti etat eva śakyate vaktum sa punar īśvara ātmānau vyāpnoti na vyāpnoti iti na vyākriyate ye api ajam saṃyogam naḥ icchanti teṣām api aṇu manaḥ saṃyoga upapatteḥ asti sambandhaḥ 
NV_4.1.21^26	 yāni pratyātma manāṃsi tāni sarvāṇi īśvara sambaddhāni iti atas sambandha sambandha upapatteḥ ātma antarāṇi adhitiṣṭhati iti yathā ātma hasta saṃyoga prayatnābhyām haste karma bhavati utpanna karmakaḥ hastaḥ sandaṃśa ādinā sambadhyate tad sambandha ādayaḥ piṇḍa ādi adhitiṣṭhati iti yadi tarhi sarga ādau īśvarasya kāraṇa tve ayam nyāyaḥ abhidhīyate idānīm īśvaraḥ na kāraṇam iti prāptam idānīm api saḥ eva nyāyaḥ mṛta śarīriṇām yau dharma adharmau tau buddhimat kāraṇa adhiṣṭhitau iti samānaḥ nyāyaḥ 
NV_4.1.21^27	 buddhimat kāraṇa adhiṣṭhitāni svāsu svāsu dhāraṇa ādi kriyāsu mahābhūtāni vāyu antāni pravartante acetana tvāt vā asya ādi vat iti evam kāryatvāt tṛṇa ādīni pakṣīkṛtya darśana sparśana viṣaya tvāt iti vaktavyam evam yatra yatra vipratipattiḥ kāryatvam ca yat tat anena eva nyāyena anena dṛṣṭāntena vāsya ādinā pakṣayitvā sādhayitavyam iti āgamāt ca āgamaḥ ca asmin pakṣe śrūyate īśvara kāraṇe yathā ajñaḥ jantuḥ anīśaḥ ayam ātmanaḥ sukha duḥkhayoḥ īśvara preritaḥ gacchet svargam vā svabhram eva vā yadā sa devaḥ jāgarti tadā idam ceṣṭate jagat yadā svapiti śānta ātmā tadā sarvam nimīlati 
NV_4.1.22–4.1.23	 aparaḥ idānīm āha animittataḥ bhāva utpattiḥ kaṇṭaka taikṣṇya ādi darśanāt yathā kaṇṭakasya taikṣṇya ādi nimittam ca upādāna vat ca tathā śarīra ādi sargaḥ api iti tat idam dṛṣṭānta sūtram kaḥ punar atra nyāyaḥ animitta racanā viśeṣāḥ śarīra ādayaḥ saṃsthāna viśeṣavat tvāt kaṇṭaka ādi vat iti na anupalabhyamāna nimittānām anumānataḥ nimitta upalabdheḥ yasya nimittam pratyakṣataḥ naḥ upalabhyate tasya anumānataḥ nimittam pratyetavyam kutas nimitta vat dravya sāmānyāt yāni khalu nimittavanti dravyāṇi saṃsthāna viśeṣavanti tāni ghaṭa ādīni saṃsthāna viśeṣa vat ca śarīram kaṇṭaka ādayaḥ ca tasmāt te api nimittavantaḥ iti uktam ca atra kim uktam pūrva kṛta phala anubandhāt tad utpattiḥ iti na ca ubhaya pakṣa sampratipannam saṃsthāna viśeṣa vat nirnimittam dṛṣṭam iti apare tu animitta nimitta tvāt na animittataḥ iti parihāram varṇayanti animittam eva nimittam yatas ca utpattiḥ tat nimittam iti animitta nimitta tvāt na animittataḥ utpattiḥ iti 
NV_4.1.24^1	 etat ca na nimitta animittayoḥ artha antara bhāvāt apratiṣedhaḥ anyat nimittam anyat ca nimitta pratyākhyānam na ca pratyākhyānam eva pratyākhyeyam bhavati nimittam iti artha abhyanujñā animittam iti tasya pratiṣedhaḥ abhyanujñā pratiṣedhayoḥ ca eka tvam ayuktam iti sa khalu ayam vādaḥ akarma nimittaḥ śarīra sargaḥ iti etasmāt na bhidyate iti abhede tu tad pratiṣedhena eva pratiṣiddhaḥ boddhavyaḥ kaṇṭaka ādīnām ca animittam janma iti bruvāṇaḥ praṣṭavyaḥ kim kaṇṭaka ādi mātrasya animittam janma uta sarvasya iti yadi kaṇṭaka ādi mātrasya animittam janma tad śeṣeṇa dṛṣṭāntena śakyam pratipādayitum nimitta vat iti atha sarvam animittam janma iti ayam pakṣaḥ tathā api vyāghātaḥ pratipādya pratipādaka nyāyasya abhyupagamāt sarvam ca animittam pratipādayasi ca iti vyāghātaḥ 
NV_4.1.24^2	 vākya upādānāt ca vyāghātaḥ animittataḥ bhāva utpattiḥ kaṇṭaka taikṣṇya ādi vat iti vākyam pratipādakam upādīyate na ca nimittam asti iti vyāghātaḥ animittataḥ bhāva utpattiḥ iti ca vākyam sa nimitta abhāva utpattiḥ iti ca vākyam yadi anayoḥ artha bhedam pratipadyase vākya bhedāt artha bheda pratipattiḥ iti vyāhatam bhavati animittāḥ bhāva utpattiḥ iti atha na vākya bhedena artha bhedam pratipadyase vākya viśeṣa upādānam vyāhatam yat kim cit vākyam upādeyam iti animittām bhāva utpattim pratipadyamānena sarva loka vyavahāraḥ ucchinnaḥ bhavati animittā bhāva utpattiḥ iti ca bhāva mātra pakṣīkaraṇe na dṛṣṭāntaḥ asti atha śarīra ādi eka deśam pakṣayasi tathā api anyatara dharma asiddhaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ saṃsthāna viśeṣavat tvasya vidyamāna tvāt animitta tvasya ca abhāvāt iti 
NV_4.1.25	 anye tu manyante sarvam anityam utpatti vināśa dharmaka tvāt kim anityam nāma yasya kadā cit bhāvaḥ tat anityam utpatti dharmakam anutpannam na asti vināśa dharmakam ca vinaṭṣam na asti iti kim punar sarvam bhautikam śarīra ādi abhautikam ca buddhi ādi tat ubhayam utpatti vināśa dharmakam iti vijñāyate iti tasmāt sarvam anityam iti sūtrasya dṛṣṭānta artha tvāt tasya sarva antarbhāvāt udāharaṇa abhāvaḥ sarvam anityam utpatti vināśa dharmaka tvāt iti yadi brūṣe dṛṣṭānta abhāvaḥ sarvasya pakṣīkṛta tvāt na sādhyam udāharaṇam yuktam iti utpatti vināśa dharmaka tvāt iti ca ayam hetuḥ avyāpakaḥ yadi sarvam pakṣayitvā utpatti vināśa dharmaka tvāt iti brūṣe paramāṇu ākāśa ādiṣu tad guṇeṣu ca keṣu cit sāmānya viśeṣa samavāyeṣu naḥ utpatti vināśa dharmaka tvam asti iti hetuḥ avyāpakaḥ 
NV_4.1.26–4.1.28^1	 sarvam anityam eva iti bruvāṇaḥ praṣṭavyaḥ kim sarvasya anitya tā nityāḥ āhosvit anityāḥ iti yadi anitya tā nityāḥ na tarhi sarvam anityam atha anityāḥ nitya tā anitya tāyāḥ abhāvāt sarvam anityam iti vyāhataḥ hetuḥ yathā agneḥ dāhyam vināśya anuvinaśyati evam anitya tā api sarvam vināśya anuvinaṃkṣyati iti ayam ca khalu vādaḥ sarvam anityam iti nityam pratyācaṣṭe nityasya pratyākhyānam aśakyam yathā upalabdhi vyavasthānāt yatra yatra ayam hetuḥ upalabhyate tatra tatra hetu sāmarthyāt anitya tvam pratipadyāmahe yatra punar ayam hetuḥ na asti teṣām anitya tvam katham pratipattavyam atha akāraṇakam anitya tvam teṣām pratipadyase vyāhataḥ tarhi hetuḥ utpatti vināśa dharmaka tvāt iti anityam iti ca bruvāṇena avaśyam nityam abhyupeyam nañaḥ prasajya pratiṣedha paryudāsa viṣaya tvāt ayam khalu nan pravartamānaḥ prasajya pratiṣedhe vā pravartate paryudāse vā tathā ca uttara pada siddhiḥ 
NV_4.1.28^2	 yadi nityam na bhavati iti anityam tarhi yat anyatra bhavati tat anyatra pratiṣidhyate iti siddham uttara padam atha nityāt anyat anityam iti tathā api uttara padena bhavitavyam na asati uttara padārthe tasmāt anyat anitya tvam sidhyati iti anitya tā bhāvāt ca sarvam anityam iti na doṣaḥ anitya tāyāḥ dharma tvena abhyupagamāt anitya tvam nāma dharmaḥ saḥ asati dharmiṇi na bhavati iti evam ca sati sarvasya anitya tvam na doṣaḥ iti atha punar utpatti vināśa dharmakeṇa anityena siddhena śeṣam sandihyamāna anitya tvam tad viparīta nitya tvam ca sattvāt anityam iti sādhayet tasya api uttara pada siddhyā nitya tva siddhiḥ iti pratijñā doṣāt vākyam nivartate iti 
NV_4.1.29–4.1.31^1	 ayam aparaḥ ekāntaḥ sarvam nityam pañcabhūta nitya tvāt iti bhūtamātram idam sarvam tāni ca nityāni bhūta uccheda anupapatteḥ sarvam nityam iti utpatti kāraṇam ca bhāvānām upalabhyate vināśa kāraṇam ca tat ubhayam nitya tve na syāt na hi nityam nāma jāyate vinaśyati vā yat idam utpadyate vinaśyati iti ca manyase na tat bhūta lakṣaṇa hīnam gṛhyate bhūta lakṣaṇa avarodhāt sarvam nityam iti sarvam anityam iti bruvāṇaḥ na kaḥ cit jāyate na vinaśyati iti pratipadyate tad pratipattau ca hita ahita prāpti parihāra arthaḥ asya parispandaḥ vyarthaḥ āpadyeta sarvasya ca pakṣīkaraṇāt dṛṣṭānta abhāvaḥ vākya upādānam ca vyāhatam yat idam vākyam para pratipādanāya upādīyate sarvam nityam pañcabhūta nitya tvāt iti anena vākyena ayam kim karoti kim asiddham sādhayati uta siddham nivartayati yadi tāvat asiddham sādhayati kā iyam siddhiḥ yā vākyena pratipādyate yadi vijñānam nanu vyāhatam bhavati sarvam 
NV_4.1.31^2	 nityam vijñānam ca jāyate iti atha pratipattiḥ na kriyate kā tarhi siddhiḥ yā pravartamānam sādhanam karoti avaśyam kārakeṇa apūrvam kim cit niṣpādyam tat niṣpatteḥ vyāghātaḥ kāraka tvam vā nivartate na hi nityasya kim cit kartavyam asti atha siddham nivartayati iti pakṣaḥ āśrīyate etasmin api pakṣe nityam nivartate ca iti vyāhātaḥ atha tirobhavati tirobhāve api ayam aśyam apūrva utpattiḥ pūrva vastu vināśaḥ vai abhyupeyaḥ iti sarvathā na vyāghātāt mucyase yat ca vastu prāc anupalabdha rūpam paścāt upalabhyate tatra api avaśyam apūrva utpattiḥ vā pūrva vastu vināśaḥ vai abhyupeyaḥ iti tad abhyupagame ca vyāghātaḥ 
NV_4.1.32^1	 yat punar etat bhūta lakṣaṇa avarodhāt sarvam nityam iti na anyathā tad upapatteḥ bhūta lakṣaṇa yogaḥ anyathā sambhavati iti naḥ utpatti tad kāraṇa upalabdheḥ utpatti tad kāraṇa upalabdheḥ kāraṇa samāna guṇasya utpattiḥ ca dṛṣyate kāraṇam ca asyāḥ dṛśyate iti na ca etat ubhayam nitya viṣayam na hi nityasya utpattiḥ na api nityasya kāraṇam asti asti ca idam ubhayam tasmāt kāraṇa samāna guṇam kāryam utpadyate iti kāraṇa samāna guṇa utpāde ca kārya bhūta lakṣaṇa guṇa avarodhaḥ siddhi ati iti vibhakta nyāyam ca etat vyaktāt vyaktānām uptattiḥ pratyakṣa prāmāṇyāt iti etasmin sūtre avyāpakaḥ ca ayam hetuḥ pañcabhūta nitya tvāt iti 
NV_4.1.32^2	 katham iti karma ādīnām avyāpteḥ karma buddhi śabda ādayaḥ pañcabhūta nitya tvāt iti anena na vyāptāḥ iti jñātuḥ prayatna darśanāt ca vyāghātaḥ utpatti vināśa kāraṇa prayuktasya ca jñātuḥ prayatnaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ sa ca sarva nitya tve na yuktaḥ prasiddhaḥ ca avayavī tad dharmā utpatti vināśa dharmā ca avayavī pratipāditaḥ atas ayuktam etat katham avyāpakaḥ anaikāntaḥ pakṣasya anta dvaye avasthānāt pakṣaḥ hi sarvam hi nityam iti tat ca sarvam bhūta lakṣaṇa yuktam itarathā ca tad pakṣasya anta dvaye avasthānāt sarvam bhūta lakṣaṇa yuktam iti anekāntaḥ svapna viṣaya abhimāna vat mithyā upalabdhiḥ iti ced 
NV_4.1.32^3	 atha manuṣe yat idam utpadyate vinaśyati ca iti tat na tattvataḥ asti asati tu etasamin abhimānaḥ bhavati utpannam vinaṣṭam iti yathā na svapne viṣayāḥ santi atha ca viṣaya abhimānaḥ bhavati iti na pramāṇa abhāvāt yat idam gavā ādi ghaṭa ādikam utpatti vināśa yuktam upalabhyate etat na asti iti na asattva pratipādakam pramāṇam abhidhīyate na ca aprāmāṇakam śakyam pratipattum yathā ca citta vyatirekiṇaḥ viṣayāḥ tathā upariṣṭāt pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ yadi ca svapna viṣaya abhimāna vat utpatti vināśa abhimānaḥ nanu bhūta upalabdhiḥ api svapna viṣaya abhimāna vat prasajyate pṛthivī ādi abhāve sarva vyavahāra vilopaḥ iti ced 
NV_4.1.32^4	 atha manyase yadi pṛthivī ādīni bhūtāni na santi nanu pṛthivī ādi āśrayaḥ vyavahāraḥ ucchidyate iti tat itaratra api samānam yadi vyavahāra uccheda bhayāt bhūtāni pratipadyase vyavahāra uccheda bhayāt eva utpatti vināśau api pratipadyasva na hi utpatti vināśau antareṇa kaḥ cana vyavahāraḥ sidhyati iti nityānām dravyāṇām atīndriya tvāt aviṣaya tvāt ca utpatti vināśayoḥ yat nityam tat atīndriyam aviṣayaḥ ca utpatti vināśayoḥ tena svapna viṣaya abhimāna vat tad abhimānaḥ iti ayuktam utpatti vināśa abhimānaḥ iti ca bruvatā utpatti vināśayoḥ viṣayaḥ vaktavyaḥ na ca sarva nitya vādinām utpatti vināśayoḥ viṣayaḥ asti viṣayam ca pratyācakṣāṇena tad anukārī viparyaya pratyayaḥ heyaḥ iti 
NV_4.1.33	 apare tu sarvam nityam iti etat anyathā varṇayanti vyavasthitatasya upādānasya dharma mātram nivartate dharma mātram āvirbhavati yat ca nivartate tad nivṛttam api asti iti yat ca āvirbhavati tat prāk api āvirbhāvāt asti na vyavasthā anupapatteḥ iti śeṣam bhāṣye yat ca nivartate tat nivṛttam api asti iti bruvāṇaḥ praṣṭavyaḥ bhavān jāyate kim uktam bhavati nivṛttam iti yadi brūṣe pūrvam upalabdham paścāt naḥ upalabhyate iti atha sataḥ anupalabdhiḥ kiṃkṛtā yadi āvaraṇa ādi kṛtā tadā āvaraṇa ādi upalabhyeta uktam ca atra yat pūrvam anupalabdham vastu paścāt upalabhyate tasya apūrva viśeṣa utpādaḥ pūrva viśeṣa pracyavaḥ vai abhyupeyaḥ iti tad abhyupagame ca vyāghātaḥ yat api uktam yat ca āvirbhavati tat prāk api āvirbhāvāt vidyate tat na vyāghātāt āvirbhavati prāk vidyate ca iti vyāhatam atha āvirbhāvaḥ abhivyaktiḥ tathā api pūrva doṣa anivṛttiḥ abhivyaktiḥ asatī bhavati iti 
NV_4.1.34	 ayam aparaḥ ekāntaḥ sarvam pṛthak bhāva lakṣana pṛthaktvāt bhāvasya lakṣaṇam bhāva lakṣaṇam śabdaḥ lakṣyate anena bhāvaḥ iti sarvaḥ bhāva samākhyā śabdaḥ aneka viṣayaḥ yathā kumbhaḥ iti bhāva samākhyā śabdaḥ anekasmin avayava samūhe rūpa ādi samūhe sa vartate iti yathā kumbha śabdaḥ evam anye api śabdāḥ iti asya prayogaḥ kumbha śabdaḥ aneka viṣayaḥ eka pada tvāt senā śabda vat pada śravaṇāt aneka artha adhigateḥ ca yasmāt pada śravaṇāt anekaḥ arthaḥ avagamyate yathā senā iti 
NV_4.1.35^1	 aneka lakṣaṇaiḥ iti madhya pada lopī samāsaḥ anekavidha lakṣaṇaiḥ iti gandha ādibhiḥ ca guṇaiḥ budhna ādibhiḥ ca avayavaiḥ sambaddhaḥ ekaḥ bhāvaḥ utapadyate atas śabdāt eka artha avagatau śeṣaḥ anuktaḥ api avagamyate iti guṇa vyatirekaḥ guṇī iti avayava vyatiriktaḥ ca avayavī iti vibhakta nyāyam etat yat punar etat eka pada tvāt aneka viṣayaḥ kumbha ādi śabdaḥ iti tat na dṛṣṭānta abhāvāt na hi kaḥ cit śabdaḥ aneka viṣayaḥ asti senā ādi śabdānām aneka viṣaya tvena asiddhi tvāt yathā eka viṣayāḥ senā ādi śabdāḥ tathā uktam iti sarvasya pakṣīkaraṇāt dṛṣṭānta abhāvaḥ 
NV_4.1.35^2	 ādhāra ādheya bhāvena anuṣaktānām rūpa ādīnām avayavinaḥ ca grahaṇāt anyathā siddhiḥ nañaḥ prasajya pratiṣedha paryudāsa viṣaya tvena avasthānāt ca viruddhaḥ anekam iti ayam nañaḥ prayogaḥ sa ca ayam prasajya pratiṣedhena paryudāsa viṣaya tvena vā kalpyate tat yadi tāvat prasajya pratiṣedhaḥ ekaḥ na bhavati iti yat ekatra pratiṣidhyate tat anyatra bhavati iti ekam abhyupagatam bhavati iti evam ca vyāghātaḥ atha paryudāsa pakṣaḥ ekasmāt anyat anekam iti evam api ekam abhyupagatam bhavati na hi asati ekasmin tasmāt anyat anekam sidhyati iti 
NV_4.1.36^1	 itas ca lakṣaṇa vyavasthānāt eva apratiṣedhaḥ na hi kaḥ cit ekaḥ bhāvaḥ iti ayuktaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ kasmāt tad lakṣaṇa vyavasthānāt na hi kumbhaḥ iti ukte anekaḥ arthaḥ avagamyate iti katham na avagamyate eka vacana anta tvāt eka vacana antaḥ eṣaḥ śabdaḥ kumbhaḥ iti na ca bahuṣu eka vacanam yuktam praiṣa sampratipattyoḥ eka viṣaya tvāt kumbham ānaya iti praiṣaḥ eka viṣayaḥ bhavati itaraḥ api kumbha śabdāt pratipadyaḥ ekam eva kumbham ānayati te ete praiṣa sampratipattī eka viṣaye jñāpayataḥ kumbha śabdena ekaḥ arthaḥ abhidhīyate iti 
NV_4.1.36^2	 yān tu atra rūpa ādīn avayavān ca pratipadyase sa na śabda arthaḥ kim tu anuṣaṅgaḥ tat na antarīyaka tvāt iti samūhe bhedasya ca anavasthānāt yatra avasthānam tat ekam go ghaṭa ādi dravyāṇi samuditāni pratipadyamānena samūhaḥ abhyupeyaḥ sa ca ayam samūhaḥ iyanti dravyāṇi etāni gavā ādi bhāvena avasthitāni iti na vyavatiṣṭhate tasya bhedaḥ alpataratama tvena yat etat parama alpam tat abhedyam tatas nivartate iti yatas ca ayam bhedaḥ nivartate tat ekam ekam ca pratyācakṣāṇenekam api pratyākhyeyam eka samuccayāt anekasya 
NV_4.1.36^3	 atha manyase yam tam abhedyam paramāṇum pratipadyase saḥ api rūpa ādīnām samudāyaḥ iti catvāri vā dravyāṇi pṛthivī ādīni sa mudhitāni paramāṇuḥ iti etasmin vai darśane ye rūpa ādayaḥ samuditāḥ te paramāṇuḥ iti yat paramāṇau rūpam sa kasya samudāyaḥ iti vaktavyam evam śeṣeṣu guṇeṣu catvāri dravyāṇi samuditāni paramāṇuh iti bruvāṇena catuṣkasya evam samuccaya nimitta tvāt yat ekam pṛthivī ādi sa kasya samudāyaḥ iti vaktavyam atha anantam samudāyam pratipadyase aṣṭau dravyāṇi samuditāni paramāṇuḥ iti śāstram vyāhatam bhavati kāme aṣṭa dravyakaḥ aṇuḥ aśabdaḥ iti eka anupapattau ca aneka upapattiḥ iti etat vyāhatam yaḥ ca ayam hetuḥ samūhe bhāva śabda prayogāt iti ubhayatas vyāghātāt na kim cit katham ubhayatas na kaḥ cit ekaḥ bhāvaḥ samūhe bhāva śabda prayogāt iti pratijñā hetvoḥ vyāghātaḥ yasmāt eka artha anupapattau na samūhaḥ upapadyate iti samūham ca āśritya ekam pratyācakṣāṇena samūhaḥ eva pratyākhyātaḥ bhavati iti saḥ ayam ubhayatas vyāghātāt yat kimcana vādaḥ iti śeṣam bhāṣye 
NV_4.1.37	 atha ayam aparaḥ ekāntaḥ sarvam abhāvaḥ bhāveṣu itaretarābhāva siddheḥ yāvat bhāva jātam tat sarvam abhāvaḥ kasmāt bhāveṣu itaretarābhāva siddheḥ asat pratyaya pratiṣedhābhyām bhāva śabda sāmānādhikaraṇyāt sarva asattvam anutpanna pradhvasta ghaṭa vat sarvaḥ bhāva śabdaḥ asat pratyaya samāna adhikaraṇaḥ pratiṣedha samāna adhikaraṇaḥ ca anutpanna pradhvasta ghaṭa vat yathā na asti ghaṭaḥ iti katham na asti kadā ca na asti iti sthālī ādi ātmanā ca anutpadyamānaḥ dhvastaḥ ca iti saḥ ayam ghaṭa śabdaḥ asat pratyaya samāna adhikaraṇaḥ ghaṭasya atyanta sattvam pratipādayati tathā ca sarve bhāvāḥ asat pratyaya samāna adhikaraṇāḥ tasmāt sarvam abhāvaḥ iti 
NV_4.1.38^1	 pratijñāpadayoḥ pratijñā hetvoḥ ca vyāghātaḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyam abhinna vibhakti kattvam eka vibhakti uccāraṇam iti bhāva abhyupagamāt tad śabda abhyupagamāt ca viruddhaḥ yat sarvam iti manyase tat abhāvaḥ iti na asati tad pratyayena bhavitum śakyam na ca bhāva pratyayena abhāvaḥ iti ca bhāvaḥ pratiṣidhyate na ca asati uttara padārthe nañaḥ prayogaḥ iti prasajya pratiṣedha paryudāsābhyām pūrvavat prasaṅgaḥ yathā aneka pade anitya pade ca evam sarva pade abhāva pade ca vyāghātaḥ ūhyaḥ śeṣam bhāṣye sarva asattve vibhakti svabhāva avadhāraṇam kartavyam yadi ca sarvam abhāvaḥ vibhaktiḥ kiṃsvabhāvikāḥ iti vaktavyam etat 
NV_4.1.38^2	 asatyām ca vibhaktau abhinna vibhaktika tvam sāmānādhikaraṇyam iti vyāhatam asat pratyaya pratiṣedhau ca sāmānādhikaraṇyāt iti bruvāṇaḥ eva sarvam abhāvaḥ iti vyāvartayasi na hi asat adhikaraṇam bhavati adhikaraṇam hi nāma yat yatra vartate tat ca abhāve na asti iti sūtreṇa ca abhisambandhaḥ na svabhāva siddheḥ bhāvānām iti svena bhāvena bhāvāḥ bhavanti iti sūtra arthaḥ kim punar anena sūtreṇa kriyate pūrva sūtrasya virodhaḥ codyate katham iti bhāveṣu itaretarābhāva siddheḥ iti abhāvaḥ bhāvatā abhidhīyate tathā ca abhidadhānaḥ svabhāvataḥ bhāvān abhyupaiṣi viśeṣaṇa vaiyarthyam vā bhāveṣu itaretarābhāva siddheḥ iti sarva asattve hi evam eva vaktavyam na santi bhāvāḥ
