NV_5.1.36	 pratiṣedhye nityam anitya tvam iti bruvatā abhyanujñātam anitya tvam bhavati abhyanujñānāt ca asamarthaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ iti atha na abhyanujñāyate nityam anitya bhāvāt nityaḥ śabdaḥ iti hetuḥ naḥ upapadyate hetu anupapatteḥ anarthakaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ iti paripraśna anupapattiḥ ca pṛthak dharma tvena anitya tvasya anabhyupagamāt api ca anātyantika sattā yogaḥ anitya tvam iti ukte na yuktaḥ praśnaḥ kim ayam atyantam bhavati uta na atyantam iti ātyantikānātyantikā abhāva yogaḥ ca ekasya na yuktaḥ anitya tā nityāḥ iti bruvatā ekasya ātyantika sattā yogaḥ anātyantika sattā yogaḥ ca abhyanujñāyate sa ca ayam virodhāt na yuktaḥ iti pratiṣedhya doṣa udbhāvanāt yuktaḥ iti ced atha manyase na mayā ekasya nitya tvam anitya tvam vā abhyupagamyate api tu anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti bruvāṇasya bhavataḥ saḥ eva doṣaḥ iti na vikalpa anupapatteḥ na ayam pakṣa doṣaḥ na sādhana doṣaḥ pakṣa doṣaḥ tāvat ayam na bhavati pakṣasya tādavasthyāt na sādhanasya pratijña ādi doṣāṇām ca anuddhāvanāt virodhasya ca ukta uttara tvāt iti 
NV_5.1.37	 anityaḥ śabdaḥ prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt iti ukte jātiḥ kārya samā prayujyate prayatna kāryam anekadhā dṛṣṭam iti kim cit prayatna anantaram vyajyate kim cit prayatna anantaram utpadyate prayatna anantaram upalabdheḥ hetu tva adhyāropeṇa anaikāntika tva deśanāt kārya samaḥ kāryaḥ śabdaḥ prayatna anantaram upalabdheḥ iti hetu artham anaikāntikam codayati prayatna anantaram upalabhamānam kāryam akāryam ca dṛṣṭam iti atha prayatna anantaram janma hetu arthaḥ tathā api asiddha deśanā iti 
NV_5.1.38	 yat khalu prayatnena vyajyate tatra anupalabdhi kāraṇam upapadyate na tu śabdasya anupalabdhi kāraṇam kim cit asti tasmāt na vyajyate iti saṃśaya samāḥ atas na bhidyate iti ced ubhaya sādharmyāt saṃśaya samaḥ ayam tu na tathā tasmāt bhidyate iti sādharmya samātaḥ na bhidyate iti ced na hetu adhyāropaṇāt sādharmya samā na hetu adhyāropeṇa pravartate iyam tu anyathā abhihite hetau anyathā ākāram pravartate 
NV_5.1.39	 evam tāvat jātayaḥ vyavasthitāḥ atha idānīm ṣaṣ pakṣīm upanyasiṣyan idam āha pratiṣedhe api samānaḥ doṣaḥ prathama pakṣa vādī jāti vādinam prati uttaram bravīti iti yadi anaikāntika tvāt ahetuḥ pratiṣedhaḥ api anaikāntikaḥ syāt kasya cit apratiṣedhāt kasya cit pratiṣedhāt iti viśeṣa hetu abhāvaḥ vā aviśeṣaḥ śeṣam bhāṣye 
NV_5.1.40–5.1.42	 sarvāsu jātiṣu eṣā pratyuktiḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ tṛtīyaḥ pakṣaḥ vipratiṣedhaḥ etasmin vipratiṣedhe samānam anaikāntika tvam doṣaḥ iti caturthaḥ pakṣaḥ pratiṣedham dvitīya pakṣam sa doṣam abhyupetya tṛtīya pakṣe api pratiṣedhe tulya doṣa tām āsañjayan vipratiṣedhe api samānaḥ doṣaḥ iti bruvan matam anujānāti sā iyam mata anujñā bhavati iti pañcamaḥ pakṣaḥ 
NV_5.1.43	 sva pakṣa samutthānam doṣam abhyupetya para pakṣe api prayuñjan sva pakṣa doṣam anujānāti iti tulyā mata anujñā śeṣam bhāṣye atra khalu sthāpanā hetu vādinaḥ prathama tṛtīya pañcama pakṣāḥ pratiṣedha hetu vādinaḥ dvitīya caturtha ṣaṣṭha pakṣāḥ teṣām sādhu asādhutāyām mīmāṃsyamānāyām caturtha ṣaṣṭhayoḥ aviśeṣāt na punar ukta doṣa prasaṅgaḥ samānaḥ tṛtīya pañcamayoḥ punarukta doṣaḥ tatra pañcama ṣaṣṭhayoḥ punarukta doṣaḥ tṛtīya caturthayoḥ mata anujñā doṣaḥ prathama dvitīyayoḥ viśeṣa hetu abhāvaḥ iti ṣaṣ pakṣyām ubhayoḥ asiddhiḥ ayukta tva vādi tvāt yadā tu anupalabdhi kāraṇa abhāve sati prayatna anantaram upalabdheḥ iti viśeṣa hetuḥ ucyate tadā na ṣaṣ pakṣī pravartate etāḥ tu jātayaḥ na tattva vivekam upakurvanti iti bheda mātram āsām uktam 
NV_5.2.1^1	 vipratipatti apratipattyoḥ vikalpāt nigraha sthāna bahu tvam iti saṅkṣepeṇa uktam tat idānīm vibhajanīyam nigraha sthānāni ca parājaya vastūni aparādha adhikaraṇāni sāmānyatas dve nigraha sthāne kartṛ karma karaṇānām kasya nigrahaḥ tatra eke varṇayanti pakṣasya iti evam ca āhuḥ dūṣaṇāni nyūna tā avayava uttara doṣa ākṣepa bhāva udbhāvanāni ebhiḥ hi asau para pakṣaḥ dūṣyate iti etat tu na samyak karmaṇaḥ tādavasthyāt na hi dūṣaṇa abhidhānena karmaṇaḥ anyathātvam bhavati yathābhūtaḥ eva arthaḥ dūṣyamāṇaḥ tathābhūtaḥ eva adūṣyamāṇaḥ api na karaṇasya viṣaya antare asāmarthyāt sādhanam api pratijña ādikam na dūṣyate viṣaya antare asāmarthyāt na hikim cit sādhanam yat viṣaya antare samartham syāt sarvam sādhanam sva viṣaye samartham iti 
NV_5.2.1^2	 tasmāt asamarthayoḥ karma karaṇayoḥ upādānāt kartuḥ nigrahaḥ iti yat karma kriyā artham upādīyamānam abhīṣṭa kriyām na nirvartayati tat idam asamartham yathā sikatā ghaṭa ādi karaṇe iti yat ca karaṇam kriyā artham upādīyamānam kriyām na nirvartayati tat asamartham yathā turya ādi ghaṭe sva viṣaye tu ubhayam samartham tat anya viṣayasya ca karmaṇaḥ anya viṣayasya ca karaṇasya anyathā upādānāt kartuḥ ajñānam ajñānam punar apratipatti vipratipattiḥ vā iti kartā nigṛhyate na karma karaṇe pāratantryāt tasmāt svatantryasya kartuḥ nigrahaḥ iti vipratipatti apratipattyoḥ ca puruṣa dharma tvāt puruṣasya iti vipratipatti apratipattī ca puruṣasya vacana dvāreṇa gamyete 
NV_5.2.1^3	 tasmāt pratijña ādi doṣāḥ iti bhaktiḥ kāni cit nigraha sthānāni ajñāna ādīni puruṣa dharmāḥ eva dvaividhya anupapattiḥ aneka abhidhānāt iti ced anekam nigraha sthānam pratijñāhānyādi sūtre paṭhyate tasmāt dve nigraha sthāne iti ayuktam na sāmānya bheda vistarasya vivakṣātaḥ pravṛtteḥ sāmānyam adhikṛtya dve nigraha sthāne bheda vistara vivakṣāyām tu dvāviṃśatidhā bhedaḥ udāharaṇa mātra tvāt ca bhedasya ānantyam iti prāyeṇa pratijña ādi avayava āśrayāṇi iti bhāṣyam vaktṛ viṣayaka tvāt pratijña ādi ava yava āśrita tvam anupapannam iti ced atha manyasevi pratipattiḥ apratipattiḥ ca nigraha sthānam iti abhidhāne pratijña ādi avayava āśri tve kaḥ prasaṅgaḥ iti na kriyā vacana doṣa dvāreṇa kartṛ vaktṝṇām ajña tva upapatteḥ 
NV_5.2.1^4	 kriyā dvāreṇa kartā dūṣyate vacana dvāreṇa vaktā iti na pratijña ādi āśraya tvam anupapannam na ca ādhāra ādheya bhāvaḥ āśraya āśrayi bhāvaḥ vivakṣitaḥ kim tu pratijña ādi mukhena udbhāvanam iti tattva vādinam atattva vādinam ca abhisaṃplavante iti bhāṣyam tattva vādinaḥ nigraha sthāna anupapattiḥ pratipādaka tvāt tattvam bravīti iti pratipādayati iti pratipādayan ca nigṛhyate iti na yuktam na para apad iṣṭa dūṣaṇa doṣān avabodha dvāreṇa tad upapatteḥ tattva vādī prathama pakṣe dvitīya pakṣa vādinā ca yaḥ dūṣaṇa ābhāsaḥ uktaḥ tasya tattva anavabodhāt nigṛhyate tattvam abhidadhānaḥ api iti tatra vastu nirṇītam nirṇīte api ca vastuni dūṣaṇa ābhāsasya apratipattyā nigṛhyate iti tatra udāharaṇa bheda pradarśana artham pratijñāhāni ādi sūtram 
NV_5.2.2^1	 lakṣaṇam ca pratidṛṣṭānta dharma abhyanujñā sva dṛṣṭānte pratijñā hāniḥ pratidṛṣṭāntasya yaḥ dharmaḥ tam yadā sva pakṣe dṛṣṭānte abhyanujānāti tadā nigṛhītaḥ veditavyaḥ yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ aindriyaka tvāt ghaṭa vat iti kṛte sāmānyam aindriyakam dṛṣṭam nityam kasmāt na tathā śabdaḥ iti dvitīyaḥ yadi sāmānyam aindriyakam nityam iti ghaṭaḥ api evam astu iti tritīyaḥ anena kila hetu doṣeṇa pratidṛṣṭānta dharma sva dṛṣṭānte abhyanujāntaḥ bhavati abhyanujñānāt ca dṛṣṭāntam jahati dṛṣṭāntam ca jahat nigamana antam eva pakṣam jahāti iti pratijñāhāniḥ iti ucyate etat tu na buddhyāmahe katham atra pratijñā hīyate iti 
NV_5.2.2^2	 hetoḥ anaikāntika tvam sāmānya dṛṣṭāntena pareṇa codyate etasya anaikāntika doṣa uddhāram anuktvā sva dṛṣṭānte nityatām pratipadyate nitya tā pratipatteḥ ca asiddha tā dṛṣṭānta doṣaḥ bhavati saḥ ayam dṛṣṭānta doṣeṇa hetu doṣeṇa vā nigrahaḥ na pratijñā hāniḥ dṛṣṭāntam ca jahat pratijñām api jahāti iti upacāreṇa nigraha sthānam na ca pradhāna asambhave upacāraḥ labhyate iti pratijñā hāneḥ mukhyaḥ viṣayaḥ vaktavyaḥ katham tarhi idam sūtram pratidṛṣṭānta dharma abhyanujñā sva dṛṣṭānte pratijñāhāniḥ iti dṛṣṭaḥ ca asau ante vyavasthitaḥ iti dṛṣṭāntaḥ svar ca asau dṛṣṭāntaḥ ca iti sva dṛṣṭāntaḥ sva dṛṣṭānta śabdena pakṣaḥ eva abhidhīyate 
NV_5.2.2^3	 pratidṛṣṭānta śabdena ca pratipakṣaḥ pratipakṣaḥ ca asau dṛṣṭāntaḥ ca iti etat uktam bhavati pratipakṣasya yaḥ dharmaḥ tam sva pakṣaḥ abhyanujānāti iti yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ aindriyaka tvāt iti dvitīya pakṣa vādini sāmānyena pratyavasthite idam āha yadi sāmānyam aindriyakam nityam dṛṣṭam iti śabdaḥ api evam bhavatu iti eṣā pratijñā hāniḥ prāk anena pratijñātam anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti sāmānyena anaikāntika tvena pratyavasthitaḥ idam āha nityaḥ iti prāk pramāṇa avadhārita artha parityāgāt vipratipattitaḥ nigraha sthānam iti prasaṅga vidhānāt iti ced atha manyase na asau paścāt api śabdasya nityatām pratipadyate kim tu prasaṅgam karoti 
NV_5.2.2^4	 yadi sāmānyam aindriyakam nityam dṛṣṭam śabdaḥ api evam bhavatu iti prasaṅgam vidhatte tat ca na atas eva tad prāpteḥ yatas eva asau hetu doṣa uddhāre kartavye prasañjayati atas eva nigṛhyate iti hetu doṣeṇa caritārtha tvāt na pratijñāhāniḥ nigraha sthānam iti anye anye tu varṇayanti naḥ eva idam nigraha sthānam yuktam hetu doṣeṇa caritārtha tvāt yasmāt aindriyaka tvāt iti asya hetoḥ anaikāntika tvam doṣaḥ tena ayam nigṛhītaḥ iti na anā ekāntika doṣa parīhāra dvāreṇa vipratipattitaḥ tad upapatteḥ tasya eva anaikāntikasya parihāram kurvāṇaḥ ayam nigṛhyate iti atas anaikāntika tvam na nigraha sthānam 
NV_5.2.3	 udāharaṇam pūrvavat sarva gatā sarva gata vikalpena pratijñāntaram karoti asarva gataḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti tatra anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti pūrvā pratijñā sāmānyena aindriyakeṇa pratihatā asarva gataḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti pratijñāntaram tat katham nigraha sthānam sādhana sāmarthya aparijñānāt aparijñāya sādhana sāmarthyam anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti pratijñā na ca pratijñā pratijñāntaram sādhayati sādhana sāmarthya aparijñānāt tat etat pratijñāntaram tat idam apratipattitaḥ vipratipattitaḥ vā nigraha sthānam iti 
NV_5.2.4^1	 yatra pratijñā hetunā virudhyate hetuḥ ca pratijñayā sa pratijñāvirodhaḥ nāma nigraha sthānam yathā guṇa vyatiriktam dravyam bhedena agrahaṇāt iti etena eva pratijñā virodhaḥ api uktaḥ yatra pratijñā sva vacanena virudhyate yathā śramaṇā garbhiṇī hetu virodhaḥ api yatra pratijñā hetunā virudhyate yathā sarvam pṛthak samūhe bhāva śabda prayogāt iti etena pratijñayā dṛṣṭānta virodhaḥ api vaktavyaḥ hetoḥ ca dṛṣṭānta ādibhiḥ virodhaḥ pramāṇa avirodhaḥ ca pratijñā hetvoḥ vaktavyaḥ para pakṣa siddhena go tva ādinā anaikāntika deśanāt viruddhaḥ 
NV_5.2.4^2	 yaḥ para pakṣa siddhena go tva ādinā vyabhicārayati tat viruddham uttaram veditavyam sva pakṣa anapekṣam ca yathā yam sva pakṣa anapekṣam hetum prayuṅkte anityaḥ śabdaḥ aindriyaka tvāt iti sa sva siddhasya go tva ādeḥ nitya tva virodhāt viruddhaḥ ubhaya pakṣa sampratipannaḥ tu anaikāntikaḥ yat ubhaya pakṣa sampratipannam vastu tathātvena tena anaikāntika deśenā iti dṛṣṭānta ābhāsāḥ tu kasmāt nigraha sthāneṣu naḥ uktāḥ hetvābhāsa pūrvaka tvāt dṛṣṭānta ābhāsānām tat abhidhānena eva uktāḥ veditavyāḥ iti 
NV_5.2.5–5.2.6	 yaḥ pratijñātam artham pratiṣedhe kṛte parityajati sa pratijñāsaṃnyāsaḥ veditavyaḥ udāharaṇam pūrvavat sāmānyena anaikāntika tve hetau kṛte brūyāt kaḥ ca evam āha anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti etat sādhanasya sāmarthya aparijñānāt vipratipattitaḥ nigraha sthānam iti udāharaṇam bhāṣye sādhana antara upādāne pūrvasya asāmarthya khyāpanāt nigraha sthānam sāmarthye vā pūrvasya hetu antaram vyartham iti 
NV_5.2.7–5.2.9	 udāharaṇam bhāṣye abhyupagata artha asaṅgata tvāt nigraha sthānam yat abhyupagatam tad sambaddham anyat asambaddham ucyate iti udāharaṇam bhāṣye sādhana anupādānāt ajñānam evam bruvan na sādhanam sādhyam jānīte iti na sādhyam na sādhanam ca upādatte iti nigṛhyate udāharaṇam bhāṣye asāmarthya khyāpanāt nigraha sthānam asāmarthyam ca ajñānam iti 
NV_5.2.10	 yathā daśa dāḍima ādi vākyam nirarthaka apārthakayoḥ abhedaḥ iti ced atha manyase nirarthakāt apārthakam na bhidyate tatra api arthaḥ na gamyate iha api iti bhidyate iti brūmaḥ katham tatra hi varṇa mātram iha tu padāni asambaddhāni tat katham nigraha sthānam vākyāt ṛte na viśeṣa avagatiḥ iti sādhana sāmarthya aparijñānāt nigraha sthānam 
NV_5.2.11^1	 avayavānām viparyayeṇa abhidhānam nigraha sthānam na evam api siddheḥ iti eke eke tu bruvate naḥ etat nigraha sthānam evam api siddheḥ iti samaya anabhyupagamāt ca na ca vayam evam samayam pratīcchāmaḥ iti prayogāt ca prayuktaḥ ca avayava vyatyayaḥ sarva śāstreṣu iti kasya ayam samayaḥ iti yat tāvat na evam api siddheḥ iti prayoga apeta śabda vat etat syāt yathā gauḥ iti asya padasya arthe gāvi iti prayujyamānam padam kakudādimantam artham pratipādayati iti na ca śabdānvākhyānam vyartham anena śabdena go śabdam eva asau pratipadyate go śabdāt kakudādimantam artham 
NV_5.2.11^2	 tathā pratijña ādi ava yava viparyāsena ānupūrvī pratipadyate ānupūrvyā ca artham iti etat katham iti pūrvam tāvat karma upādīyate tatas karaṇam mṛd piṇḍa ādi udāharaṇam anekadhā loke iti yat punar etat samaya anabhyupagamāt iti na ayam samayaḥ api tu arthasya ānupūrvī saḥ ayam arthasya ānupūrvīm anvācakṣāṇaḥ anābhyākhyeyaḥ iti yat punar etat prayogāt iti na nigraha sthāna viṣaya aparijñānāt śāstre vākyāni artha saṃgraha artham upādīyante saṃgṛhītam tu artham vākyena pratipādayitā prayoga kāle pratijña ādikayā ānupūrvyā pratipādayati iti 
NV_5.2.12	 yasmin vākye pratijña ādīnām anyatamaḥ avayavaḥ na bhavati tat vākyam nyūnam veditavyam tat katham nigraha sthānam na sādhana abhāve sādhya siddhiḥ iti eke tu pratijñānyūnam vākyam na asti iti ācakṣate etat tu na yuktam pratijñām antareṇa prayogaḥ vikalpataḥ paryanuyojyaḥ yaḥ pratijñānyūnam vākyam brūte kim ayam nigṛhyate atha naḥ iti yadi nigṛhyate katamat nigraha sthānam iti na hi hetvābhāsa ādayaḥ atra santi iti na ca hetu ādi doṣāḥ santi iti nigraham ca abhyupaiti tasmāt pratijñānyūnam eva iti atha na nigrahaḥ nyūnam vākyam artham sādhayati iti sādhana abhāve siddhiḥ abhyupagatā bhavati yat tu bravīṣi siddhānta parigrahaḥ eva pratijñā etat api na budhyāmahe karmaṇaḥ upādānam pratijñā sāmānya viśeṣavataḥ avadhāritasya vastunaḥ parigrahaḥ siddhāntaḥ iti 
NV_5.2.13	 yasmin vākye hetū dvau dṛṣṭāntau dvau tat vākyam adhikam nigraha sthānam ādhikyāt tat ca na dārḍhyāt iti eke eke tu bruvate naḥ idam nigraha shānam dārḍhyāt dārḍhyam hi jñāpyasya bhūyobhiḥ jñāpakaiḥ dṛṣṭam yathā dhūma ālokābhyām agneḥ iti na dārḍhya artha anabhidhānāt bhūyobhiḥ jñāpakaiḥ dārḍhyam bhavati iti na dārḍhya arthaḥ abhidhīyate kim bravīṣi dārḍhyāt iti sutarām pratipattiḥ dārḍhyam iti tat api tādṛś eva kim uktam bhavati sutarām iti atha bravīṣi dve api jñāpake satyam dve api jñāpake ekena eva abhidhānāt vyartham abhidhānam dvitīyasya prakāśite pradīpa antara upādāna vat iti anavasthā vā prakāśite api sādhana antara upādānāt iti 
NV_5.2.14–5.2.15	 śabda punaruktam anityaḥ śabdaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti artha punaruktam anityaḥ śabdaḥ nirodha dharmakaḥ dhvānaḥ iti anuvāde tu apunaruktam artha viśeṣa upapatteḥ na ābādhanāt iti eke eke tu bruvate naḥ idam nigraha sthānam abādhanāt na hi parīkṣā vidheḥ punar bruvatā kim cit bādhyate para pratipādana artham ca vākya prayogaḥ punar abhidhānena sutarām artham pratipadyate iti na nigraha sthānam pratipādaka tvāt satyam pratipādayati pratipādita artha pratipādaka tvāt vaiyarthyam syāt vaiyarthyāt nigraha sthānam sādhana viṣaya aparijñānāt na ca ayam śiṣyaḥ na guruḥ tasmāt na ayam punar pratipādyate iti arthāt āpannasya sva śabdena punarvacanam punar uktam pūrvavat nigraha sthānam 
NV_5.2.16	 śeṣam bhāṣye na uttarena avasthānāt na idam nigraha sthānam iti ke cit uttareṇa avasthānāt uttareṇa guṇa doṣavatā mūḍha tva āmūḍha tvam gamyate iti kim punar uccaritena asti asti hi uttare kaḥ cit samarthaḥ dṛśyate na pratyuccāraṇe na asau tāvatā nigraha sthānam arhati yaḥ ca ārabhya sva pakṣam na nirvāhayet tasya syāt khalīkāra mātram iti na uttara viṣaya aparijñānāt yadi ayam na pratyuccārayati nirviṣayam uttaram prasajyate atha uttaram bravīti katham naḥ uccārayati tat idam vyāhatam ucyate naḥ uccārayati uttaram ca bravīti iti apratijñānāt ca na idam pratijñāyate pūrvam uccārayitavyam paścāt uttaram abhidheyam api tu yathā katham cit uttaram vaktavyam uttaram ca āśraya abhāve na yuktam iti yuktam apratyuccāraṇam nigraha sthānam iti 
NV_5.2.17–5.2.19	 sphuṭam bhāṣye apratipattitaḥ nigraha sthānam śloka pāṭhā ādibhiḥ avajñām darśayan naḥ uttaram pratipadyate iti tat apratibhā nāma nigraha sthānam mūḍha tvāt iti yatra kartavyam kāryam vyāsajya kathām vicchinatti sa vikṣepaḥ vijñeyaḥ yathā rasālayā mayā bhuktam pratiśyāya kaṇaḥ me kaṇṭham kṣiṇoti iti evam ādi tat katham nigraha sthānam ajñāna nigūhana artham tu prayukta jñānam eva parihāreṇa āviṣkaroti 
NV_5.2.20	 yaḥ pareṇa coditam doṣam anuddhṛtya bhavataḥ api ayam samānaḥ doṣaḥ iti bravīti sā mata anujñā para matam sva mate anujānāti udāharaṇam bhavān cauraḥ puruṣa tvāt iti sa tam prati brūyāt bhavān api iti saḥ abhyupagamya doṣam para pakṣe abhyanujānāti iti nigṛhītaḥ veditavyaḥ anabhyupagacchatā na puruṣa tvam caurya hetuḥ iti vaktavyam kim tu para svena anati sṛṣṭena sambandhaḥ etat uttarā parijñānāt nigṛhyate iti prasaṅga vidhānāt na nigraha sthānam iti anye apare tu bruvate naḥ etat nigraha sthānam prasaṅga vidhānāt na eva asau paścāt api tam doṣam pratipadyate api tu prasaṅgam karoti yadi puruṣa tvāt cauraḥ bhavati bhavān api puruṣaḥ tasmāt cauraḥ iti etat tu na atas eva yatas eva ayam uttare vaktavye prasaṅgam karoti atas eva uttara aparijñānāt nigṛhyate iti 
NV_5.2.21–5.2.22	 yaḥ nigraha sthāna prāptam na nigṛhṇāti sa nigṛhītaḥ veditavyaḥ nigraha sthāna prāptasya aparijñānāt na anya vacanāt iti anye anye bruvate naḥ idam nigraha sthānam anya uttarasya abhidhānāt yasmāt asau nigraha sthāna prāptam na nigṛhṇāti bruvan anyat uttaram abhidhatte iti tat ca na atas eva yatas eva asau nigraha sthāne vaktvaye anyat abhidhatte atas eva nigṛhyate jānānaḥ hi asau kim artham anyat bravīti anigraha sthāne eva abhidhatte nigṛhītaḥ asti iti etat nigraha sthāna aparijñānāt nigraha sthānam iti 
NV_5.2.23–5.2.24	 asya udāharaṇam sphuṭam bhāṣye pratijñāta artha vyatirekeṇa abhyupagata artha parityāgāt nigṛhyate iti yathā eva vibhaktāḥ lakṣaṇena tathā eva teṣām nigraha sthāna bhāvaḥ iti te ime pramāṇa ādayaḥ uddiṣṭāḥ prathama sūtre lakṣitāḥ prathame adhyāye parīkṣitāḥ śeṣeṣu iti trividhā tantrasya parisamāptiḥ uktāḥ veditavyāḥ iti
